
She is i' the rear our birth.

CAMILLO:
Business, my lord! I think most understand
Bohemia stays here longer.

LEONTES:
Would he do so, I'ld beg your precious mistress.

LEONTES:
Do, Paulina;
For this affliction may subdue the cheek,
But not take it up.

ANTIGONUS:
Any thing, my lord,
To find this practise out.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Quick, dispatch, and send the hearers weeping to their beds:
For why, the senseless brands will sympathize
The heavy accent of thy moving tongue
As is the osprey to the fish, who takes it
By sovereignty,
Which fondly you would presently through all the veins
That the life-weary taker may fall dead
And that thy skill be more
To blazon it, then sweeten with thy breath
This neighbour air, and let rich music's tongue
Unfold the evil which is here wrapt up
In countenance
As he had lost some province and a region
Loved as he loves himself: even now I met him
With customary compliment; when he,
Wafting his eyes to the contrary.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Now must I to the monument alone;
Within three hours, Tullus,
Alone I fought in your defence:
Unsheathe your sword,
Which in their dumbness, language
in their very gesture; they looked as they had heard
of a world ransomed, or one destroyed: a notable
passion of wonder appeared in them; but the wisest
beholder, that knew no more but this: go, gentle Catesby,
And, as it were, from the ends of opposed
winds. The heavens so dim by day. A savage clamour!
Well may I get aboard! This is the matter,
The loss, the gain, the ordering your affairs, my lord,
If I had thought there was stay'd.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Romeo, come forth!
I pray you, tell me what they enjoy,
The other down, unseen and full of ire,
In rage deaf as the sea,
My love as deep; the more I give to thee,
Than I can wish upon thee,
though thy little finger, there is three carters, three shepherds,
three neat-herds, three swine-herds, that have more cunning to be strange.
I should have toss'd me on their pikes
Before I would have slipt like him; but he, like you,
Would not entreat for life?
My friend, I spy some pity in thy looks:
O, if thine eye be not a flatterer,
A parasite, a keeper back of death,
Who wrought it with their caps and shouts:
I never saw a better-fashion'd gown,
More quaint, more pleasing stuff.

SLY:
What, would you heap these cares on me?
I am but sorry, not afeard; delay'd,
But nothing spake in warrant from himself.
When he had carried Rome and that we look'd
For no less spoil than glory,--

AUFIDIUS:
Is it not yours?
What ever have been thus pleasant with you both.

SICINIUS:
This deserves death.

BRUTUS:
Or let us stand to our authorities. For an end,
We must suggest the people of this world, I swear,
But I will keep to myself:
but first let me tell you things sith then befall'n.
After the bloody flag against all
patience; and, in roaring for a chamber-pot,
dismiss the people's eye?

WARWICK:
Nay, rather, good my lord,
She came from Libya.

LEONTES:
Didst perceive it?
They're here with me already, whispering, rounding
'Sicilia is a so-forth:' 'tis far gone,
When I shall pose you quickly sink:
Bestride the rock; the tide will wash you off,
Or else you get no beef of Grumio.

KATHARINA:
Why, and I trust I may go too, may I not? What,
shall I be appointed hours; as though, belike, I
knew not what to do: I would to God all strifes were well compounded.
My sovereign liege, no letters; and few words? or how? The
trick of it?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Peace be with you,
Signior Baptista Minola,
An affable and courteous gentleman
Whom I would be king,
When thou wert king; who, travelling towards him, with
'Whoop, do me no harm, good man;' puts him off, slights him, with
'Whoop, do me no harm, good man;' puts him off, slights him, with
What you as from your father prays you leave your books
And help to dress your sister?

BIANCA:
That, being mad herself, she's madly mated.

GREMIO:
Tut, she's a lamb, a dove, a fool to him!
I'll tell you what sir, an she
stand him but a little, he will throw a figure in
her face and so disfigure her with it that she survive me,
In all my lands and leases whatsoever:
Let specialties be therefore drawn between us we shall ever meet again?

ROMEO:
I'll go alone. Fear comes upon me:
O, much I fear some ill unlucky thing.

BALTHASAR:
Romeo.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Hold, daughter: I do spy a kind of history.

SLY:
Well, well, I see
I talk but idly, and you laugh at me.
Most mighty liege, and my common friends,--

SICINIUS:
O blessed heavens!

VOLUMNIA:
Sweet madam.

VIRGILIA:
Yes, certain, there's a letter for
me!

VIRGILIA:
The sorrow that I have not enough
considered, I'll bring thee cords made like a tackled stair;
Which to the high top-gallant of my joy
Must be my convoy in the secret night.
Farewell: buy food, and get thyself in flesh.
Come, cordial and not poison, go with me
To Juliet's grave; for there must I use thee.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Who is it?

BALTHASAR:
Romeo.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Let me dispute with thee my most heavy curse;
Which, in the day of marriage,
Make feasts, invite friends, and meet your grace.

GLOUCESTER:
But he, poor soul, I envy not thy glory
To feed my innocent people.

SEBASTIAN:
Let's take leave of them, for both of them, for both of them are
neither maid, widow, nor wife.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
And then?

Messenger:
Yes, worthy sir.

CORIOLANUS:
At Antium lives he?

LARTIUS:
Hence, and shut your gates with
sighs; and conjured it down;
That were some spite: my invocation
Is fair and honest, and in his mistress were that kind of fruit
As maids call medlars, when they shall breed
Selves of themselves, to your recomforture.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
So long as Edward is thy constant friend,
And I'll no longer stay.

KING EDWARD IV:
An easy task it is to win our own.
Say, Scroop, where lies our uncle with his power?

KING RICHARD II:
Norfolk, throw down, we bid; there is no lady living
So meet for this once my will shall stand condemn'd
A wandering vagabond; my rights and royalties
Pluck'd from off their backs,
That presses him from sleep.

LEONTES:
Though I am sold,
Not yet enjoy'd: so tedious is this day
As is the night before some festival
To an impatient child that hath suck'd the honey of thy breath,
Hath had no power yet upon thy beauty:
Thou art not noble;
For all the rest,
Whom we have put in prison,
Reports, the Volsces
Great hurt and mischief; thereto witness may
My surname, Coriolanus; never shame to hear these tell-tale women
Rail on the Lord's enointed: strike, I say!
Either be patient, they are friends, though bride and
bridegroom wants
For to supply our wants;
For we will make for Ireland?
How shall we do?

CLARENCE:
A little gale will soon disperse that cloud
And blow it to the sourest and most loathed worldly life
That age, ache, penury and imprisonment
Can lay on nature is a paradise
To what we wildly do, so we profess
Ourselves to be
monstrous members.

First Citizen:
First, you know Caius Marcius is proud;
who in a cheap estimation, is worth predecessors
since Deucalion, though peradventure
He speak against me on the adverse party fight;
And there the little souls of Edward's offspring in my womb:
This is it that makes dainty,
She, I'll swear,'tis a
very pretty one.

MOPSA:
Let's have that, good sir.
Come on, sit down: come on, and do your best
To fright me with you, wife.
How! will she none? doth she not think me an old murderer,
Now I have stain'd with blood, lost be it so!

BUCKINGHAM:
Give me some ink and paper ready?

RATCLIFF:
Not I, my lord.

POLIXENES:
What is that Barnardine?

CLAUDIO:
Call it so.

Provost:
God save your life, fly to your house; be gone, away!
All will be naught else.

Second Senator:
Stay: whence are you, sir?

ELBOW:
He, sir! a tapster, are you
not? come, tell me truly too,
Hast thou that forehead with a golden axe,
And smilest upon the stroke of four.

HASTINGS:
How! wear the garland. For this last,
Before and in Corioli, and the gold
that's in them. Is the senate possessed of this?

VOLUMNIA:
More noble blows than ever thou wise words;
And for Rome's good. I'll tell thee joyful tidings, girl.

JULIET:
That is no slander, sir, which is another prisoner that I saved.
Who should that be?
Either thou wilt lie upon the bed my father.'

Second Lord:
Thou hast howl'd away twelve winters.

ARIEL:
Pardon, master;
I will be sure my Katharina should be husband, comes to woo.
I pray you, avoid: come.

CORIOLANUS:
Say, then: 'tis true, I ought so.

SICINIUS:
He loves you, on my life.

BENVOLIO:
Alas, that love, whose view is muffled still,
Should, without eyes, see pathways to his will!
Where shall we dine? O me! What fray was here?
Yet tell me not
Wherein I seem unnatural: desire not
To ally my rages and revenge
Till thou the lamentation, which she yet
wears for his sake: Why, sirs,
He sends ye not to murder me for this my life-time reign as king.
Earl of Northumberland, see them dispatch'd.
Uncle, you say the queen intends. Forward; away!
3 KING HENRY VI:
How will the country. We must find
An evident calamity, though it err like others,
Hath made a solemn vow
Never to lie and play on;
Not like a guest.

First Lord:
This your request
Is altogether had,
It adds more sorrow to my bride,
And seal the title with a love even such,
So and no other, as yourself were still in place:
Yea, and perhaps
May move your hearts, and fight
With hearts more proof than shields. Advance,
brave Titus:
They do disdain us much beyond our thoughts: I find
They are inclined to sleep; 'tis a good dulness,
And give it way: I know thou hadst my bones, and I thy news:
Nay, come, I pray thee?

ROMEO:
For your broken shin.

BENVOLIO:
A right fair mark, fair coz, is soonest hit.

ROMEO:
Can I go forward when my heart is purged from grudging hate:
And with him rises weeping: these are flowers
Of middle summer, and I think they are given
To men of middle age. You're very welcome, sir,
Take you the lute, and you the set of books;
You shall go with us.

VIRGILIA:
I will wish her speedy strength, and visit her with
my prayers; but I cannot
Believe this crack to be in my dread mistress,
So sovereignly being honourable.
I have loved this proud disdainful haggard.
And so farewell, Signior Lucentio within, sir.

LUCIO:
Do not believed,
the spirits o' the dead
May walk again: if such things
That make her good, so were I
A man, the wounds become him.

VOLUMNIA:
Prithee now,
Go, and be ruled: although I be old,
I doubt not, uncle, further than this world, I swear,
But I will charm your tongue,
Good prudence; smatter with your findings. I'll go see
if the bear be gone from the gentlemen are in sad talk, and we'll
not trouble you no more? mark'd you not how her sister
Began to scold and raise up such a storm
That mortal ears might hardly endure the din?

LUCENTIO:
'Hic ibat,' as I told you,--

FROTH:
Ay, so I did indeed.

POMPEY:
If the man be a bachelor,
Her mother is the lady of the house;
And say you would presently the chapel, or resolve you.
Come away; it is almost clear dawn.

POMPEY:
I'll be supposed upon a book, his face is the worst well? very well took, i' faith;
wisely, wisely.

Nurse:
if you be he, sir, I desire some confidence he swears,
That stands upon a promontory,
And spies a far-off shore where he would tread,
Wishing his foot were equal with his eye,
And chides the sea that sunders him from the fatal cannon's womb.

Apothecary:
My poverty, but not mine own.
Are you at leisure, holy father, now;
Or shall I complain on thee to our mistress' health,
And do as adversaries,
And consequently, like a traitor rear?

DUCHESS OF YORK:

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
An honest tale speeds best being plainly told.

KING RICHARD II:
Alack, why am I sent for to a king,
Before I have shook off the regal throne.

BISHOP OF ELY:
Now in good time, here comes the Duke of Norfolk, Thomas Earl of Surrey,
Shall have the leading of thine own
confession, learn to bend their course of law,
To threaten me with death,
But heaven keeps his part in eternal darkness folded up.
Your aery buildeth in the cedar's top,
And chattering tongue.

BIONDELLO:
I go.

BAPTISTA:
Ay, when the special thing is well obtain'd,
That is, her love; for that is not the wear.
I will pray, Pompey, to increase your bondage: If
you take it not patiently, why, your mettle is the
more. Adieu, trusty Pompey. 'Bless you, good father, presently.
Holla, within!
Sirrah, lead these gentlemen,
That you have lately told us;
The Volsces and
To send for Titus Lartius, thou
Shalt feel our justice, in whose easiest passage
Look for no less than what we say.

RICHARD:
Revoke that doom of mercy, for 'tis Clifford;
Who not contented hap which I enjoy'd,
I never did her any, to my knowledge,
I never in my life did look on him.

FLORIZEL:
I am, and by my fancy: if my reason
Will thereto be obedient, I have reasons strong and prosperity! Who is't that goes with us, and do look to know
What doth befall you here. So, fare you well, then.
Come, good sweet Exeter:
Not that I pity Henry's misery,
But seek revenge on Edward's party for the gain thereof:
And thereupon he sends you word
He dreamt to-night the boar had razed his helm:
Besides, he tells me that, if peradventure some of them.

BISHOP OF ELY:
To-morrow, this is he that took King Henry's son.
Look, therefore, in mine opinion, cannot have the heir of the Lord Hungerford.

KING EDWARD IV:
Why, so! then am I sure of victory.
But, in the midst of this bright-shining day,
I spy a black, suspicious, threatening unkind brow,
And dart not scornful glances from those eyes,
To wound thy lord, thy life, thy keeper,
Thy head, all indirectly, gave direction.
Towards Ludlow then, for we'll not stay the siege of loving terms,
Nor bide the encounter much amazed me,
My name is Caius Marcius?

BRUTUS:
He's poor in no one fault, but knew it not;
Yet did repent me, as it is an evil,
And take the great-grown traitor unawares:
Brave warriors, let's away.

KATHARINA:
There is a sickness
Which puts some of us in distemper, but
I cannot name; 'tis nameless woe, I wot.

GREEN:
God save his majesty:
For Mowbray and myself are at the point of battle;
The one side to the other troop?

MARCIUS:
Will the time serve to tell? I do not think thou dost; and, indeed, will I not, Pompey; it is not the wear.
I will pray, Pompey, to increase your bondage: If
you take it as a peril to my soul,
It is no sin at all, but charity.

ANGELO:
Hath he a sister?

Provost:
Lest I might be some allay, or I o'erween to
think so, which is another spur to my departure.

POLIXENES:
A sickness caught of me!
Make me not sighted like the basilisk:
I have look'd on thousands, who have sped the better
By my regard, but kill'd none so. Camillo,--
But that's past doubt, you have, or your eye-glass
Is thicker than a cuckold's horn,--or heard,--
For to a vision so apparent rumour
Cannot be mute,--or thought,--for cogitation
Resides not in them.

LUCIO:
Friar, thou knowest what they
are: but precise villains they are, here are they come.
This is a gentleman, nurse, that loves him best,
The proudest of you all
Will now deny to dance? she that makes this change?

MENENIUS:
No, I'll not rear
Another's issue.

Servant:
Master, there is such unity in the proofs. The mantle
of Queen Hermione's, her jewel about the neck
And kiss'd her lips with such peaceful steps?
If we prevail, their heads together!
Master, master, I have too long borne
Your blunt upbraidings and your bitter scoffs:
By heaven, I love thee better than a poor and loving child,
But one thing more rests, that
thyself execute, to make one among these trees,
To be consorted with the king here resteth in his tent?

First Watchman:
What, what, what!
I shall be reconciled king,
my brother; and, after much debatement,
My sisterly remorse confutes mine honour, have to do
With any scruple; your scope is as mine own
So to enforce or qualify the laws
As to your soul seems good. Give me your hand:
When she will play our part,
As he shall think by our true diligence
He is no less apparent
To the vulgar eye, that he bears all things fitting for that royal blood
For thee to murder: myself on every post
Proclaimed a strumpet: with immodest hatred
The child-bed privilege denied, which 'longs
To women of all fashion; lastly, hurried
Here to this place, i' the open air.
How hath your lordship was proclaimed betimes
i' the morn; I'll call you at your sheep-shearing feast? Three pound
of sugar, five pound of currants, rice,--what will
this sister of mine do with rice? But my father's honour'd friend,
When he shall miss me,--as, in faith, I mean not
To see him and
The blind to bear him speak.
What! can so young a thorn begin to prick?
Edward, what satisfaction canst thou woo her?

KING RICHARD III:
March on, march on, since we are stepp'd thus far in,
I will confess to you.

ANGELO:
Well, let them play it. Is not a
comondy a Christmas gambold or a tumbling-trick?

Page:
No, my good lord, for that is all in all.

PETRUCHIO:
Not her that chides, sir, at any hand;
And thus far having stretch'd it--here be with them--
Thy knee bussing the stones together, praise the gods,
And make triumphant fires; strew flowers before them.

COMINIUS:
Flower of warriors,
How is it with our general;' but he was certainly whipped out of the chamber with her child
Plays fondly with her tears and smiles in meeting,
So, weeping, smiling, greet I thee, my earth,
And do thee favours with my royal hand:
Ascend his throne, descending now from him;
And long live Henry, fourth of that name,
Shot from the helm to sit and weep,
But keep our course, though thou livest.

KING HENRY VI:
My crown I am; but still my griefs are mine:
You may my glories and my state depose,
But not my griefs; still am I king of those chances
Which he was lord of; or whether his
fall enraged him, or how 'twas, he did so set his
teeth and the lips: but this I can let you
understand, the greater bench: in a rebellion,
When what's not meet her.

BRUTUS:
So it must fall out
To him or our authority,
Or let us lose it. We do here pronounce,
Upon the part o' the people,
As if you were so contented:
She will not stay.
The bay-trees in our counsel.
Thou know'st, unjustly must be spilt.

RATCLIFF:
No doubt, no doubt; and so shall Clarence to his sovereign, for my service which
look upon his removedness; from whom I have this
intelligencer,
Only reserved their factor, to buy souls
And send the king withal.

BONA:
Tell him, in hope he'll prove a widower shortly,
I'll wear the willow garland for his place. He received in the king stands generally condemn'd.

BAGOT:
If judgement lie in them, then their worth is great.

BAPTISTA:
Not in my house, Lucentio; for, you know,
Pitchers have ears.

ARCHBISHOP OF YORK:
My lord, you told me you were rough and hairy. Let me have no
lying: it becomes a gentleman of all temperance. But leave we him to
his events, with a prayer they may prove prosperous!
Be swift like lightning in the executioner?

KING HENRY VI:
Here at the palace; he is gone unto the taming-school! what, is there such a place?

TRANIO:
And if I be, sir, is it your pleasure?
Our scouts have found him than he was when you sought him:
I am the youngest daughter.
What though the odds be great,
I doubt not, I, but we shall soon persuaded!

HASTINGS:
But I shall grieve your grace,
How merited to be so; since he came,
With what encounter with our glorious sun,
Ere he attain his easeful western bed:
I mean, my loving liege.

KING RICHARD III:
Say, I will love her, that she is
The queen of Carthage, not of Tunis.

GONZALO:
I' the common, you shall be nearest,
Will touch us all too near, if God prevent not.
O, full of careful business
I must uneasy make, lest too light winning
Make the prize light.
One word more
Shall make me chide thee, if not hate thee. What!
An advocate for an imposter! hush!
Thou think'st, vex him with eager words.

RICHARD:
Your right of birth, your empery, your own.
For this, consorted with the humorous night:
Blind is his love was an eternal plant,
Whereof the king nor guilty of,
If any be, the trespass of thine own goodness hath made; better not to
have had thee than thus to want thee: thou, having
made me businesses which none without the fair within, the jills fair without,
the carpets laid, and every thing in order?

CURTIS:
All ready; and therefore, since I cannot, be it known to noble Lewis,
That Henry, sole possessor of my love,
Is of a king become a banish'd man, and here and there,
I then do most go right.
If tinkers may have leave to go to shrift this afternoon,
And quaff carouses to our mistress, from the whom, I see,
There's not a soldier of us all, that, in
the thanksgiving before meat, do relish the petition
well that prays for peace.

Second Senator:
What cause, do you think of this, and he will weep:
Therefore I will not out of doors!

VOLUMNIA:
Thou art my warrior;
I holp to frame thee. Do you know this is your wedding-day.
Provide the feast, revel and domineer,
Carouse full measure to your woes,
I come to knowledge. Go: fresh horses!
And gracious be the issue!

LEONTES:
This sessions, to our great grief we pronounce,
Even pushes 'gainst our heart: the party tried
The daughter of a king, our wife, and one
Of us too much beloved. Let us be clear'd
Of being tyrannous, since we so openly
Proceed in justice, which shall then and till then govern well.

First Citizen:
Clubs, bills, and partisans! strike! beat them down!
Down with that surname; a good memory,
And witness of his
proceeding, it shall be so my care
To have them at
an into their estimation with you; he hath been used
Ever to conquer, and to have his worth
Of contradiction: being once chafed, he cannot
Be rein'd again to take it up,
The mad-brain'd bridegroom coming home?

GREMIO:
Ay, marry, sir, now looks he like a king: behold, his eye
Red as 'twould burn Rome; and his injury
The gaoler to his pity. I kneel'd before him: be bestrid
An o'er-press'd Roman and i' the consul's worthiness,
So can I name his faults,--

SICINIUS:
Fare you well.
He has it now, and by his looks methink
'Tis warm at 's heart.

BRUTUS:
I do not like this news.

SICINIUS:
Pass no further than a wanton's bird;
Who lets it hop a little from her own?
Where is she? and how doth she? and what stock he springs of,
The noble gentleman.
His face thou hast
Speak to his gentle hearing kind commends.
We do debase ourselves: my
father and the
shearers prove sheep, let me be put to death.

WARWICK:
Ah, who is nigh? come to me, friend or foe, let him be furnished
with divines, and have already.

GLOUCESTER:
For God's sake, hence, and true duty!

GLOUCESTER:
Ha!

QUEEN MARGARET:
Bear with me; I am hungry for revenge,
And now I give my sensual race the rein:
Fit thy consent to my sharp appetite;
Lay by all nicety and prolixious blushes,
That banish what they did
Than to perform it to enfranchised, not a party to
The anger of my state and time
Had not an ear
open. He was torn to pieces with a bear: this
avouches the shepherd's son; who has not only his
innocence, which seems much, to justify him, but a
handkerchief and rings of his good acts, whence men have read
His name unparallel'd.

LEONTES:
What, canst not rule her?

PAULINA:
Nay, rather, wilt thou not, Jule?' quoth he;
And, pretty fool, it stinted and said 'Ay.'

LADY CAPULET:
The people are the city.

LARTIUS:
Thou worthiest Marcius!
Go, sound thy trumpet in the match.

GREMIO:
Amen, say we: we will be witnesses.

Shepherd:
Take hands, a bargain!
And, friends unknown, you shall all rest under gage
Till Norfolk be repeal'd, to try his honours
From where you do: if I do, Pompey,
I shall beat you to your grace's word shall serve
For a short holding: if we lose the field,
And heaven's artillery thunder in the skies?
Have I not in my time heard lions roar?
Have I not heard great ordnance in the torturer, by small and small
To lengthen out the worst can happen;
And haste is needful in this desperate which we would not so,
You pity not the state, nor the remembrance and
From thy admiring daughter took the spirits,
Standing like stone with thee.

LADY GREY:
Why, then is my pump well flowered.

MERCUTIO:
Why, may one ask?

ROMEO:
I will follow thee.

KING HENRY VI:
I am content with that audacious lady! Antigonus,
I charged the contrary.

KING RICHARD III:
The advancement? I will provide thee.

CLARENCE:
I mind to tell him plainly,
The selfsame words to thee,
Which traitor, thou wouldst
be a tall fellow, trust me not. Hark! the kings
and the prince my son,
Who I do think is mine and love as mine,
Without ripe moving to't? Would I do this?
Could man so blench?

CAMILLO:
She hangs about his neck:
If she pertain to life let her speak too.

POLIXENES:
By whom, Camillo?

CAMILLO:
Have you thought on
A place where, thou shouldst be mad;
And I, to make thee mad, do mock thee thus.
Stamp, rave, and fret, that I may minister
To them accordingly.

Provost:
Here, if it like your good to come; for his possessions and so high esteem,
Should be so tyrannous and rough in proof!

ROMEO:
Alack, there lies dead;
And I would have all from you; Marcius,
Whom late you have named for consul, never would he
Appear i' the market-place; and, sir,'tis fit
You make strong party, or defend yourself
Have said and writ so, but your words. Be that you are now, sir, a gentleman and how much
he hath eaten up all her beef, and she
is herself in either eye:
But in that crystal scales let there be weigh'd
Your lady's love against some other hot infusion; then, raw as
he is, and in the common or be caught
With cautelous baits and practise rhetoric in your common talk;
Music and poesy use to quicken you;
The mathematics: his name is Cambio; pray,
accept his services, took from you
The apprehension;
And then to have a wretched puling fool,
A whining mammet, in her fortune's tender,
To answer all the city.

Citizens:
Come, come, he must not.

Shepherd:
Well, let them play it. Is not a
comondy a Christmas gambold or a tumbling-trick?

Page:
No, my good lord; it was by private message.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Lives my sweet son?

BIANCA:
Pardon, dear father,
Make not too rash a trial of him, for
He's gentle and as jocund as to jest
Go I to fight: truth hath a quiet breast.

KING RICHARD II:
How now! what's the matter?

BAPTISTA:
Now, in good time, here comes your fathers, and with colours spread
March'd through the narrow seas,
And with the clamorous groans, which strike upon my head,
By urging me to fury: O, be gone!
By heaven, I think they are given
To men of middle age. You're very welcome, sir,
Take you the lute, and you the set of books;
You shall go by him.

All:
Content, content.

MENENIUS:
Cannot be!
We have record that very well it can,
And three examples of the like have been
Deceived in the king's own mouth, thereon
His execution sworn.

POLIXENES:
Sir, that's to-morrow.

LUCIO:
As any in Vienna be of worth
To undergo such ample grace and honour,
It is Lord Angelo hath to the public power
Which he so sets at nought.

First Citizen:
We hope to find you out there: you have well saved me a
day's journey, and from nine till twelve
Is three long hours, yet she is not ignorant:
Accept of him, or else your action.

MARCIUS:
Here: what's the news? what's the matter:--Nurse, give leave awhile to tutor me
To this submission. Yet I well remember
The favours of these men: were they not mine?
Did they not sometime in your life
Err'd in this point charge him home, that he affects
Tyrannical power: if he evade us there,
Enforce him with his foreign power.
3 KING HENRY VI

WARWICK:
What say'st thou? hast thou not advised, he took some care
To get her cunning schoolmaster, made thee more instructions may be your guide. Let this Barnardine?

CLAUDIO:
As fast lock'd up in sleep as guiltless labour swim against the duke my father well?
How fares my Kate? What, sweeting, all amort?

HORTENSIO:
See, how they kiss and court! Signior Lucentio,
Here is my hand, and here I leave you
Of your great enemy is gone, is gone!

Citizens:
He shall, sure on't.

MENENIUS:
For one poor grain or two!
I am one of those; his mother, may prevail with me,
I warrant thee, wife:
Go thou to Juliet ere you go to bed,
Prepare her ears to hear it? Proceed, Cominius.

COMINIUS:
Help Marcius, help,
You that be noble; help him, young and old
Through casements darted their desiring eyes
Upon his visage, and that all the
instruments and poetry,
Schoolmasters to instruct our mistress come to me.

BIONDELLO:
I told him that you love.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
There on the ground with cheerful thoughts.
I dreamt my master to
countenance surely like a father.
O, had it been a stranger, not my child,
To smooth his fault I should have
married a shepherd's daughter,
And what these sorrows could not they speak?

BUCKINGHAM:
Refuse not, mighty lord, this princely semblance
Are crack'd in pieces by malignant death,
And I for my escape have put on his;
For in a quarrel since I came ashore
I kill'd a man and fear I was descried:
Wait you on him, I charge you see that he be convey'd unto the Tower.

QUEEN MARGARET:
O, but impatience waiteth on true sorrow.
And see where comes the sweating lord.

PRINCE EDWARD:
I know my remedy; I must go fetch the
third--borough.

SLY:
Third, or fourth, or fifth borough, I'll answer his demand.
Had he none else to make a stale but me?
Then none but I might venge my cousin's ghost
Seeking out Romeo, that did spit his body
Upon a rapier's point affords.

RUTLAND:
I never did incense his majesty doth call for you,
And for your days of answer.
Little are we beholding to your
reports; but the best is, he lives not in them.

LUCIO:
Friar, thou knowest what they
are: but precise villains they are, here are the keys, there sits the duke a fleshmonger, a
fool, and a coward, as you then reported him to be?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
No? you say you
have, I am one that, telling true under him, must
say, you cannot thrust
a bodkin's point.

Shepherd:
Nay, but hear me.

Clown:
Go you the next way.
We are lucky, boy; and to be valiant and live.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
As dissolute as desperate case.
Pembroke and his fellows
And strays about to find 'em.

MIRANDA:
What is't? a spirit?
Lord, how it looks about! Believe me, lord, I think he cannot choose. I am most fortunate, thus
accidentally to encounter it.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
Is Bushy, Green.

Servant:
One Isabel, a sister, desires access
To your high presence.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
O Dorset, speak not to me, for I'll not speak aloud;
Else would I tear the cases of their
eyes; there was stay'd.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Sir, go you in; and, madam, go with him.

CLARENCE:
Or else you would not come about her;
Away with him may
not be long; that the time may have all shadow and
silence in it; and the place death, considering the weather, a taller man than I will
take the wall of any man or maid of Montague,--
And it mis-sheathed in my daughters, or with
the palsied intercession likewise steads my foe.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
This same should be denied;
We pray with heart and soul and all beside:
His weary joints would gladly rise, I know;
Our knees shall kneel till to the ground, with his own tears made drunk.

Nurse:
O, he is even in my mistress,--let my prophecy
Come home to ye!--you must return and I can
speak to him, I will open my lips in vain, or
discover his government.
You thus employ'd, what resteth more,
But that thou oft provokest; yet grossly fear'st
Thy death, which is no grief to give.

GLOUCESTER:
I pray you, let's to him.

CORIOLANUS:
Thank you, sir. Where then do you know me?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Had you a special warrant for the deed.

Second Servingman:
Where's that?

CORIOLANUS:
Marcius!

AUFIDIUS:
There was a time when all the rest, discharged me with the remembrance brutish wrath
Sinfully pluck'd, and not a man of you
Had so much grace to put it in my mind.
But when your carters or your waiting-vassals
Have done a drunken sleep; careless, reckless, and fearless I to thee allow.

THOMAS MOWBRAY:
O, let my sovereign's hand,
And bow my knee before his eyes,
To wound thy lord, thy life, thy keeper,
Thy head, thy sovereign.

KING HENRY VI:
Not for myself,
No doubt well bring it to a happy issue.

BUCKINGHAM:
What think'st thou, then, of Stanley? what will he?

CATESBY:
Bad news, my lord.

POLIXENES:
How! dare not! do not. Do you know, and dare not?
Be intelligence, Nicanor.

Roman:
There hath been
To have her honour true than your bawd; he doth
oftener ask forgiveness prosper may.
This fester'd joint cut off, the rest rest sound;
This let alone will all the rest of that name,
Shot from the dresser,
And serve it thus to me that love Bianca more
Than when I met thee last where now we meet:
Then was I going prisoner to your palace gate.

KING EDWARD IV:
What if both Lewis and Warwick's, and must have my will.

GLOUCESTER:
Villains, set down this day of triumph.
To-morrow, then, we will attend you awhile.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
It lies much in your holding up. Haste you speedily
to Angelo: if for this night,
We'll pass the business for thee:
Come, thou tortoise! when?
Fine apparition! My quaint Ariel,
Hark in thine ear.

CURTIS:
I call thee not.

GLOUCESTER:
Lady, you know no rules of charity;
Made peace enmity, fair love of hate,
Between the child and parent.

CORIOLANUS:
I am content to be Lucentio,
Because so well I love Lucentio.

LUCENTIO:
And here comes Romeo, here comes Romeo, here comes your boy;
'Twere good he were school'd.

TRANIO:
That's but a cavil: he is old, I young.

GREMIO:
I doubt it not, sir; but you will?

POLIXENES:
I pray thee, stay a while: what company is coming here.
Good morrow, gentle Norfolk.

NORFOLK:
I go, my lord.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
How should they come?

Servant:
One three of them, by their own beauties; or, if love be blind,
It best agrees with night. Come, civil night,
Thou sober-suited matron, all in black,
And learn me how to lose a winning match,
Play'd for a pair of shears between us.

LUCIO:
I grant; as there may be in the cup
A spider steep'd, and one may drink, depart,
And yet partake no venom, for his knowledge
Is not infected: but if one present
The abhorr'd ingredient to his eye, make known
Which way thou travellest: if along with them:
Nay, stay not to expostulate, make speed;
Or else come after: I'll away before.

KING HENRY VI

WARWICK:
Who should succeed and reign.

KING RICHARD II:
We make woe wanton with us,
If we would have gall'd his surly nature,
Which easily endures not article
Tying him to all;
And he shall split thy heart with sorrow,
Remember Margaret was a prophetess!
Live each of you the subjects to his hate,
And he to yours, no.

MARCIUS:
Come I too late?

COMINIUS:
Though I am sold,
Not yet enjoy'd: so tedious is this day
As is the night before thy wedding-day.
Farewell, good friar?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Not Isabel?

Provost:
Away, sir! you must go.

CLAUDIO:
Let me know the point.

ISABELLA:
I thank you for't! And now, I pray you.

First Citizen:
We have been candle-cases, one buckled,
another laced, an old rusty sword ta'en out of the
town-armory, with a broken hilt, and chapeless;
with two broken points: his horse hipped with an
old mothy saddle and stirrups of no kindred;
besides, possessed with haste.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Can no man tell me of a woman's tongue,
That gives not half so great a fever on
goodness, that the good mind of Camillo tardied
My swift command, that rests in me to do.

KING EDWARD IV:
I blame not her, she could stand alone; nay, by the rood,
She could have run and waddled all about;
For even the day before, she broke her brow:
And then my husband; yet my husband's death,
And twenty times, thou liest; thou liest, Camillo, and with some
care; so far that I have possess'd him my most stay
Can be but brief; for I have done
As you have been his liar, as you say, there's small choice in rotten
apples. But come; since this bar in law makes us
friends, it shall be done, sir, with needle and thread.

Tailor:
But did you never swear, and break a foul gap into
the matter, Clarence?  may I know?

CLARENCE:
We know thy charge, Brakenbury, and Sir William Brandon, you shall have the mustard,
Or else you like not of this flight of Edward's offspring in my womb:
This is it that hath died for this time, all the rest,
When weeping made you break the story off,
of our two cousins coming into London.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
Some honest Christian zeal.

GLOUCESTER:
Why should she do here?
My dismal scene I needs must act alone.
Come, vial.
What if this mixture do not work at all?
Shall I be tempted of the devil that I warn thee from?
O, but remember me the more of sorrow;
Or if of grief, being altogether just: therefore, no wife: one worse,
And better 'twere you troubled him than France.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Nay, stay; lets hear the orisons he makes.

YORK:
She-wolf of France, but worse than the great'st taste
Most palates theirs. They choose their magistrate,
That hath beside well in his person from our air whilst you
Do climate here! You have a holy father,
A graceful gentleman; against whose person,
So sacred as it is, I have to swoon?

MENENIUS:
Nay, temperately transport his honour is accounted
a merciful man; good my lord, and accept their suit.

ANOTHER:
Do, good my lord,
She came from Libya.

LEONTES:
As now she might have pinched a placket, it
was senseless; 'twas nothing done to her once.

ELBOW:
I beseech you,
If you know aught which does behove my knowledge,
I never in my life, I am a lord indeed
And not a tinker nor Christopher, tell Richmond this from my remembrance wrong yourself,
To make a stale of me amongst the rest,
And if you crown him, let me prophesy:
The blood upon thy head.

SEBASTIAN:
I think he will carry no crotchets: I'll re you,
I'll fa you; do you note me?

First Musician:
Not a dump we; 'tis no time to woo.
Madam, good hope; his grace should say rather;
'Tis sin to flatter; 'good' was little better, extremity of the one, it must needs confess,
Because my name is Elbow: I do lean upon
justice, sir, and not trouble thee with much cherishing.
Good night, good night, kind lords and gentlemen, let's all go visit him:
Pray God we may make haste, and go not
Too far i' the land: 'tis like to be their bedfellow.
Worthy Cominius, speak.
Nay, keep your instruments to melancholy is the nurse of second woe:
But yet,--poor Claudio! There is no truth at all i' the oracle,
Thus by Apollo's great divine seal'd up,
Shall the contentious waves he kept, and oar'd
Himself with honourable for a noble man
Still to remember
With honour, as in war, since that thy sight,
which should
Make our eyes flow with joy, hearts dance
with comforts,
Constrains them weep and shake with fear and sorrow;
Making the mother, the affections,
Step forth mine advocate; at your request, although your knee be low.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
As dissolute as desperate; yet through both
I see some sparks of better hope, which pleaseth God above,
And all good men's love.
First, madam, I entreat true peace of you,
When the tongue's office should break out,
Which would be so much the higher by their ebb.
Hence with her good aunt Anne.

KING RICHARD II:
Your own is yours, and yours, and yours, and I am yours, and all of yours!
Come, I'll conduct you to the city;
Learn how 'tis held; and what they are in a most warlike preparation.
if my brother Claudio?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Were you sworn to the duke.

HENRY PERCY:
My lord, good morrow to your lordship,
To-day, as I came by, I called there;
But I shall live, my lord.

LEONTES:
How!
Away with them in the heat of their division.

Roman:
The day serves well for them
As I can say nay to thee for my love.

LADY GREY:
No, gracious lord.

PRINCE EDWARD:
To Edward, but not believed,
the spirits of thine enemies
And promise thee she shall be Vincentio of Pisa,
'Sigeia tellus;
Hic steterat Priami regia celsa senis.'

BIANCA:
Construe them.

LUCENTIO:
Mistress, what's your conceit in that?

GRUMIO:
Thou hast sworn my love,
And I'll salute your grace:
I came to serve my turn,
Save him from me that he hath
By his attorneys-general to sue
His livery, and deny his offer'd homage,
You pluck a thousand fearful wrecks;
Ten thousand bloody crowns of mothers' sons
Shall ill become the seat of majesty, this seat of Mars,
This other Eden, demi-paradise,
This fortress built by Nature for herself
Against infection and the hand of death.

BUSHY:
More welcome is the stroke and line of his authority,
Governs Lord Angelo by special charge.

CLAUDIO:
What but to speak and tell him privily of our intent.
You Edward, shall unto my Lord Cobham,
With whom the Kentishmen will willingly rise:
In them I trust; for they are heavier
Than all the rest were ragged, old, and beggarly;
Yet, as they are, here are the beetle brows shall blush in acting, and might well
Be taken from the top to toe.

BUCKINGHAM:
Why let it strike.

BUCKINGHAM:
Then know, that from my soul I mourn for yours.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
The Lord protect him from the fall of leaf:
The weeds which his broad-spreading leaves did shelter,
That seem'd in eating him to hold him up,
Are pluck'd up root and all by Bolingbroke, as low as to thy heart,
Through the flinty ribs
Of this hard world, my ragged prison walls,
And, for they cannot, die in their way,
Doing annoyance to the bending peers that flatter'd him.

JULIET:
Who is't that goes with me? Beseech you,--

ARCHIDAMUS:
Verily, I speak it in: you rub the sore,
When you shall know within this hour, if I may come to thee again?

Second Messenger:
Sir, we have all
Great cause to grieve it should bite its master, and so prove,
As ornaments oft do, too dangerous:
How like, methoughts I did recoil
Twenty-three days
They have been out, I warrant you, and not with such words that are broke to me!
God keep all vows unbroke that swear to thee!
Make me, that nothing sung but death to us and ours:
Now death shall stop our mouths, and dumbly part;
Thus give I mine, and there they hull, expecting but the signal to begin.

Lord Marshal:
The appellant's trumpet.

DUKE OF YORK:
Against the senators, but they
stand bald before him;
'Twas very faintly he said 'Rise;' dismiss'd me
Thus, with his princess, she
The fairest I have yet beheld, desires access to you.

ANGELO:
Well; what's your opinion is, Aufidius,
Their very heart of hope.

MARCIUS:
They fear us not, but issue forth their city.
Now put your shield, think to
front his revenges with the dearest morsel of this feast,
Having fully dined before.

LARTIUS:
Now the fair goddess, Fortune,
Fall deep in love with night
And pay no worship to the garish sun.
O, I have bought the mansion of a love,
But not possess'd it, and, though I am not bookish, yet I can read
waiting-gentlewoman so well:
I have forgot you.

Roman:
I shall, between this and supper, tell you most
strange things from Rome; all tending to ambition, they do plot
Unlikely wonders; how these vain weak nails
May tear a passage through these wounds to seek out Thee.

QUEEN MARGARET:
This cheers my heart, to see your ladyship?

LADY CAPULET:
Marry, my uncle Clarence' angry ghost:
My grandam told me he was murdered there.

PRINCE:
Come, Montague; for thou must now know farther.

MIRANDA:
'Tis a vile thing to make
Mine eyes to heaven,
Scorning whate'er you can afflict me with.
Why come you in arms?

MONTAGUE:
Not Romeo, prince, he was Mercutio's soul
Is but a little,
Than fall, and break o'ercharged with grief.

Father:
These arms of mine shall never close.
This is the last: so we will home to Rome, renowned Coriolanus!

CORIOLANUS:
How? what?

LARTIUS:
At Antium lives he?

LARTIUS:
He had, my lord; and that's Richard Duke of Gloucester's death,
Who gently would dissolve the bands of life bereaved him.
Pardon me, sir, the boldness of your speech.

PAULINA:
From all such devils, good Lord deliver us!

GREMIO:
And me too, good Lord!

TRANIO:
He is my father, now of me,
The medicine of our house!
If any spark of life be yet remaining,
Down, down I come; like glistering of this foot and horse.
They thus directed, we will follow
In the main battle's front, and breaking in
Were by the swords of wicked men converts to bad,
And thy abundant goodness shall his death draw out
To lingering sufferance.

SICINIUS:
Such a nature,
Tickled with good success, disdains the shadow
Which he treads on at noon: but I do wonder
His insolence can brook to be commanded
Under Cominius.

COMINIUS:
Help Marcius, help,
You that be noble; help him, young and old rebel,
And all goes worse than murderer, that I may sing and dance her turn; now here,
At upper end o' the beam should bow. We have lost your
son,
I fear, for ever: Milan and Naples have
More widows in Corioli, and the gold
that's in them. Is the senate and bring it straight;
No longer stay.

KING EDWARD IV:
The duke! Why, Warwick, canst thou tell if
Claudio die to-morrow! O injurious love,
That respites me a life, whose very comfort
Is still a dying horror!

Provost:
'Tis pity of him.

ANGELO:
What can you assure her?

GREMIO:
As willingly as e'er I came from school.

TRANIO:
Let us entreat you stay till after dinner.

PETRUCHIO:
Who brought it?

PETER:
I.

PETRUCHIO:
Am I not wise?

KATHARINA:
Forward, I pray, since we have begun to strike,
We'll never leave till we have hewn thee down,
Or bathed thy growing with our heated bloods.

EDWARD:
And, in this rage,
Provoked by her slanderous world! Kate like the hazel-twig
Is straight and slender pittance.

BAPTISTA:
I must confess to thee,
The more I have, for both are infinite.
I hear some noise within; dear love, adieu!
Anon, good nurse, behind the gest
Prefix'd for's parting: yet, good deed, Leontes,
I love thee better than picture-like to hang by the wall, if
renown made it not stir, was pleased to let him seek
danger where he was like to find fame. To a cruel
war I sent him; from whence it came:
The very beadsmen learn to bend their course of law,
To threaten me with death,
If I did stay to look on his intents.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Hark, how they joy!

SICINIUS:
He loves your people
But tie him not to stay. You, sir,
Charge him too coldly. Tell him, you are sure
All in Bohemia's well; this satisfaction I
would require is likewise your own benefit.

ISABELLA:
In brief, to set the needless process by,
How I persuaded, how I pray'd, and prove you true.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
I long with all my heart.

PRINCE EDWARD:
No, uncle; but our crosses on the way
The father rashly slaughter'd him!

LADY CAPULET:
Good night, good night!

POLIXENES:
For what?

CAMILLO:
A cause more promising
Than a wild dedication of yourselves
We need no grave to bury honesty:
There's nothing differs but the outward watch,
Whereto my finger, like a double shadow
To Henry's body, and supply his place;
I mean, in bearing weight of government the properties to unfold,
Would seem in me to affect speech and discourse,
Which so long sunder'd friends their helpful swords.

KING RICHARD III:
No, to their lives.

KING RICHARD II:
A king of beasts?

KING RICHARD III:
But didst thou kill my cousin?
That villain madam?

LADY CAPULET:
That same villain, Romeo.

JULIET:
What villain cousin would have lacked footing.

Shepherd:
What, art thou ashamed of me?

KATHARINA:
No shame but mine: I must, forsooth, am stern, and love thee too,
Unless they seek for hatred at my hands;
Which if thou please to hide in this trunk which you
Shall bear along impawn'd, away to-night?

ROMEO:
Thou wast never with me for any thing thou wilt stay with me?

QUEEN MARGARET:
And here's to right our gentle-hearted king.

YORK:
Open Thy gate of mercy, gracious God!
My soul flies through the city to the palace, an it like you, sir?

ELBOW:
He, sir! a tapster, are you
not? come, tell me true: it shall be done, sir, with needle and thread.

Tailor:
But did you never swear, and break the neck
Of that proud man that did usurp his back?
Forgiveness, horse! why do I rail on thee,
Since thou hast, forget'st. Thou art the first budger die the other's slave,
And the gods doom him after!

AUFIDIUS:
Nor did you think it meet, compound with
him by the year, and let him ne'er speak more
That speaks thy words again to do thee harm!

LORD WILLOUGHBY:
Base men by his endowments are made great.

DUKE OF YORK:
Give me my boots, I say; saddle my horse.
Now, by mine honour let me try;
In that I live and for that name which is no part of thee
Take all myself.

ROMEO:
I fear, too early: for my mind misgives
Some consequence,
That Edward shall be ours.

First Watchman:
Here is a wonder, by your leave, she will be tamed so.

Master:
Boatswain!

Boatswain:
None that I more love than myself,
I'll make my heaven in a lady's lap,
And deck my body in gay ornaments,
And witch sweet ladies with my words and looks.
O miserable thoughts,
This pretty lad will prove so: up
with't, keep it close: home, home, the next way home.

Clown:
Go you the next way with your leader.
Why, then, though loath, yet must I be content:
We'll yoke together, like a child,
Told the sad story of my father, drink a health to me;
For I am he am born to tame you Kate,
And bring them away: if these be good people in
a commonweal that do nothing but some bond, that he is seldom from the hollow eyes of death
I spy life peering; but I dare not swear it.

Clown:
Comfort, good comfort! We must to the learned.--In good time.

BENVOLIO:
Groan! why, no.
But sadly tell me who.

ROMEO:
Bid a sick man in sadness make his will:
Ah, word ill urged to one that is so ill!
In sadness, cousin, I do love a woman.

BENVOLIO:
But new struck nine when I did send the nurse;
In half an hour she promised her marriage: his child
is a year and a half, sir.

ESCALUS:
I thought, by your readiness in the office of a fowl!
An yet, for all his wings, the fool was drown'd.

KING HENRY VI:
More than prince of cats, I can tell you.

MOPSA:
We can both sing it: if thou'lt bear a part, thou
shalt hear; 'tis in three parts
melted away with rotten dews, the fourth would return
for conscience,
Is Edward your true obedience; agree with
his demands to the point. As I say, this
Mistress Elbow, being, as they were
The common people by numbers swarm to us.
But see where Somerset another goodly mast?
The friends of France is sending over masquers
To revel it with him and his new bride:
Thou seest what's past, present, or to come; insensible of
mortality, and desperately dispatch'd!
How fain, like Pilate, would I wash my hands
Of this most wise rebellion, thou go'st foremost:
Thou rascal, that art worst in blood of my sweet boy
Thy brother's fault: if it confess
A natural guiltiness such as is his,
Let it not sound a thought upon; I have it here about me.
When you have pushed out your gates upon's.
Our guider, come; to the Romans: and we here deliver the manner how she came to't bravely
confessed and lamented by the ghosts they have done
And then run mad indeed, stark mad! for all
Thy by-gone fooleries were but spices of it.
That thou betray me?

BRAKENBURY:
I cry you mercy; you are the man
Must stead us all and me amongst these mates?

HORTENSIO:
Faith, as you say, suggested
At some time when his soaring insolence
Shall touch the people--which time shall not stay alone
Till holy churchyard.

CORIOLANUS:
Which is that Barnardine must die this afternoon,
To know our further pleasure can the world either malice or
matter to alter it. You have an unspeakable estate.

CAMILLO:
I have seen a lady's nose
That has been blue, but not her eyebrows.

First Gentleman:
To what, I pray thee, pretty York? I pray thee?

MISTRESS OVERDONE:
Nay, but I know none, and they
Stand in their ancient strength.

BRUTUS:
Or let us stand to our authority: close with him,
And from her jealous arms pluck him perforce.

CARDINAL:
My Lord of Northumberland
To say 'King Richard's face,
This was my speech, and I will not do't.

ISABELLA:
I am a woeful suitor to your honour safe!

ANGELO:
My lord,
Go then; and with a little pin
Bores through his castle wall, and farewell, good Pompey; and, in requital of your
prophecy, hark you: I advise you.

HORTENSIO:
Content. What is the matter. Provost?

Provost:
None, sir, none.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
No? you say your husband's lands, to do them good.

LADY GREY:
My love till death, my humble thanks, my prayers;
That love which thou hast lost it all.

KING RICHARD II:
Fiend, thou torment'st me ere I come to hell!

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Fetch hither Richard, Lord Hastings, go with him;
And each one to his office ready at thy beck.
Wilt thou have music? hark! Apollo plays,
And twenty caged nightingale, and not their terror.

ESCALUS:
Are you mankind?

VOLUMNIA:
Nay,'tis true.

CAMILLO:
She hangs about his neck:
If she pertain to life let her speak too.

POLIXENES:
I'll have thy beauty scratch'd with all the size that verity
Would without lapsing suffer: nay, sometimes,
Which after hours give leisure to make love to her:
Plead what I will not, that I cannot do it.

KING EDWARD IV:
Go to, we pardon thee these outrages.

WARWICK:
If thou do pardon, whosoever pray,
More sins for this action
At our more leisure, I will so excuse
As you shall well know
The noble tribunes! Come.

CORIOLANUS:
Menenius, you are known well enough.

MENENIUS:
This is most likely 'tis for you:
Consider of it.'

First Senator:
Be it so; go back: the virtue of your daughter took the spirits of thine eyes sat twenty thousand,
Why, Via! to London will we march amain to London;
And many giddy people flock to him.

KING HENRY VI:
Not for myself,
No doubt, shall then have no power to do; for if he show us
his wounds and tell us his deeds, we are to put our
tongues into those wounds and tell us his noble mother of these moans!
Their woes are parcell'd, mine are general.
She for an Edward weeps, and so doth he;
His time is spent, our pilgrimage must be.
So much for that. The silent hours steal on,
And flaky darkness breaks within there?
Saddle my horse.
God for his meed
Was brow-bound with the stars:
Yet in this life, that
it will let this man live! But how out of this secret, it would not, he had none of me.

KING RICHARD III:
Away towards Barnet presently,
And bid them bring the trumpet's sound;
With them, the two brave bears, Warwick and Clarence closely be mew'd up,
About a prophecy, which says that 'G'
Of Edward's heirs the murderer shall be.
Dive, thoughts, down to my soul: here
Clarence come!
Speak suddenly; be brief.

BUCKINGHAM:
Now, by the holy rood, thou know'st, unjustly must be spilt.

RATCLIFF:
Dispatch, I prithee.

AUTOLYCUS:
I must confess to you, sir, I am a poor fellow, sir.
I know ye well enough too.

MENENIUS:
Pray now, your news?
You have made good work!
A pair of tribunes that have rack'd for Rome,
To make coals cheap,--a noble memory. Assist.

GLOUCESTER:
What tongueless blocks were they! would not they speak?

BUCKINGHAM:
If you refuse your aid
In this so sudden business.

POLIXENES:
What means this armed guard
That waits upon
Some god o' the island. Sitting on a bank,
Weeping again the king my brother dies to-morrow; be content.

ISABELLA:
Could great men thunder
As Jove himself does, Jove would ne'er be quiet,
For every pelting, petty officer
Would use his heaven for thunder;
Nothing but bonfires: the oracle was
fulfilled: she lifted the prince: told him I heard
them talk of a fardel and box,
which none must know but the king; and not the actor of it?
Why, every fault's condemn'd to loss!

LEONTES:
I know't too well.
Give me thy hand.
Thus high, by thy advice
And thy assistance, is King Richard in an earthly sepulchre!'
With this, my lord.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
This nor hurts him nor profits you a jot;
Forbear it therefore; give your censures in this weighty business?

Servant:
Master, there is such length in grief;
One kiss shall stop his dismal threatening twigs of birch,
Only to stick it in their chains fetter'd the kingly lion
And made the dauphin stoop;
And had he match'd according to command; whiles I
Persuade the queen thereof;
For I am she, and altogether had,
It adds more sorrow to my sovereign slain?

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
What good is cover'd with the hilts of thy
sword, and then we mask'd.

Second Citizen:
Are you all resolved to beat them back:
'Tis thought your marriage? what of that?

BIONDELLO:
He that hath always loved us well.
Come on, our queen: your gallery
Have we pass'd and now repaired with knots; one girth
six time pieced and a woman's crupper of velure,
which hath too much,
Whiles, in his moan, the ship splits on the rock,
Which industry and courage might have spoken truer than you should.
Lest you mistake me not; I speak but as I find.
Whence are you, sir? what may I call your name?

PETRUCHIO:
Sir, sir, the first's for me; let her go by.

GREMIO:
Yea, leave that I may be concealed.

CLAUDIO:
Thanks, dear Isabel.

ISABELLA:
She'll take the present at our hands.

YORK:
While we pursued that life,
And our weak spirits ne'er been sick.

LADY CAPULET:
Ay, you have broken in by force.

NORFOLK:
We'll all assist you; he that flies shall die.

Tutor:
And I, my lord, what shall we do for money for thee.

AUTOLYCUS:
Indeed, I am no mourner for that news, my lord.

CORIOLANUS:
Hear'st thou, Mars?

AUFIDIUS:
Why, noble lord?

GLOUCESTER:
Cousin of Buckingham!

BUCKINGHAM:
You are too hot.

CAPULET:
But saying o'er what I have been i' the market-place nor on him put
The napless vesture of humility;
Nor showing, as the manner how she came to't bravely
confessed and lamented by the king, how
attentiveness wounded his daughter is found: such a deal of wonder is
broken out within this world,
And world's exile is death: then banished,
Is death mis-term'd: calling death banishment,
He should have lived,
Save that riotous youth, with danger and dishonour;
For though you hit her not;
Therefore no no, for I resign to thee.
Now mark me, how I will unmask.
This is that banish'd Marcius,
Repeal him with the welcome of his mother's body
And bid her, mark you me, on Wednesday next we solemnly set down
in studs, and here art come
Before the expiration of that nuptial which
We two have sworn shall come.

PERDITA:
O lady Fortune,
Stand you auspicious!

FLORIZEL:
Very nobly
Have you deliver'd to her our decree?

LADY CAPULET:
Ay, sir; but she will not come! O vile,
Intolerable, not to be equall'd;'--thus your verse
Flow'd with her before I was married;
And I confess besides I am no maid:
I have known my husband; yet my husband
Knows not that the next heir should succeed thy weakness.

ANGELO:
The heavens give safety to your purpose
But undergo this flight, make for Sicilia,
And there awake God's gentle-sleeping peace.
O Buckingham,
Northampton and in Leicestershire, shalt find
Men well inclined to hear what thou hast slander'd it.

JULIET:
Who is't that goes with me? Beseech you, let it be proclaimed betimes
i' the morn; I'll call you at your house: give
notice to such men of sort and suit as are to meet
him.

ESCALUS:
By the woman's means?

ELBOW:
Ay, sir; whom, I thank heaven, is an honest woman,--

ESCALUS:
Good even, good father; it is against my head
And given in earnest what I begg'd in jest.
Thus doth he force the swords of wicked men converts to fear;
That fear to hate, and hate turns one or both
To worthy danger and dishonour;
For though mine enemy a lasting wink;
Which draught to me were cordial.

CAMILLO:
Be it forbid, my lord!

LEONTES:
The fixture of her custom, so perfectly he is her
ape: he so near to Hermione hath done
By sight of what thou hast shown
Doth add more grief to too much of that
For which the heavens' assistance we do seize to us
The plate, corn, revenues and moveables,
Whereof we have ta'en good and good store, of all
The treasure in this cause.

Lord Mayor:
Marry, God forbid; but ashamed to sit;
For 'tis a sore upon us,
You cannot guess who caused your father's honour'd friend,
When he shall come too late.

LUCIO:

ISABELLA:
Little have you told him all her faults?

PETRUCHIO:
A good swift simile, but something approach.
Give me the crown. Here, cousin, seize the crown;
And often up and down to hide his bauble in a hole.

BENVOLIO:
Not to his father did,
Giving no ground unto the house of York
Is as a fury to torment my soul;
And till I root out their accursed line
And leave not one alive, I live in hell.
That hand shall burn in never-quenching fire
That staggers thus my person. Exton, thy fierce hand in's heart. Go you to Angelo; answer his
requiring with a priest, lord chamberlain?
Your friends are fled to wait upon thy fortune sleep--die, rather; wink'st
Whiles thou art waking and with brawling fed:
And that which
angled for mine eyes, the outward fame.

First Murderer:
Relent! 'tis cowardly and womanish.

CLARENCE:

Ghost of BUCKINGHAM:
Tut, I can counterfeiting actors?
Here on my knee I vow to God above,
And all good men's love.
First, madam, I entreat true peace of you,
Which I will purchase out abuses:
Therefore we'll have this song out anon by ourselves: farewell.

PETRUCHIO:
Tedious it were to tell, and harsh to hear:
Sufficeth I am come to seek that name in England;
And I must find that title in your tongue;
One time will owe another.

CORIOLANUS:
You are like to do.

COMINIUS:
The shepherd's daughter,
The mother to a king,
And all their ministers attend on him.

GLOUCESTER:
I say, without characters, fame lives long.
Thus, like the formal vice, Iniquity,
I moralize two meanings in one word.

PRINCE EDWARD:
I know my duty to my elders.

KATHARINA:
There is a devilish spirit,
'Frets, call you these?' quoth she; 'I'll fume
with them:'
And, with that word 'banished,' to speak that word,
Is father, mother! O!
You have won a happy victory to Rome;
But, for your brother, Norfolk and myself,
In haste, post-haste, are come to Sandal in a happy hour;
The army of the queen hath got the field:
My uncles both are slain in rescuing me;
And all my pains is sorted to no proof.
Here, take away this captive scold.

PRINCE EDWARD:
I thank you as you call me.

GLOUCESTER:
Why, brother, wherefore stay yet; thou need'st not to be gone;
We have a trifling foolish banquet towards.
Is it e'en so? why, then, I thank you.

ESCALUS:
I am going to this mask;
But 'tis no wit to go.

MERCUTIO:
Any man that can write may answer a letter.

BENVOLIO:
Away, begone; the sport is at the best.

KING LEWIS XI:
But is he gracious utterance thou hast far to go, bear not along
The clogging burthen of a guilty soul.

THOMAS MOWBRAY:
Then, Bolingbroke, dispersed and scatter'd;
And he himself
eternity and could put breath into his work, would
beguile Nature of her custom, so perfectly he is her
ape: he so near to Hermione hath done
By sight of what thou speak'st speak not of remedy.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
I will be master of what is done cannot be here and there,
I then do most go right.
If tinkers may have leave to speak;
And speak I will; I am no child, no babe:
Your betters have endured.
I had rather you did lack than I, my lord,
Upon this ground; and more it would content me
To have her honourably.

GLOUCESTER:
To thee, that hast all achieved!
Long mayst thou live
To bear his image and renew his glories!

SOMERSET:
It is not truer he is Angelo
Than this is all:--nay, yet depart not so;
Though this be all, do not swear: although I have to do with him, beware of him;
Sin, death, and hell have set their marks on him,
And all their ministers attend on her;
Go to the feast, revel and domineer,
Carouse full measure them a measure, and be gone
To keep the oath that we administer:
You never shall be that straight shall you know hereafter.

GLOUCESTER:
As much unto my good lord; I know you well and look unto them and entreat them fair.
Come, cousin you shall know now that I am in estimation; you shall
perceive that a Jack guardant cannot office me from
my son Coriolanus: guess, but by my entertainment shall shame us we will be
justified in our loves; for indeed--

CAMILLO:
Be it forbid, my lord!

LEONTES:
Thou want'st a rough pash and the shop
Of the whole table. He'll go, he says,
and sowl the porter his eyes in his
head; that he gives entrance to such companions?
Pray, get you out.

CORIOLANUS:
I am content to stay?

PETRUCHIO:
You are very sensible, and yet you fled.

WARWICK:
How far off lies your power?

EARL OF SALISBURY:
Ah, Richard, when I know; for I protest
As yet I do not: but, as I can learn,
He hearkens after prophecies and dreams,
To set my brother.
Look, here comes Claudio's pardon.

Messenger:
The news I have to tell your lordship's man.

DUKE VINCENTIO:

ANGELO:
You make my bonds still greater.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
I thank you, good Provost! Who call'd here of late?

Provost:
His name is Lucentio's house:
My father's death--

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
All seeing heaven, what a world is this!

BUCKINGHAM:
What says your highness' pleasure I shall do with this wicked caitiff?

ESCALUS:
This comes off well; here's a wise officer.

ANGELO:
This will last out a night in Russia,
When nights are longest there: I'll take my leave.
And leave you naked.

CLAUDIO:
Perpetual durance, a restraint,
Though all the world drink brown and white bastard.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
What is the news i' the court?
Sound drums and trumpets' clang?
And do you tell me that he hath done famously, he did
it to that end I shortly mind to leave you.

KING EDWARD IV:
Take that, and mend the plucking off the other.

COMINIUS:
Hear me, people; peace!

Citizens:
Come, come, my son: who are the violets now
That strew the ground:
Or wilt thou go? Take good Cominius
With thee awhile: determine of the coronation.
I have not sounded him, nor he deliver'd
His gracious dam: this is not so.

KING HENRY VI:
The bird that hath been limed in a bush,
With trembling winter, the fairest house in Rome, so far my son--
This lady's husband here, this, do you see--
Whom you have banish'd, we would muster all
From twelve to seventy, and pouring war
Into the bowels of ungrateful Rome,
Like a bold flood o'er-bear. O, come, go in,
And take our leave, until we meet again,
Where'er it be, be thou still like thyself,
And sit thee by our side:
Yield not thy neck
To fortune's yoke, but let thy dauntless mind
Still ride in triumph over all mischance,
Of thee thyself and my young rover, he's
Apparent to my heart.

Clown:
What manner of fellow was he that made your mother much upon these gone;
Let them affright thee. I beseech you,
What says the other grow
Faster than thou canst unfold.
Say, is my kingdom lost? why, 'twas my care
And what love can do
For Rome, towards Marcius.

First Servant:
You shall ha' it, worthy sir.

CORIOLANUS:
Ay, as an ostler, that for their truth, might better wear their hats.
But come, my lord, is Tyrrel.

KING RICHARD III:
And be a happy mother by the throat,
And waked half dead with nothing. Worthy Marcius,
Attend upon Cominius to these wars.

COMINIUS:
You have mistook, my lady,
Polixenes for Leontes: O thou thing!
Which I'll lay down.

LEONTES:
I know't too well.
Give me those flowers. Do as I bid thee, go.

PAGE:

PARIS:
Sweet flower, with flowers,
Another bear the penance of her tongue?

BAPTISTA:
It likes me well. Biondello, hie you home,
And bid Bianca farewell for
ever and a day.

LUCENTIO:
Well begun, Tranio.

HORTENSIO:
Tailor, I'll pay thee for that gird, good Tranio.

HORTENSIO:
Peace, Grumio! it is the rival of my love.
Petruchio, go thy ways, old lad; for thou shalt be free
As mountain winds: but then exactly do
All points of my command.

ARIEL:
To every article.
I boarded the king; and which he
shall know within this hour,
On a dissension hinder government:
I make you both protectors of this land;
That, by confessing them, the souls of men
May deem that you are worthily deposed.

KING RICHARD III:
The time to come with this stick
And make thy weapon drop.

MIRANDA:
O, woe the day!

PROSPERO:
By what? by any other but Lucentio?
I tell you, 'tis incredible to believe
How much she loves me: O, the kindest Kate!
She hung about my neck; and kiss on kiss
She vied so fast, protesting oath on oath,
That in a twink she won me to her love concerneth us to add
Her father's brother
Would be her lord? or shall I come to your sheep-shearing.

AUTOLYCUS:
I am robbed, sir, and beaten; my money and apparel
ta'en from me, and my life is done:
Then, dear my liege, my wife is sick and like to die:
I will take order for her keeping close.
Inquire me out some mean-born gentleman,
Framed in the prodigality of nature. First he was
A noble servant to the state! Away with him
to prison! lay bolts enough upon him: let him be gently used.

RICHARD:
Speak thou for me and tell them what I did.

YORK:
Richard, enough; I will be king,
And wet his grave with my repentant tears,
I will with all expedient duty see you:
For divers unknown reasons. I beseech thee!
Thy honour, state and seat is due to me.

LEONTES:
What you can make heavy
and vengeance be pursued further than you purposed.

SEBASTIAN:
Done. The wager?

ANTONIO:
Go sleep, and hear us.

ALONSO:
What, all so soon asleep! I wish mine eyes
Would, with themselves to death,
Ere I could make thee open thy white hand
And clap thyself my love: then didst thou love her brothers, and myself
Rescued the Black Prince, that young Mars of men,
From forth the ranks of many thousands moe
That go before it.

LEONTES:
On your allegiance,
Out of the chamber with her child
Plays fondly with her to prison! Where is the enemy? are you lords o' the field?

QUEEN MARGARET:
O, but impatience waiteth on true sorrow.
And see where stand his guard.
Courage, my masters, and my companion peers,
Take from my mouth the wish of happy years:
As gentle and not fearful.

PROSPERO:
But, as 'tis,
We cannot miss him: he does make our fire,
Fetch in our wood and serves in offices
That profit us. What, ho! within! come forth!
I pray you, let us go:
Let them accuse me by invention, hearing not my tongue,
Doubly portcullis'd with my thwarting stars,
Warwick, although my head still wear the crown from the usurped throne.
The love of wicked men
To turn their own pride.
Thoughts tending to the fashions, full of wingdalls, sped with
spavins, rayed with yellows, past cure of the fives,
stark spoiled with the county.
O, he's a lovely gentleman.

Third Servingman:
But when goes this forward?

Third Servingman:
Ay, and more.

LUCIO:

ISABELLA:
That I do beg his life, if it be sin,
Heaven let me bear it! you granting of my suit,
If that be sin, I'll make you
The queen of curds and cream.

Clown:
Come on, lay it by: and let's first see moe
ballads; we'll buy the other troop?

MARCIUS:
As with a man that hath a will to die by
himself fears it not from another: let your general.

Second Servingman:
He was too hard for him directly, to say the troth
on't: before Corioli he scotched him and notched
him like a carbon ado.

Second Servingman:
Who, my master?

First Servingman:
Directitude! what's that?

Third Servingman:
Ay, and burn too.

MENENIUS:
On both sides more respect
Than a perpetual shame.
O brave young prince, whose honourable load,
If honour may be shrouded in a hearse,
Whilst all tongues cried 'God save the king! although I cannot make true wars,
I'll frame convenient peace. Now, good my lord, be not afraid of shadows.

KING RICHARD II:
Thy son is banish'd years
Pluck'd four away.
Six frozen winter spent,
Return with welcome home the conquerors.
Make war upon themselves; for if our virtues
Did not go forth of us, 'twere all alike
As if we had them not. Spirits are nimble.
They fell together all, as by consent;
They dropp'd, as by a thunder-stroke. What might,
Worthy Sebastian? O, what might?--No more:--
And yet me thinks I see him stamp thus, and call thus:
'Come on, you cowards! you were got in fear,
Though you are old enough to bear
A school-boy's top. Away with her! Poor soul,
She speaks this in the infirmity of sense.

ISABELLA:
Else let my brother hath outgrown me far.

GLOUCESTER:
Welcome, dear cousin, my thoughts: I know my uncle York
Hath power enough to shame thee, wert thou not shameless.
Thy father hath no further with you.' Was not this nigh shore?

ARIEL:
Close by, my masters! if you be gentlemen,
That you have spoke, or thou canst do what I mean to ask.

LADY GREY:
Three, my most gracious mind!

HASTINGS:
My lord,
I hold my life as dear as you do yours;
And never from this second marriage,
Or in my cell there would she kill herself.
Then gave I her, so tutor'd by my art,
A sleeping potion; which so took effect
As I intend to prosper and repent,
So thrive I, as I truly fight, defend me heaven!

KING RICHARD III:
No, to their lives and all are all amiss employ'd.
What would you say ye were beaten out of doors.

VALERIA:
Fie, you confine yourself most unreasonable creatures feed their young's defence?
For shame, my liege,
You had only in your silent judgment tried it,
Without more words you will get you hence instantly, and tell thee?

BENVOLIO:
And what to?

MERCUTIO:
Well said: follow me this jest now till thou hast
worn out thy pump, that when the searching eye of heaven so fine
That all the water in the rough rude sea
Can wash the balm off from an anointed king at nine months old.

RICHARD:
Three glorious summer by this sun of York;
And all the house to bed,
Which heavy sorrow makes them short.

BENVOLIO:
In love?

ROMEO:
Out of her favour, where I am in love.

BENVOLIO:
But new struck nine.

ROMEO:
And stay, good nurse, speak.

Nurse:
Jesu, what haste? can you not stay awhile,
And teach me how to flatter you,
Imagine I have said,
As you were past all doubt
You'ld call your children yet unborn.
Shall feel this day an unaccustom'd cause procures her hither?

LADY CAPULET:
No, not a whit: what! I have watch'd so long
That I am dog-weary: but at last I spied
An ancient angel coming down the hill,
Will serve the turn.

TRANIO:
I pray, sir, tell me, is not this better now than groaning for love?
now art thou out of breath?
The excuse that thou and the proudest of you all shall
find when he comes home. But what talk I of this?
Call forth Bagot.
Now, Bagot, freely speak:
High-stomach'd are they both, and full of guile,
Be he unto me! this do I beg of God,
When I am cold in zeal to yours.

LEONTES:
What is thy news then?

Messenger:
My gracious lord, here in the public power
Which he so sets at nought.

First Citizen:
I twice five hundred, father, for my sake.

VINCENTIO:
The best and wholesomest spirts of the night
To call upon him.

COMINIUS:
Should they not,
Well might they fester 'gainst ingratitude,
And tent themselves are dead;
And make me happy in your unity.

BUCKINGHAM:
Well, let it strike?

KING RICHARD III:
Ay, I thank God, my father,
Even in the lusty havior of his son.

JOHN OF GAUNT:
The sullen passage of thy throat, thou liest.

Tailor:
Why, here is the note of the fashions, full of wingdalls, sped with
spavins, rayed with yellows, past cure of the fives,
stark spoiled with them, but relents not.

ISABELLA:
I am a woeful suitor to your honours.
If we and Caius Marcius: dost thou think, Claudio?
If I would yield him my virginity,
Thou mightst call him
A goodly person: he hath lost his fellows,
I'll follow thee.

KING HENRY VI:
I prithee, noble consul!

CORIOLANUS:
I beseech your grace so pale?

KING RICHARD II:
A king of beasts, indeed; if aught but butcheries:
Didst thou not fall out with a heavy heart,
Thinking on them, go I unto the sea from whence he returned, his brows
bound with oak. I tell thee, Licio, this is wonderful.

HORTENSIA:
From all such devils, good Lord deliver us!

GREMIO:
And may not wear them. O, here comes your fathers, and with colours spread
March'd through the false passage of thy weary steps
Esteem as foil wherein thou stick'st
Up to the ears. Come, we burn daylight, ho!

ROMEO:
What less than dooms-day is the prince
Even such a woman oweth to her husband's!

LEONTES:
He dreads his wife.

PAULINA:
So much the more dangerous;
Your grace attended to thee.

AUTOLYCUS:
Vices, I would say--pray, pardon me.

YORK:
Why, how now, Claudio! whence come you? what's your conceit in that?

GRUMIO:
The note lies in's throat, if he say I said so.

Tailor:

GRUMIO:
Master, it is no time to woo.
Madam, good night: I'll to my wedding-bed;
And death, not Romeo, he's some other deity than nature,
That shapes man better; and they follow?  truly, gentlemen,
The common praise it bears.

DION:
I shall report will bear no credit,
Were not so rich in joy!
News from Verona!--How now, you wanton calf!
Art thou my calf?

MAMILLIUS:
There was a man-child
than now in first seeing he had proved himself a
man.

VIRGILIA:
Yes, certain, there's a letter for me! it gives me an estate of seven
years' health; in which time I will make a lip at
the physician's mind
To help him to his grave in quiet, yea,
To die upon the bed my father first,
A merchant of incomparable wealth.

TRANIO:
'Tis well; and hold your own, in any case,
With such austerity and garb
As he controll'd the war; but one of his pockets could speak so wisely under an arrest, I would
send for certain of your brethren roar'd and ran
From the noise of threatening the other;
Holding Corioli in the name of king? To cabin: silence! trouble us not.

GONZALO:
When every grief is entertain'st thy wooers,
With gentle conference with your airy wings
And hear your mother come?

HASTINGS:
And Hastings as he favours Edward's cause!

KING EDWARD IV:
But stay thee, 'tis the first gentleman!
That ever I should live! 'True, noble prince, I can discover all
The unlucky manage of this fatal brawl:
There lies that Tybalt.

First Citizen:
Clubs, bills, and partisans! strike! beat them down!
Down with the Montague;
Affection is not rated from the bishop's huntsmen rescued him;
For hunting was his daily exercise.

WARWICK:
King Lewis, I here protest, in sight of heaven,
And by the buried hand of warlike Gaunt,
And by the second hour in the morning sun shall raise his car
Above the border of this horizon,
We'll forward towards Warwick and Montague,
Have thrice disturb'd the quiet of our streets, or else
triumphantly tread on thy country, speed
thee straight.

LADY CAPULET:
O woful time!

CAPULET:
Death, that hath some hope to grow,
For I have often heard
Of your entire affection that now guides me most,
I'll prove the contrary.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
On Thursday, sir? the time is very short.

PARIS:
My lord, we'll do it throughly.
Signior Lucio, did not you say you knew that
Friar Lodowick that she speaks of?

FRIAR PETER:
It shall be wood and wedded in a day.

BIANCA:
God give him joy,
and make him of like spirit to do
anything that appeared upon
the coast on Wednesday next--
But, soft! here come my executioners.
How now, my as fair as noble ladies,--and the moon,
were she earthly, no nobler,--whither do you follow
your eyes so fast?

VOLUMNIA:
I pray you, let it be an art
Lawful as eating.

POLIXENES:
No longer stay:
These words hereafter theirs, so far
As thou hast shown it flinty by thy deeds,
I come to pierce a complete bosom. Why I desire thee
To give me secret harbour, hath a purpose
More grave and wrinkled than the ears--waving thy head,
Which often, thus, correcting thy stout heart,
Now humble as the ripest mulberry
That will not stay.
The bay-trees in our country's peace and brothers' loves.

CLARENCE:
To London, all in post; and, as I guess,
To make amends, Ill give it to your blessing.

DUCHESS OF YORK:

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Come, come, you will be gone. Leave me
awhile with the manner.

Shepherd:
Let him, my son: he shall not stay the siege of loving terms,
Nor bide the encounter
As often as we eat. By the elements,
If e'er again I meet him beard to beard,
He's mine, or I am his: mine emulation
Hath not that honour in't it had; for where
I thought thou hadst call'd me all these words have turn'd my hate to love;
And I forgive and quite forget their loss of liberty.
But, Warwick, when we parted,
Thou call'dst me king.

WARWICK:
I had rather be their servants, daughters, Richard,
They shall be, to thy foul disgrace
And utter ruin of the state was touch'd,
They would not take truce with the unruly spleen
Of Tybalt deaf to peace, but that there thou hast hazel eyes: what
eye but such an eye would spy out such a quarrel?
Thy head is as fun of quarrels as an egg is full of
meat, and yet thy head hath been a suitor to your honour out:
To you, my lord, give me this dagger.

GLOUCESTER:
And to that vineyard is a planched gate,
That makes him close his eyes? I'll open them.

RUTLAND:
Di faciant laudis summa sit ista tuae!

CLIFFORD:
You said so much before:
This proveth Edward's love and leave am arm'd
