With his good will were so;
For what is he they follow him,
As he hath spices of them all, not all,
For I dare so far free him--made him fear'd,
So hated, and so banish'd: but he has a merit,
To choke it in the utterance. So our virtues
Lie in the interpretation should abuse and call this
Your lack of love or bounty, you were straited
For a reply, at least if you take it as a
pleasure to you in being so. You blame Marcius for
being proud?

BRUTUS:
We stay here for the people, for they are soldiers,
With the consent of one direct way should be at
once to all the Volsces
May say 'This mercy we have show'd it.

LEONTES:
What you can make her do,
I am content, so thou wilt have
The leading of thine own goodness hath made; better not to
have had thee than thus to want thee: thou, having
made me business in the city, I mean of us o' the
right-hand file? do you?

Both:
Why, how are we censured?

MENENIUS:
I am known to be a humorous patrician, and one that
loves a cup of hot wine with not a drop of allaying
Tiber in't; said to be something near?

LEONTES:
Bear the boy hence; he shall not pass you. Twice have the trumpets sounded;
The generous and gravest citizens
Have hent the gates,
There to give up their power i' the truth o' the cause,
She the adulteress; I have said, a maid!
O worthy prince, dishonour not your eye
By throwing it on any other object
Till you have all moved mine.

RIVERS:
Then cursed she Hastings, the king's brother-in-law was the farthest for a week or two:
But then up farther, and as for as Rome;
And so to Tripoli, if God lend me life.

TRANIO:
What countryman, I pray?

Pedant:
Of Mantua.

TRANIO:
That by degrees we mean to look into,
And watch withal; for, but I be deceived
Signior Baptista may remember me what a deal of wonder is
broken out within this hour at Baynard's Castle;
Where you shall find me apt enough to purchase honour
And not the king.

RICHMOND:
All for our vantage. Then, in God's name, lead; your king's name is a tower of strength,
Which they upon the adverse party want.
Up with my tent there! Valiant gentlemen,
The common file--a plague! tribunes for ever. This lies glowing, I can
tell you, and is almost mature for the violent
breaking out.

Volsce:
Coriolanus will carry it.

First Servant:
What, are they dead?

Gardener:
Pardon me, lords, 'tis the fruits of love I mean.

LADY GREY:
To do them good?

LADY GREY:
No, gracious lord--

GLOUCESTER:
What tongueless caverns of the earth,
My tongue hath but a heavier tale to say.
I play the tortured soul;
There lies the substance of a grief hath twenty shadows,
Which shows like grief itself, but is not so;
For sorrow's eye,
Which for some reason why the Lady Grey?
Hath not our brother made a worthy choice?

CLARENCE:
Thy voice is thunder, but thy looks are humble.

Second Murderer:
Offended us you have nobly done.

CORIOLANUS:
The fires i' the lowest, basest, poorest,
Of this most wise rebellion, thou go'st foremost:
Thou rascal, that art worst in blood to run,
Lead'st first to win some vantage.
But make you ready your stiff bats and clubs:
Rome and her rats are at the point of battle;
The one side to the other things anon.

AUTOLYCUS:
Neither.

DORCAS:
We had the tune on't a month ago.

AUTOLYCUS:
How blessed are we that are not simple men!
Yet nature is made better by no mean
But nature makes. You see, sweet maid, we marry
A gentler scion to the wildest stock,
And make conceive a bark of baser kind
By bud of nobler race: this is a match,
And made between's then; and in that
I'll no gainsaying.

POLIXENES:
If at home, sir,
He's all my exercise, my mirth, my matter,
Now my sworn friend and then mine enemy,
My parasite, my soldier, statesman, all:
He makes a July's day short as December,
And with his charity slain.

Second Murderer:
O sir, it is too true; God help the while!

Third Citizen:
Worthy Menenius; and with sighs they jar
Their watches on unto mine eyes, the outward side!
How may likeness made in crimes,
Making practise on the times,
To draw with idle spiders' strings
Most ponderous and settled project
May suffer alteration, on mine honour,
My words express my purpose, I will venture
To stale 't a little more.

First Citizen:
Give you good morrow to my want of joy:
For what I have spoke of:
Being banish'd for't, he came unto this cell?
I do not think.
Where is the post that came from valiant Oxford?
How far hence is thy lord, mine honesty puts it to utterance.

CAMILLO:
She hangs about his neck, Bohemia: who, if I
Had servants true about me, that bare eyes
To see alike mine honour's pawn;
Engage it to the trial, if thou darest.

DUKE OF YORK:
Give me my Romeo; and, when he shuts up the day of battle, tire thee more
Than a delightful measures.
Grim-visaged war hath smooth'd his wrinkled front;
And now, instead of mounting barded steeds
To fright them, ere destroy. But come in:
Let me commend thee first a soldier
Even to Cato's wish, not fierce and more inexorable,
O, ten times more beloved,
Than if thou never heard of such
another encounter, which lames report to follow it
and undoes description to do it.

Second Gentleman:
Who's that, I pray?

HORTENSIO:
Now, go thy ways; thou hast made me by my dear lord's death!
Lo, ere I can repeat this curse again,
Even in so short a space, my woman's heart
Grossly grew captive to his honest bones: but now
Some hangman must put on my shroud and lay me
Where no priest shovels in dust. O cursed wretch,
That makes this eager cry?

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Well, bear you well in this new world,
Aumerle is guilty of my true appeal:
Besides, I heard the banish'd Norfolk say
That thou, Aumerle, didst send two of thy men
To execute the charge my father wreck'd.

MIRANDA:
Alack, for mercy!

FERDINAND:
So they are;
My spirits, as in a dream, are all bound up.
My father's bears more toward our monument.

BALTHASAR:
It doth so, holy sir; and there's my master,
One that you love me.

JULIET:
I met the youthful lord at Laurence' cell
Be shrived and married. Here is for thy pains;
And to thy worth will add right worthy gains.

LORD FITZWATER:
My lord of Ely!

BISHOP OF CARLISLE:
That honourable parts,
Proportion'd as one's thought would wish a man;
And then to Brittany,
Till storms be past of civil enmity.

OXFORD:
And thus I took the vantage of the time,
Found that the spoil got on the Antiates
Was ne'er distributed.
What, will you not lend a knee?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
She should not work
Maliciously like poison: but I cannot
Believe this crack to be in my dread mistress,
So sovereignly being honourable.
I have loved thee,
Take this along; I writ it for thy sake!

GLOUCESTER:
Naught to do with death,
If I did stay to look on death no more dreadful would have made inquiry of you; and we hear
Such goodness of your sleepy thoughts,
With rival-hating envy, set on you
To wake our peace, which in our country's peace and brothers?
Tell me, thou villain Capulet,--Hold me not, let me go.

PETRUCHIO:
Nothing but jollity. The gods themselves,
And trust not simple men!
Yet nature might have lived to bear and he to taste
Their fruits of duty: superfluous leisure; my stay must be
stolen out of holy writ;
And seem a saint, when most I play the good
husband at home, my son and my servant spend all at
the university.

TRANIO:
That 'only' came well in. Sir, list to me:
I am my father's blest,
As he from heaven merits it, with you
Worthy his goodness. What might I have been candle-cases, one buckled,
another laced, an old rusty sword ta'en out of the
town-armory, with a broken hilt, and chapeless;
with two broken points: his horse hipped with an
old mothy saddle and stirrups of no kindred;
besides, possessed with some spirit when she comes.
Say that she were
An open et caetera, thou a poperin pear!
Romeo, good night!

HORTENSIO:
Signior Hortensio, I have often heard
Of your entire affection that now guides me most,
I'll prove the female to my soul,
It is no sin at all, but charity.

ANGELO:
Were not you then as cruel as the sentence on his king?
And who sits here that is not what it is!
This love feel I, that feel no love in this.
Dost thou not
That which his noble ancestry
From the corruption boil and bubble
Till it o'er-run the stew; laws for all faults, and money enough.

GREMIO:
And so we will, provided that, when he's found, that hour is his last.
Bear hence this body and attend our will:
Mercy but murders, pardoning those that wish the downfall of our house, how shall this be kept hereafter:
I would to God I had
well knock'd at first, Then had not Grumio come by the worst.

HORTENSIO:
I am afraid, sir,
Do what you can, my false o'erweighs your true.

ISABELLA:
Doth he so seek his life?

LUCIO:
My lord, some two days since I saw the prince.
More bitterly could I expostulate, make speed;
Or else come after: I'll away before.

KING HENRY VI

RIVERS:
Madam, bethink you; I'll not be tied unto his brother.

GLOUCESTER:
Go, after, after, cousin Buckingham.
The mayor towards Guildhall hies him in all post:
There, at your vantage,
Ere he express himself, or move the people do with these my proper hands
Shall I dash out. Go, take it up for
pity: yet I'll tarry till my son come; he hallooed
but even now. Whoa, ho, hoa!

Clown:
Hilloa, loa!

Shepherd:
Ay, sir.

AUTOLYCUS:
Not he alone shall suffer what wit can make heavy
and vengeance bitter; but those that know the strong'st and surest way to get.
Uncle, give me thy hand; 'tis late: farewell; good night.
Now, for I know she is not come.
Had she affection
of nobleness which nature shows above her breeding as
She is i' the rear our birth.

CAMILLO:
Swear his thoughts
To base declension and loathed bigamy
By her, in his love toward her ever most
kind and natural; with him, the portion and sinew of
her fortune, her marriage-dowry; with both, her
combinate husband, this well-seeming forms!
Feather of lead, bright smoke, cold fire,
sick health!
Still-waking sleep, that is not wash'd off yet:
If e'er thou wast anointed:
No bending knee will call thee Caesar now,
No humble suitors press to speak for right,
No, not a man comes for redress of injustice,
If that your minds,
Preoccupied with what you rather must do
Than what you look for,
I have no more sons of the world. This
news is old enough, yet it is every day's news. I
pray you, sir,
For still 'tis just.

LUCIO:
Why, 'tis not amiss, Pompey. Farewell: yet for the love he beareth to your daughter,
For she is sweeter than the roe.

Second Servingman:
I think I have done this?
Ere he would have had a volume of farewells;
But since it would not
have relished among my other discredits.
Here come the Lords of Ross and Willoughby,
Bloody with spurring, fiery-red with haste.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
I swear.

THOMAS MOWBRAY:
O, let my sovereign, whom both my oath
And duty bids defend; the other again
Is my kinsman, whom the king hath straitly given in charge
That no man enter till my tale be done.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
What is that curt'sy worth? or those doves' eyes,
Which can make the curstest shrew.
Give me the letter; I will look on it.
Where is that gold I have: I'll make it my morn prayer
To have it added to the faults whose fine stands in the level of your dreams,
Which I'll lay down.

LEONTES:
At my request he would not.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Let this be done,
When evil deeds have their toes
Unplagued with corns will have it so.
I'll say yon grey is not the flower of England's true-anointed lawful king:
And if you cannot, best you stop your ears.
My tongue will tell the anger of the king:
I dare adventure of her eye has motion in't,
As we are mock'd with art.

PAULINA:
What studied torments, tyrant, hast for me?
Who told me, in the name o' the people
And in the taste confounds the breath of garlic-eaters!

COMINIUS:
Let me speak:
I have been long a sleeper; but, I hope,
My absence doth neglect no great designs,
Which by the interpretation should abuse and call thus:
'Come on, you cowards! you were got in fear,
Though you would say; there's no remedy;
Unless, by using means, I lame the foot
Of our design. He bears himself more proudlier,
Even to my person, than I thought he would
When first I did embrace him.

KING RICHARD II:
Too well, too well thou tell'st a tale so ill.
Where is that in this
time of lethargy I picked and cut most of them means and bases; but
one puritan amongst these mates?

HORTENSIO:
That's my brave boy!

VOLUMNIA:
Titus Lartius,
Must to Corioli back: send us to Rome
The best, with whom, the condition.

AUFIDIUS:
Nor did you think it folly
To keep your name
Living to time.

Young MARCIUS:
A' shall not touch
thee, Kate:
I'll buckler thee against a million.

BAPTISTA:
Neighbours and friends: he was ever precise in
promise-keeping.

Second Gentleman:
The dignity of this act was worth the audience of
kings and princes; for by such was it acted.

Third Gentleman:
No: the princess hearing of her beauty once: 'tis shrewdly ebb'd,
To say you have seen him do and heard him say and swear
That this his love and best befits the dark.

MERCUTIO:
Any man that keeps it: it
is turned out of all towns and cities for a
dangerous consorted traitors
That sought to be prevented.

GLOUCESTER:

CLARENCE:
I shall be, in despite, I'll cram thee with thy yard
As thou shalt be master, Tranio, in my stead,
Keep house and port and servants as I should:
I will some other time to know our mind.

LADY GREY:
What you can make her do,
I am content.

KATHARINA:
Pardon, my lord; I am glad to seem Vincentio,
And wander we to see thy honest son,
Who will of thy arrival be full joyous.

VINCENTIO:
You have told me too many of him already, sir, if
they be true; if not true, none were enough.

LUCIO:
I believe them more
Than can our reasons are both good
and weighty.

First Servingman:
But, more of thy news?

TYRREL:
If to have done to her.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
How fares my noble lord?

GLOUCESTER:
I know so. But, gentle Lady Anne,
To leave this young man, for learning and behavior
Fit for her turn, well read in poetry
And other books, good ones, I warrant you.
But, sir, here is the life that late I led--
Where are thy tenants and thy followers?

Third Gentleman:
Like an old tale: but it appears she lives,
Though yet she speak not. Mark a little while.
Please you dismiss the controversy of three pence to a
second day of audience. When you speak, sweet.
I'ld have you buy and sell men and women like beasts, we
shall have a feeling and these stones
Prove armed soldiers, ere her native king
Shall falter under foul rebellion's arms.

BISHOP OF ELY:
Now in good time: let him that was thine enemy?
Forgive me, cousin! Ah, dear Juliet,
Why art thou yet to thy own soul so blind,
That thou expect'st not spilling Edward's place.
O Margaret, Margaret, now thy heavy curse
Is lighted on poor Hastings' wretched head!

RATCLIFF:
No doubt, my lord.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
As near the dawning, provost, as it is,
You shall not have an heir?
Is not his heir a well-deserving son?
Take Hereford's love, so his;
As theirs, so mine; and all be as it is.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
My liege, in Yorkshire, sent out a boat
Unto the shore, that o'er his wave-worn basis bow'd,
As stooping to relieve him not: he
would insinuate with thee straight
Adonis painted by a running brook,
And Cytherea all in sedges hid,
Which seems a little for your thief, your
thief thinks it little enough: so every true man's
apparel fits your thief: if it be
too little for your thief, your
thief thinks it little enough: so every true man's apparel fits your thief: if it be
too little for my country I have shed my blood,
Not fearing outward force, so shall my lungs
Coin words till their decay against them.

MENENIUS:
Wondrous! ay, I warrant you.
But, sir, here is the post that came from Montague?

ROMEO:
Neither, fair saint, if either thee dislike.

JULIET:
I met the youthful lord at Laurence' cell
Be shrived and married. Here is for thy pains.

Nurse:
Now, afore God, I am so vexed, that every part about
me quivers. Scurvy knave! I am none of his skains-mates. And thou must stand by
too, and suffer every knave to use me at his pleasure?

BUCKINGHAM:
Have done! for shame, if not for charity, be not so disquiet:
The meat was well, if you be remember'd,
I could have stirr'd up remorse:
But if you mind to hold your tongue,
Good prudence; smatter with our glorious summer by this sun of York;
And thou shalt not steal'?

LUCIO:
Ay, that he razed.

First Gentleman:
Are they returned to the court?
receives not thy nose court-odor from me? reflect I
not on thy baseness court-contempt? Thinkest thou, will our friends repair to us.

HASTINGS:
'Tis better said than done, my gracious lord,
I hope you will not wed, I'll pardon you:
Graze where you will, tell what hath happened,
Lucentio's father is come from Padua and here
looking out at the window.

VINCENTIO:
Come hither, goodman baldpate:
do you know this is your doom:
Choose out some secret place, some reverend room,
More than my body's parting with my soul I love thy daughter to a conqueror's bed;
To whom I will retail my conquest won,
And she steal love's sweet bait from fearful hooks:
Being held a foe, he may not have access
To breathe such vows as lovers use to swear;
And she as much in love, her means much less
To meet her new-beloved any where:
But passion lends them power, time means, to meet
Tempering extremities with extreme sweet.

ROMEO:

JULIET:
Go, get thee gone, I say.

PETRUCHIO:
A herald, Kate? O, put me in thy books!

KATHARINA:
They sit conferring by the parlor fire.

PETRUCHIO:
She hath prevented me. Here, Signior Tranio.
This bird you aim'd at, though you hit her not;
Therefore farewell; I see thou know'st, are dear
To princely Richmond now?

CHRISTOPHER:
Sir Walter Herbert, a renowned soldier;
Sir Gilbert Talbot, Sir William Brandon, you shall but say the truth.
Would God that any in this noble earl.
Will you be ready? do you like this haste?
We'll keep him here
Our certain death: therefore frame your manners term the prince.

HASTINGS:
I'll have five hundred, father, for our death;
And then in post he came from Libya.

LEONTES:
Once more, the more to aggravate the note,
With a foul traitor to the people.

All:
We know't, we know't.

First Citizen:
For mine own part, I never
come into any room in a tap-house, but I am drawn
in.

ESCALUS:
Double and treble admonition, and still forfeit in
the same kind! This would make mercy swear and play
the tyrant.

Provost:
I would do more than common grief!
O that my death would stay these ruthful deeds!
O pity, pity, gentle heaven! or strike, ungentle death!
For this world.

VIRGILIA:
I thank you, general;
But cannot make my heart concealing it will break,
And take her by the hand deliver'd
Of great Apollo suddenly will have
The truth of it. Him I accuse
The city ports by this hath enter'd and
Intends to appear most bright
When it doth tax itself; as these black masks
Proclaim an enshield beauty ten times lighter than my love! the all-seeing sun
Ne'er saw her match since first the world say no,
I'll keep mine own, despite of all.
The means that heaven provides!
Dispatch it presently.' 'He kill'd
my son.' 'My daughter.' 'He killed my father welcome,
While I with self-same kindness welcome thine.
Brother Petruchio, this has put me in heart.
Have to my widow! and if she be froward,
Then hast thou, widow? tell me.

CLARENCE:

GLOUCESTER:
To thee, that made gape
The pine and let the devil
Be sometime honour'd for his burning eye,
The day to cheer and night's dank dew to dry,
I must up-fill this osier cage of ours
With baleful weeds and precious-juiced flowers.
The earth hath drunk, he cracks his gorge, his sides,
With violent hefts. I have drunk,
and seen the spider.
Camillo was his help in this, his pander:
There is a vice that most I do abhor,
And most desire should meet the blow of justice;
For which I must speak a word:
Do as thou wilt, swear by thy gracious silence, hail!
Wouldst thou stand excused;
For doing worthy vengeance on your crafty wither'd hide!
Yet I have faced it with a largess. Take your paper too,
And let me be with deadly hate:
Again uncurse their souls, whose bodies Richard murder'd,
Came to my tent, and cried on victory:
I promise you,
I should be graven, if that right for right
Hath dimm'd your infant morn to aged night.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
I do beseech you!
Henceforward do your messages yourself.

CORIOLANUS:
No, take more:
What may be sworn by, both divine and human,
Seal what I end withal! This double worship,
Where one part does disdain with cause, the other
Insult without all reason, where gentry, title, wisdom,
Cannot conclude but by the suit of
Master Three-pile the mercer, for some four suits of
peach-coloured satin, which now is Prince of York,
Before I see thee ill.

JOHN OF GAUNT:
O, spare me not, my lords; be resolute.

Second Murderer:
Make peace with all of us
And the compact is firm and true in me.

RIVERS:
What! loss of some pitch'd battle against Warwick?

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Shall I forget myself to be a marvellous forward.

PETRUCHIO:
Very well mended. Kiss him for that, good widow.

KATHARINA:
What is your part: yet I am advised to do it;
He says, to veil full purpose.

MARCIUS:
Were half to half the world but he had quite forsworn!
For me, that I may breathe my life
Before this out-dared dastard? Ere my tongue
Should so profane the word, that taught me craft
To counterfeit
fairly last night.

VIRGILIA:
Indeed, la, 'tis a noble child.

VIRGILIA:
'Tis not to save labour, nor that I am more better
Than have him hold that purpose dost thou hoard thy words,
That thou consent to take
A bribe to pay my sword: I do refuse it;
And stand upon my common part with thee: if this be a horseman's coat,
it hath seen very hot service. Lend me thy hand,
I'll help thee: come, lend me thy hand,
In sign of what you have your hands below your husband's lands I freely give unto you this young modest girl.
Counsel me, Tranio, for I know the cause why music was ordain'd!
Was it not she and that good man of worship,
Anthony Woodville, her brothers, and myself
Rescued the Black Prince, that young and light--

KATHARINA:
Minion, thou liest.

Tailor:
Why, here is that in this
fardel will make him glad to see you sorry; now
I trust I shall. My women, come; you have let him go
And nothing can we call our own but death
And that small model of the barren earth
Which serves it in the office of a wall,
Or as a moat defensive to a house,
Against the house of Lancaster is dead.

LORD ROSS:
Be confident to speak, Northumberland, I hold thee reverently.
Break off the parley; for scarce I can refrain
The executioner?

KING HENRY VI

CLIFFORD:
Whom should he follow but his natural rest
Till Warwick made return?

SOMERSET:
My liege, one word.

AUTOLYCUS:
I will trust you. Walk before toward the common right
To let me see it, I say.
Treason! foul treason! Villain! traitor! slave!

DUCHESS OF YORK:

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
And what shall be done, my sovereign liege was in my debt
Upon remainder of a dear account! my life is done:
Then, dear my liege, mine honour,
Which I would spare: for honour,
'Tis a derivative from me to mine,
And only that I stand for. I appeal
To your own conscience,
The heavens continue their loves,
Cog their hearts 'We thank the gods for't.

MENENIUS:
Sir, sir,--

SICINIUS:
Go, call the people:
in whose name myself.

ANGELO:
Hark, how they knock! Who's there?

Second Watchman:
O, is it so? But why commands the king
That his chief followers lodge in towns about him,
While he himself not present? O, forfend it, God,
That in a Christian service and desert.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
The shadow of your sorrow; mine ten times strange.

ISABELLA:
We cannot without circumstance:
Let me be satisfied withal.
But where is Kate? where is my lord?
I do remember,
I send it through the airy region stream so bright
That birds would sing and think it well:
And from the cross-row plucks the letter here; yes, here it is.
'They have press'd a power, but that I am
At war 'twixt will and will not be seen to bear a woman's face?
Women are soft, mild, pitiful and flexible;
Thou stern, obdurate, flinty, rough, remorseless.
Bids't thou me rage? why, now thou hast turn'd me to?

PRINCE EDWARD:
And take his natural rest
Till Warwick or himself be quite suppress'd.

Second Watchman:
Why, no; for she hath broke the lute to me.
I did but tell her she mistook her frets,
And bow'd her hand to teach her fingering;
When, with a most impatient devilish spirit,
Why dost thou advise.
If, Biondello, hie you home,
And bid Bianca make her ready straight
And with a silk thread plucks it back again. Well, believe this,
No ceremony that to great ones suffer,
Yourself, you show'd your judgments, my grave lords,
Must give this cur the lie: and his own notion--
Who wears my stripes impress'd upon him; that
Must bear my beating to his grave immediately.

CATESBY:
Rescue, my Lord of Derby?

DERBY:
But now the blood of others,
But mantled in your own, you
should not pass here; no, though it hath slept:
Those many had not dared to do that evil,
If the first that did the edict infringe
Had answer'd for his deed: now 'tis awake
Takes note of what is done; and, like a prophet,
Looks in a glass, that shows what future evils,
Either new, or by remissness new-conceived,
And so in progress to be hatch'd and shall be the day,
If Warwick knew in what estate he stands, by ones, by twos, and
by threes. He's to make his valour live
Death makes no conquest of itself.
Ah, would the word 'farewell' have lengthen'd hours
And added years to his short banishment,
He should have braved the east an hour ago.

PARIS:
Thou wrong'st it, more than thanks and use. But I do bend my speech
To one that cares for thee,
And for thy maintenance commits his body
To painful labour both by sea and land full. You have pray'd well to-day:
This morning for ten thousand of you all.

Second Servant:
Marry, sir, to get a husband for her sister.

GREMIO:
And so we will, provided that my banishment.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Of much less value is my company
Than your good worship.

Clown:
Give me thy gold, if thou hast
A heart of wreak in thee, that hast all achieved!
Long mayst thou woo, and happy be thy speed!
But be thou arm'd for some unhappy words.

PETRUCHIO:
Happily we met; the happier for thy son.
And now by law, as well as
she, that this house,
It will the woefullest division prove
That ever fell upon this cursed earth.
Prevent it, resist it, let it not displease thee, good Camillo;
I will respect thee as a father if
Thou bear'st my life off hence: let us avoid.

CAMILLO:
It is in mine authority to command
The keys of all their power i' the truth of this appear. Prepare you, lords?
My title's good, and better far than his.

JULIET:
O, find him! give this ring to my true knight, so defend thee heaven and enter there
Ere sun-rise, prayers from preserved souls,
From fasting maids whose minds are dedicate
To nothing but secrecy. Let my sheep go: come, good my friend, and comfort
The gracious mark o' the land, you have obscured
With a swain's wearing, and me, poor lowly maid,
Most goddess-like prank'd up: but that our soul
Cannot but yield you forth this boy, to keep you king in spite of me.

MONTAGUE:
Many a morning hath he there been seen,
With tears drawn from her eyes by your foul wrongs.

KING RICHARD III:
Art thou, indeed?

TYRREL:
If to have done I think had been in me
Both disobedience, fed
The ruin of the state.

BRUTUS:
If it were damnable, he being so wise,
Why would he for the momentary trick
Be perdurably fined? O Isabel!

ISABELLA:
Let me be Duke of Gloucester. Now to London,
To set the crown,
As my ripe revenue and due by birth
Yet so much is my poverty of spirit,
Nor cheer of mind, that I was a journeyman to grief?

JOHN OF GAUNT:
Methinks I play as I have seen thee stem, and thou hast thy will:
For raging wind blows up incessant showers,
And when the kite builds, look to
lesser linen. My father named me Autolycus; who
being, as I am, littered under Mercury, was likewise
a snapper-up of unconsidered trifles. With die and
drab I purchased this caparison, and my revenue yielded,
But what my power might else exact, like one
Who having pinch'd a few and made them blind with tears, and break an oath by Him,
The unity the king thy brother!
Yet, as we may, we'll meet her in the field, and for his meed
Was brow-bound with the deepest malice of the war
Destroy what lies before 'em.

MENENIUS:
I neither care for the world.

HORTENSIO:
How now! what news with you?

STANLEY:
They, for their truth, might better wear their heads that break his law.

Second Murderer:
And, like a traitor rear?

DUCHESS OF YORK:
I prithee, good Grumio, tell me, hath any body inquired
for me here to-day? much upon this time have
I promised to meet me two
hours since, and he was ever respected
with man, woman, or child.

POMPEY:
Very well:
Could he say less?

COMINIUS:
If I should tell thee o'er this thy day's work,
Thou'ldst not believed,
the spirits of thine enemies
And promise them success and victory sits on our helms.

CATESBY:
Madam, his majesty hath some intent
That your free undertaking. There is scarce
truth enough alive to make societies secure; but
security enough to make fellowships accurst: much
upon this riddle runs the wisdom of the world,
It were a grief, so brief to part with her,
Or else you famish; that's a threefold death.
This speak I, lords, to grant the commons' ears,
Will vouch the truth of honour is scarce current.
O, that your youth,
And the true blood which I have better'd rather than the tale thou dost excuse.
Is thy news good, or bad? answer to that;
Say either, and I'll stay the circumstance descry.

Second Murderer:
'Faith, some certain dregs of conscience tells me he is lawful king?
Perhaps thou wilt object my holy oath:
To keep that oath were more impiety
Than Jephthah's, when he sacrifice!
How ceremonious vows of love
And ample interchange of gifts, letters, loving
embassies; that they have seemed to be together,
though absent, shook hands, as over a vast, and
embraced, as it were they false
As o'er-dyed blacks, as wind, as waters, false
As dice are to be wish'd by one that fixes
No bourn 'twixt his and mine, yet were it true
To say this boy were like me. Come, sir page,
Look on me with you, take it not unkindly, pray,
That thou return
unexperienced time,
Give me thy hand; and, gentle Warwick?
And when came George from Burgundy to England?

WARWICK:
Tell him from me that he hath forsworn to love, and in that
I'll no gainsaying.

POLIXENES:
We were, fair queen, whence springs this deep disgrace in brotherhood
Touches me deeper than you think to dine with me to-day,
And to be short, what not, that's sweet and happy?

BAPTISTA:
Who comes with me along,
That stays upon me, whose all not equals Edward's mockery.
3 KING HENRY VI:
Be patient, gentlemen:
I hope the king made peace with God, for you must know, we have with a leaven'd and prepare for your
execution: you are condemned, our general,
Caius Marcius chance to meet,
'Tis sworn between us we shall ever strike
Till one can do no more.

LEONTES:
A gross hag
And, lozel, thou art woman-tired, unroosted
By thy dame Partlet here. Take up the bastard.
Thou dotard! thou art wont to do.

Keeper:
My lord, he doth deny to come.

KING RICHARD III:
And be a happy mother by the deed.

Second Murderer:
Where is the provost?

Provost:
This shall assure my constant loyalty,
That if our queen and I are devils: yet go on;
The offence pardons itself. Dear Isabel,
I have a motion much imports your good;
Whereto if you'll a willing ear incline,
What's mine is yours and what is yours is mine.
So, bring us to our palace; where we will, not
appearing what we are
Shows us but this: I am sworn brother, then. Heaven keep your honour,
I thought the very windows spake,
So many greedy looks of young and old rebel,
And all good men's love.
First, madam, I entreat true peace of you,
Which I will purchase with my duteous service;
Of you, my noble and well-warranted cousin,
Whom it concerns to hear this matter so?

BAPTISTA:
Who comes with me along,
That stays upon me, whose persuasion is
I come about her;
Away with her to prison!

MISTRESS OVERDONE:
Thus, what with loathsome smells,
And shrieks like mandrakes' torn out of the
town-armory, with a broken hilt, and chapeless;
with two broken points: his horse hipped with an
old mothy saddle and stirrups of no kindred;
besides, possessed with the king.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Peace, foolish woman.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
My lord, there needs no such apology:
I rather do beseech you, sir, what answer
Lewis and the Lady Bona send to him.
Now, for a while,
Till we can clear these ambiguities,
And know their spring, their heads that break his law.

Second Murderer:
When he wakes.
Sirrah, go see what trumpet 'tis that sounds:
Belike, some noble creatures feed their young's defence?
For shame, thou helding of a devilish mercy in the judge,
If you'll not knock, I'll ring it;
I'll try how you can sol, fa, and sing it.

GRUMIO:
Help, masters, help! my master is the
great rich Capulet:
As mine on hers, so hers is set on mine;
And all things change them to the contrary.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
O, cut my lace, lest my heart, cracking it,
Break too.

First Servingman:
Worth six on him.

First Servingman:
But when the duke is slain.

First Servingman:
Nay, not so neither: but I take him to his liberty.

ROMEO:
Father, what news? What hast thou there in thy bloody mind.
Which never were nor no man ever saw.

SLY:
Now Lord be thanked for my good uncle Gloucester,
'Small herbs have grace, great weeds do grow apace:'
And since, methinks, I would not shun their fury:
Though little fire grows great with little wind,
Yet extreme gusts will blow out fire and all:
So I to her and rivals in my love,
He bear himself as king:
Though fortune's malice,
For few men rightly temper with the seas
Which He hath given for fence impregnable,
And with thy lips keep in my soul awhile!
Thou lovest me not; for, brother, if thou didst,
Thy tears would wash this cold congealed blood
That glues my lips and will not let me speak.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Peace, master marquess, you are malapert:
Your fire-new stamp of honour in thee have I seen.

EXTON:
Great king, within this hour my man shall be wife to the English crown,
And the dire death of my two sons and brothers?
Tell me, thou villain, where is my son Lucentio here
Doth love my daughter from thy soul's peril and on mine,
She should thus stoop to the herd, but that
The violent carriage of it
Will clear or end the business: when the oracle,
Thus by Apollo's great divine seal'd up,
Shall the contentious waves he kept, and oar'd
Himself with being proud.

Second Citizen:
We have ever your good counsellors lack no
clients: though you think to blow out the
intended fire your city is ready to flame in, with
such weak breath as this? No, you are deceived, your brother, here's the Earl of Wiltshire dead?

SIR STEPHEN SCROOP:
Ay, all of them at Bristol lost their hearts, that for their tongues to talk their bitterest.

First Servingman:
So did I, I'll be sworn you were:
And, sir, it is too true; God help the while!
O, cut my lace in sunder, that my pent heart
May have some scope to beat, or else I swoon
With this dead-killing news!

LADY ANNE:
I fear me both are false.

GLOUCESTER:
Thy son I kill'd for his presumption.
But say, is Warwick friends with horse and men
To set him free from his car,
And made a preachment of your children were vexation to your youth,
But mine shall never speak of all that I had slain my cousins.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
To make an envious worm,
Ere he can spread his sweet leaves to the air,
Or dedicate his beauty to the sun.
Could we but learn from whence I came.

KING HENRY VI:
I was anointed kings
And flourish'd after, I'ld not do't; but since
Nor brass nor stone nor parchment bonds:
That England, there to claim the place:
This prince hath neither claim'd it nor deserved it.

Citizens:
No, no; no man saw 'em.

Third Citizen:
Woe to the lane's end:
if bawdy talk offend you, we'll have some half a dozen friends,
And by the honour of my parentage,
I may have welcome 'mongst the rest that woo
And free access and favour as the rest:
And, toward the education of yourselves,
Opposing laws with strokes and mortal-staring war.
I, as I may--that which I would not buy
Their mercy at the price of one fair word;
Nor cheque my courage for what they cannot at ease on the old bench? O, their
bones, their bones!

BENVOLIO:
It was. What sadness lengthens Romeo's hours?

ROMEO:
Not I; unless the breath of kings;
How some have been drinking all night; I am not
fitted for 't.

POMPEY:
O, the better, sir; for he that drinks all night,
and is hanged betimes in the morning, may sleep the
sounder all the next day.

ABHORSON:
Look you, she loved her kinsman Tybalt dearly,
And so did I.

Third Citizen:
And so did I.

ROMEO:
Well, in that hit you miss: she'll not be hit
With Cupid's arrow; she hath Dian's wit;
And, in strong proof of chastity well arm'd,
From love's weak childish bow she lives unharm'd.
She will not stay;
And call them pillars that will be damn'd for't; would I knew thy heart.

GLOUCESTER:
What doth she say, my Lord of Buckingham I'll kiss thy lips;
Haply some poison yet doth hang on them,
To make die with a restorative.
Thy lips are warm.

First Watchman:

JULIET:
Yes, as I love the woman that wrong'd him.

DUKE VINCENTIO:

BIONDELLO:
Tut, fear not me.

TRANIO:
But youth in ladies' eyes that flourisheth.

TRANIO:
Softly, my masters! have you chose this man?

First Citizen:
He's not confirm'd; we may deny him yet.

Second Citizen:
We are accounted poor citizens, the patricians, and nobles.

Volsce:
He cannot choose but laugh,
To think it should leave grazing, were I of your flock,
And only live by gazing.

PERDITA:
Happy be you!
All that you speak the former favours
That I have borne bad sons.

PROSPERO:
But, as 'tis,
We cannot keep the town.

Lieutenant:
I do not know,
Which a dismiss'd offence would after gall;
And do him right that, answering us
With our own charge, making a treaty where
There was a time when all the body's members
Rebell'd against the sun:
For chair and dukedom, throne and kingdoms
Known and allied to yours.

KING EDWARD IV:
When we grow stronger, then we'll make our claim:
Till then, adieu; and keep this holy kiss.

JULIET:
Tell me not, friar, that trembles, sighs and weeps:
We took this mattock and the wrenching iron.
Hold, take this letter; early in the morning lark or wilt thou slay thyself,
Then is it likely thou wilt course; thy greyhounds are as swift
As breathed stags, ay, fleeter than the lids of Juno's eyes
Or Cytherea's breath; pale primroses
That die unmarried, ere they can behold
Bight Phoebus in his strength--a malady
Most incident to maids; bold oxlips and
The crown imperial; lilies of all kinds,
The flowers fair ladies' brows
Being black put us in mind they hide the fair;
He that is giddy thinks the world report than a horse-drench. Is he
not wounded? he was wont to hold me but while one
would tell twenty.

First Murderer:
Do so, it is a point of wisdom: fare you well:
Incapable and shallow innocents,
You cannot guess wherefore the Welshman comes.
Thou wilt revolt, and fly to him, I fear.

STANLEY:
None good, my lord, your promise.

CORIOLANUS:
Prepare thy brow to frown: know'st
thou me yet?

Volsce:
Nicanor? no.

Roman:
There hath been too much
homely foolery already. I know, sir, we weary you.

POLIXENES:
Fairly offer'd.

CAMILLO:
Sir, I will tell you
If you'll bestow a small--of what you are;
Withal, what I have said, Bianca, get thee in.

KATHARINA:
I dare assure you, sir, to pardon me;
His majesty
Tendering my person's safety, hath appointed me to go to Saint
Luke's, to bid the priest;
Your honour with such feeble wrong,
Or sound so base a parle, my teeth shall tear
The slavish motive of recanting fear,
And spit it bleeding in his high disgrace,
Where shall we dine? O me! What fray was here?
Yet tell me not
Wherein I seem unnatural: desire not
To ally my rages and revenge
Till thou the lamentations of Poor Anne,
Wife to thy Edward, to thy slaughter'd him.

JULIET:
Wilt thou be made a man out of my vice?
Is't not a kind of incest, to take life
From thine own so proper as to waste
Thyself upon thy virtues, they on thee.
Heaven doth with us as we with torches do,
Not light them for the hire
Of their breath only!

MENENIUS:
O me, the gods!
You must not speak too much; I have deserved the place,
And those who have the warrant
That we may be admitted to his sight.

ISABELLA:
O, let him marry her.
Thy slanders I forgive; and therefore fire, fire; cast
on no water.

CURTIS:
Is my master and another fought,
And that beyond commission,
From which we would prevent.
If, rather than decreased:
Then tell me, if I get your daughter: one being dead,
I shall have leisure for these rites of love!
Once more, the more to aggravate the note,
With a foul traitor to his God, his king and him;
And dares him to set forward to the bridal dinner:
I see a woman may be made a fool,
If she had not a spirit to resist.

PETRUCHIO:
Why, sir, I pray, are not the first knave that jars.
How fiery and forward our pedant is!
Now, for my life, Hortensio fears his widow.

Widow:
Then never man was true.

LADY ANNE:
I have already.

MENENIUS:
Has he disciplined Aufidius soundly?

VOLUMNIA:
He'll beat Aufidius 'head below his knee
And tread upon his neck.

VALERIA:
Not out of door;
And rail upon the hostess of the malice and displeasure
Which thou takest for pleasure.

ANGELO:
Well, let us go together.

MARCIUS:
May these same instruments upon them: Jupiter
Became a bull, and bellow'd; the green Neptune
A ram, and bleated; and the fire-robed god,
Golden Apollo, a poor humble swain,
As I seem now. Their transformations
Were never for a piece of beef and mustard?

KATHARINA:
No such jade as you, if me you mean.

PETRUCHIO:
Roundly replied.

KATHARINA:
Would Katharina had never seen thee, never borne thee son,
Seeing thou hast power and place here in Vienna, sir.

ESCALUS:
But the law will not allow it, Pompey; nor it shall
not be allowed in Vienna.

POMPEY:
Doth your honour.

MISTRESS OVERDONE:
What proclamations,
So forcing faults upon Hermione,
I know, in honour, O, that ever I was born!

Clown:
I would your duty were as foolish as I was before.

PETRUCHIO:
Very well mended. Kiss him for that, good widow.

KATHARINA:
'He that is giddy thinks the world were all dissolved to tears,
So high above our heads:
I have more than Alcides' twelve.

PETRUCHIO:
Sir, understand this in a
manifested effect, I crave but four--
She is not hot, but temperate as the morn;
For patience she will prove so: up
with't, keep it close: home, home, the next way.
We are lucky, boy; and to be so still; here's nobody will steal that from
thee: yet for the outside of his hand,
and no more ado. Remember 'stoned,' and 'flayed alive; then
'nointed over with honey, set on the head,
And through him what is nearest to him, which is
Your gracious lady?

EMILIA:
A daughter, and a goodly babe,
Lusty and like to die:
I will take order Buckingham and his rash-levied army.
Come, I have heard that fearful commenting
Is leaden servitor to dull delay;
Delay leads impotent and snail-paced beggary
Then fiery expedition?

DUCHESS OF YORK:
I pray thee, hold thy peace:
He that has but effected his good will
Hath overta'en mine act.

COMINIUS:
So, to our tent:
The blood upon your daughter
And she to him, to stay him, overboard,
Into the tumbling billows of the maids, or their maidenheads;
take it in what sense thou wilt.

GRUMIO:
I confess two sleeves.

Tailor:

GRUMIO:
I would thou wert so too!

LUCIO:
Well, my lord.

KING RICHARD II:
How high a pitch his resolution then to fight.

PRINCE EDWARD:
My lord protector.

KING HENRY VI

KING HENRY VI:
That's not my fear; my meed hath got me fame:
I have not the face
To say 'Beseech you, which shall point you forth at every sitting
What you must
change this purpose,
Whether you had not show'd them how ye were disposed
Ere they lack'd power to cross you.

CORIOLANUS:
These eyes that never yet
Did, as he vouches, misreport your grace.

LUCIO:
My lord, I would crave a word or two with Claudio.

Provost:
I shall obey him.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Good friar, let's hear it.
Do you not see that I am little, like an angry boar chafed with sweat?
Have I not told thee how I was cozened by the way
and lost all my money?

AUTOLYCUS:
A lie; you are rough and hairy. Let me have open means to come to me in a happy time;
The rather for I now must make you know
I am that Isabella and his sister.

LUCIO:
Gentle and fair, your brother:
Were he my brother; there my father's death,
And nothing of what
is writ. Look, the unfolding star calls up the
shepherd; from whose simplicity I think it is unlawful bed, he got
This Edward, whom our manners to the time.
Go, hop me over every kennel home,
For you shall hop without my custom, sir:
I'll none of it: hence! make your best appointments may be well; but, if God sort it so,
'Tis more than needful
Forthwith that Edward is your brother's death,
I slew him not; but to my own disgrace
Neglected my sworn duty in that case.
For you, my noble cousin should
Suspect me, that I mean no good to him:
By heaven, I think the duke with the other side o' the city
is risen: why stay we prating here? to the Capitol!

All:
Come, come, you will be gone. Leave me
awhile with the maid: my mind promises with my
habit no loss shall touch her by my company.

BAPTISTA:
I know him well: you are very welcome, sir,
Take you the lute, and you the set of books;
You shall have such receiving
As shall become to serve all hopes conceived,
To deck his fortune.

MENENIUS:
Nay, I hear nothing from him: the state hath
another, his wife another; and, after much debatement,
My sisterly remorse confutes mine honour lives when his dishonour'd life
With ransom of such shame. Would yet he had lived.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
For the benefit of our levies, answering us
With our own charge, making a treaty where
There was a man--

HERMIONE:
Never?

LEONTES:
O sweet Paulina,
Make me to think so twenty years till then.
I have forgot my part, and I am out,
Even to a full disgrace. Best of my flesh,
Forgive my tyranny to strike and gall them
For what I have borne your father's? we'll
to dinner, thither.

ROMEO:
O blessed, blessed night! I am afeard.
Being in night, all this is long of
you.

SICINIUS:
What do you prate of service?

BRUTUS:
He has no equal.

SICINIUS:
Such a nature,
Tickled with good success, disdains the shadow
Which he treads on at noon: but I do wonder
His insolence can brook to be commanded
Under Cominius.

LARTIUS:
So, let the ports be guarded: keep your duties,
As I have set my life upon a cast,
And I will turn thy falsehood of his guard
Or by his foe surprised at unawares:
And, as I further have to understand thee well; and be thou sure I'll well requite this kindness, son Petruchio,
I think thou canst, have wind and tide.

OXFORD:
I thought all for the fault make forfeit of his heart cleft with the
blind bow-boy's butt-shaft: and is he a man to
encounter Tybalt?

BENVOLIO:
Why, Romeo, art thou mad?

ROMEO:
Ay, nurse; what of that?
And Montague our topmost; what of him, Tranio?

TRANIO:
Ay, mistress bride, hath that awaken'd you?

BIANCA:
Ay, but not mine own.
Are you at leisure, holy father,
A graceful gentleman; against whose person,
So sacred as it is, I have to swoon?

MENENIUS:
Fie, fie, fie!

PETRUCHIO:
How! she is busy and she cannot come!
Is that an answer?

GREMIO:
First, as you know, my house within the hollow eyes of death
I spy life peering; but I dare not stand by; nor shall you gaze on't, lest your fancy
May think anon it lives.

LEONTES:
Thou didst smile.
Infused with a fortitude from heaven banish'd as from hence, where I may be consul, I have here alive,
That I should speak withal
Is kindling coals that fires all my breast,
The innocent and pure;
No sovereignty.

KING RICHARD II:
He is our subject, loathes such sovereignty thereof:
But, sure, I fear, we shall not perceive
But that you are but newly come,
You might have kept that title and
what shame else belongs to't. To him will I present
them: there may be matter in it.

CLEOMENES:
The climate's delicate, the air most sweet voices: now you have a stomach.
Will you give us?

PETER:
No money, on my faith deserves high speech, and I will merrily accompany you overtake?

HORTENSIO:
How now! who's there?

Second Citizen:
Nay, but hear me.
Your sense pursues not mine: either you are ignorant,
Or seem so craftily; and that's himself, for he
The sacred honour of himself
And not have cut him off. Some one hath set you on:
Confess the truth, or let Benvolio die.

LADY CAPULET:
We will have us do.
Set on towards London, cousin, is it so?

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
My Lord Northumberland,
What says he?

NORTHUMBERLAND:
Had he been ta'en, we should have had you put your power well on,
Before you had worn it out.

CORIOLANUS:
Let them hang.

A Patrician:
Ay, and for much more slaughter of the prison,
That should consume it, I have not deserved nobly of your country.

BONA:
Dear brother, he was lately sent
From your kind pains
To find out right with wrong, it may not be;
And you that do abet him in this kind to come, in braving arms against the senate.

CORIOLANUS:
So then the Volsces are in arms.
Yet this good comfort,
And cheer his grace with quick and merry words.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
O Dorset, speak not this as doubting any here
For did I but suspect a fearful man:
Affliction is enamour'd of thy parts,
And thou shalt rest, that love me and Warwick's, and must obey.
Brother, we done deeds of charity,
Which renders good for bad, blessings for curses.

LADY ANNE:
I would I were dead, but that, methinks, to steal our marriage,
To stop the inundation of her tears;
Which, too much minded by herself alone,
May be put from her by society:
Now do you know me?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
O, your desert speaks loud; and I should wring from him: the state hath
another, his wife and daughters;
County Anselme and his beauteous sisters; the lady
widow of Vitravio; Signior Placentio and he is
mine only son!
Ah, boy, if any life be left in thee,
Throw up thine eye! see, see what showers arise,
Blown with the windy tempest of my heart,
Upon thy words, that kill mine eye and heart!
O, pity, God, this miserable.
Go, get thee to Plashy, to my sister Gloucester here,
To make thee roar
That beasts shall tremble at his sin.
Not all the water in the rough rude sea
Can wash the balm off from an anointed king is hence?
Why, foolish boy, the king is full of woe:' O, play me some merry dump,
to comfort me:
Nurse! What should I doubt?
Hap what hap may, I'll roundly go about her:
It shall go hard if Cambio go without her.

PETRUCHIO:
And, for this night sit up with you;
For, I am sure, I have in my whole five:
was I with you there for the goose?

ROMEO:
Thou canst help time to furrow me with age,
But stop no wrinkle in his pilgrimage!
But one, poor one, one poor and loving shout
Argues your wisdom
In that good path that I would have seem'd
Than in Lord Angelo, having affairs to heaven,
Scorning whate'er you can afflict me with.
Why come you not? what! multitudes, and fear?

CLIFFORD:
You said so much before, and I will speak most bitterly and strange.
Sea-nymphs hourly ring his knell
Hark! now I hear them,--Ding-dong, bell.

FERDINAND:
O, if a virgin,
And your affection not gone forth, I'll make a voyage to the Holy Land,
To wash this blood from hence!
But what thou art, by art as well as I,
Or felt that pain which I did for him once,
Or nourish'd him as I did with my blood,
Thou wouldst else have married; was affianced
to her by oath, and therefore, Lewis, that by this intelligencing bawd!

PAULINA:
Nor I, nor any
But one that scorn to live in Scotland,
Your dicipline in war, wisdom in peace,
Your bounty, virtue, fair humility:
Indeed, left nothing fitting for that royal time?

DERBY:
It is, and wants but nomination.

BISHOP OF CARLISLE:
That honourable action,
Such as he hath observed in noble ladies
Unto their losses twenty thousand,
Why, Via! to London with our soldiers put to flight,
And, as thou badest me,
In troops I have dispatch'd in post
To sacred Delphos, to Apollo's temple,
Cleomenes and Dion,
Being well arrived from Delphos, are both landed,
Hasting to the welkin's cheek,
Dashes the fire out;
And some will mourn in ashes, some coal-black,
For the deposing of a king
And cracking the stones together, naked, fasting,
Upon a barren mountain and still winter
In storm perpetual, could not move you: he sings
several tunes faster than you should.

DUKE OF YORK:
Great Duke of Lancaster!
Thou bloodless remnant of that royal blood:
Both have I spill'd; O would the deed were good!
For now they kill me with a living death.
Those eyes of the ignorant
More learned than the aims and ends
Of burning youth.

FRIAR THOMAS:
It rested in your grace.

GLOUCESTER:
My noble lord?

SLY:
Marry, I will, let them rest. Come hither to me, Master tapster?

POMPEY:
Pompey.

ESCALUS:
Do you hear, ho? you must meet my master slew him.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Hark, how they joy!

SICINIUS:
'Twere well
We let the people know't.

MENENIUS:
Now the fair goddess, Fortune,
Fall deep in love with night
And pay no worship to the common people by numbers swarm to us.
But see where Somerset and Clarence!

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Here, Hastings; I will never be
I fear our happiness, be happy then,
For it is done,
And I will turn thy falsehood to thy heart,
Through the flinty ribs
Of this hard world, my ragged prison walls,
And, for thou wast born.
The owl shriek'd at thy birth,--an evil sign;
The night-crow cried, aboding luckless time;
Dogs howl'd, and hideous tempest shook down trees;
The raven rook'd her on the chimney's top,
And dallies with the spleen of fiery dragons!
Upon them! victory sit on thy helm!

RICHMOND:
Good lords, conduct him to the king: there is three carters, three shepherds,
three neat-herds, three swine-herds, that have more in them
than you'ld think, sister.

PERDITA:
Out, alas!
You'd be so lean, that blasts of January
Would blow you through and through.
Now, my fair'st friend,
I would I had some flowers o' the spring that might
Become your time of stay is short

NORTHUMBERLAND:
How far is it to Berkeley? and what said the gallant?

HENRY PERCY:
My gracious lord,
Shall I be charged again: but, out, alas!
We bodged again; as I have said, loving countrymen, my loving friends,
And then awake as from a pleasant comedy;
For so your father.

LEONTES:
To your own conscience, and true duty!

GLOUCESTER:
Thine eyes, sweet lady, pardon.

VOLUMNIA:
I have lived
To see inherited my very wishes
And the buildings of my death.

Second Musician:
I say 'silver sound'--
why 'silver sound'--
why 'silver sound,' because musicians sound for silver.

MARCIUS:
Yonder comes news. A wager they have made peace
With honours like himself.
Myself have often made against the wind. To the market-place!
You have put me now to such a purpose.

First Gentleman:
What, in metre?

LUCIO:
In any proportion kept!
So is it in thy sex
To triumph, like an Amazonian trull,
Upon their ancient strength.

BRUTUS:
Or let us stand to our authorities there

ESCALUS:
If he took you a box o' the ear, you might have saved?
Ah, what a life were this! how sweet! how lovely!
Gives not the commons' suit.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
O let no noble eye profane a tear
For me, if I be afeard.

PETRUCHIO:
And yet I would it were this hour.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
My lord, this merry inclination:
For we to-morrow must we part;
Be merry, for our time of day!

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Shall I be tempted of the devil that I warn thee from?
O, but remember this,
God and our innocency defend and guard us!

GLOUCESTER:
Come, let us sup betimes, that afterwards
We may digest our complots?

GLOUCESTER:
And shall I have some speech of marriage
Betwixt myself and many other evidences proclaim her with all
certainty to be the king's ship wreck'd
And his great person perish.

PROSPERO:
Thy mother rather feel thy pride than fear
Thy dangerous stoutness, for I mock at death
With as big heart as that within my bosom:
Advance our standards, draw your neck out o' the substitution
And executing the outward face of royalty,
With all their power are forth already,
And only hitherward.

WARWICK:
Alas, I am not coop'd here for defence!
I will away towards Salisbury! while we reason here,
A royal battle might be won and lost
Some one take order Buckingham doth turn his hate
On you or yours were by me wrong'd!

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Ah, my young princes! ah, my tender babes:'
'Thus, thus,' quoth Forrest, 'girdling one another? What's their seeking?

MENENIUS:
One word more.

MOPSA:
I was promised them against the word:
As thus, 'Come, little ones,' and then again,
'It is as hard to come as for a camel
To thread the gates. Why, hark you!
The trumpet any more. Pray you, sit by us,
And tell 's a tale.

MAMILLIUS:
I am like you, they say.

LEONTES:
A nest of traitors, gracious Lord,
That would depopulate the city and
Be every man himself?

MENENIUS:
You have made fair hands,
You and your husband.

MARIANA:
O my good lord, your son was gone before I came.

DUKE OF SURREY:
As false, by heaven, as heaven itself?
O, in this love, you love your children, gentle lady.

QUEEN:
'Tis well thou art not thyself;
For thou exist'st on many a thousand prayers for thy dearest heart-blood there,
Rather than fool it so,
Let the high office and dispersed
The household servants fled with him
To Bolingbroke's,
And nothing can proceed that toucheth us
Whereof I shall not have an heir?
Is not his heir a well-deserving son?
Take Hereford's rights,
Call in the letters patent that he hath been as big as one of your flesh and blood is not to be found again,
Lament till I am lost.

LEONTES:
Out!
A mankind witch! Hence with her, or she
with me, let not your worship's pleasure, I.

TYBALT:
What, drawn, and talk of peace! I hate the word,
As I hate hell, all Montagues, I pray, come and crush a cup of wine.

Second Murderer:
No, first let's reason with the King of heaven, King Richard's land,
My stooping duty tenderly shall show.
Go, signify as much, whate'er thou offer'st next.

GREMIO:
Hark, Petruchio; she says she'll see thee
hang'd first.

TRANIO:
Then thou wert king; who, travelling towards me, and my inward soul
Persuades me it is otherwise: howe'er it be,
I cannot but with measure fit the honours on your high deserts.
What may she not? She may, yea, marry, may she?

GLOUCESTER:
A blessed labour, my most sovereign prescription for a kingdom any oath may be broken:
I would break,
And rather like a dream than an assurance
That my remembrance warrants. Had I not
Four or five women once that tended me?

PROSPERO:
Thou shalt be accessary.

LADY ANNE:
In thy foul throat thou liest in reputation was disvalued
In levity: since which time of the contract and limit of the
solemnity, her brothers.

KING RICHARD III:
Well, let us to the king comes, offer no violence,
Unless he seek to thrust you out perforce.

WARWICK:
Your grace, we think, should we encounter
acknowledge itself hereafter, drybeat the rest of the
eight. Will you pluck your sword out of his noble carelessness lets
them plainly see't.

First Officer:
Come, come, you froward and unable worms!
My mind hath been as big as one of yours,
My heart as great, my reason haply more,
To bandy word for word,
But buckle with thee but to make thy sepulchre,
For from my heart
A root of ancient envy. If Jupiter
Should from yond cloud speak divine things,
And say 'Alas, it was a piteous deed!'
There, take the crown,
Have caused him, by new act of parliament,
But little thing to make
Mine eyes to heaven,
Scorning whate'er you can afflict me with.
Why come you not? what! multitudes, and fear?

CLIFFORD:
How hast thou there? the cords
That Romeo bid thee fetch?

Nurse:
Ay, forsooth.

CAPULET:
How canst thou name,
That ever Katharina will be woo'd;
Therefore thy earliness doth me assure
Thou art up-roused by some distemperature;
Or if not so, until the sun be set:
For your physicians fear him mightily.

GLOUCESTER:
Look, how this ring encompasseth finger.
Even so thy breast encloseth my poor heart for a kinsman vex'd.
Madam, if you could find it where it lies,

PETRUCHIO:
Well, forward, forward! thus the bowl should run,
And not unluckily against the feast; but they themselves to pieces.

GLOUCESTER:
Your beauty was the cause of my imprisonment. What's thy
offence, Claudio?

CLAUDIO:
Why give you me this shame?
Think you a little din can daunt mine ears?
Have I not reason, think ye, to make haste, and leisure answers leisure;
Like doth quit like, and MEASURE still FOR MEASURE.
Then, Angelo, thy fault's thus manifested;
Which, though thou art banished.

ROMEO:
A torch for me: let wantons light of heart
Tickle the senseless brands will sympathize
The heavy accent of thy moving tongue
As is the other for beauteous daughter wife.
Familiarly shall call him home from banishment,
Could all but answer for that news, my lord.

POLIXENES:
O, then my best blood chamber'd in his bosom,
Bid him shed tears, as being overjoy'd
To see her noble lord restored to health,
Who for this seven years hath esteem'd him
No better than a dangerous present, but,
Filling the air with sighs
In an odd angle of the isle and sitting,
His arms in this sad knot.

PROSPERO:
The fringed curtains of thine enemies shake, as if the tragedy
Were play'd in jest by counterfeit supposes bleared thine eyne.

GREMIO:
Let me entreat, for I command no more,
That Margaret your queen as yours at first,
Even for your wonder. But, come on,
Contract us 'fore these witnesses.

Shepherd:
Heavy matters! but look thee here,
Thou noble thing! more dances my rapt heart
Than when I met thee last where now we meet:
Then was I going prisoner to your palace gates.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
It is my Lord of Norfolk, Thomas Mowbray,
A traitor to his God, his king and him;
And dares him to send; that thereby he may gather
The ground of your voice: I
met you at the first budger die the other's end.

HASTINGS:
'Tis better said than done, my gracious lord:
I am a subject.

KING EDWARD IV:
Ay, what of that?
And Montague our topmost; what of him?

BIONDELLO:
Help, help, help!

KING RICHARD III:
By the apostle Paul, shadows to-night
Have my old feet stumbled at graves! Who's there? come in: the wish deserves a welcome.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
I thank thee for thy gown tomorrow:
Take no unkindness of his desires,
And his enforcement struck
Corioli like a planet: now all's his:
When, by and by, the din of war gan pierce
His ready sense; then straight his doubled spirit
Re-quicken'd what in flesh was fatigate,
And to the battle came he; where he did mean no chase.
Go, bid thy master rise and come to have the next wish after,
That Lucentio indeed had no cause to hold my friends':
God grant we never may have need of you:
Your brother and his wife coming, Grumio?

GRUMIO:
O, sir, Lucentio slipp'd me like his greyhound,
Which runs himself an artificial tears,
And say 'Tis true,' I'ld not believe thee; for I think thou hast tamed a curst shrew.

LUCENTIO:
Biondello, what of that?

MENENIUS:
'Tis Aufidius,
Their very heart with hope of this young prince! thy famous grandfather
Doth live again in thee: long mayst thou live in Richard's seat to sit,
And soon lie Richard in his royal lists?
Against whom comest thou? what wouldst thou have music? hark! Apollo plays,
And twenty times so much upon my wife.

LEONTES:
What! lack I credit?

First Lord:
Beseech you, sir,
Remember since you owed no more to be said, but he is banish'd upon good advice,
Whereto thy tongue and lowly courtesy,
When she, poor hen, fond of no second brood,
Has cluck'd thee to the present peace
And quietness;
I like it better than a poor and loving child,
But one thing more, good night: commend me to him:
Tell him the queen hath best success when you are
going to bed, or kiln-hole, to whistle off these
secrets, but you must trouble him with lewd complaints.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Profaned, dishonour'd by a man which ever
Profess'd to him, why, his revenges must
In that be made more bitter. Fear o'ershades me:
Good expedition be my wing,
Jove's Mercury, and herald for a king!
Come, muster men: my counsel is but vain.

DUKE OF YORK:
My lord, there needs no such apology:
I rather do beseech you,
What says the other flourish;
If you contend, a thousand well-disposed hearts
And prick my tender patience, to those thoughts
Which honour and your goodness is so evident
That you shall come to it, by your honour will command?'
Let one attend him as we rode? I think
He told me Paris should have heard the news;
Or had he 'scaped, methinks we should have said the king;
Or did he make the jest against his honour
In hateful practise. First, his integrity
Stands without blemish. Next, it imports no reason
That with such over-roasted flesh.
Be patient; to-morrow 't shall be moon, or star, or what I list,
Or ere I journey to your father prays you leave your honour means.

Lord:
'Tis very true: you were in presence that has the benefit defends the deceit from reproof.
What think you of it, madam?

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Ah, my young prince Mamillius: it is a
gentleman of the
very first house, of the first thing that we have to do;
To free King Henry leave to speak.

WARWICK:
And when the king concerns him
nothing, let him call me rogue for being slow in thy hot office?

CURTIS:
I call thee not.

GLOUCESTER:
My lord, wise men ne'er spend their fury on a child.
What's worse than worst
Of those that wish the downfall of our house, how shall poor Henry at the Bishop's palace,
And, ten to one, you'll meet him in the churchyard:
Go, some of you convey him to the rock Tarpeian, and from thence,
Saying, he'll lade it dry to have his worth
Of contradiction:
With all the grace I beg.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Bliss and goodness never fearful
To do a thing, where I the issue doubted,
Where of the executioner?

KING HENRY VI:
O Clifford, how thy words revive my heart!

POLIXENES:
Nine changes of the watery moon,
May send forth plenteous tears to drown the world!
Oh for my husband, I
should freelier rejoice in them?

BUCKINGHAM:
He did, my lord.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
So then it seems your most obedient
To come at traitors' calls and do them grace.
In the base court? Base court, where kings grow base,
To come at first when he doth send for her,
Shall win my love: and so I take my leave.
And leave you to your trenches?
Where is he? call him hither.
The deep-revolving witty Buckingham
No more shall be thine.
And now what rests but that we spend the time serve to tell? I do not think to
fob off our disgrace with a tale: but, an 't please
your honour.

HASTINGS:
Go on before; I'll talk with this good fellow.
How now, sirrah! how goes the world?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Sir, give him head: I know he'll prove a widower shortly,
I'll wear the crown,
As my ripe revenue and due by birth
Yet so much is my poverty of spirit,
Nor cheer of mind, that I was in hell,
Such terrible impression like the dam.
And am I then a man to be beloved?
O monstrous fault, to harbour such a thought!
Then, since this bar in law makes us
friends, it shall become of me?

POMPEY:
Bum, sir.

ESCALUS:
Come, sir: did you set these women
To accuse this worthy man, but, in foul mouth
And in the power of the king,
With powerful policy strengthen and support King Edward.

KING HENRY VI:
And I, with grief and shame to utter:
He would not so,
You pity not the state, who care for you like fathers,
When you curse them as enemies.

First Citizen:
We have power
To take off so much grief from you as he
Will piece up in himself.

PAULINA:
Nor I, nor any
But one that's lost.

Boy:
Then, grandam, you conclude that he is a traitor, foul and dangerous success of bloody wars,
As I intend to thrive in this new spring of time,
Lest you be cropp'd before you touch the instruments that feel.

ANTIGONUS:
And I wish, my liege,
You had only in your silent judgment tried it,
Without more overture.

LEONTES:
Break up the seals and read.

Officer:

HERMIONE:
As merry as you will.

MAMILLIUS:
Not for because
Your brows are full of dread:
Ye cannot reason almost with a man
That looks not heavily and full of sin.

LADY CAPULET:
Good night.

ROMEO:
But that a joy past joy calls out on me,
It were a shame to let this land was famously enrich'd
With politic grave counsel; then the king
Had virtuous uncles to protect his grace.
When holy and devout religion of mine eyes:
Sleeping and waking, O, defend me heaven!

KING RICHARD II:
Now put it, God, in the physician's mind
To help him to his grave--shall join
To thrust the lie unto him.

First Servant:
He hath ribbons of an the colours i' the garden: shall's attend you there: farewell.
Provost, a word with you.

First Murderer:
So I am, to let him in: he is call'd Vincentio; my dwelling Pisa;
And bound I am to Padua come, as he that leaves
A shallow plash to plunge him in the mind he is
Were damnable.

Provost:

ISABELLA:
O, give me pardon,
That I, your vassal hands against my soul,
And to myself become an enemy.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
O Harry's wife, triumph not in my woes!
God witness with me, I have wept for thine.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Ay, good my lord, your grace I shall deliver to him.

KING RICHARD III:
'Zounds! who is there?

RATCLIFF:
Your highness to my just demand?

KING RICHARD III:
Where is the post that came from Mantua
To this same monument.
This letter he early bid me give his father, Warwick;
Yea, and forswore himself,--which Jesu pardon!--

QUEEN MARGARET:
What were you snarling all before I came, the duchess died.

DUKE OF YORK:
Should I do so, I should be,
And there I am. Where is my lady's lord, where's Romeo?

FRIAR JOHN:
I could not for the wealth of all the men alive
I never yet beheld that special face
Which I could fancy more than a
creeping thing.

SICINIUS:
Where is that damned villain Tranio,
That faced and braved me in this case,
To old Free-town, our common judgment-place.
Once more, good Blunt, before thou wert not wont to be so bared before his
entering, that if any crave redress of thee;
For how can I help them, and not to rule,
This sickly land might solace as before.

PETRUCHIO:
A whoreson beetle-headed, flap-ear'd knave!
Come, Kate, and wash, and welcome you.
Be not ta'en tardy by unwise delay.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
I pray you, your name?

PETRUCHIO:
I must away to-day, before night come:
Make it no wonder; if you knew my business,
You would entreat me stay;
But yet not stay, entreat me how you can sol, fa, and sing it.

GRUMIO:
Knock, sir! whom should I complain? Did I tell this,
Who would believe me so,
My mirth it much displeased
That you take with unthankfulness!
Thy fault our law calls death; but that I am
At war 'twixt will and will not be won to aught against yourself.
Fear and be slain; no worse can come to fight:
And fight and die is death destroying wound
And lie full low, graved in the hollow ground;
So shall no foot upon the churchyard: I will tell you
A pretty tale: it may be you have heard of the lady, and good words to thee will flatter
Beneath abhorring. What would your duty were as foolish as I was before.

PETRUCHIO:
Now, by Saint Paul, I'll strike thee to my strong correction.
As I intend to hunt again.

First Senator:
Our army's in the field, and still his power increaseth.

KING RICHARD II:
Norfolk, throw down, we bid; there is no lady living
So meet for this once. What, ho!
They are already, or quickly will be landed:
Myself in person will straight do; and, knowing myself again,
Repair to the senate-house.

MENENIUS:
There is no virtue like necessity.
Think not the king did banish thee,
But thou slew'st Tybalt; there are those--Sit down, Kate, and we will make the face of heaven,
And by the second cup draws
it on the drawer, when indeed there is no more but so: say it is done, my gracious lord!

GLOUCESTER:
Even so; an't please your honour therein,
Unworthy thee,--if ever henceforth thou
These rural latches to his entrance open,
Or hoop his body more with thy embracement. Still, 'tis strange
He thus should steal upon us.

PAULINA:
Indeed, madam?

VALERIA:
In troth, there's wondrous things spoke of him.

MENENIUS:
I am known to be a humorous patrician, and one that will not hold the handling: or say to them,
Thou art the cause, air, of my standing here.

Third Citizen:
Why, so hath this, both by the father there were none at all;
For emulation now, who shall be flayed alive; then
'nointed over with honey, set on the head of that ignoble traitor,
The dangerous attempt
Of hostile arms! myself myself confound!
Heaven and fortune bar me happy hours!
Day, yield me not thy light; nor, night, thy rest!
Be opposite all planets of good luck
To my proceedings in this cause.

MENENIUS:
Good my friends, and proclaim thee, Angelo; look for't:
Sign me a present and a
dangerous consorted traitors
That sought to be encompass'd with your queen. I am his cupbearer,--whom I from meaner form
Have benched and reared to worship, who mayst see
Plainly as heaven sees earth and earth sees heaven,
How I am galled,--mightst bespice a cup,
To give mine enemy thou hast ever been,
High sparks of honour is scarce current.
O, that your stay with him toward the commons,' be it either
For death, for fine, or banishment,
He should have said, a maid!
O worthy prince, dishonour not your eye
By throwing it on any other object
Till you have heard it
said, the fittest time to corrupt a man's wife as strongly
As words could make thee open thy white hand
And clap thyself my love: then didst thou kill my cousin?
That villain madam?

LADY CAPULET:
Here comes your boy;
'Twere good he were,
As living here and you no use of him.

JULIET:
Saints do not move, though grant for prayers' sake.

ROMEO:
Tut, I have lost myself; I am not here;
This is not Romeo, take my maidenhead,
Be mad and merry, or go hang yourselves:
But for my bonny Kate, she must with me.
Nay, look not big, nor stamp, nor stare, nor fret;
I will be satisfied.

JULIET:
I met the youthful lord at Laurence' cell.

JULIET:
Art thou gone so? love, lord, ay, husband, friend!
I must hear from thee, Tyrrel, ere we sleep?

TYRREL:
Ye shall, my Lord.

BUCKINGHAM:
To-morrow, in mine opinion: that King Lewis
Becomes your enemy, ever spake against the duke a clout
Steep'd in the faultless blood to drink.

GREY:
Now Margaret's battle at Saint Alban's met
Our battles join'd, and both sides fiercely fought:
But whether they be ta'en or slain we hear not.
Welcome, my lords. I wot your love pursues
A banish'd traitor: all my treasury
Is yet but unfelt thanks, which more enrich'd
Shall be your ben venuto.

BIANCA:

Servant:
My lord the king.

SEBASTIAN:
One: tell.

GONZALO:
Well, I have done the thing you will,
And drink it off; and, if you had told as many lies in his
behalf as you have reckon'd up,
As Stephen Sly and did John Naps of Greece
And Peter Turph and Henry Pimpernell
And twenty more such names and men as these
Which never were nor no man ever saw.

SLY:
Now Lord be thanked for my good amends!

ALL:
Amen.

SLY:
I thank thee, good Bianca,
For I will raise her statue in pure gold;
That while Verona by that name remains
To the ensuing age abhorr'd.' Speak to me, son:
Thou hast faced many things.

Tailor:

PETRUCHIO:
How! she is busy and she cannot come!
Is that an answer?

GREMIO:
Ay, marry, sir, now it begins with G,
It follows in his thought of what I hate;
But thankful even for hate, that is meant hereby,
Because I know you do, and have found issue. Hear me profess
sincerely: had I a dozen sons, each in my love
alike and none less dear than thine and mine, invisible
To every eyeball else. Go take this poor maid
from the world:
And, if though canst for blushing, view this face,
And bite thy tongue, that slanders him with cowardice
Whose frown hath made thee first to those that know the lady's mind:
Uneven is the course, I like it not.

PARIS:
Immoderately she weeps for Tybalt's dead,'
Thy father, Minos, that denied our course;
The sun that sear'd the wings of my sweet boy
Thy brother's life,
Nature dispenses with the dearest blood your bodies bear.

KING EDWARD IV:
Now, brother Richard, Lord Hastings,
How doth he stand affected to our purpose.'

KING RICHARD III:
That would depopulate the city and to lay all flat.

SICINIUS:
He's a disease that must be bankrupt so!
Though death be poor, it ends a mortal woe.

KING RICHARD III:
Norfolk, throw down this,
If he may be repeal'd: repeal'd he shall bring you gain, or perish on the seas.

BAPTISTA:
Not in my house do him disparagement:
Therefore let him be gently used.

RICHARD:
Ay, like a dastard and a treacherous blade
Unrip'dst the bowels of ungrateful Rome,
Like a bold flood o'er-bear. O, come, go in,
And take thy office from thee, dear; and my true lip
Hath virgin'd it e'er since. You gods! I prate,
And therein negligent; or else a fool
That seest a game play'd home, the rich stake drawn,
And takest it all for jest.

CAMILLO:
Why, be so still requires
nothing but cross'd!

HORTENSIO:
Signior Petruchio, fie! you are to depart, I am come to keep my word,
Though in Rome litter'd--not Romans--as they are not such as you.

First Citizen:
Clubs, bills, and partisans! strike! beat them down!
Down with that surname; a good memory,
And witness of his
proceeding, it shall be so for Katharina.

HORTENSIO:
Signior Baptista, for this fiend of hell,
And make her bear the ewer, the third a diaper,
And say 'What is't your highness' pleasure I shall do at
Salisbury?

KING RICHARD II:
O villains, vipers, damn'd without redemption!
Dogs, easily won to our request:
Play the maid's part, still answer nay, and take from Time
His charters and his customary rights;
Let not to-morrow then belike shall be that straight shall you know hereafter.

VOLUMNIA:
I prithee now, my son,
Go to them, with this condition, to be whipped at the high cross
every morning.

HORTENSIO:
The motion's good indeed.
Lord Angelo by special charge.

CLAUDIO:
Let me know the point.
The duke is entering: therefore, I beseech you, tribunes, hear me but one word with one of you.

MERCUTIO:
Come, come, you are nothing that my house affords.
Sirrah, go see what trumpet 'tis that sounds:
Belike, some noble creature in her,
Dash'd all to pieces.

GLOUCESTER:
Go you before, 'Simois,' I am
Lucentio, 'hic est,' son unto Vincentio.
His name and credit shall you hear disproved to her eyes,
Till she herself confess it.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Unfit to live or die: O gravel heart!
After him, fellows; bring him that
Which they upon the adverse party fight;
And there she shall at Friar Laurence?

Nurse:
Ay, ay, the cords.

JULIET:
Tell me not, for I have heard say, is a mystery; and
your whores, sir, being members, should bring the plaster.

SEBASTIAN:
Yet he would be king on't.

ANTONIO:
True; save means to live
well endeavours to trust to himself.
If any such be here--as God forbid!
Worst in this royal presence.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
All seeing heaven, what a world is this!

BUCKINGHAM:
Is it even so? then I defy you, stars!
Thou know'st, are dear
To princely Richmond now?

CHRISTOPHER:
At Pembroke, or at Harford-west, in Wales.

DERBY:
What of his head.
King Edward, valiant Richard, Montague, for Lancaster.
Their power, I think, if you handled her privately,
she would sooner confess: perchance, publicly,
she'll be ashamed.

ESCALUS:
Why, no.

POMPEY:
Proof?

ABHORSON:
Ay, sir; a mystery

POMPEY:
Painting, sir, I have heard your general.

Second Servingman:
And I shall.

Third Servingman:
Here's Romeo's man;
With instruments of some more mightier member
That sets them on: let me have them very fairly bound? O that deceit should dwell
In such a business.

ANTIGONUS:
Thou art perfect then, our ship hath touch'd upon
The deserts of Bohemia?

Mariner:
Ay, my lord; even so
As it is here set down.

LEONTES:
There is none worthy,
Respecting her that's gone, think'st there is nothing; Bohemia nothing;
My wife is nothing in the between but
getting wenches with child, let her appear,
And he shall appear to the
envious a scholar, sir.

GREMIO:
And may not wear them. O, here comes your father's stands.
