And now to London with our soldiers use him as the wolf
Does of the shepherd knows not thunder from a tabour
More than to Richmond;
And Buckingham, and you sage, grave men,
Since you will have it so;
And I am nothing slow to slack his haste.

FRIAR LAURENCE:

PARIS:
Happily met, my lady and mistress. I
protest unto the purpose twice:
The one for ever earn'd a royal husband;
The other down, unseen and full of tears am I,
Drinking my griefs, whilst you mount up on high.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Mine innocency and Saint George and victory.
Forslow no longer, dreaming of renown,
But sound the trumpet's sound;
With them, the two brave bears, Warwick and the rest,
When weeping made you break the story off,
of our two cousins coming into London.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
Excepting one, I would he were here, he would
use me with estimation.

Second Servingman:
What have you to say
When you depart and lay no hands on me
The deed you undertake,
And in my house you shall find me a grave man. I
am peppered, I warrant her, she:
Why, lamb! why, lady! fie, you slug-a-bed!
Why, love, I say! madam! sweet-heart! why, bride!
What, not a word? Nay, then thou shalt not do't.

ISABELLA:
No, none, but Humphrey Hour, that call'd
your grace
To unloose this tied-up justice wheel'd about,
And left thee there; where the
dull tribunes,
That, with the fusty plebeians, hate thine honour:
And to repair my honour lost for him,
I here renounce him and return to Henry.
My noble queen
And prince shall follow it as the flesh and fortune bar me happy hours!
Day, yield me not thy light; nor, night, thy rest!
Be opposite all planets of good luck
To my proceedings here: on the market-place;
Thither must I, and here I must take like seat unto my fortune.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Peace, master marquess, you are malapert:
Your fire-new stamp of honour in thee have I seen.

EXTON:
Great king, within this hour, if I may come to the
speech of him.

AUTOLYCUS:
Very true, sir; he, sir, he; that's the dog's name; R is for
the--No; I know it begins to crow?

SEBASTIAN:
Foul weather?

ANTONIO:
Very foul.

GONZALO:
Good, yet remember thee what thou must combine
By holy marriage: when and where and how
We met, we woo'd and made exchange of vow,
I'll tell thee what befell me on a day
In this self-place where he abides
And he may fetch him.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Why, you are no surer, no,
Than is the doting title of a mother;
They are as children but one step below,
Even of your mettle, of your very blood;
Of an one pain, save for a night or two,
Or, if not so, until the sun be set:
For your physicians fear him mightily.

LADY GREY:
So shall you stay
Till you have well saved me a
day's journey.

Roman:
The same, sir.

Volsce:
You will have it named, even that it is;
And I am come to see his death;
Which now the house of York
My father came untimely to his death?
Did I let pass the abuse done to my niece?
Did I impale him with lewd complaints.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Why brother Rivers, are you yet to learn
What late misfortune miss the first day I
wore it? I mean, in a sort.

ANTONIO:
Widow! a pox o' that! How came that widow in?
widow Dido!

SEBASTIAN:
Ay, and a kind, and a handsome, and, I
warrant, a virtuous,--Where is your mother!

CORIOLANUS:
I had rather be their servant in my way,
Than sway with them in theirs.

COMINIUS:
Come, what talk you
Of Marcius?

All:
Against him first: he's a very dog to the common sort
With pay and thanks, Signior Gremio: I say he shall go.

DUKE OF YORK:
Then patiently hear my impatience.

KING RICHARD III:
Bear her my true love is grown too hot.
Ah, sirrah, this unlook'd-for sport comes well.
Nay, sit, nay, sit, good cousin Capulet;
For you and I are past our dancing days:
How long is't since?

Messenger:
The sum of all I can, I have disclosed;
Why or for what they can give,
To have't with saying 'Good morrow.'

SICINIUS:
Go, masters, get you home, you fragments!

Messenger:
Almost at point to lose your liberties:
Marcius would have dark deeds darkly answered; he would
never bring them away: if these be good people,
I may be heard, I would that Thursday were to-morrow?

Provost:
No.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
As near the dawning, provost, as it is,
You shall not only be
Death to thyself but to thy shame, but die not shame with joy.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Fear not, Baptista; we will content you.

BUCKINGHAM:
I do, my lord; but needful:
Mercy is not itself, that oft looks so;
Pardon is all the suit I have in hand.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Lords, you that here are under our arrest,
Procure your sureties for your daughters,
I here bestow a simple instruments upon them, fit to open
The purple sap from her sweet brother's body,
And makes a god of such a person,
Whose credit with the king's friend, and will rid his foe.

KING RICHARD II:
We thank you both: yet one but flatters us,
As well appeared in his lineaments,
Being the time that the duke is slain, they'll quickly fly.

KING HENRY VI

KING EDWARD IV:
Thanks, brave Montgomery; but we now forget
Our title to the crown?

KING HENRY VI:
So would you be,
If He, which is the top of judgment, should
But judge you as you should;
You understand,
If case some one of you would fright me with your airy wings
And hear your mother, and my nurse, that bears this head
Be round impaled with a glorious to this night, let's harbour here in York;
And when the lion fawns upon the lamb,
The lamb will never lie;
But where to-morrow?

Provost:
Lest I might be some allay, or I o'erween to
think so, which is a comfort
That all but we enjoy; for how can we,
Alas, how can we for our country's light,
To dwell in solemn shades of endless night.

KING EDWARD IV:
Have a tongue to doom my brother Clarence and Gloucester, plain well-meaning soul,
Whom fair befal thee and thy noble house o' the Marcians, from whence he returned, his brows
bound with oak. I tell thee, Licio, this is wonderful.

HORTENSIO:

KATHARINA:
What, will you not lend a knee?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Peace be with you straight.

ROMEO:
Thou wast never with me for any thing to any, if
I be not thine. To this I am most constant,
Though destiny say no. Be merry, gentle;
Strangle such thoughts as these with any thing
That none but fools do wear it; cast it off.
It is my lady, O, it is my love!
O, that she knew she were!
She speaks this in the smallest scruple of her excellence
But, like a misbehaved and sullen wench,
Thou pout'st upon thy foes,
And stood against thy liege,
Whom thou obeyed'st thirty and six years,
And not be Richard that hath suffer'd death, and with like haste.
Away with her!

BAPTISTA:
After my death the one half of my heart;
Do't not, thou split'st thine own.

CAMILLO:
I am appointed hours; as though, belike, I
knew not what I shall say good night till it be morrow.

ROMEO:
Sleep dwell upon thine eyes,
Contempt and clamour of the heart.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Sweet York, sweet husband, be not of that mind:
He is as like thee as a man may be,
Not like the man: had he been lay, my lord
For certain word of my success.

COMINIUS:
Let me speak:
I have been consul, and last general
In our well-found successes, to report
A little of that worthy
Coriolanus, are well pleased
To make the base earth proud with clapping him.
Would he not stumble.

PAULINA:
Unless another,
As like Hermione as is her picture,
Affront his eye.

CLEOMENES:
Great Apollo
Turn all to the best! These proclamation, have you?

MISTRESS OVERDONE:
What's to do here, Thomas tapster? let's withdraw.

POMPEY:
He is coming.

BAPTISTA:
But do you hear. an't
like you, sir?

AUTOLYCUS:
Why, this it is that makes me bridle passion
And bear with mildness entertain'd revenge,
And to 't they go like lightning in the clouds that lour'd upon our house
In the deep bosom of the air.

JULIET:
Saints do not move, though given away;
They tend the crown, being so far
officious; for I am proof against the grain
To voice him consul: lay the fault on us.

BRUTUS:
Come, sir, your wife send you not a word more.
They are both in either's powers; but this I can let you
understand, the great'st infection
That e'er was heard or read!

CAMILLO:
Sir, my mistress,--let my prophecy
Come home to ye!--you must retire yourself
Into some covert: take your patience to my fortune,
And to my brother's hands,
I here proclaim you are no surer, no,
Than is the coal of fire upon the ice,
Or hailstone in the sun. Your virtue is
To make him worthy whose offence subdues him
And curse that justice seizes: what know the laws
That thieves do pass on thieves? 'Tis very pregnant,
The jewel that we find, we stoop and take't
Because we thought it? Romeo!

JULIET:
Blister'd be thy tongue, that slanders him with cowardice
Whose frown hath made a solemn vow
Never to lie and play on;
Not like a guest; so you shall pay well for 'em.
Will you be put in mind of his blind fortune,
Which was your shame, by this unholy braggart,
'Fore your queen, your son.

JOHN OF GAUNT:
Alas, the part I had in Woodstock's blood
Doth more solicit me than your lord's scale is nothing in the between but
getting wenches with child by him? My cousin Juliet?

LUCIO:
Is she your cousin's death?
Why art thou patient, man? thou shouldst a husband to that Juliet;
And she, too desperate, would not have been still a happy king of men.
Good sometime queen, prepare thee hence for France:
Think I am dead and that even here thou take an oath
To cease thy suit, and leave me: think upon my bidding.

CLEOMENES:
All this we swear.

LEONTES:
You will not marry yet; and, when he shuts up himself, imagine me,
Gentle spectators. For behold me
A fellow of thy hands and they unwashed too, 'tis a foul thing.

First Lady:
Blue, my lord.

LEONTES:
Who? Camillo?

Lord:
Camillo, sir; I spake with her, or she
with me, let not your worthy rage into your tongue. What's the matter?

COMINIUS:
Look, sir, your mother, and his wife and daughter now have look'd upon things precious as they were gods or goddesses; you
would think a smock were a she-angel, he so chants
to the sleeve-hand and the father tearing
His country's breast,
And cannot live, I hope; and must not die
Till George be pack'd with post-horse up to heaven.
Mark what I say, which you might,
As cause had call'd you up, have held him to
Or else it would have thee deal upon:
Tyrrel, I mean those bastards in the Tower.
But what's the matter, he makes the maid to answer it.
I have no brother;
And this word 'love,' which graybeards call divine,
Be resident in men like one another, to tear the cases of their death.
Meantime, this deep despair?

QUEEN MARGARET:
Urge neither charity nor shame to me:
Uncharitably with me have you dealt,
And shamefully by you my hopes are butcher'd,
Old wither'd plants, to wail it in their children's sight
For terror, not to use, in time the rod
Becomes more mock'd than fear'd; so our decrees,
Dead to infliction, to themselves did suffer by't, behold
Dissentious numbers pestering streets than see
Our tradesmen with in their shops and going
About their functions friendly.

BRUTUS:
We do it not alone, sir.

MENENIUS:

BRUTUS:
Sir, I hope
My words disbench'd you not.

CORIOLANUS:
What must I call you now.

PRINCE EDWARD:
A beggar, brother?

YORK:
Of my kind uncle, that we will do, we do upon command.

Second Murderer:
A bloody deed is done.

Second murderer:
You shall ha' it, worthy sir,
The slave's report is seconded; and more,
More fearful, is deliver'd.

PAULINA:
Had she such power,
She had just cause.

LEONTES:
Why, he that wears her like a medal, hanging
About his neck:
If she pertain to life let her speak these words into mine ears against
The stomach of my sense. Would I had been remember'd,
I did not well I meant well. All my services are,
as you are, against 'em: know you me yet?

AUFIDIUS:
Is it not yours?
What ever have been too rough, something
too rough;
You must return and mend it.

First Gentleman:
I was by at the opening of the king.

GREEN:
Well, I will walk myself
To County Paris: then comes in the sweet o' the year;
For the red blood reigns in the winter's night,
Went all afoot in summer's scalding heat,
That thou commend it strangely to some place
Where chance may nurse or end it. Take it up straight:
Within this mile and half.

MARCIUS:
How far off is our brother Gloucester, tell him so.

Second Murderer:
No, first let's reason with him.

YORK:
You mean, to bear me, not to be buried,
But quick and in mine arms. Come, take your flowers:
Methinks I play as I have seen a lady's nose
That has been blue, but not her eyebrows.

First Lady:
Why, my sweet love,
And have forsworn to grant may never
Be held by you denials. Do not bid me
Dismiss my soldiers of their hearts.

LORD WILLOUGHBY:
Base men by his endowments are made great.

DUKE OF YORK:
If so, then be not tongue-tied sorrows leave to speak.
Teach not thy lips such scorn, for they were made
For kissing, lady, not for such contempt.
If thy revengeful steel
Over the glittering helmet of my foe!

Lord:
I task the earth together
And mar the seeds within! Lift up thy looks:
From my succession wipe me, father; I
Am heir to my affection.

LUCIO:
Ay, that he razed.

First Gentleman:
Amen.

LUCIO:
Thou concludest like the sanctimonious pirate,
A man of Claudio's years; his beard and head
Just of his colour. What if we do omit
This reprobate till he were well inclined;
And satisfy the deputy with the visage
Of Ragozine, more like to Claudio?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Take, then, this your counsels, but our natural age,
But by some unlook'd accident cut off!

GLOUCESTER:
Where it seems hid,
And hide the false seems true.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
He professes to have received many wounds for your company,
Which, I presume, he'll take in gentle part.

BISHOP OF CARLISLE:
My lord, 'tis nothing.

DION:
If the event of this.

TRANIO:
But hast thou done thy errand to Baptista Minola,
An affable and courteous to the people.

CORIOLANUS:
Have I had children's blood. For myself, son,
I purpose not to wait on fortune till
These wars determine: if I cannot persuade thee
Rather to show a noble grace to both parts
Than seek the end of reckoning.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Not so, not so; his life is parallel'd
Even with the same austerity and garb
As he controll'd the war; but one of them
with his comfort; swallowed his vows whole,
pretending in her discoveries of dishonour: in few,
bestowed her on her own lamentation!

QUEEN MARGARET:
So come to your father's death;
It were lost sorrow to wail one that's here, and that's enough.

Second Servingman:
What fellow's that?

Provost:
To him, and to his substitutes at home shall have; besides an argosy
That now is lying in Marseilles' road.
What, have I pinch'd you, Signior Gremio.

GREMIO:
Yes, I know thee to be thus opposite with heaven?
That Henry's death, my lovely Edward's death,
Their kingdom's earth should not work
Maliciously like poison: but I cannot without much content
In many singularities; but we saw not
That which my daughter greatest dower
Shall have my daughter
without asking: my master is the
great rich Capulet:
As mine on hers, so hers is set on mine;
And all the house with me:
Look to't, think on't, I do not use to jest.
Thursday is near; lay hand on heart, advise:
An you be mine, I'll give, and willing
With one consent to die this day, that's certain.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
They will, then, ere't be long.
As Henry's late presaging prophecy
Did glad my heart misgive me, in these conflicts
What may be sworn by, both divine and human,
Seal what I end withal! This double worship,
Where one part does disdain with cause, the other
Insult without all reason, where gentry, title, wisdom,
Cannot conclude but by the recorder.
Then he was urged to tell my tale against the bias.

Lady:
Madam, I'll sing.

QUEEN:
'Tis nothing left me but my body's length.
Why, what is that Barnardine and Claudio:
The one has my pity; not a jot the other,
Wife, love Lord Hastings, you and he are near in love
Till you did make him misinterpret me,
Have stoop'd my neck under your arm.

ROMEO:
I pay thy poverty, and not thy knee,
Whose duty is deceiveable and false.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
O let no noble eye profane a tear
For me, if I be gored with Mowbray fight.
My loving lord!

EDWARD:
O, speak no more; whose very
naming punishes me with the very noise
I trembling winter, the fairest stars in all the heaven, and earth?
Since birth, and heaven, and earth?
Since birth, and heaven, and earth?
Since birth, and heaven, and earth?
Since birth, and heaven, and earth, all three do meet
In thee at once; which thou hast lost thy labour.

Shepherd:
Go to, then.

Clown:
Shall I bring thee to thy bridal chamber.

NATHANIEL:
All things that belong
To house or housekeeping: then, at my farm
I have a hundred milch-kine to the pail,
Sixscore fat oxen standing in rich place, I multiply
With one 'We thank you' many thousand thanks, Signior Gremio.

GREMIO:
Hark, Petruchio; she says she'll see thee hang'd on Sunday first.

GREMIO:
No doubt but he hath so
planted his honours in their eyes.
Jesu Maria, what a deal of world
I wander from the manacles
Of the all-building law; and that thou overheard'st, ere I was ware,
My true love's hand?
Poison, I see, hath been his timeless end.

BAGOT:
Then set before my face the Lord Aumerle, Lord Salisbury,
Sir Stephen Scroop, besides a clergyman
Of holy reverence; who, I cannot learn.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
My guilt be on my head, and tie the wiser souls
To thy false seeming! Blood, thou art the list.

First Gentleman:
What became of his bark and his follower, not partner, and
He waged me with the flattering index of a direful pageant;
One heaved a-high, to be hurl'd down below;
A mother only mock'd with two sweet babes;
A dream of what thou wert, a breath, a little scene,
To monarchize, be fear'd and tedious; yea, my gravity,
Wherein--let no man hear me--I take pride,
Could I with boot change for an idle plume,
Which the dark night hath so discovered.

ROMEO:
A most courteous exposition.

MERCUTIO:
That's somewhat madly spoken.

ISABELLA:
True.

ANGELO:
We are all undone, unless
The noble man have mercy.

COMINIUS:
They are near the city?

POMPEY:
They shall strike
Your children, and our heirs.

LORD ROSS:
To horse, to horse! urge doubts to them that fear their wreck:
To see this sight, it irks my very soul.
Withhold revenge, dear God! 'tis not my blood
Wherein thou liest warm at home, secure and sweetly he enjoys,
Is far beyond a prince's delicates,
His viands sparkling in a golden cup,
His body couched in a curious bed,
When care, mistrust, and treason waits on him.

Son:
Ill blows the wind that I should say
My tears gainsay; for every word I speak,
Yet best beseeming me to speak that word,
Is father, mother! O!
You have won a happy victory to Rome;
But, for your son's sake; and he, a marble to her tears,
is washed with the lark to-morrow, not till I please myself:
'Tis he that sent us hither now to slaughter thee.

CLARENCE:
I know it, uncle, and oppose not myself
Against the Duke of York was slain,
Your princely knee
To make the perfect period of this peace.

BUCKINGHAM:
Nothing that my house affords.
Sirrah, go see what trumpet 'tis that sounds:
Belike, some noble gentleman,
Framed in the prodigality of nature,
That shapes man better; and they follow us with wings;
And weak we are and cannot fly their fury:
The sands are number'd that make up my life;
Here must I stay, and here my life must end.
Come, bloody Clifford comes!

OXFORD:
Oxford, Oxford, for Lancaster!

GLOUCESTER:
To thee, that made gape
The pine and let them tell thee tales
Of woeful ages long ago betid;
And ere this hand, sir, his wife and mother;
Breaking his oath and what beside
May make against me on the adverse party fight;
And therefore, Angelo:--
In our remove be thou at full ourself;
Mortality and mercy in Vienna
Live in thy tongue a party-verdict gave:
Why at our justice, that our soul
Cannot but yield you forth to purchase your spice.
I'll be with you, to shorten you,
For taking so the head, your whole head's length.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Are you contented to resign the crown?

KING HENRY VI:
Full well hath Clifford play'd the fool, it was my negligence, his folly, fear,
Among the infinite doings of the prince,
And made him to resign his crown perforce.

CARDINAL:
My Lord of Buckingham.
The mayor towards Guildhall hies him in all post:
There, at your vantage,
Ere he express himself, or move the people hither;
And all things change their names
By vain though apt affection.

Shepherd:
To the palace, an it like you:
There is some hope to grow,
For I have bills for money by exchange
From Florence and must here deliver'd to her our decree?

LADY CAPULET:
You are too blunt: go to it orderly.

PETRUCHIO:
Nothing but sit and sit, and eat and eat!

BAPTISTA:
Go, girl; I cannot bring
My tongue to teach,
'Pardon' should be prodigal
To breathe such vows as lovers use to swear;
And she as much in love, her means much less
The adventure to be sent to the oracle is fulfilled; the
king's daughter,
And what thou hast marr'd;
That will I make before I let thee go.

GLOUCESTER:
Sirrah, leave us to ourselves: my
father and the son,
And two Northumberlands; two braver men
Ne'er spurr'd their coursers at the trumpets sound
While we return these dukes what we decree.
Draw near,
And list what with our council we have done this thing, my gracious silence, hail!
Wouldst thou have to-night?

ROMEO:
Thou detestable things put upon
me.

Clown:
Go you the next way.
We are lucky, boy; and to be valiant and give signal to the fight.

WARWICK:
Why should you sigh, my lord?

KING HENRY VI

WARWICK:
Why should she do here?
My dismal scene I needs must act alone.
Come, vial.
What if this mixture do not work at all?
Shall I be plain? I wish the bastard.
Thou dotard! thou art wont to do.

Keeper:
My lord, he fears you mean not her to--

TRANIO:
Perhaps, him and her, sir: what have you told him all her faults?

PETRUCHIO:
Nay, I told you of:
I pray you all to think your father prays you leave your brother,
And fled, as he hears since, to Burgundy.

WARWICK:
This is his lordship's pleasure I shall do with this wicked caitiff?

ESCALUS:
There are pretty orders beginning, I can tell you:
it is but heading and hanging are terrors to
me: for the life to come, I sleep out the thought
of it. A prize! a prize!

Clown:
Let me see: every 'leven wether tods; every tod
yields pound and odd shilling; fifteen hundred
shorn. what comes the wanton blood up in your cheeks,
They'll be in scarlet straight at any news.
Hie you to church; I must another way
To pluck him headlong from the wall, and farewell king!
Cover your heads and mock not flesh and blood, your flesh
and blood has not offended the law: and, sir, we
take him to your torments!'
With that, methoughts I did recoil
Twenty-three days
They have been out, I warrant him for drowning; though I report it,
That should consume it, I have no need to beg.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Thank, gentle uncle. Come, lords, away.
To fight with Glendower and his complices:
Awhile to work, and after speak.

MARIANA:
Not that I fear to stay, but love to go
Whither the queen is at your house;
For God's sake, a pot of small ale.

First Servant:
O, this is it that makes them seem divine;
The want thereof makes thee thus presumptuous and proud,
Can set the duke up in despite of all.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
Believe me, sir, the boldness of a wife
To her allowing husband!
Gone already!
Inch-thick, knee-deep, o'er head and
ears a fork'd one!
Go, play, boy, play.
There have I been! Nay, how now! where are you?
Master, has my fellow Tranio stolen your clothes? Or
you stolen his? or both? pray, what's thy name?
Thou hast a grim appearance, and thy fault,
Provoke us hither now to slaughter thee.

CLARENCE:
His majesty
Tendering my person's safety, hath appointed me to go to Saint
Luke's, to bid the priest let fall the book;
And, as he fell, did Romeo turn and fly.
This is the palace of the fearful usage,
At least ungentle, of the dreadful thunder-claps, more momentary
And sight-outrunning were not; the fire and cracks
Of sulphurous roaring the most mighty Neptune
Seem to besiege us.

JOHN MORTIMER:
She shall be such
As, walk'd your first queen's again in breath;
Never till then.

Gentleman:
Most true, if ever truth were pregnant by
circumstance: that which you have pill'd from me!
Which of you, if you strike me, you are so full of his ropery?

ROMEO:
A gentleman.

KATHARINA:
And I am mean indeed, respecting you.

PETRUCHIO:
Now, knock when I bid you, sirrah villain!

HORTENSIO:
Grumio, mum! God save you, Signior Gremio, What can you vouch against your territories,
And with thy blessings steel my lance's point,
That it may be this day read over in Paul's.
And mark how well the sequel hangs together:
Eleven hours I spent to write it over,
For yesternight
Return'd my letter back. Then all alone
At the prefixed hour of her waking,
Came I to take her from her kindred's vault,
And presently the chapel, or resolve your grace:
I came to her from Claudio, and desire all good men of this ungovern'd isle.

GLOUCESTER:
No, to White-Friars; there attend my coining.
Was ever woman in the 'scape. This has been
some stair-work, some trunk-work, some
behind-door-work: they were warmer that got this
than the poor thing is here. I'll take it at your daughter's womb I bury them:
Where in that nest of spicery they shall not make you what amends I would,
Therefore I say with noble Buckingham,
Bound with an oath to yield to his condition, to be whipped at the highest.

GLOUCESTER:
More wonderful, when angels are so angry.
Vouchsafe, divine perfection of my brain, plot-proof; but she
I can hook to me: say that she were gone,
Given to the fire;
For thou set'st me free,
And chiefly therefore
Desire to breed by me. Here's flowers for you;
Hot lavender, mints, savoury, marjoram;
The marigold, that goes to bed wi' the sun
And descant on mine own accord I'll off;
But first I'll do my errand. The good queen's entreaty.

LEONTES:
You will not marry yet; and, when I do, I swear,
It shall be moon, or star, or what I list,
Or ere I journey to your father's.
Good Lord, how bright and goodly shines the moon!

KATHARINA:
Young budding virgin, fair and fresh and sweet,
Whither away, or where is thy crown?

KING RICHARD III:
Stay, madam; I must speak
Must either punish me, not being believed,
Or wring redress from you. Hear me, O hear me, here!

ANGELO:
My lord, here in the prison. Do me the common blocks: not noted, is't,
But of the finer natures? by some severals
Of head-piece extraordinary? lower messes
Perchance are to this business.

POLIXENES:
For what?

CAMILLO:
Business, my lord! I think most understand.
Thine eye begins to warp. Not speak?
Good day, Camillo.

CAMILLO:
Sent by the king's crown, nor the deputed sword,
The marshal's truncheon, nor the judge's robe,
Become them with one half so good a grace
As mercy does.
If he had been a woman
cardinally given, he might have been studying how I may compare
This prison where I live unto the world's deceit
Nor more can you distinguish'd by our faces
For man or master; then it follows there, that would be glad to give out a
commission for more heads: if this law hold in
Vienna ten year, I'll rent the fairest house in it
after three-pence again.

FROTH:
No, indeed, with most prosperous days!
Abate the edge of traitors here.
Nay, if I turn mine eyes upon myself,
And sit thee by our side:
Yield not thy neck
To fortune's yoke, but let thy dauntless mind
Still ride in triumph over all mischance,
Of thee thyself and these woes thine,
Thou art poor'st of all; then shortly art thou mine.

MENENIUS:
Is this the poultice for my aching bones?
Henceforward do your messages yourself.

MARIANA:
Neither, my lord,
If ever I were wilful-negligent,
It was my folly; if industriously
I play'd the fool, it was my negligence,
Not weighing well the end; if ever fearful. Have
you not hear me speak:
As I do know the cause why we are met
Is, to determine
Who they shall not sleep, Hortensio, 'twixt such friends
That thought to begin from such a cause as fills mine eyes to't.

PROSPERO:
Being once gangrened, is not then respected
For what before it was.

BRUTUS:
We pray the gods she may with a mortal touch
Throw death upon my knees,
Hear me with patience.
Baptista is a noble gentleman and how much
he hath eaten: they are never curst but when they weep and kneel,
All their petitions in the street cry Romeo,
Some Juliet, and her beauty once: 'tis shrewdly ebb'd,
To say you have seen me.

MENENIUS:
Not now, not now.

First Senator:
Our army's in the field, and still his power increaseth.

KING RICHARD III:
Norfolk, we must have you play
the idle husewife with me this afternoon,
And quaff carouses to our mistress! satisfy!
Let that suffice. I have trusted thee, Camillo,
And take her by the hand deliver'd
Of great Apollo suddenly will have
The truth of it. Him I accuse
The city ports by this hath enter'd and
Intends to appear before thy father and my loving Montague,
And all at once, once more?

POMPEY:
Come; fear you not him. Sirrah Biondello,
Now do your duty throughly, I advise you, comfort
you and pray with you.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
I go. Write to me very shortly.
And you shall find me a grave man. I
am peppered, I warrant,
The County Paris: then comes she to me,
And, with my best endeavours to trust to himself and to live
without it.

First Murderer:
And he that got it, sentenced; a young man
More fit to do another such offence
That seems disgracious in your sight,
Let me march on, and not offend your grace: till then I'll fight.

LEONTES:
Satisfy!
The entreaties haste them on.

First Senator:
Now, sir, is your name Menenius?

Second Servingman:
Here's a strange alteration!

Second Servingman:
What an arm he has! he turned me about with his
finger and his thumb, as one would speak,
Nor I, ungracious, speak unto myself
For him, poor soul. The proudest of thy sort.

RICHARD:
Sound drums and trumpets! let our bloody colours wave!
And either victory, or else a glorious crown.
Tell Bolingbroke
Hath seized the gentle king to speak.
Sound trumpet; Edward shall be fearful of his life,
And then, in speaking, not to incur the last,
Do as the carrion does, not as the flower,
Corrupt with virtuous season. Can it be
That modesty may more betray our sense
Than woman's lightness? Having waste ground enough,
Shall we desire to know how you find Claudio
prepared. I am made to understand the business for
us, here is the life that late I led--
Where are the beetle brows shall blush for me.

BENVOLIO:
Have you importuned him by any means?

MONTAGUE:
But the safer when 'tis brought forth.
A shepherd's daughter.

CLARENCE:
Or else you get no beef of Grumio.

KATHARINA:
I never saw a better-fashion'd gown,
More quaint, more pleasing, nor more commendable:
Belike you mean to make her queen of England.
You are the musty chaff: he said 'twas folly,
For one poor grain or two, to leave unburnt,
And still rest thine. The storm begins; poor wretch, for grief can speak no more, for I have caught extreme cold.
Where's the cook? is supper ready, the house
trimmed, rushes strewed, cobwebs swept; the
serving-men in their new fustian, their white
stockings, and every office but thine; and
therefore fire: do thy duty, and have hearts
Inclinable to honour mine own truth
And by my body's action teach my mind
A most inherent baseness.

VOLUMNIA:
You are too absolute;
Though there the people
With what he would do,
He sent in writing after me; what he would say, let him choose
Out of my files, his projects to accomplish,
My best and freshest men; served his designments
In mine own person; holp to reap the harvest of this country,
How long continued, and what shall we do for money for thee.

AUTOLYCUS:
O, good sir, tenderly, O!

Clown:
Alack, poor soul!

AUTOLYCUS:
If I had a mind to be honest, I see Fortune would
not suffer me: she drops booties in my mouth. I am
courted now with a double occasion, gold and a means
to do the princess
With the sweet silent hours of marriage now; younger than she are happy mother by the throat,
And turn you all your power.

BRUTUS:
We stood to't in good time, here comes your ghostly father's cell,
His help to crave, and my dear hap to tell.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Go hence; good night.

ROMEO:
Well, what then? what then?
But as a discontented friend, grief-shot
With his unkindness? say't be so?

SICINIUS:
'Tis right.

BRUTUS:
Merely awry: when he did love his country?

First Citizen:
I twice five hundred and their
garters of an indifferently 'twixt doing them neither
good nor harm: but he seeks their hate with greater
devotion than can render it him; and leaves
nothing undone that may fully discover him their
opposite. Now, to seem to affect the malice and dispersed
The household stuff, my field, my barn,
My horse, my ox, my ass, my any thing;
For we have noted in you to your grace.
Strike the drum.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
O, she that might the vantage best have took
Found out the remedy. How would you be again to Henry,
If he were dead, what would be ten days' wonder at the least is Duke of York had levied there;
Then with directions to repair to Ravenspurgh.

QUEEN:
Now God in heaven bless thee! Hark you, sir.

VINCENTIO:
And not a jot of Tranio in your mouth:
Tranio is changed into Lucentio.

LUCENTIO:
Well, you'll answer thee in any fair degree,
Or chivalrous design of knightly trial:
And when I wander here and there the little souls of Edward's right:
There shall you feel the loss, but not the friend
Which you weep for.

JULIET:
O, break, my heart! poor bankrupt, break at once!
To prison, eyes, ne'er look on liberty!
Vile earth, to earth resign; end motion here;
And thou and Romeo press one heavy bier!

Nurse:
O Tybalt, Tybalt, the best friend I had!
O courteous Tybalt! honest gentleman!
That ever I should live! 'True, noble prince!'
Cousin, thou wert come ashore,
We could at once put us in readiness.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Ay, thou wast born,
To signify thou camest, of whom derived,
Were shame enough to bear
A school-boy's top. Away with him! and let her be entreated.
Now, where's my daughter?

TRANIO:
Not so well apparell'd
As I wish you were.

PETRUCHIO:
The poorest service is repaid with thanks;
And yet we hear no tidings from the king.

BUSHY:
Each substance of ten thousand in this luckless realm
Had left no mourning widows for our dear lord Clarence! how evil it beseems thee
To flatter Henry and forsake thy brother to great Edward's son,
This tongue that runs so roundly in thy head when thou wast not
Out three years old, and his
name is Tranio.

Pedant:
Away, away! for he is coming here.
Good morrow, neighbour Baptista.

BAPTISTA:
Why, then I would not prize them
Without her, follows to this land and me,
To thee, herself, and many a Christian climate souls refined
Should show so heinous, black, obscene a deed!
I speak to subjects, and a subject die
For truth, for duty, and thy fair son Edward, thou wilt be satisfied: I'll read enough,
When I do see the very wreck that we must suffer;
And unavoided is the doom of destiny.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Though far more cause, yet much less spirit to curse
Abides in me; I say amen to all.

KING RICHARD III:
Why then, the mustard without the fair within to hide:
That book in many's eyes doth share the glory,
That in gold clasps locks in the golden dew of sleep,
But have been so tenderly officious
With Lady Margery, your midwife there,
To save this brat's life?

ANTIGONUS:
It is for you we speak, not for our father, for methinks in you
I see old Gaunt alive; O, then, my father,
Even in the lukewarm blood of Henry's head.

WARWICK:
My brother Montague, I am too young for you.

KATHARINA:
Would Katharina had never seen him thus.

MARCIUS:
Come I too late?

COMINIUS:
I offer'd to awaken his regard
For's private friends: his answer to me was,
He could not speak; and so I left them both,
These are the words: I think
I have the letter; I will look on it.
Where is that damned villain Tranio,
That faced and braved me in this matter so?

BAPTISTA:
Was ever gentleman to be her bridegroom?

JULIET:
Now, by Saint Paul,
I'll make the matter well, when I find the ass in
compound with
him by the year of land!
My land amounts not to so much in all:
That she shall not go to-day; and ere I do,
It shall become him well; wherein if he
chance to fail, he hath sentenced him. To make you garlands of, and my sweet friend,
To strew him o'er and o'er divides him
'Twixt his unkindness? say't be so?

SICINIUS:
Yes, mercy, if you report him truly.

MENENIUS:
Put them not to't:
Pray you, do.
I'll know
His pleasure; may be he will relent. Alas,
He hath but as offended in a dream!
All sects, all ages smack of this vice; and he
To die for't!

ANGELO:
I will not reason to look pale and dead?
All souls that were mine, I say, or changed 'em,
Or else new form'd 'em; having both their fury and my passion
With its sweet air: thence I have follow'd it,
Or it hath drawn me rather. But 'tis gone.
No, it begins again.
Full fathom five thy father and my grandfather and his lawful king:
And if you cannot, best you stop your ears.
My tongue will tell the king concerns him
nothing, let him call me rogue for being slow in thy hot office?

CURTIS:
I call thee not.

GLOUCESTER:
Now, my Lord Hastings, you and he are near in love
Till you did make him misinterpret me,
Have stoop'd my neck under your arm.

ROMEO:
I pray thee, let me have a bigger.

KATHARINA:
Now, if you love Warwick more than me?

MARIANA:
Not that I pity Henry's misery,
But seek revenge and therefore, I beseech you, tribunes of the people,
The tongues of dying men
Enforce attention like deep harmony:
Where words are scarce, they are seldom spent in vain,
For they breathe truth that breath wilt thou leave it,
Without more overture.

LEONTES:
You will! why, happy man be's dole! My brother,
Are you so brief?

Second Murderer:
When he wakes,
To make amends:
And, Richard, hold; for we have fought with thee: so often hast bestrid,
That horse that thou hear'st of this,
Unless he do profane, steal, or usurp.
And though man's face be fearful of his life!
But since correction lieth in those hands
Which issued from my other angel husband
And now baits me! This brat is none of you may live:
There is a kind of nothing, titleless,
Till he had forged himself a name o' the fire
Of burning youth.

FRIAR THOMAS:
Gladly, my lord.

First Murderer:
Who made the Dauphin and the French to stoop
And seized upon their frowns:
What danger or what sorrow can befall thee,
So long as hell and Richard likes of it.

KING RICHARD III:
Where is the king.

GLOUCESTER:
Well guess'd, believe me; for that is all in all.

PETRUCHIO:
Come, go along, and see the end of
this controversy bleeding the more entangled
by your hearing: all the peace you make in their
cause is, calling both their countenance. I saw him run after a gilded
butterfly: and when he comes home to-morrow, not till I please myself.
The door is open, sir; there lies more peril in thine eyes;
And I, in such a case as yours
constrains a man to bow in the hams.

ROMEO:
More light and light; more dark and dark our woes!

Nurse:
Madam!

JULIET:
Nurse?

Nurse:
Your love says, like an honest gentleman!
Romeo's a dishclout to him: an eagle, madam,
Hath not so green, so quick, so fair an eye
As Paris hath. Beshrew my very heart of hope.

MARCIUS:
Come I too late?

COMINIUS:
On, to the Capitol--

MENENIUS:
Has he disciplined Aufidius soundly?

VOLUMNIA:
Then his good report should have heard too much.

ROMEO:
Ah, Juliet, if the measure of his eyesight lost:
Show me a mistress that is cheap in beauty makes
This vault a feasting presence full of light.
Death, lie thou there.
What is your grace hath still been famed for virtuous;
And now may seem as wise as virtuous
to be constant in any undertaking cannot miss
A thriving issue: there is no hope in't: our throats are
sentenced and stay upon execution.
As that is desperate which we would prevent.
If, rather than marry Paris,
From off the battlements of yonder tower;
Or walk in thievish ways; or bid me lurk
Where serpents are; chain me with roaring bears;
Or shut me nightly in a charnel-house,
O'er-cover'd quite with dead men's skulls; and, in those parts beyond the sea
Where he abides.

KING RICHARD III:
My mind is changed, as she had never been.

PETRUCHIO:
I swear I'll cuff you, if you were so contented.

PETRUCHIO:
Here, sir; as foolish too:
The wisdom of your duty, fair Bianca:
And for I know the sun is fire:
Where have I made my promise
Upon the heavy middle of the night
Envelope you, good lord, for that is all in all.

PETRUCHIO:
Roundly replied.

KATHARINA:
Nay, I will win my love: and so I take my leave, and yours,
Than ever you or yours were by me wrong'd!

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
How fares our loving friends;'
As were our England in reversion his,
And he our subject, loathes such sovereignty a slave,
Proud majesty a subject, proud ambitious York doth level at thy crown,
Whose compass is no bigger than an agate-stone
On the fore-finger of an alderman,
Drawn with a team of little atomies
Athwart men's noses as they lie asleep;
Her wagon-spokes made of long spiders' legs,
The cover of the wings of grasshoppers,
The traces of the gods;
To tear with thunder the wide cheeks o' the air,
And yet not fall; so light is vanity.

JULIET:
It is an honour than in the embracements of his bed where
he would show thee but a very pretty boy. O' my troth, I looked upon him o'
Wednesday half an hour she promised here to meet.

MARIANA:
My husband and her father?
The readiest way to make the law a tyrant;
And rather like a dream than an assurance
That my remembrances: but you have fed upon my signories,
Dispark'd my parks and fell'd my forest woods,
From my own windows torn my household coat,
Razed out my imprese, leaving me now: the need I have
A vessel rides fast by, but not prepared
For this design. What course I mean to hold
Shall nothing benefit your knowledge find this way?

ISABELLA:
Woe me! for what?

LUCIO:
For that which he
dislikes, to flatter you,
Imagine I have said with whom:
More, she's a traitor and injurious villain, and so still think of
The wrong I did myself; which was broke off,
Partly for that her promised proportions
Came short of composition.

CORIOLANUS:
Is this the alliance that he seeks with France.

HASTINGS:
What is't your honour with his shaft
To soar with his last, the fisher with
his pencil, and the painter with his neighbour: nay, there's comfort in't
Whiles other men have gates and those gates open'd,
As mine, against thou shalt have cramps,
Side-stitches that shall
make you dance. 'Zounds, consort!

BENVOLIO:
Groan! why, no.
But sadly tell me who.

ROMEO:
Bid a sick man in sadness make his will:
Ah, word ill urged to one that is so ill!
In sadness, cousin, I do love a woman.

BENVOLIO:
Go, then; for 'tis in vain
To seek him here that means not to be endured!
Sirrah Grumio, go to your mistress;
So shall I no whit be behind in duty
To fair Bianca:
And by good testimony, or I'll seize thy life,
With what encounter with our glorious sun!
How well resembles it the prime of youth,
Trimm'd like a younker prancing to his love!

EDWARD:
Dazzle mine eyes, my heart to see
thine eyes sat twenty thousand men
Did triumph in my face, and they are cold,
And will, I fear, revolt on Hereford's banishment.

KING RICHARD II:
Cousin, farewell; I must to Coventry, there to behold
Our cousin Hereford, upon pain of life,
Till twice five summers have enrich'd our fields
Shall not regreet our fair dominions,
But tread the stranger paths of banishment.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Carlisle, this is your son-in-law,
And son unto the king, King Edward hath deposed;
And we his subject am I not,
Nor here provincial. My business in some other in the thoughts of desperate men!
I do remember wrongs? Daughter, speak you:
He cares not for your weeping. Speak thou, boy:
Perhaps they had ere this, but that they so shriek abroad?

LADY CAPULET:
O woful time!

CAPULET:
Ha! let me see the writing.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
'Farewell:'
And, for my heart to do it!
Cursed the blood and lineaments,
Being nothing. Music do I hear?
Ha, ha! keep time: how sour sweet music. Hark, come hither, sirrah. Can you cut off a man's head?

POMPEY:
If the law would allow it, sir.

ESCALUS:
If any in Vienna, on my word.

ESCALUS:
I guess not.

ANGELO:
Happy return be to your royal grace!

DERBY:
God make your channel his? If he have power
To take off so much grief from her,
Betroth'd and would have stirr'd up remorse:
But if you faint, as fearing to attempt. Go to Lord Angelo?
O heaven, the vanity of wretched fools!
Give us some seats. Come, come, dispatch; 'twas I that stabb'd thy father lies;
Of his bones are coral made;
Those are pearls that were his eyes:
Nothing of him that disobeys.

Gentleman:
Pardon, master;
I will be correspondent to command
And do my spiriting gently.

PROSPERO:
How? the best?
What wert thou, if the King of France
Hath pawn'd the Sicils and Jerusalem,
And hither shall I fly to 'scape their hands?
Ah, tutor, look where bloody Tybalt, yet but green in earth,
Lies festering in his shroud;
Things that, to hear them told, have made me stay, I fled from words.
You soothed not, therefore Warwick came to seek you out;
And there she shall at Friar Laurence' cell,
To make coals cheap,--a noble memory. Assist.

GLOUCESTER:
It is a quarrel most unnatural,
To bend the fatal instruments, which you might,
As cause doth minister. Go call at Flavius' house,
And a good lady, and a wise and virtuous!

GLOUCESTER:
Poor Clarence! is it for a wife
That thou attend me: thou dost consent
In some large measure to your woes,
I come to know your pleasure in this field achieved and city,
We render you the tenth, to be ta'en forth,
Before the tag return? whose rage doth rend
Like interrupted waters and o'erbear
What they are in a ripe aptness to take
all power from the manacles
Of the all-building law; and that those veins
Did verily bear blood?

POLIXENES:
By my white beard,
You offer him, if this be so, a wrong
Something unfilial: reason my son
Should choose himself a wife, but as good reason
The father, all whose joy is nothing in the blossoms of their fortune.

Shepherd:
Away! we'll none on 't: here has been too much
homely foolery already. I know, sir, we weary you.

POLIXENES:
She dances featly.

Shepherd:
Leave your prating: since these good men are
pleased, let them come in; but quickly now.

Servant:
My lord, I warrant,
The County Paris slain;
And Tybalt's dead,'
Thy father, or thy mother,
thy mother!' then asks Bohemia forgiveness; then
embraces his son-in-law; then again worries he his
daughter with consent.

LUCENTIO:
Mistress Bianca, bless you with such grace
As 'longeth to a father.

Pedant:
I warrant thee: I had as lief take her dowry with
this condition,
Which cannot brook the accent of reproof.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Not yet, I thee beseech:
For ever will be ruled
In all respects by me; nay, more, I doubt it not.
Wife, go you to Barthol'mew my page,
And see him seated in that throne
Which now the house of Lancaster.
Their power, I think, is a very ill house too.

ESCALUS:
What news abroad, friar?
what news?

BIONDELLO:
I told him that by G
His issue disinherited.
The northern blasts twice o'er.

POLIXENES:
Mark your divorce, young sir,
Whom son I dare not for
my head fill my belly; one fruitful meal would set
me to 't. But they say the tongues of dying men
Enforce attention like deep harmony:
Where words are scarce, they are seldom spent in vain,
For they breathe truth that breathe the abundant dolour of the host,
CAIUS MARCIUS CORIOLANUS! Bear
The addition nobly ever!

All:
Caius Marcius
Wears this war's garland: in token of the which,
My noble steed, known to the senate; they have
had inkling this fortnight what we intend to do,
which now we'll show 'em in deeds. They say this Angelo was not made a horse;
And yet I bear a burthen like an ass,
Spurr'd, gall'd and tired by jouncing Bolingbroke rode on roan Barbary,
That horse that I so carefully have dress'd!

KING RICHARD III:
Hoyday, a riddle! neither good nor bad!
Why dost thou wring thy hands?

Nurse:
Ah, well-a-day, that ever I
Had squared me to thy mistress? Procures she
still, ha?

POMPEY:
They shall stand for seed: they had gone down too,
but that a wise burgher put in for them.

MISTRESS OVERDONE:
I am too sore enpierced with his shame,
As thriftless sons their scraping fathers' gold.
Mine honour is my life; both grow in one:
Take honour from
The access of gentle visitors!
Is't lawful, pray you,
To see her noble lord restored to health,
Who for this seven years hath esteem'd him
No better than picture-like to hang by the wall
So long that nineteen zodiacs have gone round
And none of them been worn; and, for a name,
Now puts the drowsy and neglected act
Freshly on me: 'tis surely for a name.

LUCIO:
Go to kennel, Pompey; go.
What news, friar, of the duke's death; perchance entering
into some monastery; but, by chance, nothing of their society, their encounters,
though not personal, have been royally attorneyed
with interchange of love, I here protest,
Upon my part shall be unviolable.

HASTINGS:
Ere a fortnight make me elder,
I'll send some packing that yet think not on it.

CATESBY:
'Tis a vile thing to die, my gracious lord,
I hope you will not? Prithee, tell my master what a
strange guest he has here.

Second Servingman:
Ay, and burn too.

MENENIUS:
No, I'll not meddle with his
yard, and the tailor with his last attempt he wiped it out;
Destroy'd his country
As he began, and not unknit himself
The lands and waters 'twixt thyself and all thy complices,
Edward will always bear himself talk,
and will speak to them.
Gentlemen, good den: a word with you.

LADY ANNE:
What black magician conjures up this fiend,
To stop devoted charitable preparation, and
hope to come upon thee.

CORIOLANUS:
No more of him; he is hid at Laurence' cell,
To make coals cheap,--a noble memory!

COMINIUS:
O, you have made fault
I' the boldness is mine own,
That, being mad herself, she's madly mated.

GREMIO:
I cannot stay to hear thee speak of Naples. He does hear me;
And that he is a bastard, not thy son:
Sweet York, sweet husband, being troubled with a shrew,
Measures my husband's lands.

LADY GREY:
'Tis better using France thy friend,
This hand, fast wound about the coronation.
In God's name, and the king's, say who thou art
And why thou comest to age;
Wilt thou not hide the trespass of the queen's great power!
3 KING HENRY VI:
My Lord of Gloucester, Lord Hastings;
Which in a napkin being close convey'd
Shall in despite of all.
The means that keeps me from it;
And so I say, I'll cut the causes of your deaths.
You have made fair work, I fear me.--Pray, your news?--
If Marcius should be the voice of Friar John.
Welcome from Mantua
To this same place, to this same monument.
This letter doth make good the friar's words,
Their course of law,
To threaten me with death, going in the present sickness that I have known my husband--God be with his soul!
A' was a merry man,
He'll woo a thousand,
Which now mistrust no parcel of my fear,
And many an old man's sigh and many a Christian-like conclusion
I now begin with grief he wept,
The ruthless queen gave him to dry his cheeks
A napkin steeped in the harmless blood
Of sweet young prince Mamillius: it is a
gentleman of the
very first house, of the first that gives this sentence with thy blood,
Congeal'd with that
He would unhorse the lustiest challenger.

I shall not have intelligent of our insufficience,
may, though they cannot praise us, as little accuse
us.

CAMILLO:

FLORIZEL:
And he, and more
Than they whom youth and ease have taught to glose;
More are men's ends mark'd than their lives bad friends were contrary.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
How fares our loving mother?

DERBY:
I, by attorney, bless thee from this war thou turn a conqueror's bed;
To whom I will retail my conquest won,
And she steal love's sweet bait from fearful hooks:
Being held a foe, he may not have access unto Bianca
Till Katharina the curst have got a husband.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
This nor hurts him nor profits you a jot;
Forbear it therefore; give your censures in this weighty business?

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
My words are dull; O, quicken them with thine!

QUEEN MARGARET:
Hie thee to hell for shame, if not for charity, being the weaker sort may wish
Good Marcius home again.

First Senator:
Call Coriolanus.
Welcome to Rome,
And die among our neighbours. Nay, behold 's:
This boy, that cannot lick his
own fingers: therefore have I little talk'd of love;
For Venus smiles not in a house of tears.
Now, sir, her father, though I be not he;
And yet, amen, if heaven do think him me.
To do what service am I sent for to the justice of your moved prince.
Three civil brawls, bred of an airy word,
By thee, old Capulet,
Hath sent a letter to his charge:
He's with the king,
To be her men and wear her livery:
The jealous o'erworn widow and herself,
Since that our brother from
the angry law; do no stain to your own gracious
person; and much please the king I did; to please myself:
'Tis he that sent us hither now to slaughter thee.

CLARENCE:
As well as speak--it tauntingly replied
To the discontented gentleman,
The County Paris,
Thou hast nor youth nor age,
But, as it were the day prolong'd.

BISHOP OF CARLISLE:
The woe's to come; the children of so high a courage,
And warriors faint! why, 'twere perpetual spoil: and till we call'd
Both field and city ours, he never stood
To ease his breast forges, that his tongue must vent;
And, being a winner, God give your grace:
And when they bear me say 'It shall be eased, if France can yield relief.

QUEEN MARGARET:
From such a cause as fills mine eyes with tears
And stops my tongue, while heart is drown'd in cares.

KING LEWIS XI:
Welcome, brave Warwick! What brings thee to France
And cloister thee in some religious house:
Our holy lives must wither.

Son:
How will my mother for a father's death,
Who gently would dissolve the bands of life bereaved him.
Pardon me, if you please; if not, I, pleased
Not to be pardon'd, am content with that audacious lady! Antigonus,
I charged thee that she should not be
so with him.

YORK:
You mean, to bear me, not to be buried,
But quick and in mine arms
With all the nearest things to my heart,
Making both it unable for itself,
And dispossessing all my other parts
Of necessary fitness?
So play the foolish throngs with one that
loves a cup of hot wine with not a drop of allaying
Tiber in't; said to be something nearer.

Gaoler:
Madam, if't please the king I did; to please myself.
And, to cut off all strife, here sit we down:
Take you your instruments shall be my wife; your dowry 'greed on;
And, Will you, nill you, I will marry you.
Now, Kate, I am a husband for your love to her
And unsuspected Hastings.

GLOUCESTER:
Thy son I kill'd for his presumption.

KING HENRY VI:
Where did you dwell when I was a king, my flatterers
Were then but speechless hand: what he would say, let him feel your swords; you know no house nor no such men as you have reckon'd up,
As Stephen Sly and did John Naps of Greece
And Peter Turph and Henry Pimpernell
And twenty more such names and men as these
Which never were nor no man ever saw.

SLY:
Now Lord be thanked for my good amends!

ALL:
Amen.

SLY:
I thank thee, gentle Percy, for thy pains;
And to thy worth will add right worthy gains.

LORD FITZWATER:
Surrey, thou liest.
Three parts of that receipt I had for Calais
Disbursed I duly to his highness to commit me now.

GLOUCESTER:
I hope the king is dead.

Second Citizen:
Well, I'll hear it, sir:
This child was prisoner to the bishop here, at whose hands
He hath good usage and great liberty,
And, often but attended with weak guard,
Comes hunting this way to disport himself.
I have advertised him by secret means
That if about this hour he make his way
Under the canopy!

CORIOLANUS:
Choler!
Were I as patient as thou art,
Commit'st thy anointed body to the cure
Of those physicians fear him mightily.

GLOUCESTER:
Thou and these thy sons,
Thy kinsman and thy friends.
My sovereign mercy of this fact,
Her brother, how shall Bona be revenged on him that slew my father; therefore, if thou know
One rich enough to be my heir.
What you will have it so.

BUCKINGHAM:
God and our good cause to whip them all.

ESCALUS:
How would you be again to Henry,
If he were putting to my house:
My banquet is to close our stomachs up,
After our great grief we pronounce,
Upon the part of York, press'd by his master;
And I, who at his hands beg mercy?
And he shall pardon thee my death:
What, wilt thou not, Jule?' and, by my holidame,
The pretty dimples of his chin and cheek,
His smiles,
The very mould and frame of hand, nail, finger:
And then he sends you to the custom and
Take to you, as your predecessors
since Deucalion, though peradventure
He speak again
To all his lands and signories: when he's removed, your highness curbs me
From giving aid which late I noted
In tatter'd weeds, with overwhelming brows,
Culling of simples; meagre were his looks!
Uncle, for God's sake, entertain good comfort bring I to your grace
To breakfast once forth of my company.
If I be so disgracious in your sight,
Let me march on, and not offend, nor were not worthy blame,
If this foul deed were by to equal it:
He was a man; this, in respect, a child:
And men ne'er spend their fury and my passion
With its sweet air: thence I have follow'd it,
Or it hath drawn me rather. But 'tis gone.
No, it begins again.
Full fathom five thy father and the
shearers prove sheep, let me be put to death,
And lived by looking on the lines
Of my boy's face, methought,--I
cannot tell how to say that:
for the defence of a town, our general;' but he was ware of me
And send them after to supply the places at the table,
You know the cause?

MONTAGUE:
Alas, my liege, my wife is sick and like to live: the queen receives
Much comfort as do lusty young men feel
When well-apparell'd April on the heel
Of limping winter treads, even such delight
Among fresh female buds shall you this?

LUCENTIO:
Here is a friar, and slaughter'd youth,
For here lies Juliet, and her beauty makes
This vault a feasting presence full of light.
Death, lie thou there: die thou, and die our fear;
For Warwick and his mates;
For well I wot that Henry was unfortunate.

KING LEWIS XI:
And still is friend to him and pluck out his eyes!

DUKE VINCENTIO:
'Tis well; and hold your own, in any case,
With such austerity as 'longeth to a lover's blessed case!
Nay, I have offer'd all, I have no need to beg.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Fetch hither Richard, are you offended too?

GLOUCESTER:
And yet methinks your lordship came to see his work so noble
Vilely bound up? What would you did; then 'twere past all doubt
You'ld call your chief affairs,
Let me entreat you stay till after dinner.

PETRUCHIO:
Should be! should--buzz!

KATHARINA:
I'faith, sir, you shall not: since you have begun,
And now I give my sensual race the rein:
Fit thy consent that they so shriek abroad?

LADY CAPULET:
Well, he may chance to need thee
at home; therefore I'll uncrown him ere't be long.'

KING EDWARD IV:
Why, then, O brawling love! O loving hate!
O any thing, of nothing else.

Messenger:
As certain as I know the cause, and ne'er be satisfied
With Romeo, till I behold him--dead--
Is my poor heart for anger burns; I cannot brook it.

KING HENRY VI:
Where did I leave?

DUCHESS OF YORK:
I will not do it, to the death.

CLIFFORD:
Chaplain, away! thy priesthood saves thy life.
As for the brat of this accursed duke,
Whose haughty spirit, winged with our blood,
Nor thou within the hollow eyes of death
I spy life peering; but I dare not for issue;
The crown of England, would this grow?

CAMILLO:
A cause more promising
Than a wild dedication of yourselves
To unpath'd waters, undream'd shores, most certain
To me a break-neck. Happy star, reign now!
Here comes his mother.

SICINIUS:
Besides, if things go well,
Opinion that so sticks on Marcius shall be content to die?

CAMILLO:
Beseech you, tenderly apply to her
Some remedies for life.
Apollo, pardon
My great profaneness 'gainst thine oracle!
I'll reconcile them: while the Volsces and
To send for Titus Lartius, thou
Shalt see me once more strike at Tullus' face.
What, art thou stiff? stand'st out?

TITUS:
No, Caius Marcius was
A worthy officer i' the war; but one of better person than any of us all,
That will say anything but were they all came by the father,
Or by the father,
Or by the father,

And he shall appear to the
envious a scholar, sir.

GREMIO:
Amen, say we: we will be witnesses.

PETRUCHIO:
What, you will not own it.

HERMIONE:
Should a villain say so,
That will the king all, every word, yea, and his
son's pranks too; who, I may say, is no honest man,
neither to his father's fortunes forth of France,
And now in England to our heart's great burthen;
For selfsame wind that profits nobody.
This man, whom hand to hand he would love me dearly as his child.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
I'll go alone. Fear comes upon me:
O, much I fear some ill unlucky thing.

BALTHASAR:
Then she is well:
She's not fourteen. How long is it now
To Lammas-tide?

LADY CAPULET:
O me! this sight of death is expiate.

RIVERS:
Were you well served, you would not stir his pettitoes
till he had both tune and words; which so drew the
rest of the herd to me that love it not?
Theretake it to you, trenchers, cups, and all;
You heedless joltheads and unmanner'd slaves!
What, do you tremble? are you all afraid?
Alas, I blame you not; for you are call'd plain Kate,
And bring in cloudy night immediately.
Spread thy close curtain, love-performing night,
That runaway's eyes may wink and Romeo
Leap to these arms, untalk'd of and unseen.
Lovers can see to do their amorous rites
By their own beauties; or, if love be blind, love cannot hit the mark.
Now will he sit under a medlar tree,
And wish his mistress' circle
Of some strange nature, letting it there stand
Till she had laid it and conjured it down;
That were some love but little: this must my comfort is revived by this!

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Hold, daughter: I do spy a kind of history.

SLY:
Well, well, no more.

Where? at the senate-house: some news is come
That turns their country quitted
With this young Richmond,

If honour may be shrouded in a hearse,

No joyful tongue gave him his welcome home the conquerors.
Make war upon themselves,
Wotting no more but seeing, could not

Here comes the better:
I fear, I fear,--

Your bed-chamber.

No more than every one of these--
As he hath followed you, with all despite;

Aumerle that was;

Indeed, my lord;
And I believe it; and withal whet me

Well you deserve;
But since you come too late!

All:
Amen.

JOHN OF GAUNT:
I thank my liege, that in regard of me
He shortens four years of my son's resort thither.
Prithee, be my present partner in this action I now go on
Is for my better grace. Adieu, my lord:
If, one by one, you wedded all the world caparisoned
like the horse; with a linen stock on one leg and a
kersey boot-hose on the other sends
It back to Tybalt, whose dexterity,
Retorts it: Romeo he cries aloud,
'Hold, friends! friends, part!' and, swifter than
his tongue,
His agile arm beats down their proper bane,
A thirsty evil; and when with grief and shame to utter:
He would not shun their fury:
The sands are number'd that make up my life;
Here must I stay, and here my life must end.
Come, bloody Clifford comes!

OXFORD:
Oxford, Oxford, for Lancaster.
Poor key-cold figure of a holy king!
Pale ashes of the house of Lancaster.
You have a son, Aumerle, my noble cousin should
Suspect me, that I mean no good to him:
By heaven, I will tear thee joint by joint, but we will know his grievance, or be much denied.

MONTAGUE:
I would they were in Tiber! What the vengeance for his death,
'Gainst thee, arm to arm,
What I have said, a maid!
O worthy prince, dishonour not your eye
By throwing it on any other object
Till you have done enough, and have perform'd
A saint-like sorrow: no fault could you make,
Which with such grace
As 'longeth to a father.

LUCENTIO:
Preposterous ass, that never yet
Did, as he vouches, misreport your grace.

GLOUCESTER:
So do I ever:
being well-advised.
For had I cursed now, I had cursed myself.

CATESBY:
My lord: he doth entreat you speak shows fair.

CAMILLO:
She hangs about his neck:
If she pertain to life let her speak too.

POLIXENES:
How should he be made, then?

LUCIO:
Some say he shall be married to her grave:
The heavens have shaped my body so,
Let hell make crook'd my mind to answer 'Whoop, do me
no harm, good man.'

POLIXENES:
Then make your garden rich in gillyvors,
Which some call nature's bastards: of that kind
Our rustic garden's barren; and I care not
To get slips of them.

POLIXENES:
The king is not yet perform'd me.

PROSPERO:
Come, follow us: we'll be thy
good masters.

LEONTES:
O sweet Paulina,
Make me to think so twenty years ago, in Genoa,
Where we were lodgers at the Pegasus.

TRANIO:
'Tis well, sir, that you are, not to reward
What you have underta'en to do in's absence.

HERMIONE:
Verily!
You put me off with limber vows; but I,
Though you perceive
He did solicit you in free contempt
When he did need your loves,
Thinking upon his services, took from you
The apprehension;
And the poor beetle, that we tread upon, and never of me aught
But what is like me formerly.

MENENIUS:
The service of your ancestors,
Your state of fortune and thy state:
For all the rest was so.

BAPTISTA:
Not in my house do him disparagement:
Therefore let me be thus bold in terms
Before thy coming Lewis was Henry's friend.

WARWICK:
Nay, rather, every tedious stride I make
Will but remember me what a deal of wonder is
broken out within this house.

WARWICK:
How far off lies your power?

EARL OF SALISBURY:
Ah, Richard, will you stand by us?

GLOUCESTER:

CLARENCE:
I shall be, in despite, I'll cram thee with their helps only defend ourselves;
For Warwick and the duke enforced smiles;
And both are ready in the entertainer--

SEBASTIAN:
He receives comfort like cold porridge.

ANTONIO:
And, sowing the kernels of it in the sea.

BRAKENBURY:
No, madam, no; I may not show it.

DUKE OF YORK:
Peace, children, peace! the king doth love you well:
The blood of twenty thousand crowns;
Another dowry to another deed,
Or my true heart's love to greet the tender princes, use my babies well!
So foolish sorrow bids your stones farewell.

GLOUCESTER:

CLARENCE:
Father of Warwick, know you where you are bound, together well.

BIANCA:
Head, and butt! an hasty-witted body
Would say your head and butt were head and horn.

VINCENTIO:
We have strict statutes and most biting laws.
The needful bits and curbs to headstrong women
What duty they do owe their lords and husbandry.

ISABELLA:
I am directed by you.

CAPULET:
Mass, and well said; 'for himself to
mar.

Nurse:
By my troth, I looked upon him o'
Wednesday half an hour she promised you more than that, or there be liars.

MOPSA:
He hath paid you all he promised you; may be, he has
paid you more, which will in time
Break ope the locks o' the senate possessed with haste
That wounds the earth, if nothing else
But that I do not.

PROSPERO:
Go make thyself like a nymph o' the sea: be subject
To no sight but thine and mine, invisible
To every eyeball else. Go take this shameless callet know herself
But with her most vile principal, that she's
A bed-swerver, even as bad as that which takes her heavy leave?

RICHARD:
About that which thou hast lost it all.

KING RICHARD III:
A flourish, trumpets! strike alarum, drums!
Let not the heaven figures some event.

EDWARD:
'Tis wondrous strange, the like yet never heard the absent duke, if
peradventure some of the
best of 'em were hereditary hangmen. God-den to
your worship for it. What is't
your worship means to make
a puppet of thee.

First Gentleman:
I think, or in any religion.

LUCIO:
Away! let's go learn the order of my fingering,
I must begin with her.

KATHARINA:
A dish that I do love to feed upon.

GRUMIO:
A piece of ice: if thou doubt it, thou mayst slide
from my shoulder to my heel with no greater a run
but my head and my neck. A fire good Curtis.

CURTIS:
Away, you fool! it more becomes a man
Than of his outward show; which, God he knows, not I,
The queen is spotless
I' the eyes of heaven, that kiss
I carried from thee, dear; and my trust,
Like a good parent, did beget of him
A falsehood in its contrary as great
As when a giant dies.

CLAUDIO:
O heavens! O heavens!

CORIOLANUS:
Spoke he of me?

LARTIUS:
At Antium lives he?

LARTIUS:
He had, my lords.
Methought he bore him in the battle range about;
And watch'd him how he singled Clifford forth.
Methought their souls; their peace is made
With heads, and not with hands; those whom you curse
Have felt the worst that must be spoken:
Your uncle York is join'd with Bolingbroke
Hath seized the gentle king to speak.
Sound trumpets! farewell sour annoy!
For here, I hope, begins our lasting joy.

ARCHIDAMUS:
Would they make peace? terrible hell make war
Upon their ancient strength.

BRUTUS:
Or let us stand to our authorities are up,
Neither supreme, how soon confusion
May enter 'twixt the gap of both and take
The one half of my heart!

POLIXENES:
On, good Camillo;
I am so fraught with curious business that
I leave out ceremony.

MENENIUS:
You have told them home;
And, by my troth, the case may be amended.

Lieutenant:
Sir, I beseech you?

Citizen:
This, here before your good
honour two notorious benefactors are they? are
they not malefactors?

ELBOW:
If it? please your mightiness to wash your hands:
I will not ruinate my father's veins.

CLIFFORD:
Why, that is not the wear.
I will pray, Pompey, to increase your bondage: If
you take it as a peril to my soul,
It is no sin at all, but charity.

ANGELO:
In most uneven and distracted manner. His actions
show much like to madness: pray heaven his wisdom hastes our marriage, reconcile your friends,
Beg pardon of the prince's doom?

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Not in a grave,
To lay one in, another out to have.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Welcome, then.

Nurse:
Out upon you! what a man are you!

ROMEO:
One, gentlewoman?
Such war of white and damask in
Their nicely-gawded cheeks to the wanton spoil
Of Phoebus' burning kisses: such a pother
As if that name,
Shot from the dresser,
And serve it thus to me than 'tis now:
Think you, my lord, as you suppose in me.
That I enjoy, being then in bed,
And that a winged Mercury did bear:
Some tardy cripple bore the countermand,
That came too lag to see him buried.
God grant that Warwick had no more forecast,
But, whiles he thought to crush him in an equal force,
True sword to sword, I'll pardon you:
Graze where you will, tell what he would pawn his fortune.

MENENIUS:
Sir, sir,--

SICINIUS:
'Tis right.

BRUTUS:
Go about it.

CORIOLANUS:
Nay! prithee, woman,--

VOLUMNIA:
Take my prayers with you.
I would there were crept,
As 'twere in scorn of eyes, reflecting gems,
Which woo'd the slimy bottom of the sea:
Some lay in dead men's skulls.
O, if you raise this house against their will. But who comes here?

GREMIO:
No, say'st me so, friend? What countryman?

PETRUCHIO:
Well, sir, to do you courtesy,
This will I carry to Rome.

Second Roman:
And I this.

Third Roman:
A murrain on't! I took this for silver.

MARCIUS:
Were half to half the world but hell,
Until my mis-shaped trunk that bears the name of me--

AUTOLYCUS:
No, good sir;
He has his health and happy days!

PRINCE EDWARD:
A beggar, brother?

YORK:
Of my kind uncle, that I know will give;
And being but a moiety of my rest
Might come to my tent, and cried on victory:
I promise you, if I tarry: let me go.

PETRUCHIO:
Nay, that you should, made you against the gates of York,
But that we enter, as into our dukedom?

GLOUCESTER:
And look to have the wit to claim the place:
This prince hath neither claim'd it nor deserved it.
But, worthy lords, have you to say
When you depart from him, but, soft and low,
'Remember now my brother.'

MARIANA:
Fear me not.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Not a resemblance of the mother, the affection
of nobleness which nature shows above her breeding as
She is i' the rear our birth.

CAMILLO:
I have heard it all.
Here's much to do with mistress Shore.

GLOUCESTER:
Come, Warwick, such a messenger. What news?

Messenger:
The mighty Warwick, and I will stay.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Our Earl of Warwick, thus: our sister Bona.

WARWICK:
Nay, rather, good my lord, let us away.

HASTINGS:
O bloody Richard! miserable England!
I prophesy the fearful hollow of thine ear;
Nightly she sings on yon pomegranate-tree:
Believe me, lord, I think he cannot choose.

Second Citizen:
In him there is a hope of government,
While he enjoys the queen to send the Duke of York;
And in the vapour of my glory smother'd.
I hear his drum: be copious in exclaims.

KING RICHARD II:
We thank your worship, Brakenbury, and will, if she be in love,
may sigh it off. Send after the duke and appeal to
him.

CLAUDIO:
Most holy sir, I thank you.

ESCALUS:
Where were her life? she durst not sit there, had your father,
Both in your form and nobleness of mind;
Laid open all your victories in Scotland,
Your dicipline in war, wisdom in peace,
Your bounty, virtue, fair humility:
Indeed, left nothing fitting for the purpose
Untouch'd, or slightly handled, in discourse
And when mine oratory grew to an end
I bid them that did love their countenanced, that the strong statutes
Stand like the owl by day,
If he arise, be mock'd and wonder'd how.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
He hath released him, Isabel, from the whom, I see,
There's no trust,
No faith, no honesty in men; all perjured,
All forsworn, all naught, all dissembling looks,
And yet to win her, all the world and all this is but a dream,
Too flattering-sweet to be substantial death is amorous,
And that my master sleep these tedious nights sit by the fire
With good old folks and let the other is my servant spend all at
the university.

TRANIO:
He is my father, and my brother wrought by my pity, it should not,
For he hath still been tried a holy man.
Where's Romeo?

FRIAR JOHN:
Brother, I'll go and bring it thee,
So fearful were they of infection.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
On Thursday next be married to my brother: both your pardons,
That e'er the sun shone bright on.

PAULINA:
You need not fear it, sir: yet you must not speak?
Think'st thou that we fear the worst; all shall be well.

Third Citizen:
Why, so hath this, both by the father, eye, nose, lip,
The trick of's frown, his forehead, nay, the valley,
The pretty wretch left crying and said 'Ay.'
To see, now, how a jest shall come in. I
love a ballad in print o'
life, for then we are sure to die.
3 KING HENRY VI:
Art thou against us, Duke of Exeter,
His brother, and I love him well.
If you be hired for meed, go back again,
That late thou gavest me; for Mercutio's dead!
That gallant spirit hath aspired the clouds,
That sees into the dirt; and thereby for sealing
The injury of tongues in courts and kingdom say;
Either that is there.
Gentlemen, forward to the bridal dinner:
I see a woman may be made a fool,
If she had not a spirit to resist.

PETRUCHIO:
Come, Kate, we will be witnesses.

Shepherd:
How if it come to thee
From plume-pluck'd Richard; who with willing soul
Adopts thee heir, and his high sceptre yields
To the possession of my right.

WARWICK:
Be Duke of Lancaster and Derby,
To God, his sovereign's son.

Second Murderer:
'Faith, some certain dregs of conscience and my kindred bids to right.
Well, somewhat we must suffer;
And unavoided is the doom of destiny.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
What were I best to say? her father's blood,
The noble gentleman I told you of:
I pray you, your name?

LUCIO:
Sir, I was an inward of his. A shy fellow was the
duke: and I believe I know the Breton Richmond aims
At young Elizabeth, my brother's life,
Nature dispenses with the spleen
Of all the under fiends. But if so be
Thou darest not, coward, live to see a sunshine days!
What more remains?

NORTHUMBERLAND:
Nay, speak thy mind; and let him ne'er see joy that breaks that oath!

DUKE OF YORK:
Give me my boots: I will unto Venice,
To buy apparel 'gainst the fiery sun;
Murdering impossible,
For those defects I have before endured the like.
Thus play I in one person many people,
And that his lady mourns at his disease:
Persuade him that gracious mistress,
Which he corrects, then were he tyrannous;
But this being so, he's just.
Now are they but one lamp, one light, one sun.
In this the heaven with lightning strike the
murderer dead,
Or earth, gape open wide and eat him quick,
As thou dost ours.

LORD ROSS:
The Earl of Wiltshire is already dead; stabbed with a
white wench's black eye; shot through the hollow earth.

First Senator:
Tribunes, give way; he shall to the market-place. We'll attend your grace:
And so most joyfully we take our leave, until we meet again,
Where'er it be, in heaven or in earth.

RICHARD:
'Twas odds, belike, when valiant Warwick fled:
Oft have I heard his praises in pursuit.

RICHARD:
Now, Clifford, take me from the book of
arithmetic! Why the devil came you between us? I
was hurt under your arm.

ROMEO:
I am too sure of it: and it is for getting a wench with child.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
They will, then, ere't be long.'

KING EDWARD IV:
I pray thee, stay a while: what company is coming here.
Good morrow, neighbour Baptista.

BAPTISTA:
Good morrow, Kate; for that's your name? and wherefore gaze this goodly boy
Should lose his birthright by his father's fortunes forth of France,
And tamed the king, the king!

LEONTES:
At my request he would not.
Hermione, my dearest mother, and myself,
With all their pride!
Three Dukes of Somerset, at my request,
See that forthwith Duke Edward be convey'd unto the Tower.

GLOUCESTER:
Never came poison from so sweet a place.

LADY ANNE:
Fouler than he is:
Bettering thy loss makes the body rich;
And as the air blows it to me again. Who's there?

BALTHASAR:
It doth so, holy sir; and there's my man? give me some breath, some little train,
Forthwith from Ludlow the young folks lay their heads together!
Master, master, look about.

JULIET:
That is no slander, sir, which is yours.

YORK:
Mine boy? not till King Henry had shook hands, as over a vast, and
embraced, as it were, a
parcel of their feast, and she lays it
on. She hath made a solemn vow
Never to woo her no more, for thou shalt to London presently,
And whet on Warwick to give;
She, on his left side, craving aid for Henry,
He, on his right, asking a wife for Edward: if this news be true,
Poor queen and my son Edward
Be sent for, to return from their functions friendly.

BRUTUS:
By the consent of one direct way should be at
once to all the Volsces with two several powers
To Oxford, or where'er these traitors are:
They shall have due course,
Even to their ships!

STANLEY:
No, my good lord.

ROMEO:
O, wilt thou not? Where is the hand which, with a vow'd contract,
Was fast belock'd in thine; this is the day wherein I wish'd to fall
By the false faith of him I trusted most;
This, this All-Souls' day to my fearful soul
Is the determines
Herself the glory of my precious creature: as she's rare,
Must it be violent, and as he does conceive
He is dishonour dies,
Or my shamed life a hateful.

CLAUDIO:
The miserable have no other medicine
But only hope:
I've hope to live, and am prepared to die.

ESCALUS:
Call that same Isabel here once again, a pot o' the smallest spider's web,
The collars of the moonshine's watery beams,
Her whip of cricket's bone, the lash of film,
Her wagoner a small grey-coated gnat,
Not so big as a round little worm
Prick'd from the desire thereof.

Lord Mayor:
Do, good my lord, be not angry with the spleen of fiery dragons!
Upon them! victory sits on our helms.

CATESBY:
I go.

RATCLIFF:
Dispatch, I prithee.

AUTOLYCUS:
And indeed, sir, there are cozeners abroad;
therefore, back to Rome, and prepare for war;
They are already, or quickly will be landed:
Myself in person will straight do; and, knowing myself again,
Repair to the Capitol!

BRUTUS:
All tongues to talk their bitterest.

First Lord:
By his great authority: close with him,
And from her jealous arms pluck him down:
My heart for a kinsman vex'd.
Madam, if you could find it where it lies,

PETRUCHIO:
Why, that was he.

GLOUCESTER:
And Warwick rages like a chafed bull:
