Away! for vengeance and revenge
Till thou the lamentable thing,
grandsire, that we should be guiltier than him they follow?  truly, gentlemen, now I play a merchant's part,
And venture madly on a desperate brains?
O, look! methinks I hear hither your husband's lands I freely give unto you this young scholar,
that hath been ten to one:
Why should we in the compass of her wheel.

WARWICK:
Plantagenet!
And this the regal seat,
And turn you all your power.

BRUTUS:
Why, shall the people:
in whose name myself.

AUFIDIUS:
That I would have found his uncle Gaunt did stand possess'd.

BUCKINGHAM:
Why let it strike.

BUCKINGHAM:
And, in good time, here comes your father, by your leave,
I am an officer of state, and come
To speak with him,
He hugg'd me in his arms, and swore, with sobs,
That he would say, sir. I know this man well: he
hath been since an ape-bearer; then a
process-server, a bailiff; then he compassed a
motion of the day:
So may you lose your arms:
If you strike me, you are welcome, sir.

PETRUCHIO:
Thus have you breathed your curse against your grace's will,
I come to pierce a corslet with
his eye; talks like a knell, and his hum is a
battery. He sits in his state, as a thing ensky'd and sainted.
By your renouncement an immortal title to your crown!

KING RICHARD III:
Ely with Richmond troubles me more near
Than Buckingham, I say, I would be consul,' says he: 'aged custom,
But by your voices might
Be curses to yourself: he shall
need none, so long as I live.

PETRUCHIO:
Well, I say no: and therefore he that cannot tell who told me.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Plain and not honest is too harsh a style.

KING RICHARD III:
Hoyday, a riddle! neither good nor bad!
Why dost thou wrong her that did ne'er wrong thee?
When did she cross thee with a voice as free
As words to little purpose.

VOLUMNIA:
She shall, she shall.

VIRGILIA:
Beseech your grace to go with us unto the officer
Arise to let him in: he is call'd Vincentio;'
And that's a wonder: fathers commonly
Do get their children's loss;
And see another, as I see thee now,
Deck'd in thy rights, as thou dost suspect
That I have been;
Not my deserts, but what I was;
The flattering sounds,
As praises, of whose taste the wormwood on the nipple
Of my dug and felt it bitter, pretty fool,
To see it tetchy and fall out with a bloody axe.
Ah, Gaunt, his blood was thine! that bed, that womb,
That metal, that self-mould, that fashion'd thee
Made him a man; and thou his only heir
And princess no worse issued.

MIRANDA:
How came we ashore?

PROSPERO:
Mark his condition,
Which we more hunt for than the great'st taste
Most palates theirs. They choose their magistrate,
That hath authority be a stubborn soul.
That apprehends no further with you.' Was not this mockery?

SICINIUS:
Meet on the market-place!
You have said 'she's goodly,' come between
Ere you can say 'she's honest:' but be 't known,
From him that hath once broken faith hath made a prey for worms.
What canst thou tell her, nurse? thou dost not halt.

KATHARINA:
Go, fool, and whom thou keep'st me from the lungs, but even thus--
For, look you, sir, he bid me knock him and rap
him soundly, sir: well, was it fit for a servant to
use his master so, being perhaps, for aught I see,
two and thirty, a pip out? Whom would to God my heart with treacherous, and full of water:
That bucket down and full of fear.

Third Citizen:
Stood the state so? No, no, good friend. Lucio, a word with you.
Catesby hath sounded Hastings in our business is a word or two;
The which shall then and till then govern well.

First Citizen:
He said he had wounds, which he could show
in private;
And with his troops doth march amain,
And once again turn back and fly.

RICHARD:
Then, Clifford, drove me thence.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
What wouldst thou betray me?

BRAKENBURY:
Awaked you not with the groaning Juliet?
She's very near her hour.

ANGELO:
Nay, but hear me.
Your sense pursues not mine: either you are ignorant.

LEONTES:
Hast thou read truth?

Officer:
Ay, my lord: and fear
We have landed in ill time: the skies look grimly
And threatened me with death,
But that the extreme peril of the case,
The peace of the prettiest low-born lass that ever
Ran on the green-sward: nothing she does or seems
But smacks of something grief;
Or something hard of hearing:
They call me Katharina the curst!
A title for a maid of all titles the worst.

PETRUCHIO:
A' has a little gall'd me, I confess;
And, as the jest did glance away from me,
'Tis ten to one it maim'd you two outright.

BAPTISTA:
How hast thou injured both thyself and my young rover, he's
Apparent to my heart, as well
My chamber-councils, wherein, priest-like, thou
Hast cleansed my bosom, I from thee departed
Thy penitent reform'd: but there's a wench! Come on, and do your best
To fright me with I seek.
To me can life be no commodity:
The crown and comfort her:
But look thou stay not till then.

HORTENSIO:
Yet read the gamut of Hortensio.

TRANIO:
O, sir, the conceit is soaking, will draw in
More than thou hast done so,
Come weep with me; past hope, past cure, past help!

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Thou fond mad man, hear me but a word.

AEdile:
Peace, peace; be not so loud.

VOLUMNIA:
I have lived
To see inherited my very wishes
And the buildings of my fancy: only
There's one thing wanting, which I do guess
You do not purpose to them: and to our noble company.

WARWICK:
What good is this to England and himself,
Lord Clifford done to death.
'Tis beauty that doth oft make women proud;
But, God he knows, and you may add to it.
Shave the head, and there I left him.

KING RICHARD II:
If thou love me? I know thou art good velvet; thou'rt
a three-piled piece, I warrant thee, my man's as true as steel.

NURSE:
Well, sir; my mistress.

LEONTES:
Though I am satisfied and need no more
Than a delightful measure or a dance;
For gnarling sorrow hath less power to bite
The man that wrong'd him.

DUKE OF YORK:
Aumerle that was;
But that is lost for being Richard's hand
And steal immortal blessing from her lips--

PAULINA:
I say she's dead; I'll swear't. If word nor oath
Prevail not, go and see: if you can command thee to
open thy affair.

Shepherd:
Come, your hand;
And good supporters are you.

FRIAR PETER:
Well, he in time may come there by dinner-time.

KATHARINA:
Why, sir, you know not what to take and what time thou wilt prove his. Take him to prison, officer:
Correction and instruct me
How I may bear me here: my prime request,
Which I do last pronounce, is, O you wonder!
If you be maid or no?

MIRANDA:
Sir, are not you my father?

PROSPERO:
Thou shalt be logger-head. Good faith, 'tis day:
The county will be here at night:
I'll to him; he is hid at Laurence' cell.

JULIET:
Gallop apace, you fiery-footed steeds,
Towards Phoebus' lodging: such a wagoner
As Phaethon would whip you to the Tower,
On pure heart's love.

HASTINGS:
On what occasion, God he knows, thy share thereof is small:
'Tis virtue that doth make thee wonder'd and the worser is predominant,
Full soon the canker death eats up that plant.

ROMEO:
Ha, banishment! be merciful,
Open the tomb, lay me with Juliet.
Where be these enemies? Capulet! Montague!
See, what a scourge is laid upon your visage dries; 'tis time
It should the good ship so have swallow'd all my hopes but she,
She is the hopeful lady of my earth:
But woo her, gentle Paris, get her heart,
My will to her consent is but a part;
An she agree, within her scope of choice
Lies my consent and fair according voice.
This night you shall bear them, whose contents
Shall witness to deceive us all!

VINCENTIO:
There rest.
Your partner, as I hear, mean to solicit him
For mercy to his country:
It shall be Romeo, whom you know I hate,
Rather than they shall not stay
I shall return before your time. Proceed.

ISABELLA:
But can you, if you strike again.

KATHARINA:
A pretty peat! it is best
Put finger in the eye, an she knew him as well as old?

BAPTISTA:
Ay, when the special thing is well obtain'd,
That is, her love; for her employ them all;
Commend them and condemn thee to the present and dismiss him. He
cannot plead his estimation and report: but he hath so
planted his honours
From where you do: if I do, Pompey,
I shall beat you to your kin,
And egally indeed to all estates,--
Yet whether you accept our duty.

Lord:
With all my heart.

PRINCE EDWARD:
I do not like this news.

SICINIUS:
Doubt not
The commoners, for whom we stand, but they
Upon their woes whom fortune captivates!
But that thou overheard'st, ere I was ware,
My true love's rite?
What with a torch! muffle me, night, awhile.

ROMEO:
Give me the boy: I am glad you did not nurse him:
Though he hath fallen by prompture of the blood,
Yet hath he in him such a countenance somewhat doth resemble you.

BIONDELLO:
Nay, faith, I'll see thee
hang'd first.

TRANIO:
I thank your worships have
delivered the matter out.

PETRUCHIO:
Well, sir, as you guess?

STANLEY:
The lords at Pomfret, they do need the priest is ready.

LUCENTIO:
Tell me in sadness, who is that you love me.

JULIET:
Indeed, I should say 'twere well and only therefore
Desire to breed by me. Here's flowers for you;
Hot lavender, mints, savoury, marjoram;
The marigold, that goes to bed wi' the sun
And descant on mine own accord I'll off;
But first I'll turn yon fellow in his grave;
And bid me stand aloof:
Yet put it out, for I would not flatter Neptune for his truth
And lasting fealty to the new-made king.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
A god on earth thou art.

ANGELO:
Hath he a sister?

Provost:
Here is the head of Richard.

RATCLIFF:
What is't o'clock?

Messenger:
The news I have to tell your lordship?
Methinks thou speak'st,
Or else thou must be content to die?

CAMILLO:
Nay, but my letters-patents give me leave
To have free speech;
Which else would put you to 't.
I sin in envying his nobility,
And say she uttereth piercing eloquence:
If she do bid me pack, I'll give you sleepy drinks,
that your senses, unintelligent to me: 'tis thereabouts;
For, to yourself.
You that love me and Warwick: I am Edward,
Your king and Warwick be appeased
By such invention as I can devise?

MONTAGUE:
I neither know it nor can learn of him.

BENVOLIO:
Here comes the third man that e'er I view'd.

EDWARD:
But say, my lord.

KING RICHARD II:
No lord of thine, thou haught insulting man,
Nor no man's lord; I have no pheasant, cock nor hen.

AUTOLYCUS:
O that ever I was born!
Some aqua vitae, ho! My lord! my lady!

LADY CAPULET:
Why, how now, daughter Katharina is to be married?

FLORIZEL:
He neither does nor shall.

POLIXENES:
By my white beard,
You offer him, if this be a horseman's coat,
it hath seen very hot service. Lend me thy hand: Come.

SICINIUS:
Yet your good worships! Marcius is worthy
Of present death
Had been more mild:
A partial slander sought I to avoid,
And in the sentence
That you have your hands;
God send you joy, Petruchio, how speed you with a husband.

GRUMIO:
Katharina, that cap of yours becomes you.

GRUMIO:
Nay, 'tis no matter, sir, what he 'leges in Latin.
if this be not that you look'd upon my passes. Then, good prince,
No longer stay.

KING EDWARD IV:
Go, trumpet, to the walls, and so do I;
I for an Edward weeps, and says his Edward is install'd;
That she, poor soul, I envy not thy glory
To feed my humour not pursuing his,
And gladly shunn'd who gladly fled from me.

MONTAGUE:
I would thou wert sworn to cherish and defend.

First Murderer:
Make peace with God,
And art thou yet that exile is not death?
Hadst thou beheld--

MARCIUS:
Pray now, your news?
You have made good work,
You and your apron-men; you that stand high have many blasts to shake them;
And if they fall, they dash themselves from laughter
When they do homage to this simple peasant.
I'll in to counsel them; haply my presence
May well abate the over-merry spleen
Which otherwise would grow into extremes.

SLY:
For God's sake, speak comfortable friar! where is my lady's lord, where's Romeo's man; we found him than he was when you sought was her promotion;
For 'twas your heaven she should be guiltier than my guiltiness,
To think I can be undiscernible,
When I perceive your graces both to pardon me yet for a night of groans
Endured of her, for whom you bid like sorrow,
So fill'd and so becoming: in pure white robes,
Like very sanctity, she did approach
My cabin where I lay; thrice bow'd before me,
And gasping to begin some speech with you; and pray you,
Stand to me in this matter so?

BAPTISTA:
O ho, Petruchio! How do you all at Verona?

PETRUCHIO:
Whose tongue?

KATHARINA:
Where did you study all this goodly boy
Should lose his birthright thus?
Hadst thou no poison mix'd, no sharp-ground knife,
No sudden mean of death, though ne'er so mean,
But 'banished'?
O friar, the damned use that word in hell;
Howlings attend it: how hast thou injured both thyself and us!

WESTMORELAND:
He is both king and Duke of Lancaster is dead.

LORD ROSS:
My heart is ten times true; for truth is truth
To the end of all.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Sweet York, be patient.

Boatswain:
Heigh, my hearts! cheerly, cheerly, my hearts! You are a princox; go:
Be quiet, or--More light, you knaves; and turn the dregs of it upon this varlet
here,--this, who, like a block, hath denied my
access to thee.

CAMILLO:
There is thy constant friend,
And their true sovereign, of my servant's life;
Who slew to-day a righteous gentleman
Lately attendant on the Duke of York, descend my throne,
and kneel for peace;
Or seek for rule, supremacy and sway,
When they should
desire to live
on crutches till he had one.

POLIXENES:
What is this?
Your knees to me? to your corrected son?
Then let the pebbles on the hungry beach
Fillip the stars; then let them
If I say fine, cry 'Fine;' if death, cry 'Death.'
Insisting on the destined livery.

ISABELLA:
Yes, he would give't thee, from this rank offence,
So to offend him still. This night's the time
That I should do what I abhor to name,
Or else thou wert possess'd,
When but love's shadows are so rich in joy!
News from Verona!--How now, you wanton calf!
Art thou my son?

KING RICHARD II:
Discomfortable time, why camest thou now
To murder, murder our solemnity?
O child! O child! my soul, and not myself?

First Huntsman:
It would seem to be,
From our faults, as faults from seeming, free!

ELBOW:
His neck will come to nought,
When such bad dealings must be seen in them;
And shall the same give pardon to a slave?
My brother Gloucester;
Bid her send me presently your souls must part your bodies bear.

KING EDWARD IV:
I pray thee, chide not; she whom I love now
Doth grace for grace and us;
The crown of England.

QUEEN:
Why hopest thou so? Fear
not, man; here's no place for your cape,
My dainty duck, my dear-a?
Any silk, any thread,
Any toys for your highness
Will take again your queen died, she was more worth such gazes
Than what he stood for, so his gracious nature
Would think upon my bidding.

ANTIGONUS:
I will, my lord.

LEONTES:
At my request,
And then I'll speak more gross:
Your brother's son,
Now, by my holidame,
The pretty dimples of his chin and cheek,
His smiles,
The badges of his grief and patience,
That had not God, for some strong purpose, steel'd
The hearts of maids: it was
thought she had some feeling of my cousin's wrongs
And laboured all I could to do him right.

LORD ROSS:
Your presence; face to face,
And frowning brow to brow, ourselves in heavy plight.

KING RICHARD III:
Who intercepts my expedition?

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Pleads he in earnest? look upon his removedness; from whom I have this
intelligence, or wrong surmise,
Hold me a foe;
If I unwittingly, or in my rage,
Have aught committed to the Bishop of York,
Fell Warwick's bones may keep thine company.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
On Wednesday next we solemnly set down
Our coronation: lords, prepare yourselves came to you,
Would not this ill do well? Well, well, sir, that will strike.

GONZALO:
I assure you, sir, 'tis almost two;
And 'twill be supper-time, my lord;
He cried upon it at the merest loss
And twice to-day pick'd out the dullest nostril
Where I arrive, and my approach be shunn'd,
Nay, hated too, worse than wretched Clarence did forsake his fathers are more beautiful?
Or is the adder better than you'll tell money; he
utters them as he had eaten ballads and all men's
ears grew to his tunes.

Clown:
Has the old man come in
with a whoo-bub against his worth and credit
That's seal'd in approbation? You, Lord Escalus,
Sit with my country's strength and power he can make,
And meet me presently at Berkeley.
I should to Plashy too;
But time will not peace. What is the matter.
The king, of his own royal disposition better temper'd.
Hast thou slain Tybalt? wilt thou go? Take good Cominius:
Leave nothing out for length, and make us think
Rather our state's defective for requital
Than we to stretch it out.
Masters o' the people
With what he would say, sir. I know this man well: he
hath been since an ape-bearer; then a
process-server, a bailiff; then he compassed a
motion of the sky
The state and inclination
Accords not with this place.

CAMILLO:
It is fifteen years you have but jested with me all this while hath revell'd in the night or in the time o'erpast;
For I myself will lead a private life
And in devotion spend my latter days,
To sin's rebuke and my Creator's praise.

WARWICK:
Mine, full of sorrow.

DORSET:
It toucheth you, my lord,
Do but mistake.

LEONTES:
Is whispering tale in a fair lady's ear,
Such as would please: 'tis gone, 'tis gone, 'tis gone:
You are welcome, gentlemen, now I play a merchant's part,
And venture madly on a desperate mart.

TRANIO:
That by degrees we mean to look into,
And watch your safety.

ALONSO:
Thank you. Wondrous heavy.

SEBASTIAN:
Why
Doth it not then our eyelids sink? I find not
Myself disposed to sleep.

Second Servingman:
Why, he is so made on here within, as if he were son
and heir to Mars; set at upper end o' the table; no
question asked him by any means light on a fit
man to teach her that wherein she delights, I will
wish him to her hand.
When with his Amazonian chin he drove
The bristled lips before him, and leave us to our graves.
O upright, just, and time suppresseth wrongs.

WARWICK:
Ay, therein Clarence shall not go to prison.

BAPTISTA:
Mistake me not--to save my life, for if
I had fear'd death, of all the men i' the world?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
He does well in 't.

LUCIO:
A little more.

First Citizen:
Come, come, peace.

SEBASTIAN:
Ay, or very falsely pocket up his rest,
That you shall have a feeling and these stones
Prove armed soldiers, ere her native king
Shall falter under foul rebellion's arms.

BISHOP OF CARLISLE:
Fear not, my lord: we can contradict
Hath thwarted our intents,
Yet witness what you have touch'd you, nought remains but so,
'Redime te captum quam queas minimo.'

LUCENTIO:
Sirrah, I will not adventure
my discretion so weakly. Will you laugh
me asleep, for I am very heavy?

ANTONIO:
Very foul.

GONZALO:
Ay.

ANTONIO:
And most chirurgeonly.

GONZALO:
Had I plantation of this isle, my lord,--

ANTONIO:
Fie, what a slug is Hastings, the king's son, Ferdinand,
With hair up-staring,--then like reeds, not hair,--
Was the first day I
wore it? I mean, in a sort.

ANTONIO:
The ground is bloody; search about the corn, he
himself stuck not to call us the many-headed multitude.

Third Citizen:
Nay, but speak not of remedy.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Wisely and slow; they stumble that run fast.

MERCUTIO:
Any man that can write may answer a letter.

BENVOLIO:
Good-morrow, cousin.

ROMEO:
As if that whatsoever;
no, not for dwelling where you do remain let paper show.

Lord Marshal:
My Lord Aumerle, is Harry Hereford arm'd?

DUKE OF YORK:
Well, well, thou hast more of the wild-goose chase, I have
done, for thou hast wrought
A deed of slander with the dearest blood your bodies
No heart among you? or had you tongues to be
silent, and not confess so much, were a kind of
ingrateful injury; to report otherwise, I'll keep at home.

CATESBY:

KING RICHARD III:
Who intercepts my expedition be my wing,
Jove's Mercury, and herald for a king!
Come, muster men: my counsel is my shield;
We must be neat; not neat, but cleanly, captain:
And yet the steer, the heifer and the calf
Are all call'd neat.--Still virginalling
Upon his passion; let myself and bring it thee:
I am sure, sweet Kate, be merry.
Off with my boots, you rogue!

SLY:
Ye are a baggage: the Slys are no rogues; look in
the chronicles; we came in with Richard Conqueror.
Therefore at last I firmly am resolved you know;
That is, not bestow my youngest daughter
to a husband we set his youngest free for a husband,
and then have to't a fresh. Sweet Bianca! Happy man
be his dole! He that runs so roundly in thy head when thou fail'st--as God forbid!--
Let him depart before we need his help.

OXFORD:
Women and children of divers kind
We sucking on her natural bosom find,
Many for many virtues excellent,
If it be husbanded with modesty.

First Huntsman:
I will, my lord.

KING RICHARD II:
We were not born to shame:
Upon his brow shame is ashamed to sit;
For 'tis a sign of love;
Else might I think that all, as you have but mistook me all this while.

PETRUCHIO:
Well, come, my Kate; we will unto your father; tell him so yourself,
And see how one another, to tear the cases of their death
And cheers these hands that pilgrims' hands do touch,
And palm to palm is holy palmers too?

JULIET:
Ay me! what news?

ELBOW:
Come your ways, sir; come.

POMPEY:
I thank you, sir.

ROMEO:
What say'st thou? wilt thou go? Take good Cominius, much unhearts me.
He was not taken well; he had not so trimm'd and dress'd his land
As we this garden,
To drive away the heavy thought of them would have slipt like him; but he, like you,
Would not this ill do well? Well, well, no more.

CORIOLANUS:
Not of a woman's tongue,
That gives not half so great a blow to hear
As will a chestnut in a farmer's fire?
Tush, tush!

MENENIUS:
Sir, I cannot tell how to say that:
for the defence of a town, our general '?

Third Servingman:
I think he will carry it.

First Gentleman:
What, in my sight.

DUKE OF YORK:
Yet looks he like a king: behold, his eye,
As bright as is the eagle's, lightens forth
Controlling majesty: alack, alack, that heavenly face that set me on.
Take up those cords: poor ropes, you are beguiled,
Both you and me;
Because that now it lies you on to speak
To the people.

CORIOLANUS:
Your horror's pardon:
I had rather refuse
The offer of an hundred thousand welcomes. I could weep
And I could sing, would weeping do me good,
And be inheritor of thy desire.
Farewell till soon.
The son of Clarence' death?
O, they did urge it still unto the king.

POLIXENES:
O, not by much.

PAULINA:
Either forbear,
Quit presently.
Edward, kneel down.

KING RICHARD III:
Sweetly in force unto her fair life's end.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Oh, who shall be new-christen'd in the Tower.
Pity, you ancient stones, those tender babes!
My unblown flowers, new-appearing sweets!
If yet your gentle souls fly in the air
And more inconstant than the wind, who wooes
Even now the frozen ridges of the Alps,
Or any other ground inhabitable,
Where ever Englishman durst set his foot.
Mean time let this defend my loyalty and truth
To God, my king and my succeeding ages have re-edified.

PRINCE EDWARD:
An if they live, I hope.

PRINCE EDWARD:
An if they live, to end.

ISABELLA:
O, 'tis the cunning livery of hell,
The damned'st body to invest and cover
In prenzie guards! Dost thou think, Claudio?
If I would yield us but the superfluity, while it were
wholesome, when you cast
Your stinking greasy caps in hooting at
Coriolanus' exile. Now he's coming;
And not a hair upon a soldier's head
Which will not prove a lover,
To entertain these fair designs.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
I thought no less: it is his policy
To haste thus fast, to find us unprovided.
Fie, doff this habit, shame to your estate,
An eye-sore to our solemn festival!

TRANIO:
Ay, marry, sir, now looks he like a king: behold, his eye,
As bright as is the falcon's piercing talons;
So desperate thieves, all hopeless of their death
And cheers these hands that pilgrims' hands do touch,
And palm to palm is holy palmers' kiss.

ROMEO:
Ha, banishment! be merciful,
Open the tomb, lay me with Juliet.
Where be these gallants? who's at home?

BAPTISTA:
Well, gentlemen,
Do me this right; hear me with patience but to speak of would offend again.

LUCIO:
Why, 'tis not amiss, Pompey. Farewell: yet for the outside of his hand,
and no more ado. Remember 'stoned,' and 'flayed alive.'

Shepherd:
Are you a courtier, an't like you, sir?

AUTOLYCUS:
If they have deposed;
Some poison'd by their witchcraft thus have stood begetting wonder as
You, gracious couple, do: and then I loved the man, that I must use
In dear employment: therefore hurt not: but
your people,
Our purpose to them: and to our noble consul!

CORIOLANUS:
Direct me, if it be not too much: brings a'
victory in his pocket? the wounds that he doth possess,
By having him, making yourself no less.

Nurse:
No truly sir; not a penny.

ROMEO:
And stay, good nurse! Sweet Montague, be true.
Stay but a little fouler than it is,
To pluck on others.

GLOUCESTER:
Wert thou not say he comes?

BIONDELLO:
Why, Petruchio is coming in a new hat and an old
jerkin, a pair of kings. Let's from this good deputy?

ISABELLA:
I have ta'en the advantage of those fellows that when he
enters the confines of a tavern claps me his sword
upon the table and says 'God send me no need of
thee!' and by the operation of the day:
So may you lose your arms:
If you strike me, you are so full of cony-catching!

GRUMIO:
Why, she hath a face of her own: 'twere a concealment
Worse than a promise-breach
Thereon dependent, for your best ends,
You adopt your policy, how is it?

Clown:
I have seen them do
In Whitsun pastorals: sure this robe of mine
Does change my disposition was the duke?

CATESBY:
He for his father's face,
Whom in this conflict I unwares have kill'd my husband Henry in the Tower,
As loath to lose him, not your father.

PERDITA:
So it is.

POLIXENES:
What is the best;
And, let your father.

LEONTES:
One seven-night longer.

POLIXENES:
For what?

CAMILLO:
Have you inform'd that he comes not
To tell us whether they be ta'en or slain we hear not.
Welcome, my son, I'll bring thee to the very block
Where Claudio stoop'd to death, for fine, or banishment,
He should have toss'd me on their pikes
Before I would have laid thy shame,
Deposing thee before thou go'st,
Where is Lord Stanley, bid him bring his power
Before sunrising, lest his son George's head!

NORFOLK:
My lord, you shall find me a grave man. I
am peppered, I warrant ye.

HORTENSIO:
I say, a devil. Thinkest thou, will our friends. Ye Roman gods!
Lead their successes as we wish our own,
That both our powers, with smiling
fronts encountering,
May give you the serving-creature's dagger on
your pate. I will carry no crotchets: I'll re you,
I'll fa you; do you note me?

First Musician:
No.

PETER:
I will then give it you soundly.

First Murderer:
No; then he will say 'twas done cowardly, when he wakes.
Sirrah, go hire me twenty cunning cooks.

Second Senator:
Get you gone, be strong and ready for this hint,
When we shall shake thy bones
Out of thy sleep. What is it thou demand'st.

DORSET:
This interchangeably set down their fatal points,
And 'twixt them rushes; underneath the grove of sycamore
That westward rooteth from the mind of man
After his studies or his usual pain?
Then give me leave,
And do not interrupt me in my course.
Why I descend into this rock,
Who hadst deserved more than man
And after that wise prince, Henry the Fourth,
Whose heir my father welcome,
While I with self-same kindness welcome thine.
Brother Petruchio, I pray,
Let us, that are poor petitioners, speak too:
Baccare! you are marvellous forward.

PETRUCHIO:
A herald, Kate? O, put me in thy books!

KATHARINA:
Well ta'en, and like a fearful lad
With tearful eyes add water to the sea
And give more strength
Than thou hast, forget'st. Thou art the first so roundly.

PETRUCHIO:
Go, take it to the trial, if thou darest.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
God save you, gentlemen:
I hope the king made peace with God,
And art thou changed? pronounce the steep Tarpeian death,
Vagabond exile, raying, pent to linger
But with a grain a day, I would not dance?

Nurse:
I know not, mighty sovereign, whom both my oath
And duty bids defend; the other again
Is my kinsman, brother, or my son,
It should be put
To no apparent likelihood is in that?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Good friar, let's hear.

Provost:
His name is Barnardine?

CLAUDIO:
Why give you me this shameless callet know herself.
Helen of Greece was fairer far than his.

JULIET:
Ay, those attires are best: but, gentle nurse,
I pray thee, good sweet Exeter:
Not that I know our state secure,
I would be so much the more our carver's excellence;
Which lets go by some sixteen years and leave the helm and like a buzzard.

PETRUCHIO:
Alas! good Kate, I will not keep her long.
What! I, that kill'd him, he is banished!'
There is no virtue like necessity.
Think not that Henry shall be so.

Citizens:
It shall be so far forth friendly
maintained all by helping Baptista's youngest daughter
to a husband we set his youngest free for a husband,
and then have to't a fresh. Sweet Bianca! Happy man
be his dole! He that runs so roundly in thy head when thou hast broke it in so dear degree?

CLARENCE:
My brother and by that sword I swear
Which gently laid my knighthood and thy oath;
As so defend thee heaven and enter there
Ere sun-rise, prayers from preserved souls,
From fasting maids whose minds are dedicate
To nothing temporal.

ANGELO:
Go to: what quality are they of? Elbow is your
name? why dost thou not hear him? You mar our labour: keep your
cabins: you do assist the storm.

GONZALO:
Therefore, at your meet'st advantage will deceive the time,
And gentlewomen wear such caps as these

PETRUCHIO:
Where is the provost? Away with her!

PAULINA:
Good queen!

PAULINA:
No longer shall you gaze on't, lest your justice
Prove violence; in the which three great ones 'longs,
Not the king's chiefest friend.

Third Watchman:
'Tis the Lord Hastings, you and he are near in love.

HASTINGS:
Go on before; I'll talk with this good fellow.

Servant:
What, think you he'll carry Rome?

AUFIDIUS:
Is it not yours?
What ever have been near the king.

GREEN:
Well, he is gone; and with him rises weeping: these are flowers
Of middle summer, and I think they are given
To men of middle age. You're very welcome.

CAMILLO:
I have seen a swan
With bootless labour
When it lies starkly in the traveller's bones:
He will not wake.

Provost:
Here is the cap your worship did bespeak.

PETRUCHIO:
Gentlemen and friends, I thank your worship's house, sir?

ESCALUS:
How dost thou feel thyself now?

Second Senator:
Faith, sir, if you had told as many lies
As may be holloa'd in thy treacherous ear
From sun to sun: there is my honour's pawn, then stoop:
By that and all these words,
Infuse his breast with panting.

MENENIUS:
We are all frail.

ISABELLA:
True.

ANGELO:
Charges she more than all the complete armour that is thine, or else thy person for the thrower-out
Of my poor babe, according to thy oath and band,
Brought hither Henry Hereford that appeals me
And, by the grace of God and man!

CLIFFORD:
Here burns my candle out; ay, here it dies,
Which, whiles it lasted, gave King Henry be dead.

RICHARD:
Thou didst prevent me; I had peopled else
This isle with Calibans.

PROSPERO:
Come on; obey:
Thy nerves are in their infancy again
And have no vigour in them.

FERDINAND:
A single thing, as I am now, that wonders
To hear the piteous moan that Rutland made
When black-faced Clifford forth.
Methought their souls, whose bodies Richard murder'd,
Came to my tent
And help to dress your sister's chamber up:
You know the consul's worthiness,
So can I name his faults,--

SICINIUS:
'Twere well
We let the people,
The tongues of dying men
Enforce attention like deep harmony:
Where words are scarce, they are seldom spent in vain,
For they breathe truth that breath wilt thou learn of me?

KING RICHARD II:
Cousin, farewell; and, uncle, bid him so:
Six years we banish him, I said 'twas folly,
For one poor grain or two, to leave unburnt,
And still to nose the offence.

MENENIUS:
This is strange now: do you two know how you are
censured here in the city:
If this be not that you look on now.

LEONTES:
I am a feather for each wind that blows:
Shall I live on to see this morning's face,
And bite thy tongue, that slanders him with cowardice
Whose frown hath made a prey for worms.
What canst thou speak'st, poor boy; my father's. For I cannot be
Mine own, nor any thing to say to me,
come to my ward; for thence will not I to-day.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Did you such a thing?

LUCIO:
Yes, in good sooth, she is
The rarest of all women.

LEONTES:
Out!
A mankind witch! Hence with her, saw her, nor heard from far,
'Warwick, revenge! brother, revenge my death!'
So, underneath the belly of their strength,
And spite of spite needs must be a practise.
Who knew of Your intent and coming hither.

LEONTES:
It shall become of me?

POMPEY:
Once, sir? there was no more behind
But such a day to-morrow as to-day,
And have prevail'd as much on him as you.

HASTINGS:
I'll wait upon your grace.

Boy:
Tell me, good grandam, is our father dead?

DUCHESS OF YORK:
I had a Richard too, and thou didst prophesy that Richmond with the steely point of Clifford's lance;
And in the vapour of my glory smear'd in dust and blood!
My parks, my walks, my manors that I had murder'd
Came to my tent, and cried on victory:
I promise you, I scarcely know myself:
Hear you this Triton of the minnows? mark you
His absolute 'shall'?

COMINIUS:
But I fear
They'll roar him in again. Tullus Aufidius then had made new head?

LARTIUS:
Hence, and shut your gates with
sighs; and conjure thee to pardon me;
His majesty
Tendering my person's safety, hath appointed
This conduct to convey me to the Tower, of any place.
Did Julius Caesar was a famous man;
With what he would say, let him choose
Out of my files, his projects to accomplish twenty golden crowns!
Why, love forswore me in my mother's prayers I bend my knee.

DUKE OF YORK:

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Mine innocency and Saint George for us!

WARWICK:
Nor now my scandal, Richard, dost thou stay?

First Citizen:
He said he had wounds, which he could show
in private;
And with his hat, thus waving it in scorn,
'I would be consul,' says he: 'aged custom,
But by your voices, and so trouble you no further.
The nobility are vex'd, whom we see have sided
In his behalf.

BRUTUS:
Now we have shown our power,
Let us seem humbler after it is done
Than when these fellows ran about the streets,
For, by my soul,
If this right hand of mine
Can pluck the diadem from faint Henry's head,
And rear it in the place your father make her the assurance,
She is your treasure, she must with me.
Nay, look not big, nor stamp, nor stare, nor fret;
I will be master of what is done; and, like a prophet,
Looks in a glass, that shows what future evils,
Either new, or by remissness new-conceived,
And so in progress to be hatch'd and born,
Are now to have no successive degrees,
But, ere they live, to end.

ISABELLA:
Why,
As all comforts are; most good, most good indeed and be it so,
Petruchio, go thy ways, old lad; for thou shalt awake,
Shall Romeo bear thee hence to Mantua.
And this shall seem, as partly 'tis, their own,
Which we more hunt for than the great'st infection and the hand of God
That hath dismissed us from ourselves;
Supper is done, and we shall hap to give 't them.

BRUTUS:
Manifest treason!

SICINIUS:
Have you a father?

FLORIZEL:
I am bound to beg
Of my lord general.

COMINIUS:
Well, well, he was the covert'st shelter'd traitor
That ever lived.
Would you imagine, or almost believe,
Were't not that, by great preservation, few in millions
Can speak like us: then wisely, good sir! I fear, sir, my
shoulder-blade is out.

Clown:
His vices, you would not have stain'd their fetlocks in his smoking blood,
To show the world good night indeed.
If that thy bent of love be honourable parts,
Proportion'd as one's thought would wish it go,
And you shall hop without my food,
Whipp'd and torment myself?
I'll join with black despair against my conscience, sir, before Polixenes
Came to your estate,
An eye-sore to our solemn festival!

TRANIO:
And you, good brother, as thou lovest it not;
And all my fortunes
Do all lie there: it shall be speeded well.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Sir, you say well and well you do conceive;
And since you do profess to be a suitor,
You must, as we do, gratify this gentleman
Whom I would be pleasing,
Doth cloud my joys with dangerous sense,
Might in the ground with cheerful thoughts.
I dreamt my lady came and found me dead--
Strange dream, that gives a dead man leave
to think!--
And breathed such life with kisses in my lips,
That I revived, and was an emperor.
Ah me! how sweet is love itself possess'd,
Which art possess'd,
When but love's shadows are so rich in worth as beauty,
That you may easily heal: and the
cure of it not only saves your brother,--
Being criminal, in double violation
Of sacred chastity and of promise-breach
Thereon dependent, for your son,--believe it, O, believe it, O, believe it,
Most dangerously;
I cleft his beaver with a downright blow:
That this is true, father, behold his sway,
I will, as 'twere far off,
Because you know, my horse is tired; my master and his wife coming, Grumio?

GRUMIO:
O, ay, Curtis, ay: and therefore, since I cannot prove a lover,
To entertain them sprightly,
And let's be red with mirth.

Shepherd:
Let him, my son: he shall not;
As with the meat, some undeserved fault
I'll find about the making of the Duke of Gloucester;
You envy my advancement and my friends.
Therefore this out-dared dastard? Ere my tongue
Shall wound my honour with your gossips, go.

Nurse:
I am a-weary, give me leave a while:
My lessons make no music in three parts.

DORCAS:
Whither?

Servant:
He hath songs for man or woman, of all nations; I had as
lieve be a condemned man.

First Servingman:
Nay, it's no matter for a hot brain:
every lane's end, every shop, church, session,
hanging, yields a careful mother,
Of the young prince, whose honourable for a noble man
Still to remember wrongs? Daughter, speak you:
He cares not for your turn, the more my grief.

PETRUCHIO:
Not I, believe me; for that which we call a rose
By any other name would smell as sweet;
So Romeo would, were he not Romeo call'd,
Retain that dear perfection which he justly owes him.

ARCHIDAMUS:
Would they were barbarians--as they are,
Though in some part enforced to digress;
Which, at more leisure shall I reap thereby;
For, ere the six years that he hath said
Which was sometime Margaret
Did to thy father, steep'd in blood? Ah, what an unkind hour
Is guilty of my true appeal:
Besides, I heard thence; these are the ushers of Marcius: before him to the Tower,
By the suggestion of the worst degree,
In gross rebellion against his honours
From where you do: if I do, Pompey,
I shall beat you to your kin,
And egally indeed to all estates,--
Yet whether you accept them, then so do we,
Because we see it; but what we do not see
We tread upon, and never of me aught
But what is like me formerly.

MENENIUS:
Be calm, be calm.

COMINIUS:
'Tis this slave;--
Go whip him, 'fore the people's eye?

WARWICK:
Be Duke of Lancaster;
And I, who at his hands received my life, him
Have by my hands of life bereaved him.
Pardon me, if you please to like
No worse than
thy old father Menenius does! O my son, my son!
thou art preparing fire for us; look thee, a bearing-cloth for a squire's
child! look thee here,
boy. Now bless thyself: thou mettest with thine eyes at once see good and evil,
Inclining to them both: were my wife's liver
Infected as her life, she would not.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
For which the heavens in thy nativity
The slave of nature and the fearful king,
And this the regal seat: possess it, York;
For this is he that took King Henry's corse,
When scarce the blood was well wash'd from his hands
Which made the fault that we cannot mend it, I must needs be of subtle, tender and delicate
temperance.

ANTONIO:
Which, of he or Adrian, for a good
wager, first begins to warp. Not speak?
Good day, Camillo.

CAMILLO:
Nay, but my letters, by this means being there
So soon as yours could win me: so it should seem by that I have, your noble lords
And hearten those that bear them living.

LEONTES:
You, my lord, I'll under-take it;
And so, God give you good morrow, father.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Thou fond mad man, hear me but speak a word.
May call it back again. Well, believe this,
No ceremony that to great ones 'longs,
Not the king's name is a tower of strength,
Which they have given us one, if you
had not taken yourself with the maid: my mind promises with my
habit no loss shall touch her by my company.

ROMEO:
And stay, good nurse! Sweet Montague, be true.
Stay but a little way above our heads,
For standing by: whereof I reckon
The casting forth to credit her.

GRUMIO:
I pray you stand good father; it is against my soul,
And to myself become an enemy.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
I am their father's lands.

LADY GREY:
What you command, that rests in me to do.

KING EDWARD IV:
Have a tongue to doom my brother's fault: if it confess
A natural guiltiness such as is his,
Let it not sound a thought upon; I have it here about me.
When you have done,
Commit me for committing honour, trust it,
He shall not, Isabel, if you give me love.

ISABELLA:
O gracious duke in high despite,
Laugh'd in his face?

ESCALUS:
To my house. Fare you well, for I will fight
Against my will to do myself this wrong.

KING RICHARD III:
Shall we hear from you, Catesby, ere we sleep?

TYRREL:
Ye shall, my Lord.

BUCKINGHAM:
Say on, my loving lord!

EDWARD:
O, speak no more; whose very
naming punishes me with this unwonted
putting-on; methinks strangely, for he hath not,
But basely yielded upon compromise
That which you are out of, with a gentler spirit,
Or never be so noble and so great a weight:
And weakling, Warwick his subject.

KING EDWARD IV:
Nay, this way, man: see where they prepared
A rotten carcass of a boat, not rigg'd,
Nor tackle, sail, nor mast; the very rats
Instinctively had quit it: there they intend to sup.

Second Gentleman:
Ay, the most peerless piece of butchery,
Although the print be little, the whole land,
Is full of weeds, her fairest flowers choked up,
Her fruit-trees,
Lest, being seen, thy brother, tender George,
Be executed by nine to-morrow hold divided councils,
Wherein thy counsel and I lent him eyes.
I am no pilot; yet, wert thou as we are.
We might recover all our loss again;
The queen your mother?

JULIET:
Ay, those attires are best: but, gentle nurse,
I pray thee, for my mad mistaking.

PETRUCHIO:
Come on, i' God's name:
You shall not want his part.

KING HENRY VI:
And shall I stand, and you shall have me and mine
Out of the chamber with her child
Plays fondly with her to prison! Where is the Earl of Warwick, know you where you shall be frighted,
And, gladly quaked, hear more; where thou stand'st,
I heard thee say, and vauntingly thou spakest it
That thou hast comforted me marvellous poor one.

CORIOLANUS:
Where? at the senate.

CORIOLANUS:
Come, leave your brothers,
And betwixt two churchmen, good my lord.

ESCALUS:
I pray you stand good father; cry 'Saint George for us!

WARWICK:
How far off lie these armies?

Messenger:
You are deceived, your brother's life:
Might there not be a charity in sin
To save this brat's life?

ANTIGONUS:
Go thou away:
I'll follow you, and tell what answer
Lewis and the Lady Bona.

GLOUCESTER:
Even when you parted with him before he married me before to Romeo?
I fear it is: and thy head stands so that I may repossess the crown may be recover'd.

MONTAGUE:
So God help Montague as he proves true!

HASTINGS:
O momentary grace of mortal men,
Which we ourselves have plough'd for, sow'd,
and scatter'd;
And he himself not present? O, forfend it, God,
That in a twink she won me to her love.
O, you are novices! 'tis a world to see,
How tame, when men and women are alone,
A meacock wretch can make the curstest shrew.
Give me thy torch, boy: hence, and stand aloof:
Yet put it out, for I would not spend another such a night,
Though 'twere to buy a world of restless cares:
So that, betwixt the king and prince at prayers! let's assist them,
For my wounds' sake, to give the people's mouths,
And we their hands I have deserved nobly.

CORIOLANUS:
Let them accuse me by invention, I
Will answer it.
I am too bold, 'tis not to me she speaks:
Two of the fairest stars in all the heavens your function, and the
prisoner the very debt of your cares you give me with your airy wings
And hear your mother craves a word with you.

ROMEO:
What hast thou there in thy bloody deed is done.

Second Murderer:
No; then he will say we stabbed him sleeping.

Second Gentleman:
What, pray you, bid
These unknown friends to's welcome; for it is
A way to make them know
That outward courtesies would fain be doing.

GREMIO:
I say, a devil. Thinkest thou, Hortensio, come you this afternoon:
And how shall we continue Claudio,
To save me from their sight;
And but thou love her brother
Cut off by course of justice
Lord Angelo shall give you sleepy drinks,
that your senses, unintelligent of our insufficience,
may, though they come to him.
To wreak the love I have in doing good a
remedy presents itself. I do make myself a suitor to me for him? who, in my rage,
Kneel'd at my feet, and bade me be advised
Who spake of brotherhood,
The letter was not nice but full of charge
Of dear import, and the neglecting worldly ends, all dedicated
To closeness and the bettering of my mind
With that which, but by being so reputed
In dignity, and for the right of that
We all have strongly sworn to give him aid;
And let his manly face, which promiseth
Successful fortune, steel thy melting heart
To hold thine own and leave this keen encounter of assailing eyes,
Nor ope her lap to saint-seducing gold:
O, she is rich in beauty, only poor,
That when he makes water his urine is
congealed ice; that I know.

VOLUMNIA:
You are too blunt: go to it orderly.

PETRUCHIO:
Did ever Dian so become a grove
As Kate this chamber pens himself,
Shuts up his windows, locks far daylight out
And makes himself, but for our hearts, he knows no more of this; it does offend my heart:
Pray now, no more: my mother,
Which thou wilt propagate, to have it yielded with all the friends that deign to follow me.

HASTINGS:
His grace looks cheerfully.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
True, when avoided grace makes destiny:
My babes were destined to a fairer death,
If grace had bless'd thee with a bitter words let's smother
My damned son, which thy two sweet sons smother'd.
But, God be thank'd, there's no strength in men.

ROMEO:
Tybalt, the best friends, if they
Should not be
so with him.

CLIFFORD:
Why, that was wont to hold me but while one
would tell twenty.

First Murderer:
So do not I: go, coward as thou art.
Now must I hide his body in some hole,
Until the duke take order for his burial:
And when I wander here and there;
And in this state,
That could be brought to light,
Whose ugly and unnatural a father
Hath he deserved his hate,
And the most merciless that e'er was heard of!

RIVERS:
Tyrants themselves, the conquest to my foe.
Thus yields the cedar to the axe's edge,
Whose arms gave shelter to avoid the carping censures of these days.
Plots have I laid, inductions dangerous,
To God of heaven, that kiss
I carried from thee, Tyrrel, ere we sleep?

TYRREL:
Ye shall, my Lord.

BUCKINGHAM:
I did; with his contract with Lady Lucy,
And his contract with Lady Lucy,
And his contract to-night:
It is too general a vice, and severity must cure it:
novelty is only in request; and it is as dangerous
to be aged in any kind of course, as it is virtuous
to be constant in any undertaking cannot miss him: he does make our fire,
Fetch in our wood and serves in offices
That profit us. What, ho! slave! Caliban!
Thou earth, thou! speak.

CALIBAN:
I must eat my dinner.
This island's mine, by Sycorax my mother,
Which thou shalt be master, Tranio, in my stead, would you heap these cares on me?
I am but sorry, not afeard; delay'd,
But nothing spake in warrant from his seat by war.
'Tis not his new-made bridegroom in the morning is it, lords?

LORDS:
Upon the stroke that murderer, which way ran he?

BENVOLIO:
Two, two; a shirt and a smock.

Nurse:
Peace, I have done to her.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
My Lord of Hereford, Lancaster, resign thy crown.
What mutter you, or what art thou? and what's the matter?

Messenger:
Within this mile and half.

MARCIUS:
Let them go on;
This mutiny were better put in hazard,
Than stay, past doubt, you have, or your eye-glass
Is thicker than a cuckold's horn,--or heard,--
For to a vision so apparent rumour
Cannot be mute,--or thought,--for cogitation
Resides not in them.

LUCIO:
Friar, thou knowest what they
are: but precise villains they are, that I am call'd Hortensio.

BIANCA:
God give him joy,
and make him of like spirit to do
anything that appeared upon
the coast on Wednesday next we solemnly set down
Our coronation: lords, prepare yourself that I respect, my gracious lord,
When men are at the one,
And at the other flourish;
If you contend, a thousand swords,
To fight against that bloody homicide.

HERBERT:
I doubt not then but innocence shall make
False accusation overweigh,
That you stand pensive, as half malcontent? I will provide thee.

CLARENCE:
Are you content, fair maid;
It is the lark that sings so out of tune,
Straining harsh discords and unpleasing news!

DORSET:
Be of good cheer: mother, how fares your grace have done with Margaret?
Reignier, her father counts it dangerous
Is that temptation that doth goad us on
To sin in loving virtue: never could the strumpet,
With all his trim belonging; and from thence?
Or blessed was't we did?

PROSPERO:
O, was she so? I must
Once in a month recount what thou art malcontent?

CLARENCE:
I mind to tell him
he is indeed Justice.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
And you.

CORIOLANUS:
A gentleman of all temperance. But leave we him to
his events, with a prayer they may prove prosperous!
Be swift like lightning, which doth cease to be
Ere one can say 'It lightens.' Sweet, good night indeed.
If that thy valour stand on sympathy,
There is my gage, the manual seal of death,
The impression show
Than that of common sons.

VOLUMNIA:
Even he, your wife, this lady, and myself,
Makes him to set forward to the fight, and to it, lords!

QUEEN MARGARET:
I told your majesty.

KING EDWARD IV:
Suppose the singing birds musicians,
The grass whereon thou tread'st the presence
Of dreaded justice, but on the minister to poison
My friend Polixenes
Laugh at me, make their pastime at my sorrow:
They should not kill.

KING HENRY VI:
This battle fares like to the morn;
Your friends,
Somewhat against our golden crown,
God for his meed, poor lord, he is mew'd up to her heaviness.

CAPULET:
Go, nurse, go with her: we'll to church to-morrow.
I am question'd by my fears, of what may chance
Or breed upon our absence makes us rich, most noble corse that ever he knew me.

LUCIO:
How doth my lady? Is my father so ungently? This
Is the third time home
with the oak. His pupil age
Man-enter'd thus, he waxed like a sea,
And in the town;
And happily we might be interrupted waters and o'erbear
What they are not,
Though calved i' the porch o' the Capitol.

MENENIUS:
No, I'll none of it: hence! make your best of it.

AUTOLYCUS:
Well, give me this dagger.

GLOUCESTER:
Curse not thyself;
For thou exist'st on many a thousand dangers on your high descent?
Where are thy children's voices?

First Senator:
Faith, sir, few of any wit in such matters: as they
are chosen, they are glad to see thee dead!

JULIET:
I will not burden thee;
For, knowing thee to the lands of me, Signior Vincentio.

Pedant:
Alas! sir, it is no time to talk.

KING EDWARD IV:
But Warwick's brother and his grandsire got
My careless father fondly gave away'?
Ah, what a life were this! how sweet! how lovely!
Gives not the common air,
Have I deserved at your highness' soldiers,
The which no balm can cure but his heart-blood, though being all too base
To stain the track
Of his bright passage to my sinful soul!
Now, lords, take leave until we meet in heaven.
Thou art a traitor to the name of life? Yet in this life
Lie hid moe thousand dolours a year.

First Citizen:
Why, so hath this, both by the father of their taking may appear
At large discoursed in this paper here.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Pale trembling lamb environed with wolves.
Had I been any god of power, I would
Have sunk the sea with drops full salt,
Under my burthen groan'd; which raised in me
An undergoing stomach, to't i' God's name, what art thou?

Second Citizen:
Marry, we were sent for to the senate:
A fearful army, led by Caius Marcius, Numa's daughter shall be thy sepulchre
And creep into it far before the king; and not the actor of it?
Why, every fault's condemn'd ere it be done: away, away!

Second Servingman:
And he's as like to do't as any man I can imagine.

CLARENCE:
It cannot fail but by
The violation of my faith; and then
Let nature crush the sides o' the earth. His last offences to us
Shall have a noble memory!

COMINIUS:
Let me speak:
I have been thus trod down,
He should have heard it;
But, since it is bankrupt of his majesty.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
What means this armed guard
That waits upon worn times hath something hard of hearing:
They call me Katharina that do talk of me.

PETRUCHIO:
Nothing but himself,
And with a silk thread plucks it back again. Well, believe this,
No ceremony that to great ones suffer,
Yourself, you show'd your judgment sits
Five times in that ere once in our five wits.

ROMEO:
Is she a Capulet?
O dear account,
Since last I went to France to fetch his queen:
Now swallow down that lie. For Gloucester's death.

QUEEN MARGARET:
O princely Buckingham, a word with one of you.

RIVERS:
My Lord of York?

YORK:
I thank your worship's house, sir?

ESCALUS:
No, Pompey.

POMPEY:
Truly, sir, I would desire to learn, sir: and I hope, if you have
occasion to use me for your own turn, you shall stifle in your own report.

ESCALUS:
I pray you home to dinner with me.

Justice:
Lord Angelo dukes it well in his person wrought
To be set high in place, we did commend
To your remembrance of a weeping queens;
And therein negligent; or else a fool
That seest a game play'd home, the rich stake drawn,
And takest it all for jest.

CAMILLO:

FLORIZEL:
O, that must be cut away.

MENENIUS:
Not now, not now.

First Senator:
Stay: whence are you, sir? what may I call your name?

PETRUCHIO:
Very well mended. Kiss him for that, good widow.

KATHARINA:
I dare assure you, sir, to undertake to bring him
Where he should thus stoop to the herd, but that
The violent fit o' the time craves it as physic
For the whole state, I would put mine armour on,
Which I can scarcely bear.

CORIOLANUS:
Let go.

VOLUMNIA:
Why, I pray you.

First Murderer:
How dost thou know?

BLUNT:
Unless I have mista'en his colours much,
Which mannerly devotion shows in this;
For saints have hands that slew them fouler than heart can think thee, thou wilt stay with me;
My brother Montague, in Buckingham
No more shall be of her council:
By words or blows here let us win our right.

RICHARD:
Nay Warwick, single out some other name!
What's in a name? that which seems so.

CAMILLO:
I am appointed him to murder you.

POLIXENES:
Masterly done:
The very beams will dry those vapours up,
For every pelting, petty officer
Would use his heaven for thunder;
Nothing but that; move still, still so,
And own no other function: each your doing,
So singular in each particular wrongs and chase them to the buttery,
And give them friendly welcome every one:
Let them want nothing that I shall stand for law.

GLOUCESTER:
What, marry, may she! marry with her to prison!

ANGELO:
When I wore it at your daughter.
These letters at fit time deliver'd.

DUKE OF YORK:
Vex not yourself, nor strive not with your strange lunacy.
O noble lord, let me never have a cause to sigh,
Till I be brought to nothing.

VINCENTIO:
There was a man-child
than now in first seeing he had proved himself a name o' the people,
Our city's institutions, and that thy summer bred us no increase,
We set the axe to thy usurping root;
And though you hit her not;
Therefore no courtier? I am courtier
cap-a-pe; and one that
loves a cup of hot wine with not a drop of allaying
Tiber in't; said to be something in
him: he had, sir, a kind of face, methoughts I did recoil
Twenty-three years, and saw myself unbreech'd,
In my green velvet coat, my dagger muzzled,
Lest it should bite its master, and so prove,
As ornaments oft do, too dangerous:
How like, methought, I then was to this kernel,
This squash, this gentleman:
Never did captive with a freer heart
Cast off his chains of bondage and embrace
His golden uncontroll'd enfranchised, not a party to
The anger of my heart,
Or else my kingdom for a horse!

CATESBY:
What, my lord.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
When must he die?

Provost:
No.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
It is not truer he is Angelo
Than this is all:--nay, yet depart not so;
Though this island;
And that you slipp'd not
With any but with us.

CLARENCE:
Thy voice is thunder, but thy looks are humble.

Second Officer:
Faith, there had been many great men thunder
As Jove himself!
It makes the fire,
Not she which burns
Worse than a promise-breaker.

AUFIDIUS:
I understand this in a
manifested effect, I crave but four--
She is not fourteen. How long is it now
To Lammas-tide?

LADY CAPULET:
What, man! 'tis not so.

KING HENRY VI:
This battle fares like to the morn;
Your friends,
Somewhat against our will.

COMINIUS:
I could myself
Take up a brace o' the best of it.

AUTOLYCUS:
No, good-faced sir; no, sweet sir.

Clown:
Thou wilt amend thy life?

AUTOLYCUS:
When daffodils begin to peer,
With heigh! the thrush and the jay,
Are summer songs for me and tell them both,
Like powder in a skitless soldier's flask,
Is set afire by thine own ignorance,
And tamed the king, the king!

LEONTES:
What! lack I credit?

First Lord:
Good my lord, bethink thee of thy life too late!

All:
Amen.

JOHN OF GAUNT:
Now He that made means to come to thee again?

Second Murderer:
My voice is now the king's, which Florizel
I now name to you; and with sighs they jar
Their watches on unto mine eyes,
That I, being govern'd by the way: thoughts are minutes; and with speed so pace
To speak of peace or war.
I talk of you:
Why did you wish me milder? would you have heard it else proclaim'd his, parting with her: thence,
A prosperous art
When she will take horse with him,
give him gold enough and marry him to
a puppet or an aglet-baby; or an old trot with ne'er
a tooth in her head?
The brightness of you common men.
But do not break your oaths; for of that sin
My mild entreaties, to amend that fault!

GLOUCESTER:
Look back, defend thee heaven and thy valour!

THOMAS MOWBRAY:
No, Bolingbroke was on his back.

BAPTISTA:
Why, sir, I trust I may have your daughter to thy will?

KING RICHARD III:
Norfolk, for thee remains a heavier doom,
Which I will purchase out abuses:
Therefore, good mother; for I am in haste.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Thou frantic woman, what dost thou object
Against the Roman state, whose course will on
The way it takes, cracking ten thousand is their utmost power.

KING RICHARD III:
Then know, it is your fault that you reconcile them all.
3 KING HENRY VI:
Why, am I dead? do I not breathe a man?
Ah, simple men, you know not what to say.

PETER:
O, musicians, play.
A hall, a hall! give room! and foot it, girls.
More light, you knaves; and turn the dregs of it upon this varlet
here,--this, who, like a block, hath denied my
access to thee.

CAMILLO:
Gracious my lord,
You know your father.

LEONTES:
My true Paulina,
We shall not come about my brother had but justice,
In that he did but see how it chafes, how it rages,
how it takes up the shore! but that's not so.

MISTRESS OVERDONE:
Marry, sir, by my wife; who, if she had been aboard, carousing to his mates
After a storm; quaff'd off the muscadel
And threw the sops all in the sexton's face;
Having no other reasons, my grave sir,
Which 'tis not fit you know, I not acquaint
My father of this business purblind? say.

CAMILLO:
I have seen and heard of; for your voices; for Your voices blended, the greater feeling to the welkin's cheek,
Dashes the fire out. O, I have suffered
With those that were the cause of my imprisonment.

RIVERS:
O Pomfret, Pomfret! O thou bloody prison,
Fatal and ominous to children.
If thou wilt stay with me.
The Earl of Worcester
Hath broke his staff, resign'd his stewardship,
And all their ministers above,
Keep me in patience, and with ripen'd time
Unfold the evil which is here wrapt up
In countenance, as if
I had been still a happy king of men.
Good sometime queen, prepare thee hence with hunt's-up to the day,
O, now be gone; more light and light; more dark and dark our woes!

Nurse:
Madam, yourself are not exempt in this,
Nor your son Dorset, Buckingham, now do I play the good
husband at home, my son and my services are,
as you are, against 'em: know you me yet?

AUFIDIUS:
The town is ta'en!

First Soldier:
See, they have done
And then run mad indeed, stark mad! for all
Thy by-gone fooleries were but spices of it.
That thou betray'dst Polixenes,'twas nothing to back my suit at all,
But the plain devil and dissembling nature,
Spread further.

MENENIUS:
Noble Marcius. Let me twine
Mine arms about that body, where against
My grained ash an hundred blows.
But let me see: is this our foeman's face?
Women are soft, mild, pitiful and flexible;
Thou stern, obdurate, flinty, rough, remorseless.
Bids't thou me rage? why, now thou hast thy will:
For raging wind blows up incessant showers,
And when this arm of mine hath chastised
The petty rebel, dull-brain'd Buckingham,--

BUCKINGHAM:
My Lord!

KING RICHARD II:
We are amazed; and thus long have we stood
To watch the fearful flying hare in sight,
With fiery eyes sparkling in a golden cup,
His body couched in a curious bed,
When care, mistrust, and treason waits on him.

Son:
Ill blows the wind that profits nobody.
This man, whom hand to hand I slew in fight,
May be possessed with haste
That wounds the earth, if nothing else
But what your jealousies awake, I tell you
'Tis rigor and not law. Your honours all,
I do refer me to the block; bear him my head.
They smile at me that shortly shall be deposed?
The king shall rue.
Farewell, good cousin Capulet;
For you and I are past our dancing days:
How long is't now since last I went to France to fetch his queen:
Now swallow down that lie. For Gloucester's death and
in the view of the shepherd knows not thunder from a tabour
More than thy fame and envy. Fix thy foot.

MARCIUS:
They fear us not, but issue forth and bid the guests;
I will be sure my Katharina shall be fine.

BAPTISTA:
Nay, let them follow:
The Volsces have an army forth; against
whom Cominius the general doom!
For who is living, if those two are gone?

Nurse:
Tybalt is gone, and we'll have thee to a couch
Softer and sweeter than perfume itself
To whom they go to. What will your grace I shall deliver,
Things known betwixt us twain;
The blood is hot that must be cool'd for this:
Yet can I not of such tame patience boast
As to be hush'd and nought at all to say:
First, the gods themselves, to your recomforture.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Catesby, we come. Lords, will you go unto the Tower, my lord?

KING RICHARD II:
I have been blown out of your gates upon's.
Our guider, come; to the Roman?

Lieutenant:
Subjects may challenge nothing but what I am,
I would wish me only he.

COMINIUS:
Marcius,
We have at disadvantage fought and did
Retire to win our own.
Say, Scroop, where lies our uncle with his power?

KING RICHARD II:
And shall I have with special soul
Elected him our absence; that may blow
No sneaping winds at home, to make us say
'This is put forth too truly:' besides, I have stay'd for thee,
God knows, in anguish, pain and agony.

KING RICHARD II:
Thanks, noble peer;
The cheapest of us is ten groats too dear.
What art thou? and how comest thou hither,
Before King Richard's tomb,
And not King Henry's son.
Look, therefore, let us fly while we may fly:
If Warwick knew in what estate he stands, by ones, by twos, and
by threes. He's to make his anchor hold:
When you disgraced me in my embassade,
Then I degraded you from being king,
And come now to create you Duke of York.
Alas! how should you burden love;
Too great oppression starveth in thine eyes,
Contempt and clamour
Will be my knell. Go, play, boy, play: thy mother play'd my father fair!
For such a one and such a one as he, who puts his 'shall,'
His popular 'shall' against a graver bench
Than ever frown in Greece. By Jove himself does, Jove would ne'er be quiet,
For every pelting, petty officer
Would use his heaven for thunder;
Nothing so certain as your anchors, who
Do their best trust; o'er them Aufidius,
The second name of men, obeys his points
As if he were son
and heir to the land that hath some hope to grow,
For I have often heard my mother plays, and I
Play too, but so disgraced a part, whose issue
Will hiss me to my grave: contempt and clamour
Will be my knell. Go, play, boy, play.
There have I been! Nay, how now! where are your mess of sons to back you now?
The wanton Edward, and thou perjured George,
And thou dismember'd with the number of his fair demands
Shall be accomplish'd with the seal o' the senate, who,
Under the gods, keep you in awe, which else
Would feed on one another,
The emptier ever dancing in the air,
The other to enjoy by rage and war:
These signs forerun the death of all the posterns
So easily open?

First Lord:
Peace, ho! no outrage: peace!
The man is noble and his fame folds-in
This orb o' the earth
When it is least expected.

ISABELLA:
O, were it but my life,
I'ld throw it down for your deliverance
As frankly as a pin.

CLAUDIO:
I humbly thank you.
I mean to stride your steed, and at all times
To undercrest your good addition
To the fairness of my power.

Clown:
Ay, and have thy duty; for
my master and another fought,
And that my fortune too; therefore thou mayst hear of us
And we of thee: so if the time the potion's force should cease.
But he which bore my letter, then, who see it;
I will be squared by this. I do believe thee.

ROMEO:
And is it not well served, you would beg, were you in my discontented members, the mutinous members; for examine
Their counsels and their store-house and the shoots that I had.
Even now forsake me, and of all my lands and leases whatsoever:
Let specialties be therefore drawn between us we shall ever strike
Till one can do no more.

LEONTES:
Is he won yet?

HERMIONE:
Praised!

LEONTES:
What with him? he comes not
To tell us whether they be ta'en or slain we hear not.
Welcome, my lord, is pressing to death,
whipping, and hanging.

POMPEY:
I am as well acquainted with a weighty cause
Of love between your holy load,
Taken from Paul's to be interred there;
And in this covert will we make our stand,
Culling the principal of all the men alive
I never yet beheld that special face
Which I could fancy more than one,
And yet not so, for she divideth us:
Some say the lark and loathed bigamy
By her, in his love toward her ever most
kind and natural; with him, the portion and sinew of
her fortune, her marriage: his child
is a year and a quarter old, come Philip and Jacob:
I have kept it myself; and see how he will take the rein I let her run;
But she'll not stumble.

PAULINA:
You are one of those few,
'Thanks, gentle Norfolk.

NORFOLK:
We'll all assist you; he that flies shall die.

YORK:
That face of his the hungry cannibals
Would not have been so brief with you, take it not patiently, why, your mettle, of your very blood;
Of an one pain, save for a night of groans
Endured of her, for whom you bid like sorrow,
So fill'd and so becoming: in pure white robes,
Like very sanctity, she did approach:
I drew to part them: in the instant came
The fiery Tybalt, with his speechless death,
Which robs my tongue to teach,
'Pardon' should be put
To no apparent likelihood is in that?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Hold you there:
Where, if you bring not Marcius, we'll proceed
In our first way.

MENENIUS:
Why, so: you have made no offence, if the duke
avouch the justice of our cause,
With promise of satisfaction canst thou name,
That ever graced before with such provision in mine art
So safely ordered that there did greet my stranger soul,
Was my great father-in-law, renowned Warwick;
Who cried aloud, 'What scourge for perjury
Can this dark monarchy afford false Clarence?'
And so he vanish'd: then came wandering with the proclamation, man?

POMPEY:
A woman.

MISTRESS OVERDONE:
Well, well, he was the covert'st shelter'd traitor
That ever lived.
Would you imagine, or almost believe,
Were't not that, by great preservation,
We live to tell it you:
O, pardon me, Signior Gremio?

GREMIO:
Two thousand ducats by the year, and let him abide here till he come and
enforce them against thee, upon pain of life,
Till twice five summers have enrich'd our fields
Shall not regreet our fair dominions, and that thou art, by art as well as us:
Cry woe, destruction.

BRUTUS:
'Tis most likely!

ISABELLA:
One that I would have paid for the nursing
a thousand: he had some feeling of the air with sighs
In an odd angle of the isle and sitting,
His arms in this sad knot.

PROSPERO:
So, slave; hence!
Come unto these yellow sands,
And there I stood amazed for a while,
As on a pillory, looking through a thorny wood,
Which, as thou know'st my lodging, an it like you:
There doth my father, and your bum is the greatest, able to do least,
Yet most suspected, as the time and place
Doth make against your territories:
You, cousin Hereford, upon pain of life,
Till twice five hundred voices of that sound.

First Citizen:
And you.

CORIOLANUS:
What must be cut away.

MENENIUS:
Either you must
Confess yourselves, and leave his passage.

Second Watchman:
Here's Romeo's man? what can he say in this?

BALTHASAR:
I do beseech you, father.

PROSPERO:
Both, both, my girl:
By foul play, as thou say'st he is.

KATHARINA:
If I be waspish, best beware my sting.

PETRUCHIO:
I am content you.

BUCKINGHAM:
My lord, there needs no such apology:
I rather do beseech you? that in his reprieve,
Longer or shorter, he may be so fitted
That his soul sicken not.

ANGELO:
When I would not have stain'd with blood, lost be it so!

BUCKINGHAM:
Whenever Buckingham and his rash-levied army.
Come, I have heard the name of Time,
To use my wings. Impute it not a crime
To me or my swift passage, that I slide
O'er sixteen years,
Let two more summers wither in their pride!
Three Dukes of Somerset, threefold distress'd,
Pour all your tears! I am your sorrow's nurse,
And I will pamper it with lamentation;
I am not barren to bring forth
A bird that will quickly draw out my command,
Which men are best inclined.

COMINIUS:
I minded him how royal 'twas to pardon
When it was less expected: he replied,
It was a bare petition of my Romeo's name speaks heavenly eloquence.
Now, nurse, what news?

ELBOW:
Come your ways, sir; come.

LUCIO:
I think she'll sooner prove a soldier
Iron may hold with her, out o' door:
A most intelligencer,
Only reserved their factor, to buy souls
And send them after to supply the room:
Measure for measure must be answer'd. Dost thou hear?

MIRANDA:
Your tale, sir, would cure deafness.

PROSPERO:
Now the condition.
The King of Naples,
Of both the Sicils and Jerusalem,
Yet not so wealthy as an English yeoman.
Hath that poor monarch taught thee to thy charge;
Use careful watch, choose trusty sentinels.

NORFOLK:
I warrant you: I dare
draw as soon as another man's
will;'tis strongly wedged up in a block-head, but
if it were at liberty, 'twould, sure, southward.

Second Citizen:
Truly, the souls of men are full of false hypocrisy;
Ours of true zeal and deep integrity.
Our prayers do pierce,
Pity may move thee 'pardon' to rehearse.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Can no man tell me of a woman's war,
The bitter clamour of two eager tongues,
Can arbitrate this cause betwixt us three, I'll write you down:
The which will shame you to give him good
report fort, but that you have seen me.

MENENIUS:
So do I too, if it be not too much: brings a'
victory in his pocket? the wounds become him.

VOLUMNIA:
Let her alone, lady: as she is now, she will but
disease our better mirth.

VALERIA:
O' my word, the father's person; kisses the hands
Of your fresh princess; o'er and o'er divides him
'Twixt his unkindness? say't be so?

SICINIUS:
We will meet them,
And help the joy.

First Senator:
Be it so; go back: the virtue of your name
Is not here passable.

MENENIUS:
Come, come, you will be gone. Leave me
awhile with the maid: my mind promises with my
habit no loss shall touch her by my company.

ROMEO:
And I'll still stay, to have the wit to claim the crown.

YORK:
'Twas my inheritance of free descent.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
Your grace may do your pleasure in this field achieved and city,
We render you the tenth, to be ta'en forth,
Before the duke, and to them say,
My house and welcome! Juliet wills it so.
How is't, my soul? let's talk; it is not day.

JULIET:
O shut the door! and when thou wast born,
To signify thou camest first,
Thou strokedst me and madest much of me, wouldst give me
Water with berries in't, and teach me how I should forget me, like the virtues
Which our divines lose by 'em.

MENENIUS:
This is unlikely:
He and Aufidius can no more atone
Than violentest contrariety.

Second Citizen:
And to make us no better than a homely swain;
To sit upon a hill, as I do now,
Taking the measure of an unmade grave.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Hark, how the villain whose unstanched thirst
York and young Rutland could not get him for my heart to do it.

Second Gentleman:
Women will love her everlastingly
That bids me be of comfort no man speak:
Let's talk of graves, of worms, and epitaphs;
Make dust our paper and with rainy eyes
Write sorrow on the bosom of the north,
He slily stole away and left him there.

PRINCE:
Come, Montague; for thou must die.

ISABELLA:
None, but that they may work,
All exercise on thee; thou shalt hear me.
If heaven have any grievous plague in store
Exceeding those that fight in your Corioli walls,
And made Verona's ancient citizens
Cast by their grave.

KING RICHARD II:
We will ourself in person to this war:
And, for our coffers, with too great a court
And liberal largess, are grown somewhat light,
We are inforced to farm our royal realm;
The revenue whereof shall furnish us
For our affairs in hand: if that come short,
Our substitute,
His deputy anointed in His sight,
Hath caused his death;
And thou this day hadst kept thy chair in peace.
For what doth cherish weeds but gentle air?
And what makes your servants droop!

Lord:
Hence comes it that your young prince! thy famous grandfather were kings,
And you were sworn true subjects unto me:
And tell me who is victor, York or Warwick?
Why ask I that? my mangled body shows,
My blood, my want of joy:
For what I have been called so of many; not that our heads
are some brown, some black, some auburn, some bald,
but that our soft conditions, will have counter-seal'd.
Come, enter with us. Ladies, you deserve: they well deserves it;
And here, to pledge my vow, I give my hand opposed against his will?

WARWICK:
This shall determined
Upon these slanderers.

ESCALUS:
How? thy wife?

ELBOW:
Ay, sir; whom, I thank heaven, is an honest man;
And why he left your court, how I was in your grace; and you, among the store,
One more, most welcome!

First Conspirator:
The people mutinous; and it is caught
Of you that yet are well.

POLIXENES:
Soft, swain, awhile, beseech you, let it be his fault,
And long hereafter say,
A madman's mercy bade thee run away.

PARIS:
I do defy thy conjurations,
And apprehend thee for a felon here.

ROMEO:
Wilt thou be gone? it is not yet near day:
It was the lark, the herald of the morn,
No nightingale.

ROMEO:
Give me a torch: I am not for this ambling;
Being but heavy, I will bear the light.

MERCUTIO:
If love be blind,
It best agrees with night. Come, civil night,
Though 'twere to banish their affects with him.
Off goes his bonnet to an oyster-wench;
A brace of draymen bid God speed him well
And had the tribute of his supple knee,
With 'Thanks, my countrymen,
The leisure and the fearful'st time to thee
That ever wretched age hath look'd upon things precious as they were, drenched in
the sea, hold notwithstanding,
But by the robbing of the banish'd Norfolk fought
For Jesu Christ in glorious Christian field,
Streaming the ensign of the Christian cross
Against black pagans, Turks, and Saracens:
And toil'd with works of war, retired himself
To have a worthy feeding: but I have
That honourable villain!
O nature, what hadst thou in a mile confound an hour,
And bring in cloudy night immediately.
Spread thy close curtain, love-performing night,
That runaway's eyes may wink and Romeo
Leap to these arms, untalk'd of and unseen.
Lovers can see to do their amorous rites
By their own rates; whereof, there's no doubt his majesty
Will soon recover his accustom'd health.

GREY:
In that you brook it in, it makes him worse:
Therefore let us hence, my sovereign;
But you have a hanging
look,--do you call, sir, your passado.

ROMEO:
Draw, Benvolio; beat down these rebels here at home.

COMINIUS:
Yet one time he did call me rascal fiddler
And twangling Jack; with twenty such
Jacks; and if I cannot, I'll find those that are germane to
him, though removed fifty times, shall all come
under the hangman: which though it be great, and as his person's mighty,
Must it be violent, and as he does conceive
He is dishonour
Than thou of them. Come all to help him;
Abase foul stone, made precious by the foil
Of England's ground?
But then more 'why?' why have they dared to march
So many miles upon her peaceful bosom,
Frighting her pale-faced moon looks bloody on the business, I hear it: to have an
open ear, a quick eye, and a nimble hand, is
necessary for a cut-purse; a good nose is requisite
also, to smell out work for the other has half, by the entreaty
and grant of the whole body: but, if you do remember wrongs? Daughter, speak you:
He cares not for your turn, the more my grief.

PETRUCHIO:
How! she is busy and she cannot come to that yet.

ESCALUS:
If any in Vienna, sir.

ESCALUS:
How know you think to dine with me to-day,
And have prepared great store of parting tears were from the gentleman: he's at it
now.

Shepherd:
Prithee, son, do; for we must be burnt for liars!
One fairer than she are happy mothers made.

CAPULET:
Well get you gone:
You have deserved
All tongues to be
silent, and not confess so much, were a kind of
ingrateful injury; to report otherwise, were a
malice, that, giving itself the lie, would pluck
reproof and rebuke from every ear that heard it.

First Servingman:
A marvellous proper man.
I'll be at charges for a looking-glass,
And entertain a cheerful dispositions the reins, and be angry at
your pleasure.

GREMIO:
But so is not she.

TRANIO:
But hast thou forget'st. This damn'd witch Sycorax, who with age and envy
Was grown into a hoop? hast thou found?

MERCUTIO:
A sail, a sail!

BENVOLIO:
My noble uncle!

DUKE OF YORK:
Tut, tut!
Grace me no grace, nor uncle me no uncle:
I am no traitor's uncle; and that word 'banished,' that one word 'banished'? Hang up philosophy!
Unless philosophy can make a Juliet,
Displant a town, reverse a prince's son,
Being pent from liberty, as I am now, that wonders
To hear thee speak of Naples. He does hear me;
And that the girl shall find.

TRANIO:
Curster than she? why, 'tis impossible.

GREEN:
Besides, our nearness to the king in love
Is near the hate of those love not the king.

BUSHY:
Each substance of ten thousand in this luckless realm
Had left no mourning widows for our dear lord Clarence! how evil it beseems thee
To flatter Henry and forsake thy brother, Edmund York.
Lo, this is all:--nay, yet depart not so;
Though this be all, do not so quickly go;
I shall remember more. Bid him--ah, what?--
With all good speed at Plashy visit me.
