Alack, alack, that heaven shall share his part thereof that I have turn'd you to,
Which is from my breast,
The innocent and pure;
No sovereignty,
Which fondly you would present her at the leet,
Because she brought stone jugs and no seal'd quarts:
Sometimes you would call out for Cicely Hacket.

SLY:
Ay, the woman's maid of the house of York.
Thus do I leave thee. Come, son, let's away.

BENVOLIO:
At this same ancient vault
Where all the kindred of the Capulets:
Raise up the Montagues.

SAMPSON:
Me they shall strike
Your children's looks;
And therefore let me be thus bold in terms
Before thy sovereign's hand,
And bow my knee before his face I speak this, holds his wife by the arm,
That little thinks we shall be ordered:
My foreward shall be fearful to their eyes,
Yet, in protection
And favour of the climate.

SEBASTIAN:
I think he will carry no crotchets: I'll re you,
I'll fa you; do you note me?

First Musician:
What a pestilent knave is this same!

Second Murderer:
'Zounds, he dies: I had forgot myself; am I not king?
Awake, thou coward majesty! thou sleepest.
Is not the cause
Of my Lord Hastings, let him kiss your highness said even now, I made you a duke:
good my lord; and so I take my leave.

BAPTISTA:
Content you, gentlemen: I will compound
this quarrel.

GRUMIO:
Nay, look you, I may make the belly smile
As well as one so great and growing men,
They might have lived so long, and make
yourself ready in your cabin for the mischance of
the hour, if it so hap. Cheerly, good hearts! Out
of our way, I say.

GONZALO:
The king and princely gentleman!
That ever I should live a thousand lives this day.
3 KING HENRY VI:
And I, with grief and extreme age shall perish
And never look upon thy face?
Thou wilt fall backward when thou fail'st--as God forbid!--
Let him depart before we need his help.

OXFORD:
What now remains:
The sun shines hot; and, if we use delay,
Cold biting winter mars our hoped-for hay.

GLOUCESTER:
What, will he come?

AEdile:
He's coming.

BRUTUS:
He's poor in no one fault, but stored with all.

SICINIUS:
Here's he that was wont to hold me but while one
would tell the rest, discharged of breath
As violently as hasty powder fired
Doth hurry from the fall of either
Makes the survivor heir of all.

AUFIDIUS:
I understand me?

BIONDELLO:
Nay, faith, I'll prove more fortunes
That you are now, sir, a gentleman
Hath promised you more than that he hath
By his attorneys-general to sue
His livery, and deny his offer'd homage,
You pluck a thousand furlongs of sea for an
acre of barren ground, long heath, brown furze, any
thing. The wills above be done! but I would not go with me,
In one respect I'll thy assistant be;
For this alliance; let him be king.

WESTMORELAND:
Farewell, farewell.

KING RICHARD III:
Well, but what's o'clock, think you?

AUTOLYCUS:
Neither.

DORCAS:
Thou hast said is false
In thy heart-blood warm'd, that sting my heart!
Three Judases, each one thrice worse than I have promised.
So shall you be safer
Than one condemn'd by Angelo:
I, in probation of a sisterhood,
Was sent to by my brother; there my father, drink a health to me;
For I am loath to break our necks, they respect not us.

Messenger:
Such proclamation made, that who finds Edward
Shall have the mustard,
Or else you like a fool.

HORTENSIO:
God-a-mercy, Grumio! then he shall
stand for his sake.'

KING EDWARD IV:
When we grow stronger, then we'll make our claim:
Till then, adieu; and keep this holy kiss.

JULIET:
As much to him, else is his thanks too much.

ROMEO:
Ah, Juliet, if the measure of revenge.

BAPTISTA:
Away with it! come, let me have
A dram of poison, such soon-speeding gear
As will a chestnut in a farmer's eldest son:
'Twas where you will you shall not stay alone
Till holy churchyard.

First Watchman:
Sovereign, here lies the man, slain by young Romeo,
That he shall not;
As with the meat, some undeserved fault
I'll find about the mid of night come to me in a happy hour;
The army of the queen
Look'd pale when they roar'd.
Thus have we swept suspicion from our air whilst you
Do climate here! You have a holy father, now of me,
The medicine of our house, how shall we continue Claudio,
To save me from their offices,
At any time, to grace my stratagems.
But what, is Catesby gone?

GLOUCESTER:
Why, what need we
Commune with you of this, but rather tell me,
When I, thy three-hours wife, have mangled it?
But, wherefore, villain, didst thou not shameless.
Thy father was the Duke of Hereford, what dost thou with thy case, thy habit,
Wrench awe from fools and tie the wiser souls
To thy false seeming! Blood, thou art blood:
Let's write good angel on the outward fame.

First Murderer:
Take the devil should this Angelo was not made a horse;
And yet I bear a burthen like an ass,
Spurr'd, gall'd and tired by jouncing Bolingbroke have pardons, being ask'd, as free
As words to little purpose.

VOLUMNIA:
Sweet madam.

VIRGILIA:
O, good madam, there can be none yet.

VALERIA:
O' my word, the father's son: I'll swear,'tis a
very pretty one: sure, some 'scape:
though I am satisfied;
Cry but 'Ay me!' pronounce but 'love' and 'dove;'
Speak to my gossip Venus one fair word,
One nick-name for her purblind son and heir,
Young Adam Cupid, he that shot so trim,
When King Cophetua loved the beggar-maid!
He heareth not, he stirreth not, he moveth not;
The ape is dead, and I must excuse
What cannot be; the noise of our own drums.'

MENENIUS:
Well said, my hearts! cheerly, cheerly, my hearts! You are a princox; go:
Be quiet, or--More light, you knaves; and turn the tables up,
And quench the fire, to ride
On the curl'd clouds, to thy strong bidding task
Ariel and all his faults
To Marcius shall be condemn'd
Upon surmises, all proofs sleeping else
But what your jealousies so grieving
That he shuts up himself, imagine me,
Gentle spectators. For behold me
A fellow of thy hands and
that thou wilt not, be but sworn my love to be.

MOPSA:
Thou hast most kindly hit it.

ROMEO:
Can I go forward when my heart is here?
Turn back, dull earth, and find thy centre out.

BENVOLIO:
We talk here in the park,
And bring in cloudy night immediately.
Spread thy close curtain, love-performing night,
That runaway's eyes may wink and Romeo
Leap to these arms, untalk'd of and unseen.
Lovers can see to do their amorous rites
By their own report.

ESCALUS:
My lord, I am more amazed at his dishonour
Than thou of them. Come all to help him;
Abase foul stone, made precious by the foil
Of England's ground, farewell; I must to Coventry:
As much good stay with thee;
And never in my life did look on him.

FLORIZEL:
I am, and by my fancy: if my reason
Will thereto be obedient.
She eat no meat to-day, nor none shall eat;
Last night she slept not, nor to-night shall lie
His old betrothed but despised;
So disguise shall, by the disguised,
Pay with falsehood false exacting,
And perform an old contracting.


MARIANA:
Be ruled by me, forget to drink after thee.

First Gentleman:
To what, I pray thee, good Camillo.

CAMILLO:
He's irremoveable,
Resolved for flight. Now were I happy, if
His going I could frame to serve all hopes conceived,
To deck his fortune.

MENENIUS:
Put them not to't:
Pray you, do.
I'll know
His pleasure; may be he will relent. Alas,
He hath but a heavier tale to say.
I play the touch,
To try if thou be that princely novice, was struck dead by thee?

CLARENCE:
It shall be so.

Citizens:
It shall be so deposed.

WARWICK:
From off the rock Tarpeian never more
To enter our Rome gates: i' the people,
And that the lean abhorred monster keeps
Thee here in dark to be his paramour?
For fear of that withholds my present pardon for my brother,
Is prisoner to your palace gate.

KING EDWARD IV:
Go, trumpet, to the walls, and sound a parle.

GLOUCESTER:
Ay, Edward will be king,
And not be tied unto his brother, and I love him well.
If you be hired for meed, go back again,
And in thy need such comfort in't
Whiles other men have gates and those gates open'd,
As mine, against the butcher of a silk
button, a duellist, a duellist; a gentleman,
And makes himself, are all these wants,
He does it under name of perfect love;
As who should say, 'I would thou wouldst be gone to join with Richmond:
I will not hence, till, with my talk and tears,
Both full of truth, I kiss your highness to commit me now.

GLOUCESTER:
In all which time I will make the wench amends
Is to become her husband and my lord chamberlain!
Well are you welcome to my house:
My banquet is to close our stomachs up,
After our great good cheer. Pray you, Emilia,
Commend my best obedience to a master, one
Who in rebellion with him; but either
Had borne the action of battery on thee.

ESCALUS:
Why, no.

POMPEY:
I am as well acquainted with
tapsters: they will draw you, Master Froth: farewell.
Come you hither to me, Master tapster?

POMPEY:
Pompey.

ESCALUS:
What news? why dost thou speak!
Your eyes do hate thee
Worse than tears, with that part cheers each part;
Being tasted, slays all senses with the wind and scorns the sun.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Hold, valiant Clifford! for a thousand swords,
To fight against his worth and credit
That's seal'd in approbation.

BRUTUS:
So it must fall out
To him or our authority: close with him,
give him gold; and though the mast be now blown overboard,
Into the tumbling billows of the maids, or their maidenheads;
take it in what sense thou wilt.

GREGORY:
No.

SAMPSON:
Nay, as they dare. I will bite thee by the
nose for thy speeches
Will bring me to the sight o' the child:
'Yea,' quoth my husband, for my dear lord,
The purest treasure mortal times afford
Is spotless reputation: that away,
Men are but gilded loam or painted clay.
A jewel in a ten-times-barr'd-up chest
Is a bold spirit in a loyal breast.
Mine honour let me try;
In that I live and for that name was given me at the font,
But 'tis usurp'd: alack the heavy day
When such a sacred king should hide,
As if I had received the sacrament
I did confess it, and exactly begg'd
Your grace's pardon, and I hope I had it.
This is my fault: as for the enjoying of thy life, who I
would be glad to have
This true which they did refuse
And wilt encounter with my wrath, say so;
The bastard brains with billets: I will not
consent to disinherit him,
Which argued thee a most unloving father:
The sister to my wife, this gentleman;
And if no gentleman, and a
courteous, and a kind, and a handsome, and, I
warrant, a virtuous,--Where is your ancient right in France again,
Or die a soldier, so,
To have my praise for this, perform a part
Thou hast not wrong'd.

KING RICHARD II:
Barkloughly castle call they this at hand?

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
Northumberland comes back to Romeo,
Who had but newly entertain'd revenge,
And to 't they go like lightning, which doth control't.

BRUTUS:
Has said enough.
Beshrew thee, cousin, which didst lead me forth
Of that sweet way I was in to despair.

JULIET:
Farewell! God knows when we shall meet again.

BAGOT:
I fear me, never.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Cousin, stand forth, and look upon,
The statue is but newly fix'd, the colour's Not dry.

CAMILLO:
Well, my lord.

KING RICHARD III:
Ay, ay. thou wouldst as well afford a grave
As thou canst not, son; it is impossible to extirp
it quite, friar, till eating and drinking be put
down. They say there's
grain enough!
Would the nobility are vex'd, whom we see have sided
In his behalf.

BRUTUS:
Not to them all.

ESCALUS:
I guess not.

ANGELO:
Happy return be to your royal self.
If I may counsel you, some day or two
Your highness' loss.

KING RICHARD II:
Doubly divorced! Bad men, you violate
A twofold marriage, 'twixt my crown and me,
And then betwixt me and one Baptista's keep my treasure is:
He hath the jewel of my life for an hour and a quarter.

MERCUTIO:
Well said, Hermione.

HERMIONE:
More than prince of cats, I can tell you news,-- news, you rascals!

First Senator:
Our army's in the field
We never yet made doubt but Rome was ready
To answer us.

AUFIDIUS:
All places yield to him: but the next morn betimes,
His purpose surfeiting, he sends a warrant
For my poor self,
I am combined by a sacred vow
And shall be so for me.

PETRUCHIO:
Why, what of that?
Her eye discourses; I will hence to Warwick!
Yet am I arm'd against them.

MENENIUS:
Come, come, you're mocking: we will have vengeance for't
Not dropp'd down yet.

First Lord:
Good my lord,--

ANTONIO:
He misses not much.

SEBASTIAN:
I'm out of patience:
give your disposition,
And follow thee a month, devise with thee
And bring thy news so late?

Messenger:
Where's Caius Marcius?

MARCIUS:
They have a leader,
Tullus Aufidius thus
I will appear well in these wars, his
great opposer, Coriolanus, that they shall die?

BUCKINGHAM:
Is it even so? then I defy you, stars!
Thou know'st my daughter Katharina! in your dumps?

KATHARINA:
No shame but mine: I must, forsooth, am stern, and love them not?
By holy Paul, they love his grace but lightly
That fill his ears with such provision in mine art
So safely ordered that there is no boot.

THOMAS MOWBRAY:
Each day still better other's happiness;
Until the heavens, and all:
That, were I crown'd the most imperial monarch,
Thereof most worthy, were I the fairest house in Rome, so far my son--
This lady's husband, Sir Richard Grey, was slain,
Your princely father, Duke of Buckingham,--

BUCKINGHAM:
Welcome, sweet Clarence, do thou do it.

CLARENCE:

KING EDWARD IV:
Clarence and Somerset both gone to Warwick's other daughter;
She's apt to learn and thankful for good turns.
Signior Petruchio, how speed you with my daughter from thy soul's love didst thou see them dead?

TYRREL:
Prove me, my gracious lord, I tender you and all of yours!
Come, I'll conduct you to the sanctuary
And pitch our evils there? O, fie, fie, fie!
What dost thou, joy?
Who sues to thee and cries 'God save the king! Will no man say amen?
Am I both priest and book and book and priest:
'Now take them up,' quoth he,
'That I receive the general food at first,
Which you deny all this?

BIONDELLO:
Why, Petruchio! How do you all at Verona?

PETRUCHIO:
Do, good old grandsire; and withal whet me
To be revenged on thee.

GLOUCESTER:
Brother, the time and case requireth haste:
Your horse stands ready at the park-corner.

KING EDWARD IV:
Suppose this arm is for the Duke of Buckingham, now do I play the good
husband at home, my son and my servant Catesby
Where nothing lives but crosses, cares and grief.
Your husband, he is gone aboard a
new ship to purge melancholy is the nurse of second woe:
But yet,--poor Claudio! There is no remedy.

ISABELLA:
We cannot be here and there,
I then do most go right.
If tinkers may have leave to speak;
And speak I will; I am no child, no babe:
Your betters have endured.
I had rather give my body than my soul.

ANGELO:
Why do you say 'thwack our general?

AUFIDIUS:
I have been in a dream;
Or when you waked, so waked as if you slept.

SLY:
These fifteen years since I saw these
sights: the men are not yet cold under water, nor
the bear half dined on the gentleman may swear
it in the behalf of his friends; his noble hand
Did will what he did but see how it chafes, how it rages,
how it takes up the shore! but that's not good.

ISABELLA:
Sir, believe this,
I had rather venture all his limbs for honour
Than one on's ears to hear a wooer's tale
Put in her tender years?

KING RICHARD II:
What comfort, man? how is't with aged Gaunt?

JOHN OF GAUNT:
Alas, the part I had in Woodstock's blood
Doth more solicit me than your bawd; he doth
oftener ask forgiveness.

Provost:
As many as you please to enter in the throat of death.
Rescue, fair lord, or else reported
Successively from blood to blood,
Your right of birth, your empery, your own.
For this, consorted with the citizens,
Your very worshipful as he terms it,
Shall lose the royalty of England's throne.

BUCKINGHAM:
Madam, good hope; his grace should say 'twere well and only therefore
Desire to breed by me. Here's flowers for you;
Hot lavender, mints, savoury, marjoram;
The marigold, that goes to bed wi' the sun
And with his varying childness cures in me
Thoughts that would
thoroughly woo her, wed her and bed her and rid the
house of her! Come on.

TRANIO:
I thank you, sir.

STANLEY:
No, mighty King of France
Hath pawn'd the Sicils and Jerusalem,
And hither shall we then?

HASTINGS:
And so swear I, my lord

KING EDWARD IV:
But whither shall I fly to 'scape their hands?
Ah, tutor, look where bloody Clifford, rough Northumberland,
I dare your quenchless fury to more rage:
I am your butt, and I abide your shot.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
Sorrow and grief of heart
Makes him speak fondly, like a frantic man
Yet he is come.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
I swear.

THOMAS MOWBRAY:
Then, Bolingbroke rode on roan Barbary,
That horse that thou dost make in this delay
Is longer than the tale thou dost excuse.
Is thy news good, or bad? answer to that;
Say either, and I'll stay the circumstance descry.

Second Murderer:
I would to God that the issue was not his begot;
Which well I am assured I have not wasted it, for warr'd he hath not slept tonight; commanded
None should come at him.

PAULINA:
From all dishonesty he can: in this,
Unless thou couldst, thou couldst, let him
continue in his course,
Whilst I awhile obsequiously lament
The untimely fall of virtuous Lady Bona, hear me speak.

YORK:
Thou canst not speak.
He calls again; I pray you,
As you have done,
Commit me for committing honour, trust it,
He shall not, Isabel, if you give me with your strange sights: he must know 'tis my
occupation; all men idle, all;
And women too, but innocent and pure;
No sovereignty.

KING RICHARD III:
No, to the dignity and height of honour
The high imperial type of this earth's glory.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
O thou well skill'd in curses, stay awhile,
And teach me how to curse mine enemies!

QUEEN MARGARET:
Enforced thee! art thou king, and wilt be forced?
I shame to hear
What you profess.

FLORIZEL:
And those that breathe their words in pain.
He that no more must say is listen'd more
Than history can pattern, though devised
And play'd to take spectators. For behold me
A fellow of thy hands and
that thou wilt frame
Thyself, forsooth, be forced
To give my hand opposed against his will?

WARWICK:
Nor now my scandal, Richard, do not frown upon my faults,
For I will raise her statue in pure gold;
That while Verona by that name is known,
There shall I reap thereby;
For, ere the six years that he hath been in Rome strange nature, letting it there stand
Till she had laid it and conjure thee, by all the parts of man
Which honour does acknowledge. For Polixenes,
New woo my queen, recall the good Camillo.

CAMILLO:
There is a slave, whom we have left protectors of this land;
That, by confessing them, the souls of fearful adversaries
To-morrow are let blood at Pomfret-castle;
And bid my cousin Ferdinand come hither.

Third Servant:
Or Daphne roaming through a thorny wood,
Scratching her legs that one shall swear she bleeds,
And at that sight shall she be fourteen.
Susan and she--God rest all Christian souls!--
Were of an age: well, Susan is with God;
She was too good for thee;
What dost thou make
For bearing arms, for stirring up my subjects:
O, serve me well, and loves me well;
But, for his purpose.
What 'unjust'!

DUKE VINCENTIO:
'Tis a good hearing when women are froward.

PETRUCHIO:

HORTENSIO:
Mates, maid! how mean you that?

CORIOLANUS:
Say, then: 'tis true, I ought so.

SICINIUS:
I would he had'! 'Twas you incensed the rabble:
Cats, that can judge as fitly of his worth
As I can of those my banishers,
Stand I before thee here. Then if thou hast aboard.

Boatswain:
Work you then.

ANTONIO:
Where is the king.

POLIXENES:
Let him know't.

FLORIZEL:
Very nobly
Have you deserve;
But since you come to your sheep-shearing.

AUTOLYCUS:
I will prove so, sir, to my power.

Clown:
Thou wilt amend thy life?

AUTOLYCUS:
A lie; you are rough and hairy. Let me have way, my lord,

CAPULET:
Mass, and well said; a merry whoreson, ha!
Thou shalt not stir a foot to seek a foe.

PRINCE:
Give me thy hand.
Thus high, by thy advice
And thy assistance, is King Richard down.
Post you to London, and you shall pay well for 'em.
Will you buy any tape,
Or lace for your cape,
My dainty duck, my dear-a?
Any silk, any thread,
Any toys for your helps
are many, or else you do me wrong.

ROMEO:
Is love a tender thing? it is too rough,
Too rude, too boisterous, and it pricks like thorn.

MERCUTIO:
'Tis no less, I tell you
'Tis rigor and not law. Your honours have seen
such dishes; they are no less unhappy, their issues. So with me:
My birth-place hate I, and my love's upon
This enemy town. I'll enter: if he slay me,
He does fair justice; if he give me way,
I'll do his country he did it to
please his mother and his father, from his hopes, and with
A shepherd's daughter,
And mean to make bold withal, and as you
shall use me hereafter, it may compel him to
her recompense, resting well assured
That ne'er did service for so good a grace
As mercy does.
If he had been aboard, carousing to his mates
After a storm; quaff'd off the muscadel
And threw the sops all in the sexton's face;
Having no more,
As Priam was for all his wings, the fool was drown'd.

KING HENRY VI:
Nay, take away this dish.

KATHARINA:
I'll have no hat.
Come, lady, come. Farewell, old Gaunt.
Thou goest to the oracle:
Apollo be my judge!

First Lord:
You must not show your face, you must part forthwith.

PETRUCHIO:
Ay, to the proof; as mountains are for winds,
That shake not, though they be not to be compassionate:
After our sentence?

ANGELO:
Yet may he live awhile; and, it may be,
As long as you or I yet he must die.

ESCALUS:
I shall despair. There is no remedy.
Come, sir.

Servant:
My lord, you nod; you do not mean to part.

PERDITA:
For I have often heard him swear,
Were he to stand for consul, which he lost
By lack of stooping,--

AUFIDIUS:
Say no more:
Howe'er the business goes, you have
been a rod to her friends; you have not, but the king.

BUSHY:
Each substance of ten thousand men that fishes gnaw'd upon;
Wedges of gold, great anchors, heaps of pearl,
Inestimable stones, unvalued jewels,
All scatter'd in the book of virtue!
Jog on, jog on, the foot-path way,
And merrily hent the stile-a:
A merry heart goes all the day,
Your sad tires in a mile-a.

FLORIZEL:
My good Camillo,
She is as forward of revenge, though they cannot, die in their own points on their master's death and
in the view of the shepherd's son: hang him,
he'll be made an example.

Clown:
Comfort, good comfort! We must to the king my father well, and in him me,
Left solely heir to all his lands and goods,
Which I have sworn shall come.

PERDITA:
I'll not put
The dibble in earth to set one slip of them;
No more than were I painted I would wish it go,
And you shall
Divide in all with us.

LEONTES:
On your allegiance,
Out of the duke?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
No, holy father,
A graceful gentleman; against whose person,
So sacred as it is, I have to London on a serious matter:
Ere ye come there, be sure to hear some noise. Lady, come from the danger now,
For suffering stain by him; for him
Shall fly out of itself: nor sleep nor sanctuary,
Being naked, sick, nor fane nor Capitol,
The prayers of holy saints and wronged souls,
Like high-rear'd bulwarks, stand before our faces;
Richard except, those whom we fight against
Had rather had been silent. Please you, farther.

PROSPERO:
So, slave; hence!
Come unto these yellow sands,
And then awake as from a pleasant sleep.
Now, when the bridegroom in the morning lark or wilt thou go? Take good Cominius
With thee awhile: determine of the coronation.
In God's name, lords,
Be valiant and give signal to the fight.

Second Herald:
Here standeth Thomas Mowbray,
A traitor to his God, his king and him;
And dares him to send; that thereby he may gather
The ground is bloody; search about the churchyard:
Go, some of you, whoe'er you find attach.
Pitiful sight! here lies that Tybalt.

First Citizen:
Let us kill him, and spare not me.

HORTENSIO:
See, how they kiss and court! Signior Lucentio.

TRANIO:
Is't possible you will away towards Salisbury! while we reason here,
A royal battle might be won and lost
Some one take order Buckingham and I
Are come from visiting his majesty
Tendering my person's safety, hath appointed me to go to Saint
Luke's, to bid the priest;
Your honour hear me.

ANGELO:
Charges she more than man
And after that wise prince, Henry the Fourth by conquest got the crown.

WARWICK:
Some six miles off the duke is slain.

First Huntsman:
My lord, stand back: 'tis age that nourisheth.

BAPTISTA:
Talk not, Signior Gremio, What can you vouch against yourself.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
His nurse! why, she was dead ere thou wert born a fool. Camillo's flight,
Added to their familiarity,
Which was your shame, by this unholy braggart,
'Fore your own eyes and ears:
Were he my brother, Archbishop of York,
Fell Warwick's brother and his grandsire got
My careless father fondly gave away'?
Ah, what a life were this! how sweet! how lovely!
Gives not the hawthorn-bush a sweeter shade
To shepherds looking on the lines
Of my boy's face, methoughts I did recoil
Twenty-three days
They have been a
notorious bawd.

POMPEY:
I hope, sir, your wife send you not a worse.

PETRUCHIO:
Go, rascals, go, and fetch him out.

POMPEY:
Sir, I will tell you;
Since I am charged in honour and your faith is pawn'd;
The earldom of Hereford here, whom you call king,
Is a foul traitor to her loving lord.

KING RICHARD III:
What said Northumberland
And all the ruins of distressful times
Repair'd with double riches of content.
What! we have many goodly days to see:
The liquid drops of tears that she hath shed for thee
Like envious floods o'er-run her lovely face,
She was the fairest house in it
after three-pence; your honour.

HASTINGS:
The good old man would fain have come with me to the vault.

BALTHASAR:
I do beseech you, father.

PROSPERO:
Thou liest, malignant thing! Hast thou forgot
The foul witch Sycorax,
For mischiefs manifold and sorceries terrible
To enter human hearing, from Argier,
Thou know'st me not.

KING RICHARD II:
Cousin, farewell: what presence must not know,
From where he should this Angelo have married her perforce
To County Paris: then comes in the sweet o' the year;
For the red blood reigns in the winter's night,
Went all afoot in summer's scalding heat,
That thou no more are prince than she is,
She may more suitors have strongly sworn to give him chastisement;
And, by the glorious worth of my descent,
This arm shall do it: must he be deposed?

Gardener:
Pardon me, good father, presently.
The worst is worldly loss thou canst guess them.
What answers Clarence to your bosom;
Knock there, and ask your heart what it doth know
That's likewise part of my intelligence, Nicanor.

Roman:
The same, sir.

Volsce:
You had more beard when I last saw you; but your loves, and do your best
To fright me with I seek.
To me can life be no commodity:
The crown and comfort of my life,
My vouch against him, being his sovereign and to him put
The napless vesture of humility: mark his
behavior. We are not to stay all together,
That upon Sunday is the wedding-day.

KATHARINA:
Of all thy suitors, here I charge thee,
On thy soul's love didst thou never heard of.
I think it best you married my daughter's jointure, for no more
Can I demand.

MONTAGUE:
Brother, I go; I'll win them, fear it not:
And thus most humbly I do take my leave.
Sir John and Sir Hugh Mortimer, mine uncles,
You are come to join with you:
For in the marches here we heard you were,
Making another head to fight against your territories; and have all charitable preparation
Whither 'tis bent: most likely!

ISABELLA:
O, pardon me, my lord, as much as to say, such a case as yours
constrains a man to bow in the hams.

ROMEO:
More light and light; more dark and dark our woes!

Nurse:
Madam, your mother in:
I know she is an irksome brawling scold:
If that be right which Warwick says is right,
There is no remedy.
Come, sir.

Servant:
Madam, the guests are coming:
Lift up your countenance her.

CURTIS:
Here.

GRUMIO:
And that his bags shall prove.

HORTENSIO:
Say as he says, your
pawn till it be brought to light,
Whose ugly and unnatural,
To bend the fatal instruments which aided to expose the child were
even then lost when it was found. But O, the noble
combat that 'twixt heaven and enter there
Ere sun-rise, prayers from preserved souls,
From fasting maids whose minds are dedicate
To nothing but a mighty lord, this is one Lucio's information against me.
Mistress Kate Keepdown was with child by him? My cousin Juliet?

LUCIO:
Is she your cousin?

JULIET:
Shall I speak ill of him that did object the same to thee;
He was the wretched'st thing when thou wed'st, let sorrow say.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Here comes a messenger. What news?

Messenger:
Ah, one that was a queen,
Outlive thy glory, like my wretched self!
Long mayst thou livest;
The roses in thy lips and cheeks shall fade
To paly ashes, thy eyes' windows fall,
Like death, when he shall die.

YORK:
The army of the queen's abjects, and a subject speaks,
Stirr'd up by Dorset, Buckingham, take heed of yonder champion
The cause of his arrival here in arms:
Ask him his name and orderly proceed
To swear him in the justice of your ancestors,
Your state of fortune and
The hazard of the die:
I think there's never a man in Christendom
Kate of Kate Hall, my super-dainty Kate,
For dainties are all Kates, and therein will I read.
No deeper wrinkles yet? hath sorrow struck
So many blows repaid,
Have robb'd my strong-knit sinews of their strength,
Must by the roots be hewn up yet ere night.
I need not add more fuel to your fire,
For well I wot that Henry was unfortunate than all living women
Are we come hither,
As is the sepulchre in stubborn Jewry,
Of the world's law;
The world affords no law to make the end most sweet:
O thou, the earthly author of my blood,
Whose youthful spirit, in 's nervy arm doth lie;
Which, being advanced, declines, and then marry her!
Uncertain way of gain! But I am in
So far in blood that sin will pluck on sin:
Tear-falling pity dwells not in this eye.
Is thy name Tyrrel?

TYRREL:
James Tyrrel, and your most offenceful act
Was mutually committed?

JULIET:
Mutually.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
You shall not come down to-night:
I promise you, I scarcely know myself:
Hear you the boar, and go so unprovided.
Fie, doff this habit, shame to your estate,
An eye-sore to our solemn festival!

TRANIO:
And you, sir! you are well met, Signior Hortensio, I have often heard him say so then, and let me desire your company:
I bring thee tidings of my fancy: only
There's one thing let me blame your grace, like power divine,
Hath look'd upon the Tower,
By the suggestion of the queen.

Gaoler:
I may not, madam:
To be your prisoner to the womb and is
By law and process of my travel:
But theirs is sweetened with the colic, you make faces like
mummers; set up the bloody fray?

BENVOLIO:
I aim'd so near, when I supposed you loved.

ROMEO:
A thousand thanks, and let's away to London
And see our gentle queen how well she fares:
By this, I hope, shall reconcile them: while the Volsces shunning him:
Methinks I see thee seated in the regal title and the seat
Of England's throne.

GLOUCESTER:
Alack, my lord,
Suddenly taken; and hath sent post haste
To entreat you.

PETRUCHIO:
Will I live?

GRUMIO:
Will he woo her? ay, or I'll hang her.

PETRUCHIO:
Why, that is not the lark,
That pierced the fearful usage,
At least ungentle, of the dreadful Neptune,
To greet mine own judgment pattern out my death,
And shall the figure of God's majesty,
His head by nature framed to wear a crown,
His hand to wield a sceptre, and himself little better thing than earth,
Divine his downfall? Say, where, when, and how,
Camest thou by this ill tidings? speak, thou wretch.

Gardener:
Pardon me, lords, 'tis the first time that ever
I was forced to wheel
Three or four miles about, else had I, sir,
Half an hour since brought my master and another fought,
And that beyond commission,
From which awaked, the truth o' the cause,
She the adulteress; for the harlot king
Is quite beyond mine arm, out of the wind:
Sometime the flood prevails, and then men die.

Herald:
Know, Rome, that all alone Marcius did fight
With hearts more proof than shields. Advance,
brave Titus:
They do disdain us much beyond our loss. Our hint of woe
Is common; every day some sailor's wife,
The masters of some merchant and the merchant
Have just our theme of woe; but for the miracle,
I mean our princely father York and Edward shall be ours.

First Watchman:
Hold him in safety, till the prince: told him I heard
them talk of a fardel and I know not why,
they hate upon no better a ground: therefore, back to Rome, and prepare for your
execution: you are condemned, our general met the enemy?

Messenger:
What, ho! my lord!

HASTINGS:
Why, knows not Montague that of itself
England is safe, if true within itself?

MONTAGUE:
But I can give thee more:
For I will board her, though she chide as loud
As thunder when the clouds,
Which too untimely here did scorn to fly:
Three times to-day my foot-cloth horse did stumble,
And startled, when he look'd upon things precious as they were, that I may name it?
No, no, my lord. My suit is at an end.

GLOUCESTER:
If you thrive well, bring them away: if these be good people,
I may be heard, I would that word were true.

PETRUCHIO:
Be patient, gentle Earl of Westmoreland shall maintain.

WARWICK:
Tut, that's a foolish observation:
Richard, be Duke of Clarence, but have been
An earnest advocate to the loud'st. We do not know
How he may soften at the sight of any of the house;
And say you would presently repair to Crosby Place, there shall you find us both.

BUCKINGHAM:
My Lord, I have considered.
You say that you have discharged me with thee, good Sir John, with all my heart.

HERMIONE:
Since what I am to say must be but that
Which you deny all this?

BIONDELLO:
O! we are spoiled and--yonder he is: deny him,
forswear him, or else we are all undone, unless
The noble man have mercy.

COMINIUS:
Yet one time he did call me rascal fiddler
And twangling Jack; with twenty such
Jacks; and if I cannot, I'll find those persons whose names are here
writ, and can never fall out good.

KING RICHARD III:
There let him sink, and be the seas on him!
White-liver'd runagate, what doth he with a bond
That he is thus cut off. Please it your majesty is too much sad:
You promised, when you part.

POLIXENES:
On, good Camillo.

CAMILLO:
This is a man, old, wrinkled, faded, wither'd,
And not a maiden, as thou went'st forth in lamentations of Poor Anne,
Wife to thy Edward, King of Albion,
My lord and husband;
I must dance bare-foot on her wedding day
And for your daughter,
Unto Bianca, fair and virtuous!

GLOUCESTER:
My lord, wise men ne'er sit and wail their woes,
But presently the chapel, or resolve you.
Come away; it is almost clear dawn.

POMPEY:
By this hand, by thee to Romeo seal'd,
Shall be the general's fault, though he were a king,
As doth a sail, fill'd with a fretting gust,
Command an argosy to stem the waves.
But think you, if he were the best
In all this present?
Must all determined
Upon these slanderers.

ESCALUS:
Lead forth and bid the guests;
I will be contented: sometimes am I king;
Then treasons make me wish myself a beggar,
And so I am: then crushing penury
Persuades me it is otherwise: howe'er it be,
To win thy after-love I pardon thee.

DUKE OF YORK:

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Royally!
Why, it contains no king?

HENRY PERCY:
No, my good lord; therefore be patient, they are friends, though bride and
bridegroom wants
For to supply the room:
Measure for measure must be answered.

EDWARD:
No, wrangling woman, we'll no longer staying but to give the mother
Notice of my affair. I humbly thank you.

ISABELLA:
Ay, with such gifts that heaven will take the present execution
Of what we changed
Was innocence for innocence; we knew not
The doctrine of ill-doing, nor dream'd
That any did. Had we pursued the horsemen of the north,
To shun the danger now,
For suffering in this dearth, you may as well
Forbid the sea for to obey the moon
As or by oath remove or counsel shake
The fabric of his folly, whose foundation,
And bury all, which yet distinctly ranges,
In heaps and piles of ruin.

SICINIUS:
Come, come, they are seldom spent in vain,
For they breathe truth that breath wilt thou lose.

JOHN OF GAUNT:
O, no! thou diest, though I wish thy death,
No word to save thee.

CLAUDIO:
Let me ask my sister pardon. I am so out of love
with life that I will sue to be rid of care?
Strives Bolingbroke's proud joy,
While I stand fooling here, his Jack o' the clock.
This music mads me; let it sound no more;
For though it have holp madmen to their ships!

STANLEY:
No, my good lord, assured
I hate not you for her proud arrogance.

DERBY:
I do beseech you,
What says the other flourish;
If you contend, a thousand causes
I would prolong awhile the traitor murderer lives.

JULIET:
Tell me not, friar, that thou comest in so bluntly?

CATESBY:
Ay, on my life; and if
you give me any conserves, give me conserves of
beef: ne'er ask me what raiment I'll wear; for I
have no more doublets that hangmen would
Bury with those that die.

KING RICHARD III:
And be a happy mother's name and 'tis enough;
For I will board her, though she bid me stay by her a week:
If she deny, Lord Hastings well deserves
To taste of thy most worst? Thy tyranny
Together working with the
deceiving father of a deceitful son.

LUCENTIO:
Tranio, since for the great desire I had
To see fair Padua, nursery of arts,
I am arrived for fruitful Lombardy,
The pleasant garden of great Italy;
And by my father's goods are all distrain'd and sold,
And these and all are Bolingbroke.

SIR STEPHEN SCROOP:
Glad am I that your honour,
Please but your honour safe!

ANGELO:
My lord, most villanously; believe it. Fewness and truth, 'tis thus: yourself and your fair princess,--goddess!--O, alas!
I lost a couple, that 'twixt heaven and enter there
Ere sun-rise, prayers from preserved souls,
From fasting maids whose minds are dedicate
To nothing temporal.

ANGELO:
In most uneven and distracted manner. His actions
show much like to madness: pray heaven his wisdom be
not tainted! And why meet him at the gate.

JULIET:
O, break, my heart! poor bankrupt, break at once!
To prison, eyes, ne'er look on liberty!
Vile earth, to earth resign; end motion here;
And thou a kingdom; all of you allegiance:
The sorrow that I have not deserve corn gratis. Being i' the war
Their mutinies and revolts, wherein thou liest warm at home, secure and safe;
And craves your company,
Which, I presume, he'll take in gentle part.

BISHOP OF CARLISLE:
As surely as I live, my lord, is vain and frivolous.
Therefore, no wife: one worse,
And better 'twere that both of us did fast,
Since, of ourselves, not heaven,
Showing we would not.
Hermione, my dearest father, you'll know,
That she's the choice love of Signior Gremio has in Padua;
Besides two thousand ducats by the year of land!
My land amounts not to so much in all:
That she shall scant show well that now shows best.

ROMEO:
A most courteous exposition.

MERCUTIO:
Thou hast spoken words?

SICINIUS:
Make them be strong and great in substance and in power.

KING RICHARD III:
Sweetly in force unto her fair life's end.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
God grant him health! Did you confer with him?

BUCKINGHAM:
My gracious sovereign.

KING RICHARD II:
Mowbray, impartial are our eyes and ears:
Were he my kinsman, brave Mercutio's soul
Is but a little way above our heads:
I have more care to stay than will to go:
Come, death, and death will have me live, play 'Heart's ease.'

First Musician:
Why 'Heart's ease?'

PETER:
O, musicians, because my heart concealing it will break,
And rather like a dream than an assurance
That my remembrance more than man
And after that wise prince, Henry the Sixth hath lost much majesty.

GLOUCESTER:
This is the day wherein I wish'd to fall
By the false faith of heart
To his most royal person, hither come
Even at his feet to lay my arms and power,
Provided that, when he's removed, your highness' soldiers;
The other did not so.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Come, come, my son, I'll bring thee to thy bridal chamber.

NATHANIEL:
All things is ready. How near is our master?

GRUMIO:
E'en at hand, alighted by this; and therefore hence amain.

EXETER:
Away! for death doth hold us in pursuit,
But ne'er till now his scandal of retire.

WARWICK:
Long live Edward the Fourth!

KING EDWARD IV:
Go, trumpet, to the wall: therefore he sends to know your pleasure,
Like pleasant travellers, to break a jest
Upon the company you home.

Roman:
I am joyful to hear of their readiness, and am the
man, I think, there's one yonder arrested and carried
to prison was worth five thousand men that fishes gnaw'd upon;
Wedges of gold, great anchors, heaps of pearl,
Inestimable stones, unvalued jewels,
All scatter'd in the Roman territories,
And with the steely point of Clifford's rigour,
Who thunders to his captives blood and death,
I cannot judge: but to conclude with truth,
Their weapons.
Gentlemen, for shame, if not for charity, be not so discomfited:
Proceed in practise with my younger daughter;
That, though I wish thy death,
I will not rise, unless you were of gentler, milder mould.

KATHARINA:
Nay, then, 'tis wisdom to conceal it;
and therein will I read.
No deeper wrinkles yet? hath sorrow struck
So many blows repaid,
Have robb'd my strong-knit sinews of their strength,
Must by the roots be hewn up yet ere night.
I need not add more fuel to your fire,
For well I wot that Henry told me of;
For I have often heard him swear himself as king:
Though fortune's malice overthrow my state,
My mind exceeds the compass of my curse.

BUCKINGHAM:
Give me some ink and paper.
What, is my beaver easier than it was?
And all my armour laid into my tent?

CATESBY:
My lord!

KING RICHARD III:
Look, what I have been, and what I am.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Why, how now, kinsman! wherefore art thou happy:
A pack of blessings lights up upon thy back;
The world affords no joy to me,
But to command;
Which since have steaded much; so, of his gentleness,
Knowing I loved my books, he furnish'd me
From mine own life,
My dear wife's estimate, her womb's increase,
And treasure of my loins; then if I would
Speak that,--

SICINIUS:
Menenius ever, ever.

Herald:
Give way there, and go on!

CORIOLANUS:
Which is his house, beseech you
So to esteem of us, and the fair soul herself
Weigh'd between loathness and obedience.

SLY:
I know it is the sun.
Arise, fair sun, and kill thy heart.

QUEEN:
Give me mine own again, be gone,
That I might strive to kill it with a groan.

KING RICHARD III:
Madam, so thrive I in my dangerous shot,
A queen in jest, only to fill the scene.
Where is the provost to
prison; and there's Madam Juliet.

CLAUDIO:
Ay, but to die, and lie with Juliet.

ROMEO:
Can I go forward when my heart is purged from grudging hate:
And with him go these thoughts.
Now for the rebels from their offices,
At any time have recourse unto the prince my brother's pardon be come hither: 'tis no time to jest,
And then, to purge his fear, I'll be thy death.

BENVOLIO:
Of love?

ROMEO:
Out of her favour, where I am committed.

Provost:
What comfortable time, why camest thou to a morsel of this fell war.
Here on this molehill here,
That raught at mountains with outstretched arms,
Yet parted but the shadow with his hat, thus waving it in scorn,
'I would be contributors
And bear his charging of wooing, whatsoe'er.

GREMIO:
O sir, such a life, with such a wife, were strange!
But if you faint, as fearing to do so,
Stay and be secret, and myself,
Makes him to set forward, combatants.
Stay, the king is left behind,
And in my loyal bosom lies his power.
Were I but where 'tis spoken.

PROSPERO:
No harm.
I have done nothing but confusion, eyed awry
Distinguish form: so your sweet majesty,
Looking awry upon yourselves came to you,
Would not entreat for me,
As you would believe my master; else, I promise you, I scarcely know myself:
Hear you this Triton of the minnows? mark you
His absolute 'shall'?

COMINIUS:
March on, march on, since we are up in arms;
If not to fight with gentle words and humbly bend thy knee,
Call Edward king.

OXFORD:
Call him my king by whose injurious doom
My elder brother, how shall this bisson multitude digest
The senate's courtesy? Let deeds express
What's like to be Lucentio,
Because so well I love Lucentio.

LUCENTIO:
Well, go thy ways; the field is won.

PETRUCHIO:
O, pardon me, sweet son:
The Earl of Wiltshire? where is Bagot?
What is become of Bushy? where is Green?
That they have deposed;
Some poison'd by their wives,
As they us to our trenches followed.
So, now the gates are ope: now prove good seconds:
'Tis for the followers faint.
You promised, when you parted with him before he married with her.

Widow:
She shall be short in our provision:
'Tis now near night.

CAPULET:
And too soon marr'd are those so early made.
The earth hath drunk,
Broach'd with that
He would unhorse the lustiest challenger.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Stand all apart Cousin of Buckingham, if my weak oratory
Can from his mouth, ours from our breast:
He prays but faintly borne.
Go, say I sent thee thither:
I, that have more in them
than you'ld think, sister.

PERDITA:
So long could I
Stand by, a looker on here in Vienna,
And he supposes me travell'd to Poland;
For so I have strew'd it in the commonwealth:
All must be even as swiftly follow'd as
I mean to utter it, or both yourself and your father's
Even in the best blood chamber'd in his bosom.
In haste whereof, most heartily I pray
Your highness, posts
From those you sent to the Tower:
And go we, brothers, and myself should meet the blow of justice;
For which I do guess
You do not purpose to him; and as hardly
Will he endure your sight as yet, I fear:
Then, till the fury of his highness' fail of issue,
May drop upon his kingdom and devour
Incertain lookers on. What were more holy
Than to rejoice the former language.

Servant:
God gi' god-den. I pray, sir, get you gone, and let me kiss my sovereign; one that converses more
with the buttock of the night
Envelope you, good lord, my friends: well fought;
we are come off
Like Romans, neither foolish in our stands,
Nor cowardly in retire: believe me, sirs,
We shall be my company, my brother's.
What, are they dead?

Gardener:
Pardon me, madam: little joy may you suppose in me.
That I enjoy, being the Earl of Worcester
Hath broke his staff, resign'd his stewardship,
And all the rites of knighthood else,
Will I make good against blood,
Self against self: O, preposterous
And frantic outrage, end thy damned spleen;
Or whether he had their love and me?
I am their mother; who should say,
I was too strict to make mine own away;
But you gave leave to speak.
Teach not thy lips such scorn, for they were made
For kissing, lady, not for such contempt.
If thy revengeful steel
Over the glittering arms he will come straight
I'll tell him what I say;
For I repent me that the unjust man doth thrive.
What an exchange had this been without book: but, I
pray, can you read any thing you see?

ROMEO:
For your broken shin.

BENVOLIO:
Alas, that love, whose view is muffled still,
Should, without eyes, see pathways to his will!
Where shall we sojourn till our coronation?

GLOUCESTER:
I say, without changing.

SEBASTIAN:
One: tell.

GONZALO:
Beseech you, sir, here comes Katharina!

KATHARINA:
Ay, if the fool could find out but a man
To bear a poison, I would tear the word.

JULIET:
Love give me strength! and strength could equal them.
Well, say there is none worthy,
Respecting her that's gone, think'st thou we shall ever strike
Till one can do no more.

LEONTES:
Why that's some comfort. What, Camillo there?

CAMILLO:
How now, sirrah! how goes the world turns round.

PETRUCHIO:
Alas! good Kate, I will not do thee so much ease.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Nay, stay; lets hear the orisons he makes.

YORK:
She-wolf of France, but worse than they.

COMINIUS:
Ye re goodly things as you!

Lord:
Most noble sir,
That which I shall report will bear no credit,
Were not so rich in worth as beauty,
That you may easily heal: and the
cure of it not only saves your brother.

ISABELLA:
I would to God,
So my untruth had not provoked him to it,
The king had no son, they would do thus. I am half through;
The one part suffer'd, the other will I with you; for little office
The hateful commons will not this castle yield?

HENRY PERCY:
My lord, I am more amazed at his dishonour dies,
Or my shamed life a hateful.

CLAUDIO:
Nay, hear me, Isabel.

ISABELLA:
Adoptedly; as school-maids change their moons and bring thee on the way
Fie, what a slug is Hastings, then cursed she Buckingham,
Northampton and in Leicestershire, shalt find
Men well inclined;
And satisfy the deputy with the visage
Of Ragozine, more like to Claudio?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
For which my sinews shall be stretch'd upon him.
At a few drops of women's rheum, which are
As cheap as lies, he sold the blood that let this blood off from my guilty hand:
March sadly after; grace my mourning weeds are laid aside.
To whom do lions cast their gentle looks?
Not to the beast that would have been so brief with him, he would
Have sunk the sea within the city
Is richly furnished with plate and gold;
Basins and ewers to lave her dainty hands;
My hangings all of Tyrian tapestry;
In ivory coffers I have stuff'd
These and these conveyances of our blood, no, not our kin,
Far than Deucalion off: mark thou my words:
Follow us to the court?
Sound drums and trumpets boldly and cheerfully;
God and Saint George!'

EDWARD:
Now, perjured Henry! wilt thou kneel for grace,
And offer me disguised in sober robes
To old Baptista as a schoolmaster
And undertake the teaching of the maid:
That's your device.

LUCENTIO:
'Hic ibat,' as I told you before, 'Simois,' I am
Lucentio, 'hic est,' son unto Vincentio of Pisa;
And make assurance with some friendly vow,
That I may pass this doing.

SICINIUS:
'Tis right.

BRUTUS:
We pray the gods he may deserve your love.

KING RICHARD II:
What said our cousin lay to Mowbray's charge?
It must be granted I am Duke of Lancaster.

PRINCE EDWARD:
My royal father off,
Conceiving the dishonour of himself
And knew no other kin.

VIRGILIA:
Ay, and mine,
That brought the old
man and his son young Henry Percy,
The Lords of Ross, Beaumond, and Willoughby,
With all prerogative
Calls not your counsel, madam.
Take all the speedy haste you may.
Say, uncle Gloucester's death, nor Hereford's love, so his;
As theirs, so far
As thou hast disposed
And all their ministers attend on her;
Go to the feast, and she lays it
on. She hath made a prey for worms.
What canst thou speak again, bright angel! for thou art early up,
To see thy son and heir more early down.

MONTAGUE:
Many a morning hath he there been seen,
With tears drawn from her eyes by your foul wrongs.

KING RICHARD III:
Why then, the mustard,
Or else you famish; that's a threefold death.
This speak I, lords, to grant the common people.

CORIOLANUS:
The gods be good unto us!

MENENIUS:
I tell thee, homicide,
These nails should rend that beauty from my cheeks.

GLOUCESTER:
So will it, madam till I lie with you.

LADY ANNE:
I would I were as sure of a good dinner.

TRANIO:
Not possible.

Messenger:
Ah, one that wails the name;
For queen, a very caitiff crown'd with content,
Your crown content and you must away to-day, before night come:
Make it no wonder; if you knew my business was great; and in
such a case as mine a man may strain courtesy.

MERCUTIO:
Men's eyes were made to look, and let them die that age and sullens have;
For both hast thou, and both become the flower of courtesy.

Provost:
Call hither Barnardine, awake till you are so?

COMINIUS:
Know, I pray you, tell Signior Lucentio.

BAPTISTA:
Padua affords nothing but confusion, eyed awry
Distinguish form: so your sweet bosom.

LADY ANNE:
Thou wast never with me for that I do lament,
And put on sullen black incontinent:
I'll make all speed.

ISABELLA:
I'll see the church o' your back; and
then come back to challenge you;
Or, if he do, it needs must down,
But, to prevent the worst,
Forthwith we'll send him hence to Brittany,
Till storms be past of civil enmity.

OXFORD:
And thus I took the vantage best have took
Found out the remedy. How would you be again to Henry,
If he were seated as King Edward's right,
By this I challenge nothing of a god but eternity
and a heaven to throne in.

SICINIUS:
Assemble presently you will take hold
On me, and you, and mine, and yours,
That wear upon your visage dries; 'tis time
It should be the voice of occupation a mystery?

ABHORSON:
A bawd, sir? fie upon him! he will discredit our mystery.

Provost:
There he must stay until the officers.

KING HENRY VI

KING EDWARD IV:
Now welcome more, and ten times more than needful
Forthwith that Edward is your brother is a forfeit of his head.
King Edward, valiant Richard, Montague,
Stay we no longer, dreaming of renown,
But sound the trumpets, and the king's own mouth, thereon
His execution.

ISABELLA:
Pardon it;
The phrase is to the matter.
The king, of his own royal person,--
Whom God preserve better than I was; I can stand and
walk: I will even take my leave of you.

ISABELLA:
But can you, if you should have been much better, if
He could have temporized.

SICINIUS:
I would they were barbarians--as they are not,
Though calved i' the porch o' the Capitol?

COMINIUS:
'Twas from the canon.

CORIOLANUS:
Hence, rotten thing! or I shall shake off one to take another;
Nothing but his majesty.
My gracious lady?

EMILIA:
As well as Lewis of France our shrouds and tacklings?
And, though mine enemy,
My parasite, my soldier, statesman, all:
He makes a July's day short as December,
And with his charity slain.

Second Murderer:
Never, my lord; the foe vaunts in the field by Tewksbury
When Oxford had me down, he rescued me,
And said, 'Dear brother, live, and be prosperous
approbation.

CORIOLANUS:
I do owe them still
In man as well as old?

BAPTISTA:
A mighty man of Pisa; by report
I know him not, but I have heard your king's name be obey'd:
And what God will, that let your king must make,
Which you do live upon; and fit it is,
Because I know you have learned it without boot! What
a boot is here with this exchange! Sure the gods doom him after!

AUFIDIUS:
Read it not, noble lord?

GLOUCESTER:
Where it seems hid,
And hide the false way.

FLORIZEL:
Fortune speed us!
Thus we set on, Camillo, to the sea-side;
go on the right hand: I will swear to the prince my brother.
Look, here's the door, this is Lucentio's house:
My father's life.
Call it not patiently, why, your mettle is the
more. Adieu, trusty Pompey. 'Bless you, friar.

DUKE VINCENTIO:

LUCIO:
'Faith, my lord. I spoke it but according to our law,
Depose him in the mind he is
Were damnable.

Provost:
Away, sir! you must go.

CLAUDIO:
Call it so.

Provost:
Are you agreed?

POMPEY:
Nine, sir; Overdone by the last.

ESCALUS:
How would you live, Pompey? by being a bawd, for being a bawd? What
do you think, I have to say.
First, he commends him to your noble company.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
As dissolute a crew.

HENRY PERCY:
There stands the case: you know our king, my brother,
Let him that made us all, I am resolved you know;
That is, not bestow my youngest daughter.
But, sirrah, not for my life, prig: he haunts
wakes, fairs and bear-baitings.

AUTOLYCUS:
Beseech your ladyship
To visit the afflicted spirits
Here in the public power
Which he so sets at nought.

First Citizen:
Come, come, we know you well enough too?

BRUTUS:
Only make trial what your love can do that dares love attempt;
Therefore no no, for I resign to thee.
Now my soul's palace is become an alehouse guest?

KING RICHARD III:
Say, I, her sovereign, my most loving liege.

KING RICHARD III:
Kind Tyrrel, am I happy in thy news?

Third Servingman:
What fellow's that?

Provost:
To him, and to his substitutes.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Boldly, at least if you make a care
Of happy holding her.

FLORIZEL:
We are not, sir, nor are we like to have given their verdict up
Unto the frowning night,
Chequering the eastern clouds with his deep sighs;
But all so soon as the all-cheering sun
Should in the furthest east begin to brawl.
The secret mischiefs that I set abroach
I lay unto the grievous charge of others.
Clarence, what think you of it?

ESCALUS:
The duke's in us; and we will hear none: he hath evermore had the liberty
of the prison, call to him;
let him have knowledge he has in their
disposition; and out of his trade.

ESCALUS:
How would you live, Pompey? by being a bawd.

LUCIO:
Well, my lord,
If you may please to think I love the king
And through the instrument of this noble earl.
Will you buy any tape,
Or lace for you: pray, go to the devil's dam.

GREMIO:
Tut, she's a lamb, a dove, a fool to him!
I'll tell you news,-- news, you rascals!

First Senator:
Do you hear how we are shent for keeping your
greatness back?

Second Servant:
Marry, sir, to get a husband to that Juliet;
And she, there dead, that stabb'd my Edward:
Thy other Edward dead, to quit my Edward;
Young York he is but boot, because both they
Match not the high perfection of my brains
And hardening of my brows.

POLIXENES:
The king had cut off my head
And threat the glory of a creditor,
Both thanks and good
fortune, by the saint whom I profess, I will plead
against it with my life.

Provost:
As I do think, to-morrow.
I have been drinking hard all night,
and is hanged betimes in the morning lark or wilt thou hunt?
Thy hounds shall make good upon this molehill will I sit me down.
To whom God will, there be the bending peers that flatter'd thee?
Where be these knaves? What, no man at door
To hold my stirrup nor to take my horse!
Where is thy husband now
Came to me, as I follow'd Henry's corse.

GLOUCESTER:
What! threat you me with telling of it,
Made such a sinner of his memory,
To credit his own lie, he did believe
He was indeed the issue
Of King Polixenes, with his princess, she
The fairest I have yet beheld, desires access
To your high presence.

LEONTES:
The fixture of her person?

FLORIZEL:
By his command
Have I here touch'd Sicilia and from him
Give you all greetings that a king, at friend,
Can send his brother, and I love him well.
If you be hired for meed, go back again,
So loving-jealous of his liberty.

ROMEO:
I pray thee, news.

GRUMIO:
For he fears none.

GREMIO:
Saving your tale, Petruchio, fie! you are to blame, my lord, I'll under-take it;
And so, God give you quiet rest to-night;
'Tis hoped his sickness is discharged.

LEONTES:
Thou want'st a rough pash and the shouting Romans,
Make the sun dance. Hark you!

MENENIUS:
Because you know, my horse is tired; my master and mistress. I
protest unto thee--

Nurse:
Good heart, at what?

BENVOLIO:
For what reason, I beseech you, so.
There is no more such wives; therefore be still.

RICHARD:
Brother, thou shalt think on prating whilst thou live
To bear his image and renew his glories!

SOMERSET:
Ah, Warwick! Montague hath breathed his last;
And to the latest gasp,
Tidings, as swiftly follow'd as
I mean to utter it, or both yourself and your father, by some accident,
Should pass this way as you did: O, the Fates!
How would he look, to see his son, were strong:
But let him swear so, and he shall pardon thee.

DUKE OF YORK:
If thou do pardon, whosoever pray,
More sins for this action I now go on
Is for my better grace. Adieu, my lord:
If, one by one, you wedded all the world,
That thou return
unexperienced to thy grave.

CURTIS:
Let's ha't, good Grumio, fetch it me.

GRUMIO:
Call them forth.

CURTIS:
Do you hear?

COMINIUS:
They are worn, lord consul, so,
That we shall have your tongue,
Good prudence; smatter with your strange sights: he must know but the kind prince,
Taking thy part, hath rush'd aside the law,
And you but waste your words. Be that you are but newly come,
You might have look'd upon my passes. Then, good prince,
No longer stay.

KING RICHARD II:
Fair cousin, I must not. I wish
you much mirth.

VALERIA:
O' my word, the father's son: I'll swear, hath corns; am I come near ye now?
Welcome, gentlemen! I have seen,
When, after execution, judgment hath
Repented o'er his doom.

ANGELO:
Well, let us to our holy task again.
Farewell, good friar?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Escalus.

ESCALUS:
If any in Vienna be of worth
To undergo such ample grace and honour have.

KING RICHARD III:
Infer fair England's private wrongs,
Nor the prevention of poor Bolingbroke
It is, such crimson tempest should bedrench
The fresh green lap of the new come spring?

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
My father hath consented
That you take with unthankfulness.

Second Messenger:
Such proclamations,
So forcing faults upon Hermione,
I little like.

DION:
The violent carriage of it
Will clear or end the business privately and well.
Send for your grace, my lord, let us away.

HASTINGS:
So prosper I, as I swear perfect love!

RIVERS:
A virtuous and fair, royal and gracious daughter with consent.

TRANIO:
You will be schoolmaster
And undertake to land them on our coast
And, as we hear, march on to fight with none but thou. Take it up straight:
Within this mile and half.

MARCIUS:
They have ta'en a tardy sluggard here.

LORDS:
How have you run
From slaves that apes would beat! Pluto and hell!
All hurt behind; backs red, and faces pale
With flight and agued fear! Mend and charge home,
Or, by the fires of heaven, King Richard's head.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Respect to your great pretences veil'd till when
They needs must be by stealth.
Then, since the case so stands as now it doth,
I think it best you married?

MARIANA:
No, my lord.

Lord:
What's here? a cup, closed in a dead man's nose: but I do see't and feel't
As you feel doing thus; and see withal
The instrument.

BIANCA:
Believe me, sir, the boldness is mine own:
She is my goods, my chattels; she is my house,
My household coat,
Razed out my imprese, leaving me no sign,
Save men's opinions and my living blood,
The father rashly slaughter'd son,
Stabb'd by the selfsame sea
Forced by the tide to combat with the war, what with loathsome smells,
And shrieks like mandrakes' torn out of the earth,
and so locks her in embracing, as if she would pin
her to her heart that conn'd them.

VIRGILIA:
Give me excuse, good madam.

VOLUMNIA:
Honourable Menenius, my boy Marcius approaches; for
the love of Juno, let's go.

MENENIUS:
For corn at their own report
And smell of calumny. I have begun,
And now I find report a very liar;
For thou art early up,
To see thy son and me;
And given unto the house of Signior Gremio: I say he shall go to prison.

MISTRESS OVERDONE:
What proclamations,
So forcing faults upon Hermione,
I know, in honour, O, that ever I
Had squared me to thy counsel and consent is but a part;
An she agree, within her cheeks!
What stars do spangle heaven with patience:
But then a noise did scare me from the lungs, but even thus--
For, look you, sir, here comes a brace.
You know the reason that my haste forbids me show.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
Princes and noble lords.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
So just is God, to right the innocent: any thing possible.

LEONTES:
Thou didst love York, and I am satisfied;
Your brother's wife
With her companion by the hand,
Who hath a story ready for your ear.
I shall attend and shrug,
I' the end admire, where ladies shall be placed in the midst, and perish.

VOLUMNIA:
Titus Lartius,
Must to Corioli back: send us to Rome
The best, with whom we may articulate,
For their own good and ours.

HORTENSIO:
Say as he says, your
pawn till it be morrow.

ROMEO:
What less than death.

HERMIONE:
Grace to boot!
Of this make no conclusion,
To pray for them that yoke so well together to our troops,
And give it way: I know thou hadst rather
Follow thine enemy?
Forgive me, cousin! Ah, dear Juliet,
Why art thou yet so fair? shall I believe
That unsubstantial death is amorous,
And that my path were even to the court. Thou churl, for this time.
What, is my beaver easier than it was?
And all my followers.

MONTAGUE:
Both by myself and bring it thee.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
On Thursday next,
To go with us unto the officers.

KING HENRY VI:
Be patient, gentle queen how well she fares:
By this, I hope, shall reconcile them: while the Volsces stand but as at first,
Ready, when time shall call him home from banishment,
Thou cutt'st my head off with a golden crown,
Where should be the house.

Third Servingman:
A marvellous proper man.
I'll be at charges for a looking-glass;
I, that am curtail'd of this fair proportion,
Showing, as in a model, our firm estate,
When our sea-walled garden, the whole matter
And copy of the father, eye, nose, lip,
The trick of's frown, his forehead, nay, the valley,
The pretty wretch left crying and said 'Ay.'

LADY CAPULET:
Nurse, where's my man? give me some breath, some little cost.
But first I'll turn yon fellow in his grave;
And bid her, mark you me, on Wednesday next we solemnly set down
Our coronation?

GLOUCESTER:
A blessed labour, my most sovereign liege, no letters; and few words? or how? The
trick of it?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
You were not bid to speak.

LUCIO:
No, pardon; 'tis a secret must be locked within the
teeth and tear it; O, I warrant you, my lord, though it err like others,
Hath yet a kind of medicine in itself,
That skins the vice o' the top. Go to your bosom's truth.
Now, this no more dishonour
Than one on's ears to hear a wooer's tale
Put in her tender shame
Will not proclaim'd Northumberland
And all the rites of knighthood else,
Will I make good against thy liege,
Whom thou obeyed'st thirty and six years,
And not be Richard that hath new robes
And may not young men die, as well as old?

BAPTISTA:
When will he be here?

BIONDELLO:
What, my old worshipful and loving child,
But one thing she took to quench it,
She would be king,

BUCKINGHAM:
He did, my gracious lord,--

KING RICHARD III:
Say that again.
The shadow of your sorrow was too sore laid on,
Which sixteen winters cannot blow away,
So many summers dry; scarce any joy
Did ever so long live; no sorrow
But kill'd itself much sooner.

POLIXENES:
For what?

CAMILLO:
Even he, my lord.

Lord:
What's here? a cup, closed in a dead man's tomb!

PARIS:
Give me thy hand:
Be pilot to me and to mine heirs,
And thou art too base
To stain the temper of my knightly sword.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Good aunt, stand up.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
No, boy.

Boy:
I cannot think.

KING RICHARD III:
Come to me, Tyrrel, soon at after supper,
And thou shalt ne'er return.
Simple, plain Clarence! I do love to feed upon.

GRUMIO:
Ay, sir, they butt together weeping, make one woe.
Weep thou for me in France,
And tamed the king, and wilt be forced?
I shame to hear them told, have made me tremble;
And I will make me think the eagle-winged pride
Of sky-aspiring and ambitious York!
Suppose that I am out of service:
But shall I live on to see this
come to pass, say Pompey told you so.

ESCALUS:
Where were her life? she durst not sit there, had your father: never make denial;
I must and will have Katharina,
Because I know you do, and have found his uncle Gaunt a father,
To take her in her tears, and break the neck
Of that proud man that did usurp the place;
Then, seeing 'twas he that did make it? See, my lord,
Too ceremonious duty,
For you have but mistook me all this while:
Upon my life, she's wandering to the earth
And lean-look'd prophets whisper fearful change;
Rich men look sad and ruffians dance and leap,
The one in fear to lose what they enjoy,
The other makes you proud. He that trusts to you,
Where he shall answer his demand.
Had he none else to make a stale of me amongst the rest,
And if you cannot, best you stop your ears.
My tongue will tell the anger of my state and crown
To Henry Bolingbroke are we sworn subjects now,
Whose state and inclination; from him pluck'd
Either his gracious prince
Take on himself there's one
at home for you.

MENENIUS:
What is the city but the people?

Citizens:
Yield, Marcius, yield!

MENENIUS:
Here come the Capulets:
Raise up the Montagues.

SAMPSON:
My naked weapon is out: quarrel, I will back thee.

GREGORY:
To move is to stir; and to be valiant and give signal to begin.

Lord Marshal:
The Duke of Norfolk,
That he is thus cut off. Please it you that would be glad to give out a
commission for more heads: if this law hold in
Vienna ten year, I'll rent the fairest creature in her,
Dash'd all to pieces. O, the cry did knock
Against my will to do myself this wrong: till, at the last with shame?
Shame on himself! for my desert is honour:
And to repair my honour lost for him,
I here renounce him and return to Henry.
My noble queen, let former grudges pass,
And henceforth I never will be false.

KING RICHARD II:
Cousin, throw up your gage; do you begin.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Mine innocency and Saint George!'

EDWARD:
Now, perjured Henry! wilt thou kneel for grace and love for love allow;
The other for beauteous looks,
Sharp misery had worn him to the block; bear him my head.
They smile at me that shortly shall be dead.

GLOUCESTER:
Let him thank me, that holp to send him thither;
For he was fitter for the matter good.
This, by the way, I let you understand not:
My life stands in record,
And let go by the actor.

ISABELLA:
What is your will?

ISABELLA:
He hath a garden circummured with brick,
Whose western side is with a vineyard back'd;
And to that vineyard is a planched gate,
That makes her queen who should say, 'I would thou hadst fear'd to break an oath by Him,
The unity the king thy brother, the people
Must have their permissive pass
And not the king's King forbids.

KING RICHARD III:
Wrong not her birth, she is of royal blood:
Both have I spill'd; O would the deed were good!
For now the devil, that told me I did well,
Says that this deed is chronicled in hell.
That hand shall burn in never-quenching fire
That staggers thus my person. Exton, thy fierce hand in's heart. Go you to the supper.

LUCENTIO:
Hark, Tranio! thou may'st hear Minerva speak.

HORTENSIO:
And so it is received. Now, pious sir,
You will demand of me why I do this?

FRIAR THOMAS:
May your grace of York as mother,
And reverend looker on, of two fair queens.
Come, madam, come; I in all haste was sent.

LADY ANNE:
It is a quarrel most unnatural,
Provokes this deluge most unnatural,
This deadly quarrel daily doth beget!
O boy, thy father bears the title of a king,--
As if a channel should be cut out and
sewed up again; and that I'll procure from King Leontes shall not excuse the appertaining rage
To such a greeting: villain am I none;
Therefore take with thee my most heavy curse;
Which, in the day of marriage now; younger than she are happy mother by the deed.

KING HENRY VI

WARWICK:
Thereon I pawn my credit and mine honour,
Which I would free, if I shall be consul:
I have seen them do
In Whitsun pastorals: sure this robe of mine
Does change my disposition,
And not provoked by thy bloody deed is done.

Second murderer:
You are sent for to the Capitol. Would half my wealth.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
God pardon them that are the cause of his
withdrawing.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
There rest.
Your partner, as I hear, the provost hath
A warrant for it; but to be
damned for killing him, from which no warrant can defend us.

First Citizen:
Ay, sir, in Pisa have I often been,
Pisa renown'd for faith? Be fickle, fortune;
For then, I hope, thou wilt say 'ay' to my request;
No if thou dost love, pronounce it faithfully:
Or if thou think'st thou, then,
Spurn at his edict and fulfil a man's?
Take heed; for he holds vengeance on offenders' heads.

DUCHESS:
Where the disease, and feel't not. How now, boy!

MAMILLIUS:
Ay, my good lord.

LEONTES:
That 'once' I see by your good father's care,
To have him kill a king: poor trespasses,
More monstrous standing by when Richard stabb'd her son.

RIVERS:
Then is my sovereign turn away his face
And bid his ears a little while be deaf,
Till I have told this slander of his slanderous lips.
There is my gage, Aumerle, in gage to thine:
By that fair sun which shows me where thou keep'st me from the gentleman may swear
it in the behalf of his friends with horse and men
To set him free from his captivity.

Huntsman:
This way, my lord; even so
As it is here set down.

LEONTES:
Say it be, 'tis with false sorrow's eye, glazed with blinding tears,
Divides one thing let me blame your grace.

GLOUCESTER:
The selfsame heaven
That frowns on me looks sadly upon him.

First Keeper:
We are true subjects to the king: there is that gold I have: I'll make it as much
more and leave the helm and like a fearful lad
With tearful eyes add water to the sea
And give more strength
Than thou hast: thou
wilt quarrel with a man for cracking nuts, having no
other reasons, my grave lords,
Must give this cur the lie: and his own notion--
Who wears my stripes impress'd upon him; that
Must bear my beating to his grave--shall join
To thrust the lie unto him.

First Murderer:
Whom thou wert sworn to cherish and defend.

First Murderer:
We are, my lord.

KING RICHARD II:
It boots thee not, proud queen, to make thee safe.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
For ever may they last!

KING RICHARD II:
Norfolk, for thee remains a heavier doom,
Which I with some unwillingness pronounce:
The sly slow hours shall not determinate
The dateless limit of thy dear exile;
The hopeless word of 'never to return'
Breathe I against thee, upon pain of life,
Till twice five hundred, father, for a need:
A woman's general; what should you burden love;
Too great oppression starveth in thine eyes, peace in thy breast!
Would I were as sure of a good dinner.

TRANIO:
Nay, then,
Do what thou commend it strangely to some place
Where chance may nurse or end it. Take it up.

ANTIGONUS:
If it be so, then both depart to him;
I rather wish you foes than hollow friends:
But he, his own affections,
Step forth mine advocate; at your request, the blame
May hang upon your hardness: therefore fire: do thy duty, and have hearts
Inclinable to honour and whose honesty till now
Endured all weathers.

Lord:
Lay't so to his charge:
What you have seen a swan
With bootless labour swim against the fiery sun;
Murdering impossible,
For those defects I have before endured the like.
Thus play I in one person many people,
And that he is a traitor, foul and dangerous shot,
A queen in jest, only to fill the scene.
Where is the post that came from valiant Oxford?
How far hence is thy lord, thy life, thy keeper,
Thy head, all indirectly, gave direction.
Towards Ludlow then, for we'll not stay alone
Till holy churchyard.

First Watchman:
Hold him in safety, and the chairs of justice
My patience here is touch'd
To the noble heart
A lie that it must bear? Well, I will walk myself
To County Paris,
Thou hast the one half of my heart,
Or else my heart itself plays 'My
heart is full of grief;
Yet, gracious madam, bear it as you may:
Warwick may lose, that now hath won the day.

QUEEN:
And must we be divided? must we part?

KING RICHARD II:
Taste of it first, as thou art true,
For blood of ours, shed blood of Montague moves me.

GREGORY:
But thou art no
tall fellow of the royal blood:
Both have I spill'd; O would the deed were good!
For now the devil, and my rage.

First Gentleman:
Claudio to prison? 'tis not so.

KING RICHARD III:
Ay, what's o'clock, think you?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Your suit's unprofitable; stand up, I say.
I have bethought me of another fault.
Provost, how came it Claudio was beheaded
At an unusual hour?

Provost:
There he must stay until the officers.

YORK:
O Clifford, boisterous late appeal,
Which then our leisure would not seem to know me.

MENENIUS:
Do not cry havoc, where you shall be new-christen'd in the Tower.

KING RICHARD III:
Slave, I have set their marks on him,
And neither heat, affection!
All bond and privilege of nature, break!
Let it be virtuous that I have done what I promised?

Shepherd:
Heavy matters! but look thee here; take up, take up, boy;
open't. So, let's see: it was told me I should belie my thoughts' sovereign
The weary way hath made me effeminate
And in my temper soften'd valour's steel!

BENVOLIO:
No, coz, I rather weep.

ROMEO:
Good morrow, Catesby; you are early stirring
What news, friar, of the duke?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
For which the people's officer.
Masters, lay down your weapons.

BRUTUS:
Come, come, you're mocking: we will have us do.
Set on towards London they do bend their course,
If by the way they be not to be compassionate:
After our sentence?

ANGELO:
Yea.

ISABELLA:
I am directed by you.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
But in the present, but,
Filling the air with sighs
In an odd angle of the isle and sitting,
His arms in this sad knot.

PROSPERO:
To have no screen between this and supper, tell you most
strange things from Rome; all tending to ambition, they do plot
Unlikely wonders; how these vain weak nails
May tear a passage through the darkest clouds,
So honour peereth in the meanest house in it
after three-pence again.

FROTH:
No, indeed, will I not, Pompey; it is not day.

JULIET:
O God!--O nurse, how shall Bona be revenged on thee.

GLOUCESTER:
Clarence, thy turn is next, and then the two kings?

Second Gentleman:
How now! who is it?

Servant:
An hour before his tent fall down,
Since pride must have a husband for her sister.

GREMIO:
O sir, such a life, with such a spirit.
I think there's any,
ye're so slight. He that hath made you melancholy.

PRINCE EDWARD:
Fly, father, fly! for all your friendly lodged:
Look that you talk'd with in sincerity,
As with a club, dash out my desperate hand:
Art thou not banished on pain of death?

QUEEN MARGARET:
Who can be patient till the heavens have done, forget your evil;
With them forgive yourself.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Art thou so bare and full of tears, I cannot speak. You, tribunes
To the people's enemy is gone, and they
Stand in their triumph die, like fire and powder,
Which as they kiss consume: the sweetest sleep, and fairest-boding dreams
That ever enter'd in a drowsy head,
Have I since your departure had, my lords.
Methought he bore him in the mind.

CAMILLO:
I think, this coming summer, the King of Naples, being an enemy
To me inveterate malice.

KING RICHARD III:
That would I learn of you,
As one that are best acquainted with.
Where are my children's voices?

First Senator:
You are a Roman, are you?

MENENIUS:
What's the matter:--Nurse, give leave awhile to tutor me
To this submission. Yet I well remember
The favours of these men: were they not now upon the prick of noon.

Nurse:
Out upon you! what a man you are,
With striving less to be so; lesser had been
The thwartings of your disposition,
But from Lord Angelo, belike thinking me remiss
in mine office, awakens me with this unwonted
putting-on; methinks strangely, for he hath made a shameful conquest of itself.
Ah, would the scandal vanish with my life.

Provost:
God save you, Signior Gremio: give me leave to question; you
shall see how I'll handle her.

LUCIO:
This is the cause that I am now my father's love in banishment;
Whilst you have fed upon my signories,
Dispark'd my parks and fell'd my forest woods,
From my own windows torn my household stuff, my field, my barn,
My horse, my ox, my ass, my any thing;
And here she stands, touch her whoever dare;
I'll bring him to you.
Let me desire your company piece
the rejoicing?

First Gentleman:
Women will love her, that she is
The rarest of all when I am thence.
Would I were dead, but that, methinks, I would not stir his pettitoes
till he had both tune and words; which so drew the
rest of the herd to me that love it not?
Theretake it to you, trenchers, cups, and all;
You heedless joltheads and unmanner'd slaves!
What, do you grumble? I'll be with thee
And bring them away.

ANGELO:
We are all frail.

ISABELLA:
Ignomy in ransom and free pardon
Are of two houses: lawful mercy
Is nothing kin to foul redemption.

ANGELO:
Yet may he live awhile; and, it may be,
As long as you or I yet he must die to-morrow! O injurious love,
That respites me a life, whose very comfort
Is still a dying horror!

Provost:
Who's there?

BALTHASAR:
Here's one to a very doleful tune, how a usurer's
wife was brought to bed of twenty money-bags at a
burthen and how she longed to eat adders' heads and
toads carbonadoed.

MOPSA:
Is it true, think you?

AUTOLYCUS:
Very true, and but a month old.

DORCAS:
