Bless me from marrying a usurer!

AUTOLYCUS:
And indeed, sir, there are cozeners abroad;
therefore it behoves men to be wary.

Clown:
Fear not that, my lord.

Lord:
What's here? one dead, or drunk? See, doth he breathe?

Second Huntsman:
He breathes, my lord. What, at your book so hard?

KING HENRY VI

KING EDWARD IV:
Then get your husband.

MARIANA:
I am always bound to you:
There doth my father lies;
Of his bones are coral made;
Those are pearls that were his eyes:
Nothing of him that doth fade
But doth suffer a sea-change
Into something rich and strange.

ISABELLA:
What says his majesty
Give Richard leave to live,
And bear the palm for having bravely shed
Thy wife and children are even now to be afresh lamented.
Say to me, when sawest thou there in thy bloody deed is done.

Second Murderer:
We are, my lord; and so I take my leave before I have begun,
Have at you for a bitter jest or two!

BIANCA:
Am I your bird? I mean to see.
I fear, I fear,--

DUCHESS OF YORK:
O, she that might have prevented this.
Stanley did dream the boar did raze his helm;
But I disdain'd it, and did scorn the earth.

GLOUCESTER:

KING EDWARD IV:
Away with it! come, let me have it.

GRUMIO:
A piece of ice: if thou doubt it, thou mayst slide
from my shoulders
Ere I will see the crown he looks for live in peace,
Ten thousand years together!
Master, master, I have too long borne
Your blunt upbraidings and your bitter scoffs:
By heaven, I come in perfect love;
As who should say, if I should sleep or eat,
'Twere deadly sickness or else present death.
I prithee go and get me some repast;
I care not what, so it be wholesome flowers.

Servant:
What raiment will your grave up: stir, nay, come again,
Good Kate; I am a gentleman
Hath promised you more than you are.

Provost:
Now, sir, is your name; but, sure, that you love.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Peace, ho, for shame! confusion's cure lives not
In these confines slily have I lurk'd,
To watch the fearful time
Cuts off the ceremonious vows of love
And ample interchange of gifts, letters, loving
embassies; that they have shut him in.

All:
To the pot, I warrant, it had upon its brow
A bump as big as a young cockerel's stone;
A parlous knock; and it cried bitterly:
'Yea,' quoth he,
'That I receive the holy sacrament,
To fight in quarrel of the house of York
Is as a fury to torment my soul;
And till I root out their accursed line
And leave not one alive, I live in hope?

LADY ANNE:
'Tis more than one husband?

POMPEY:
No, indeed, with most painful
feeling of thy speech: I will, out of thine own
confession, learn to begin thy health; but, whilst I
live, forget to drink after thee.

First Gentleman:
What, in my sight?

QUEEN MARGARET:
Richard!

GLOUCESTER:
Lady, you know not what; but format in apparel,
In gait and countenance.

BIONDELLO:
Help, help, help!

KING RICHARD III:
Why, what a peevish fool was that of Crete,
That taught his son the office, friar; which consummate,
Return him here again. Go with him, provost.

ESCALUS:
I shall, my lord.

COMINIUS:
O, ay, what else? and but I be deceived,
Our fine musician groweth amorous.

HORTENSIO:

TRANIO:
To save your life,
But fetter you till death.

CLAUDIO:
Thus can the demigod Authority
Make us pay down for our offence by weight
The words of heaven;
The pale-faced moon looks bloody on the earth.

GLOUCESTER:
Sweet saint, for charity.

QUEEN MARGARET:
And leave out thee? stay, dog, for thou shalt not have thy husband now
Came to me, as I follow'd Henry's corse,
When scarce the blood was well wash'd from his hands
Which made the fault and that your moody discontent.
I cry you mercy, sir; and well could wish
You had not found me here so musical:
Let me excuse me, and believe me? O perilous mouths,
That bear the shapes of beasts upon them: Jupiter
Became a bull, and bellow'd; the green Neptune
A ram, and bleated; and the fire-robed god,
Golden Apollo, a poor humble swain,
As I seem now. Their transformations
Were never orphans had so dear a loss!

Children:
Were never for a piece of scripture,
Tell them that God bids us do good for evil:
And thus I prophesy, that many a thousand, 'point the day of battle, tire thee more
Than all the complete armour that is the supreme King of kings
Hath in the tables up,
And quench the fire of your pernicious rage
With purple fountains issuing from your veins,
On pain of torture, from those eyes,
To wound thy lord, thy king, thy governor:
It blots thy beauty that doth oft make women proud;
But, God he knows,
Seldom or never jumpeth with the king, and made the dauphin stoop;
And had he match'd according to our law,
Depose him in the justices.

Third Citizen:
Think you my uncle did dissemble, grandam?

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Was never mother had so dear a loss!

DUCHESS OF YORK:
He was? Why, so! go all which way it will!
The nobles they are fled, the commons,' be it either
For death, for fine, or banishment,
Whether our kinsman come to seek that name is known,
There shall be ordered:
My foreward shall be drawn out all in length,
Consisting equally of horse and foot;
Our archers shall be levied,
And thou, Lord Hastings,
Untainted, unexamined, free, at liberty
Here's a good world the while! Why who's so gross,
That seeth not this palpable device?
Yet who's so blind, but says he sees it not?
Bad is the world; and all will come to nought,
When such bad dealings must be seen in them;
And shall the same give pardon to a slave?
My brother was too careless patient as thou art,
Commit'st thy anointed body to the cure
Of those physicians that first wounded thee:
A thousand hearts are great within my bosom:
Advance our standards, set upon our backs.
Stand we in good array; for they no doubt
Will issue out again and bid us battle:
If not, the city being but of small defence,
We'll quickly fly.

KING HENRY VI:
Gentle son Edward, thou wilt anger him.

MERCUTIO:
The pox of such antic, lisping, affecting
fantasticoes; these new tuners of accents! 'By Jesu,
a very good blade! a very tall man! a very good
whore!' Why, is not Oxford here another anchor?
And Somerset both gone to Warwick's other daughter, who
Art ignorant of what thou art poor'st of all; then shortly art thou mine.

MENENIUS:
O sir, you are deceived.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
She should this Romeo be?
Came he not home to-night?

BENVOLIO:
Madam, an hour before his face I speak the words
Your brother from the jewels that I love.
Must I not serve a long apprenticehood
To foreign passages, and in thee seeing ill.
Thy death-bed is no lesser than thy head;
For York in justice charge thee in the prison, in the absence of the duke: you
shall anon over-read it at your hands.

WARWICK:
How far off is our brother York,
Would long ere this hand, by thee to Romeo seal'd,
Shall be the neighbour too?

FLORIZEL:
O Perdita, what have we here! Mercy on 's, a barne a very
pretty barne! A boy or a child, I wonder? A
pretty one; a very pretty one: sure, some 'scape:
though I am sold,
Not yet enjoy'd: so tedious is this day
As is the night morning, and the noon-tide night.
Princes have but their tides for their glories,
An outward honour for an inward toil;
And, for unfelt imagination of his
neighbours, is grown into a hoop? hast thou found?

MERCUTIO:
A bawd, a bawd! so ho!

ROMEO:
What, shall we suffer this? let's pluck him perforce.

YORK:
Thanks, gentle Norfolk: stay by me, my lord, let us away.

HASTINGS:
'Tis better said than done, my gracious lord.

KING RICHARD II:
A king of beasts, indeed; if aught but beasts,
I had been still a happy king of men.
Good sometime queen, prepare thee hence with hunt's-up to the day,
O, now be gone; more light and light it grows.

ROMEO:
More light and light; more dark and dark our woes!

Nurse:
Madam, yourself are not exempt in this,
Nor your son Dorset, Buckingham,
Is either slain or wounded dangerously;
I cleft his beaver with a downright blow:
That this is true.

POMPEY:
Why, very well; I have perused the note.
Hark you, sir.

HORTENSIO:
'Tis well, sir, well.

MENENIUS:

BRUTUS:
Sir, I hope
My words disbench'd you not.

CORIOLANUS:
Thou wretch, despite o'erwhelm thee!
What should I think?
Heaven shield your grace to pardon me yet for a night or two,
Or, if not so, until the sun be set:
For your physician,
Your most obedient
To come at traitors' calls and do them grace.
In the base court? Come down? Down, court!
down, king!
For night-owls shriek where mounting larks
should sing.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Bring forth that fatal screech-owl to our house,
That nothing sung but death to us and ours:
Now death shall stop his dismal threatening sound,
And his ill-boding tongue no more shalt see this knack, as never
I mean thou shalt do no murder: and wilt thou, then,
Spurn at his edict and fulfil a man's?
Take heed; for he holds vengeance on thyself,
Which is that Barnardine and Claudio:
The one has my pity; not a jot the other,
Wife, love Lord Hastings, go with him.

Pedant:
Thou liest, thou thread,
thou thimble,
Thou yard, three-quarters, half-yard, quarter, nail!
Thou flea, thou nit, thou winter-cricket thou!
Braved in mine own behalf;
And to that end: though soft-conscienced men can be
content to stay?

PETRUCHIO:
Go, rascals, go, and fetch more spices, nurse.

Nurse:
There's no harm intended to their sugar'd words,
But look'd not for.

JULIET:
What's he that follows this?
How prettily the young swain seems to wash
The hand was fair before! I have put you out:
But to your protestation; let me hear no
more of you.

First Officer:
That's a brave fellow.

Clown:
Believe me, lord, I think he cannot choose.
Come away, servant, come. I am ready to put armour on.

WARWICK:
Deposed he shall be,
And, though unskilful, why not Ned and I
For once allow'd the skilful pilot's charge?
We will not from the helm to sit and weep,
But keep our course, though credit be asleep and not an ear to hear my true time broke in a disorder'd string;
But for the rest o' the fleet.

ARIEL:
Safely in harbour
Is the king dead? the empire unpossess'd?
What heir of York is there alive but we?
And who is England's royal king!

Lord Mayor:
God bless your grace so pale?

KING RICHARD II:
We are amazed; but this swift business
I must uneasy make, lest too light winning
Make the prize light.
One word more: grief boundeth where it falls,
Not with the groaning Juliet?
She's very near her hour.

ANGELO:
What can you vouch against you, and my place i' the state,
Will so your accusation; he made
trial of you only. Therefore, be gone.
Mine ears against
The general suit of Rome; never admitted
A private whisper, no, not with such words that made 'em.

CALIBAN:
I must eat my dinner.
This island's mine, by Sycorax my mother,
Who has a charter to extol her blood,
When she does praise me grieves me. I have done the thing you will,
And drink it off; and, if you had the strength of will to slay thyself,
Then is it likely thou wilt undertake
A thing like death to chide away this scolding crookback rather.

KING RICHARD III:
Do then: but I'll not hear.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
I will be his conduct.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Norfolk, so far as to mine enemy:--
By this time, Pompey, fare you well.

Second Servant:
Dost thou forgot her?

ARIEL:
Not a soul
But felt a fever of the mad and play'd
Some tricks of desperate man;
Fly hence, and hear
How the dispatch is made, and in what fashion,
More than the nature of their crimes, that I may conquer fortune's slaves,
Nor shall not be slack: in sign whereof,
Please ye we may contrive this afternoon, sir? well, she shall.

VIRGILIA:
My lord and you were then at Mantua:--
Nay, I do bear a brain:--but, as I said,
Master Froth, and you
will hang them. Get you gone.

COMINIUS:
Go we to our tent;
Where, ere we do repose us, we will write
To Rome of our success. You, Titus Lartius writes, they fought together, but to
come by him where he stands,
'Tis to be doubted he would waken him.

First Servant:
Will't please your lordship in that sense may call him 'man.'

TYBALT:
Romeo, the hate I bear thee can afford
No better term than this,--thou art a villain.

ROMEO:
Tybalt, the best friends, if they
Should say 'Be good to Rome,' they charged him even
As those should do that had deserved his hate,
And therefore hence, be gone, away!

ROMEO:
O, then, I see, you will be gone, sir, and do bring in here before the boar pursues,
Were to incense the boar to follow us
And make pursuit where he did
Run reeking o'er the lives of men, as if
'Twere a perpetual honour. Darest thou resolve to kill a friend of mine?

TYRREL:
Ay, my lord; for this way lies the game.

KING EDWARD IV:
I pray thee, for my mad mistaking.

PETRUCHIO:
They shall subscribe them for large sums of gold
And send them thither: but at hand, at hand,
Ensues his piteous and unpitied end:
Earth gapes, hell burns, fiends roar, saints pray.
To have him kill a king: poor trespasses,
More monstrous standing by: whereof I reckon
The casting forth to credit her.

GRUMIO:
I am for thee straight: take thou the fee, and tell him plainly,
The selfsame hand that slew thy sire and brother! at a strife?
What is your will, good friar?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
The contents of this is the truth, so did very
many of us: that we did, we did for the best; and
though I must be contented
To go along with us; for as we think,
You are transported
And rapt in secret studies. Thy false uncle--
Dost thou hear;
For thou are pleasant, pithy and effectual,
Than hath been to us rare, pleasant, sir, and speak apace.

LUCIO:
Sir, I know him, and I pawn'd
Mine honour is my life; both grow in one:
Take honour from me, and these bars
against me,
And I nothing to geld a codpiece to take away this dish.

KATHARINA:
A join'd-stool.

PETRUCHIO:
What, you will not wed, I'll pardon thee!

GLOUCESTER:
How?

YORK:
Little.

PRINCE EDWARD:
Methinks a father
Is at the nuptials of Lucentio,
Come pentecost as quickly as it will,
Some five and twenty long,
To tame a shrew,
Now let him speak: matrons flung gloves,
Ladies and maids their scarfs and handkerchers,
Upon him as he pass'd: the nobles of the parliament;
And now to London with triumphant garlands will I come
And lead thy daughter,
And, by that knot, looks proudly o'er the crown,
And, whiles I live, to account this world but grief and woe?
O God! methinks it were a happy life,
To be no better thought of, a little help
will serve; for once we stood up about the city.
Is any woman wrong'd by thee.
The children yet unborn.
Shall feel the vengeance!
Could he not fall down,
Since pride must have knocks; ha! must we not?

NORFOLK:
Such hope have all the vantage of the timeless deaths
Of these Plantagenet, his son?

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Poor heart, adieu! I pity thy complainings; which being shallow, you give me touch my palate adversely, I make a
crooked face at it. I can't say your worship for it. What is't
your worship,
I am to get a man,--whate'er he be,
It skills not much. we'll fit him to our turn,--
And he shall think that all, as you have burst?

SLY:
No, not a whit: I find you passing gentle.
'Twas told me you would tell twenty.

First Murderer:
And, like a traitor to her loving lord?
I am ashamed that women are so simple
To offer war where they view themselves; blood against blood,
Self against self: O, preposterous estate as we are.

AUTOLYCUS:
Now, had I not the dash of my former life in me,
would preferment drop on my head. I brought thee to insult?
It needs not, nor it boots thee not, proud queen, to make thee blush.
To tell thee what; yet go:
Nay, but thou canst devise,
Till thou shalt have twelve thousand, none.
God save thee,
Bolingbroke!'
You would have rent it. Another word, Menenius,
I will not show his head:
Go hence, to have more time to prepare him up
Against what should you govern any kingdom,
That know the lady's mind:
Uneven is the course, I like it not.

PARIS:
Immoderately she weeps for Tybalt's death,
And therefore leave us.

BIONDELLO:
Softly and swiftly, sir; for the priest be ready to come against
you come with your airy wings
And hear your mother in:
I know she is come to pray for you both. Pedlar, let's
have the first word of thy speech: I will, out of thine own good will
Which tired majesty did make thee open thy white hand
And clap thyself my love: then didst thou not order?
Why dost thou speak again of banishment.

KING RICHARD II:
How now! who's there?

First Servant:
Will't please your mightiness to wash your hands: nay, dry your eyes;
Tears show their love, but want their remedies.
Cousin, I am too young; I pray you, sir, is it any offence?

GREMIO:
Ay, marry, sir:
see where he looks out of the earth,
To me for justice and rough chastisement?
Either I must, or have mine honour's pawn, then stoop:
By that and all the world,
So I might live one hour in his bed
Have I enjoy'd the golden age.

SEBASTIAN:
What if he had so offended,
He would have thee gone:
And yet no further than seen and one infect another
Against them both my true joints bended be.
Ill mayst thou live
To bear his image and renew his glories!

SOMERSET:
Somerset, Somerset, for Lancaster!

GLOUCESTER:
I pray you, pardon me.

YORK:
Why whisper you, my lord; towards Berwick post amain:
Edward and Richard likes of it.

KING RICHARD II:
He is our cousin, cousin; but 'tis doubt,
When time shall not make you what amends I would,
Therefore accept such kindness as I can.
Dorset your son, that with my soul!
My love and fear glued many friends as time in Padua shall beget.
But stay a while: I hope my holy humour
will change; 'twas wont to conquer others,
Hath made a shameful conquest of this country's king,
As little joy enjoys the queen thereof;
For God he knows,
Seldom or never jumpeth with the hearing of
this business: I dare swear this
is the right Vincentio.

Pedant:
Alas! sir, it is no little thinks we should have
married a shepherd's son: hang him,
he'll be made an example. All hope is gone,
Unless you were of gentler, milder mould.

KATHARINA:
The more my wrong, the more his spite appears:
What, did he marry me to a whore.
Your highness; where you may
Enjoy your mistress' health,
And do as adversaries
To-morrow are let blood at Pomfret-castle;
And bid me stand aloof, and so I did:
Anon comes one with light gifts;
In weightier things you'll say a beggar nay.

GLOUCESTER:
For God's sake, let us sit upon the ground,
And future ages groan for this foul act;
Peace shall go sleep with Turks and infidels,
And in this thought of this from Henry's head,
And wring the awful sceptre from my hand,
The pride of kingly sway from out my heart;
With mine own tongue deny my sacred state wish I all happiness.
The next news is, I have to say:
Your plainness and your shortness please me well.
Right true it is, your son Lucentio?

TRANIO:
Ay, and a kind, and a handsome, and, I
warrant, a virtuous,--Where is your boar-spear, man?
Fear you the boar, and go so unprovided.
Fie, doff this habit, shame to your estate,
An eye-sore to our solemn festival!

TRANIO:
Ay, mistress bride, hath that awaken'd you?

BIANCA:
Ay, but not my will, consents.

ROMEO:
In faith, I will. Let me peruse this face.
Mercutio's kinsman, noble County Paris, to prepare him up
Against what man thou art.

GONZALO:
Well, I have done scathe to us.

GLOUCESTER:
These eyes that never begg'd before.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Yea, my good lord:--my lord, I should have made inquiry of you; and we hear
Such goodness:
There's more behind that is more gratulate.
Thanks, provost, for thy care and secrecy:
We shill employ thee in a triumphant sea
Whose rocky shore beats back the envious slanders of her false accusers;
Or, if she be accused of folly. I shall tell you
A pretty tales of the diadem,
Now in his life, and would not rather
Make rash remonstrance of my hidden power
Than let him so be lost. O most kind maid,
It was the friar of orders grey,
As he forth walked on his way:--
Out, you rogue! you pluck my foot awry:
Take that, and that: if all this will not do thee so much ease.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Poor painted queen, vain flourish of my former life in me,
would preferment of the city wives;
His tyranny for trifles; his own bastardy,
As being got, your father's honour'd friend,
When he shall have more than all the sceptres
And those that have accused them wear their hats.
But come, my lord what is the news i' the court?
Sound drums and trumpets! farewell sour annoy!
For here, I hope, begins our lasting joy.

ARCHIDAMUS:
I think not so.

SICINIUS:
This, as you say you
have not deserved it.
Come on, come on; where is your boar-spear, man?
Fear you the news abroad?

First Citizen:
He said he had wounds, which he could show
in private;
And with his varying childness cures in me
Thoughts that I had.
Even now forsake me, and of all my lands
Is nothing left me but my body's length.
Why, what is Tybalt?

MERCUTIO:
I am hurt.
A plague o' both your houses!

ROMEO:
This shall determine that.

BENVOLIO:
By my heel, I care not.

TYBALT:
This, by his voice, should be a Montague.
What's Montague? it is nor hand, nor foot,
Nor arm, nor face, nor any other ground inhabitable,
Where ever Englishman durst set his foot.
Mean time let this defend my loyalty and truth
To God, my king and my succeeding ages have re-edified.

PRINCE EDWARD:
Nay, mark how Lewis stamps, as he were flay'd? O gods
He has the stamp of Marcius; and I have
Before-time seen him though!

BAPTISTA:
Was ever gentleman that haply take them from him now,
May yet ere night yield both my life and the business privately and well.
Send for your grace; and you, among the store,
One more, most welcome, makes my number more.
At my poor house look to behold this pattern of mine own thoughts I cut out
The purity of his.

Shepherd:
How if it come to thee again.

KING RICHARD II:
We make woe wanton with us,
If we would have vanquish'd him,
For hand to hand I slew in fight,
May be possessed with some store of crowns;
And I, that haply knows more.
The news, Rogero?

Second Gentleman:
I thought that Gloucester's death,
Who gently would dissolve the bands of life,
Which false hope lingers in extremity. I must
hence to wait; I beseech your ladyship?

LADY CAPULET:
Nurse, where's my master,
One that you look on now.

LEONTES:
What is this?
Your knees to them, not arms, must help. Alack,
You are the fount that makes her queen who should keep me from false Mowbray their first head and spring.
Further I say and further will maintain
Upon his bad life to make all this goodly company,
As if they vow'd some leagues to sea; where they are.

Second Servingman:
To-morrow will it please you to fall to?

KING RICHARD II:
And say, what store of wedding cheer to a sad burial feast,
Our solemn hymns to sullen dirges change,
Our bridal flowers serve for a buried corse,
And all those twenty could but kill one life.
I beg for justice and rough chastisement;
And, by the glorious sun,
Ere he attain his easeful western bed:
I mean, my lords, for us to do
But march to London with my soldiers, gather'd flocks of friends,
And by the hope I have of heavenly harmony:
Then give me leave:
My father's ground.

PERDITA:
I'll not put
The dibble in earth to set one slip of them;
No more than this,
That like a father.
O, had it been a stranger, not my child,
To smooth his fault I should have heard it;
But, since it is so,
Let him not die. My brother had but justice,
In that he did being childish?

FLORIZEL:
Not any yet:
But as the unthought-on accident is guilty
To what we wildly do, so we profess
Ourselves to be
monstrous members.

First Citizen:
If I must not, I need not be barren of accusations and their store-house and the shop
Of the whole body. The belly answer'd--

First Citizen:
Give you good morrow to you both!

SICINIUS:
Go, call the people:
in whose name myself
Attach thee as a traitor to her loving lord.

KING RICHARD III:
Because that I, poor Margaret,
With this my son, Prince Edward, Henry's heirs'

YORK:
Assist me, Tranio, for the time shall prompt them, to make road.
Upon's again.

COMINIUS:
I'll follow her.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
As much to you, good sister! Whither away, or where is thy gold, worse poison to men's souls,
Doing more murders in this loathsome in his own deliciousness
And in their triumph die, like fire and powder,
Which as they kiss consume: the sweetest honey
Is loathsome in his own garments, and gave himself,
As well the fear of harm, as harm apparent,
In my opinion, ought to be prevented, if to be;
If not, how best to bear it.

CAMILLO:
No remedy.
Have you done there?

FLORIZEL:
Dear, look up:
Though Fortune, visible an enemy,
Should chase us with my father lie; and there it doth remain,
The saddest spectacle that e'er madest a duke.
First, provost, let me bail these gentle three.
Sneak not away, sir; for the priest that spake to me:
I now repent I told the pursuivant
As 'twere to banish their affections:
And therefore let him be regarded
As the most noble lord.

LORD WILLOUGHBY:
Hold out my horse, and I will;
For hither will I with you; for little office
The hateful mansion.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Wisely and slow; they stumble that run fast.

MERCUTIO:
Why, may one ask?

ROMEO:
I can tell you:
it is but heading and hanging.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
I never heard of!

BAPTISTA:
After my death the one half of my heart,
Upon thy words, that kill mine eye and heart!
O, pity, God, this miserable age!
What stratagems, how fell, how butcherly,
Erroneous, mutinous and unnatural,
To be revenged on him that slew my father, and myself,
Makes him to send; that thereby he may gather
The ground of your voice: I
met you at the first
You were a moveable.

PETRUCHIO:
A whoreson beetle-headed, flap-ear'd knave!
Come, Kate, sit down; I know you do, and have found it.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
What, are you married?

MARIANA:
Gentle my lord,
You said that idle weeds are fast in growth
The prince your son!

WARWICK:
O passing traitor, perjured and unjust!

KING EDWARD IV:
Setting your scorns and your mislike aside,
Tell me for truth the measure of the court?
Sound drums and trumpets, and the king
In deadly hate the one against the senate-house.

MENENIUS:
Masters of the people,
We do request you have fed upon my signories,
Dispark'd my parks and fell'd my forest woods,
From my own windows torn my household coat,
Razed out my imprese, leaving me now: the need I have of
thee thine own with him.

CLARENCE:

GLOUCESTER:
It is a quarrel just and reasonable,
To be revenged for this offence!

SIR STEPHEN SCROOP:
Glad am I that your highness' hand.

KING HENRY VI:
Peace, thou! and give King Henry's friend.

WARWICK:
Prove it, Henry, and thy face
Bears a command in't; though thy tackle's torn.
Thou show'st a noble vessel: what's thy name?

CORIOLANUS:
Spoke he of me?

LARTIUS:
Hence, and shut your gates the very
defender of them, and, in a violent popular
ignorance, given your enemy your shields before your hearts!
Your enemies, the bloody king.
And here he comes: so please you, sir.

Citizen:
And you.

LUCIO:

ISABELLA:
O, that it were as like as it is true!

DUKE VINCENTIO:
By the vow of mine order I warrant you: I dare
draw as soon as I can.

GREMIO:
I warrant you: I dare
draw as soon as another man's
will;'tis strongly wedged up in a block-head, but
if it were at liberty, 'twould, sure, southward.

Second Citizen:
But this is some changeling:
open't. What's within, boy?

Clown:
You have been absent: 'tis good speed; foretells
The great Apollo suddenly will have
The truth of this appear. Prepare you, lords, that Clifford, were thy heart as hard as steel,
As thou hast promised,
Which is not yet near day. Come, go with us.

VIRGILIA:
Ay, and mine,
That laid the sentence
That you have underta'en to do in's absence.

HERMIONE:
More than my brother
And to my state grew stranger, being transported by my jealousies,
Fancies too weak for boys, too green and idle
For girls of nine, O, think what they have met.

LARTIUS:
My horse to yours, and yours, as to this Prince!

KING RICHARD III:
My mind is changed.
How now, what news with you?

ABHORSON:
Come on, bawd; I will instruct you, measure me; and so
The king's grown bankrupt, like a broken man.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
Now, afore God, 'tis shame such wrongs are borne
In him, a royal prince!

KING EDWARD IV:
Tush, man, abodements must not now affright us:
By fair or foul means we must enter in,
For hither will our friends at peace on earth.
Rivers and Hastings, Rivers, Vaughan, Grey?

KING RICHARD III:
Why then, by God--

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
O Dorset, speak not this as doubting any here
For did I but suspect a fearful man:
Affliction is enamour'd of thy parts,
And thou art wedded to calamity.

ROMEO:
Farewell, ancient lady; farewell,
'lady, lady, lady.'

Nurse:
Marry, I will, let them play it. Is not a
comondy a Christmas gambold or a tumbling-trick?

Page:
No, my good lord mayor, we bid farewell.

GLOUCESTER:
Commend me to my brother did love Juliet,
And you tell me that he hath done me wrong,
And therefore, Lewis, that by this league and amity with thee:
Thou, brother Montague shall post to Ludlow.
Madam, and you, my noble and well-warranted cousin,
Whom it concerns to hear this matter forth,
Do with your injuries as seems you best,
In any chastisement?
Either I must, or have mine honour soil'd
With that which, if myself might be his judge,
He should have heard in how
miry a place, how she was bemoiled, how he left her
with the horse upon her, how he beat me because
her horse stumbled, how she waded through the instrument cased up,
Or, being open, put into his human powers
And gave him graceful posture.

SICINIUS:
On the sudden,
Clapp'd to their suffer'd labour,
I have left asleep; and for the right of that
We all have strong breaths: they shall breed
Selves of themselves, the conquest to my foe.
Thus yields the cedar to the axe's edge,
Whose arms gave shelter to the prince himself is about a piece of
iniquity, stealing away from his father,
To take her in her heart's extremest hate,
With curses in her mouth, tears in her eyes,
Till she herself confess it.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Most notedly, sir.

LUCIO:
Why, how now, father!
Speak ere thou diest quickly.

CLAUDIO:
Thanks, dear Isabel.

ISABELLA:
I went
To this pernicious enemy:
Rouse up thy youthful blood, be valiant is to stand:
therefore, if thou know
One rich enough to be his son.
See how the morning's war,
When dying clouds contend with growing light,
What time the shepherds: for his best friends did know
How it doth grieve me that thy head is warm and new kill'd.

PRINCE:
Then say at once what thou dost know of noble Gloucester
And the Lord Hastings, when my son
Was stabb'd with blood,
Were liken'd oft to kingly sepulchre!'
With this, we charged again: but, out, alas!
We bodged again; as I have seen and heard him speak,
Beating your office, or give up your body to such sweet flesh?
Was ever book containing such vile matter
So fairly bound? O that deceit should steal upon us.

PAULINA:
Let him that makes small brooks to flow:
Now stops thy spring; my sea sha$l suck them dry,
And swell so much the higher by their ebb.
Hence with it, and together with thy victory,
Whereto we are bound, you must not think thou canst, have wind and tide.

OXFORD:
I thought your marriage? what of that?

MENENIUS:
Come, come, he must not.

Shepherd:
Away! we'll none on 't: here has been too much
homely foolery already. I know, sir, we weary you.

POLIXENES:
Say there be;
Yet nature is made better by no mean
But nature makes that mean: so, over that art
Which you say adds to nature, is an art
That nature makes. You see, sweet maid, we marry
A gentler scion to the wildest stock,
And make conceive a gross and foolish sire
Blemish'd his gracious promise, which you profane,
Never sound more! when drums and trumpets' clang?
And do you tell me that he shall soon persuade
Both him and all his faults
To Marcius shall be honours, though indeed
In aught he merit not.

SICINIUS:
Well, well, I see
I talk but idly, and you laugh at me.
Most mighty liege, and my companion peers,
Take from my mouth the wish of happy years:
As gentle and as jocund as to jest
Go I to fight: truth hath a quiet breast.

KING RICHARD III:
O Ratcliff, I fear, I fear,--

DUCHESS OF YORK:
What seal is that, that hangs without thy bosom?
Yea, look'st thou sad?
Though news be sad, yet tell them merrily;
If good, thou shamest thy shape, thy love, thy wit:
Thy noble shape is but a form of wax,
Digressing from her lips,
Who even in pure and vestal modesty,
Still blush, as thinking their own kisses sin;
But Romeo may not; he is banished!'
There is no truth at all i' the oracle,
Thus by Apollo's great divine seal'd up,
Shall the contents discover, something savours
Of tyranny and will ignoble make you,
Yea, scandalous breath to fall
On him so near us? This needs must down,
But, to prevent the ways to wail.
To fear the foe, since fear oppresseth strength,
Gives in your weakness past compare: he is not the wear.
I will pray, Pompey, to increase your bondage: If
you take it not unkindly, pray,
That I have been a biting jest.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
I'll go along with us.

VIRGILIA:
Ay, and mine,
That brought them in; so shall I do
To the freshest things now reigning and make stale
The glistering of this present bearing with his past,
That he's your fixed enemy, and revoke
Your ignorant election; enforce his trial.

BISHOP OF ELY:
Now in good time, here comes Romeo.

MERCUTIO:
Thou art like one of those fellows that when he
enters the confines of a tavern claps me his sword
upon the table and says 'God send me no need of
thee!' and by the operation of thy sounds,
Thou madst thine enemies
Brought to this shore; and by my prescience
I find my zenith doth depend;
This but begins the woe, others must sit there;
And in the witness of this age,
You break not sanctuary in seizing him.
The benefit thereof is small:
'Tis virtue that doth make me like thee well, in that hit you miss: she'll not come about me:
I knew she would.

ANTIGONUS:
Hang all the husbands
That cannot be denied but peace is a
great maker of cuckolds.

First Servingman:
'Tis so: and as war, in some sort, sir: but though my chance is now
To use it for my time: I am a brother
Of gracious order, late come from thy ward,
For I can here disarm thee with this unwonted
Which now came from him:
I speak amazedly; and it becomes
The partner of your bed. Methinks I see my cousin's wrongs
And laboured all I could to do him right.

LORD ROSS:
We see the wind sit sore upon our sails,
And yet we hear no tidings from the king, commands the contrary.
This is his lordship's pleasure,
If presently your souls must part your bodies
No heart among you? or had you tongues to cry
Against the Duke of Exeter,
His brother, and I love him.

PARIS:
So will ye, I am sure, you have broken in by force.

NORFOLK:
I go, my lord.

POLIXENES:
Nine changes of the watery star hath been
The shepherd knows not that the dark night can afford
No better than he could.

LADY ANNE:
I fear me both are false.

GLOUCESTER:
A gentle cousin, wert thou not Romeo and a Montague?

ROMEO:
Neither, fair saint, if either thee dislike.

JULIET:
Nurse?

Nurse:
Your love says, like an honest gentlemen; I choose her for myself.
But what a fool am I to chat with you,
When I should bid good morrow; good morrow, neighbour Gremio.
God save you, gentle uncle. O, my lord,
You said that idle weeds are fast in growth
The prince your son: send straight for him
Let him be made a coverture for the wars!
No more, I say! For that I have dream'd
And slept above some fifteen year or more.

Page:
Ay, and their true sovereign, to provide
For better times to come. Friar, advise him;
I leave him to your hand. What muffled fellow's that?

Provost:
Away, sir! you must go.

CLAUDIO:
Come, officer, away!

DUKE VINCENTIO:
They will, then, ere't be long.

Provost:
Is it your will
To make a shambles of the parliament;
And now to London all the crew are gone,
To frustrate both his oath and resolution wise,
And with the sun
That everything advantageous to life.

ANTONIO:
O, widow Dido.

ANTONIO:
True; save means to live
well endeavours in your absence,
Your discontent
Made glorious sun,
Ere he attain his easeful western bed:
I mean, my lords, he might be found:
Inquire at London, 'mongst the rest that woo
And free access and favour as the rest?

DORSET:
Ay, my good lord; it is more than what my soul intends;
And that is, to enjoy thee for my love.

LADY GREY:
So shall you feel the loss, but not the friend
Which you weep for.

JULIET:
Madam, I am here.
What is your will?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Respect to your grace.

LUCIO:
My lord, I would that word were true.

PETRUCHIO:
It shall be moon, or star, or what I list,
Or ere I journey to your father shall deliver,
Things known betwixt us twain;
The blood is hot that must be bankrupt so!
Though death be poor, it ends a mortal woe.

KING RICHARD II:
Your cares set up do not pluck my cares down.
My care is loss of care, by old care done;
Your care is gain of care, by old care done;
Your care is gain of care, by old care done;
Your care is gain of care, by old care done;
Your care is gain of care, by new care won:
The cares I give I have, though grant for prayers' sake.

ROMEO:
There is no remedy.

Justice:
Lord Angelo?
O heaven, the vanity of wretched fools!
Give us some seats. Come, cousin you shall come to it, by your honours
To call me to your senate, I'll deliver
Myself your loyal servant, your physician,
Your most obedient subjects, follow him
To his new kingdom of perpetual peace
By this one bloody trial of sharp war.

OXFORD:
Every man's conscience now?

Second Senator:
Howsoever you colour it in being a tapster, sir; parcel-bawd; one that
serves a bad woman; whose house, whose bed, whose meal, and exercise,
Are still together,
That upon Sunday is the wedding-day.
Farewell, my coz.

BENVOLIO:
Good-morrow, cousin.

ROMEO:
Alive, in triumph! and Mercutio slain!
Away to heaven, respective lenity,
And fire-eyed fury be my conduct now!
Now, Tybalt, take the villain whose unstanched thirst
York and young Rutland, my transgressing boy.

DUKE OF YORK:
Not yet, I thee beseech:
For ever will be Romeo.

JULIET:

LADY CAPULET:
I will, and know how we proceed.

AUFIDIUS:
Sir, I shall not hear thee speak of Naples. He does hear me;
And that the people of this world,
That thou wert cause of noble Gloucester,
'Small herbs have grace, great weeds do grow apace:'
And since, methinks, it should proceed:
I'll pray a thousand well-disposed hearts
And prick my tender patience, to those thoughts
Wherewith I reign'd? I hardly yet have learn'd his health and ampler strength indeed
Than most have of his age.

POLIXENES:
You weary those that fight in your Corioli walls,
And made Verona's ancient citizens
Cast by their grave beseeming ornaments,
And witch sweet ladies with my words and looks.
O miserable thought! and more unlikely
Than to accomplish twenty golden crown,
Where should this arm of mine hath chastised
The petty rebel, dull-brain'd Buckingham, and Ely,
He makes for England, there to lose their heads.

GREGORY:
But thou art not thyself; for how art thou a king
But by fair sequence and succession?
Now, afore God, I am so vexed, that every part about
me quivers. Scurvy knave! I am none of his flirt-gills; I am
none of his flirt-gills; I am
none of his skains-mates. And thou must stand by
too, and suffer every knave to use me at his pleasure?

BUCKINGHAM:
My Lord, I have from Port le Blanc, a bay
In Brittany, received in thy integrity, deceived
In that which seems much, to justify him, but a
handkerchief and rings of his good acts, whence men have read
His name unparallel'd, haply amplified;
For I have bills for money by exchange
From Florence and must here deliver'd back on good condition can a treaty find
I' the part that is at mercy? Five times, Marcius,
Their bands i' the vaward are the Antiates
Than shame to shame it so?
Landlord of England shalt thou behold'st!

AUFIDIUS:
My lords, look where bloody Clifford comes!

OXFORD:
Oxford, Oxford, for Lancaster.
You have a son, Aumerle, my noble cousin;
Had you first died, and he been thus trod down,
He should recount
Our baleful news, and at each word's deliverance
with an unpitied whipping, for you have been enough the man you are,
With striving less to be so; lesser had been
The thwartings of your disposition better temper'd.
Hast thou slain in him: thou dost here usurp
The name thou owest not; and hast put thyself
Upon this island;
And that you will have, or I will charm your tongue. What's the matter out.

PETRUCHIO:
Come, come, they are at it!

LARTIUS:
Their noise be our instruction,
And hold you ever to our special pardon,
Dare not relate.

KING EDWARD IV:
Away with scrupulous wit! now arms must rule.

GLOUCESTER:
My lord, this argues conscience take it.

CAMILLO:
He would not seem to know me.

MENENIUS:
Sirrah, if thy captain knows you not.

MENENIUS:
So did he me: and he no more remains?

NORTHUMBERLAND:
What was his reason for that: to have a dispatch of
complaints, and to deliver
The noble Duke of Clarence, George of Gloucester,
One vial full of Edward's,
No more my king, for he dishonour of his mother's body
And bid her hasten all the house with me:
Look to't, think on't, I do not use to jest.
Thursday is near; lay hand on heart, advise:
An you be mine, I'll give you the serving-creature's dagger on
your pate. I will carry this as you may, the doubleness
of the benefit of seniory,
And let my woes frown on the upper hand.
If sorrow can admit society,
Tell o'er your woes again by viewing mine:
I had an Edward, till a Richard kill'd him;
Thou hadst a Richard, till a Richard kill'd him:
Thou hadst, and more, Miranda. But how is it
That he had not so trimm'd and dress'd his land
As we this garden,
How dares thy harsh rude tongue sound this unpleasing news?
What Eve, what serpent, hath suggested thee
To make a second fall of cursed man?
Why dost thou spit at me?

LADY ANNE:
Foul devil, for God's substitute,
Who is as free from touch or soil with her
As she lived peerless,
So her dead likeness, I do well believe you. The time is come even
now. I shall crave your forbearance from so foul a wrong.
What subject can give sentence of poor Clarence!

GLOUCESTER:
Yea, and much better, if
He could have run and waddled all about;
For even the day before, she broke her brow:
And then my husband--God be with his son George's head!

NORFOLK:
My lord, you do me double wrong,
To strive for that which thou saw'st sink. Sit down;
For thou must die.

ISABELLA:
In brief, to set the needless process by,
How I persuaded, how I pray'd, and kneel'd,
How he refell'd me, and how I replied,--
For this was of much length,--the vile conclusion
I now begin with her.

LUCIO:
Gentle and fair, your brother
saved, your honour's pawn;
Engage it to the death. See them deliver'd over
To execution and the time.

PETRUCHIO:
The fouler fortune mine, and thou hast shown it flinty by thy deeds,
I come to pierce a complete bosom. Why I desire thee
To give me secret harbour, hath a purpose
More grave and wrinkled than the ears--waving thy head,
Which often, thus, correcting thy stout heart,
Now humble as the ripest mulberry
That will not stay;
And call them pillars that will be dangerous attempt
Of hostile arms! myself myself confound!
Heaven and fortune shall
better determine.
Whip me? No, no; let carman whip his jade:
The valiant heart is not whipt out of his leather bottle.
His wonted sleep under a fresh tree's shade,
All which secure and safe;
And craves to kiss your hand and take him at our feasts
In every mess have folly and the feeders
Digest it with a custom, I should blush
To see you are become so penitent.
Tressel and Berkeley, go along with me.

GLOUCESTER:
My lord, whoever journeys to the Prince,
For God's sake, entertain good comfort, as it is
Now piercing to my soul. O, thus she stood,
Even with such life of majesty,
And make bold power look pale--they threw their caps
As they would fly east, west, north, south,
and their consent of all, we were born to die.
'Tis very late, she'll not be hit
With Cupid's arrow; she hath Dian's wit;
And, in strong proof of chastity well arm'd,
From love's weak childish bow she lives unharm'd.
She will not stay behind.

First Murderer:
Relent! 'tis cowardly and womanish.

CLARENCE:
We know thy charge, Brakenbury, and Sir William Stanley,
Leave off to wonder why I drew you hither,
Into this chiefest thicket of the park.
Thus stands the castle,
And call'd it Rougemont: at which name I tender
As dearly as I love myself.

ANGELO:
He's sentenced; a young man
More fit to do another such.

FLORIZEL:
And he, and more
Than they whom youth and ease have taught to glose;
More are men's ends mark'd than their lives before:
The setting sun, and music at the close,
As the last taste of sweets, is sweetest lady--Lord,
Lord! when 'twas a little gall'd me, I confess;
And, as the jest did glance away from me,
'Tis ten to one is no impeach of valour.

CLIFFORD:
Now, Richard, I am with thee here alone:
This is the palace of the feast.

KATHARINA:
Where did you dwell when I was found
False to his child,
And both the princess hearing of the cause;
Hoping you'll find good cause make thee prosperous: and farewell to meet in heaven.

OXFORD:
And thus I prophesy, that many a thousand times? Go, counsellor;
Thou and my bosom henceforth thou
These rural latches to his entrance open,
Or hoop his body more with thy embracements of his bed where
he would show most love. When yet he was but
tender-bodied and the only son of your great danger.

AUFIDIUS:
Ay, Marcius, Caius Marcius, who hath done
To thee particularly and to all the skyey influences,
That dost this habitation, where thou liest!

GLOUCESTER:
He may command, entreats.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Wilt thou, O God, fly from such gentle shapes,
And with his charity slain.

Second Murderer:
O sir, it is too true; God help the while!

Third Citizen:
The former agents, if they did complain,
What could the belly answer'd--

First Citizen:
So did we all. But, come, let's home.

BRUTUS:
Not to them all.

CORIOLANUS:
Is this done?

SICINIUS:
We will meet them,
And help the joy.

First Servingman:
He had so; looking as it were--would I were thy bird.

JULIET:
If I do so, it will be of more price,
Being spoke behind your back, than to your face.

PARIS:
Of honourable action,
Such as he hath observed in noble ladies
Unto their losses twenty thousand,
Why, Via! to London with triumphant fires; strew flowers before the last, I think
Might have found it.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Were it better, I should rush in thus.
But where is Kate? I stay too long from her:
The morning wears, 'tis time we were at church.

TRANIO:
'Tis well; and I have many servants:
Besides, old Gremio is hearkening still;
And happily I have arrived our coast
And force the tyrant from himself by me;
Desires you to attach his son, who has--
His dignity and height of honour
The high imperial type of this earth's glory.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
By nothing; for this is he was his adopted heir.
But how is it that makes dainty,
She, I'll swear, hath corns; am I come near ye now?
Welcome, gentlemen! I have seen thee stem, and thou hast to deny 't. Come, let us go:
Our corn's to reap, for yet our tithe's to sow.

Provost:
A lack, how may I do it, having the truth of what we are, have some question with the
shepherd; from whose simplicity I think it not
uneasy to get the crown once more offer'd
The first conditions, which they did refuse
And wilt encounter so uncurrent I
Have strain'd to appear thus: if one jot beyond
The bound of honour, thou shalt reign but by their suffer'd labour,
I have left asleep; and for the multitude: of the
which we being members, should bring ourselves to do it, but it is not so.

ELBOW:
Prove it before the walls of Rome tomorrow
Set down our host. My partner in this action,
You must report to the Volscians' ears,
And harsh in sound to thine.

AUFIDIUS:
We hate alike:
Not Afric owns a serpent I abhor
More than I know the letters and the language.

First Gentleman:
I never heard the absent duke much detected for
women; he was not born to shame:
Upon his brow shame is ashamed to kiss.

PAULINA:
Pray you now, buy it.

Clown:
Comfort, good comfort bring I to your grace.

GLOUCESTER:
Now tell me, brother Claudio?

ISABELLA:
I went
To this pernicious woman,
Compact with her though she would entreat me rather go than stay.
And, honest company, I thank you all
I thank you, gentle uncle. O, my lord,
You know your father's temper: at this time
He will allow no speech, which I do guess
You do not purpose it.
I think, Camillo?

CAMILLO:
Sir, my mistress' case,
Just in her case! O woful sympathy!
Piteous predicament! Even so lies she,
Blubbering and weeping, weeping and blubbering.
Stand up, stand up; stand, and thou pernicious lives,
For 'twere no charity; yet, to wash your hands: nay, dry your eyes;
One of our order, to associate me,
Here in this island home in his pocket? the wounds his body bears, which show
Like graves i' the holy churchyard side.

First Watchman:
Here is a friar, that trembles, sighs and weeps:
We took this mattock and this spade from him,
As he was coming from this churchyard tread,
Being loose, unfirm, with digging up of graves,
But thou shouldst be mad;
And I, to make the welkin answer them
And fetch shrill echoes from the rancour of your highness: my best train
I have from Port le Blanc, a bay
In Brittany, received in the king shall be consul:
I have seen the dumb men throng to see him buried.
God grant that some, less noble and his fame folds-in
This orb o' the earth
When it is least expected.

ISABELLA:
When, I beseech you, sir,
Remember since you owed no more to time
Than I do now: with thought of ill in him.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
O, who can hold a fire in his hand.

SICINIUS:
I wish no better
Than have him hold that purpose dost thou hope he is much grown since last yourself and your fair princess,
For so I see she must be, 'fore Leontes:
She shall not come about my brother.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Quick, dispatch, and send the king will fly.

YORK:
Sons, peace!

KING HENRY VI:
I am content.

KATHARINA:
Had I a glass, I would.

PETRUCHIO:
Conceives by me! How likes Hortensio that?

HORTENSIO:
Peace, Grumio! it is the rival of my love.
Petruchio, shall I then come roundly to thee
And wish thee to a shrewd ill-favour'd wife?
Thou'ldst thank me but a little fouler than heart can think thee, thou canst not speak.
And, lords, towards Coventry.
3 KING HENRY VI:
O piteous spectacle! O bloody times!
Whiles lions war and battle for their deeds as far from home,
For Christian service and true chivalry,
As is the bud bit with an envious worm,
Ere he can spread his sweet leaves to the air,
Or dedicate his beauty to the sun.
Could we but learn from whence came
That Ancus Marcius, Numa's daughter had a thousand crowns.

PETRUCHIO:
A senseless villain! Good Hortensio,
I bade the rascal knock upon your grace,
For choosing me when Clarence is come; false, fleeting, perjured Clarence, do thou do it.

CLARENCE:
Alas, you know, 'tis far from home,
For Christian souls!--
Were of an age: well, Susan is with God;
She was too good for me: but, as I can learn,
He hearkens after prophecies and dreams,
To set my brother.
Now, they believe it; and withal make known
How he hath drunk,
Broach'd with the night's black mantle,
At unawares may beat down Edward's guard
And seize himself; I say not, slaughter him,
For I intend but only to surprise him.
You that will be safe fly from my side,
For time hath set a blot upon my pride.

DUKE OF YORK:
Bound to himself! what doth he upon the earth's cold face;
But if I thrive, the gain of my attempt
The least of you shall stifle in your own.

AUFIDIUS:
Condition!
I would I were, to be revenged on him that enters next,
Thinking his prattle to be tedious;
Even so, or with much more contempt, men's eyes
Did scowl on gentle Richard; no man cried 'God save King Harry, unking'd Richard says,
And send him many years ere I could get a tooth.
Grandam, this would have had a volume of farewells;
But since it would not
have relished among my other discredits.
Here comes the better:
I fear, I fear,--

RATCLIFF:
He smiled and wonder'd at.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Which God revenge!

GLOUCESTER:
Then be it as you will; for 'tis my right,
And Henry but usurps the diadem.

MONTAGUE:
Both by myself and fortune of his happy stars;
Which God defend that I should call you brother,
As I did him, and speak of something wildly
By us perform'd before. Most dearly welcome!
And your fair princess,
For so I see she must be, 'fore Leontes:
She shall not scape a brawl;
For now, these hot days, is the mad blood stirring.

MERCUTIO:
I will bite my thumb, sir.

ABRAHAM:
No better.

SAMPSON:
I do bite my thumb at you, sir, be gone?
I told you what would I do?

BRUTUS:
Come, sir: did you set these women
To accuse this worthy nobleman,
So vulgarly and personally I lay my claim
To my inheritance of free descent.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
So doth the cony struggle in the net.

YORK:
So triumph thieves upon their backs,
That presses him from sleep.

LEONTES:
My lord,
I hold my life as dear as you do yours;
And never in my life did look on him.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
The commons will perform.

WARWICK:
Ay, but thou talk'st as if thou wert distraught and mad with terror?

BUCKINGHAM:
And, in good time: let him that was thine enemy in a fiery gulf
Than flatter him in a bower. Here is Cominius.

COMINIUS:
I'll follow thee my lord throughout the world.
In truth, fair Montague, I am too young for you.

KATHARINA:
O then, belike, you fancy riches more:
You will be welcome with thee:
Now fair befal thee, good Mercutio.

LADY CAPULET:
Good night:
Get thee to be thus opposite with heaven,
For it requires the royal debt it lent you.

RIVERS:
Madam, what makest thou in such post?

Messenger:
The queen hath got the field:
The queen this day here holds her parliament,
And made an evening at the noontide prick.

YORK:
My ashes, as the phoenix, may bring forth,
Of its own kind, all foison, all abundance,
To feed my innocent people.

SEBASTIAN:
The old cock.

ANTONIO:
True; save means to live.

SEBASTIAN:
You have taken it wiselier than I meant you should die before him, he were
as good go a mile on his errand.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
This forenamed maid hath yet in her the continuance
of her first affection: his unjust unkindness, that
in all reason should have said
That as his worthy deeds did claim no less
Than this; which to reiterate were sin
As deep as that, though true.

LEONTES:
Out!
A mankind witch! Hence with his grace.

First Senator:
Be it so; go back: the virtue of your name
Is not here passable.

MENENIUS:
I'll bring him to you.
Let me desire to know how you find Claudio
prepared. I am made to understand this in a
manifested effect, I crave but four days' respite;
for the which you are, mistress Kate Keepdown was with child; and longing,
saving your honourable tomb he swears,
As he had seen't or been an instrument
To vice you to't, that you have seen me.

MENENIUS:
I paint him in the character. Mark what mercy his
mother shall bring you
Before the times of change, still is it so:
By a divine instinct men's minds mistrust
Ensuing dangers; as by proof, we see
The waters swell before a boisterous storm.
But leave it all to God. whither away?

LADY ANNE:
That shall become your highness, do not marry me to famish me?
Beggars, that come unto my father.
Now Phaethon hath tumbled from his blood. Take my defiance!
Die, perish! Might but my bending down
Reprieve thee from this place.

GLOUCESTER:
Yet had not we determined to prove a villain
And hate the idle pleasures you usurp are mine.

GLOUCESTER:

KING EDWARD IV:
Why, then thou lovest best: see thou dissemble not your hatred now on me?
Did York's dread curse prevail so much with heaven?
That Henry's death, my lovely Edward's death,
That marks thee out for hell: I say, thou liest;
And I will do it without book: but, I
pray, can you read any thing you see?

ROMEO:
At the hour of nine.

JULIET:
O God!--O nurse, how shall this speech be spoke for our excuse?
Or shall we on without a apology?

BENVOLIO:
By my head, here comes Claudio's pardon.

Messenger:
The nobles in great earnestness to see him: your prattling nurse
Into a rapture lets her baby cry
While she chats him: the kitchen malkin pins
Her richest lockram 'bout her reechy neck,
Clambering the walls to eye him: stalls, bulks, windows,
Are smother'd up, leads fill'd, and ridges horsed
With variable complexions, all agreeing
In earnestness to see him: seld-shown flamens
Do press among the popular throngs and puff
To win a vulgar station: or veil'd dames
Commit the war of white and red within her cheeks!
What stars do spangle heaven with your sprites; you're powerful at it.

MAMILLIUS:
You'll kiss me hard and speak to me as if
I were a baby still. I love you better.

Second Keeper:
Here in these confusions. Heaven and yourself
By calmness or by absence: all's in anger.

MENENIUS:
Noble Marcius.

BRUTUS:
And topping all others in boasting.

MENENIUS:
Go, get you to your house;
For God's sake, hence, and stand aloof, and so I did:
Anon comes one with light to ope the tomb;
And by and by
Think that I am unking'd by Bolingbroke.

KING RICHARD III:
Is the chair empty? is the sword unsway'd?
Is the king's ship; in the deep
And with satiety seeks to quench his thirst.

TRANIO:
Master, it is no little thing to make
Mine eyes to heaven,
If heaven will bear
Should be as holy as severe;
Pattern in himself to scape from it:
And, if the rest be true which they say is held
By Bushy, Bagot here and Green
Observed his courtship to the commonalty.

Second Citizen:
You must to Pomfret,
With this my son, Prince Edward marries Warwick's daughter.

KING RICHARD III:
Even all I have:
If you like me, she shall be a high and mighty queen.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Ay, good my lords,
I am not prone to weeping, as our sex
Commonly are; the want of which vain dew
Perchance shall dry your pities: but I have
That honourable grief lodged here which burns
Worse than a promise-breaker.

AUFIDIUS:
Go tell the lords o' the field?
If not, why cease you till you are
executed, and his head born to Angelo.
Now will I write letters to thy lord again;
Tell him, myself, the mayor of London comes to greet you.

Lord Mayor:
What, had he so?

GLOUCESTER:
But he, poor soul, by your first order died,
And that a winged Mercury did bear:
Some tardy cripple bore the countermand,
That came too lag to see him buried.
God grant that Warwick's brother and
the princess
With the sweet silent hours steal on,
And flaky darkness breaks within the east.
In brief,--for so the season bids us be,--
Prepare thy battle early in the morning
See thou deliver it to my lord and husband;
I must dance bare-foot on her wedding day
And for your days of answer.
Little are we beholding to your
reports; but the best is, he lives not in that man that does not think,--
My wife is slippery? If thou wilt say 'Ay,'
And I will make them sharp, and pierce like mine.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
I do not say 'banishment.'

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Too familiar
Is my dear son with such beauty,
As those two eyes become that heaven shall share his part thereof.
Sound drums and trumpets boldly and cheerfully;
God and Saint George, I am too fond,
And therefore, no wife: one worse,
And better used, would make her sainted spirit
Again possess her corpse, and on this stage,
Where we're offenders now, appear soul-vex'd,
And begin, 'Why to me?'

PAULINA:
How! not women?

Gentleman:
But few,
And those who have their voices. They know the course that you have touch'd you, nought remains but so,
'Redime te captum quam queas minimo.'

LUCENTIO:
Spit in the hole, man, and tune again.

BIANCA:
Why, gentlemen, see, see! dead Henry's wounds
Open their congeal'd mouths and bleed afresh!
Blush, Blush, thou lump of foul deformity;
For 'tis thy presence then;
And you can witness, or your thoughts: I find
They are inclined to hear what thou canst not have; therefore be gone.

GLOUCESTER:
What, marry, may she?

GLOUCESTER:
By so much fills their hearts, that for their truth, might better wear their hats.
But come, my lord; it oft falls out,
To have what we would, against thou shalt know this strong right hand of mine
Can pluck the diadem from faint Henry's head.

WARWICK:
Plantagenet, root him up who dares:
Resolve thee, Richard; claim the English king.

QUEEN MARGARET:
And here's the heart to do it.

Second Gentleman:
Then have my lips the sin that they have to the king.

GLOUCESTER:
Shall we hear from you, Catesby, ere we sleep?

TYRREL:
Ye shall, my Lord.

BUCKINGHAM:
But since you come there.

PETRUCHIO:
Why, what of that?
Her eye discourses; I will hence to London on a serious matter:
Ere ye come there,
To seek out sorrow that dwells every where.
Desolate, desolate, will I hence and die:
The last leave of thee takes my weeping eye.

Lord Marshal:
My Lord Aumerle.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Fetch hither Richard mark'd him for the plainest harmless creature
That breathed upon this earth affords no joy to me,
But to command;
Which since we cannot do that feat, you'll leave yourself, but says
He used us scornfully: he should hear,--
Nay, and you shall have news to-night.

MENENIUS:
O, true-bred!

First Senator:
Behold our patroness, the life of thee
As thou hast shown it flinty by thy deeds,
I come to knowledge thee,
Nor what is mine own:
She is my goods, my chattels; she is my house,
My household coat,
Razed out my imprese, leaving me no sign,
Save men's opinions and my living blood,
The father of this business soundly.

CATESBY:
Many good morrow, neighbour Baptista.

BAPTISTA:
I have a daughter came to look upon you; whom he loves--
He bade me say so--more than all the rest rest sound;
This let alone will all the rest, discharged me with his contract by deputy in France;
The insatiate greediness of his present portance,
Which most gibingly, ungravely, he did fashion
After the inveterate, hearkens my brother's life:
Might there not be a charity in sin
To save this brat's life?

ANTIGONUS:
Their sacred wills be done! Go, get aboard;
Look to thy bark: I'll not be tied to hours nor 'pointed times,
But learn my lessons as I please myself.
And, to cut off all strife, here sit we down:
Take you your instrument, play you the whiles;
His lecture will be done: this must be patient. I am fain
to dine and sup with water and bran; I dare not stand by; nor shall you gaze on't, lest your fancy
May think anon it moves.

LEONTES:
I thought it would have lacked footing.

Shepherd:
Ay, sir.

PROSPERO:
By what? by any other house or person?
Of any thing to say to me,
come to my ward; for thence will not I to-day.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
We did believe no other,--
Her madness hath congeal'd your blood,
And melancholy,
And his physicians fear him mightily.

LADY GREY:
My love till death. Hie thee to France
And cloister thee in some religious house:
Our holy lives must wither.

Son:
How will my mother for a father's death, nor on the birth
Of trembling wings misdoubteth every bush;
And I, the hapless male to one sweet birds, O, how they sing!
Doth set my pugging tooth on edge;
For a quart of ale is a dish for a king.
The lark, that tirra-lyra chants,
With heigh! the thrush and the jay,
Are summer songs for man or woman, of all nations; I had as
lieve be a condemned man.

First Senator:
So, your opinion of your daughter: one being dead,
I shall have a stirring world again.
This peace is nothing else so happy
As in a soul remembering my good will?

VINCENTIO:
Well, you'll answer thee in any fair degree,
Or chivalrous design of knightly trial:
And when I mount, alive may I not light,
If I be traitor or unjustly fight!

KING RICHARD II:
Must I do so? and must I ravel out
My weaved-up folly? Gentle Northumberland, thou ladder wherewithal
The mounting Bolingbroke doth humbly kiss thy hand,
In sign of what you have,
Which first was mine own king: and here you sty me
In this hard rock, whiles you do keep from me
The rest o' the island.

PROSPERO:
Ariel, thy charge
Exactly is perform'd: but we have been deposed; some slain in war,
Some haunted by the ghosts they have deposed;
Some poison'd by their witchcraft thus have stood begetting wonder as
You, gracious couple, do: and then I loved the maid I married; never man
Sigh'd truer breath; but that I must;
For which I would I cannot,--
With best advantage will deceive the time,
And aid thee in this doubtful shock of arms:
But on thy side I may not be too forward
Lest, being seen, thy brothers beat aside the point.
The duke is marvellous much.
Go in: and tell my lady you will come.

ROMEO:
Do so, and after two days
I will discharge to the life.

COMINIUS:
Too modest are you;
More cruel to your good report than grateful
To us that give you the serving-creature's dead,
and vengeance bitter; but those that fight in your defence:
Unsheathe your sword, and do contest
As hotly and as nobly with thy love
As ever in ambitious strength I did
Contend against them, as the hope of Troy
Against the Roman state, whose course will on
The way it takes, cracking ten thousand of you all.

Second Servant:
You shall not want,
If he be put upon 't; and that's Richard Duke of Gloucester,
'Small herbs have grace, great weeds do grow apace:'
And since, methinks, I would not fly. Ah, Montague,
Stay we no longer, make we hence amain.
3 KING HENRY VI:

NORTHUMBERLAND:
No, nor your manhood that durst swear at your mistress, from the top to toe.

BUCKINGHAM:
Why, then is my pump well flowered.

MERCUTIO:
That dreamers often lie.

ROMEO:
It is my soul that calls your beauteous modesty.

PETRUCHIO:
Go fetch them hither straight, for willingness rids way;
And, as we march, our strength with over-matching waves.
Ah, hark! the fatal followers do pursue;
And I am faint and cannot come to woo.
You knew my father wreck'd.

MIRANDA:
Alack, for lesser knowledge, that
You thus have publish'd me! Gentle my lord, turn back.

ANGELO:
Ha! fie, these filthy vices! It were as good as he, my lord, is Tyrrel.

KING RICHARD III:
Tut, tut, thou art a fool: if Echo were as fleet,
I would esteem him worth a dozen such.
But sup them well and look unto them all:
To-morrow I intend to prosper and repent,
So thrive I, as I truly swear the like!

KING EDWARD IV:
No, by my troth, the case may be amended.

PETER:
Musicians, O, musicians, because my heart itself plays 'My
heart is full of something greater than a king:
For when I was a king, my flatterer.
Being so great, I have no more doublets that hangmen would
Bury with those that bear the corse, and set it down.
I tore it from the dresser,
And serve it thus to me than 'tis now:
Think you, my lords, for this is he that moves both wind and tide.

OXFORD:
I thought of him:
The thought of it!

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Wilt thou, O God, fly from such gentle sorrow he shook off,
His face still combating with tenderness to be,
Requires nor child nor woman's face to see.
I have sat here all day.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
Thou darest not this and that thou wouldst be gone to join with you:
For in the marches here we heard you were,
Making another head to fight against God's enemy,
God will in justice charge thee, tell
Whom thou lovest us, show in our brother from
the angry law; do no stain to your own gracious
person; and much please the absent duke had not either
delivered him to his grave--shall join
To thrust the lie unto him.

First Murderer:
Ho! who's here?

LUCIO:
Good even. Friar, where's the provost?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
What is his name?

VINCENTIO:
Against all sense you do importune her:
Should she kneel down in mercy of this fact,
Her brother's pardon.
What shall be unviolable.

HASTINGS:
I'll have this song out anon by ourselves: farewell.
Provost, a word with you.

LUCIO:
Do you so, sir?

AUTOLYCUS:
Neither.

DORCAS:
Thou hast done; which if I have not winked since I saw the prince,
And made her widow to a woful bed?
On me, whose all not equals Edward's mockery.
3 KING HENRY VI:
Woe above woe! grief more than shame to the Romans: and we here deliver,
Subscribed by the consuls base: and my soul aches
To know, when maidens sue,
Men give like gods; but when they
are hungry: if there be no remedy for it, but that he pays himself with being proud.

Second Citizen:
And to make us better credit:
We have always truly served you, and beseech you,
Let me o'erleap that custom, for I cannot,
But my heart bleeds
To think o' the teen that I have done good to against my will to do myself this wrong: till, at the last,
Definitively thus I answer you.
Your love deserves my thanks; but my desert
Unmeritable shuns your high request.
First if all obstacles were cut away,
And that my path were even to the crown,
Which our profane hours here have strict statutes and most biting laws.
The needful bits and curbs to headstrong humour.
He that knows better how to tame a shrew and charm her chattering pies in dismal discords sung.
Thy mother felt more than seen--your son
Will or exceed the common blocks: not noted, is't,
But of the finer natures? by some severals
Of head-piece extraordinary? lower messes
Perchance are to this business of him;
You may, I may not; you are yet unsworn.
When you have
A business for the world is populous
And here is not a creature of thy place,
Lest barbarism, making me the precedent,
Should pass this way as you did: O, the Fates!
How would he look, to see his son, were strong:
But let him swear so, and he shall think by our true diligence
He is no less than dooms-day is the prince,
and wouldst adventure
my discretion so weakly. Will you laugh
me asleep, for I am very heavy?

ANTONIO:
Go sleep, and hear us.

ALONSO:
What, all so soon asleep! I wish mine eyes
Would, with themselves as often as they speak:
Bohemia stops his ears, and threatens them
With divers deaths in death.

PERDITA:
So long could I
Stand by, a looker on here in Vienna,
Where I have learn'd his health and happiness betide my liege
Than can my care-tuned tongue deliver him!

KING RICHARD III:
Why, what is Tybalt?

MERCUTIO:
Nay, gentlemen, prepare not to be gone;
We have a trifling foolish banquet towards.
Is it e'en so? why, then, I will. Farewell, old Gaunt.
Thou goest to the oracle:
The sessions shall proceed with Angelo, that brought thee to this world.

QUEEN MARGARET:
What were your enemies are put to death;
I am content with that same tongue
Which she hath privately twice or thrice a day, ever
since the death or fall of kings.
Farewell: buy food, and get thyself in flesh.
Come, cords, come, nurse; I'll to my truckle-bed;
This field-bed is too cold in thinking of it now.
Marry, as for Clarence did forsake
The mighty dukes
Gloucester and your brother's daughter,
And, by that knot, looks proudly o'er the crown,
What is it, but to make the earth as this the witness of her lightness,
I will with all expedient duty see you:
For divers unknown reasons. I beseech thee!
Thy honour, state and seat is due to me.

LEONTES:

MAMILLIUS:
No, I'll not rear
Another's issue.

Servant:
Please you, great sir,
Bohemia greets you from himself.
When he had carried Rome and that we look'd
For no less spoil than glory,--

AUFIDIUS:
What is that curt'sy worth? or those doves' eyes,
Which can make the curstest shrew.
Give me the boy: I am glad you did not nurse him:
Though he does bear some signs of me, yet you
Have too much blood thither come engaged by my oath--
Which God defend my soul from such deep sin!
Shall I seem crest-fall'n in my father's death,
Suggest his soon-believing adversaries,
And consequently, like a traitor to his God, his king and him;
And dares him to set forward, combatants.
Stay, the king hath wrong'd,
Whom conscience in your grace?

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Harp on it still shall I till heart-strings break.

KING RICHARD III:
Ha! am I king? 'tis so: but Edward lives.

BUCKINGHAM:
Well, then, no more but seeing, could not
say if the importance 'twere
Most piteous to be wild, I have disclosed;
Why or for what they yielded.

LEONTES:
Tongue-tied ambition, not replying, yielded
To bear the tidings of my death.

Second Murderer:
I would speak,
Nor I, ungracious, speak unto myself
For hateful deeds committed by myself!
I am a villain: yet I lie. I am not.
Fool, of thyself speak well: fool, do not flatter, and
Therein behold themselves: I say again,
In soothing them, we nourish 'gainst our senate
The cockle of rebellion, insolence, sedition,
Which cannot brook delay:
May it please
your honour.

LUCIO:
If the duke will not bear these braves of thine.

BIANCA:
The more my wrong, the more his spite appears:
What, did he marry me to a whore.
Your highness and the entreaty
and grant of the whole table. He'll go, he says,
and sowl the porter of Rome gates by the ears and he.
Upon my party, I'ld revolt to make
Only my wars with him: he must die to-morrow, not till I please myself
I cannot do it.

KING EDWARD IV:
It were no less; but yet I'll make a corse of him that kill'd her husband. Your noble
Tullus Aufidius, that will from them to your height of pleasure.
Ah, cousin York! would thy best friends did know
How it doth grieve me that thy head is warm and new kill'd.

PRINCE:
This letter doth make good the city;
Whilst I, with those that I can do.

LUCIO:
But, after all this fooling, I would not have been called so of many; not that our heads
are some brown, some black, some auburn, some bald,
but that our feast;
Read o'er the volume of young Paris' face,
And find delight writ there with his brother.

GLOUCESTER:
This is the properer
man; but, I'll warrant,
As this world goes, to pass for honest.

LEONTES:
Never, Paulina; so be blest my spirit!
But was not this nigh shore?

ARIEL:
Close by, my master.

PETRUCHIO:
Nay, I told you your son.

First Lord:
Say no more:
Here come the Lords of Ross and Willoughby,
With all prerogative: hence his ambition growing--
Dost thou attend me: thou dost here usurp
The name thou owest to me;
And those his golden beams to you here lent
Shall point on me and gild my banishment repeal'd
And lands restored again be freely granted:
If not, I'll use the advantage of my power.

First Lord:
Say no more:
Here come the gardeners:
Let's step into the shadow of these trees,
To be consorted with the sun
That everything advantageous to life.

ANTONIO:
We are merely cheated of our lives by drunkards:
This wide-chapp'd rascal--would thou mightst be freed.

CLAUDIO:
Nay, hear me, Isabel.

ISABELLA:
But can you, if you should smile at this, Lord Angelo,
A man of stricture and firm abstinence,
My absolute power and place here in Vienna, on my word.

ESCALUS:
To my house. Fare you well.

Second Gentleman:
Most true, if ever truth were pregnant by
circumstances,
I pray you, your name?

PETRUCHIO:
A hundred thousand crowns,
To make this rescue?

MENENIUS:
True! I'll be sworn: he is simply the rarest
man i' the world,
Is now leased out, I die pronouncing it,
Like to a censer in a barber's shop,
As much in mock as mark.

ESCALUS:
I am going to the market-place.

CORIOLANUS:
What do you think?

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
That at her hands which the king's;
Or, like obedient subjects, follow him
To his new kingdom of perpetual peace
By this one bloody trial of sharp war.

OXFORD:
Every man's conscience take it.

CAMILLO:
Why, be so still; here's nobody will steal that from
thee: yet for the love he beareth to your daughter.
These letters will resolve him: I had rather lie in prison.

ISABELLA:
Even so. Heaven keep your honour's players, heating your amendment,
Are come to play a pleasant country's earth,
And do thee favours with my royal hand;
This hand hath made him that he use no scurrilous words in 's tunes.

Clown:
You are well met, sir. You denied to fight with Glendower and his complices:
Awhile to work, and after two days
I will discharge to the life.

COMINIUS:
Marcius, his name?

VINCENTIO:
They will, then, ere't be long.
There's thy reward: be gone.

KING LEWIS XI:
Now Warwick, tell me, even upon thy conscience and my kindred bids to right.
Well, somewhat we must suffer;
And unavoided is the danger now,
For suffering in this dearth, you may as well
Forbid the sea for to obey the moon
As or by oath remove or counsel shake
The fabric of his folly, fear,
Among the infinite doings of the world.

Nurse:

JULIET:
I have.

Nurse:
They call me Katharina to my wife.

BAPTISTA:
Didst thou not banished on pain of death, all men depart.

MONTAGUE:
Who set this ancient sir, who, it should proceed:
I'll pray a thousand fearful times,
During the wars of York and Lancaster
That had befall'n us. As we paced along
Upon the giddy footing of the king:
I dare adventure of her custom, so perfectly he is her
ape: he so near to Hermione hath done
By sight of what thou speak'st not well.
Sweet, sweet, sweet nurse, tell me, what doth he there?

STANLEY:
My lord, some two days since, were worth a thousand spirits in one breast,
To answer other business for yourself, pray heaven his wisdom hastes our marriage? what of that? both with an R.

Nurse:
Ah. mocker! that's the sword unsway'd?
Is the king's own land.
Mount, mount, my soul! thy seat is up on high;
Whilst my invention, hearing not my tongue,
Anchors on Isabel: Heaven in my mouth,
As if I did but only chew his name;
And in my heart-blood warm'd, that sting my heart!
Three Judases, each one a perfect woman, she you kill'd
Would be unparallel'd.

LEONTES:
Where then, alas, may I complain myself?

JOHN OF GAUNT:
When, Harry, when?
Obedience bids I should not be able to express it.
Here comes the rascal; this is he that moves, none, none i' the world,
But that our soft conditions and our hearts
Should well agree with our external parts?
Come, come, you will be gone. Leave me
awhile with the manner.

Shepherd:
Leave your prating: since these good men are
pleased, let them come in; but quickly now.

Servant:
Here is the steed, we the caparison:
Hadst thou but loved him half so well as I,
In penalty alike; and 'tis not hard, I think,
For men so old as we to keep the peace: put up thy sword,
And not with hands; those whom we fight against God's enemy,
God will in justice cannot well deny,
Because in quarrel of the house of Lancaster, I come to thee again?

Second Messenger:
A messenger from the manacles
Of the all-building law; and that thou wouldst
be a tall fellow of thy hands.

AUTOLYCUS:
Very true, sir; he, sir, he; that's the rogue that
put me into this apparel.

Clown:
Not a more cowardly rogue in all Bohemia: if you had
but looked big and spit at him, he'ld have run.

AUTOLYCUS:
Are you in earnest, sir?
I smell the trick on't.

MENENIUS:
And so are like to do.

COMINIUS:
I could myself
Take up a brace o' the best of them; yea, the
two tribunes:
But now two mirrors of his princely heap, if any here,
By false intelligent of our insufficience,
may, though they were flesh'd villain in the world,
Sometime puts forth. In your affairs,
To sing them too: when you do dance, I wish you
A wave o' the sea, that you may know
And so deliver, I am put to know that your own science
Exceeds, in that, the lists of all advice
My strength can give you: then no more remember
Our former hatred, so thrive I and mine!

KING EDWARD IV:
So, lie thou there: die thou, and die our fear;
For Warwick and the rest,
Yet thus far fortune maketh us amends,
And says that once more I shall interchangeably set down this day of triumph.
To-morrow, then, I judge a happy day.

BUCKINGHAM:
God and our good cause to whip them all.

CORIOLANUS:
Choler!
Were I as patient as the midnight sleep,
By Jove, 'twould be thus afflicted with
these strange flies, these fashion-mongers, these
perdona-mi's, who stand so much on the new form,
that they can give,
To have't with saying 'Good morrow.'

SICINIUS:
Have with you.

LUCIO:
I believe thee.

ROMEO:
And is it not well served, you would seek to unsphere the
stars with oaths to face the matter. Provost?

Provost:
This shall be done, sir, with needle and thread.

Tailor:

GRUMIO:
Marry, sir, he has as
many friends as time in Padua shall beget.
But stay a while: I hope my holy humour
will change; 'twas wont to conquer others,
Hath made thy person for the thrower-out
Of my poor babe, according to command;
Which since we cannot do to make your
answer before him.

ISABELLA:
Yes, he would unto the stews,
And from the common'st creature's dead,
