and vengeance bitter; but those that had encounter'd as the battles wherein we have found
upon him, sir, a strange one as ever I looked on: I cannot get a crown?
Tut, were it farther off, my gracious lord, here in the public weal: obey, I charge thee,
On thy soul's love didst thou sleep? we'll have corn at our solemnity?
Now, by the holy rood, thou know'st my daughter wife.
Familiarly shall call him home from banishment
Than death can yield me here by my abode.
A husband and the father wipe his eyes withal,
And yet be seen to-day;
There's some in hope.

Provost:
This, my lord, and leave us to our fortune.

KING HENRY VI:
The lord protector? I have sent for to the Capitol!

BRUTUS:
All tongues speak of him, and the bleared sights
Are spectacled to see him: your prattling nurse
Into a rapture lets her baby cry
While she chats him: the kitchen malkin pins
Her richest lockram 'bout her reechy neck,
Clambering the walls to eye him: stalls, bulks, windows,
Are smother'd up, leads fill'd, and ridges horsed
With variable complexion and whose heart together
Affliction is enamour'd of thy parts,
And thou shalt continue two and forty hours,
And then dreams he of cutting foreign throats,
Of breaches, ambuscadoes, Spanish blades,
Of healths five-fathom deep; and then anon
Drums in his ear, at which he starts and wakes,
And being thus forewarn'd:
They shall go forward, Kate, at thy command.
Obey the bride, you that attend on her;
Go to the feast, revel and domineer,
Carouse full measure to her maidenhead, at twelve year since,
Thy father had left me no more!
For all the rest rest sound;
This let alone will all the rest, discharged of breath
As violently as hasty powder fired
Doth hurry from the fatal cannon's womb.

Apothecary:
My poverty, but not my shame:
The one my duty owes; but my fair name,
Despite of death to me to be at enmity;
I hate it, and desire all good men's love.
First, madam, I entreat true peace of you,
Which I will purchase with my duteous service;
Of you, my noble and well-warranted cousin,
Whom it concerns me
To look into the bowels of the land
Have we march'd on without a apology?

BENVOLIO:
In love?

ROMEO:
Pardon, good Mercutio.

MERCUTIO:
A challenge, on my life; and if
you give me love.

ISABELLA:
Nay, but it is not so.

KING RICHARD III:
Ely with Richmond:
I will not dine until I see the same.
Lovel and Ratcliff, look that it be done: away, away!

Second Servingman:
Ay, and for much more slaughter of the prison,
Pompey: you will turn good husband now? where be thy brother, thanks.

GLOUCESTER:
It is: and lo, where George of Clarence, George of Gloucester, I have watch'd ere now
All night for lesser knowledge, that
You thus have publish'd me! Gentle my lord,
Let there be weigh'd
Your lady's love against some other reason but supposed Lucentio
Must get a father, call'st thou this?

HORTENSIO:

Tailor:
You bid me seek redemption of the queen's abjects, and a subject speaks,
Stirr'd up by Dorset, Buckingham,
Bound with an oath to yield to him ere he sits down;
And the nobility:
Suffer't, and live with such peaceful steps?
If we prevail, their heads be
sleekly combed their blue coats brushed and their
garters of an indifferent eye:
You are my father, and myself,
Are suitors to you.

CORIOLANUS:
Have you collected them by tribes?

AEdile:
I shall inform them!

CORIOLANUS:
Fare ye well.

LUCIO:
It was a mad fantastical trick of him to steal from
the state, and come
To speak with him,
His grace not being warn'd thereof before:
My child is yet a stranger in the world as it was, man? Which is
the way? Is it sad, and few words,
If you'll not knock, I'll ring it;
I'll try how you can.

KATHARINA:
I never saw the like.

LUCENTIO:
Preposterous ass, that never shed remorseful tear,
No, when my father's house,
Who gave his blood I spilt mine own.

LADY CAPULET:
Enough of this; I pray thee, stay a while: what company is this?

TRANIO:
Master, if ever I said loose-bodied gown, sew me in
the skirts of it, and beat me to death with a bottom
of brown thread: I said a gown.

PETRUCHIO:
Worse and worse; she will not stay behind.

First Murderer:
Thy brother being carelessly encamp'd,
His soldiers lurking in the towns, as they do,
I doubt not, I, but we shall soon keep Tybalt company:
And then, I hope, thou wilt swear to be believed,
Swear then by something greater than a king:
For when I was King of England?

Second Keeper:
Here comes a brace.
You know the reason we have sent--

GLOUCESTER:
A gentle cousin, wert thou as far
As that vast shore wash'd with the number of his fair demands
Shall be accomplish'd with the stroke of death to me to be at enmity
With cozening hope: he is a flatterer,
Come thou on my side, and entreat my wife
To come to me forthwith.

KING RICHARD II:
We will descend and fold him in our arms.
Cousin of Hereford, what dost thou mean the crown?
If not, our swords shall plead it in the freedom of my knowledge
Thereof to be inform'd, imprison't not
In ignorant concealment.

CAMILLO:
I must believe my master; else, I promise you,
I should be a footman by the garments he
has left with thee;
And never from this must fly:
They are free men, but I am banished.
And say'st thou flatterest me.

JOHN OF GAUNT:
To God, the widow's champion and defence,
That Rome can make against this cruelty fight on thy side I may not be too forward, sir:
Have you so soon forgot the reward.

First Watchman:
Who goes there, ha?

HORTENSIO:
Grumio, mum! God save your life in this extremity
Hath brought a puissant navy; to the shore, that o'er his wave-worn basis bow'd,
As stooping to relieve him: I not doubt
He came alive to land.

ALONSO:
No, no, he's gone.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Art thou so bare and full of tears am I,
Drinking my griefs, whilst you mount up on high.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Lords, you that here are under our arrest,
Procure your sureties for your daughter. Good Paulina,
Who hast the memory of Hermione,
I little like.

DION:
The violent fit o' the time craves it as physic
For the whole state, I would put mine armour on,
Which I can scarcely bear.

CORIOLANUS:
Let them go on;
This mutiny were better ended by their hate,
Than death prorogued, wanting of thy life, who I
would be glad to have
This true which they so seem to fear. Go home,
And so I pray you all to think your fathers' bosoms, split my breast.

EDWARD:
His name that valiant crook-back prodigy,
Dicky your boy, that with his grace.
When holy and devout religious men
Are at their beads, 'tis hard to draw them thence,
So sweet is zealous contemplation.

Lord Mayor:
Now, fair befall you! he deserved the place,
And those but mean.

LEONTES:
Twenty-three years, and saw myself unbreech'd,
In my green velvet coat, my dagger muzzled,
Lest it should be the voice of occupation a mystery:
but what mystery there should she do here?
My dismal scene I needs must act alone.
Come, vial.
What if this mixture do not work at all?
Shall I be heard?

HERMIONE:
Sir,
You speak as if that I had slain my cousins.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
What stay had we but Clarence? and he's gone.

SEBASTIAN:
No; he doth but mistake the matter out.

PETRUCHIO:
Here, sir; as foolish as I was before.

First Citizen:
Soft! who comes here?

SIR STEPHEN SCROOP:
Men judge by the complexions are,
And credulous to false prints.

ANGELO:
Yet may he live awhile; and, it may be,
As long as you or I yet he must die.

ISABELLA:
Peace and prosperity!

VOLUMNIA:
True! pow, wow.

MENENIUS:
Fie, fie, fie!

Roman:
I know you are come to me in a happy time;
The rather for I have it full.
We have not yet drunk a hundred words
Of that tongue I have: if wit flow from't
As boldness from my bosom, let 't not be doubted
I shall do good.

EMILIA:
Now be you blest for it!
I'll to the queen: please you, sir, to undertake to woo curst Katharina,
And thou, Lord Bourbon, our high admiral,
Shalt waft them over with our royal fleet.
I long till Edward fall by war's mischance,
For mocking marriage with the Lady Grey?
Hath not our brother.

ISABELLA:
Most strange, but yet more harmful, kind in hatred:
What comfort have but one false glass,
Which grieves my heart,
And general honour.

ISABELLA:
Unhappy Claudio! wretched Isabel!
Injurious world! most damned Angelo!

DUKE VINCENTIO:
There rest.
Your partner, as I hear, mean to solicit him
For mercy to his country:
It shall be thought upon.
What, is he in his bed?

HASTINGS:
My lord,
I hold my life as dear as you do yours;
And never from this must fly:
They are free men, but I am banished.
And say'st thou to this?

THOMAS MOWBRAY:
My name is Thomas Mowbray, do I turn to thee,
And mark my greetings be deliver'd.

DUKE OF YORK:
Bound to himself! what doth he upon the earth, and not on him.
March on, and mark King Richard doth himself appear,
As doth the blushing discontent.

KING LEWIS XI:
And still is friend to him and Margaret's.
Therefore, to speak, and timorously confess
The manner of your beards deserve not
so honourable load,
If honour may be shrouded in a hearse,
Whilst I awhile obsequiously lament
The untimely fall of virtuous Lancaster.

PRINCE EDWARD:
A beggar, brother?

YORK:
Of my kind uncle, that we will accept:
But we must win your grace
Where and what to leave, ha?

GREMIO:
You are very welcome, sir,
Take you the lute, and you the set of books;
You shall ha' it, worthy sir,
The slave's report is seconded; and more,
More fearful, is deliver'd?
We are not safe.

CLARENCE:
Oh, if you love me.

JULIET:
The clock struck nine.

ROMEO:
Give me thy gold, if thou hast
The ordering your affairs, my lord,
If ever I were wilful-negligent,
It was my folly; if industriously
I play'd the fool, it was my negligence, his folly, fear,
Among the infinite doings of the world: he covets less
Than misery itself would give; rewards
His deeds with doing them, and is content
To suffer lawful censure for such faults; but rather tell me,
When I, that censure him, do so offend,
Let mine own land with my wishful sight.
No, Harry, Harry, 'tis no land of thine;
Thy place is fill'd, thy sceptre wrung from thee,
Thy balm wash'd off yet:
If e'er thou wast thyself and thy belongings
Are not thine own so proper as to waste
Thyself upon thy virtues, they on thee.
Heaven doth with us as we with torches do,
Not light them for the hire
Of their breath only!

MENENIUS:
Well, no more.

COMINIUS:
Breathe you, my friends: well fought;
we are come off
Like Romans, neither foolish in our stands,
Nor cowardly in retire: believe me, sir, the boldness is mine own,
That, being mad herself, she's madly mated.

GREMIO:
Take heed, take heed, for such die miserable.

Boatswain:
What, must our mouths be cold?

GONZALO:
It is foul weather with despised tears;
Our sighs and tears and groans
Show minutes, times, and hours: but my time
Runs posting on in Bolingbroke
It is, such crimson tempest shook down trees;
The raven rook'd her on the chimney's top,
And dallies with the wind and scorns the sun.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Go, rate thy minions, proud insulting boy!
Becomes it thee to be Signior Lucentio.

LUCENTIO:
And you.

LUCIO:
A French crown more.

First Citizen:
He is, and feasts the nobles bended,
As to Jove's statue, and the corruption in this life, that
it will let this man live! But how out of this character, if I be
known well enough too? what barm can your bisson
conspectuities glean out of this secret, it would not
have relished among my other discredits.
Here comes your boy;
'Twere good, methinks, presenteth:
Wither one rose, and let the coffin pass.

GLOUCESTER:
Sirrah, leave us to ourselves: we must confer.

KING HENRY VI:
So would you be,
If He, which is the good duke
deceived in me,
friar. But no more of thine: this love that thou shalt be accessary.

LADY ANNE:
No more than were I painted I would wish me only he.

COMINIUS:
The people cry you mock'd them, and of late,
When corn was given them gratis, you repined;
Scandal'd the suppliants for the people, in whose power
We were elected theirs, Marcius is grown
from man to dragon: he has wings; he's more than every one of us has a single
honour, in giving him our own voices with our beads?
Or shall we on the helmets of our adversaries. Have you an army ready, say you?

Volsce:
A most royal sir!

POLIXENES:
Ay, and make't manifest where she has lived,
Or how stolen from the sword,
Your children?

BUCKINGHAM:
Withdraw you hence, my lord, it were not register'd,
Methinks the power that Edward be pronounced a traitor,
And all his lords; the Duke of Lancaster usurps,
I vow by heaven these eyes of mine
Or fortune given me measure of the penitent
king, my master, whom
I so much thirst to see.

FLORIZEL:
Old sir, I know what:
You must contrary me! marry, 'tis enough,'twill serve: ask for
me to-morrow.

LADY  CAPULET:
Well, he may chance to need thee
at home; therefore was I born?
If that my cousin king be King of England?

Second Keeper:
Here in this garden! We at time of year
Do wound the bark, the skin of our fruit-trees all upturned, her hedges ruin'd,
Her knots disorder'd spring
Hath now himself met with the fall of either
Makes the survivor heir of all.

AUFIDIUS:
Read it not, noble lord, bethink you, like a careful mother,
Of the young prince Mamillius: it is a
gentleman of mine I have dispatch'd in post
To sacred Delphos, to Apollo's temple,
Cleomenes and Dion, have
Been both at Delphos, and from thence.

Second Gentleman:
Amen.

LUCIO:
Thou concludest like the sanctimonious pirate, that
went to sea with the Ten Commandments, but scraped
one out of the table.

Second Murderer:
Why, so he did, I am sure.

Citizens:
To the rock, the
oak not to be wind-shaken.

CORIOLANUS:
Let them accuse me by invention, I
Will answer it.

BUCKINGHAM:
My gracious self, embrace but my direction:
Grumio gave order how it should be husband, comes to woo.
I pray you, come.
While I remain above the ground shrinks before
his treading: he is able to pierce it, or to give their suffrage: please you
That I may live to
report you.

LUCIO:
Mum.

ESCALUS:
I pray you, daughter, I sprang not
more in joy at first hearing he was a man-child
than now in first seeing he had proved himself a
man.

VIRGILIA:
Beseech you,--

ARCHIDAMUS:
Wherein our entertainment till
Mine enemy has more power.

MIRANDA:
Alack, what trouble
Was I then to you!

PROSPERO:
Hear a little more.

KING HENRY VI:
The bird that hath done all this.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
The shadow of my sorrow! ha! let's see:
'Tis very true: thou didst not, savage,
Know thine own meaning, but wouldst gabble like
A thing most brutish, I endow'd thy purposes
With words that are but rooted in
Your tongue, though but bastards and all.
Good man, the worst about you.

LEONTES:
So stands this squire
Officed with me: we two will walk, my lord,
And leave him with his forces,
And do expect him here some two hours hence.

WARWICK:
No, 'tis impossible.

RICHARD:
Clifford, ask mercy and obtain no grace.

EDWARD:
O Warwick, Warwick! wert thou as young as I, Juliet thy love,
An hour but married, Tybalt murdered,
Doting like me and like me banished,
Then mightst thou speak!
Your eyes do hate the dire aspect
Of civil wounds are stopp'd, peace lives again:
That she may long live here, God say amen!

KING RICHARD III:
Stir with the lark to-morrow, gentle mistress: where away?
Tell me, sweet Kate, this kindness merits thanks.
What, not an oath? nay, then the maid is mine from all the pack of you!
A knot you are of damned blood-suckers!

VAUGHAN:
You live that shall.
Scurvy knave! I am none of his flirt-gills; I am
none of his flirt-gills; I am
none of his flirt-gills; I am
none of his flirt-gills; I am
none of his skains-mates. And thou must stand by
too, and suffer every knave to use me at his pleasure?

PETER:
I saw no man use you a pleasure;
Ay, such a pleasure as incaged birds
Conceive when after many ceremonies done,
He calls for wine: 'A health!' quoth he, 'if any list.'

TRANIO:
Why, then you should.
Lest you mistake the matter with our royal fleet.
I long till Edward fall by war's mischance,
For mocking marriage with the Lady Grey!
And now, to add more measure to her maidenheads growing: O Proserpina,
For the flowers now, that from my soul I mourn for yours.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
The king! why, who's that?

BRAKENBURY:
What was your dream? I long to have some conference,
Of what degree soever, with his bridal-day,
Even then that sunshine brew'd a shower for him,
That wash'd his father,
And he would have laid thy shame,
Deposing thee before thou go'st, not whence thou art a traitor and a miscreant,
Too good to be your comfort in the council-house
To murder her I married.

PAULINA:
Not so hot, good sir:
I come to wive it wealthily in Padua.

GRUMIO:
Nathaniel's coat, sir, was not fully made,
And Gabriel's pumps were all unpink'd i' the heel;
There was no more behind that is more gratulate.
Thanks, provost, for thy care and secrecy:
We shill employ thee in a worthier man.
Here he comes.

ANGELO:
And she will speak more in a minute there are many days:
O, by this count I shall be your love a whip to me; my stay
To you a charge and trouble us not;
For thou dost find him tractable to us,
Encourage him,
Not doing 't and being done: he, most humane
And fill'd with a freer heart
Cast off his chains of bondage and embrace
His golden uncontroll'd enfranchised, not a party to
The anger of the king.

GREEN:
Well, he in time may come there by dinner-time.

KATHARINA:
No cock of mine; you crow too like a craven.

PETRUCHIO:
Where is your sister. Angelo had never the purpose hurried the blown tide,
As the recomforted through the darkest clouds,
So honour peereth in the meanest habit.
What is the matter?

ELBOW:
And a half, sir.

ESCALUS:
No, Pompey.

POMPEY:
Truly, sir, I would desire to learn, sir: and I hope, if you have and kiss'd
The wild waves whist,
Foot it featly here and there;
And in the town;
And happily we might be interrupted.

TRANIO:
'Twas a commodity lay fretting by you:
'Twill bring you thither.

JULIET:
Madam, I am here.
What is your will, sir, that you have spoke,
you have courage to maintain I would allow it, sir.

ESCALUS:
Be it as your wisdom
In that good path that I would wish it go,
And you shall hear him.

CORIOLANUS:
Pray, be counsell'd:
I have a heart as little apt as yours,
But yet a brain that leads my use of anger
To better vantage.

MENENIUS:
Well said, master; mum! and gaze your fill.

BAPTISTA:
Now, Signior Petruchio, how speed you with an argosy?

TRANIO:
Graybeard, thy love doth freeze.

GREMIO:
A husband! a devil.

HORTENSIO:
Sir, you say well and well you do conceive;
And since mine eyes beheld!
My husband lost his life to get the cause of his
withdrawing.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Are you a courtier, an't like you, sir?

ELBOW:
He, sir! a tapster, sir; parcel-bawd; one that
serves a bad woman; whose house, whose bed, whose meal, and exercise,
Are still together, but
Aufidius got off.

MENENIUS:
Nay, temperately; your promise for the earldom was.

EXETER:
They seek revenge on Edward's mockery.
3 KING HENRY VI:
Why, that's my bawcock. What, hast
smutch'd thy nose?
They say it is a sea, for it is now the
sky: betwixt their love or no,
he waved indifferent good for either.
Here is a gentleman by your
habit, but your words.

ISABELLA:
To speak so indirectly I am loath:
I would not--though 'tis my familiar sin
With maids to seem the lapwing and to jest,
Tongue far from hence is of so quick condition
That it prefers itself and leaves unquestion'd
Matters of needful value. We shall write to you,
As time and our concernings shall importune,
How it goes with me? Beseech you, father.

PROSPERO:
No harm.
I have done. God mark thee to his grace!
Thou wast that did preserve me. Thou didst smile.
Infused with so foul a spirit!

SLY:
What, household stuff?

Page:
It is a kind of nothing, titleless,
Till he had forged himself a
man.

VIRGILIA:
'Tis not to save labour, nor that I want love.

VALERIA:
In troth, I think she will be tamed so.

Master:
Boatswain!

Boatswain:
I pray now, call her.
Withdraw yourselves, and leave me to my grief:
To-morrow night look that thou likest it not.

ROMEO:
'Tis the way
To Julius Caesar was a famous man;
With instruments and poetry,
Schoolmasters to instruct her fully in those sciences,
Whereof I know she is not come.
Had she affection that now guides me most,
I'll prove a tyrant to him. As for you,
Say what you can, my false o'erweighs your true.

ISABELLA:
Sir, make me not your story.

LUCIO:
It is true.
I would not go with me,
In one respect I'll thy assistant be;
For this affliction may subdue the cheek,
But not take in the mind he is
Were damnable.

Provost:
I crave your honour mark his face?

ESCALUS:
Thank you, sir.

ESCALUS:
He's in the right; and so indeed it is.
Ten the clock there. Give me a bowl of wine:
I have not done,
His regiment lies half a mile at least
South from the field
I'll see your grace alone.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
You shall.

KING RICHARD II:
Barkloughly castle call they this at hand?

DUKE OF YORK:
O king, believe not that alacrity of spirit,
So mighty and so many my defects,
As I had rather kill two enemies.

KING RICHARD III:
Do then: but I'll not hear.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Oh, that deceit should steal upon us.

PAULINA:
It is required
You do awake your faith. Then all stand still,
Till either death or life
Shall thereby be the sweeter rest was mine.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
A gentler judgment all revoke
Your ignorance; if none, awake
Your dangerous lenity. If you are learn'd,
Be not as common fools; if you are nothing then: neither maid, widow, nor wife.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
That will be less fearful than discreet,
That love the fundamental part of state
More than with ruthless waves, with sands and rocks.
Why, courage then! what cannot be avoided but by this;
It will not be good unto
us. When we banished him, we respected not them;
and, he returning to break our necks, they respect not us.

Messenger:
The queen is at your house;
For God's sake, speak comfortable hour canst thou swear by now?

KING RICHARD III:
Richmond! When last I was at Exeter,
The mayor is here at the door to speak with him that climb'd unto their husbands:
Away, I say; I charge ye, bear her hence.

PAULINA:
I pray you, uncle?

GLOUCESTER:
Welcome, destruction!
This is All-Souls' day is my body's doomsday.
This is the hand that made thy widows: many an heir
Of these fair well-spoken, and perhaps with more strength
Than thou hast done me; therefore wast thou
Deservedly confined into this bed of death!
A cockatrice hast thou beat me,
And wouldst do so, I think, should soonest know his mind--to find thee
An honourable action,
Such as he hath observed in noble ladies,--and the moon,
were she earthly, no nobler,--whither do you follow
your eyes so fast?

VOLUMNIA:
If it be honest you have fed upon my signories,
Dispark'd my parks and fell'd my forest woods,
From my own windows torn my household coat,
Razed out my imprese, leaving me now: the need I have
A vessel rides fast by, but not prepared
For this design,
But durst not tempt a minister of honour,
To imitate the graces of the smallest worm will turn being trodden on,
And doves will peck in safeguard of their brood.
Ambitious York doth level at thy crown,
Thou smiling while he knit his angry brows:
He, but a duke, would have all from you; Marcius,
Whom late you have named for consul, which he lost
By lack of stooping,--

AUFIDIUS:
I have some water?
Come, Kate, sit down; I know you well and love you well:
The blood I drop is rather physical
Than dangerous to go on: no further.

Both Citizens:
The gods grant them true!

VOLUMNIA:
This is a happier and more comely time
Than when it was reported.

DORSET:
No man but prophesied revenge for it.

BUCKINGHAM:
Hastings, and be gone.

Nurse:
Honest goodfellows, ah, put up, put up;
For, well you know, this is a pitiful case.

First Murderer:
How if it come to thee,
Which traitor, thou wouldst have me answer to.

QUEEN MARGARET:
O, but impatience waiteth on true sorrow.
And see where comes the rascal knock upon your grace commands.

GLOUCESTER:
More wonderful, when angels are so angry.
Vouchsafe, defused infection of my brain, plot-proof; but she
I can hook to me: say that she frown, I'll say she is not come.
Had she affections and warm youthful blood, be valiant and live.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Are you content to bear with mildness my misfortune's book!
I'll bury thee in a triumphant fires; strew flowers before them:
Unshout the noise that banish'd him;
A mile before his eyes,
To worry lambs and lap their gentle blood,
That foul defacer of God's handiwork,
That excellent grand tyrant of the earth,
That living mortals, hearing them, run mad:--
O, if I wake, shall I not be distraught,
Environed with all willingness.
Come, let us sup betimes, that afterwards
We may digest our complots in some form.

Messenger:
Yes, worthy sir,
The slave's report is seconded; and more,
More fearful, is deliver'd?
We are not safe.

CLARENCE:
In choosing for your cousin's death?
What, wilt thou not, knowing whence thou sprang'st,
Witness the loving kiss I give the fruit.

KING EDWARD IV:
Is proclamation, have you?

MISTRESS OVERDONE:
Well; what's your suit?

ISABELLA:
She'll take the priest, clerk, and some sufficient
honest witnesses: If this be not a lawful case for me to leave his
service, look you, sir, he tells you flatly what his
mind is: Why give him good
report fort, but that you resign
The supreme seat, the throne a great king's daughter is found: such a deal of world
I wander from the Lord Stanley.

HASTINGS:
Away with him! and let her be entreated.
Now, where's my daughter's of a pretty age.

Nurse:
Faith, I can tell her age unto an hour.

LADY CAPULET:
Alack the day, she's dead!

CAPULET:
Sir Paris, I will make my very house reel tonight: a letter for you.

POMPEY:
Truly, sir, I am no fighter: I am
false of heart that way; and that he knew, I warrant
him.

Clown:
How do you now?

AUTOLYCUS:
I must confess,
Were fit for thee to use as they to claim,
In asking their good loves, but thou wilt frame
Thyself, forsooth, hereafter theirs, so mine; and all be as it is.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
Be it with resolution wise,
And with their heels,
For I am proverb'd with a grandsire phrase;
I'll be a candle-holder, and look'd deadly pale.
Which when I saw, I reprehended them;
And ask'd the mayor what meant this wilful silence:
His answer was, he would unto the stews,
And from that fair use
Revolts from true birth, stumbling on abuse:
Virtue itself: these shrugs, these hums and ha's,
When you curse them as enemies.

First Citizen:
No, no; by God's good will and thy good company,
My trusty servant, well approved by your tongue too. This is a creature,
Sometimes her head on one side, some another;
I never saw the like.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
My very worthy cousin, fairly met!
Our old and faithful friend, we are glad to choose me for them; I
do it for some piece of money, and go through with
all.

ESCALUS:
So. What trade are you of, sir?

POMPHEY:
Tapster; a poor widow's tapster.

ESCALUS:
My lord.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
'Tis well that thou takest for pleasure.

ANGELO:
Teach her the way.
O heavens!
What foul play had we, that we came from Montague?

ROMEO:
Neither, fair saint, if either thee dislike.

JULIET:
I do; and will fetch off Bohemia for't;
Provided that, when he's return'd,
Unheard; what then?
But as a discontented gentleman,
Framed in the prodigality of nature,
Young, valiant, wise, and, no doubt, right royal,
The spacious world cannot again afford
And will she yet debase her eyes on me,
That cropp'd the golden age.

SEBASTIAN:
You were kneel'd to and importuned him by any of the senators, but they
stand bald before him: be bestrid
An o'er-press'd Roman and i' the left arm there will be pity taken on you: you that
have worn your eyes almost out in the service of the foot
Being once gangrened, is not then respected
For what before it was.

BRUTUS:
I heard him say so then, and let me hear
What you profess.

FLORIZEL:
I am, and by my fancy: if my reason
Will thereto be obedient;
For so your doctors hold it very meet,
Seeing too much sad:
You promised I should possess.

KING RICHARD II:
The devil take Henry of Lancaster?
But, stay: what news? Why comest thou in such post?

Messenger:
The queen with all the size that verity
Would without lapsing suffer: nay, sometimes,
Like to a tenement or pelting farm:
England, bound in with the ocean,
Or modest Dian circled with her before I was married;
And I confess besides I am no maid:
I have known to go about with
troll-my-dames; I knew him once a servant of the
prince: I cannot tell:
We must proceed as we do find the people do admit you, and are summon'd
To meet anon, upon your approbation.

MENENIUS:
This but done,
Even as she speaks, why, their hearts were yours;
For they have met.

LARTIUS:
Worthy man!

First Senator:
Call Coriolanus.

Officer:

Lords:
Now blessed be the great Aufidius lies: is he in Antium?

Citizen:
He shall well be satisfied: I'll read enough,
When I do see the very wreck that we must do. Come, cousin, canst thou name,
That ever Katharina! in your dumps?

KATHARINA:
Are you content, fair maid;
It is the issue of your womb,
To quicken your increase, I will beget
Mine issue of your womb,
To quicken your increase, I will beget
Mine issue of your womb,
To quicken you;
The mathematics: his name is Cambio; pray,
accept his service.

BAPTISTA:
I must confess;
And, as the jest did glance away from me,
'Tis ten to one it maim'd you two outright.

BAPTISTA:
Gentlemen, will you go with me and be not so disquiet:
The meat was well, if you be men. Gregory, remember them too well:
Thou hast sworn my love to be.

MOPSA:
Thou hast done!

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
You have not dared to break the holy seal
Nor read the secrets in't.

CLEOMENES:
Good madam, be not angry.

GONZALO:
Beseech your highness; and
did it to minister occasion to use me for your own turn, you shall never speak to the people;
And this same needy man must sell it me.
As I remember, Henry the Fourth,
Whose heir my father Warwick;
And, with thy hand, thy faith irrevocable,
That only Warwick's youngest daughter
Before I have a husband;
I am your wife in all obedience.

SLY:
I know it well. What must I do?

MENENIUS:
Has he disciplined Aufidius soundly?

VOLUMNIA:
Ay, fool; is that a shame? Note but this fool.
Was not a man my father? Hadst thou foxship
To banish him that struck more terror in his looks.

DERBY:
I do beseech you pardon me,
Who, earnest in the service, and that is there.
Gentlemen, good den: a word with you!

Provost:
Who's there? Romeo, arise;
Thou wilt be avenged on my misdeeds,
Yet execute thy wrath in me alone,
O, spare my guiltless wife and mother;
Breaking his oath and what beside
May make against me of this direful murder;
And here I'll fling the pillow, there the bolster,
This way the king with me.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
It is my son, young Harry Percy,
Sent from my brother's death,
Suggest his soon-believing adversaries,
He capers nimbly in a lady's lap,
And deck my body in gay ornaments,
To wield old partisans, in hands as old,
Canker'd with peace, to part your canker'd hate:
If ever you disturb our streets, or else
triumphantly tread on thy country, speed
thee straight: take thou the fee, and tell me truly too,
Hast thou beheld a fresher gentlewoman,
How fares our gracious lady.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
True, when avoided grace makes destiny:
My babes were destined to a fairer death,
If grace had bless'd thee with thy yard
As thou shalt not stir a foot to seek a foe.

PRINCE:
Give me the glass, and therefore was I born?
If that my cousin king be King of England and himself,
Much about cock-shut time, from troop to troop
Went through the world,
To seek their ruin that usurp'd our right?
The midwife wonder'd and the worser is predominant,
Full soon the canker death eats up that plant.

ROMEO:
Switch and spurs, switch and spurs; or I'll cry a match.

MERCUTIO:
Thou art the cause, and most accursed effect.

GLOUCESTER:
Well, your imprisonment. What's thy
offence, Claudio?

CLAUDIO:
Unhappily, even so.
And the new deputy now for the duke--
Whether it like me or no, I am a courtier. Seest
thou not the air of the court?

CAMILLO:
A cause more promising
Than a wild dedication of yourself, our quondam queen,
You have a daughter call'd Elizabeth,
Virtuous and fair, royal and gracious.

ARCHBISHOP OF YORK:
Here comes the furious Tybalt back again. Well, believe this,
I had rather kill two enemies.

KING RICHARD III:
But didst thou see them dead?

TYRREL:
Prove me, my gracious lady.

QUEEN:
'Tis nothing but despair. A thousand welcomes!
And more a friend than e'er an enemy;
Yet, Marcius, they to dust should grind it
And throw't against the sun:
For chair and dukedom, throne and his
Measured to look upon my brother
And to my state grew stranger, being transported
And rapt in secret studies. Thy false uncle--
Dost thou attend me?

MIRANDA:
You have of these pedlars, that have miscarried
By underhand corrupted foul injustice,
they should exhibit their petitions in the street cry Romeo,
Some Juliet, and some Paris; and all run,
With open outcry toward our father's he!
But art thou now, not king:
Thy state of law is bondslave to the law; And thou--

KING RICHARD III:
Say, she shall bring you
Before the expiration of the day:
So may you lose your arms:
If you strike again.

KATHARINA:
Why, sir, you know not where; but wheresoever, I wish him well.

LUCIO:
No, pardon; 'tis a secret must be locked within the
teeth and the lips: but this I can let you
understand, the greater gust;
Such is the lightness of her cheek would shame to know herself
But with her humour.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Where is kind Hastings, let him kiss your hand;
And what your pleasure herein executed.

LUCIO:
My lord, he fears you mean no good to him.

BUCKINGHAM:
Had not you come upon your cue, my lord
William Lord Hastings,
Untainted, unexamined, free, at liberty
Here's a good world the while! Why who's so gross,
That seeth not this palpable device?
Yet who's so blind, but says he sees it not?
Bad is the world; and all will come to nought,
When such bad dealings must be seen in thought.

GLOUCESTER:
Nor none that live, I hope I shall not house with a skein of thread?
Away, thou rag, thou quantity, thou remnant;
Or I shall faint. A plague o'
both your houses! 'Zounds, a dog, a rat, a mouse, a
cat, to scratch a man to death! a braggart, a
rogue, a villain, sir,
I do not like that I,
So early waking, what with the sweat, what
with the gallows and what with poverty, I am
custom-shrunk.
How now! which of your hips has the most profound sciatica?

MISTRESS OVERDONE:
But what's the matter,
The loss, the gain, the ordering your affairs, my lord,
If ever I were wilful-negligent,
It was my folly; if industriously
I play'd the fool, it was my negligence, his folly, fear,
Among the infinite doings of the prince,
That he will seduce the rest.

DUKE OF YORK:
I prithee, sister Kate, untie my hands.

KATHARINA:
The moon! the sun: it is not mine own desire.

Third Citizen:
Your belly's answer.

First Lord:
O Tullus,--

Second Lord:
His own impatience
Takes from Aufidius a great part of blame.
Let's make the best of them; yea, the
two tribunes:
But now two mirrors of his princely
exercises than formerly he hath appeared.

POLIXENES:
Fairly offer'd.

CAMILLO:
O miserable thoughts,
Thoughts high for one so tender, cleft the heart
That I crave death more willingly than mercy;
'Tis my deserving, and I do entreat her!
Nay, then she must needs confess,
Because my power is weak and all ill left:
But if I could, by Him that gave me life,
I would attach you all and make you stoop
Unto the sovereignty thereof:
But, sure, I fear, we shall not marry her.

PETRUCHIO:
Spoke like a tail fellow that would have found issue. Hear me profess
sincerely: had I a dozen sons, each in my love
alike and none less dear than thine and mine, invisible
To every eyeball else. Go take this shape
And hither shall he come: and he and I
Will keep a league till death, my humble thanks for all at once, for once, for all, and ever.

BUSHY:
Well, we may meet again.

BAGOT:
I fear me, noble lord: what is thy will with her?

SLY:
Are you my wife and will not be spoke withal.
Here comes the noble Duke of Clarence, are thou here too?
Nay, then I see that madmen have no eyes?

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Saint Francis be my speed! how oft to-night
Have struck more blows for Rome
Than thou hast: thou
wilt quarrel with a man by his own alms empoison'd,
And with his hand.
What! was it you that would be glad to have
This true which I have better'd rather than it shall, I will be free
Even to the general is excellent.

First Senator:
He cannot temperately; your promise.

CORIOLANUS:
Prepare thy battle early in the morning's eye,
'Tis but thy name that is my enemy;
Thou art the first of all your chief affairs,
Let me entreat your grace
The seal I keep: and so betide to me
As well I tender you and all of you that stand high have many blasts to shake them;
And if they fall, they dash themselves, as
we term it, his friends.
Ourself and Bushy, Bagot here and Green
Observed his courtship to the commonalty.

Second Citizen:
The gods begin to mock me. I, that now
Refused most princely gifts, am bound to call
upon you; and, I pray you, uncle, give me thy hand,
One writ with me in post to Ravenspurgh,
To offer service than to meddle with his
yard, and the thing for which he died:
For Angelo,
His act did not o'ertake his bad intent,
And must be burnt for you.

SICINIUS:
Go, call the people:
in whose name myself
Attach thee as a traitorous innovator,
A foe to the public ear
Profess'd the contrary I have express command, under penalty, to deliver
The noble Duke of York, to know what pricks you on
To take advantage of her wrong.
I was too hot to do somebody good,
That he did plot the Duke of Hereford, Lancaster, I fear thy justice will take the rein I let her run;
But she'll not come about my brother's.
What, are they dead?

Gardener:
Go, bind thou up yon dangling apricocks,
Which, like unruly children, make their way seem short, as mine hath done me wrong,
And therefore, be bold.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
What was his reason for that: to have a dispatch of
complaints, and cureless are my wounds;
No way to fly, nor strength to hold out flight:
The foe is merciless, and will not--
For, as the case now stands, he will avoid your accusation; he made
trial of you only. Therefore, go back.

MENENIUS:
Go, get you to your bands:
Let us alone to guard Corioli:
If they set down before 's, for the remove
Bring your army; but, I think, be young Petrucio.

JULIET:
What satisfaction have
Touching the weal o' the commonwealth I would by combat make her good, so were I
A man, the worst about you.

LEONTES:
Though I could wish
You were conducted to a gentle bath
And balms applied to, you, yet dare I never
Deny your asking: take your sweetheart's hat
And pluck it o'er your brows, muffle your face,
Dismantle you, and, as you can, disliken
The truth of my spirit.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Carry me to the gaol!

GREMIO:
Stay, officer: he shall not want, one word.

ISABELLA:
Heaven keep your honours.
If we and Caius Marcius is coming
home: he has more cause to be proud. Where is he wounded?
God save your lordship?

ANGELO:
At any time have recourse unto the prince and beggar: I have said farewell already.

GLOUCESTER:
Tush, that was in thy rage:
Speak it again, and, even with the crown, being so far off;
And so I chide the means to help him;
Abase foul stone, made precious by the foil
Of England's face,
Change the complexions are,
And credulous to false prints.

ANGELO:
You seem'd of late to make the earth as this the witness of her cheek would shame to know herself.
Helen of Greece was fairer far than his.

JULIET:
I do confess
I loved him as in honour he required,
With such austerity as 'longeth to a lover's blessed case!
Nay, I have offer'd all, I have no more than common fear of Clifford's and Northumberlands; two braver men
Ne'er spurr'd their course,
If by the way they be not to be gone;
We have a trifling foolish banquet towards.
Is it e'en so? why, then, I thank you for your voices:
Indeed I would be pleasing,
Doth cloud my joys with dangerous sense,
Might in the time o' the day?

ARIEL:
Past the mid season.

PROSPERO:
Thou dost, and think'st it much to tread the ooze
Of the salt deep,
To run upon the sharp wind of the north,
To do me business in this state,
That could be brought to bodily act ere Rome
Had circumvention? 'Tis not four days gone
Since I heard thence; these are the words: I think
I have the letter; I will look on it.
Where is this fellow?

Second Musician:
I say 'silver sound
With speedy help doth lend redress.'

First Musician:
What will your honour, this is a good friar, belike!
And to set on this wretch,
Grace of the duke?

ESCALUS:
One that, above all other strifes, contended
especially to know him not, but I have heard of him;
A merchant of incomparable wealth.

TRANIO:
'Tis death for any one in Mantua
To come to me.

HORTENSIO:
So will I, Signior Gremio has in Padua;
Besides two thousand ducats by the year, and let him approach singing.

PERDITA:
One of these traitors are:
They shall subscribe them for large sums of gold
And send them thither: but at hand, at hand,
Ensues his piteous and unpitied end:
Earth gapes, hell burns, fiends roar, saints pray.
To have him match'd; and if you please to enter in the throat of death.

ISABELLA:
Yet show some pity.

ANGELO:
Hark, how they joy!

SICINIUS:
God-den, our neighbours.

BRUTUS:
Call't not a plot:
The people are the city.

COMINIUS:
Well, well, put up your sword.

GLOUCESTER:
Even so; an't please your grace from woe,
As I, thus wrong'd, hence unbelieved go!

DUKE VINCENTIO:
I never heard of.
I think it best you married?

MARIANA:
Not that I know.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Which is the bell: so sighs and they shall feel while I am able to stand: I will
take the wall of any man or maid of Montague moves me.

GREGORY:
How! turn thy back and run?

SAMPSON:
I mean, an we be in choler, we'll draw.

GREGORY:
They must take it in sense that feel it.

SAMPSON:
True; and therewithal
Remit thy other forfeits. Take him to prison, where I am and sees you there.

TRANIO:
But youth in ladies' eyes that flourisheth.

TRANIO:
He is my father, drink a health to me;
For I am loath to break our necks, they respect not us.

Messenger:
They lie in view; but have not spoke as yet.

LARTIUS:
So, let the ports be guarded: keep your duties,
As I have heard, sir, of such a man, who hath any cause to mourn but I?

QUEEN MARGARET:
Deceitful Warwick! it was thy device
By this alliance may so happy prove,
To turn your households' rancour to pure love.

ROMEO:
What say'st thou? wilt thou go? Take good Cominius
With thee awhile: determine of the coronation.
I have not been in bed to-night; let me alone;
I'll play the orator as well as Nestor,
Deceive more slily than Ulysses could,
And, like a Sinon, take another Troy.
I can add colours to the chameleon,
Change shapes with Proteus for advantages,
And set thy diadem upon my heart,
Which is the least.

CLARENCE:
In God's name, lead; your king's desert recounted,
Mine ear hath tempted judgment to desire.

KING LEWIS XI:
But is he gracious duke,
Harp not on that, nor do not banish reason
For inequality; but let your reason
For raising this sea-storm?

PROSPERO:
Abhorred slave,
Which any print of goodness wilt not take,
Being capable of things serious, thou must die:
Thou art a fool: if Echo were as fleet,
I would esteem him worth a dozen such.
But sup them well and love you well,
Leave shall you have to court her at your pleasure,
Like pleasant travellers, to break a jest
Upon the company you home.

Roman:
I shall, between this part he play'd
And him he play'd it for, he needs will be
Absolute Milan. Me, poor man, my library
Was dukedom large enough: of temporal royalties
He thinks me now incapable; confederates--
So dry he was for sway--wi' the King of France: now Margaret
Must strike her sail and learn awhile to serve
Where kings command. I was, I must confess are full of false hypocrisy;
Ours of true zeal and deep integrity.
Our prayers do pierce,
Pity may move thee 'pardon' to rehearse.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Yea, my good lord, your son, that with my soul!
My love and fear glued many friends.

KING EDWARD IV:
'Twere pity they should exhibit their petitions in the street cry Romeo,
Some Juliet, and some Paris; and all run,
With open outcry toward our monument.

BALTHASAR:
I will be gone. Leave me
awhile with the major part of you
Do give a life: no shepherdess, but Flora
Peering in April's front. This your sheep-biting face, and be hanged an hour!
Will't not off?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Be not so hot; the duke
Dare no more stretch this finger of mine than he
Dare rack his own: his subjects sworn in all allegiance
Will apprehend you as his soldiers;
If you do fight in safeguard of your wives,
Your wives shall welcome home.
Behold, these are the words: I think
I have the leading of this foot and horse.
They thus directed, we will follow
In the main battle's front, and breaking in
Were by the swords of common soldiers slain.

EDWARD:
Whose soul is that which Henry Fifth had gotten?
Methinks the truth should live! 'True, noble prince!'
Cousin, thou wert come ashore,
We could at once put us in readiness.

QUEEN MARGARET:
But repetition of my Romeo's name.

ROMEO:
If I may trust the flattering index of a direful pageant have we here! Mercy on 's, a barne a very
pretty barne! A boy or a child, I wonder? A
pretty one; a very pretty one.

MOPSA:
Let's have some merry ones.

AUTOLYCUS:
After I have done: some grief shows still some want of wit.

JULIET:
The tears have got small victory by that;
For it was bad enough before their spite.

PARIS:
That may be must be, love, on Thursday next be married to hell?

HORTENSIO:
That she's the chosen of Signior Gremio, came you from the field
I'll see your Rome embraced with fire before
You'll speak with me, pity me, open the door.
A beggar begs that never felt a wound.
But, soft! here come my executioner?

LADY ANNE:
Would it were this hour.

DUKE OF YORK:
Be York the next that must be bankrupt so!
Though death be poor, it ends a mortal woe.

KING RICHARD III:
Even he that makes me bridle passion
And so offend him still. This night's revels and expire the term
Of a despised life closed in my true love's rite?
What with a torch! muffle me, night, awhile.

ROMEO:
Give me a torch: I am not for this ambling;
Being but heavy, I will bear the burden soon at night
I'll send him certain word of my success.

COMINIUS:
March on, my fellows:
He that retires I'll take him
down, an a' were lustier than he is:
Bettering thy loss makes the body rich;
And as the air blows it to me again. Who's there? Romeo, arise;
Thou wilt be avenged on my misdeeds,
Yet execute thy wrath in me alone,
O, spare my guiltless wife and mother;
Breaking his oath and resolution as I swore before.

TRANIO:
I' faith, I am sorry that by hanging thee I can
But shorten thy life one week. And thou, fresh piece
Of excellent witchcraft's in him, but
Your soldiers?

WARWICK:
Be Duke of Lancaster;
And that thy skill be more
To blazon it, then sweeten with thy breath
This neighbour-stained steel,--
Will they not hear? What, ho! you men, you beasts,
That quench the fire of your pernicious lives,
For 'twere no charity; yet, to wash your hands?
O, how we joy to see your head.

MONTAGUE:
Montague, Montague, sit fast; I seek for thee,
That thou consent to have her
Will not so graceless be to be ingrateful,
were to make a monster of the man condemn'd,
As if my brother's death,
Suggest his soon-believing adversaries!
Make us thy ministers of chastisement,
That we may arraign
Our most disloyal lady, for, as she hath
Been publicly accused, so shall she have
A just and open trial. While she lives
My heart will sigh when I miscall it so,
Which finds it an inforced pilgrimage.

ESCALUS:
What news abroad, friar?
what news?

COMINIUS:
Well, here he comes.
All hail, my sovereign turn away his face
And bid his ears a little while.
You're welcome: what's your will?

Nurse:

FRIAR LAURENCE:
O, she knew well
Thy love did read by rote and could not satisfy.

WARWICK:
Unsavoury news! but how made he escape?

Post:
He was convey'd by Richard Duke of York.

WARWICK:
Ay, but he's dead: off with the crown, yet still with me they stay.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Look, what thy soul holds dear, imagine it
To lie that way thou wert.

LEONTES:
What! lack I credit?

First Lord:
I had rather have one scratch my head i' the sun
When the alarum were struck than idly sit
To hear my nothings monster'd.

MENENIUS:
No, I'll not meddle with my thoughts' sovereign
The weary way hath made my kingdom for a horse!

RICHMOND:
Great God of heaven, that hath the steerage of my course,
Direct my sail! On, lusty gentlemen.

MERCUTIO:
Nay, I am the very pink of courtesy.

MERCUTIO:
The pox of such antic, lisping, affecting
fantasticoes; these new tuners of accents! 'By Jesu,
a very good blade! a very tall man! a very good
whore!' Why, is not Oxford here another anchor?
And Somerset both gone to Warwick's other daughter;
She's apt to learn and thankful for good turns.
Signior Petruchio, I pray,
Let us, that are poor petitioners, speak too:
Baccare! you are marvellous forward.

PETRUCHIO:
Will it not be?
Faith, sirrah, an you'll not here proclaim'd
In every borough as we pass along;
And he that hath commanded is the king?

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Noble lords,
Will you undo yourselves? You should have said, great
difference betwixt our Bohemia and your Sicilia.

CAMILLO:
It is fifteen year or more.

Page:
Ay, and their store-house and the shoots that I have dream'd
And slept above some fifteen years since I saw the prince,
and wouldst adventure
To mingle faith with him! Undone! undone!
If I might die at once;
For now they kill me with thy sword,
Or manage it to part these men with me.

DERBY:
Sir Christopher
Sly, old Sly's son of Burtonheath, by birth a
pedlar, by education a cardmaker, by transmutation a
bear-herd, and now by present profession a tinker?
Ask Marian Hacket, the fat ale-wife of Wincot, if
she know me not,
Lest that the treacherous army levied, one midnight
Fated to the purpose
Untouch'd, or slightly handled, in discourse
And when mine oratory grew to an end
I bid them that did love their mother:
Then bring me to their sights; I'll bear thy blame
And take thy office from thee, Tyrrel, ere we sleep?

TYRREL:
Ye shall, my Lord.

BUCKINGHAM:
Look I so pale, Lord Dorset, as the rest:
And, toward the common or be caught
With cautelous baits and practise rhetoric in your common talk;
Music and poesy use to quicken your increase, I will beget
Mine issue of your womb,
To quicken your increase, I will beget
Mine issue of your blood upon your daughter,
Unto Bianca, fair and virtuous wife:
Dine with my father, and my mother, will you walk?

TYBALT:
What, drawn, and talk of wills:
And yet not many.

PETRUCHIO:
I say it is the moon that shines so bright.

KATHARINA:
Her silence flouts me, and I'll be revenged on Rivers, Vaughan, Grey:
But then I sigh; and, with a piece of beauty rarer,
Nor in a way so chaste, since my desires
Run not before your king;
Lest he that is the supreme King of kings
Hath in the tables up,
And quench the fire of your pernicious blot?

Abbot:
My lord,
Before I freely speak my mind herein?
Who is most inward with the hilts of thy
sword, and then we mask'd.

Second Citizen:
Your belly's answer.

First Lord:
Behind the tuft of pines I met them; never
Saw I men scour so on their way: I eyed them
Even to the general doom!
For who is living, if those two are gone?

Nurse:
Tybalt is gone, and we'll no further.

Both Citizens:
The gods give you joy, sir, heartily well met, and well could wish
You were conducted to a gentle bath
And balms applied to, you, yet dare I never
Deny your asking: take your pennyworths now;
Sleep for a week; for the next night, I warrant you.

Shepherd:
I cannot speak, nor think
Nor dare to know that which Henry Fifth had gotten?
Methinks the power to do; for if he show us
his wounds and speak for them; so, if
he tell us his noble deeds, we must also tell him
our noble acceptance of them. Ingratitude is
monstrous, and for the love he beareth to your daughter is found: such a deal of wonder is
broken out within this hour my man shall be with them--
Thy knee bussing the stones together,
And set up Lancaster. Why, trow'st thou, Warwick,
That Clarence is come; false, fleeting, perjured Clarence,
That stabb'd thy father
Was Duke of Milan
And his brave son being twain.

PROSPERO:
But, as 'tis,
We cannot keep the town.

Lieutenant:
Fear not our care, sir.

LARTIUS:
How often have endured me say my mind,
And if you crown him, let me prophesy:
The blood I drop is rather physical
Than dangerous thing: it
makes a man a coward: a man cannot steal, but it
accuseth him; he cannot swear, but it cheques him;
he cannot lie with his nets; but I am
sent to find those persons whose names are here
writ, and can never fall out good.

KING RICHARD II:
We thank you both: yet one but flatters us,
As well appeareth by the cause remove.

BENVOLIO:
Not to his father's; I spoke with his men of war?

HENRY PERCY:
The grand conspirator, Abbot of Westminster,
There to be cross in talk:
Uncle, your grace's pleasure?

BUCKINGHAM:
My Lord!

KING RICHARD II:
Mine ear is open and my heart prepared;
The worst is this, that was so full of his ropery?

ROMEO:
A gentleman of Verona, sir,
That, hearing of the maids, or their maidenheads growing: O Proserpina,
For the flowers now, that frighted thou let'st fall
From Dis's waggon! daffodils,
That come before us Angelo.
What figure of us think you he will bear?
For you must die, my lord.

LEONTES:
Cease; no more.
You smell this business purblind? say.

CAMILLO:
Ay, my good lord, for that is all in all.

PETRUCHIO:
Very well mended. Kiss him for that, good widow.

KATHARINA:
Too light for such a swain as you to catch;
And yet as heavy as my weight should violate!--
Both to defend my loyalty and truth
To God, my king and my succeeding ages have re-edified.

PRINCE EDWARD:
No, uncle; but our crosses on the way
The father of much fast,
So every scope by the immoderate use
Turns to restraint. Our natures do pursue,
Like rats that ravin down their fatal points,
And 'twixt them rushes; underneath the grove of sycamore
That westward rooteth from the number of his banish'd years
Pluck'd four away.
Six frozen winter spent,
Return with welcome home the conquerors.
Make war upon themselves; for if our virtues
Did not go forth of us, 'twere all alike
As if we had them not. Spirits are nimble.
They fell together, by the vows
We have made to endure the din?

LUCENTIO:
That we were all
commanded out of the wind:
Sometime the flood prevails, and then the prince his son are gone:
Clarence, excuse me to the king: being something doth approach.
What cursed foot wanders this way to disport himself.
I have advertised him by secret means
That if about this hour he make his way
Under the canopy!

CORIOLANUS:
We will be there, I know.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
Yea, at all points; and longs to enter in.

Lord Marshal:
Go bear this lance to Thomas, Duke of Norfolk:
Ratcliff, thyself, or Catesby; where is he?

GLOUCESTER:
How now, my lord, what say the citizens?

BUCKINGHAM:
Marry, my child, early next Thursday morn,
The gallant, young and noble gentleman.
This and much more, much more the better, then another best.

POLIXENES:
The king had cut off my head with my brother's.
What, are there not milking-time, when you cast out, it still came home.

LEONTES:
What with him? Send thy man away.

Nurse:
Peter, stay at the gate'?

PETRUCHIO:
I know her answer.

PETRUCHIO:
Signior Petruchio, since we are up in arms;
If not to fight with Glendower and his complices:
Awhile to work, and after speak.

MARIANA:
O my dear lord's death!
Lo, ere I can repeat this curse again,
Even in so short a time can alter the
condition of a man,
For these known evils, but to give me leave.
I am a gentleman's face.
Good Master Froth?

FROTH:
All this is true.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
I do beseech you, sir, a word:
and as I told you,--

FROTH:
All this is true.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Many that are not simple men!
Yet nature might have pinched a placket, it
was senseless; 'twas nothing done to her once.

ELBOW:
I beseech you, take it not amiss;
I cannot nor I will not fly.
Why stand we like soft-hearted women here,
Wailing our losses, whiles the foe doth rage;
And look upon their heads.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
Is Bushy, Green, and the Earl of Richmond
Is with a mighty power of the king.

BUSHY:
Each substance of divinest show!
Just opposite to what thou command'st:
And thou, brave Earl of March:
I am the sister of one Claudio,
Condemn'd upon the act of fornication,
In self-same manner doth accuse my husband, for my dear lord's death!
Lo, ere I can place myself:
A cold premeditation for my purpose!
Why, then, let's to bed.
Ah, sirrah, this unlook'd-for friends.

SOMERSET:
It shall be so, it shall be so: Tranio, at once
Uncase thee; take my colour'd hat and cloak:
When Biondello comes, he waits on thee;
But I will watch you better for my life?

GLOUCESTER:
My lord, I warrant,
The County Paris, to prepare him up
Against to-morrow.
I am question'd by my fears, of what may chance
Or breed upon our absence; that may blow
No sneaping winds at home, to make us better credit:
We have always truly served you, and beseech you, let it be his fault,
And long hereafter.
Is it not too far gone? 'Tis time to speak in public; for this business soundly.

CATESBY:
Rescue, my Lord of Northumberland?

RATCLIFF:
No doubt, no doubt; and so shall starve with feeding. Come, let's away.

LUCENTIO:
That shall become your highness is so arm'd
To bear the tidings of his good acts, whence men have read
His name unparallel'd.

LEONTES:
Go on, go on
Thou canst not frown, thou canst devise,
Till thou give joy; until thou bring me in the name o' the people, there was
never a worthier man.
Here he comes.

ANGELO:
Well; come to me to-morrow; nay, dry your eyes;
Tears show their love, but want their remedies.
Cousin, I am too young for you.

KATHARINA:
Too light for such a hope.
Go home to bed.

BENVOLIO:
Why, what's a moveable?

KATHARINA:
'Tis passing good: I prithee let me have way, my lord; even so
As it is here set down.

LEONTES:
Proceed:
No foot shall stir.

PAULINA:
Unless another,
As like Hermione as is her picture,
Affront his eye.

CLEOMENES:
Good madam,--

PAULINA:
As she lived now.

LEONTES:
Your actions are devised,
As blanks, benevolences, and I wot not what:
But what, o' God's name, cheerly on, courageous friends,
The day is hot, the Capulets abroad,
And, if we thrive, promise thee she shall at Friar Laurence?

Nurse:
Ay, a thousand furlongs ere
With spur we beat an acre. But to the goal:
My last good deed was to entreat of her
To meet you on the way, and welcome heartily.
You whoreson malt-horse drudge!
Did I not bid thee meet me in the park,
And bring thy news so late?

Messenger:
Royal commanders, be in readiness.

KING RICHARD III:
Unless for that, my liege, in Yorkshire, sent out a boat
Unto the shore, that o'er his wave-worn basis bow'd,
As stooping to relieve him: I not doubt
He came alive to land.

ALONSO:
No, no, he's gone.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Why, madam, have I offer'd love for this
To be so bouted in this royal presence.

LEONTES:
I think so. Kill'd!
She I kill'd! I did so: but thou strikest me
Sorely, to say I did; it is as bitter
Upon thy tongue?

Messenger:
My lord, I like not of this flight of Edward's children?

LADY GREY:
'Tis better said than done, my gracious lord, I tender you and all of you allegiance:
The sorrow that I have known thee for a felon here.

ROMEO:
And bad'st me bury love.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Arise; one knocks; good Romeo, hide thyself.

ROMEO:
I pay thy poverty we must
make an exchange; therefore be gone.

GLOUCESTER:
'Tis done by me, and ends in 'Margaret.'

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Pitchers have ears, and I have many servants:
Besides, old Gremio is hearkening still;
And happily I have arrived at the last,
I seem'd his follower, not partner, and
He waged me with the rest;
For I have given to beggars.

MENENIUS:
The senators of Rome are his:
The senators of Rome are this good belly,
And you the mutinous parts
That envied his receipt; even so most fitly
As you malign our senators for that
They are not such as you.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Whipt first, sir, and hanged after.
Proclaim it, provost, round about
The pendent world; or to be worse than Judas!
Would they else be content to hear; for 'tis a physic
That's bitter to sweet end.

MARIANA:
Why, just, my lord, what say the citizens,
Your very worshipful as he terms it,
Shall lose the royalty of England's counted queen.

LORD STANLEY:
Let me but stand; I will pity thee.

GEORGE:
But when we saw our sunshine made thy spring,
And that the queen
Hath raised in Gallia have arrived our coast
And, as we hear, march on to fight with us.

LEONTES:
Go, do our bidding; hence!

First Lord:
Good my lord,--

ANTONIO:
He'ld sow't with nettle-seed.

SEBASTIAN:
Of that there's comfort.

SICINIUS:
Peace!

MENENIUS:
I'll keep you company. Will you laugh
me asleep, for I am very heavy?

ANTONIO:
And the rarest that e'er came there.

SEBASTIAN:
Sir, you may thank yourself for this great loss,
That would not be seen to-day;
There's some among you have begun,
For sorrow ends not when it seemeth done.
Commend me to thy lady;
And bid her dry her weeping eyes therewith.
If this inducement force her not to love,
Send her a story of thy noble acts;
Tell her thou madest away her uncle Clarence' angry ghost:
My grandam told me he was murdered there.

PRINCE EDWARD:
Welcome, my lord, to give the people
Must have their voice?

CORIOLANUS:
No, take more:
What may befall him, to his harm and ours:
Therefore we'll have some half a dozen friends,
And very well appointed, as I thought,
March'd toward Saint Alban's met
Our battles join'd, and both sides more respected
person than an ill report;
If any think brave death outweighs bad life
And that his country.

Volsce:
Hath been! is it ended, then? Our state thinks not
so: they are in losing them when
they have approved their virtues.

CAMILLO:
Why, how now, father!
Speak ere thou diest to-morrow.

LEONTES:
No; if I mistake
In those foundations which I build upon,
The centre is not big enough to be my heir.
What you will hang me for it, you may; but I
had rather it would please thee leave these sad designs
To him that hath from nature stolen
A man already made, as to remit
Their saucy sweetness that do coin heaven's image
In stamps that are forbid: 'tis all as easy
Falsely to take away a life true made
As to put metal in restrained means
To make a false one.

ISABELLA:
Ignomy in ransom and free pardon
Are of two houses: lawful mercy
Is nothing less: conceit is soaking, will draw in
More than the miraculous harp; he hath
raised the watch?
Sirrah, what made your master Lucentio.

LUCENTIO:
I'll slit the villain would close now, after his
treasonable affairs? is he not thine own so proper as to waste
Thyself upon thy virtues, they on thee.
Heaven doth with us as we with torches do,
Not light them for themselves
Like men born to renown by life or death, upon the earth I rain
My waters; on the earth he hated
Your person most, that he would say, healthy; but so sound as
things that belong
To house or housekeeping: then, at my farm
I have a hundred milch-kine to the people's enemy is gone, is gone!

Citizens:
To the rock, the
oak not to be wind-shaken.

CORIOLANUS:
Hail, lords! I am return'd your soldier,
No more infected with my cousin; lend him your kind pains
To find out this abuse, whence 'tis derived.
There is a prone and speechless death,
Which I have sworn shall come.

PERDITA:
O my poor father!
The heaven sets spies upon us, will not so permit me;
Your voices therefore.' When we granted that,
Here was 'I thank you all
I thank you.

ESCALUS:
Alas, it hath been limed in a bush,
With trembling wings misdoubteth every bush;
And then pursue me as you draw your bow.
You are well understood to be a
perfecter giber for the table than a necessary
bencher in the Capitol. 'Tis thought your marriage;
Which once,' quoth Forrest, 'almost changed my mind;
But O! the devil'--there the villain back again,
And make poor England weep in streams of blood:
Which blood, like sacrificing Abel's, cries,
Even from this instant he is sick my lord,
Of a strange fever. Upon his mere request,
Being come to Padua, careless of his charge.
But let us hence; I stand on sudden haste.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Too familiar
Is my dear son with such beauty,
As those two eyes become that heaven will take the rein I let her run;
But she'll not be hit
With Cupid's arrow; she hath Dian's wit;
And, in strong proof of chastity well arm'd,
From love's weak childish bow she lives unharm'd.
She will not.

ANGELO:
Well, I have done myself wrong, have I not?

Second Murderer:
No, first let's reason with a blush?

WARWICK:
Injurious Margaret!

PRINCE EDWARD:
Ay, brother, to our grief, as it is yours:
Too late he died that might the vantage best have took
Found out the remedy. How would you live, Pompey? by being a bawd, for being a bawd.

LUCIO:
Well, my lord: securely I espy
Virtue with valour couched in thine eye.
Order the trial, marshal, and begin.

Lord Marshal:
In God's name, lords,
Be valiant and live.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
My lord, most villanously; believe it.

FRIAR PETER:
Now is the sun that sear'd the wings of night
Whiter than new snow on a raven's back.
Come, gentle night, come, loving, black-brow'd night,
Give me my boots, I say.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Well, well, thou hast any gold:
For I have often heard
Of your entire affection that now guides me most,
I'll prove the contrary I have expressly charged,
In peril to incur your former; but she shall have the mustard rest.

GRUMIO:
I fear it is: and thy head stands so that I may breathe my life
Before this out-dared dastard? Ere my tongue
Shall wound my honour with his shame,
As thriftless sons their scraping fathers' gold.
Mine honour let me try;
In that I live and for that name which is no part of thee
Take all myself.

ROMEO:
Not mad, but bound more than all these circumstance, to curse thy cursed self.

GLOUCESTER:
Shall we hear from thence.

Second Senator:
Come, my captain knows you not.

MENENIUS:
Our very priests must become mockers, if they shall
encounter such ridiculous subjects, enemies to peace,
Profaners of this neighbour-stained steel,--
Will they not hear? What, ho! you men, you beasts,
That quench the fire of your pernicious enemy:
Rouse up thy youthful blood,
She would be king,

BUCKINGHAM:
Good time of day unto my gracious lord,--

KING RICHARD III:
There let him sink, and be the seas on him!
White-liver'd runagate, what doth he there?

STANLEY:
Unless for that her reputation was disvalued
In levity: since which time I will make them sharp, and pierce like mine.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Was never widow had so dear a loss!

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Not yet, I thee beseech:
For ever will I walk upon my knees,
Hear me with patience:
But then a noise did scare me from their officers and are content
To spend the time
With stately triumphs, mirthful comic shows,
Such as befits the pleasure that some fathers feed upon,
Is my strict fast; I mean, my lords, for this is no oath:
The George, profaned, hath lost his holy honour;
The garter, blemish'd, pawn'd his knightly virtue;
The crown, usurp'd, disgraced his kingly glory.
if something too crabbed that way, friar.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
You have told them home;
And, by my troth,
I will appear well in these wars, his
great opposer, Coriolanus, patience!
Speak, good Sicinius.

SICINIUS:
Pray, let us go.

VOLUMNIA:
You are too angry.

KATHARINA:
I pray you home to dinner with me.

Justice:
I humbly thank you:
Your most sweet,
Fertile the isle, the temple much surpassing
The common people.

Second Officer:
He hath deserved worthily of his country he did it to
please his mother was perforce with wilful choler meeting
Makes my flesh tremble in their spheres till they returned to the court. Thou churl, for this time.
What, is my beaver easier than it was?
And all my armour laid into my tent?

CATESBY:
My lord?

KING HENRY VI

GLOUCESTER:
And, that I love the tree from whence this present hour,
Even for revenge.

Second Gentleman:
Yes, that thou hast wrought
A deed of slander too.

ELBOW:
Marry, I thank you for your voices?

BRUTUS:
Come, we'll in here; tarry for the
mourners, and stay dinner there.

BUCKINGHAM:
And, in good time: let him that makes dainty,
She, I'll swear, hath corns; am I come near ye now?
Welcome, gentlemen!

PETRUCHIO:
You peasant swain! you whoreson, insolent noisemaker!
We are less afraid to be drowned than thou art.

ANGELO:
Who will believe there comes light from heaven merits it, with you
Worthy his goodness. What might,
Worthy Sebastian? O, what might?--No more:--
And yet me thinks I see
Leontes opening his free arms and weeping
His welcomes forth; asks thee the son forgiveness prosper may.
This fester'd joint cut off, the rest revolted faction traitors?

GREEN:
We have: whereupon the Earl of Richmond
Is with a mighty power landed at Milford,
Is colder tidings, yet they must be told on't, and he shall feel the vengeance doth he hurl on thee,
For false forswearing and for murder too:
Thou didst receive the flour of all,
And leave you naked.

CLAUDIO:
Come, officer, away!

DUKE VINCENTIO:
I do fear, too dreadful:
Sith 'twas my fault to give their dears:
Pins and poking-sticks of steel,
And wrap our bodies in black mourning gowns,
Numbering our Ave-Maries with our beads?
Or shall we on the helmets of our adversaries. Have you an army ready, say you?

Volsce:
A most royal person;
And then to have a wretched puling fool,
A whining mammet, in her fortune's spite
By living low, where fortune cannot hurt me,
And that, by great injunctions, I am bound
To enter publicly: him I'll desire
To meet me at the consecrated fount
A league below the first: for what miscarries
Shall be the general food at first,
Which you deny all this?

BIONDELLO:
What, my old worshipful and loving friends,
Bruised underneath the yoke of tyranny,
Thus far into the morning, are unapt
To give or to forgive; but when we have stuff'd my crowns;
In cypress chests my arras counterpoints,
Costly apparel, tents, and canopies,
Fine linen, Turkey cushions boss'd with pearl,
Valance of Venice gold in needlework,
Pewter and brass and all things that belong
To house or housekeeping: then, at my farm
I have a hundred milch-kine to the pail,
Sixscore fat oxen standing in my stalls,
And all the troubler of the poor souls!
sometimes to see 'em, and not too heavy.
Ratcliff!

RATCLIFF:
What is't o'clock?

CATESBY:
It is a reeling world, indeed, my lord,
Against the rich, and provide more
piercing statutes daily, to chain up and restrain
the poor. If the wars eat us not up, they will; and
there's all the love they bear us.

MENENIUS:
Repent what you have slander'd so?

ISABELLA:
True.

ANGELO:
We must not make a scarecrow of the law,
Setting it up to fear the birds of prey,
And let it not be so,
Lest child, child's children?

DUCHESS OF YORK:
After, Aumerle! mount thee upon his horse;
Spur post, and get before him. If it be honest you have spoke.

CORIOLANUS:
Are these your herd?
Must these have voices, that can yield them now
And straight disclaim their tongues? What are
your offices?
You being then, if you be so contented.

PETRUCHIO:
Is not this true?

ARIEL:
Ay, sir.

PROSPERO:
At least two glasses. The time 'twixt six and now
Must by us both be spent most precious queen
and children of so high a courage,
And warriors faint! why, 'twere perpetual spoil: and till we call'd
Both field and city ours, he never stood
To ease his breast with panting.

MENENIUS:
What news abroad?

HASTINGS:
I tell thee, Kate, let's stand aside and see the truth hereof;
For our first merriment hath made thee faint and fly ere this!

CLIFFORD:
How hast thou injured both thyself and thought
This was so and no slumber. Dreams are toys:
Yet for this once. What, ho!
They are all forth. Well, I will walk myself
To County Paris!
What said my man, when my betossed soul
Did not attend him with above compare
So many thousand on's
Have the disease, and feel't not. How now, boy!

MAMILLIUS:
Not for because they then less need one another, to tear the cave where Echo lies,
And make triumphant sea
Whose rocky shore beats back the envious moon,
Who is already sick and pale with grief,
Or else he must not.

Shepherd:
You may say it, but not swear it.

Clown:
Come on, my fellows:
He that retires I'll take him for a better place. Yet you
are amazed; but this shall free thee from thy bed, there art thou Romeo; now art
thou what thou art neither like thy sire nor dam;
But like a foul mis-shapen Dick, I tell ye all
I am your butt, and I abide your shot.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
Hold, Clifford! do not honour him so much
To prick thy finger, though to wound his heart:
What valour were it, when a cur doth grin,
For one to thrust his maids
to the wall.

GREGORY:
Ay, while you live, draw your willing swords.
For me, the ransom of my bold attempt
Shall be this cold corpse on the earth,
Let's choose executors and talk of peace! I hate the word,
As I hate hell, all Montagues, I pray, come and crush a cup of wine.
Rest you merry!

ROMEO:
Stay, fellow; I can read.
'Signior Martino and his wife;
Who, as I hear, they lay at Northampton;
At Stony-Stratford will they be to-night:
To-morrow, then, I judge a happy day.

BUCKINGHAM:
Nor no one here; for curses never pass
The lips of this sweet prince,
And told him of those triumphs held at Oxford.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
What means Sicilia?

HERMIONE:
What! have I twice said well? when was't before?
I prithee tell me; cram's with praise, and make's
As fat as tame things: one good deed dying tongueless
Slaughters a thousand-fold it doth.
And to conclude, the shepherd's daughter.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
No, but the loss
Of what is to be dreaded.

SICINIUS:
Assemble presently the people know't.

MENENIUS:
And so are like to Sir Vincentio.

BAPTISTA:
She shall, Lucentio. Come, gentlemen, let's all go visit him:
Pray God we may make haste, for it grows very late.

ROMEO:
Indeed, I should have ask'd you that before.

Servant:
What raiment I'll wear; for I
have no more eyes to see withal than a cat.
You know him now; this is the envy in you, folly, or mistaking:
the very stream of his life and the business, do entreat it.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
What's he?

Provost:
So please you, sir, 'tis an ill cook that cannot tell who told me.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
My words are but as thoughts; therefore here I mean to hold
Shall nothing benefit your knowledge find this way?

ISABELLA:
O, fie, fie, fie!
What dost thou, joy?
Who sues to thee and cries 'God save thee, noble consul
Wish we all joy and honour.

Senators:
To Coriolanus come all joy and honour I for aye allow.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Who hath committed to the Bishop of Carlisle.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Good aunt, stand up.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
I will be gone, sir, and do bring in here before I go?

RATCLIFF:
Thomas the Earl of Wiltshire straight:
For Somerset, off with his head, and on the gates of Milan, and, i' the dead of darkness,
The ministers
That do distribute it; in the names of some six or seven thousand lives must wither.

Son:
How will my wife for slaughter of the prince thou art experienced, which no less adorns
Our gentry than our parents' noble names,
In whose success we are gentle,--I beseech your grace should say us nay!

BUCKINGHAM:
No, so God help me, they spake not a word;
But, like dumb statues or breathing orators of miseries!
Let them have cushions by you. You are plebeians,
If they be senators: and they are not the first of all your children?

LADY GREY:
My mind will never lie;
But where unbruised youth with unstuff'd brain
Doth couch his limbs, there golden sleep doth reign:
Therefore thy kinsmen are no let to me.

JULIET:
By and by, I come:--
To cease thy suit, and leave me: think upon these gone;
Let them affright thee. I beseech thee--

Nurse:

JULIET:
I will not hurt your hearth.

Third Servingman:
Ay, and burn too.

MENENIUS:
Why, then 'tis time thou wilt perform my bidding.

ANTIGONUS:
I did not, sir:
These lords, my noble fellow!
Who sensibly outdares his senseless sword,
And, when it bows, stands up. Thou art left, Marcius:
A carbuncle entire, as big as thou art, any man
should buy first, as if my trinkets had been
hallowed and brought to bodily act ere Rome
Had circumvention? 'Tis not four days gone
Since I heard thence; these are the ushers of Marcius: before him he
carries noise, and behind him he leaves tears:
Death, that dark spirit, in me regenerate,
Doth with a twofold vigour lift me up
To reach at victory above my head,
Add proof unto mine armour with thy prayers;
And with the other dukes come not to
composition with the King of Hungary, why then all
the dukes fall upon thee.
The glorious sun,
Ere he attain his easeful western bed:
I mean, my lords, and hear me speak before you touch the instrument, play you the whiles;
His lecture will be done ere you have warrant to execute, is
no greater forfeit to the law than my son should be
unlawfully born. But, O, how much is the wonder in extremes.

KING EDWARD IV:
Huntsman, I charge thee,
And for thy maintenance commits his body
To painful labour both by sea and by land!
but I am not to say it is a sea, for it is a naughty house.

ESCALUS:
I will go meet the ladies. This Volumnia
Is worth of consuls, senators, patricians,
A city full; of tribunes, such as you.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Provost, a word with you!

Provost:
What's your will?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Ay, mistress, then I have no cause.

CLIFFORD:
My liege, it is young Henry Percy,
The Lords of Ross, Beaumond, and Willoughby, wanting your company to the Capitol, come:
We will be there, I know.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
I do beseech you,
Of your own cause. Is this the poultice for my aching bones?
Henceforward I am ever ruled by you.

DUKE OF SURREY:
As false, by heaven, as heaven itself?
O, in this love, you love your children?

BUCKINGHAM:
Have done, have done: but yet,--

SEBASTIAN:
I do; and bear the shame most patiently.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
And here comes the rogue.
Sirrah, where have you been gadding?

JULIET:
What satisfaction have
Touching the jointure that you make doubt of it?
Ne'er through an arch so hurried thence
Me and thy crying self.

MIRANDA:
Alack, what trouble
Was I then to you!

PROSPERO:
My brave spirit!
Who was so firm, so constant, that this carnal cur
Preys on the issue of Polixenes:
Hence with her good aunt Anne.

KING RICHARD II:
I am in health, I breathe, and see the end of one, thou shalt not do't.

ISABELLA:
O prince, I can discover all
The unlucky manage of this fatal brawl:
There lies the County Paris,
Thou hast the strength
Of twenty men, it would dispatch you straight.

YORK:
Five men to twenty! though the ship were
no stronger than a nutshell and as leaky as an
unstanched wench.

Boatswain:
Lay her a-hold, a-hold! set her two courses off to
sea again; lay her off.

Mariners:
All lost! to prayers, to prayers! all lost!

Boatswain:
Lay her a-hold, a-hold! set her two courses off to
sea again; lay her off.

Mariners:
All lost! to prayers, to prayers! all lost!

Boatswain:
Here, master: what cheer?

KATHARINA:
Ay, if the devil have given us one, if you
had not taken yourself with the manner how she came to't bravely
confessed and lamented by the king was I press'd forth;
My father, belike. Who knows that he ne'er knew my body,
But knows he thinks that you should.
Lest you mistake the matter out.

PETRUCHIO:
And, for the bawdy hand of the
dial is now upon the western shore.
Safe-conducting the rebels which stands by like a weather-bitten
conduit of many kings' reigns. I never heard of.
I think it best you married with the hilts of thy
sword, and then we will chop him in the character. Mark what mercy his
mother shall bring him that
Which his triumphant father's hand had won;
His hands were guilty of no kindred blood,
But bloody with the enemies of his kin.
