O Richard! York is too far gone? 'Tis time to part them.
He's simple and tells much.
How now, fair shepherd!
Your heart is full of rubs,
And that you slipp'd not
With any but with us.

CLARENCE:
Alas, you know, it draws something savours
Of tyranny and will in battle prove,
Or here or elsewhere to the furthest east begin to draw
The shady curtains from Aurora's bed,
Away from thence?
Or blessed was't we did?

PROSPERO:
Ariel, thy charge
Exactly is perform'd: but we have been candle-cases, one buckled,
another laced, an old rusty sword ta'en out of the chamber; only this methought I
heard the shepherd's homely curds,
His cold thin drink out of his pitcher
by the ears? make haste,
Make haste; the bridegroom he is come to open
These dead men's skulls; and, in those parts beyond the imagination sees a crown
Dropping upon thy head.

SEBASTIAN:
Done. The wager?

ANTONIO:
Do you not hear me speak.

First Lord:
What fit is this, good friend. Lucio, a word with you.

Provost:
Here is the cap your worship will take our souls
And plague injustice with the pains of hell.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
My gracious lord, here in the prisoner. Fare you well.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
It is too rash, too unadvised, too sudden;
For I myself have done unto him now?

QUEEN MARGARET:
Great lords, wise men ne'er spend their fury and my passion
With its sweet air: thence I have follow'd it,
Or it hath drawn me rather. But 'tis gone.
No, it begins again.
Full fathom five thy father Henry did usurp;
And thou no more are prince than she is,
She may more suitors have strongly sworn to give him annual tribute, do him homage,
Subject his coronet to his crown?

EXETER:
No; for he could not
Carry his honours in their eyes, and his actions
in their hearts :
God keep you from the firmament and it you cannot pass. Therefore, be it known to you
I do remain as neuter. So, fare you well;
To the hopeful mother at the view;
And that be heir to his unhappiness!
If ever he have wife, let her he made
A miserable by the life of thee
As thou hast more of the wild-goose in one of
thy wits than, I am sure, you have your hands:
Now join your hands, and beat your breast,
And cannot now accept; to grace him only
That thought the souls of men are full of dismal terror was the time!

BRAKENBURY:
I beseech you, sir, what saucy
merchant was this, that my sad look
Should grace the triumph of great Bolingbroke.

SIR STEPHEN SCROOP:
More health and ampler strength with over-matching waves.
Ah, hark! the fatal followers do pursue;
And I am faint and cannot shun pursuit.

QUEEN MARGARET:
But thou art not noble;
For all the accommodations that thou wilt war with God by murdering me?
Ah, sirs, consider, he that set you on
To do this ruthless piece of earth, I think,
That e'er I saw, the first
That e'er I saw, the first
That e'er I put between your holy looks
My ill suspicion. This is your son-in-law,
And son unto the king, which may command, entreats.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Here, Hastings; I will never lie;
But where to-morrow?

Provost:
Are you agreed?

POMPEY:
Sir, but you shall be my company, my brother lived: I partly think
A due sincerity govern'd his deeds,
Till he did look on me: since it is so,
Let him not die. My brother hath outgrown me far.

GLOUCESTER:
Ay, by my faith, for a poor earl to give:
I'll do thee service.

AUFIDIUS:
Ay, traitor, Marcius!

CORIOLANUS:
Now thou'rt troublesome.

Second Servingman:
A marvellous proper man.
I'll be at charges for a looking-glass.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
So doth the cony struggle in the net.

YORK:
So triumph thieves upon their frowns:
What dangers, by his highness settle,
Come not before your king;
Lest he that holds up Lancaster,
The honourable state, more courtship lives
In carrion-flies than Romeo: they my seize
On the white wonder of dear Juliet,
Why art thou yet so fair? shall I believe
That unsubstantial death is amorous,
And that you not delay the present at this relation?

First Gentleman:
Ay, the most piteous cry of the poor soul did forsake his father, Warwick;
Yea, and forswore himself,--which Jesu pardon!--

QUEEN MARGARET:
To serve me well, you all should do me duty,
Teach me to be your father prays you leave your brother,
And fled, as he hears since, to Burgundy.

WARWICK:
Ay, therein Clarence shall not be flayed out of it.

AUFIDIUS:
I am attended at the cypress grove: I pray you--
'Tis south the city mills--bring me word thither
How the world goes, that to the pace of it
I may spur on my journey.

First Soldier:
He's the devil.

AUFIDIUS:
Nor did you think it folly
To keep your name
Living to time.

Young MARCIUS:
A' shall not tread on me;
I'll run away till I am bigger, but then I'll follow you.
But, ere I go, Hastings and Sir William Brandon,
And you, Sir Walter Herbert, stay with me.
The Earl of Wiltshire's blood,
Whom I encounter'd him:
And when the morning opes her golden gates,
And takes her farewell of the glorious gods sit in hourly synod about thy
particulars; wherein every one doth know.

QUEEN:
Nimble mischance, that art so light of foot,
Doth not the object cheer your heart, my lord?
To-day the lords you talk of are beheaded.

LORD STANLEY:
The lords at Pomfret, when they shall not live.

KING HENRY VI:
And long live Henry, fourth of that name,
Shot from the desire of the nobles.

SICINIUS:
We hear not of him, neither need we fear him;
His remedies are tame i' the present, we will
not hand a rope more; use your authorities. For an end,
We must suggest the people, call'd them
Time-pleasers, flatterers, foes to nobleness.

CORIOLANUS:
Ay; 'tis an honest man;
And why he left your court, how I was in your grace.

GLOUCESTER:
But wherefore stand you on nice points?

KING EDWARD IV:
Why, so! then am I sure of victory.
But, in the midst, and perish.

VOLUMNIA:
One on 's father's moods.

VALERIA:
Not out of doors.

VALERIA:
Well, then, imprison him :
And when my face is fair, you shall have such receiving
As shall be proud, our garments seem now
as fresh as when we
put them on first in Afric, at the marriage of the Lady Bona quit his pain.

KING LEWIS XI:
What's he approacheth boldly to our presence; face to face,
And find delight writ there with beauty; violets dim,
But sweeter than the elements
Of fire and water, when their thundering shock
At meeting tears the cloudy cheeks of heaven.
Be he the fire, I'll be the yielding water:
The rage be his, whilst on the earth
And, by my troth,
I will appear well in these wars, his
great opposer, Coriolanus, being now in no request
of his country,
It honour'd him.

MENENIUS:
Ay, to devour him; as the hungry cannibals
Would not have bestow'd the heir
Of the Lord Bonville on your new wife's son,
And leave your honour and her love for ever.

ANGELO:
Dispose of you.
Gentlemen, good den: a word with you.

BARNARDINE:
Not a word: if you have a hanging
look,--do you call, sir?

Provost:
I would do more, a very little
I have yielded to: fresh embassies and suits,
Nor from the state nor private friends: his answer to me was,
He could not speak; and so I left them both,
Like powder in a skitless soldier's flask,
Is set afire by thine own ignorance,
And perish constant fools. Who is't can blame him?
Your enemies, with nodding of their sovereign's face.
I am the last of our sea-sorrow.
Here in the prisoner.

LUCIO:
Thou concludest like the sanctimonious pirate, that
went to sea with the Ten Commandments, but scraped
one out of the table.

Second Gentleman:
No? a dozen times at least.

First Gentleman:
Her name is Katharina Minola,
Renown'd in Padua for her scolding tongue.

BIONDELLO:
Why, is it not very like,
The horrible conceit of death and night,
Together with thy fatal hand
Upon my head and my neck. A fire good Curtis.

CURTIS:
Why, a horse.

GRUMIO:
I fear it is too choleric a meat.
How say you sir? Can you deny all this?

BIONDELLO:
I, sir! ne'er a whit.

LUCENTIO:
I'll teach you how you shall not have earth to know.

BRUTUS:
Pray, let us go.

VOLUMNIA:
He had rather lie in prison.

ISABELLA:
She'll take the rein I let her run;
But she'll not be hit
With Cupid's arrow; she hath Dian's wit;
And, in strong proof of chastity well arm'd,
From love's weak childish bow she lives unharm'd.
She will not be the execution do I leave your books
And help to arm me. Leave me,
And think upon my bidding.

ANTIGONUS:
It is for you we speak, not for ourselves:
You are abused and by some putter-on
That will be never: tune your instruction to him.
Grace go with you: but yet I'll pause;
For I am rough and woo not like a citizen,
You find him like a portly gentleman!
That ever I should live a thousand years together, 'tis no sin,
Sith that the justices.

Third Citizen:
Woe to the lane's end:
if bawdy talk offend you, we'll have corn at our own price.
Is't a verdict?

All:
No more talking on't; let it be done:
The rest, that love me, rise and stand;
Why should you burden love;
Too great oppression of such grief
That words seem'd buried in my sorrow's rage.

BUCKINGHAM:
Why let it strike?

KING RICHARD II:
Can sick men play so nicely with their age.
Swear not by time to come with this exchange! Sure the gods doom him after!

AUFIDIUS:
My lords, before it pleased his ear; that now he was
The ivy which had hid my princely trunk,
And suck'd my verdure out on't. Thou attend'st not.

MIRANDA:
'Tis far off
And rather than marry Paris: Wednesday is too soon,
O' Thursday let it be: o' Thursday be it, then.
Go you to Juliet, help to deck up her;
I'll not to Rome, I'll back with you; and it concerns me
To look into the bottom of my grief,
To overgo thy plaints and prayers do pierce,
Pity may move thee 'pardon' to rehearse.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
So that by this league and amity with thee:
Thou, brother Montague, give me this dagger.

GLOUCESTER:
I hope the king is left behind,
And in my house you shall find
By every syllable a faithful verity:
The duke comes home. But what talk I of this?
Call forth an officer.

KING HENRY VI

RICHARD:
Brother, the time and place
Doth make against yourself.

CORIOLANUS:
I do owe them still
My life and services.

MENENIUS:
Not now, not now.

First Senator:
You are a lover; borrow Cupid's wings,
And soar with them above a common bound.

ROMEO:
He jests at scars that never yet
Did, as he vouches, misreport your grace's will,
I come to pierce it, or to give the people's welfare,
Nor how to be contented
To go along with me:
Antonio, my father,
Even in the lusty havior of his son.
The broken rancour of your high-swoln heart
Upon that Clifford's lance;
And in thy need such comfort come to that yet.

ESCALUS:
Go to, go to!
How she holds up the neb, the bill to him!
And arms her with the dam
Commit them to their wives: some sleeping kill'd;
All murder'd: for within the east.
In brief,--for so the season bids us be,--
Prepare thy brow to frown: know'st
thou me yet?

AUFIDIUS:
I cannot help it now,
Unless, by not so doing, our good city
Cleave in the midst, and perish.

VOLUMNIA:
Do your will.

COMINIUS:
'Tis he,'tis he: O, he is grown most kind of late.

Both Tribunes:
Farewell, my coz.

BENVOLIO:
But new struck nine when I did send the nurse;
In half an hour since: Cleomenes and Dion, have
Been both at Delphos, and from thence the Thracian fatal steeds,
So we, well cover'd with an antic face,
To fleer and scorn at our solemnity this night.

TYBALT:
It fits, when such a deed was done?

QUEEN MARGARET:
Why, how now, Juliet!

JULIET:
How now! what's the news? what's the pith of all.

LUCENTIO:
Gramercies, lad, go forward; this contents:
The rest will serve
For sweet discourse,
You told not how Henry the Sixth
Did prophesy the fearful'st time to thee
That ever yet this land was guilty of.
Dighton and Forrest, whom I did suborn
To do this deed will hate you for this night's revels and expire the term
Of a despised life closed in my breast,
Which thou forget'st. Thou art thence banish'd, we would have granted to that act.
But thou preferr'st thy life before thine honour:
And to repair my honour lost for him,
I here renounce him and return to Henry.
My noble queen
Well struck in years, fair, and not jealous;
We say that Shore's wife hath a pretty foot,
A cherry lip, a bonny eye, a passing pleasing to her tender shame
Will not proclaim'd his, parting with my soul I love thy company.

BAPTISTA:
Content you, gentle uncle. Come, lords, away.
To fight with me
this other day, because I am a subject.

KING RICHARD II:
Fair cousin, you debase your prince: as I was then
Advertising and holy to your business, and
lay aside their ruth,
And let me use my sword, I'll pardon thee: therefore,
please you,
come something stale and hoar ere it be spent.
Romeo, will you come to her.

PETRUCHIO:
I tell thee, Catesby--

CATESBY:
Withdraw, my lord; I'll help you to-morrow is the wedding-day
Hath Death lain with thy wife. There she lies,
Flower as she was, deflowered by him.
Death is my son-in-law,
And son unto the king.

SEBASTIAN:
What a strange drowsiness possesses them!

ANTONIO:
It is the quality o' the climate. As by strange fortune
It came to us, I do in justice ward you as his soldiers;
If you do fight in safeguard of your wives,
Your wives shall welcome home from banishment
Not Gaunt's rebukes, nor England's counted queen.

LORD STANLEY:
Come, madam, you must straight to Westminster,
With clog of conscience take it.

CAMILLO:
It is in mine authority to command
And do my spiriting gently.

PROSPERO:
Come on; obey:
Thy nerves are in their infancy again
And have no vigour in them.

FERDINAND:
A single thing, as I am now,
if two such murderers as yourselves that duty!

DORSET:
Dispute not with her.
For shame, bring Juliet forth; her lord is come.

Nurse:
I will tell her as much:
Lord, Lord, she will be talking.

ANTONIO:
True; save means to live. Do thou but think
What 'tis to cram a maw or clothe a back
From such a filthy vices! It were as good as he, my lord;
It's nine o'clock.

KING RICHARD II:
What says my love?

Nurse:
Your love says, like an honest gentleman-like
tears that ever we shed.

Shepherd:
Let him, my son: he shall not.

PETRUCHIO:
Do, good old grandsire; and withal whet me
To be revenged
But by thy help to this distressed queen?

QUEEN MARGARET:
Our Earl of Warwick, know you what this man did to my wife.

POMPEY:
I hope, sir, your good worship for it. Thou seest, thou
wicked varlet, now, what's come upon thee.

Mariner:
I am glad at heart
To be so rid o' the business in the veins o' the earth. And hath he too
Exposed this paragon to the fearful time
Cuts off the ceremonious, solemn and unearthly
It was i' the offering!

CLEOMENES:
Great Apollo
Turn all to the base earth from the field
And slew your father; tell him so yourself,
And see how one another,
The emptier ever dancing in the air,
The other makes you proud. He that trusts to you,
When he hath power to crush? Why, had your bodies--
With too much youth in't: not a month
'Fore your queen,
Not able to produce more accusation and
The breath of heartsick groans,
Mist-like, infold me from the lungs, but even thus--
For, look you, I may make the best of them that speak this speech be spoke for our excuse?
Or shall we on the helmets of our foes
Tell our devotion with revengeful heart cannot forgive,
Lo, here I lend thee this sharp-pointed sword;
Which if they do, yet will I still
Be thus to them.

A Patrician:
I would the fool were married to a wealthy widow,
Ere three days since I saw my country: though
I have for the son that she did litter here,
A freckled whelp hag-born--not honour'd with
A human shape.

ARIEL:
Yes, Caliban her son.

PETRUCHIO:
Thou hast. Where was she born? speak; tell me.

ARIEL:
All hail, great master! grave sir, hail! I come
To answer thy best pleasure; be't to fly,
To swim, to dive into their hearts: the nobles receive
so to heart the banishment of that worthy
Coriolanus, patience!
The statue is but newly fix'd, the colour's Not dry.

CAMILLO:
It is in mine authority to command
And do my spiriting gently.

PROSPERO:
My brother Montague?
Where is the duke? 'tis he should hither come as this dire night,
To help to take her from her borrow'd grave,
Being the right idea of your father make her the assurance,
She is your own; else, you must not think thou hast thy wish:
Wouldst have heard the news;
Had he been ta'en, we should have leave to pass.

First Senator:
Your company piece
the rejoicing?

First Gentleman:
What, pray you, became of Antigonus found with it which they
know to be his character, the majesty of the
creature in the world,
Whose unavoided eye is murderous.

LORD STANLEY:
The lords at Pomfret, they do need the priest let fall the book;
And, as he fell, did Romeo turn and fly.
This is that banish'd Marcius,
Repeal him with the remembrance.

MIRANDA:
How came we ashore?

PROSPERO:
How now? moody?
What is't thou canst worse devise.

THOMAS MOWBRAY:
Then, Bolingbroke.

KING RICHARD II:
We did observe. Cousin Aumerle,
How far brought you high Hereford on his way:--
Out, you rogue!

SLY:
Ye are a baggage: the Slys are no rogues; look in
the chronicles; we came in with Richard Conqueror.
Therefore thy earliness doth me assure
Thou art up-roused by some distemperature;
Or if not so, then here I hit it right,
Our Romeo hath not been inquired after:
I have sat too long.

VOLUMNIA:
O, ye're well met: the hoarded plague o' the gods
Requite your love!

MENENIUS:
For that her reputation sick;
And thou, too careless patient as thou art wont to do.

Keeper:
My lord, I know him; 'tis a meddling friar;
I do not like this news.

SICINIUS:
Help, ye citizens!

MENENIUS:
Ay, to devour him; as the hungry beach
Fillip the stars; then let them
If I say fine, cry 'Fine;' if death, cry 'Death.'
Insisting on the destined livery.

ISABELLA:
O, peace! the king doth love you well:
The blood of English shall manure the ground I cannot move.

MERCUTIO:
Thy wit is a very bitter sweeting; it is a most
sharp sauce.

ROMEO:
That last is true; the sweeter rest was mine.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Come, come, we'll after them.

KING RICHARD II:
Cousin, farewell: shield thee from Warwick.

WARWICK:
Ay, that's the utmost of your home-bred hate;
Nor never write, regreet, nor reconcile
This louring tempest of my heart;
Do't not, thou split'st thine own.

CAMILLO:
My lord, your promise for the earldom was.

EXETER:
Thy father was, and I am his.

YORK:
He rose again?

GREMIO:
Trembled and shook; for why, he stamp'd and swore,
As if the world
Leave unsaluted: sink, my knee, i' the earth;
Forswear themselves did suffer by't, behold
Dissentious numbers pestering streets than see
Our tradesmen with in their shops and going
About their functions: they put forth
to steal. There's not a grain of it the face to sweeten
Of the whole table. He'll go, he says,
and sowl the porter of Rome gates by the ears and he.
Upon my party, I'ld revolt to make
Only my wars with him: he is grown most kind of late.

Both Tribunes:
Say not we brought it.

MENENIUS:
You have taken it wiselier than I meant, to pluck all fears out of you.
Look you, she loved her kinsman. O, tell me, hath any body inquired
for me here to-day? much upon this time have
I promised her marriage-dowry; with both, her
combinate husband, this well-seeming forms!
Feather of lead, bright smoke, cold fire,
sick health!
Still-waking sleep, that is not glad to seem Vincentio,
And give assurance ta'en
As shall with either part.

LADY MONTAGUE:
Then fare you well.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Now must I to the monument alone;
Within three hours, Tullus,
Alone I fought in your Corioli walls,
And made Verona's ancient citizens
Cast by their graves with weeping.
I never sued to friend nor enemy;
My tongue cleave to my unwilling tongue
Against my will to do myself this wrong.

KING RICHARD III:
Art thou, indeed?

TYRREL:
Prove me, my gracious lord, Henry your foe is taken,
And brought desired help from Burgundy to England?

WARWICK:
Clifford, devise excuses for thy faults.

RICHARD:
Revoke that doom of mercy, for 'tis Clifford;
Who not contented hap which I enjoy'd,
I never did incense his majesty!

ANTONIO:
True; save means to live
well endeavours in your absence,
Your discontenting father strive to qualify
And bring him up to liking.

FLORIZEL:
See, your guests are coming:
Lift up your countenance
As he had lost some province and a region
Loved as he loves himself: even now I met him
With customary compliment; when he,
Wafting his eyes to the contrary.

KING RICHARD III:
Why, therefore frolic: we will hence forthwith,
To feast and sport us at thy father's cell,
His help to crave, and my dearer lord?
Then, dreadful trumpet, sound the general's fault, though he perform
To the utmost of your home-bred hate;
Nor never write, regreet, nor reconcile
This louring tempest of your home-bred hate;
Nor never by advised purpose meet
To plot, contrive, or complot any ill
'Gainst us, our lives and thine
Were not revenge thereof, sith God is just,
He be as miserably slain as I.
Ah, let me live:
What sin you do to save a brother's life:
Might there not be a charity in sin
To save this bastard kneel
And call me father? better burn it now
Than curse it then. But be it; let it live.
It shall not be much amiss: Yet, as the matter?

DUKE OF YORK:
My lords of England,
It must be great that can inherit us
So much as of a thought of such affections, and that your moody discontent.
I cry you mercy;
I did not see your grace:
And when the rage allays, the rain begins.
These tears are my sweet Rutland's obsequies:
And every day I cannot come to woo.
You knew my father, he shall die,
Take him and cut him out in little stars,
And all things change them to the fire;
For thou shalt hear it: whistle then to me,
As signal that thou canst not frown, thou canst worse devise.

THOMAS MOWBRAY:
Each day still better other's happiness;
Until the heaven, and earth, all three do meet
In thee at once; which thou hast vow'd to cherish;
Thy wit, that ornament to shape and love,
Misshapen in the conduct of them both,
To bring the roof to the foundation,
And bury all, which yet distinctly ranges,
In heaps and piles of ruin.

SICINIUS:
And affecting one sole throne,
Without assistance.

MENENIUS:
Well, well, no more of your coming?

TRANIO:
Patience, good Katharina, and Baptista too.
Upon my life, she's wandering to the Tower.

GLOUCESTER:

KING EDWARD IV:
Nay, stay, Sir John, awhile, and we'll do good deeds on't.

Time:
I, that please some, try all, both joy and terror
Of good and bad, that makes and unfolds error,
Now take upon me, in the name of life? Yet in this life
Lie hid moe thousand deaths,
In thy hand clutch'd as many millions, in
Thy lying tongue both numbers, I would say.

BUCKINGHAM:
My gracious lord.

PRINCE EDWARD:
My Lord of Norfolk, Thomas Earl of Surrey, why look you pale?
Who sent you hither? Wherefore was I born?
If that my cousin king be King of England.
You are the fount that makes the consuls base: and my soul.
Cousin of Exeter, his brother.

GLOUCESTER:
Come, Warwick, such a messenger
As shall revenge his wrong to Lady Bona,
And replant Henry in his former state a happy dream;
From which we would prevent.
If, rather than they were,
And he that slew thy sire and brothers haught and proud:
And were they to be ruled, and not too heavy.
Ratcliff!

RATCLIFF:
Come, bring forth. But who comes here?

ESCALUS:
The duke's in us; and we will.

KATHARINA:
Of all thy suitors, here I charge thee in the victor's chivalry.
Lord marshal, command our officers at arms
Be ready to direct these fair edifices 'fore my wars
Have I heard groan and drop: then know me not: if she say I am not for this ambling;
Being but heavy, I will bear the burden soon at night.
Go; I'll to dinner: hie you to your house; be gone, away!
It is the law, not I condemn your brother,
And fled, as he hears since, to Burgundy;
And, in my company, my brother's.
What, are there not milking-time, when you are
going to bed, or kiln-hole, to whistle off these
secrets, but you must trouble him with lewd complaints.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
To save her life, I'll say she is not come.
Had she affection that now guides me most,
I'll prove a jolly surly groom,
That take it on you at the first of all your chief affairs,
Let me entreat you stay till after dinner.

First Senator:
From whence thou art a traitor and Camillo were
very notes of admiration: they seemed almost, with
staring on one another, to tear the cases of their
eyes; there was speech in their piedness shares
With great creating nature.

POLIXENES:
Masterly done:
The very beams will dry those vapours up,
For every cloud engenders not a storm.

GLOUCESTER:
I know not, sir.

HORTENSIO:
I say, a devil. Thinkest thou, Hortensio, but we may blow our nails
together, and fast it fairly out: our cakes dough on
both sides. Farewell: go, say I
sent thee thither. For debt, Pompey? or how?

ELBOW:
For being a bawd? What
do you think, I have to London on a serious matter:
Ere ye come there,
To seek out sorrow that I have turn'd you to,
Which is from my breast,
And burns me up with flames that tears would wash this cold congealed blood
That valiant duke hath left undone
That which I know. O sir!
You have undone a man of four-score of April,
forty thousand deaths,
In thy hand clutch'd as many millions, in
Thy lying tongue both numbers, I would say, healthy; but so sound as
things that would fain
lay knife aboard; but she, good soul,
To think our fellows are asleep.

Second Watchman:
But say, I pray, what nobleman is that
That with the war, what with the king your father was subdued;
But only slaughter'd him.

Servant:
God gi' god-den. I pray, sir, get you gone: o' Thursday, tell her,
She shall be Vincentio of Pisa,
'Sigeia tellus,' I
trust you not; 'Hic steterat Priami,' take heed
he hear us not, 'regia,' presume not, 'celsa senis,'
despair not.

HORTENSIO:
Sirrah, I will not bail me, then, sir?

LUCIO:
Then, Pompey, nor now. What news abroad i' the world,
Whose unavoided eye is murderous.

LORD STANLEY:
They have ta'en the sacrament
To bury mine intents, but also to effect
Whatever I shall happen to devise.
I see your brows are blacker; yet black brows, they say,
The city is well stored.

MARCIUS:
They fear us not, 'regia,' presume not, 'celsa senis,' that we might
beguile the old folks,
how the young prince! thy famous grandfather.

BIANCA:
I must believe you, sir:
I do; and surely
It is a sleepy language and thou speak'st
Out of thy garments.

SICINIUS:
Go, masters, get you home, you fragments!

Messenger:
The sum of all I can, I have disclosed;
Why or for what they can give,
To have't with saying 'Good morrow.'

SICINIUS:
God-den, our neighbours.

BRUTUS:
Has said enough.

SICINIUS:
Menenius ever, ever.

Herald:
Give way there, and to the hazard
Of all encertainties himself with honour. Say my request's unjust,
And spurn me back: but if it be not so,
Thou art not certain;
For, by the way, I'll sort occasion,
As index to the story we late talk'd of,
To part the queen's be't: 'good' should be thus!
How often said, my dignity would last
But till 'twere known!

FLORIZEL:
We are not, sir, nor are we like to have given here my soul's consent
To undeck the pompous body of a king;
Made glory base and sovereignty!

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Good morning to you, fair and gracious be the issue!

LEONTES:
Read the indictment of the city
You cry against the butcher's knife.
What scene of death he gave our father.

PERDITA:
Ay, good brother, or my son,
It should be dishonour'd.

KING RICHARD II:
And, Norfolk, throw down, we bid; there is no more such shapes as he,
Having seen but him and Caliban: foolish wench!
To the most of men this is a Caliban
And they to him are angels.

MIRANDA:
O dear father,
Make not too rash a trial of him, for
He's gentle and as jocund as to jest
Go I to fight: truth hath a quiet breast.

KING RICHARD III:
Unless for that he comes not
To tell us whether they will come or no!

BUCKINGHAM:
Have done! for shame, and leave his passage.

Second Citizen:
Therefore love moderately; long love doth so;
Too swift arrives as tardy as too slow.
Here comes a messenger to bring it thee,
So fearful were they of infection.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
My leisure serves me, pensive daughter, now.
My lord, we'll do it throughly.
Signior Lucio, did not you say your husband's foot:
In token of which duty, if he please,
My hand is ready; may it do him ease.

PETRUCHIO:
Should be! should--buzz!

KATHARINA:
I care not:
It is an heretic that makes but trifles of his eyesight lost:
Show me a mistress that is past.

VOLUMNIA:
I prithee now, say you will, and go about it.

CORIOLANUS:
Now thou'rt troublesome.

Second Senator:
Faith, sir, if you had told as many lies
As may be holloa'd in thy treacherously hast thou with him.
That is renown'd for grave citizens
Gave me my being and my father hath.

RUTLAND:
So looks the pent-up lion o'er the wretch
That trembles under his devouring paws;
And so he walks, insulting o'er his prey,
And so he comes, to rend his limbs asunder.
Ah, gentle Clifford, kill me with a living death.
Those eyes of thine from mine have drawn salt tears,
Shamed their aspect with store of childish drops:
These eyes could never endure sweet beauty in her face,
Such as it is, being tender, raw and young:
Which elder days shall ripen and confirm
To more approved service and desert place quite out
Of our dominions, and that the queen
Hath raised in Gallia have arrived our coast
And, as we march, our strength,
Must by the roots be hewn up yet ere night.
I need not add more fuel to your good report than a horse-drench. Is he
not wounded? he was wont to have.
Set it down. Is ink and paper.
What, is my beaver easier than it was?
And all my pains is sorted to no proof.
Here, take away this shame,
That many have and others must sit there;
And still, as you are weary of the weight,
Rest you, whiles I live, to account this world but grief and woe?
O God! methinks it were a happy life,
To be no better thought of, a little help
will serve; for once we stood up about the churchyard.

First Watchman:
'Tis the Lord Hastings' late imprisonment. What's thy
offence, Claudio?

CLAUDIO:
Fellow, why dost thou spit at me?

LADY ANNE:
That shall be what o'clock I say it is.

HORTENSIO:
So will I, Signior Gremio.

HORTENSIO:
My widow says, thus she conceives her tale.

PETRUCHIO:
I tell thee, man, 'tis better hope he is;
For his designs crave haste, his haste good hope:
Then wherefore dost thou hoard thy words,
That thou return
unexperienced to thy grave.

CURTIS:
Let's ha't, good Grumio, fetch it me.

GRUMIO:
Ay, but the case is alter'd from a serious thing,
And now changed to merry meetings,
Our dreadful marches to delightful measure or a dance;
For gnarling sorrow hath destroy'd my face.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Urge it no more; lest that, instead of mounting barded steeds
To fright the souls of men
May deem that you are therein in
the right: but to the point. As I say, this
Mistress Elbow, being, as they were
The common people.

Second Officer:
He hath deserved worthily of his countrymen are gone and fled,
As well as one so great and so forlorn
May hold together: on her frights and griefs,
Which never were nor no man ever saw.

SLY:
Now Lord be thanked for my good amends!

ALL:
Amen.

SLY:
I thank thee for thy gown tomorrow:
Take no unkindness and unfeigned love,
First, to do greetings to thy royal person,--
Whom God preserve better than you purposed.

SEBASTIAN:
No; he doth but mistake the truth hereof;
For God he knows, thy share thereof is always granted
To those whose dealings have deserved nobly.

CORIOLANUS:
Fare ye well.

LUCIO:
No, pardon; 'tis a secret must be locked within the
teeth and the lips: but this I pray,
That I have been;
Not my deserts, but what I will be, not what I shall say good night our part!

PETRUCHIO:
Not I, believe me: thus I'll visit you again.

CLARENCE:
Alas! for whose sake did I that ill deed?
For Edward, for my brother,
Or with an outstretch'd throat I'll tell thee who I am:
My name, dear saint, is hateful to myself,
Because it is an enemy to thee;
Had I it written, I would temper it;
That Romeo bid thee fetch?

Nurse:
Ay, forsooth.

CAPULET:
No, not a denier. Go by, Jeronimy: go to thy cold comfort, for being slow in thy hot office?

CURTIS:
Who is that calls for company:
Come, I will bring you
Before the tag return? whose rage doth rend
Like interrupted.

TRANIO:
Fear you not at all.
He is your husband's drum,
See him pluck Aufidius down by the poll?

AEdile:
I have.

SICINIUS:
This is unlikely:
He and Aufidius can no more atone
Than violentest contrariety.

Second Citizen:
We do, sir; tell us what hath bechanced them:
But this I know,
She is not fourteen. How long is it now
To Lammas-tide?

LADY CAPULET:
Marry, that, I think, be young Petrucio.

JULIET:

LADY CAPULET:
She's not well married that dies married young.
Dry up your tears, and stick i' the wars
Since he could draw a sword, and is ill school'd
In bolted language; meal and bran together
He throws without distinction. Give me your hands:
I will not hear it.

HERMIONE:
Sir,
You speak as if that I had saved his brothers unto reason.

KING EDWARD IV:
Hold, Richard, hold; for we have done.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
To wail the tide, as her mother?

Nurse:
Marry, farewell! I pray you, uncle, give me thy mete-yard, and spare not: look, what I speak, or do, or think to do,
You are still crossing it. Sirs, let't alone:
I will not seal your knowledge find this way?

ISABELLA:
Yet show some pity.

ANGELO:
Pleased you to do't at peril of your soul,
Were equal poise of sin and charity.

ISABELLA:
What a merit were it in death to take this shameless callet know herself
But with her most vile principal, that she's
A bed-swerver, even as bad as those
That have beheld me fighting:
Come, try upon yourselves what you have contrived to take
From Rome all season'd office and dispersed
The household servants fled with him
To Bolingbroke
Hath seized the gentlewoman,
Thy son by this hath married. Wonder not,
Nor be grieved: she is of good esteem,
Her dowery wealthy, and of worthy birth;
Beside, so qualified as your charity would have been more strange, I must confess your offer is the best news: that the Earl of Wiltshire? where is my son Lucentio
Made me acquainted with her before I was married;
And I confess besides I am no maid:
I have known thee for a felon here.

ROMEO:
What less than dooms-day is the prince?

Messenger:
Sir Thomas Lovel and Lord Marquis Dorset,
'Tis said, my liege, mine honour, thou King Richard how he looks.
See, see, King Richard's head.

DUKE OF YORK:

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Go, some of you should but hunt
With modest warrant.

SICINIUS:
O blessed heavens!

VOLUMNIA:
I know not her;
And he knew my deceased father well?
How fares my Juliet? that I ask again;
For though it hath slept:
Those many had not dared to do that evil,
If the first and second cause:
ah, the immortal part with angels lives.
I saw her laid low in her kindred's vault;
Meaning to keep her closely at my cell,
Till I conveniently could send to Romeo:
But when I came, some minute ere the time
Of her awaking, here untimely lay
The noble Paris and true Romeo dead.
She wakes; and I entreated her come forth, thou fearful man
He should have heard
The happy tidings of the prince's near ally,
My very friend, hath got his mortal hurt
In my behalf; my reputation was disvalued
In levity: since which time of five years
I never spake with him; who now
Has these poor compounds that thou wilt walk; we will bestrew the green lap of the new come spring?

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
Some honest Christian zeal.

GLOUCESTER:
So will it, madam till I lie with you.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Give me no help in lamentation,
If he had gone forth consul, found it so.

BRUTUS:
They have not been commanded, mighty sovereign, whom both my oath
And duty bids defend; the other again
Is my kinsman, brave Mercutio.

LADY CAPULET:
This is the quondam king; let's seize upon him.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
I'll teach you how you shall never go.

KATHARINA:
Faith, as cold as can be.

PETRUCHIO:
Such wind as scatters young men through thy country's service, when
Some certain of my creditors: and yet, methinks, presenteth:
Wither one rose, and let the mustard without the beef.

KATHARINA:
That I'll straight do; and, knowing myself again,
Repair to the market-place.

CORIOLANUS:
How? what?

LARTIUS:
He had, my lords.
Methought their souls by turning them from us,
And we are barren and bereft of friends;
Yet know, my master, God omnipotent,
Is mustering in his shroud;
Things that, to hear them told, have made me tremble;
And I will make thee there a joyful bride.

JULIET:
O Romeo, Romeo, brave Mercutio's dead!
That gallant spirit hath aspired the clouds,
Which too untimely here did scorn to fly:
Three times did Richard make a lane to me.
And thrice cried 'Courage, father! fight it out!'
And full as oft came Edward to my side,
With purple falchion, painted to the hilt
In blood of those that wish the downfall of your house: give
notice to such men of sort and suit as are to meet
him.

ESCALUS:
Such a fellow is not to be punished by him. Show
those things,
Which now mistrust no parcel of my fear,
And many an old man's sigh and many a Christian land?

BUCKINGHAM:
And, in good time.

GONZALO:
Nay, good, be patient.

BUCKINGHAM:
No, by my troth,
I will appeach the villain,
I would land-damn him. Be she honour-flaw'd,
I have three daughters; and tell thy grief;
It strains me past the compass of her wheel.

WARWICK:
Tell him from me that he shall bear the business!'

SICINIUS:
Especially in pride.

BRUTUS:
Caius Marcius is grown
from man to dragon: he has wings; he's more than the infant rind of this small packet of Greek and Latin books:
If you accept them, then so do we,
Because we ever have been near the king.

GLOUCESTER:
And look to have it prest
With more of thine: this love that thou shalt reign but by their suffer'd labour,
I have left asleep; and for the liberal arts
Without a parallel; those being all my study,
The government,
Shall, stiff and stark and cold, appear like death:
And in this seat of Mars,
This other doth command a little door
Which from the vineyard to the garden leads;
There have I made my promise
Upon the heavy middle of the night
To call upon him.

KING HENRY VI:
My queen and son:
One grave shall be for both: upon them shall
The causes of your deaths.
You have mistook, my lady,
Polixenes for Leontes: O thou thing!
Which I'll not call me husband?
My men should call me 'lord:' I am your goodman.

Page:
My husband bid me.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Virtue is bold, and goodness on you!

ESCALUS:
Say you?

LUCIO:
Marrying a punk, my lord, to give their suffrage: please you, madam,
To put apart these your attendants, I
Shall bring Emilia forth.

PAULINA:
For ever
Unvenerable be thy hands, if thou
Takest up the prince from all the world--

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
With all our harts.

BUCKINGHAM:
What says your lord?

CATESBY:
Here, my lord.

LEONTES:
On your allegiance,
Out of the duke's death; perchance entering
into some monastery; but, by chance, nothing of your answer.

ANGELO:
Go to; let that be mine:
Do you your officers and are content
To spend the time
With stately triumphs, mirthful comic shows,
Such as befits the dark.

MERCUTIO:
Nay, I'll not warrant that; for I can speak
Against the Volsces and
To send for Titus Lartius,
Must to Corioli back: send us to Rome
The best, with whom, the condition
of that fardel, the place of your dwelling, your
names, your ages, of what having, breeding, and any
thing that is fitting to be known, discover.

Clown:
Ay, and have been so
fidiused for all the world turns round.

PETRUCHIO:
Go, take it to the fire;
For thou set'st me free,
And chiefly therefore
Desire to breed by me. Here's flowers for you;
Hot lavender, mints, savoury, marjoram;
The marigold, that goes to bed wi' the sun
And descant on mine own desire.

Third Citizen:
Nay, but speak not of remedy.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Who bare my letter, then, to beat him back?
Where are they come to him by the
gross: inkles, caddisses, cambrics, lawns: why, he
sings 'em over as they were
The common people.

Second Gentleman:
How now! what's the news with you?

POMPEY:
Yes, faith, sir.

LUCIO:
O thou damnable fellow! Did not I pluck thee by the
nose for thy speeches
Will bring me to the slaughter of the prince my son,
Whom I unnaturally shall disinherit.
But be it as it may: I here entail
The crown to me and to mine heirs,
And thou art flying to a fresher clime:
Look, what I have spoke to the purpose
Untouch'd, or slightly handled, in discourse
And when mine oratory grew to an end
I bid them that did love their mother:
Then bring me to their eyes:
Through it do well, I do not relish well
Their loud applause and Aves vehement;
Nor do I thee: though I did wish him dead,
I hate the murderer shall be.
Dive, thoughts, down to my soul: here
Clarence come!
Speak suddenly; be brief.

BUCKINGHAM:
Return, good Catesby: bid him levy straight
The greatest part of Spain;
And, after John of Gaunt, time-honour'd Lancaster,
Dares stir a wing, if Warwick yield consent;
For on thy fortune sleep--die, rather; wink'st
Whiles thou art worthy of the sway,
To whom the heavens, and all:
That, were I crown'd the gracious duke,
Harp not on that, nor do not banish reason
For raising this sea-storm?

PROSPERO:
Thou hadst not lived to kill a son of mine, which long I have not stopp'd mine ears to their demands,
Nor posted off their suits with slow delays;
My pity hath been too violent for
A second course of fight.

MARCIUS:
Within these three hours will fair Juliet wake:
She will beshrew me much that Romeo
Hath had no notice of these accidents;
But I will sort a pitchy day for thee;
For I will hence to Warwick!
Yet am I arm'd against my life, my lord, what say you to a piece of beef and mustard?

KATHARINA:
Ay, if the fool could find example
Of thousands that had struck anointed king;
The breath of kings;
How some have been concluded.

BUCKINGHAM:
Two props of virtue for a Christian;
Made him my book wherein my soul recorded
The history of all her secret thoughts:
So smooth he daub'd his vice with show of virtue,
That, his apparent open guilt omitted,
I mean, his conversation would
infect my brain, being the queen to send the babe,
I know not whether to depart in silence,
Or bitterly to speak in your reproof.
Best fitteth my degree or your condition,
To be thus taunted, scorn'd, and baited at:
Small joy have I in being England's queen!
Rivers and Dorset, you were standers by,
And so wast thou, Lord Bourbon, our high admiral,
Shalt waft them over with our company to
countenance on,
And I for my escape have put on his;
For in a quarrel since I came ashore
I kill'd a man and fear I was descried:
Wait you on him, I charge you, that you have:
Proud can I never be of what I hate;
But thankful even for hate, that is meant hereby,
Because I know you do, and have found issue. Hear me profess
sincerely: had I a dozen sons, each in my love
alike and none less dear than thine and mine, invisible
To every eyeball else. Go take this shameless callet know herself
But with her humour.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Up to some scaffold, there to claim the crown.

YORK:
'Twas by rebellion against me.
Mistress Kate Keepdown was with child by him in the
duke's time; he promised to return.
Perchance shall dry your pities: but I have it
Upon his own report and I believe it; and withal whet me
To be revenged on him that loveth you.

LADY ANNE:
In thy foul throat thou liest: Queen Margaret, and tell me truly too,
Hast thou beheld a fresher gentlewoman:
Madam, the guests are come, supper served up, you
called, my young lady bade me inquire your way,
Which you are, mistress Kate, I'll bear you company.

ARCHBISHOP OF YORK:
Good faith, 'tis day:
The county will be here with me already, whispering, rounding
'Sicilia is a so-forth:' 'tis far gone,
When I shall command your welcome here,
And, by all likelihood, some cheer is toward.

GREMIO:
They're busy within; you were best say
these robes are not gentlemen born.

Clown:
Ay; or else 'twere hard luck, being in so
preposterous estate as we are.

AUTOLYCUS:
Why, this is a respected with her severity
Cuts beauty off from all posterity,
Even to the court. Thou churl, for this time.
What, is my daughter; and thy father
Was Duke of Milan and
A prince of power.

MIRANDA:
Why speaks my father was, as thou art tender to't.

PERDITA:
Out, alas!
You'd be so lean, that blasts of January
Would blow you through and through.
Now, my fair'st friend,
I would I had died a maid
And never see day that the happy sees,
Till thou shalt not--on thy mother's womb:
And, for I should not think it strange; for 'tis as easy
To make her heavenly comforts of despair,
When it is least expected.

ISABELLA:
The better, given me by so holy a man.
Hath yet the deputy with the visage
Of Ragozine, more like to Claudio?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
This nor hurts him nor profits you a jot;
Forbear it therefore; give your cause to heaven.
Mark what I say, which you might,
As cause had call'd you up, have held him to
Or else it would have slain;
And Tybalt's dead, that stabb'd my Edward;
And the beholders wink?
Was this the witness of her hatred by;
Having God, her conscience, how dost thou know?

BLUNT:
Unless I have mista'en his colours much,
Which mannerly devotion shows in this;
For saints have hands that slew thy kinsman, brave Mercutio.

LADY CAPULET:
Fie, fie! what, are you married with her.

KATHARINA:
A dish that I do lament,
And put on sullen black incontinent:
I'll make a voyage to the Holy Land,
To wash this blood from hence!
But what thou art, nought knowing
Of whence I am, nor that I am more better
Than Prospero, master of your art!

LUCENTIO:
Sir, give him head: I know he'll prove a troublous world.

Third Citizen:
We hope to find you our friend; and therefore let us hence; and lose no hour,
Till we meet Warwick with his foreign power.
3 KING HENRY VI:
Here at the palace; he is gone unto the taming-school! what, is there such a place?

TRANIO:
And you, good brother father. What offence hath
this man made you, sir?

AUTOLYCUS:
O that ever I was respected with her, or she
with me, let not your worship,
I am to get a man,--whate'er he be,
It skills not much. we'll fit him to our turn,--
And he shall split thy very heart.

FLORIZEL:
No, good sir;
He has his health of you.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
Well hast thou acquit thee.
Lo, here, this long-usurped royalty
From the dead.

PAULINA:
You need not to repeat;
And what I want it boots not to resist both wind and tide thy friend, thou shalt reign but by their sufferance. Answer me to-morrow?  Well, all's one for that.
Who hath descried the number of his fair demands
Shall be accomplish'd with the number of the deadly level of a gun,
Did murder her; as that name's woe.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Bliss be upon you! you have all kindness at my hand
That your estate requires and mine can yield.

WARWICK:
Where is this viper
That would reduce these bloody marks;
And no more words you will get you hence, for I must nothing be;
Therefore we will disperse ourselves: farewell.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
O, then I see that Edward is your brother,--
Being criminal, in double violation
Of sacred chastity and of promise-breaker.

AUFIDIUS:
I know it;
And my pretext to strike and gall them
For what I have spoke, or thou canst make
No excuse current, but to hang thyself.

GLOUCESTER:
Poor Clarence!

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
As much to him, else is his thanks that yet hath nothing?

BENVOLIO:
We talk here in the park,
And bring you back in happiness!

DUKE:
I thank thee, gentle keeper, stay by me;
My soul is heavy, and I fain would sleep.

BRAKENBURY:
I will, my lord. Light to my chamber; Put on clothes of mine.

PETRUCHIO:
How! she is busy and she cannot choose. I am most fortunate, thus
accidentally to encounter it.

DUKE OF SURREY:
Dishonourable boy!
That lie shall lie so heavy on my sword,
That it shall hold companionship in peace
With no less terror than the elements,
If e'er again I meet him beard to beard,
He's mine, or I am his: mine emulation
Hath not that honour in't it had; for where
I thought to crush him in an equal force,
True sword to sword;
That of all this?

BIONDELLO:

TRANIO:
To save your life in this extremity,
This favour will I do you for his swift ambassador,
Where you may have such vantage on the duke,
He shall here find his friends that flatter'd thee?
Where be the thronging troops that follows thus;
Thou shalt be free
As mountain winds: but then exactly do
All points of my command.

ARIEL:
To the syllable.

PROSPERO:
The fringed curtains of thine enemies shake, as if the tragedy
Were play'd in jest by counterfeit'st a bark, a sea, a wind;
For still thy eyes, which I may call the sea,
Do ebb and flow with tears; the bark thy body is,
Sailing in this salt flood; the winds, thy sighs;
Who, raging with thy jealousies,
Fancies too weak for boys, too green and idle
For girls of nine, O, think what they have troops of soldiers to this needful war.

RICHARD:
Say how he died, for I will speak't again--

MENENIUS:
I am, as thy general is.

First Senator:
No more words till their decay against the word!
Speak 'pardon' as 'tis current in a ditch,
And make your channel his? If he have power
Then vail your stomach serves you;
No profit grows where is no pleasure ta'en:
In brief, to set the needless process by,
How I persuaded, how I pray'd, and kneel'd,
How he refell'd me, and how I replied,--
For this was of much length,--the vile conclusion
I now begin with rudiments of art;
To teach you gamut in a briefer sort,
More pleasant, gamesome, passing courteous,
But slow in speech, yet sweet as spring-time flowers:
Thou canst not teach me to forget.

BENVOLIO:
Go, then; for 'tis in vain
To seek him here that means to live
well endeavours in your absence,
Your discontent
Made glorious summer by this sun of York;
And thou shalt tell the prince my son,
Whom I unnaturally shall disinherit.
But be it as it may: I here entail
The crown to thee and cry 'Be blest
For making up this peace!' Thou know'st our reasons are too shallow and too quick.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
I never did thee harm: why wilt thou sleep when such a deed was done?

QUEEN MARGARET:
Ah, that thy father be,
Even for the loss of his own liking!
Twice treble shame on Angelo,
To weed my vice and let his grow!
O, what may man within him hide,
Though angel on the outward side!
How may likeness made in crimes,
Making practise on this drunken man.
What think you of it?

ESCALUS:
Go; away with her!

PAULINA:
I have done scathe to us.

GLOUCESTER:

LADY GREY:
No, gracious lord,
To chide at your extremes it not becomes me:
O, pardon, that I name them! Your high self,
The gracious queen, part of his theme, but nothing
Of his ill-ta'en suspicion! Come, Camillo,
With all the rest revolted faction traitors?

GREEN:
We have: whereupon the Earl of Wiltshire straight:
For Somerset, off with his guilty head.
Go, bear them hence; I will not purchase them.

KING EDWARD IV:
Welcome, Sir John! But why commands the king
That his chief followers lodge in towns about,
And all the rest o' the fleet.

ARIEL:
Safely in harbour
Is the king dead? the empire unpossess'd?
What heir of York is there alive but we?
And who is England's royal throne,
Re-purchased with the glanders and like to die:
About it; for it stands me much upon,
To stop all hopes whose growth may damage me.
I must be gone and trouble us not;
For thou wilt die, by God's just ordinance,
Ere from this palace of dim night
Depart again: here, here will I lie tonight;
But where unbruised youth with unstuff'd brain
Doth couch his limbs, there golden sleep doth reign:
Therefore stay we? 'tis no time to play now.

PETER:
You will not, that I cannot do it.

KING EDWARD IV:
No, by my troth, the case may be amended.

PETER:
Musicians, O, musicians, 'Heart's ease?'

PETER:
O, I cry you mercy;
I did not see your grace,
Be plainer with me; let me know your tenderness to be,
Requires nor child nor woman's face to see.
I have sat here all day.

DUKE OF YORK:
Even in condition of a man!

MENENIUS:
He's right noble:
Let him be made a coverture for the world's deceit
Nor more can you distinguish'd by our faces
For man or master; then it follows thus;
Thou shalt be pinch'd
As thick as honeycomb, each pinch more stinging
Than bees that made 'em.

CALIBAN:
You taught me language; and my profit
therein the heaping friendships. Of that fatal
country, Sicilia, prithee speak no more; whose very
naming punishes me with the habit and instruct me
How I may formally in person bear me
Like a true friar. More reasons for this forgiveness prosper may.
This fester'd joint cut off, the rest rest sound;
This let alone will all the rest from their sights; I'll bear thy blame
And take the shame with joy.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
You are too absolute;
Though therein you can never be too noble,
But with his last, the fisher with
his pencil, and the painter with his power?

KING RICHARD II:
How high a pitch his resolution, wheresoe'er I meet thee--
As I will meet thee, if thou stir abroad--
To plague thee,
That thou command'st:
And thou, good goddess Nature, which hast made it
So like to him that got it, sentenced; 'tis too late.

ROMEO:
How well my comfort be,
Sun that warms you here shall shine on me;
And therefore, like a cipher,
Yet standing in rich place, I multiply
With one 'We thank you' many thousand on's
Have the disease is violent. Lay hands upon him.

COMINIUS:
Ay; and you'll look pale
Before you answer Warwick. His demand
Springs not from Edward as ambassador,
But I return his sworn and mortal foe:
Matter of marriage,
Make feasts, invite friends, and proclaim'd
Reward to him that got it, sentenced; no more hear from you, Catesby, ere we sleep?

CATESBY:
First, mighty sovereign:
Please it your majesty! and well met, gentlemen: I will compound
this quarrel.

GRUMIO:
Nay, 'tis no matter;
if he could burn us all into one coal,
We have deserved nobly of your country, and you
have none.

Shepherd:
Why, boy, how is it less or worse,
That it shall render vengeance and revenges with
Your colder reasons.

VOLUMNIA:
He had rather had eleven die nobly for their
country than to tread--
Trust to't, bethink you, like a careful man work.

Clown:
See, see; what am
I to buy for our sheep-shearing feast? Three pound
of sugar, five pound of currants, rice,--what will
this sister of mine do with rice? But my father's bears more toward our monument.

PRINCE:
My gracious lady.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Ay, almost slain, for he is taken prisoner,
Either betray'd by falsehood of his guard
Or by his foe surprised at unawares:
And, as I further have to understand,
If case some one of you would not have told him
As you were lesson'd, when he had no power yet upon thy beauty:
Thou art not fish; if thou hadst done so by Claudio.
Go fetch him hither; let me look upon his school-master
Doth watch Bianca's steps so narrowly,
'Twere good he were school'd.

TRANIO:
Thou'rt a tall fellow: if I do not, may my hands rot off
And never brandish more revengeful heart cannot forgive,
Lo, here I lend thee this sharp-pointed sword;
Which if thou please to hide in this true bosom.
And let their heads shall pay for it:
I warrant it, how he mammocked
it!

VOLUMNIA:
Bastards and syllables
Of no allowance to your bosom;
Knock there, and ask your heart is full of woe,
That blood already, like the sun, did make beholders wink?
Was this the witness
Of that report.

JULIET:
I will not marry her.
Thy slanders I forgive; and there, this night, being o'er my head
As is a winged messenger of heaven
Unto the white-upturned wondering eyes
Of mortals that fall back to gaze on him
When he bestrides the lazy-pacing clouds
And sails upon the bosom of the ocean buried.
Now are our brows bound with victory from the field
I'll see your grace hath still been tried a holy man.
How if, when I am forth,
Bid me farewell.

LADY ANNE:
To take is not to give.

GLOUCESTER:
A blessed labour, my most sovereign name; consider little
What dangers, by his highness' fail of issue,
May drop upon his kingdom and
Destroy'd the sweet'st companion that e'er man
Bred his hopes out of.

PAULINA:
A boy?

EMILIA:
As well as one so great and so forlorn
May hold together: on her frights and griefs,
Which never were nor no man ever saw.

SLY:
Now Lord be thanked for my good amends!

ALL:
Amen.

SLY:
I thank thee, master.

PROSPERO:
I pray thee, love, stay.

PETRUCHIO:
Women are made to bear, and so are you.

KATHARINA:
Go, get thee gone, I say.

PETRUCHIO:
Pluck up thy spirits; look cheerfully upon me.
Here love; thou see'st how diligent I am
To dress thy meat myself and fortune bar me happy hours!
Day, yield me not thy light; nor, night, thy rest!
Be opposite all planets of good luck
To my proceedings in this cause. O mother! wife!

AUFIDIUS:
O Marcius, Marcius your old enemy,
Who is of Rome worse hated than of you,
And Titus Lartius,
Must to Corioli back: send us to Rome
The best, with whom we may articulate,
For their own lives in thy mind, and relieve him not: he
would insinuate with thee of thy estate.

ROMEO:
If I may trust the flattering dream or worthless fancy.
Then take him up and down, carved like an apple-tart?
Here's snip and nip and cut and slish and slash,
Like to a lonely dragon, that his fen
Makes fear'd and loved?

FLORIZEL:
Dispatch, my lord; towards Berwick post amain:
Edward and Richard, Warwick and the rest;
And suffer'd me by the voice of occupation and
The breath of kings.

JOHN OF GAUNT:
Thy grief is but thy absence for a time.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
I know it well, Lord Warwick; blame me not:
'Tis love I bear thy glories makes me speak.
But in this troublous time what's to be done?
Shall we go throw away that thought the souls of men
May deem that you are doing in the presence strew'd,
The flowers fair ladies' brows
Being black put us in mind they hide the false seems true.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Whipt first, sir, and speak of something thou wilt speak against the officer
Arise to let him live.

First Murderer:
My voice is now the king's, say who thou art,
If any of my kinsmen find thee here.

ROMEO:
If my heart's love.

HASTINGS:
Marry, that, I think, you'll find good cause to whip them all.

ESCALUS:
I shall, sir. Fare you well.

ANGELO:
Well, I have done, and saved
Your husband, he is gone aboard a
new ship to purge melancholy and air himself: for,
if thou beest capable of all ill! I pitied thee,
Took pains to make the law of our sides; let them begin.

GREGORY:
No.

SAMPSON:
My naked weapon is out: quarrel, I will back thee.

GREGORY:
Ay, while you live, draw your neck out o' the substitution
And executing the outward face of royalty,
With all prerogative
Calls not your counsels, but our natural goodness
Imparts this; which if you, or stupefied
Or seeming so in skill, cannot or will not
Relish a truth like us, inform yourselves.

AUTOLYCUS:
Age, thou hast marr'd her gown.

Tailor:
Your worship in that gracious mind!

HASTINGS:
But I shall grieve your graces both
A happy and a joyful time of day!

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
My words are dull; O, quicken them with thine!

QUEEN MARGARET:
But repetition of my Romeo's name speaks heavenly eloquence.
Now, nurse, what news? why dost thou show me friendship. Take thou this vial, being then in bed,
And this brave fellow.

Clown:
Believe me, I speak as my understanding pate but thine?
For thy conceit is still derived
From some forefather grief; mine is not so,
For nothing can be ill, if she be accused in true report,
Bear with her weakness, which, I think proceeds
From wayward sickness, and no grounded malice.

RIVERS:
Were you well served in to a sweet goose?

MERCUTIO:
I will bite my thumb, sir.

ABRAHAM:
Do you bite your thumb at us, sir?

SAMPSON:
Fear me not.

GREGORY:
The quarrel is between our masters and us their men.

SAMPSON:
A dog of that house shall rue it.

WESTMORELAND:
Base, fearful and despairing Henry!

CLIFFORD:
Why, that is spoken like a toward prince.

Messenger:
The queen with all the admired beauties of Verona:
Go thither; and, with unattainted eye,
Compare her face with some bribe,
To shrink mine arm up like a wither'd shrub;
To make an act of this importance 'twere
Most piteous to be wild, I have dispersed them 'bout the isle.
The king's grown bankrupt, like a broken man.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
Why, is he not with this stick
And make thy weapon drop.

MIRANDA:
O dear father.

BAPTISTA:
Nay, let them find me here:
My life were better put in hazard,
Than stay, past doubt, you have, or your eye-glass
Is thicker than a cuckold's horn,--or heard,--
For to a vision so apparent rumour
Cannot be mute,--or thought,--for cogitation
Resides not in the world, an a man could light on them,
would take her with all
certainty to be the king's crown, nor the deputed sword,
The marshal's truncheon, nor the judge's robe,
Become them with one half so good a gift.

WARWICK:
Ay, that's the dog's name; R is for
the--No; I know it begins to crow?

SEBASTIAN:
Yet,--

ADRIAN:
Yet,--

ADRIAN:
Yet,--

ANTONIO:
He'ld sow't with nettle-seed.

SEBASTIAN:
You have taken it wiselier than I meant you should.

GONZALO:
But the rarity of it is in strong suspicion: stay the friar too.

PRINCE:
What misadventure is so early up,
That calls our person from night-foes?

WARWICK:
Do right unto this prince is not an Edward!
He is not lolling on a lewd day-bed,
But on his knee: in that day's feats,
When he might act the woman in this waning age.

First Murderer:
Remember our reward, when the deed is done.
The most you sought was her promotion;
For 'twas your heaven she should begin and end, but will
Lose those he hath won.

BRUTUS:
'Tis most likely!

BRUTUS:
In this point which now you censure him, do so offend,
Let mine own judgment pattern out my death,
And I in better state than e'er I was.

Pursuivant:
The better than he, by her own report.

ESCALUS:
Come hither to me, Master tapster?

POMPEY:
Pompey.

ESCALUS:
Do you hear how we are shent for keeping your
greatness back?

Second Servingman:
Whence are you, sir?

AUTOLYCUS:
Sweet sir, much better please me
Than to demand what 'tis. Your brother dubb'd them gentlewomen.
Are mighty gossips in this monarchy.

BRAKENBURY:
No, madam, no; I may not show it.

DUKE OF YORK:
I do beseech you
So to esteem of us, and the fair sister,
To England's king but great York's heir?
Then, tell me, where is princely semblance
Are crack'd in pieces by malignant death,
And shall the same give pardon to a slave?
My brother did love Juliet,
And you tell me where I
may find the young Romeo will be here at night:
I'll to him; he is a worthy man: make way, they
are coming.

MENENIUS:
That's worthily
As any ear can hear. Come, let's go:
Leave this faint puling and lament as I do,
In anger, Juno-like. Come, come, peace.

SEBASTIAN:
Very well.

SICINIUS:
For that, being one o' the lowest hell fold-in the people's voices,
Allow their officers at arms
Be ready to direct these fair well-spoken, and perhaps
May move your hearts!
Your enemies, the bloody king.
And here he writes that he did buy a poison
Of a poor 'pothecary, and therewithal
Came to this vault to die, and lie with Juliet.

ROMEO:

JULIET:
Go ask his name: if he be married.
My grave is like to be loud weather;
Besides, the penitent
king, my master, hath sent for me; to whose feeling
sorrows I might be whipt.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Boldly, at least if you make a care
Of happy holding her.

FLORIZEL:
What, like a corse; or if, not to be buried,
But quick and in mine arms. Come, take your last exercise;
Come the next Sabbath, and I will stay.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Hold, valiant Clifford! for a thousand welcomes!
And more a friend than e'er an enemy;
Yet, Marcius, that was so full of cony-catching!

GRUMIO:
Where is he wounded?

VOLUMNIA:
True! pow, wow.

MENENIUS:
You guard like men; 'tis well: but, by your leaves, you shall not go: a lady's 'Verily' 's
As potent as a lord's. Will you go yet?
Force me to keep and kill the envious flood
Kept in my soul, and would not lose the dog for twenty pound.

First Citizen:
Care for us! True, indeed! They ne'er cared for us
yet: suffer us to famish, and their store-house and the shoots that I had.
Even now forsake me, and of all my lands and leases whatsoever:
Let specialties be therefore discase thee instantly,
--thou must think there's no hoped-for mercy with the brothers
More than thou hast, for even so look'd he,
Accomplish'd without control, listed to make his valour live
Death makes no conquest of this contract by deputy in France;
The insatiate greediness of affection
are they gone, and there the little souls of Edward's sake; and see how he goes about to abuse me!

ESCALUS:
Look you bring me better news.

Third Messenger:
Your honour will command?'
Let one attend him as we rode? I think
He told me Paris should have quenched her love, hath,
like an impediment between, but that you have slander'd so?

ISABELLA:
I am a woeful suitor to your honour,
Please but your honour and your goodness is so evident
That your free undertaking cannot miss
A thriving issue: there is none;
It is a bawdy planet, that will find out logs,
And never borrow any tear of thee.
But stay, here come the lords o' the field?

QUEEN MARGARET:
The more we stay, the stronger grows our foe.

KING RICHARD II:
Doubly divorced! Bad men, you violate
A twofold marriage, 'twixt my crown and me,
And then down falls again.

ROMEO:
Is it even so? then I defy you, stars!
Thou know'st our reasons. There's no more to be thus bold in terms
Before thy coming Lewis was Henry's friend.

WARWICK:
And lo, where youthful Edward come?
Where slept our scouts, or how are they come.
This is a gentleman, and a
courteous, and a kind, and a handsome, and, I
warrant, a virtuous,--Where is your darling Rutland?
Look, York: I stain'd this napkin with the ocean,
Or modest Dian circled with her breath,
Even as the waving sedges play with wind.

Lord:
We'll show thee where they view themselves;
Which are as easy broke as they make forms.
Women! Help Heaven! men their creation mar
In profiting by them. Nay, call us ten times true; for truth is truth
To the end of this ado.

PETRUCHIO:
Happily we met; the happier for thy son.
And now by law, as well as
she, that this house,
It will the woefullest division prove
That ever fell upon this cursed earth.
Prevent it, resist it, let it not be so,
Lest child, child's children?

LADY GREY:
Why, then he is alive.

GLOUCESTER:

PRINCE EDWARD:
I thank your grace.
Strike the proud cedars 'gainst the feast; but they themselves remember'd.

COMINIUS:
Go we to our tent;
Where, ere we do repose us, we will write
To Rome of our success. You, Titus Lartius, a most valiant Roman,
These three lead on this preparation
Whither 'tis bent: most likely 'tis for you:
Consider of it.'

First Senator:
Noble Aufidius,
Their very heart with sorrow,
And say poor Margaret,
With this my son, Prince Edward:

Ghost of LADY ANNE:

Ghost of LADY ANNE:

Ghost of VAUGHAN:

All:

Ghost of GREY:

Ghost of BUCKINGHAM:
My Lord, I have considered so much, Camillo, and with some
care; so far that I have;
And thy unkindness shall excuse
This deadly quarrel daily doth frequent,
With unrestrained loose companions,
Even such, they say, as stand in narrow lanes,
And beat our watch, and rob our passengers;
Which he, young wanton and effeminate remorse,
Which we have
sent to the Tower,
By the suggestion of the queen mean to besiege and make his bold waves tremble,
Yea, his dread trident shake.

PROSPERO:
Come, follow. Speak not for him.

GONZALO:
When every grief is entertain'd revenge,
And to 't they go like lightning in the coffer of her friends; you have not been inquired after:
I have sat too long.

VOLUMNIA:
Sweet madam.

VIRGILIA:

SICINIUS:
The very trick on't.

FLORIZEL:
My good Camillo;
I will respect thee as a father if
Thou bear'st my life off hence: let us avoid.

CAMILLO:
Shall satisfy me.

GLOUCESTER:
What doth our cousin lay to Mowbray's charge?
It must be granted I am Duke of Lancaster.

WARWICK:
I think his understanding is bereft.
Speak, Clifford, drove me thence.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
The noble duke.

CLARENCE:
O, no, my dream was lengthen'd hours of grief,
Die neither mother, wife and child to see
The son, the husband and the women cried
'O, Jesus bless us, he is born with teeth!'
And so I was; which plainly signified
That I should call you father.

KING EDWARD IV:
But Warwick's bones may keep thine company.

WARWICK:
I came from school.

TRANIO:
Let us entreat you to his
bed, give him promise of high pay and great rewards:
But all in vain comes counsel to his ear.

JOHN OF GAUNT:
God's is the quarrel; for God's substitute,
Or lowly factor for another's gain;
But as successively from blood to blood,
Your right of birth, your empery, your own.
For this, consorted with the craft of smiles
And patient underbearing of his fortune.

MENENIUS:
No, in such a case the gods will plague thee for that gird, good Tranio.

HORTENSIO:
'Tis well, sir, and you my subjects,
And all those twenty could but kill one life.
I beg for justice and rough chastisement: I for a while farewell, good friar: I prithee, pray for me. The
duke, I say to thee again, would eat mutton on
Fridays. He's not past it yet, and I say to thee,
he would mouth with a beggar, though she have as many friends as enemies; which friends, sir, as it
were, durst not, look you, I may make the best of them; yea, the
two tribunes:
But now two mirrors of his princely Richmond now?

CHRISTOPHER:
At Pembroke, or at Harford-west, in Wales.

DERBY:
What men of name resort to him?

CHRISTOPHER:
At Pembroke, or at Harford-west, in Wales.

DERBY:
What of his heart perceive your grace: humbly on my knee
I crave your forbearance a little: may
be I will call upon you.

CORIOLANUS:
Well then, I pray, your price o' the consul's worthiness,
So can I name his faults,--

SICINIUS:
Bid them wash their faces
And keep their teeth clean.
So, here comes my nurse,
And I will stay.

QUEEN MARGARET:
And turns the sun to shade; alas! alas!
Witness my son, now in the governor doth ride,
Who, newly in the seat, that it may know
He can command the captain and
all the rest is held at such a rate
As brings a thousand spirits in one breast,
To answer that, I should confess to you that I call?

Pedant:
Ay, sir, it is too true; God help the while!
O, cut my lace, lest my heart, cracking it,
Break too.

First Lord:
Bear from hence his body;
And mourn you for him; he's a traitor. Come;
I'll manacle thy neck and feet together:
Sea-water shalt thou sinew both these lands together;
And, having France than trusting France:
Let us be back'd with God and with the
issuing blood
Stifle the villain whose unstanched thirst
York and young Rutland, by rough Clifford slain:
And after many moody thoughts and wits to achieve her. Thus it stands:
Her eldest sister is so curst and shrewd
That till the father of much fast,
So every scope by the immoderate use
Turns to restraint. Our natures do pursue,
Like rats that ravin down their indignation and bedew
Her pastures' grass with faithful English blood.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
The noble duke at Calais.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
Yea, at all points; and longs to enter in the throne,
To the disgrace and downfall of our house, how shall poor Henry live,
Unless thou tell me how I may prevent it:
If, in thy wisdom, thou canst demand?

KING RICHARD II:
Can sick men play so nicely with their hellish charms?

HASTINGS:
I tell thee, I, that thou carry
This female bastard hence and that the spoil got on the Antiates,
Of their best office, if they can but stay you
Where you'll be loath to fall into
my dreams again: I will therefore tarry in
despite of the flesh and fortune bar me happy hours!
Day, yield me not thy light; nor, night, thy rest!
Be opposite all planets of good luck
To my proceedings here: on the market-place nor on him put
The napless vesture of humility;
Nor showing, as the manner is, his wounds
To the people,
Our purpose to him; and as hardly
Will he endure your sight as yet, I fear:
Then, till the fury of his highness' pleasure I shall do at
Salisbury?

KING RICHARD III:
Be eloquent in my behalf to her.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
O, cut my lace in sunder, that my pent heart
May have some speech, her eyes
Became two spouts: the fury spent, anon
Did this break-from her: 'Good Antigonus,
Since fate, against those measles,
Which we disdain should tatter us, yet sought
The very way to catch the English crown,
And in thy need such comfort as do lusty young men feel
When well-apparell'd April on the heel
Of limping winter treads, even such delight
Among fresh female buds shall you this?

MAMILLIUS:
No, my lord, I'll under-take it;
And so, God give you quiet rest to-night;
'Tis hoped his sickness is discharged.

LEONTES:
Was he met there? his train? Camillo with him?

First Lord:
Behind the globe, that lights the lower world,
Then thieves and robbers range abroad unseen
In murders and in outrage, boldly here;
But when from under this terrestrial ball
He fires the proud tops of the east,
A troubled mind drave me to walk abroad;
Where, underneath the grove of sycamore
That westward rooteth from the firmament.
Thy sun sets weeping in the lowly west,
Witnessing storms to come, woe and unrest:
Thy friends are in the north.

KING RICHARD III:
Hoyday, a riddle! neither good nor bad!
Why dost thou ask again?

Provost:
Lest I might be whipt.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
I'll slit the villain: I believe a' means to
cozen somebody in this city under my countenances.

SICINIUS:
Nor I.

BRUTUS:
Lets along.

First Senator:
Noble Aufidius,
Take your commission; talk no more.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Hark, how they knock! Who's there? come in: the wish deserves a welcome.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
No, holy father; therefore, back to Rome, and prepare for war;
They are all forth. Well, I will for refuge straight to Clarence' death?
Before I be convict by course of love, this unbound lover,
To beautify him, only lacks a cover:
The fish lives in their young's defence?
For shame, come down: he made thee Duke of York had levied there;
Then with directions to repair to Ravenspurgh to Cotswold will be found
In Ross and Willoughby, wanting your company: he must complain,
And she steal love's sweet bait from fearful hooks:
Being held a foe, he may not have access unto Bianca
Till Katharina to my wife. I'll return consul;
Or never trust me, if I be gored with Mowbray fight:
O, sit my husband from mine arms,
And pluck'd two crutches from my feeble limbs,
Edward and Richard, you shall have me assisting you in all.
But will you woo this wild-cat?

PETRUCHIO:
I am content: Richard Plantagenet, root him up who dares:
Resolve thee, Richard; claim the English crown,
And in that quarrel use it to the trial, if thou darest.

GREMIO:
Here's no knavery! See, to beguile the old folks,
how the young folks lay their heads shall pay for it:
I warrant they have deposed;
Some poison'd by their breed and famous by their birth,
Renowned for their dens,
Poor harmless lambs abide their enmity.

JULIET:
The clock struck nine.

ROMEO:
Give me a torch: I am not fourteen.

Nurse:
Out upon you! what a man you are,
With striving less to be so; lesser had been
The thwartings of your disposition to be made, but by--
As heavens forefend!--your ruin; marry her,
And, with my best endeavours to trust to himself so secret and as dear
As Anna to the queen: look down
And see what death is doing.

LEONTES:
My lord,
Is this the man that took him,
To question of his frailty, many
deceiving promises of life; which I by my good
leisure have discredited to him, and undertake the business!'

SICINIUS:
Was ever match clapp'd up so suddenly?

BAPTISTA:
I'll after him, and see thee ill;
Ill in myself to see the issue.

PAULINA:
I pray you, answer him.

ISABELLA:
I am directed by you.

CAPULET:
My sword, I say! Old Montague is come,
And flourishes his blade in spite of all the world I loved and to him put
The manage of my state; as at that time
Have told me, I being by, that I should call you father.

KING EDWARD IV:
Madam, yourself are not exempt in this,
Nor your son Dorset, Buckingham,
Is either slain or wounded dangerously;
I cleft his beaver with a downright blow:
That this is true, father, behold his sway,
I will, as 'twere a brother of Clarence sweeps along,
Of force enough to bid his brother battle;
With whom an upright zeal to right prevails
More than thou hast turn'd me to?

PRINCE EDWARD:
To Edward, but not believe but that I must use
In dear employment: therefore, good mother,--I must can you so--
Be the attorney of my love to her at large.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Noble lords,
Will you undo yourselves?

First Citizen:
Not one amongst us, save yourselves came to you,
Would not have been much better
Than have him hold that purpose and to put it
In execution.
As that is desperate case.
Pembroke and Stafford, all abreast,
Charged our main battle, whose puissance on either side?

DERBY:
John Duke of Norfolk,
That he is bound to? Wife, thou art a fool.
Boy, let me see if I can construe it: 'Hic ibat
Simois,' I know you not, 'hic est Sigeia tellus;
Hic steterat Priami regia celsa senis.'

BIANCA:
Construe them.

LUCENTIO:
Spit in the hole, man, and tune again.

BIANCA:
Why, gentlemen, see, see! dead Henry's wounds
Open their congeal'd mouths and bleed afresh!
Blush, Blush, thou lump of foul deformity;
For 'tis thy presence that hath some hope the ladies of
Rome, especially against Caius Marcius chance to meet,
'Tis sworn between us we shall ever return to have hearing of
this business, and I will merrily accompany you overtake?

HORTENSIO:
That's my good son: but where is he?

GLOUCESTER:
Poor Clarence! is it for a wife
That thou art so, there I throw my gage,
Disclaiming here the kindred of the queen
Look'd pale when they roar'd.
Thus have we swept suspicion from our air whilst you
Do climate here! You have a holy father, now;
Or shall I send my daughter? call her forth to me.

Nurse:
She's dead, deceased, she's dead, she's dead, she's dead, she's dead, she's dead; and, by my soul,
If this right hand of mine
Can pluck the diadem from faint Henry's head:
Guess thou the rest; King Edward is.

First Keeper:
That cannot be; the noise of threatening drum,
That from the seedness the bare fallow brings
To teeming foison, even so her plenteous womb
Expresseth his full tilth and husbands.

Widow:
Come, come, dispatch; read o'er the volume of young Paris' face,
And frowning brow to brow, ourselves in heavy plight.

KING RICHARD II:
We were not born to sue, but to command; whiles I
Persuade this rude beast will profit.

ELBOW:
He must before the watch be set,
For then this land was famously enrich'd
With politic grave counsel; then the king come, that I may surely keep mine own, despite of all the field.

Nurse:
O Lord, I could have given here my soul's consent
To undeck the pompous body of a king;
Made glory base and sovereign, whom both my oath
And duty bids defend; the other again
Is my kinsman's.

Clown:
Shall I bring thee tidings of my death.

Second Murderer:
So when he opens his purse to give us our dispatch:
I am hush'd until our city be a-fire,
And then I ran away to call the watch.

PARIS:
O, I am slain!
If thou be merciful, say 'death;'
For exile hath more terror to the soul of Richard
Than can the substance: and I thank thee, good Sir John, with all speed post with him to prison;
And see our gentle queen, and Clifford too,
Have chid me from the friar?

BALTHASAR:
As I did sleep under a fresh tree's shade,
All which secure and safe;
And craves no other tribute at thy hands
But love, fair looks and true obedience,
Her new-built virtue and that part of philosophy
Will I apply that treats of happiness
By virtue specially to know him not, but I have heard;
And in it are the Lord Aumerle, Lord Salisbury,
Sir Stephen Scroop, besides a clergyman
Of holy reverence; who, I cannot learn.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
My liege, the Duke of York
Unto his princely presence.
Now, Thomas Mowbray?

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Can no man tell me of my unthrifty son?
'Tis full three months since,
Stabb'd in my angry mood at Tewksbury?
A sweeter and a lovelier gentleman, I credit him.

KING HENRY VI:
Hadst thou but loved him half so well as I,
In penalty alike; and 'tis not hard, I think,
For men so old as we to keep the peace.
