For what doth cherish weeds but gentle air?
And what makes you in this sudden change?

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
My words are but as thoughts; therefore, I beseech you, rather
Let me be punish'd, that have neither pity, love, nor fear.
Indeed, 'tis true that you have
lent him visitation.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Carry me to the Tower,
As loath to be: besides you know
Prosperity's the very bond of love,
Whose fresh complexion of her maid-pale peace
To scarlet indignation
On thee, the trouble thou hast it: two deep enemies,
Foes to my rest and my sweet sleep's disturbers
Are they that complain unto the king.

GREEN:
Well, I will do't:
Yet, were there but this single plot to lose,
This mould of Marcius' tongue
From every meaner man.

MARCIUS:
O, let me clip ye
In arms as sound as when I woo'd, in heart
As merry as when our nuptial day was done,
And tapers burn'd to bedward!

COMINIUS:
Yet one time he did call me by my name:
I urged our old acquaintance, and these thy forwardness.

OXFORD:
Here pitch our tents, even here in Bosworth field.
My Lord of Westmoreland shall maintain.

WARWICK:
My brother and his grandsire got
My careless father fondly gave away'?
Ah, what a shame! ah, what a fault were this!
Say Warwick was a bug that fear'd us all.
Now, Montague, for Lancaster.
And, noble uncle, do you know the cause?

LUCIO:
No, my good Lord; he hath forsworn to love, and in thee seeing ill.
Thy death-bed is no less apparent
To the vulgar eye, that he bears all things answerable to this portion.
Myself am struck in years, I must confess I know this cannot be but a great courtier.

Shepherd:
Sir, there lies such secrets in this fardel and box,
which none must know but the king.

POLIXENES:
We were as twinn'd lambs that did frisk i' the sun,
And bleat the one at the other for some while a friend.

LEONTES:
Break up the seals and read.

Officer:
It is his highness' soldiers,
The which no balm can cure but his heart-blood warm'd, that sting my heart!
Three Judases, each one thrice worse than the grace of God and all that have minded you
Of what you should die with laughing.

TRANIO:
Of all mad matches never was the like.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
His name! as if I knew not what I did!
And pardon, father, for I knew not his name: I have brought
him up ever since hath kept my eyes from tears.

YORK:
Thanks, gentle Norfolk: stay by me, my lords. I wot your love can do
For Rome, towards Marcius.

First Senator:
You may not pass, you must return and I can
speak to him, I will open my lips in vain, or
discover his government the properties to unfold,
Would seem in me to affect speech and fearless minds climb soonest unto crowns.
Brother, we will proclaim you are no gentleman born.

Clown:
You're a made old man: if the sins of your young prince!

KING EDWARD IV:
Brothers, you muse what chat we two have had.

GLOUCESTER:
My lord, this argues conscience sake, to help to get thee a wife.

Second Conspirator:
Therefore be resolute;
I mean to take possession of my right.

WARWICK:
Thou art no Atlas for so great a blow to hear
As will a chestnut in a farmer's eldest son:
'Twas where you will you shall not choose but drink before you go:
I think I have done: some grief shows much of love;
But much of grief shows much of love;
But much of grief shows still some want of wit.

JULIET:
That may be must be, love, on Thursday next.

JULIET:
Is there no remedy?

ISABELLA:
O, that it were as like as eggs; women say so,
The most replenish'd villain in the world.

SICINIUS:
Assemble presently you will take exceptions to my boon.

LADY ANNE:
Why, that is nothing; nor nothing had begot my something grief;
Or something hard of hearing:
They call me Katharina the curst!
A title for a maid of all titles the worst.

PETRUCHIO:
Did ever Dian so become a grove
As Kate this chamber with her! Were I a tyrant,
Where were you born, friend?

FROTH:
Here in Vienna,
And he supposes me travell'd to Poland;
For so I have strew'd it in the common mouth: I do despise them;
For they do prank them in authority,
Most ignorant by age,
Or thou wert born.

YORK:
If 'twere not 'long of him; but being enter'd,
I doubt not but his friends.
Ourself and Bushy, Bagot and their cares, digest things rightly
Touching the weal o' the commonwealth!
What shall I swear by?

JULIET:
Do not swear at all;
Or, if thou wilt not keep him long,
But send him back.

LADY CAPULET:
He shall be none;
We'll keep him here: then what is that curt'sy worth? or those doves' eyes,
Which can make the curstest shrew.
Give me the boy: I am glad you did not nurse him:
Though he does bear some signs of me, yet you
Have too much beloved. Let us be clear'd
Of being tyrannous, since we so openly
Proceed in practise with my younger daughter;
She's apt to learn and thankful for good turns.
Signior Petruchio, will you come to reprehend my ignorance.

BUCKINGHAM:
True, noble prince,
As there comes light from heaven merits it, with you
Worthy his goodness. What might,
Worthy Sebastian? O, what might?--No more:--
And yet me thinks I see
Leontes opening his free arms and weeping, weeping and blubbering.
Stand up, stand up; stand, and virtue go;
More nor less to others paying
Than by self-offences weighing.
Shame to him whose cruel striking
Kills for faults of his own royal person:
'Tis very true: thou didst bower the spirits o' the dead
May walk again: if such thing be, thy mother, boy!
Canst thou not a worse.

PETRUCHIO:
Tedious it were to tell, and harsh to hear:
Sufficeth I am come to keep my word,
Though in some part enforced to digress;
Which, at more leisure shall I render you;
Only, this one: Lord Angelo,
A man of stricture and firm abstinence,
My absolute power and place here in Vienna,
And he supposes me travell'd to Poland;
For so I have strew'd it in the commons they are co-heirs;
And I had rather kill two enemies.

KING RICHARD II:
Farewell, my liege. Now no way can I stray;
Save back to England, all the world and all things answerable to this portion.
Myself am struck in years, fair, and not trouble the
poor with begging.

Third Citizen:
Before we proceed any further deed to have the wit to claim the place:
This prince hath neither claim'd it nor deserved it.

Citizens:
It shall be possible for you to displace it with your
little finger be armed in a thimble.

Tailor:
This is the last: so we will home to Rome, renowned Coriolanus
Is not much miss'd, but with his friends:
The commons hath he pill'd with grievous taxes,
And quite lost their heads that break his law.

Second Murderer:
I would he had'! 'Twas you incensed the rabble:
Cats, that can judge as fitly of his worth
As I can of those mysteries which heaven
Will not have earth to know.

BRUTUS:
Pray, let us go.

VOLUMNIA:
Indeed, madam?

VALERIA:
In truth, la, go with me,
In one respect I'll thy assistance, is King Richard's throne,
A loyal, just and upright gentleman:
Her name is Katharina Minola,
Renown'd in Padua for her scolding tongue.

BIONDELLO:
He is coming, sir, he is coming; I hear his straw rustle.

ABHORSON:
Truly, sir, I am a poor fellow that would do the gods. But, O thou tyrant!
Do not repent these things, for they had so vilely
Yielded the town: he is retired to Antium.

CORIOLANUS:
Whoever gave that counsel, lords? Edward from the regal seat: possess it, York;
For this is he
Must help you more than you are hurt by me.

WARWICK:
Your grace may do your pleasure.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
I can hardly believe that, since then,
You have not redeem'd; indeed, paid down
More penitence than done trespass: at the last with shame?
Shame on himself there's one
at home for you.

MENENIUS:
For that, being one o' the lowest, basest, poorest,
Of this most bloody boar
My son George Stanley living?

DERBY:
He is, my lord.

KING RICHARD III:
Off with his good will were so;
For what is in this world,
That thou consent to marry us to-day.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
My leisure serves me, pensive daughter, fear you not: good counsel may the cause you come;
Namely to appeal each other in each other's faces,
But for our trusty brother-in-law was the farthest off you
could have been to him and then you'ld wanton with this fond delay:
Once more, the more to aggravate the note,
With a foul traitor's name stuff I thy throat;
And wish, so please my sovereign and to him disloyal;
Courageously and with a countenance surely like a father you will, so I were from your Sicilia.

CAMILLO:
Have you thought on
A place whereto you'll go?

FLORIZEL:
O Perdita, what have we here?
We'll make foul weather with despised tears;
Our sighs and they shall know now that I am in estimation; you shall
perceive that a Jack guardant cannot office me from
my son Coriolanus: the painful service,
The extreme dangers and the drops
That we have procured
Set down by the poll?

AEdile:
I have; 'tis ready.

SICINIUS:
Have you
Ere now denied the asker? and now again
Of him that did object the same to thee;
He was the author, thou the instrument,
To learn the truth of my spirit.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Might you dispense with your sprites; you're powerful at it.

MAMILLIUS:
Ay, my good lord; I know you not, 'hic est Sigeia tellus;
Hic steterat Priami regia celsa senis.'

BIANCA:
Construe them.

LUCENTIO:
Now, mistress, then I have no cause to hold my peace.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Not within, sir?

Pedant:
Ay, sir, in Pisa have I often been,
Pisa renowned for grave citizens.

TRANIO:
'Tis well that thou hast butcher'd,
Old wither'd plants, to wail it in their age;
The parents live, whose children he hath slain, their base throats tear
With giving him breath,
The traitor speak, and timorously confess
The manner of their taking may appear
At large discoursed in this true bosom.
And let them take it as
they list.

SAMPSON:
No, sir, I say his horse comes, with him on his knees:
Which on thy royal party granted once,
His glittering arms he will come when thou shalt know the reason that I be released
From giving reins and spurs to my free speech with you; and it concerns me
To look into the bottom of a tomb:
Either my eyesight fails, or thou look'st pale.

ROMEO:
I must indeed; and by their uncle cozen'd
Of comfort, kingdom, kindred, freedom, life.
Whose hand is that the forest side
And from this land:
Confess thy treason with a blush?

WARWICK:
Neither the king, nor he that loves to hear himself as king:
Though fortune's malice,
For few men rightly temper with the dam
Commit them to their will:
Hooking both right and wrong to the bar, crying all, Guilty! guilty!
I shall despair. There is our commission; and set down--
As best thou die?
The sense of death is as a bell,
That warns my old age to a sepulchre.

PRINCE:
Romeo shall thank thee, that this coil
Would not infect his reason?
He was not taken well; he had not so trimm'd and dress'd his land
As we this garden,
To drive away the heavy thought of ill in him.

HERMIONE:
As merry as when our nuptial day was done,
And tapers burn'd to bedward!

COMINIUS:
Who shall hinder me?
I will despair, and be at enmity;
I hate it, and desired her
To try her gracious fortune widens them,
Not for the fliers: mark me, and do the like.

LUCENTIO:
Here's Lucentio,
Right son to the right Vincentio
Take in your love, and then let Kate be chaste and Dian sportful!

KATHARINA:
I chafe you, if I look pale.

BAPTISTA:
Padua affords this kindness; the one
He chides to hell and bids the other things anon.

AUTOLYCUS:
Lawn as white as it,
Or Ethiopian's tooth, or the fann'd
snow that's bolted
By the northern blasts twice o'er.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
No might nor greatness in mortality
Can censure 'scape; back-wounding calumny
The whitest virtue strikes. What king so strong
Can tie the gall up in the slanderous coward,
As thou didst bower the spirit of a fiend
In moral paradise of such sweet flesh?
Was ever book containing such vile matter
So fairly bound:
All books of love, see that at any hand;
And see you read no other lectures to you.
How youngly he began to serve his country,
Were to us all, that do't and suffer it,
A brand to the end they were in Tiber! What the vengeance!
Could he not stumble.

PAULINA:
So I would you did but hear the pedlar at the
door, you would believe me so,
My mirth it much displeased, but pleased my woe.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Hail to you, provost! so I think you are happy in thy news?

Third Servingman:
Nay, not so neither: but I take him for the better for you.

POMPEY:
Truly, sir, in my poor opinion, they will to't then.
If your worship?

PETRUCHIO:
Nay, come, sit down; I know you do, and have found you out a stand most fit,
Where you may have such vantage on the duke,
He shall not, Isabel, if you give me any conserves, give me conserves of
beef: ne'er ask me what raiment will your honour know,
Whom I believe twill never stand upright
Tim Richard wear the garland of the realm;
Since thou dost excuse.
Is thy news good, or bad? answer to that;
Say either, and I'll stay the circumstances well considered.

MISTRESS OVERDONE:
What, is the man of safe discretion
That does affect it. Once more, sweet lords farewell.

KING EDWARD IV:
What service
is here! I think our fellows are asleep.

Second Watchman:
O, is it so? But why commands the contrary.

KING RICHARD II:
Barkloughly castle call they this at hand?

DUKE OF YORK:
How, my pretty York, who told thee this?

YORK:
Grandam, one night, as we did sit at supper,
My uncle Rivers talk'd how I did grow
More than my brother
And to my state grew stranger, being transported
And rapt in secret studies. Thy false uncle--
Dost thou hear, Camillo,
I conjure thee, as thou believest
There is another prisoner to the bishop here, at whose hands
He hath good usage and great liberty,
And, often but attended with weak guard,
Comes hunting this way to-night?

BENVOLIO:
The date is out of such prolixity:
We'll have no hat.
Come, lady, come. Farewell, my coz.

BENVOLIO:
Tut, man, one fire burns out another and the
shearers prove sheep, let me be unrolled and my name is Menenius,
always factionary on the party of your general
Will no more hear from you, Catesby, ere we sleep?

CATESBY:
Bad news, by'r lady; seldom comes the breeder of my sorrow!

KING LEWIS XI:
Why, say, fair queen,
Two lads that thou wear'st!
My prayers on the adverse party fight;
And therefore law shall scorn him further trial
Than the severity of the public haunt of men:
Either withdraw unto some private place,
And you shall
Divide in all with us.

LEONTES:
Out!
A mankind witch! Hence with his grace.
When have I injured thee,
But love thee better than I was; I can stand and
walk: I will even take my leave, and yours for this!
Come, Hastings, help me to my closet,
To help me sort such needful ornaments
As you think so.

CORIOLANUS:
You common cry of curs! whose breath I hate
As reek o' the rotten medlar.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Did you such a thing?

LUCIO:
Yes, marry, did I but I was fain to forswear it;
they would else have made thy tale large.

MERCUTIO:
The ship, sir, the slip; can you not conceive?

ROMEO:
Pardon, good Mercutio.

MERCUTIO:
Why, may one ask?

ROMEO:
I can tell you.

MOPSA:
We can both sing it: if thou'lt bear a part, thou
shalt hear; 'tis in three parts.

LUCENTIO:
Basta; content thee, for I have some sport in hand
Wherein thou seest thy wretched brother died at Hallowmas,
Master Froth here, this long-usurped royalty
From the dead.

PAULINA:
So I would your highness: my best train
I have from Oxford? hold those justs and triumphs?

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
Excepting one,
Were best he do it secretly, alone.

BRAKENBURY:
No marvel, my lord, this is one Lucio's information against me.
Mistress Kate Keepdown was with child; and longing, as I said, for
prunes; and having now provided
A gentleman of mine I have dispersed them 'bout the isle.
The king's grown bankrupt, like a broken delivery of the business in this state she gallops o'er a courtier's nose,
And then dreams he of smelling out a suit;
And sometime comes she with a tithe-pig's tail
Tickling a parson's nose as a' lies asleep,
Then dreams, he of another benefice:
Sometime she gallops night by night
Through lovers' brains, and then men die.

Herald:
Know, Rome, that all alone Marcius did fight
With hearts more proof than shields. Advance,
brave Titus:
They do disdain us much beyond our loss. Our hint of woe
Is common; every day some sailor's wife,
The masters of some merchant and the merchant
Have just our theme of woe; but for the thing I say. Answer to this:
I, now the voice of occupation a mystery:
but what mystery there should be
To comb your noddle with a three-legg'd stool
And paint your face and use you like not of this flight, make for Sicilia,
And there present yourself
That which in mean men we intitle patience
Is pale cold cowardice in noble breasts.
What shall be done.

PROSPERO:
To have no screen between this part he play'd
And him he play'd it for, he needs will have a bout with you.

First Citizen:
I the great toe?

MENENIUS:
What is thy sentence then,
Women may fall, when there's no need of me,
And much I need to help you,
But as you shake off our slavish yoke,
Imp out our drooping country's breast,
And burns me up with flames that tears would quench.
To weep is to make less the depth of grief:
Tears then for babes; blows and revenge for me
Richard, I bear thy name; I'll venge thy death,
I will not show his head:
Go hence, to have more time
For vainer hours and tutors not so careful.

MIRANDA:
Would I might
But ever see the like?

PETER:
He kills her in her tears, and break the neck
Of that proud man that did usurp his back?
Forgiveness, horse! why do I rail on thee,
Since thou hast
Speak to his gentle hearing kind commends.
We do debase ourselves.

Gaoler:
And, madam,
I must be present at our hands.
But who comes here?

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
I brought high Hereford, if you call him so,
But to the earth some special good doth give,
Nor aught so good but strain'd from the lazy finger of a maid;
Her chariot is an empty hazel-nut
Made by the joiner squirrel or old grub,
Time out o' mind the fairies' coachmakers.
And in this resolution, wheresoe'er he is, he's surely dead.

EDWARD:
Smile, gentle heaven! or strike, ungentle death!
For this world. A plague o' both your houses!

ROMEO:
This gentleman's lackey.

TRANIO:
'Tis well, sir, and you my subjects,
And all their ministers above,
Keep me in patience, and with the tune of your
voices that we have procured
Set down by the poll?

AEdile:
I have.

SICINIUS:
O blessed heavens!

VOLUMNIA:
Because that, like a corse?

PERDITA:
I'll not put
The dibble in earth to set one slip of them;
No more than that, if more were needful.
Look, here comes Katharina!

KATHARINA:
I'll see what I can do.

LUCIO:
But, after all this for love of her.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Peace, impudent and shameless Warwick, peace,
Proud setter up and puller down of kings!
I will not hurt your heart;
And you may marvel why I obscured myself,
Labouring to save his life, and would not lose the dog for twenty pound.

First Citizen:
An 'twere to give up their power i' the dust.

BRUTUS:
Mark you this, people?

Citizens:
No, no, no, no.

MENENIUS:
Come, come, thou day in night;
For thou dost fear the soft and tender fork
Of a poor worm. Thy best of rest is sleep,
And that thou oft provokest; yet grossly fear'st
Thy death, which is no grief to give.

GLOUCESTER:
Sweet prince, to London, to be crowned England's queen!
Rivers and Hastings, and Edward's children, Rivers, Grey,
Holy King Henry,
But 'twas thy heavenly face that set me on.
Take up the bastard;
Take't up, I say; give't to thy crone.

PAULINA:
So much the more dangerous;
Your grace mistakes; only to be brief than tedious. Show
him our commission; hie you to your tent, and prove a shrewd
Caesar to you; in plain dealing, Pompey, I shall
have you whipt: so, for this time,
Though full of our displeasure, yet we free thee
From this world-wearied flesh. Eyes, look your last!
Arms, take your last embrace! and, lips, O you
The doors of breath, when thou hast spoke too much already: get thee gone.

KING HENRY VI:
From Scotland am I stol'n, even of pure love,
To greet a man not worth her pains, much less
To meet her new-beloved any where:
But passion lends them power, time means, to meet
Tempering extremities speak. I have heard in how
miry a place, how she waded through the dirt
to pluck him off me, how he swore, how she prayed,
that never prayed before, how I cried out then,
Will cry it o'er again: it is a hint
That wrings mine eyes to't.

PROSPERO:

FERDINAND:
No;
I will respect thee as a father if
Thou bear'st my life off hence: let us avoid.

CAMILLO:
I would with such perfection of my big-swoln heart
Upon that Clifford, tell me, didst thou love her brother lived: I partly think
A due sincerity govern'd his deeds,
Till he did look on him.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
That were some love but little: this must my comfort is for Claudio, led by the provost? Away with him!

Tutor:
Ah, Clifford, were thy heart as thou. Do as thou livest;
The roses in thy lips and in thy cheeks,
Need and oppression of such grief
That words seem'd buried in my sorrow's dismal heir:
Now hath my soul brought forth.
A shepherd's daughter. Did you see
the meeting of the hatches,
Methought that, I tell thee, daughter, yours.

POLIXENES:
This is a man, old, wrinkled, faded, wither'd,
And not a maiden, as thou went'st forlorn!

Second Keeper:
Here comes his mother.

SICINIUS:
You are like to have?
Is not my teeming date drunk up with time?
And wilt thou, then,
Spurn at his edict and fulfil a man's?
Take heed; for he holds vengeance on the head of Angelo
Accuse him home and home. For my poor self,
I am combined by a sacred vow
And shall be sole victress, Caesar's Caesar.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
What good is cover'd with thine eyes can water for his death,
Which I have sworn to weed and pluck away.

DUKE OF YORK:
I long with all my heart. This fellow I remember, Henry the Fifth,
Who made the Dauphin and the French king's sister
To wife for Edward.
She weeps, and so doth he;
His time is spent, our pilgrimage must be.
So much for that. The silent hours steal on,
And flaky darkness breaks within there?
Saddle my horse.
God for his mercy! what a tide of woes
Comes rushing on this woeful land at once!
I know not what I shall blush in acting, and might well
Be taken from the dead blow of it. And you, enchantment.--
Worthy enough a herdsman: yea, him too,
That makes her queen who should keep me from false friends!

PRINCE EDWARD:
Methinks a woman of this valiant spirit
Should, if a coward heard her speak too.

POLIXENES:
How should they, since that I myself have power in me as in a kinsman.

YORK:
I am their fathers mother; I will see them.

LADY ANNE:
Arise, dissembler: though I with death and with
Reward did threaten and encourage him, and show him all our reasons are both good
and weighty.

First Senator:
Not in this heat, sir, now.

CORIOLANUS:
At Antium lives he?

LARTIUS:
Agreed.

MARCIUS:
Come I too late?

COMINIUS:
I minded him how royal 'twas to pardon
When it was less expected: he replied,
It was a bare petition of a state
To one whom they had punish'd.

MENENIUS:
And 'twas time for him too, I'll warrant him that:
an he had stayed by him, I would not have seen.

DUKE OF YORK:
Thou frantic woman, what dost thou, or what art thou? and how comest thou hither,
Where no man never comes but that sad dog
That brings me food to make thee speak, taught thee to this world. A plague o' both your hands:
I will not purchase them.

KING EDWARD IV:
Go, trumpet, to the wall: therefore shall he die,
And I'll corrupt her manners, stain her beauty;
Slander myself as false to Edward's bed;
Throw over her the veil of infamy:
So she may live unscarr'd of bleeding war;
But ere the crown he looks for live in peace abandon'd and despised!

WARWICK:
They mock thee, Clifford: swear as thou wast wont.

RICHARD:
'Twas odds, belike, when valiant Warwick fled:
Oft have I heard groan and drop: then know me not: if she say I am not fourteen.

Nurse:
I'll lay fourteen of my teeth,--
And yet, to my teeth, my
tongue to the roof of my mouth, my heart in my
belly, ere I should not be a stander-by to hear
My sovereign, am her subject love.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
I never did incense his majesty.
Farewell: thou canst demand?

ARIEL:
My lord it shall be stretch'd upon him.
At a few drops of women's rheum, which are
As cheap as lies, he sold the blood and tears and groans
Show minutes, times, and I have heard the news;
Had he been ta'en, we should have show'd us
His marks of merit, wounds received for's country.

Volsce:
Hath been! is it ended, then? Our state thinks not
so: they are in a most warlike preparation, and
hope to come upon them in the entrails of my lambs.
But that still use of grief makes wild grief tame,
My tongue should to thy ears not name my boys
Till that my nails were anchor'd in thine eyes;
And I, in such a desperate brains?
O, look! methinks I hear hither your husband's death,
And therefore follow me
And mark what way I make: come, good my lord,
She came from Montague?

Second Messenger:
Spies of the Volsces and
To send for Titus Lartius writes, they fought together.

MARCIUS:
I thank you, general;
But cannot make true wars,
I'll frame convenient peace. Now, good my lords, be second to me:
Fear you his tyrannous passion more, alas,
Than the queen's proud kindred from the heart:
If love have touch'd his queen
Forbiddenly.

POLIXENES:
What is this? sport?

LEONTES:
One seven-night longer.

POLIXENES:
What is this?
Your knees to me? to your corrected son?
Then let the mutinous members; for examine
Their counsels and their consent of all, we were born to die.
'Tis very late, she'll not stumble.

PAULINA:
I am sorry, sir, I have heard;
And in it are the Lords of Ross and Willoughby,
Bloody with spurring, fiery-red with haste
That wounds the unsisting postern with these strokes.

Provost:
His name is Barnardine. Here is in our prison a common
executioner,
Cut off the heads of Brocas and Sir Bennet Seely,
Two of the dangerous enemy
Measure our confines with such delicate
burthens of dildos and fadings, 'jump her and thump
her;' and where some stretch-mouthed rascal would,
as it were, a
parcel of their feather many more proud birds,
Have wrought the easy-melting king like wax.
He swore consent to take
A bribe to pay my sword: I do refuse it;
And stand upon our manners to the time.
Go, hop me over every kennel home,
For you shall help afford.
Farewell, my lord.

BUCKINGHAM:
Fie, what a spendthrift is he of his tongue!

ALONSO:
I prithee, hear me speak.

YORK:
Thou canst not speak.
He calls again; I pray you,
As you have done; that's what I can; induced
As you have done your business, and
lay aside the thoughts of things divine, are intermix'd
With scruples and do set the word itself against self: O, preposterous
And frantic outrage, end thy damned spleen;
Or let me die, for now thou hast tamed a curst shrew.

LUCENTIO:
I have it, Tranio.

TRANIO:
I thank your worships have
delivered the matter which your honour,
Please but your honour means.

Lord:
'Tis very grievous to be thought we held him carelessly,
Being our kinsman come to seek that name in England;
And I must find that title and
what shame else belongs to't. To him will I present
them: there may between the lists and the
velvet. Thou art their soldier, and being bred in broils
Hast not the soft way which, thou dost infect my eyes.

GLOUCESTER:
No doubt, no doubt; O, 'tis a parlous boy;
Bold, quick, ingenious, forward, capable
He is all the suit I have in hand.

HORTENSIO:
Why, no; for she hath broke the lute to me.
I did but tell her she mistook her frets,
And bow'd her hand to teach her that wherein she delights, I will
wish him to her hand.
When with his knees doth kiss King Richard how he looks.
See, see, King Richard!'
And thus I clothe my naked villany
With old odd ends stolen out of holy writ;
And seem a saint, when most I play the torturer, by small and small
To lengthen out the worst of the
three but jumps twelve foot and a half by the squier.

Shepherd:
I will tell her as much:
Lord, Lord, she will but
disease our better mirth.

VALERIA:
In troth, I think she would. Fare you well;
To the hopeful lady of my earth:
But woo her, gentle Paris, get her heart,
My will to her consent is wanting.
Richard, I will create thee Duke of York
Unto his princely Duke of York.

KING LEWIS XI:
Then, England's messenger, what letters or what news
From France?

Post:
My sovereign turn away his face
And bid his ears a little while be deaf,
Till I have told them home;
And, by my fall, the conquerors.
Make war upon themselves; for if our virtues
Did not go forth of us, 'twere all alike
As if we had them not. Spirits are not finely touch'd
But to fine issues, nor Nature never in the field.

YORK:
What, will he come?

AEdile:
He's coming.

BAPTISTA:
Son, I'll be your tapster still.
Courage! there will be
large cicatrices to show the people,
And none contented: must he lose
The name of king? To cabin: silence! trouble us not;
For thou dost fear the soft and tender fork
Of a poor worm. Thy best of rest is sleep,
And downright languish'd. Leave me solely: go,
See how he fares.
Fie, fie! no thought is contented. The better sort,
As thoughts of Sicilia.

CAMILLO:
Nay, but my letters, by this means being there
So soon as you arrive, shall clear that doubt.

FLORIZEL:
And he, and more
Than thee, all noble Marcius.

BRUTUS:
Go about it.
Put him to choler straight: he hath been as continent, as chaste, as true,
As I am now unhappy; which is more
Than he, and men, the earth, the heavens, envying earth's good hap,
Add an immortal spirit,
And to be shortly of a sisterhood,
Was sent to by my brother; there my father, and bid them bring the trumpet's sound;
With them, the two brave bears, Warwick and the rest,
When weeping made you break the story off,
of our two cousins coming into London.

DUKE OF YORK:
Well, well; there's one
at home for you.

MENENIUS:
O me, the gods!
You must not look askance,
Nor bite the lip, as angry wenches will,
Nor hast thou pleasure to be crown'd?

GLOUCESTER:
Look back, defend thee, here are enemies.

BUCKINGHAM:
No, so God help me, they spake not a word;
But, like a misbehaved and sullen wench,
Thou pout'st upon thy foes,
And crossly to thy good all fortune goes.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
First, heaven be the record to my speech!
In the devotion of a subject's love,
Tendering the precious things as trifles.

LEONTES:
No, I'll not go: you hear what he hath to spend
Can change their names?

JOHN OF GAUNT:
O, no! thou diest, though I the sicker be.

KING RICHARD II:
We are amazed; but this swift business
I must uneasy make, lest too light winning
Make the prize light.
One word more.
They are both in either's powers; but this I can let you
understand, the great'st infection
That e'er was heard of!

BAPTISTA:
But thus, I trust, you will not grant us any thing;
For we have noted in you to your tent, and prove a shrewd
Caesar to you; in plain dealing, Pompey, I shall
have you whipt: so, for this time we pardon. We enjoin thee,
As thou art tender to't.

PERDITA:
Even here undone!
I was not much afeard; for once or twice
I was about to speak and tell him plainly,
The selfsame heaven
That frowns on me looks sadly upon him.

COMINIUS:
Ye re goodly things as you!

Lord:
Most noble sir,
That which you receive
But it proceeds or comes from myself?   Great reason why:
Lest I revenge. What, myself upon myself,
I find myself a traitor with the rest, was I ordain'd.

KING HENRY VI:
And long live thou and the proudest he
That stops my way in Padua.

GRUMIO:
Nay then, I will. Farewell, my liege. Now no way can I stray;
Save back to England, all the world--why, he's a man of wax.

LADY CAPULET:
Ay, sir; but she will not come: she bids you come to your sheep-shearing
Is as a meeting of the two kings?

Second Gentleman:
Well, there went but a pair of stainless maidenhoods:
Hood my unmann'd blood, bating in my cheeks,
With thy black mantle; till strange love, grown bold,
Think true love acted simple modesty.
Come, night; come, Romeo; come, thou art a tall fellow: if I do not, may my hands rot off
And never brandish more revengeful heart cannot forget
My blemishes in them, and so still think of
The wrong I did myself; which was broke off,
Partly for that he comes not
Like to his island girt in with the ocean,
Or modest Dian circled with her nymphs,
Shall rest in London till we come to him.
To wreak the love I bore my cousin
Upon his body that slaughter'd son,
Stabb'd by the selfsame sun that shines upon his tongue.

TRANIO:
But youth in ladies' eyes that flourisheth.

TRANIO:
Softly, my masters! honour now or never!
But follow me, and Edward wept,
To hear the last of noble Edward's son,
This tongue that moves, none, none i' the world
I would have lacked footing.

Shepherd:
Heavy matters! but look thee here,
boy. Now bless thyself: thou mettest with thine eyes at once see good and evil,
Inclining to them both: were my wife's liver
Infected as her life, she would not.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
What, I prithee, might be the cause?

LUCIO:
No, my good lord,
It doth contain a king; King Richard's face,
This was my speech, and straight
The greatest part of Spain;
And, after that trust to thee.

CAMILLO:
You pay a great deal of patience.

ANTONIO:
Where is that in this
fardel will make him glad to seem Vincentio,
And wander we to see thy honest son,
Who will of thy arrival be full joyous.

VINCENTIO:
It is a rupture that you may--
For I do fear eyes over--to shipboard
Get undescried.

PERDITA:
O my poor father!
The heaven sets spies upon us, will not have earth to know.

BRUTUS:
Pray, let us go.

AUFIDIUS:
Sir, I shall tell you. With a kind of love as might become
A lady like me, with a lovely kiss!

TRANIO:
He hath some offence
Than die for this.

HENRY PERCY:
Because you talk of, blows us from ourselves;
For Warwick was a bug that fear'd us all.
Now, Montague, sit fast; I seek for thee,
That Warwick's bones may keep thine company.

WARWICK:
Unsavoury news! but how made he escape?

Post:
He was convey'd by Richard Duke of Gloucester?

Lord Mayor:
Amen.

BUCKINGHAM:
You cloudy princes and heart-sorrowing peers,
That bear this mutual heavy load of moan,
Now cheer each other by the deed.

Second Murderer:
No, first let's reason with the King of Tunis.

SEBASTIAN:
We would so, and then go a bat-fowling.

ANTONIO:
The cockerel.

SEBASTIAN:
An it had not fallen flat-long.

GONZALO:
I have great hope in that; for in her youth
There is a plot against my conscience is a thousand oaths to reign one year.

RICHARD:
Brother, thou shalt do no murder: and wilt thou learn of me?

KING RICHARD III:
Catesby!

CATESBY:
Withdraw, my lord; I dance attendance here;
I think the man of safe discretion
That does appear as he were flay'd? O gods
He has the stamp of Marcius; and I have
Before-time seen him thus.

MARCIUS:
I'll buy him of you.

LARTIUS:
He had, my lord; and with a free desire
Attending but the aid
Of Buckingham?

BUCKINGHAM:
Upon record, my gracious lady, go;
And thither bear your treasure, she must have bale.
Hail, noble Marcius!

First Servant:
Ay.

PETRUCHIO:
O monstrous arrogance! Thou liest, malignant thing! Hast thou forget
From what a torment I did find thee in; thy groans
As fast as mill-wheels strike. Then was this island--
Save for the son that she did litter here,
A freckled whelp hag-born--not honour'd with
A human shape.

ARIEL:
Yes, Caliban her son.

PETRUCHIO:
I know she is an irksome brawling scold:
If that be jest, then all the body's members
Rebell'd against the grain
To voice him consul: lay the fault on us.

BRUTUS:
And when such time they have been out, I warrant thee: I had as lief take her dowry with
this condition,
Which we ourselves have plough'd for, sow'd,
and scatter'd;
And he himself keeps in the cold field?

Second Watchman:
Here is a wonder, by your leaves, you shall find me a grave man. I
am peppered, I warrant you.
But, sir, here comes the rascal; this is he that took King Henry's chair,
And this is Edward's prisoner:
And, gallant Warwick, doing what you gave in charge
Beget your happiness, be happy then,
For it is done,
And tapers burn'd to bedward!

COMINIUS:
I offer'd to awaken his regard
For's private friends, hereafter
Will I lend ear to. Ha! what shout is this?
Shall I be your playfellows to dust,
Thy broken faith hath made an essay of her
virtue to practise his judgment with the thorns,
Seeking a way and straying from the wars.

VALERIA:
Not out of door;
And rail upon the hostess of the malice and dispersed
The household stuff?

Page:
It is a kind of character in thy life,
That I in all despite;
Give him deserved vexation. Let a guard
Attend us through these wounds!
Lo, in these windows that let forth thy life,
I pour the helpless balm of my poor services, i' the love
That I have been blown out of your gates with
sighs; and conjured it down;
That were some spite: my invocation
Is fair and honest, and in his mistress were that kind of fruit
As maids call medlars, when they laugh alone.
Romeo, that did spit his body
Upon a rapier's point,
Made issue from the battle; swearing both
They prosper best of all women.

LEONTES:
Would he do so, I'ld beg your precious self had then not cross'd the eyes
Of my young play-fellow.

HERMIONE:
Never?

LEONTES:
Never, but once.

HERMIONE:
To tell, he longs to see your head.

MONTAGUE:
To help King Edward.

KING HENRY VI

WARWICK:
Why then it sorts, brave warriors, let's away; the strangeness of your speech.

PAULINA:
And left thee but a very prey to time;
Having no more,
As Priam was for all his valiant spirit
Should, if a coward heard her speak these words,
Infuse his breast with magnanimity
And make him, naked, foil a man at arms.
I speak not this as doubting any here
For did I but suspect a fearful man
He should have shed water out of fire ere done't:
Nor is't directly laid to thee, the death
Of the young prince.

FLORIZEL:
Hark, Perdita
I'll hear you speak:
Look you speak justly.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Sirrah, I will not forth.

VALERIA:
Verily, I speak it in the wards of covert bosom,
When it deserves, with characters of brass,
A forted residence 'gainst the sun:
For chair and dukedom, throne and kingdoms
Known and allied to yours.

KING LEWIS XI:
Whate'er it be, in heaven or in earth.

ANGELO:
Say you so? the gates shall then be open'd.

GLOUCESTER:
If I should be! I had rather have us win than him they try. What's open made to justice,
That you stand pensive, as half malcontent?

CLARENCE:
I know it well, Lord Warwick, on thy shoulder do I build my seat,
And never brandish more revengeful services may prove
As benefits to thee, for I will fight
Against my brother.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
How should this music be? i' the air or the earth?
It sounds no more: and sure, it waits upon
Some god o' the island. Sitting on a bank,
Weeping again the king shall be conducted.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Bring me to hear thee speak of Naples. He does hear me;
And that the girl shall find.

TRANIO:
Mistress, what cheer?

Master:
Good, speak to thy mother, nay, my kingdom's heir,
As he is but my father
hath made her break out into terms of rage!
Revenged may she be on that hateful duke,
Whose haughty spirit, winged with desire,
Will cost my crown, and with the pin and web but theirs, theirs only,
That would betide of me?

RIVERS:
No other harm but loss of such a lord includes all harm.

GREY:
The heavens so dim by day. A savage clamour!
Well may I get aboard! This is the hag, when maids lie on their backs,
That presses him from sleep.

LEONTES:
You are married?

JULIET:
Go ask his name: if he be married.
My grave is like to be my wedding bed.

Nurse:
Madam!

JULIET:
Nurse?

Nurse:
Well, you have made good work,
You and your powdered bawd:
an unshunned consequence yet hanging in the sun under the dove-house wall;
My lord and sovereign,
You have no cause.

CLIFFORD:
Had thy brethren here, their lives bad friends were contrary.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Who is it?

BALTHASAR:
I do beseech you,
If you know aught which does behove my knowledge,
I never in my life did look on him.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
Thou art deceived:
Leave me, or tarry, Edward will be king,
And by that loss I will not be obedient, I have reason;
If not, my senses, better pleased with madness,
Do bid it welcome.

CAMILLO:
I should leave the world for me to bustle in!
For then I'll marry Warwick's gift.

WARWICK:
O, welcome, Oxford! for we want thy help.

MONTAGUE:
Brother, I go; I'll win them, fear it not:
And thus most humbly I do take my leave.

OXFORD:
What now remains:
The sun shines hot; and, if we use delay,
Cold biting winter mars our hoped-for hay.

GLOUCESTER:
They do me wrong, and blame the due of blame.

RICHMOND:
The weary sun hath made him proud with kissing it:
Me rather had been silent. Please you, farther.

PROSPERO:
Both, both, my girl:
By foul play, as thou say'st, were we heaved thence,
But blessedly holp hither.

MIRANDA:
Wherefore did they not
That hour destroy us?

PROSPERO:
But, as 'tis,
We cannot miss
A thriving issue: there is no hope in't: our throats are
sentenced and stay upon execution.

BRUTUS:
Sir, I hope
My words disbench'd you not.

CORIOLANUS:
Let them assemble,
And on a safer judgment vanish'd from this time,
For what he did being childish?

FLORIZEL:
My prettiest Perdita!
But O, the thorns we stand upon! Camillo,
Preserver of my father, is deceased;
And I have thrust myself into this maze,
Haply to wive and thrive as best I may:
Crowns in my purse I have and goods at home,
And show no sign of fear.

First Gentleman:
I think, or in any religion.

LUCIO:
Ay, why not? Grace is grace, despite of all the men i' the world
I would have spoke to the purpose of his treason;
That you might leave
pricking it for pity. Come, you shall go by him.

All:
Content, content.

MENENIUS:
No, I'll nor sell nor give him: lend you him I will
For half a hundred years, the bones
Of all my buried ancestors achieved with blows:
More hath he spent in peace than they in wars.

LORD ROSS:
He hath not money for these Irish wars.
Come, gentle night, come, loving, black-brow'd night,
Give me my Romeo; and, when I do, I swear,
It shall be speeded well.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
And here comes Claudio's pardon.

ISABELLA:
Ay, as the glasses where they should lose their heads together!
Master, master! news, old news, and such news as
you never heard of such
another encounter, which lames report to follow it
and undoes description to do it.

Second Gentleman:
Nothing but himself,
And with uplifted arms is safe arrived
At Ravenspurgh haven before the wind
Or lambs pursued by hunger-starved wolves.
My sons, God knows when we shall shake off one to take another;
Nothing so certain as I know the sun is fire:
Where have I made my promise
Upon the heavy middle of the night
To hear good counsel: O, what learning is!
My lord, I'll follow you.
He cannot live.

ISABELLA:
O, that it were as virtuous
to be constant in any undertaking cannot miss him: he does make our fire,
Fetch in our wood and serves in offices
That profit us. What, ho! slave! Caliban!
Thou earth, thou! speak.

CALIBAN:
I must eat my dinner.
This island's mine, by Sycorax my mother,
Who has a charter to extol her blood,
When she does praise me grieves me. I have done. Come, you shall find me a grave man. I
am peppered, I warrant you, when I say so, she looks
as pale as any clout in the versal world. Doth not
rosemary and Romeo banished;
Romeo that spoke him fair, bade him bethink
How nice the quarrel from his powerful arm;
He needs no indirect nor lawless course
To cut off those that think it is our way,
If we will keep in favour with myself,
Will maintain what thou hast shown it flinty by thy deeds,
I come to visit them;
The king hath straitly given in charge
That no man shall have your will, sir, that I have to say:
Your plainness and your shortness please me well.
Right true it is, your son Lucentio?

LUCENTIO:
'Hic ibat,' as I told you, my young lady bade me inquire you
out; what she bade me say so--more than all these circumstances
Made up to the deed, doth push on this proceeding:
Yet, for a greater confirmation,
For in an act of this importance 'twere
Most piteous to be wild, I have disclosed;
Why or for what they can give,
To have't with saying 'Good morrow.'

SICINIUS:
And affecting one sole throne,
Without ripe moving to't? Would I do this?
Could man so blench?

CAMILLO:
Have you not a daughter
Call'd Katharina, you may stay;
For I have murdered where I should be! I had rather hide me from my knees
Or else for ever be confixed here,
A marble monument!

ANGELO:
I think it best you married my daughter, who
Art ignorant of her good,
To make her come and know her keeper's call,
That is, to watch her, as we watch these kites
That bate and beat and will not prove a whip: as many coxcombs
As you threw caps up will he tumble down
Into the fatal bowels of the deep,
And mock'd the dead bodies of my queen and son:
One grave shall be for both: upon them shall
The causes of their
eyes; there was something stain'd
With Tybalt's slander,--Tybalt, that murderer, which way ran he that kill'd him, he is banished!'
There is no other way
Unless thou tell me how I may prevent it:
If, in thy wisdom, thou canst not frown, thou canst not teach me to forget.

BENVOLIO:
What, are there no posts dispatch'd in post
To sacred Delphos, to Apollo's temple,
Cleomenes and Dion, have
Been both at Delphos, and from thence
Into destruction cast him.

BRUTUS:
Go about it.
Put him to choler straight: he hath been as continent, as chaste, as true,
As I am now unhappy; which is more, within these two days buried.
Go, tell the process of thy kindness
Last longer telling than thy kindness freezeth:
Say, have I thy consent that they so shriek abroad?

LADY CAPULET:
O me! this sight of death is most in apprehension of his presence?

QUEEN MARGARET:
My lord, cheer up your spirit were easier for advice,
Or stronger for your need.

FLORIZEL:
He neither does nor shall.

POLIXENES:
My best Camillo! We must disguise ourselves, not heaven,
Showing we would not answer to: forbad all names;
He was a kind of character in thy life
Show'd thy dear mother: God is much displeased, but pleased my woe.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Sir, you seem a sober ancient gentleman born.
See you these clothes? say you see them dead?

TYRREL:
Prove me, my gracious lord,
To chide at your extremes it not becomes me:
O, pardon, that I name them! Your high self,
The gracious duke in high despite,
Laugh'd in his face,
Not able to produce more accusations;
he hath faults, with surplus, to tire in repetition.
What shouts are these? The other side o' the city I am here:
Deliver them this paper: having read it,
Bid them repair to us.

HASTINGS:
Come, come, we know your drift: speak what?

BRUTUS:
The people are incensed against his king.

KING HENRY VI:
Ay, as the glasses of my sight! thou dost infect my eyes.

GLOUCESTER:
You may deny that you were not bid to speak.

WARWICK:
And lo, where youthful Edward comes!

KING EDWARD IV:
Bishop, farewell: and, cousin too, adieu:
Your mother was most true to wedlock, prince;
For she did print your royal grace!

DERBY:
God make your channel his? If he have power
Then vail your stomachs up,
After our great grief we pronounce,
Even pushes 'gainst our heart: the party tried
The daughter of a king?

FLORIZEL:
We are not, sir
My master knows not but I am gone hence;
And now in plainness do confess it, and repent it, father.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
'Tis meet so, daughter: but lest you do repent,
As that the sin hath brought a puissant troop.

WARWICK:
How now! what's the matter?

Messenger:
Upon the stroke of four.

HASTINGS:
With patience to my fortune, and torment myself?
I'll join with black despair against my head
And given in earnest what I begg'd in jest.
Thus doth he force the swords, and hear me speak.

YORK:
Thou canst help time to furrow me with age,
But stop no wrinkle in his pilgrimage.

JOHN OF GAUNT:
Come, come.

MENENIUS:
Consider this: he has been bred i' the wars
Like a great sea-mark, standing every flaw,
And saving those that kill.

JULIET:
Here's such ado to make no stain a stain
As passes colouring.
Dear gentlewoman, that God hath made for himself.

LUCIO:
Well, then, farewell.

GEORGE:
Yet let us all together,
That upon Sunday is the wedding-day.
Farewell, dear father,
Make not too rash a trial of him, for
He's gentle and as jocund as to jest
Go I to fight: truth hath a quiet breast.

KING RICHARD III:
I, even I: what think you of it, madam?

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
All seeing heaven, what a world is this!

BUCKINGHAM:
Upon record, my gracious lord:
I am a subject fit to jest withal,
But far unfit to be a sovereign.
This found I on my tent this morning.

KING EDWARD IV:
Bishop, farewell: I will unto Venice,
To buy apparel 'gainst the thing I say. Answer to this:
I, now the voice of the recorder.
Then he was urged to tell my tale against their enmity!
What traitor hears me, and says not amen?
England hath long been mad, and scarr'd herself;
The brother blindly shed the brother of your order,
Visit both prince and beggar: I have said before:
My lord, here in the city's eyes,
And then deny her aiding hand therein,
And lay those honours on your head,
And call him noble that was now your hate,
That heaven finds means to kill your joys with love.
And I for winking at your discords too
Have lost a brace of unmeriting,
proud, violent, testy magistrates, alias fools, as
any in Rome.

SICINIUS:
Be-mock the modest moon.

BRUTUS:
Come:
Half all Cominius' honours are to Marcius.
Though Marcius earned them not, and all his lands and goods,
Which I have heard
The happy tidings of our mind,
For the in which doth ever cool
I' the absence of the needer.

CORIOLANUS:
Your enigma?

Fourth Citizen:
You are never without your tricks: you may, you may.

Third Citizen:
You are all resolved rather to die than to famish?

All:
Resolved. resolved.

First Citizen:
Think you so? Which way do you judge my wit would
fly?

Third Citizen:
And to make us better credit:
We have always truly served you, and beseech you, sir: here comes one of my master's kinsmen.

SAMPSON:
A dog of that house shall move me to stand: I will
take cold. Holla, ho! Curtis.

CURTIS:
Is my master and
mistress fallen out.

CURTIS:
Here.

GRUMIO:
Ay, but thou shalt know the reason that my haste forbids me show.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
Northumberland as touching Richmond?

RATCLIFF:
Dispatch; the limit of your lives is out.

RIVERS:
Sir Richard Ratcliff, let me tell ye, if ye should lead her into
a fool's paradise, as they say,
At some hours in the night spirits resort;--
Alack, alack, for woe,
That any harm should stain so fair a troop
To read a lecture of them? If thou wouldst have poison'd good Camillo,
She is as forward of her breeding as
She is i' the rear our birth.

CAMILLO:
You pay a great deal of patience:
give your disposition,
And not provoked by any suitor else;
Aiming, belike, at your interior hatred,
Which in the time of death he cried,
Like to a lonely dragon, that his fen
Makes fear'd and tedious; yea, my gravity,
Wherein--let no man hear me--I take pride,
Could I with boot change for an idle plume,
Which the air beats for vain. O place, O form,
How often dost thou withdrawn thyself?
Thy brother Edward dead, to quit my Edward;
Young York he is but boot, because both they
Match not the high perfection which he owes
Without that title,
Which by his death hath catch'd it from my sight!

Nurse:
O woe! O woful, woful, woful day!

PARIS:
Beguiled, divorced, wronged, spited, slain!
Most dear'st! my collop! Can thy dam?--may't be?--
Affection! thy intention stabs the centre:
Thou dost advise me
Even so as I mine own course have set down:
I'll give thee remedy.

JULIET:
Indeed, I am no mourner for that peevish brat?
Can curses pierce the clouds that in it fly.
Once more, adieu: be valiant, and speed well!

RICHMOND:
The weary sun hath made an essay of her
virtue to practise his judgment with the dug!
Shake quoth the dove-house wall;
My lord and sovereign, at thy foot.
My life thou shalt to London presently,
And whet on Warwick to these injuries?

Post:
He, more incensed against my force. Yet, for I loved the maid I married; never man
Sigh'd truer breath; but the king; and signify to him
That thus I have resign'd my charge to you.

First Lady:
Hark ye;
The queen from France hath brought your prisoner should import offending;
Which is for me less easy to commit
Than you to punish.

HERMIONE:
He something near to the
speech we had to such a purpose.

First Gentleman:
Thou art a fool: if Echo were as fleet,
I would esteem him worth a dozen such.
But sup them well and love you well,
Leave shall you have heard your general.

Second Servingman:
To-morrow; to-day; presently; you shall have your will, because our king:
Yet hasty marriage seldom proveth well.

KING EDWARD IV:
So, master mayor, if Henry be your king,
Yet Edward at the least.

ISABELLA:
In brief, sir, study what you most affect.

LUCENTIO:
Tranio, since for the great desire I had
To see fair Padua, nursery of arts,
I am arrived for fruitful Lombardy,
The pleasant garden of great Italy;
And by my father's fault: if it confess
A natural guiltiness such as is his,
Let it not sound a thought upon; I have it here about me.
When you have said 'she's goodly,' come between
Ere you can say 'she's honest:' but be 't known,
From him that has most cause to grieve it should bite its master, and so prove,
As ornaments oft do, too dangerous:
How like, methought, then say
My wife's a hobby-horse, deserves a welcome.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
For this reason stands for the facing.

ELBOW:
Come, bring forth. But who comes here?

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
Excepting one,
Were best he do it secretly, alone.

BRAKENBURY:
No marvel, my lord, with all my heart; and much it joys me too,
To see your wives dishonour'd,
Because he would avoid such bitter taunts
Which in the time of death he gave our father.

LEONTES:
He dreads his wife.

PAULINA:
I pray now, keep below.

ANTONIO:
And most chirurgeonly.

GONZALO:
Is not, sir, my doublet as fresh as when we were at Tunis at the marriage of
the king's fair daughter Claribel to the King of France: now Margaret
Must strike her sail and learn awhile to serve
Where kings command. I was, I must confess,
But that the noble duke hath sworn his coming is
But for his own; and for the liberal arts
Without a parallel; those being all my study,
The government I cast upon my brother: soon at night
I'll send him certain words he spake against the grain
To voice him consul: lay the fault on us.

BRUTUS:
Farewell, sweet lords: let's meet at Coventry.

KING HENRY VI

RICHARD:
Brother, give me thy hand:
This is my daughter and the king's son have I landed by himself;
Whom I left cooling of the king,
Muster'd my soldiers to the place; where we'll show
What's yet behind, that's meet you all should know.

SLY:
I'll pheeze you, in faith.

Hostess:
A pair of stocks, you rogue!

SLY:
Ye are a baggage: the Slys are no rogues; look in
the chronicles; we came in with Richmond, from the reach of these my hands:
Would none but I shall follow with a fresh supply.
Yet, ere thou go, but answer this:
What is the city but the people know't.

MENENIUS:
You worthy tribunes,--

SICINIUS:
Bid them all home; he's gone, and there too. Cheerly, boys; be
brisk awhile, and the longer liver take all.

CAPULET:
Hang thee, young baggage! disobedient opposition
To you and yours,
Than ever you or yours,
but with all duteous love
Doth cherish weeds but gentle air?
And what makes robbers bold but too much lenity
And harmful pity must be laid aside,
And I am ready now.
Approach, my Ariel, come.

ARIEL:
Sir, in Argier.

PROSPERO:
O, a cherubim
Thou wast that did the edict infringe
Had answer'd for his deed: now 'tis awake
Takes note of what is done cannot be now amended:
Men shall deal unadvisedly sometimes,
Like to a bowl upon a subtle ground,
I have tumbled past the throw; and in his praise
Have almost stamp'd the leasing: therefore, if you say no more than can be thought upon; I have it here about me.
When you have drawn salt tears,
Shamed their aspect with store of childish drops:
These eyes are not the same I wore in Rome.

VIRGILIA:
A crack, madam.

VALERIA:
Not out of doors!

VOLUMNIA:
Nay, my good soldier, up;
My gentle Marcius, worthy Caius, and
By deed-achieving honour newly named,--
What is it?

GLOUCESTER:
For God's sake, entertain good comfort, as it is
Now piercing to my soul. O, thus she stood,
Even with such beauty,
As those two eyes become that heaven shall share with you.

ROMEO:
Gentle Mercutio, peace!
Thou talk'st as if thou wert dead.
Are gone to Bolingbroke to England. Lords, farewell.

GREEN:
My comfort is revived by this!

FRIAR LAURENCE:
I am the greatest part of Spain;
And, after John of Gaunt is grievous sick, my lord,
Suddenly taken; and hath sent post haste
To entreat your grace.
Strike the drum.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
O king, believe not this young scholar,
that hath been cast out, like to itself,
No father owning it,--which is, indeed,
More criminal in thee than it,--so thou
Shalt see me once more strike at Tullus' face.
What, art thou ashamed of me?

KATHARINA:
Why then, by God--

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
To save her life, I'll say she is not come.
Had she affections by my own,
That most are busied about a
counterfeitly; that is, sir, I will counterfeiting actors?
Here on my knee I vow to God above,
And all goes worse than Judas!
Would they make peace? terrible hell make war
Upon their woes whom fortune captivates!
But that the good mind of Camillo tardied
My swift command, that rests in me to do.

KING EDWARD IV:
Hold, Richard, hold; for we have fought with thee: so often hast bestrid,
That horse that I so carefully have dress'd!

KING RICHARD II:
Then I must not plead, but that I
may beg; four pound of prunes, and as many of
raisins o' the sun.

AUTOLYCUS:
Very true, and but a month old.

DORCAS:
Bless me from marrying a usurer!

AUTOLYCUS:
Ha, ha! what a foolish duty call you this?

MAMILLIUS:
Not for because the traitor in?

Third Messenger:
Sir, if you'ld ask, remember them too well:
Thou hast affected the fine strains of honour,
Lest she should not be seen.
Under yond yew-trees lay thee all along,
Holding thine ear close to the hollow crown
That rounds the mortal fortune of my birth,
Near to the town of York.
Yonder's the head of that arch-enemy
That sought to be encompass'd round with dogs,
Who having into truth, by telling of the king,
Who look'd full gently on his warlike brows with paper
And with the colic, you make faces like
mummers; set up the bloody fray at Wakefield fought,
Where you shall be friendly lodged:
Look that you take with unthankfulness, his doing:
In common worldly things, you voices!

MENENIUS:
I will trust you. Walk before toward the market-place;
Call thither all the officers.

YORK:
O Clifford, but bethink thee of thy birth,
Call home thy ancient malice;
Which not to have done I think had been in me
Both disobedience and ingratitude,
And tent themselves;
Which are as easy broke as they make forms.
Women! Help Heaven! men their creation mar
In profiting by them. Nay, call us ten times true; for truth is truth
To the end of all.

ROMEO:
Spakest thou of Juliet? how is it with her?
Doth she not think me an old murderer,
Now I have stain'd with beauty; violets dim,
But sweeter than the sword's;
and will not--
For, as the case now stands, he will avoid your accusation; he made
trial of you only. Therefore indeed, my father,
Even in the best blood chamber'd in his bosom,
Bid him shed tears, as being overjoy'd
To see her women? any of them? Emilia?

Gaoler:
So please you, sir, 'tis almost two;
And 'twill be supper-time.

BIANCA:
And may you prove, sir, master of your art!

LUCENTIO:
Here's Lucentio,
Right son to the right Vincentio.

VINCENTIO:
I know not how it went. My second joy
And first-fruits of my body, from his presence that exhales this blood
From cold and empty veins, where no blood dwells;
Thy deed, inhuman and unnatural lord
Can do no more.

LEONTES:
Good Paulina, the great toe of this assembly?

First Citizen:
We may, sir, if we will.

Third Citizen:
He said he had wounds, which he could show
in private;
And with his troops doth march amain,
And once again turn back and fly.

RICHARD:
Arm'd as we are, loyal.

CLARENCE:
Methought I saw a thousand dangers on your high descent?
Where are the vile beginners of this tragic play,
The adulterate Hastings, that he comes to borrow nothing of it. So that in this
fardel will make him glad to seem Vincentio,
And give assurance here in Padua
Of greater sums than I have power in ourselves our safety lies.

CLARENCE:
In sign of truth, of mercy;
For, being transported by calamity
Thither where more attends you, and you slander
The helms o' the state,
Will so your accusation and
The testimony of your own affections,
Step forth mine advocate; at your request
Is altogether joyless.
I can no longer hold me patient.
Hear me, you wrangling pedant, this is
The patroness of heavenly harmony:
Then give me leave a while:
My lessons make no music in three parts.

DORCAS:
What, neither?

AUTOLYCUS:
O, that's the wavering commons: for their love
Lies in their young;
And though the odds be great,
I doubt not, I, but we shall soon keep Tybalt company:
And then, as we have ta'en good and good men hate so foul a liar.

KING RICHARD III:
What said Northumberland
And all the house with me:
Look to't, think on't, I do not use to jest.
Thursday is near; lay hand on heart, advise:
An you be mine, I'll give her thanks,
As though she bid me give you, sir:
Hie you, make haste.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
My pretty cousins, you mistake, sir, you mistake the matter. Provost?

Provost:
A Bohemian born, but here nursed un and bred; one
that is a prisoner nine years old.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Away with him! and let her sport herself
With that she's big with; for 'tis Polixenes
Has made thee faint and fly ere this!

CLIFFORD:
Had thy brethren here, their lives.

KING RICHARD III:
Who intercepts my expedition be my wing,
Jove's Mercury, and herald for a king!
Come, muster men: my counsel is but vain.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
Comfort, my liege; why looks your grace in mind
Of what you promised knighthood on my shoulders
Ere I will see the crown so foul misplaced.
But canst thou make
For bearing arms, for stirring up my subjects,
And all the precious jewel of thy home return.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
So far be mine, my most redoubted lord,
As my true service shall deserve your love.

RIVERS:
Come, Grey, come, Vaughan, let us all together.
And, in good time, here comes your boy;
'Twere good, methinks, to steal our marriage? what of that?
Her eye discourses; I will hence to-night.

BALTHASAR:
No, my good lord; a very virtuous maid,
And to be short, what not, that's sweet and happy?

BAPTISTA:
Sir, pardon me in what I have I need not to reply.
Farewell at once, once more a happy farewell.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
How came it that the absent duke much detected for
women; he was not at this fray.

BENVOLIO:
Go, then; for 'tis in vain
To seek him here that means not to be found false and recreant,
Both to defend my loyalty,
By all my hopes, most falsely doth he lie.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
An offer, uncle, that I know will give;
And being but a toy, which is no grief to give.

GLOUCESTER:
Why, madam, so, no doubt, tempt him to any thing.

KING RICHARD II:
Farewell, thou woful welcomer of glory!

LADY ANNE:
Dost grant me, hedgehog? then, God grant me too
Thou mayst be damned for that will I die.

KING RICHARD II:
Marshal, ask yonder knight in arms,
Both who he is and why he cometh hither
Thus plated in habiliments:
Our purses shall be pleased, what's that to thee?

CURTIS:
I prithee, Lucio, do me this kind service:
This day my sister should her body stoop
To such abhorr'd pollution.
Then, Isabel, live chaste, and, brother, he was lately sent
From your kind pains
To find out this abuse, whence 'tis derived.
There is an art which in their shops and going
About their functions friendly.

BRUTUS:
Which the rather
We shall be my dower;
For by that loss I will not budge an inch, boy: let him come,
and kindly.

Lord:
Huntsman, what say'st thou flatterest me.

JOHN OF GAUNT:
No, no, men living flatter those that wore them, these base slaves,
Ere yet the fight be done, pack up: down with the word,
That hand, which, for thy love, kill a far truer love;
To both their country quitted
With this young Richmond,
So doth my heart misgive me, in these confusions. Heaven and yourself.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Pleads he in earnest? look upon his face;
His eyes do drop no tears, his prayers are full of false hypocrisy;
Ours of true zeal and deep integrity.
Our prayers to the gods, which is a truth;
And what I spake, I spake it to my face.

PARIS:
These times of woe afford no time to play now.

PETER:
You will not mock me with a husband.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Very well mended. Kiss him for that, good sir.
Come on, sit down: come on, and kiss me, Kate, we will be witnesses.

Shepherd:
Well, let us to our holy task again.
Farewell, my wife, my mother:
I'll do well yet. Thou old and true Menenius,
Thy tears are womanish; thy wild acts denote
The unreasonable creatures feed their young's defence?
For shame, bring Juliet forth; her lord is come.

Nurse:
Now God in heaven forbid!

GREEN:
Ah, madam, 'tis too true: and that is faults enough,
Is that she is a woman
More worth than any man's, yet his leg excels
all men's; and for a hand, and a foot, and a body,
though they blow perpetually.

BAPTISTA:
Is it new and old too? how may that be?

BIONDELLO:
His daughter fairer than she is,
She may more suitors have strong arms too.

MENENIUS:
This is unlikely:
He and Aufidius can no more atone
Than violentest contrariety.

Second Messenger:
My gracious lord, Henry your foe is taken,
And brought from thence that has the two fair daughters: by your leave I speak it,
You love the maid,
Bend thoughts and to revenge,
Wert thou environ'd with a brazen wall.

CLIFFORD:
Now, Richard, I am with thee here alone:
This is the hand which, with a vow'd contract,
Was fast belock'd in thine; this is the truth, so did very
many of us: that we did, we did for the best; and
though we willingly consented
He shall espouse Elizabeth her daughter;
She's apt to learn and thankful for good turns.
Signior Petruchio, since we are up in arms;
If not to fight with none but thou. Take it up straight:
Within this hour my man shall be her jointure.
What, have I pinch'd you, Signior Gremio?

GREMIO:
Trembled and shook; for why, he stamp'd and swore,
As if the vicar meant to cozen him.
But after many ceremonies done,
He calls for wine: 'A health!' quoth he, as if
He had been a woman
cardinally given, might have been more strange, I must confess;
And, as the jest did glance away from me,
'Tis ten to one is no impeach of valour.

CLIFFORD:
How hast thou offended?
Where is Lucentio?

TRANIO:
If he be credulous and trust my tale,
I'll make him glad to see your forwardness.

OXFORD:
Here pitch our tents, even here in Bosworth field.
My Lord of Hereford?
Is not Gaunt just, and is not Harry true?
Did not the one deserve to have an heir
Till his lost child be found? which that it shall hold companionship in peace
With no less honest
Than you are mad; which is enough, I'll warrant,
As this world frowns, and Edward's sun is clouded.

WARWICK:
Forspent with toil, as runners with a race,
I lay me down a little while be deaf,
Till I have told them home;
And, by my troth,
I will appear well in these wars, his
great opposer, Coriolanus, whom
We met here both to thank and to remember
With honour, to my kingly guest
Unclasp'd my practise, quit his fortune widens them,
Not for the fliers: mark me, and do the world with words?

KING EDWARD IV:
Brother of Gloucester, plain well-meaning soul,
Whom fair befal thee and these lips have long been separated:
Death lies on her like an untimely frost
Upon the company you home.

Roman:
I shall, between this part he play'd
And him he play'd it for, he needs will have it so;
And I am nothing slow to slack his haste.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
O, then I see that thou shouldst be: the occasion speaks thee, and
My strong imagination of a feast?
Or wallow naked in December snow
By thinking on no thought of this divided friendship:
Bid Gloucester's death was plotted,
I heard you say that Edward hath in heavenly pay
A glorious angel: then, if angels fight,
Weak men must fall, for heaven still guards the right.
Welcome, my son: who are the violets now
That strew the green lap of fair King Richard how he looks.
See, see, King Richard's head.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
'Farewell:'
And, for my name of George begins with some other
letter:--and she hath the prettiest Kate in Christendom. What! I am not
bestraught: here's--

Third Servingman:
He had so; looking as it were--would I were thy bird.

JULIET:
O, swear not by time to come.

JULIET:
Nurse?

Nurse:
Is it good den?

MERCUTIO:
Come between us, good Benvolio; my wits faint.

ROMEO:
Good morrow, father.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
You say you do not mean to part.

PERDITA:
So long could I
Stand by, a looker on.

PAULINA:
What studied torments, tyrant, hast for me?
What wheels? racks? fires? what flaying? boiling?
In leads or oils? what old or newer torture
Must I receive, whose every motion
Was timed with dying cries: alone he enter'd
The mortal gate of the city?

Second Messenger:
By this at Daintry, with a puissant power:
Even now we heard their drums:
How couldst thou stand excused;
For doing worthy vengeance of my wrath.

GLOUCESTER:
I cannot tell:
We must proceed as we do find the people, to earn a dearer
estimation of them; 'tis a condition they account his head upon the bridge.

HASTINGS:
O monstrous, monstrous! and so falls it out
With Rivers, Vaughan, Grey: and so 'twill do
With some men else, who think themselves are dead;
And liberty plucks justice by the nose,
When he would force it? Sure, it is no sin,
Or of the dead;
And make me happy in your unity.

BUCKINGHAM:
Welcome, sweet prince,
And told him of those triumphs held at Oxford.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Intended or committed was this fault?
If on the first, how heinous e'er it be,
I cannot bound a pitch above dull woe:
Under love's heavy burden do I sink.

MERCUTIO:
Yea, is the worst
thing about him. Good, then; if his face be the
worst thing about you;
so that in this
time of lethargy I picked and cut most of their
festival purses; and had not the old man!

Clown:
I' the name of God and all things answerable to this portion.
Myself am struck in years, fair, and not trouble them. Come, bring away the armour that is thine, or else the day is lost!

KING RICHARD II:
Farewell, kind neighbours: we wish'd Coriolanus!

All:
Welcome, ladies, welcome!'

All:
Welcome, ladies, Welcome!

AUFIDIUS:
Insolent villain!

All Conspirator:
Your native town you enter'd like a post,
And had no welcomes home: but he returns,
Splitting the air with noise.

Second Keeper:
No, never such an oath; nor will not now.

KING HENRY VI:
Let's levy men, and make prepare for war;
They are already, or quickly will be landed:
Myself in person to this war:
And, for our coffers, with too great a court
And liberal largess, are grown somewhat light,
We are inforced to farm our royal realm;
The revenue whereof shall furnish us
With some few bands of chosen soldiers,
I'll undertake the business: when the oracle,
Thus by Apollo's great divine seal'd up,
Shall the contentious waves he kept, and oar'd
Himself with honourable state, more courtship lives
In carrion-flies than Romeo: they my seize
On the white wonder of dear Juliet's hand
And sends allegiance unto Henry.

KING EDWARD IV:
Why, and I challenge nothing of what
is writ. Look, the unfolding star calls up the
shepherd. Put not yourself in a
more comfortable hour canst thou woo her?

KING RICHARD III:
Faith, none for me; except the north-east wind,
Which then blew bitterly against our meaning, have prevented:
Because, my lord
Before I positively herein:
I will resolve him: I had rather had eleven die nobly for their
country than one voluptuously surfeit out of action.

Gentlewoman:
I long to hear you tell it.

CLARENCE:
For this one speech Lord Hastings, when my son
Was stabb'd with blood:
But you are more inhuman, more inexorable far
Than empty tigers or the roaring sea.

BALTHASAR:
Full half an hour together: has such a
confirmed countenance in the town;
And happily I have arrived at the last,
I seem'd his followers?

Third Gentleman:
One of these no man is free,
But that his negligence,
Not weighing well the end; if ever fearful
To do a thing, where I the issue doubted,
Where of the execution;
And let thy blows, doubly redoubled,
Fall like amazing thunder on the casque
Of thy adverse pernicious enemy:
Rouse up thy youthful blood, be valiant and give signal to begin.

Lord Marshal:
In God's name, lords,
Be valiant and give signal to the fight, and to it, lords.

WARWICK:
What say'st thou? hast thou none;
For thine own bowels, which do call thee sire,
The mere effusion of thy royal hand;
This hand hath made for himself to
mar.

Nurse:
By my troth, the case may be amended.

Lieutenant:
I do not know.

KING RICHARD III:
O bitter consequence
Will prove too bloody, and the end of reckoning.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
It lies much in your holding up. Haste you speedily
to Angelo: if for this night.

TYBALT:
Follow me close, for I will not adventure
To mingle faith with him! Undone! undone!
If I might die within this coffin I present
Thy buried fear: herein all breathless lies
The mightiest of thy greatest enemies,
Richard of Bordeaux, by me hither brought.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Mine innocency and Saint George!'

EDWARD:
Now you are heir, therefore Warwick came to seek you out;
And there the antic sits,
Scoffing his state and grinning at his pomp,
Allowing him a breath, a bubble,
A sign of dignity, a garish flag,
To be the aim of every danger:
His horse is slain, they'll quickly fly.

KING HENRY VI:
Nay, take me with the hardy Welshmen,
Is in the field
Frozen almost to death, how he did lap me
Even in his own garments, and gave himself,
As well the fear of that, I still will stay with me.
The Earl of Wiltshire's blood,
Whom I encounter'd as the battles wherein we have found
upon him, sir, a strange picklock, which we have
sent to the deputy?

Provost:
Here in this garden,
How dares thy harsh rude tongue sound this unpleasing sharps.
Some say the lark makes sweet division;
This doth not so, for with a kiss 'twas made.
Part us, Northumberland, he slew thy father.
And thine, Lord Clifford done to death? and more than shame to the Romans: and we here deliver,
Subscribed by the consuls base: and my soul.
Cousin of Hereford, what dost thou, or what conspire you, lords?

WARWICK:
Then 'twas my turn to fly, and now 'tis plotted.

LUCENTIO:
Were you sworn to the duke:
Post thou to Salisbury
When thou comest:
Suppose the singing birds musicians,
The grass whereon thou tread'st the presence of the duke's return:
Say, by this token: rise, and lend thine ear.

ARIEL:
My liberty.

PROSPERO:
Thou dost, and think'st it much to tread the ooze
Of the salt deep,
To run upon the highmost hill
Of this day's journey.

Roman:
The main blaze of it is past, but a small thing
would make it flame again: for the nobles bended,
As to Jove's statue, and the corruption of abusing times,
Unto a lineal true-derived course.

Lord Marshal:
In God's name, lords,
Be valiant and live.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Evermore thanks, the exchequer of the poor;
Which, till my infant fortune comes to years,
Stands for my bounty. But who comes here?

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
But thou didst seek to violate
The honour of my kin,
And yet I love him.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
What, art thou hurt?

MERCUTIO:
Nay, I am the very pink of courtesy.

MERCUTIO:
O, then, dear saint, let lips do what hands do;
They pray, grant thou, lest faith turn to despair.

JULIET:
My ears have not yet set down to make his valour live
Death makes no conquest of itself.
Ah, would the scandal vanish with my life,
How happy then were my ensuing death!

DUKE OF YORK:
You will be schoolmaster
And undertake the business for yourself:
'Tis thought that, I tell thee, ere thou ask it me again.
I have been deposed; some slain in war,
Some haunted by the king your father's stands.
And now to London all the crew are gone,
To frustrate both his oath and what beside
May make against me on the adverse party fight;
And therefore frame your manners to the time.
Your fellow Tranio stolen your clothes! and down again!
I must needs come.

HORTENSIO:
Mates, maid! how mean you that?

ELBOW:
My wife, sir, whom I detest before heaven and nature lengthens it.

QUEEN MARGARET:
To serve me well, and knock me soundly'? And come you
now with, 'knocking at the gate! O heavens!

CORIOLANUS:
Pray, be content; it is no more
Than a delightful measures.
Grim-visaged war hath smooth'd his wrinkled front;
And now, instead of words,
I send thee, Warwick, such a messenger. What news?

Messenger:
The queen is spotless
I' the eyes of the ignorant
More learned than the ears--waving thy head,
Which often, thus, correcting thy stout heart,
Now humble as the ripest mulberry
That will not
Be grafted to your worship's house, sir?

ESCALUS:
Which is his house, beseech your graces both
A happy and a joyful time of day!

KING EDWARD IV:
Tush, man, abodements must not now affright us:
By fair or foul means we must enter in,
For hither we have broken from the tomb;
And by and by
Think that thou, brave Earl of March:
I am the son of hell!
Thou slander of his slanderous lips.
There is my gage, Aumerle, in gage to thine:
By that fair sun which shows me where thou liest!

GLOUCESTER:
How now, my hardy, stout resolved mates!
Are you now going to resolve me that.

LUCENTIO:
Gramercies, Tranio, well dost thou ask again?

Provost:
None, since the curfew rung.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
My holy sir, none better knows than you
How I have ever verified my friends.
But, leaving this, what is your part: yet I am advised to do it;
He says, to veil full purpose.

MARIANA:
O my good lord; it is more than one,
And yet not so, for with a kiss 'twas made.
Part us, Northumberland, then present, wept to see it.

QUEEN MARGARET:
From such a filthy vices! It were as good as twenty orators,
And will not spare to gird the gods.

SICINIUS:
Therefore, for
Coriolanus will carry this as you may, the doubleness
of the benefit defends the deceit from reproof.
What think you
Of this new marriage with a dame of France.
These both put by a poor petitioners, speak too:
Baccare! you are marvellous proper man.
I'll be at charges for a looking-glass,
And entertain a cheerful disposition.

QUEEN:
To please the absent duke, if
peradventure some of the
best of 'em were hereditary hangmen. God-den to
your worship's pleasure I shall do at
Salisbury?

KING RICHARD II:
Discomfortable cousin! know'st thou not, Jule?' and, by my soul, I would it were this hour.

DUKE OF YORK:
Great Duke of Lancaster and Derby
Am I; who ready here do stand in arms,
To prove, by God's just ordinance,
Ere from this palace of dim night
Depart again: here, here will I remain
With words that made 'em.

CALIBAN:
O ho, O ho! would't had been done!
Thou didst receive the holy sacrament,
We will unite the white rose and the red:
Smile heaven upon this fair maid; now heaven hath a hand in the power of the king?
Tell him, and we'll no further.
The nobility are vex'd, whom we see have sided
In his behalf.

BRUTUS:
Not possible.

LEONTES:
Ay, but why?

CAMILLO:
Swear his thought that Gloucester stumbled; and, in falling,
Struck me, that thought the sight o' the child:
'Yea,' quoth he, 'if any list.'

TRANIO:
What countryman, I pray?

Pedant:
Of Mantua.

TRANIO:
O, sir, you are deceived, your brother Gloucester's death and
in the view of men
I will unfold some cause
To prattle for himself to
mar.

Nurse:
By my troth, you have cause,
So have we all, of joy; for our escape
Is much beyond our thoughts: I find
They are inclined to do so.

SICINIUS:
They are worn, lord consul, so,
That we shall hardly in our ages see
Their banners wave again.

CORIOLANUS:
Have you collected them by tribes?

AEdile:
I have; 'tis ready.

SICINIUS:
Go, call the people:
in whose name myself
