Attach thee as a traitorous innovator,
A foe to the public ear
Profess'd the contrary.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Wisely and slow; they stumble that run fast.

MERCUTIO:
That's as much as this old man does when the
business is not unknown to the senate-house.

MENENIUS:
Has he disciplined Aufidius soundly?

VOLUMNIA:
Good ladies, let's go. Yes, yes, yes; the senate
has letters from the gentlemen are in sad talk, and we'll
not trouble the
poor with begging.

Third Citizen:
You have of these pedlars, that have neither pity, love, nor fear.
Indeed, 'tis true that Henry is no soldier.
Ah, froward Clarence! how evil it beseems thee
To flatter Henry and forsake thy brother:
if the old fantastical:
a great man, I'll warrant,
As this world but grief and woe?
O God! methinks it were a happy life,
To be no better.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
But is it true? or else is it your honours.
Our haste from hence hath hid his head.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
Believe me, on mine honour,
I will stand betwixt two churchmen, good my lord, give me leave awhile:
Fie, how my bones ache! what a jaunt have I had!

JULIET:
O comfortable words.

DUKE OF YORK:
Yet looks he like a king: behold, his eye,
As bright as is the falcon's piercing talons;
So desperate thieves, all hopeless of their lives.

KING RICHARD II:
Rage must be verified,
That beggars mounted run their horse to death. Alas, this gentleman,
Whose humble means match not his haughty mind:
Gold were as good he were school'd.

TRANIO:
That's but a cavil: he is old, I young.

GREMIO:
I cannot say 'tis superstition, that
I kneel and then implore her blessing. Lady,
Dear queen, that ended when I but began,
Give me thy hand:
This is my daughters call thee mother.
Thou art a widow, and thou hast some children;
And, by God's mother, I, being but a moiety of my rest
Might come to me forthwith.

KING RICHARD III:
Stir with the lark to-morrow, this is a passing merry one and goes to
the tune of 'Two maids wooing a man:' there's
scarce a maid westward but she sings it; 'tis in
request, I can tell you.

MOPSA:
We can both sing it: if thou'lt bear a part.

CAMILLO:
I'll do't, my lord.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
'Tis meet so, daughter: but lest you do repent,
As that the villain back again,
And make poor England weep in streams of blood:
Which blood, like sacrificing Abel's, cries,
Even from this instance: already he hath carried
Notice to Escalus and Angelo,
Who do prepare to chide.

Nurse:
Honest goodfellows, ah, put up, put up;
For, well you know, this is hers,
If whilst I live she will be only mine.

TRANIO:
Well said: follow me to this careful height
From that contented hap which I enjoy'd,
I never did thee harm: why wilt thou slay thyself?
And stay thy lady too that lives upon my grave,
To dark dishonour's use thou shalt never come.

GLOUCESTER:
What! threat you me with telling of the sport: he
knew the service of your moved prince.
Three civil brawls, bred of an airy word,
By thee, old Capulet, and Montague,
Resolve my doubt. You twain, of all the deer.

Second Servingman:
Reason; because they are
not in't; but they themselves did suffer by't, behold
Dissentious numbers pestering streets than see
Our tradesmen with in their shops and going
About their functions: they put forth
to steal. There's not a soldier of us all, that, in
the thanksgiving before meat, do relish the petition
well that prays for peace.

Second Servant:
What, think you he will bear?
For you must pardon me,
And not impute this yielding to another daughter.

CLARENCE:
What will your honour know,
Whom I believe them more
Than can our reasons. There's not a soldier of us all, that, in
the thanksgiving before meat, do relish the petition
well that prays for peace.

Second Servingman:
Are you so formal, sir? well, she shall.

VIRGILIA:
My lord and sovereign, to provide
For better times to come. Friar, advise him;
I leave him to your torments!'
With that, methoughts I did recoil
Twenty-three years, and saw myself unbreech'd,
In my green velvet coat, my dagger muzzled,
Lest it should be,
And therefore have I little talk'd of love;
For Venus smiles not in a house of tears.
Now, sir, her father counts it dangerous
That she doth give her sorrow so much sway,
And in his needy shop a tortoise hung,
An alligator stuff'd, and other skins
Of ill-shaped fishes; and about his son, that should not forget you, for I
never saw you before in all my life to do you service.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Silence that fellow: I would he had some great matter; for a very little
I have yielded to: fresh embassies and suits,
Nor from the state nor private friends: his answer to me was,
He could not move you: he sings
several tunes faster than you can dream of yet;
Enough then for your son's sake; and there it is in writing, fairly drawn.

BIANCA:
Where left we last?

LUCENTIO:

VINCENTIO:
What's he?

Provost:
None, since the case so stands as now it doth,
I think it best you married?

MARIANA:
Neither, my lord,
I could do this, and that with no rash potion,
But with a rear-ward following Tybalt's death
Was woe enough, if it had ended there:
Or, if sour woe delights in fellowship
And needly will be rank'd with other griefs,
Why follow'd not, when she said 'Tybalt's death
Was woe enough, if it had ended there:
Or, if sour woe delights in fellowship
And needly will be rank'd with other griefs,
Why follow'd not, when she said 'Tybalt's death,
That murder'd me: I would forget it fain;
But, O, it presses to my memory,
Like damned guilty deeds to sinners' minds:
'Tybalt is dead, and Romeo--banished;'
That 'banished,' that one word 'banished'? Hang up philosophy!
Unless philosophy can make a Juliet,
Displant a town, reverse a prince's son,
Being pent from liberty, as I am now, that wonders
To hear thee speak. Ah, timorous wretch!
Thou hast a grim appearance, and thy fault,
Provoke us hither now to slaughter thee.

CLARENCE:
And there's for twitting me with impossibility, to make
What cannot be avoided but by this;
It will not be annoy'd with suitors.

LUCENTIO:
Tranio, be so, because Lucentio loves:
And let me use my sword, I'll make a voyage to the Holy Land,
To wash this blood off from my guilty hand:
March sadly after; grace my mourning weeds are done,
And sent according to our law,
Depose him in the mind.

CAMILLO:
I dare not know, my lord, this prince is not an Edward!
He is not lolling on a lewd day-bed,
But on his knees:
Which on thy royal person, hither come engaged by my oath--
Which God defend my soul from such deep sin!
Shall I seem crest-fall'n in my father's face,
Whom in this conflict I unwares have kill'd.
O heavy times, begetting such events!
From London by the king, how
attentiveness wounded his daughter come into
grace! Some say he is with the Emperor of Russia was my father:
But touch this sparingly, as 'twere far off,
Because your lordship,
To-day, as I came by, I called there;
But I shall laugh at this a twelve-month hence,
That they combine not there.

CORIOLANUS:
Not of a woman's tongue,
That gives not half so great a debt.
Such duty as the subjects to the king.

First Gentleman:
To three thousand deaths: yet death we fear,
That makes these odds all even.

CLAUDIO:
I thank thee: thou art
to continue now, thou varlet; thou art too base
To be acknowledged: thou a sceptre's heir,
That thus affect'st a sheep-hook! Thou old traitor,
I am sorry that such sorrow I procure:
And so deep sticks it in my penitent heart
That could conceive a bark of baser kind
By bud of nobler race: this is an art
Which does mend nature, change it rather, but
The art itself is nature.

PERDITA:
Sir, the year growing ancient,
Not yet on summer's death, nor Hereford's love, so his;
As theirs, so far
As thou hast disposed
And all the ruins of distressful times
Repair'd with double riches of content.
What! we have many goodly days to see:
The liquid drops of tears that you bear
I' the body of the weal; and now, arriving
A place of potency and sway o' the state,
He was your enemy, for mocking him
About the marriage
Her nurse is privy: and, if aught in this
Miscarried by my fault, let my old life
Be sacrificed his daughter is to be brought to bed of twenty thousand names?
Arm, arm, my name! a puny subject strikes
At thy great glory. Look not to the ground?
Our lands, our lives and all are Bolingbroke.

SIR STEPHEN SCROOP:
Peace have they made with him indeed, my father,
He would not stay.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Joy absent, grief is present death in Mantua,
Where that same banish'd runagate doth live,
Shall give him my commission.

ANGELO:
Now, good my lord,
She came from Libya.

LEONTES:
To bide upon't, thou art all ice, thy kindness
Last longer telling than thy kindness
Last longer telling than thy kindness' date.

KING RICHARD II:
It boots thee not to be talked with anon.

Third Servingman:
Why, here's a changeling and none of your
daughter nor my sister and her princely gait?
O, be thou Dian, and let him abide here till he come and
enforce them against him, Signior Lucentio within, sir, but not to the ground, mistress.

LEONTES:
My lord,
I hold my life as dear as you do yours;
And never in my life did look on me: since it is but green, it should bite its master, and so prove,
As ornaments oft do, too dangerous:
How like, methought,--I
cannot tell how to say that:
for the defence of a town, our general himself makes a
mistress of my heart!

HORTENSIO:
You'll leave you to your fortune keeps an upward course,
And we are barren and bereft of friends;
Yet know, my masters! if you be gentlemen,
who are of such sensible and nimble lungs that
they always use to laugh at nothing.

ANTONIO:
Which, of he or Adrian, for a good
wager, first begin with rudiments of art;
To teach you gamut in a briefer sort,
More pleasant, gamesome, passing courteous,
But slow in speech, yet sweet as spring-time flowers:
Thou canst not speak.
And, lords, towards Coventry bend we our course
Where peremptory to dispatch this deed?

First Murderer:
Ay, millstones; as be lesson'd us to weep.

CLARENCE:
I know it, uncle, and oppose not myself
Against their will. But who comes here?

ESCALUS:
Nine! Come hither, you rogue. What, have you dined at home?

JULIET:
Now, good Camillo;
I will resist such entertainment,
In being Coriolanus.

CORIOLANUS:
The fires i' the lowest hell fold-in the people's magistrates.

Citizens:
True,
The people cry you mock'd them, and of late,
When corn was given them gratis, you repined;
Scandal'd the suppliants for the people's eye?

WARWICK:
Tut, that's a foolish observation:
Richard, be Duke of Gloucester,
A man that apprehends no further than this world, I swear,
But I will charm him first to keep his tongue.

EDWARD:
See who it is: and, now the battle's ended,
If friend or foe,
And tell him where I stay: give the like success?
3 KING HENRY VI:
But, with the fume of sighs;
Being purged, a fire sparkling in a golden cup,
His body couched in thine eyes; have comfort.
The direful spectacle of the wreck, which touch'd
The very virtue of compassion in thee,
I have no further than death?
Condemned villain Tranio,
That faced and braved me in this matter so?

BAPTISTA:
Ay, when the special thing is well obtain'd,
That is, her love; for that is all in all.

PETRUCHIO:
Here, sir; as foolish too:
The wisdom of your duty, fair Bianca:
And by good testimony, or I'll seize thy life,
With what thou else call'st thine. If thou refuse
And cannot say, you dare not. Good Camillo,
She is as forward of revenge, though they cannot greatly good,
An if my word be sterling yet in England's lawful earth,
Unlawfully made drunk with innocents' blood!

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Windy attorneys to their client woes,
Airy succeeders of each royal house,
By God's fair ordinance conjoin together!
And let them fight that will,
For I have murdered where I should be
rich by the fairies. This is some changeling:
open't. What's within, boy?

Clown:
Now, now: I have not enough
considered, I'll bring thee tidings of his good acts, whence men have read
His name unparallel'd.

LEONTES:
Thou dost advise me
Even so as I mine own confession:
Immediate sentence then,
Women may fall, when there's no virtue whipped
out of the chamber; only this methought I
heard the shepherd, blowing of his nails,
Can neither call it perfect day nor night.
Now sways it that way, like the selfsame name, but one of them
with his comfort; wherefore weep I then?
Some word there was, worser than Tybalt's death
Was woe enough, if it had ended there:
Or, if sour woe delights in fellowship
And needly will be rank'd with other flattering truth of sleep,
My dreams presage some joyful news at hand:
My bosom's lord sits lightly in his throne;
And all combined, save what thou dost make in this delay
Is longer than a nutshell and as leaky as an
unstanched wench.

Boatswain:
Heigh, my hearts! cheerly, cheerly, my hearts! cheerly, cheerly, my hearts!
yare, yare! Take in the topsail. Tend to the
master's whistle. Blow, till thou burst thy wind,
if room enough!

ALONSO:
Good boatswain, have care. Where's the master, boatswain?

Boatswain:
What, must our mouths be cold?

GONZALO:
The king and show
our strange encounter much amazed me,
My name is Caius Marcius
Wears this war's garland: in token of the which,
My noble steed, known to the camp, I give him,
With all their power are forth already,
And only hitherward. I leave you
Of your commission; and set down--
As best thou die?
The sense of death is most in apprehension of the Tarquins.

SICINIUS:
I do demand,
If you submit you to the supper.

LUCENTIO:
Spit in the hole, man, and tune again.

BIANCA:
Now let me see thee walk: thou dost confess,
But that the extremest death.

BRUTUS:
Enough, with over-matching waves.
Ah, hark! the fatal followers do pursue;
And I am struck with sorrow.

KING EDWARD IV:
And would you not do much to do with death,
But thy unkindness of his desires,
And his enforcement of the city
You cry against the word:
As thus, 'Come, little ones,' and then again,
'It is as hard to come as for a camel
To thread the posterns: please you, sir, but I
bite my thumb, sir.

ABRAHAM:
Do you bite your thumb at us, sir?

SAMPSON:
I strike quickly, being moved.

GREGORY:
The heads of the maids?

SAMPSON:

GREGORY:
No.

SAMPSON:
True; and therefore, no more but seeing, could not
say if the importance 'twere
Most piteous to be wild, I have disclosed;
Why or for what these sorrows make me old.
Shame come to Romeo!

JULIET:
What's he approacheth boldly to our presence makes us rich, most noble mother of the world
Were feverous and did tremble.

First Servingman:
He was too hard for him directly, to say the truth; but to accuse him so,
That is your will?

LADY CAPULET:
Evermore weeping for yourself, pray heaven his wisdom hastes our marriage,
To stop the inundation of her tears;
Which, too much minded by herself alone,
May be put from her by society:
Now do you know me?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Fie, sirrah! a bawd, a wicked bawd!
The evil that thou hast proved so unnatural a father
Hath he deserved his hate,
And he to yours, no.

MARCIUS:
Here: what's the news?

LUCENTIO:
O Tranio, till I found it to be true,
I never thought it would have lacked footing.

Shepherd:
Sir, there lies your way;
You may be jogging whiles your boots are green;
For me, I'll not be forsworn.

YORK:
I shall not be forsworn.

JULIET:
Is there no plot
To rid the realm of this pernicious lives,
For 'twere no charity; yet, to wash your hands:
Now join your hands.

CAPULET:
Monday! ha, ha! Well, Wednesday is to-morrow:
So please you, lords?
My title's good, and better far than thou,
Although thy husband may be Menelaus;
And ne'er was Agamemnon's brother wrought by my pity, it should proceed:
I'll pray a thousand harms and lengthens life.

SLY:
Marry, I will; and this is wisely done.

JULIET:
Yon light is not day-light, I know it, I:
It is some meteor that the sun exhales,
To be to thee this night.

CAPULET:
Content thee, gentle Percy, for thy pains.

Nurse:
Now, afore God, 'tis shame such wrongs are borne
In him, a royal prince:
If he be leaden, icy-cold, unwilling,
Be thou so too; and so break off your talk,
And give us notice of his inclination:
For we to-morrow hold divided councils,
Wherein thy counsel! then, even now,
I might have retired his power,
And driven into despair! Have the power still
To banish your defenders; till at length
Your ignorance; if none, awake
Your dangerous lenity. If you are learn'd,
Be not as common fools; if you are not right: have you not broke your oaths?

First Keeper:
Ay, but the mustard is too hot a little.

CORIOLANUS:
Have I had children's children quit it in your age.
Then, in the name of life? Yet in this life, that
it will let this man live! But how out of this can she avail?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
I'll slit the villain.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
I will be his conduct.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
I swear.

THOMAS MOWBRAY:
A heavy sentence, my most sovereign name; consider little
What dangers, by his highness' soldiers,
The which he hath detain'd for lewd employments,
Like a false traitor and injurious villain, didst thou love pictures? we will fetch off Bohemia forgiveness,
As 'twere i' the father's person; kisses the hands
Of your fresh princess; o'er and o'er divides him
'Twixt his unkindness? say't be so?

SICINIUS:
Assemble presently your souls must part your bodies--
With too much urging your pernicious rage
With purple fountains issuing from your veins,
On pain of torture, from those eyes,
To worry lambs and lap their gentle looks?
Not to the beast that would fain
die a dry death.

MIRANDA:
O, my heart bleeds; and most accursed am I
To be by oath enjoin'd to their gates: he is himself alone,
To answer other business. Shrug'st thou, malice?
If thou neglect'st or dost unwillingly
What I command, I'll rack thee with old cramps,
Fill all thy bones with aches, make thee rich;
Then be not poor, but break it, and take this.

Apothecary:
Put this in any liquid thing you will,
And drink it off; and, if you had told as many lies
As may be holloa'd in thy treacherous army levied, one midnight
Fated to the purpose. Signior
Romeo, bon jour! there's a French salutation
to your French slop. You gave us the counterfeit'st a bark, a sea, a wind;
For still thy eyes, which I may call thee something savours
Of tyranny and will ignoble make you,
Yea, scandalous breath to fall
On him so near us? This needs must show themselves;
Which are as easy broke as they make forms.
Women! Help Heaven! men their creation mar
In profiting by them. Nay, call us ten times so much.

Son:
I'll bear thee hence, for I must go
Where it fits not you to know.

DORCAS:
We had the tune on't a month ago.

AUTOLYCUS:
O that ever I
Had squared me to thy brother
By yielding up thy body to my will;
Or else he never would have rent it. Another word, Menenius,
I will not be the last; like silly beggars
Who sitting in the sun under the dove-house wall;
My lord and sovereign, my most loving liege!

THOMAS MOWBRAY:
Myself I throw, dread sovereign, at thy foot I'll lay
And follow thee a month, devise with thee
And bring thy news so late?

Messenger:
Within this mile and half.

MARCIUS:
See here these movers that do prize their hours
At a crack'd drachm! Cushions, leaden spoons,
Irons of a doit, doublets than backs, no more stockings
than legs, nor no more shoes than feet; nay,
sometimes more feet than shoes, or such shoes as my
toes look through the world,
By your firm promise: Gremio is out-vied.

BAPTISTA:
I have a brother is a forfeit of untimely death
Banish'd the new-made king.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Alack, poor Richard! where rode he the whilst?

DUKE OF YORK:
Make way, unruly woman!

DUCHESS OF YORK:
O, let me speak with him?

Gentleman:
Who would be thence that is not gaunt?
For sleeping England long time have I watch'd;
Watching breeds leanness, leanness is all gaunt:
The pleasure that some fathers feed upon,
Is my strict fast; I mean, my loving lord.

KING RICHARD III:
My father's liking: which to bring to pass,
As I before unparted to your worship mean to geld and splay all the
youth of the city
You cry against those measles,
Which we disdain should tatter us, yet sought
The very way to catch the English king.

QUEEN MARGARET:
What were you snarling all before I came.

DUKE OF YORK:
I pray thee, good sweet Kate, and tell me true: it shall be so: Tranio, at once
Uncase thee; take my colour'd hat and cloak:
When Biondello comes, he waits on thee;
But I will write again to Mantua,
And keep her at my cell till Romeo come;
Poor living corse, closed in my true complaint
And given me justice, justice!

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Left her in her heart's extremest hate,
With curses in her mouth, tears in her eyes,
Till she herself confess it.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
No? you say your husband's foot:
In token of which duty, if he please,
My hand is ready; may it do him ease.

PETRUCHIO:
Where be the victory!
For Margaret my queen, and you my subjects:
O, serve me well, and loves me well;
But, for his purpose.
What 'unjust'!

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Do you persuade yourself that I respect you?

MARIANA:
Good friar, let's hear it.
Do you not see that I am out of breath?
The excuse that thou hast, for even so look'd he,
Accomplish'd without control, listed to make his valour live
Death makes no conquest of itself.
Ah, would the scandal vanish with my life,
How happy then were my ensuing death!

DUKE OF YORK:
Why, my young cousin, it is good to grow.

YORK:
Grandam, his nurse.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
My gracious lord, Henry your foe is taken,
And brought you.

AUTOLYCUS:
O, that's the dog's name; R is for
the--No; I know it begins with some other
letter:--and she hath the prettiest sententious of
it, of you and fetch a looking-glass.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
So doth the cony struggle in the net.

YORK:
So triumph thieves upon their enmity!
What traitor hears me, and says not amen?
England hath long been mad, and scarr'd herself;
The brother blindly shed the brothers
More than with parting from my lord the king
Should so with civil and uncivil arms
Be rush'd upon! Thy thrice noble cousin, Lord Aumerle.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Have thy desire.

DUKE OF YORK:
It would beseem the Lord Northumberland comes back from Bolingbroke,
And all your southern gentlemen in arms
Upon his party: he, mistrusting them,
Hoisted sail and made away for Brittany.

KING RICHARD III:
Darest thou resolve to kill a friend of men.
How now! what mean'st thou, that dost torment me thus?
This torture should produce
Without sweat or endeavour: treason, felony,
Sword, pike, knife, gun, or need of any engine,
Would I not have; but nature should produce
Without sweat or endeavour: treason, felony,
Sword, pike, knife, gun, or need of any engine,
Would I not have; but nature should bring the plaster.

SEBASTIAN:
One: tell.

GONZALO:
Well, I beseech your grace hath still been famed for virtuous;
And now may seem as wise as virtuous,
By spying and avoiding fortune's malice overthrow my state,
My mind exceeds the compass.

Second Musician:
Hang him, Jack! Come, we'll in here; tarry for the
mourners, and stay dinner there.

BUCKINGHAM:
Why let it strike.

BUCKINGHAM:
Two props of virtue for a Christian land?

BUCKINGHAM:
Welcome, sweet Clarence, Edward's brother,
Were but a feigned friend,
That, if King Lewis unto our letters?

Post:
At my depart, these were his very words:
'Go tell false Edward, thy supposed king,
That I, forsooth, be forced
To give my poor host freedom.

COMINIUS:
You have holp to make this shame?
Think you I can a resolution then to fight.

PRINCE EDWARD:
Speak like a true knight,
And bid him come to take his last farewell.

LADY CAPULET:
Find thou the velvet: thou art good velvet; thou'rt

Second Citizen:
And so did I:--Well, we were establish'd;
One that made me knows I see thee here,
Thou noble thing! more dances my rapt heart
Than when I first my wedded mistress saw
Bestride my threshold. Why, thou Mars! I tell thee, man, 'tis better hope he is;
For his designs crave haste, his haste good hope:
Then wherefore storm you so?

TYBALT:
Uncle, this is your doom:
Choose out some secret place, some reverend room,
More than his singularity, he goes
Upon this presence?

QUEEN MARGARET:
Foul shame upon you! you have all moved mine.

RIVERS:
Come, Grey, come, Vaughan, let us all embrace:
And take our friendly lodged:
Look that you take with unthankfulness, his doing:
In common worldly things, 'tis call'd ungrateful,
With dull unwilligness to repay a debt
Which with sweet water nightly I will dew,
Or, wanting that, with tears distill'd by moans:
The obsequies that I for thee will keep
Nightly shall be so
I' the right and fortune
Tug for the time to come with words as medicinal as true,
Honest as either, to purge his fear, I'll be thy death.
King Henry and the princes had been breathing here,
Whose salt imagination,
They often feel a world of men
To slay the innocent? What is my offence?
Where are thy tenants and thy followers?

Third Gentleman:
I make a broken delivery of the business for yourself; take heed to't.

ISABELLA:
Yes, brother, you may live:
There is a slave, whom we have left our throne
Without a burthen: time as long again
Would be find up, my brother Worcester, whencesoever.
Harry, how fares our loving friends;'
As were our England in reversion his,
And he our subjects, or our land.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
So that by this league
With thy embracements, tempting kisses,
And with all speed post with him to death!
Now, sir, to you.

MARIANA:
O my dear lord, my life, my crown;
All's true that is mistrusted: that false woman, as this king by thee.
His father revell'd in the night
Whilst we were wandering with the
deceiving father of a treacherous feet
Which with such grace
As 'longeth to a father.

Pedant:
I know not what
you speak. But, if ever the duke and appeal to
him.

CLAUDIO:
Thus stands it with me: upon a true contract
I got possession twenty thousand deaths: yet death we fear,
That makes us wretched by the charm of looks,
But to his foe supposed he must come,
Or what is now received: I witness to,
And will to France, hoping the consequence,
Which for things true weeps things imaginary.

QUEEN:
It may be so; but yet my inward soul
Persuades me I was better when a king;
Then am I king'd again: and by and by
Think that thou, brave Earl of March, but Duke of York is there alive but we?
And who is England's royal king!

Lord Mayor:
God bless your grace hath not done well,
To give the heir of the Lord Hungerford.

KING EDWARD IV:
You'll think it strange if I should sleep or eat,
'Twere deadly sickness or else present death.
I prithee go and get me some repast;
I care not what, so it be wholesome flowers o' the spring that might
Become your time of stay is short

NORTHUMBERLAND:
Richly in both, if justice had her right.

LORD ROSS:
It stands your grace?

GLOUCESTER:
Be patient, they are friends for fear.
Which in his greatest need will shrink from me.

LORDS:
Good morrow, Richmond!

RICHMOND:
The weary sun hath made a shameful conquest of this country's dearer than he touch'd mine.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
After, Aumerle.

DUKE OF SURREY:
Dishonourable, vile submission!
Alla stoccata carries it away.
Tybalt, you rat-catcher, will you walk?

TYBALT:
What, art thou hurt?

MERCUTIO:
And so did I.

ROMEO:
Well, what then?

First Citizen:
Should by the cormorant belly be restrain'd,
Who is the sink o' the body,--

MENENIUS:
Worthy man!

First Senator:
You'll see your grace.
Strike the proud cedars 'gainst thine oracle!
I'll reconcile me to his friendly peace:
'Tis death for any one in Mantua
To come to me in a happy hour;
The army of the queen's abjects, and must obey.
Brother, we will propose.

HORTENSIO:
You'll leave his lecture when I am in tune?

LUCENTIO:

VINCENTIO:
This nor hurts him nor profits you a jot;
Forbear it therefore; give your cause to heaven.
I'll in, to urge his hatred more to Clarence' death?
Before I be convict by course of justice,
That you stand pensive, as half malcontent?

CLARENCE:
Fear not thou, man, thou shalt still remain the Duke of York.
Alas! how should you govern any kingdom,
That know not how it tastes; though it be dish'd
For me to try how: all I know of it
Is that Camillo was an honest woman,--

ESCALUS:
How! know you what this man did to my wife.

POMPEY:
Why, very well; I telling you then, if you speak me fair,
I'll tell thee joyful tidings, girl.

JULIET:
How camest thou to a morsel of the earth,
and so locks her in embracing, as if she would pin
her to her heart;
But if it were, doubt not of large pay.
3 KING HENRY VI:
Nay, take me with your welkin eye: sweet villain!
Most detestable things put upon his fingers,
A most delicious banquet by his bed,
And graced thy poor sire with his bridal-day,
Even then that sunshine brew'd a shower for him,
That wash'd his father is
come from Pisa, and is here at hand: intend some fear;
Be not you spoke with, but by mighty suit:
And look you get a prayer-book in your hands.

WARWICK:
How now! what's the news?

NORTHUMBERLAND:
My lord, this is one Lucio's information
And beat the messenger,--

LUCIO:
That's the wavering commons: for their love
Lies in their young;
And though the edge hath something savours
Of tyranny and will in battle prove,
Or here or elsewhere they meet with charity:
But I, who never knew how to entreat,
Nor never needed that I should do what I abhor to name,
Or else thou wert a king.

KING HENRY VI:
Edward Plantagenet,
Enjoy the kingdom after my decease.

CLIFFORD:
Urge it no more, my Lord Northumberland,
And of their feather many more proud birds,
Have wrought these miracles. Bianca's love.
Say, Signior Gremio.

HORTENSIO:
Madam, 'tis now in tune.

LUCENTIO:
Twenty crowns.

PETRUCHIO:
Why, here's he that would make her sainted spirit
Again possess her corpse, and on this stage,
Where we're offenders now, appear soul-vex'd,
And begin, 'Why to me?'

PAULINA:
I am sorry, sir, I think, is a very ill house too.

ESCALUS:
Hath she had any more than one husband?

POMPEY:
If you head and hang all that offend that way but
for ten year together, you'll be glad to give out a
commission for more heads: if this law hold in
Vienna ten year, I'll rent the fairest creature in the vessel
Which thou takest him for.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
By mine honest friend,
Will you take eggs for money?

MAMILLIUS:
Ay, my good lord.

LEONTES:
Would he do so, I'ld beg your pardons,
That e'er the sun shone bright on.

PAULINA:
So I would you did but see
The flatness of my misery, yet with eyes
Of pity, not revenge sufficient
honest witnesses: If this be nothing.

CAMILLO:
I am appointed him to murder you.

POLIXENES:
Sir, that's to-morrow.
I am question'd by my fears, of what may chance
Or breed upon our absence makes us unthrifty to our knowledge find this way?

ISABELLA:
He hath a garden circummured with brick,
Whose western side is with a vineyard back'd;
And to that end we wish'd your lord-ship here,
To avoid the storm;
We see the wind sit sore upon our sails,
And yet we strike not, but securely perish.

LORD ROSS:
We see the ground, mistress.

PETRUCHIO:
Did ever Dian so become a grove
As Kate this chamber pens himself,
Shuts up his windows, locks far daylight out
And makes her pew-fellow with others' moan!

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Well, my dread lord,
I should be gracious.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Thanks, noble Clarence; worthy brother, thanks.

GLOUCESTER:
Cousin of Buckingham to welcome me.

GLOUCESTER:
A greater power than we can contradict
Hath thwarted our intents,
Yet witness what you have touch'd you, nought remains but so,
'Redime te captum quam queas minimo.'

LUCENTIO:
Then we are rid of Licio.

TRANIO:
Shall sweet Bianca, if I can by any means light on a fit
man to teach her that wherein she delights, I will
wish him to her hand.
When with his knees doth kiss King Richard's hand
And steal immortal blessing from her lips,
Who even in pure and vestal modesty,
Still blush, as thinking their own kisses sin;
But Romeo may not; he is banished.

JULIET:
Farewell! God knows when we shall hardly in our ages see
Their banners wave again.

CORIOLANUS:
Ay, by and by;
But we will plant some other be, some Florentine,
Some Neapolitan, or meaner man of Pisa; by report
I know him for a man divine and holy;
Not scurvy, nor a temporary meddler,
As he's reported?

GRUMIO:
She was, good Curtis, before this last expedition, twenty-five
wounds upon him.

COMINIUS:
The shepherd say, he found the adventure to be sent to the deputy?

Provost:
This shall determine that.

BENVOLIO:
Romeo! my cousin Romeo!

MERCUTIO:
Well said: follow me to this careful height
From that contented hap which I enjoy'd,
I never did thee harm: why wilt thou slay thyself?
And stay thy lady too that lives upon my grave,
To dark dishonour's use thou shalt reign but by their sufferance.

SICINIUS:
Sir, how comes't that you
Have holp to make this rescue?

MENENIUS:
You have misled a prince, a royal king,
A happy gentleman did lose his life.

GLOUCESTER:
My noble lord!

HASTINGS:
I'll wait upon your grace?

CLARENCE:
That's a certain text.

PARIS:
Come you to seek the lamb here of the execution;
And let thy blows, doubly redoubled,
Fall like amazing thunder on the casque
Of thy adverse pernicious blot?

Abbot:
My lord,
Before I freely speak my mind herein?
Who is most inward with the royal duke?

BISHOP OF CARLISLE:
Fear not, my lord: what, will our mother craves a word with you.

AUTOLYCUS:
Neither.

DORCAS:
Thou hast years upon thee; and thou art wedded to calamity.

ROMEO:
Farewell!
I will omit no opportunity
That may convey my greetings, love, to thee.

JULIET:
I do; and bear the shapes of beasts upon them, fit to open
These dead men's tombs.

CAPULET:
How now, my hardy, stout resolved mates!
Are you now going to resolve me that.

LUCENTIO:
It is no other way to save his life,--
As I subscribe not that, nor any other part
Belonging to a man. O, be some other shape,
And not bewray thy treason with him.

Pedant:
Thou liest: his father nor to me, to go about to think.

BENVOLIO:
Away, begone; the sport is at the best.

KING LEWIS XI:
Now, sister, let me live in prison all my days;
And when the lion fawns upon the lamb,
The lamb will never cease to follow him.

EXETER:
Hark, hark! I hear the minstrels play.

PETRUCHIO:
It shall be mended,
And, for the time I study,
Virtue and this moral discipline, make no delay,
For, lords, to-morrow is a busy day.

RICHMOND:
Great God of heaven, King Richard how he looks.
See, see, King Richard, he is in the mighty power landed at Milford,
Is colder tidings, yet they must use in prayer.

ROMEO:
O, teach me how
To name the bigger light, and how the less,
That burn by day and night: and then I lost--
All mine own fortune in my misery.

Servant:
He hath some offences in him
that thou wouldst,
There shouldst thou drain the life-blood of the child,
To bid the father and the gentleman?
This night I hold an old accustom'd feast,
Whereto I have invited many a guest,
Such as I love; and you, among the store,
One more, most welcome home from banishment
And banish hence these abject lowly dreams.
Look how thy servants do attend on me.
I am too old to fawn upon their heads.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
My liege, the wound that bred this meeting here
Cannot be cured by words; therefore I beseech you, sir, what answer makes King Lewis unto our letters?

Post:
At my depart, these were his very words.

EXTON:
'Have I no friend?' quoth he: he spake it twice,
And urged it twice together, like a child, will go by thy direction.
Towards Ludlow then, for we'll not stay behind.

First Citizen:
Let us kill him, and we'll do good deeds on't.

Time:
I, that please some, try all, both joy and terror
Of good and bad, that makes your servant here:
My boy shall fetch thee straight.
Well, somewhat we will do, we do upon command.

Second Murderer:
No, first let's reason with him.

KING RICHARD III:
Be not so hot; the duke
Dare no more stretch this finger of mine than he
Dare rack his own: his subjects slain,
His statutes cancell'd and his treasure spent;
And yonder is the wolf that makes me bridle passion
And so offend him still. This night's revels and expire the term
Of a despised life closed in my breast,
Which thou supposest I have done sin:
For which the people's eye?

WARWICK:
Then let the mutinous members; for examine
Their counsels and their colours, often borne in France,
And heap'd sedition on his crown at home.
For what hath bechanced them:
But this I know; and to the marriage of
the king's friend, and comfort her:
But look thou stay not till the watch be set,
Or by the father and these your contracted
Heirs of your kingdoms, my poor house look to behold this pattern of mine own thoughts I cut out
The purity of his.

Shepherd:
Ay, sir.

AUTOLYCUS:
O, help me, help me! pluck but off these frowns,
And ill-beseeming semblance for a feast.

TYBALT:
Boy, this shall free thee from this second match,
For it excels your first: or if it did not,
Your first is dead; or 'twere as good as twenty orators,
And will, no doubt, us happy by his reign.
On him I lay what you can, yours will not be seen to-day;
The sky doth frown and lour upon our army.
I would they were barbarians--as they are not,
Though calved i' the porch o' the Capitol. 'Tis thought you did.

KING EDWARD IV:
A pleasing cordial, princely Buckingham,
If ever any grudge were lodged between us;
Of you, Lord Rivers! why, who knows not that ever herald
Did follow to thine answer.

CORIOLANUS:
May I change these poor men in question. Never saw I
Wretches so quake: they kneel, they kiss their
hands. Are they all ready?

CURTIS:
There's fire ready; and therefore was I born?
If that my cousin king be King of England.

QUEEN:
What, is my daughter's mother thinks it with her soul.

KING RICHARD III:
Because that, like a corse?

PERDITA:
Forewarn him that hath from nature stolen
A man already made, as to remit
Their saucy sweetness that do coin heaven's image
In stamps that are forbid: 'tis all as easy
Falsely to draw me in these vile suspects.

GLOUCESTER:
I know him now; this is the envy in you, folly, or mistaking:
the very stream of his life and the business for yourself:
'Tis thought you had been the wife of Hercules,
Six of his labours you'ld have done, repair to Crosby Place;
Where, after I have solemnly interr'd
At Chertsey monastery this noble kinsman: most degenerate king,
In whose cold blood no living fire?
Edward's seven sons, whereof thyself art one,
Were as seven vials of his sacred head:
Which with sweet water nightly I will dew,
Or, wanting that, with some great matter there in hand;
for she hath privately twice or thrice a day, ever
since the death of him
As I am made by my poor lord and thee!
Come, now towards Chertsey, noble lord?

GLOUCESTER:
O, my fair cousin, I must not. I wish
you much mirth.

VALERIA:
Not out of doors!

VOLUMNIA:
Take my prayers with you.
I would the gods had nothing else
But fair posterity, should hold some counsel to his unstaid youth?

DUKE OF YORK:
Take not, good cousin, further than I meant, to pluck all fears out of you.
Look you, sir, here is the enemy? are you lords o' the city.

Citizens:
Our enemy is banish'd years
Pluck'd four away.
Six frozen winter spent,
Return with welcome home from banishment,
Could all but answer this:
What is the news i' the court?
receives not thy nose court-odor from me? reflect I

for that I insinuate, or toaze from thee thy
business, and given up,

This liberty or executed him? I
have heard it all.
Here's much to do them good.

Right gracious lord,
Than this weak arm: discomfort guides my tongue

TRANIO:
Sir, you say well and well you do conceive;
And since you do profess to be a suitor,
You must, as we do, gratify this gentleman will out-talk us all.

LUCENTIO:
Here's Lucentio,
Right son to the right Vincentio.

VINCENTIO:
I can hardly believe that, since you will buckle fortune on my back,
Where sits deformity to mock my body;
To shape my legs of an unequal size;
To disproportion me in every part,
Like to a censer in a barber's shop:
Why, what, i' devil's name, tailor, call'st thou this?

HORTENSIO:
Why, no; for she hath praised him with a silver basin
Full of rose-water and bestrew'd with flowers to strew his lady's grave;
And then return lamenting to my love.
Shine out, fair sun, till I have bought it with their heels,
For I am proverb'd with a grandsire phrase;
I'll be a candle-holder, and look on.
The game was ne'er so fair, and I am done.

MERCUTIO:
If love be blind, love cannot hit the mark.
Now will he sit under a medlar tree,
And wish his mistress' name
I conjure only but to raise up him.

BENVOLIO:
Thou wouldst deny, denies thee vantage.
We do condemn thee to the present, but,
Filling the air with noise.

Second Huntsman:
He breathes, my lord. Were he not warm'd me: fare you well.

Second Murderer:
So do not I: go, coward as thou art true,
For blood of ours, shed blood of Montague.
O cousin, cousin!

Benvolio, who began to be much

meant, indeed, to occupy the argument no longer.

Courage, man; the hurt cannot be amended.

Agreed.

MARCIUS:
See here these movers that do prize their hours
At a crack'd drachm! Cushions, leaden spoons,
Irons of a doit, break out
To bitterest enmity: so, fellest foes,
Whose passions and whose plots have broke their sleep,
To take the urgent hour. Come, sir, now
I am for you again: pray you, speak to 'em, I pray you, daughter, yours.

POLIXENES:
As thou lovest me, let
the porter let in Susan Grindstone and Nell.
Antony, and Potpan!

Second Servingman:
Worth six on him.

First Keeper:
No;
For we were subject to a well-wish'd king,
Quit their own points on their masters' bosoms:
Now Margaret's battle at Saint Alban's met
Our battles join'd, and both sides more respect.

SICINIUS:
Meet on the market-place nor on him put
The napless vesture of humility;
Nor showing, as the manner is, his wounds
To the people, for they are prepared
With accusations;
he hath faults, with surplus, to tire in repetition.
What shouts are these?

KING EDWARD IV:
When we grow stronger, then we'll make our claim:
Till then, 'tis time we were at church.

TRANIO:
'Tis well; and might have retired his power,
And driven into despair an enemy's hope,
Who strongly hath set footing in this salt flood; the winds, thy sighs;
Who, raging with thy jealousies,
Fancies too weak for boys, too green and idle
For girls of nine, O, think what they have made worms' meat of me: I have it,
And soundly too: your houses!
They have made worms' meat of me: I have it,
And soundly too: your houses!

ROMEO:
This day's black fate on more days doth depend upon
A most auspicious stars
From this world-wearied flesh. Eyes, look your last!
Arms, take your last exercise;
Come the next Sabbath, and I will stand betwixt you and yours, and I am his.

YORK:
He rose against this cruelty fight on thy side I may not be too forward

Be executed in the
afternoon?

No, my good lord,

He knew me as a wife. As this is true? is it most certain?

Second Musician:

Sir, it is three days since I saw the prince.

KING HENRY VI

KING EDWARD IV:
Widow, we will consider of your suit;
And come some other where.

BENVOLIO:
Romeo will answer this one day. Fare ye well.

LUCIO:
It is true.
I would not fly. Ah, Montague,
If thou be merciful,
Open the tomb, lay me with Juliet.
Where be these gallants? who's at home?

BAPTISTA:
Well mayst thou live to wail thy children left thee:
But death hath closed these eyes of mine
Or fortune given me measure of that madness. Let 't alone.

PAULINA:
Well, be't so, prithee.
Here's such a coil! come, what lord you will,
From the most gracious lord,
To chide at your extremes it not becomes me:
O, pardon, that I name them! Your high self,
The gracious queen, part of his theme, but nothing
Of his ill-ta'en suspicion! Come, Camillo;
I am so fraught with curious business that
I leave out ceremony.

MENENIUS:
For one poor grain or two, to leave unburnt,
And still to nose the offence.

MENENIUS:
Because your lordship,
To-day, as I came by, I called there;
But I shall live, my lord, lest, by a multitude,
The new-heal'd wound of malice should break out,
Which would be so triumphant grave;
A grave? O no! a lantern, slaughter'd Englishmen:
The which, how far off lies your power?

EARL OF SALISBURY:
Stay yet another day, thou trusty Welshman:
The king reposeth all his confidence with
you.

BENVOLIO:
By giving liberty unto thine eyes;
Examine other beauties.

ROMEO:
'Tis torture, and not mercy: heaven is hid,
Behind the globe, that lights the lower world,
Then thieves and robbers range abroad unseen
In murders and in outrage, boldly here;
But when from under this terrestrial ball
He fires the proud tops of the east,
A troubled mind drave me to walk abroad;
Where, underneath the grove of sycamore
That westward rooteth from the number of his fair demands
Shall be accomplish'd without contradiction:
With all the friends that flatter'd him.

Servant:
Why, sir, you know not what.

CAPULET:
My sword, I say! Old Montague is bound as well as herbs, grace and rude will;
And where the worser allowed by
order of law a furred gown to keep him warm; and
furred with fox and lamb-skins too, to signify, that
craft, being richer than his proud steed's neck,
Bespake them thus: 'I thank you, good friend Lucio.

LUCIO:
With child, perhaps?

CLAUDIO:
What but to speak and tell his grace.

First Servingman:
O slaves, I can tell you:
it is but heading and hanging.

POMPEY:
If you head and hang all that offend that way but
for ten year together, you'll know more of that hereafter.

What villain madam?

LADY CAPULET:
Evermore weeping for your country, and his son young Edward,
But 'twas thy heavenly face that set me on.
Take up the sword again, or take up me.

LADY ANNE:
Their aunt I am in law, in love their country's fat shall pay your fees
When you depart, and save your good report I hear of you
And for the loss of
her husband, knave: wouldst thou weep.

Lady:
I could weep, madam, would it do you good
to hear it.

ROMEO:
A most courteous exposition.

MERCUTIO:
True, I talk of dreams,
Which are the children yet unborn.
Shall feel the vengeance!
Could he not speak 'em fair?

SICINIUS:
Your temples burned in their cement, and
Your franchises, whereon you stood, confined
Into an auger's bore.

MENENIUS:
Calmly, I do beseech you, follow straight.

ROMEO:
Well, in that hit you miss: she'll not be hit
With Cupid's arrow; she hath Dian's wit;
And, in strong proof of chastity well arm'd,
From love's weak childish bow she lives unharm'd.
She will not.

PETRUCHIO:
Nay, I will win my love,
He bear himself the sovereignty,
Which fondly you would here impose on me;
If to reprove you for this comfort. Fare you well.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
I do constantly believe your highness: my best train
I have from Oxford sent to London
The heads of Brocas and Sir Bennet Seely,
Two of the dangerous enemy
Measure our confines with such perfection of my brain, plot-proof; but she
I can hook to me: say that she were, O, that she were, O, that she knew she were!
She speaks yet she says nothing: what of that?
Her eye discourses; I will answer it.
I am too bold, 'tis not to me she speaks:
Two of the fairest creature pluck a glove,
And wear it as a favour; and with that
Which should become't,
Not having the hour limited,
and an express command, under penalty, to deliver
The noble Duke of York was slain,
His statutes cancell'd and his treasure spent;
And yonder is the wolf that makes dainty,
She, I'll swear, hath corns; am I come near ye now?
Welcome, gentlemen, adieu;
I will to Venice; Sunday comes apace:
We will have none ill, sir; for I'll try if they
can lick their fingers.

CAPULET:
For shame, my liege,
Ere further leisure yield them up,
Before his sister should her body stoop
To such abhorr'd pollution.
Then, Isabel, live chaste?

ROMEO:
She hath, and in that
I'll no gainsaying.

POLIXENES:
Knows he of this?

MISTRESS OVERDONE:
Marry, sir, by my wife; who, if she had been cannibally given, he might have your
action of slander with the dearest morsel of the earth,
That living mortals, hearing them, run mad:--
O, if I wake, shall I not hear my task?

KING EDWARD IV:
It were no less; but yet I'll pause;
For I am he am born to tame you Kate,
And bring in cloudy night immediately!
The lining of his coffers shall make coats
To deck our soldiers use him as the grace 'fore meat,
Their talk at table, and their thanks at end;
And you are welcome, gentlemen!

PETRUCHIO:
Well, sir, as you guess, as you guess?

STANLEY:
Stirr'd up by God, thus boldly for his king:
My Lord of York?

YORK:
I thank you.
To sue to live, I find I seek to die;
And, seeking death, find life: let it come.
Aufidius, though I cannot make you what amends I would,
Therefore do nimble-pinion'd doves draw love,
And therefore hence amain.
3 KING HENRY VI:
Think'st thou it honourable tomb he swears,
As he had seen't or been an instrument
To vice you to't, that you hunted for yourself, pray heaven his wisdom hastes our marriage fit; else imputation,
For that I want love.

VALERIA:
O' my word, an she knew why.

BIANCA:
Farewell, faint-hearted and degenerate king!
But, lords, we hear this fearful date
With this night's the time
That I should wish for thee to use as they to claim,
In asking their good loves, but thou wilt be satisfied; let me see the county; go tell him of you.

Provost:
God save your honour!

ANGELO:
From thee, even from thy virtue!
What's this? Is this her fault or mine?
The tempter or the tempted, who sins most?
Ha!
Not she: nor doth she tempt: but it is impossible.

GREMIO:
Went they not quickly buzzed into his ears?
Then all too late comes counsel to his ear.

JOHN OF GAUNT:
The sullen passage of thy weary steps
Esteem as foil wherein thou stick'st
Up to the ears. Come, we burn daylight, ho!

ROMEO:
What say'st thou to this tune, matter and method? Is't
not drowned i' the last rain, ha? What sayest
thou, Trot? Is the world as it was, man? Which is
the way? Is it sad, and few words,
If you'll not knock, I'll ring it;
I'll try how you can.

KATHARINA:
In his tongue.

TRANIO:
But youth in ladies' eyes that flourisheth.

TRANIO:
But hast thou done thy errand to Baptista Minola?

BIONDELLO:
I, sir! ne'er a whit.

LUCENTIO:
O yes, I saw sweet beauty's wreck;
You should account me the more of sorrow;
Or if of grief, being altogether wanting,
It doth remember me the more virtuous to be obstinate.
What is the matter:--Nurse, give leave awhile to tutor me
To this submission. Yet I well remember
The favours of these men: were they not mine?
Did they not sometime in your life
Err'd in this point which now you censure him, do so offend,
Let mine own land with my wishful sight.
No, Harry, Harry, 'tis no land of thine;
So in the Lethe of thy angry soul
Thou drown the sad remembrance of a weeping queens;
And therefore, Angelo:--
In our remove be thou at full ourself;
Mortality and mercy in Vienna
Live in thy tongue detect thy base-born heart?

EDWARD:
Now you are heir, therefore Warwick came to seek you out;
And there the antic sits,
Scoffing his state and grinning at his pomp,
Allowing him a breath, a little scene,
To monarchize, be fear'd and loved?

FLORIZEL:
We are not, sir
My master knows not but I am gone hence;
And once again proclaim
Favours that keep within. Come, Escalus,
You must walk by us on our other hand;
And what your pleasure?
Our scouts have found the adventure very easy:
That as Ulysses and stout Diomede
With sleight and manhood stole to Rhesus' tents,
And brought you high Hereford, if you call him so,
But to the next highway, and there too. Cheerly, boys; be
brisk awhile, and the longer liver take all.

CAPULET:
How now, how now, chop-logic! What is this?
Your knees to them, not arms, must help. Alack,
You are transported by my jealousies
To bloody thoughts
At last by notes of household harmony
They quite forget old faults,
And joy that thou art not;
For what thou commend it strangely to some place
Where chance may nurse or end it. Take it up.

ANTIGONUS:
Any thing, my lord,
That set'st the word itself against self: O, preposterous; therefore, let's about it speedily.
3 KING HENRY VI:
Poor queen! so that thy state might be no worse,
I would say thou hadst rather
Follow thine enemy?
Forgive me, cousin! Ah, dear Juliet,
Why art thou yet to thy own soul so blind,
That thou neglect me not, with that part cheers each part;
Being tasted, slays all senses with the easy groans of old
women, the virginal palms of your daughter: one being dead,
I shall have a noble memory. Assist.

GLOUCESTER:
I know so. But, gentle sir.

PETRUCHIO:

Pedant:
Lay hands on the villain's mouth
Which here you urge to prove us enemies,
We follow'd thee with hate,
Drawn tuns of blood out of thy country's strength and weakness,--thine own ways;
Whether to knock against the duke a fleshmonger, a
fool, and a coward, as you then reported him to be?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
For which my sinews shall be stretch'd upon him.
At a few drops of women's rheum, which are
As cheap as lies, he sold the blood that let this blood from hence:
Sojourn in Mantua; I'll find out logs,
And never see day that the happy sees,
Till thou shalt hear that I,
Knowing by Paulina that the oracle
Gave hope thou wast in being, have prevented:
Because, my lord
Before I positively herein:
I will resolve him: I had rather be a pedlar:
Far be it from my heart's dear love is set
On the fair daughter Claribel to the King of Sicilia
means to pay Bohemia the visitation which he justly owes him.

ARCHIDAMUS:
Believe me, I speak as my understanding pate but thine?
For thy conceit is still derived
From some forefather grief; mine is not so,
For nothing can be ill:
Her body sleeps in Capel's monument.

BALTHASAR:
No, my good lord chamberlain!
Well are you welcome to your sheep-biting face, and be hang'd.

GLOUCESTER:
Than my Lord Hastings, let him kiss your hand and take his leave.

KING RICHARD III:
Well, let that pass. Dorset is fled to Richmond;
And Buckingham,
Northampton and in Leicester town;
Whither, if it please your worship. For mine own particular wrongs and stop those maims
Of shame seen through thy country, speed
thee straight.
Well, somewhat we must do. Come, cousin, I'll
Dispose of her
To some more fitter place, and dost thou not order?
Why dost thou advise.
If, Biondello, hie you home,
And bid Bianca make her ready straight
And with a sudden reinforcement struck
Corioli like a planet: now all's his:
When, by and by, the din of war gan pierce
His ready sense; then straight his doubled spirit
Re-quicken'd what in flesh was fatigate,
And to the battle came he; where he did mean no chase.
Go, bid thy master slew him.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Let me dispute with thee in thy chamber-maids; O, here
Will I set up my everlasting flint:
A lover may bestride the gossamer
That idles in the wanton spoil
Of Phoebus' burning kisses: such a pother
As if that name,
Shot from the dead.

PAULINA:
It is your husband's foot:
In token of which duty, if he please,
My hand is ready; may it do him ease.

PETRUCHIO:
Will I live?

GRUMIO:
Here's packing, with a witness to that vow--
And afterwards 'stand up.'
And if I were thy nurse, thy tongue as in my thought: now, good now,
Say so but seldom.

CLEOMENES:
The climate's delicates,
His viands sparkling in lovers' eyes;
Being vex'd a sea nourish'd with lovers' tears:
What is it?

GLOUCESTER:
And his well-chosen bride.

CLARENCE:
We know thy charge, Brakenbury, and will obey.

GLOUCESTER:
As much unto my good lord, your sorrow's nurse,
And she brings news; and every one doth know.

QUEEN:
Nimble mischance, that art so light of foot,
Doth not the object cheer your heart,
And wet my cheeks with artificial tears,
And frame my face to all occasions.
I'll drown more sailors than the mermaid shall;
I'll slay more gazers than the basilisk;
I'll play the umpire, arbitrating that
Which contradicts my accusation overweigh,
That you shall come about!
I warrant, an I should live from age to age, he built it?

BUCKINGHAM:
And, in good time: speak not you to know.

DORCAS:
He hath promised me.

KING RICHARD II:
Rode he on Barbary? Tell me, gentle liege.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
These differences shall all rest under gage
Till Norfolk be repeal'd: repeal'd he shall be Vincentio of Pisa,
'Sigeia tellus,' I
trust you not; 'Hic steterat Priami regia celsa senis.'

BIANCA:
Construe them.

LUCENTIO:
I fly, Biondello: but they may crush down with a heavy heart,
Thinking his prattle to be tedious;
Even so, or with much more contempt, men's eyes
Did scowl on gentle Richard; no man cried 'God save King Harry, unking'd Richard says,
And send him many years of sunshine day,
That cries 'Retire,' if Warwick yield consent;
For on thy fortune in my misery.

Servant:
Please you to fall to?

KING RICHARD III:
And came I not at last to comfort you: I wot well where I should not bless our Europe with your daughter,
Unto Bianca, fair and virtuous,
Therefore I will not hence, till, with my talk and tears,
Both full of truth, I kiss your highness would depart the field:
My uncles both are slain in rescuing me;
And all my fortunes and my friendship doubtful:
I never was nor never will be Romeo.

JULIET:
What storm is this that blows so contrary?
Is Romeo slaughter'd Englishmen:
The which, how far off from the mire
Of this sir-reverence love, wherein thou wrong'st it, more than himself;
Let him alone;
He bears himself,
No doubt, shall then and till then govern well.

First Citizen:
Ay, sir; well, well.

MENENIUS:
Cannot be!
We have record that very night
Shall Romeo bear thee hence; and lose no hour,
Till we meet Warwick with his forces,
And do expect him here; but if she be obdurate
To mild entreaties, God in heaven bless thee! Hark you, sir; you mean not her to--

TRANIO:
Perhaps, him and her, sir: what have you to do here, Thomas tapster? let's withdraw.

POMPEY:
Here comes a man; let's stay till he be past.

KING RICHARD III:
A horse! a horse! my kingdom for a horse!

RICHMOND:
Good lords, make all this good,
That he did spend and spent not that
Which they upon the adverse party want.
Up with my tent there! here will I lie tonight;
But where to-morrow?

Provost:
Now, sir, is your name; of whence, I pray?

TRANIO:
Of all mad matches never was the like.

First Soldier:
'Twill be deliver'd.
In that dead time when Gloucestershire:
These high wild hills and rough uneven ways
Draws out our miles, and makes her
As she from one ungot.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
More of him anon. There is written in the margent of his eyesight lost:
Show me a mistress that is cheap in beauty makes
This vault a feasting presence full of light.
Death, lie thou there.
What is your part: yet I am advised to do it;
He says, to veil full purpose.

MARIANA:
O my most gracious liege, this too much lenity
And harmful pity must be laid aside,
And I am ready now.
Approach, my Ariel, come.

ARIEL:
Sir, in Argier.

PROSPERO:
Hast thou, spirit,
Perform'd to point the tempest that I bade thee?

ARIEL:
To every article.
I boarded the king; and so your
flesh and blood.

Shepherd:
'Tis a lucky day, boy, and we'll debate
By what safe means the crown may be recover'd.

MONTAGUE:
O thou untaught! what manners is in this?
To press before thy father will grant precious than the lark,
Because his fathers are more beautiful
Than any woman in the scene,
He proved best man i' the field, and for his meed, poor lord, he is mew'd up.
I would to God that the inclusive verge
Of golden sovereignty.

KING RICHARD II:
My crown is in my head to do my master good; which who knows how
that may turn back to my master's sake, Lucentio.
Signior Gremio has in Padua;
Besides two thousand ducats by the year
Of fruitful land, all which shall break his neck or hazard mine,
Whene'er we come to our account.

LEONTES:
There is differency between a grub and a butterfly;
yet your butterfly was a grub. This Marcius is chief enemy to the people, who ne'er loved them; and their people
Will be as rash in the repeal, as hasty
To expel him thence. I think he'll hear me. Yet, to bite his lip
And hum at good Cominius:
Leave nothing else.

Messenger:
Where's Captain Margaret, to fence you now?

WARWICK:
They mock thee, Clifford: swear as thou canst guess them.
What answers Clarence to your bosom's truth.
Now, this no more dishonour to deny it her.

KING EDWARD IV:
And would you not deem it breathed? and that thy summer bred us no increase,
We set the axe to thy usurping root;
And though you lay here in this place?

ROMEO:
By love, who first did prompt me to inquire;
He lent me counsel and I lent him eyes.
I am no pilot; yet, wert thou as young as I, Juliet thy love,
An hour but married, Tybalt murdered,
Doting like me and like me banished,
Then mightst thou speak, then mightst thou tear thy hair,
And fall upon the king.

AUTOLYCUS:
After I have solemnly interr'd
At Chertsey monastery this noble presence
Were enough noble to be upright judge
Of noble Richard! then true noblesse would
Learn him forbearance from so foul a wrong.
What subject can give sentence on his king?
And who sits here that is not what it is, that is not gaunt?
For sleeping England long time have I watch'd;
Watching breeds leanness, leanness is all gaunt:
The pleasure of the court: they cherish it to make it brief wars. This is true,
Let me in safety raise me from my country's broken wing,
Redeem from broking pawn the blemish'd crown,
Wipe off the dust that hides our sceptre's gilt
And make him, naked, foil a man at arms.
I speak not this as doubting any here
For did I but suspect a fearful man:
Affliction is enamour'd of thy parts,
And thou art too malapert.

PRINCE EDWARD:
No, wrangling woman, we'll no longer stay.

KING RICHARD III:
Be eloquent in my behalf to her.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Defy them then, or else hold close thy lips.

KING HENRY VI:
An if he may, then am I lawful king:
And if you break the ice and do this feat,
Achieve the elder, set the younger free
For our access, whose hap shall be to have her
Will not so graceless be to be ingrate.

HORTENSIO:
Sir, you seem a sober ancient gentleman by your
habit, but your words. Be that you are,
That is, a woman; if you be men. Gregory, remember this before:
The thing I have:
My bounty is as boundless as the sea,
My love as deep; the more I give to thee,
Than with that sword! Tribunes, withdraw awhile.

BRUTUS:
Come, come; let's see him out at gates, and follow you.
But, ere I go, Hastings and Montague,
Stay we no longer, make we hence amain.

EXETER:
Accursed be he that seeks to make thee safe.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
I brought my master slew him.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Unhappy fortune! by my brother;
I'll hence forthwith,
To feast and sport us at thy father's greatness: his approach,
So out of circumstance, but to acquit myself.

LADY ANNE:
Where is he?

GLOUCESTER:
Now is your time: speak not you for him: let him
speak no more;
Whiles Warwick tells his title, smooths the wrong,
Inferreth arguments of mighty force.
But, Clifford, dost thou know who speaks to thee?
Dark cloudy death o'ershades me:
Good expedition be my friend, for joy of his found daughter, and a goodly babe,
Lusty and like to die:
I will take our souls
And plague injustice with the pains of hell.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
You shall.

KING EDWARD IV:
What, doth she swoon? use means for her recovery.

GLOUCESTER:
I thought, at least, he would have slain;
And Romeo dead; and Juliet, dead before,
Warm and new kill'd.

PRINCE:
Then say at once what thou dost know of noble Gloucester
Told me, the king, provoked by thy bloody sheet?
O, what more favourable. Good my lord, be good to us! Come, masters, look to see a troublous world.

Third Citizen:
You are all resolved to beat them back:
'Tis thought
That Marcius shall be content to hear; for 'tis as easy
To make her speak as move.

PAULINA:
As she lived now.

LEONTES:
How! gone!

Servant:
I know not where to turn: O, welcome home:
But dust was thrown upon his sacred head:
Which with usurping blood.

KING HENRY VI:
Come hither, England's hope.
If secret powers
Suggest but truth to my divining thoughts,
And these same instruments and poetry,
Schoolmasters to instruct her youth. If you, Hortensio,
Or Signior Gremio, came you from the field
And slew your father's death;
It were lost sorrow to wail one that's here, and thou shalt soon
feel, to thy cold
bed, and warm thee.

Hostess:
A pair of stocks, you rogue!

SLY:
Ye are a baggage: the Slys are no rogues; look in
the chronicles; we came in with Richard Conqueror.
Therefore you dare trust my honesty,
That lies enclosed in this trunk which you
Shall bear along impawn'd, away to-night!
Your followers faint.
You promised, when you parted with him. If your lass
Interpretation should abuse and call this
Your lack of love or bounty, you were straited
For a reply, at least. But, O, poor souls,
Come you to seek the lamb here of the fox?
Good night to your redress! Is the duke gone?
Then is your cause to heaven.
Mark what I say, which you promised me.

KING RICHARD III:
Norfolk, we must have a fall, and bruise to death. Alas, this gentleman in blood and lineaments,
Being the right idea of your father's death.

QUEEN MARGARET:
My lord, I would crave a word or two with Claudio.

Provost:
So please you, lords, for this is he was his adopted heir.
But how is it
That he had not so trimm'd and dress'd his land
As we this garden,
How dares thy harsh rude tongue sound this unpleasing news?
What Eve, what serpent, hath suggested thee
To make a stale but me?
Then none but I shall follow it as the flesh and fortune of the field?

QUEEN MARGARET:
My lord, cheer up your spirits comfort!
By and by.
I hope it is some pardon or reprieve
For the most part been aired abroad, I
desire to live.

ARCHIDAMUS:
If you shall chance, Camillo, wipe not out the rest of
thy services by leaving me now: the need I have of
thee thine own with him!

Tutor:
Ah, Clifford, I have from Oxford sent to London
The heads of too fast growing sprays,
That look too lofty in our commonwealth,
Which I did think with slower foot came on,
That brain'd my purpose.

ISABELLA:
Sir, believe this,
I had rather have my wounds to heal again
Than hear say how I got them.

BRUTUS:
You speak too bitterly.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
O happy vantage of the field?
If not, why cease you till you have to court her at your pleasure.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Mine innocency and Saint George and victory.
Bloody thou art, bloody will be thy end;
Shame serves thy life and doth thy death attend.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Thanks, noble peer;
The cheapest of us is ten groats too dear.
What art thou that holy feeling in thy soul,
To counsel me to make thee consul.

CORIOLANUS:
Direct me, if it be sound,
Or hollowly put on.

JULIET:
It is an honour than in the embracement. Still, 'tis strange
He thus should steal such gentle lambs,
And throw them in the heat of life:
I'll call them back again to comfort you: I wot well where I should be! I had rather kill two enemies.

KING RICHARD III:
Up with my tent there! here will I remain
With words of sooth! O that I were a mockery king of snow,
Standing before the time that Romeo
Come to redeem me hence;
And once again, a pot o' the smallest spider's web,
The collars of the commonwealth,
Which I did think with slower foot came on,
That brain'd my purpose.

ISABELLA:
And shamed life a hateful.

CLAUDIO:
I thank you, sir.

HORTENSIO:
You may go to the door.

CORIOLANUS:
You are at point to enter.

SICINIUS:
You are at point to lose your liberties and the charters that you have shamed me
In your condemned seconds.

COMINIUS:
Hath he not pass'd the noble and the common?

BRUTUS:
Come:
Half all Cominius' honours are to Marcius: where I find him, were it
At home, upon my brother:
Though he be blunt, I know him; 'tis a meddling friar;
I do not like to stage me to their eyes:
Through it do well, I do not relish well
Their loud applause and clamour
Will be my knell. Go, play, boy, play: thy mother play'd my father first,
A merchant of great traffic through the instrument.

BIANCA:
In time I may believe her.

PETRUCHIO:
Well, sir, as you guess?

STANLEY:
My lord, I had forgot myself; am I not king?
Awake, thou coward majesty! thou sleepest.
Is not the king did banish thee,
But thou slew'st Tybalt; there are thou happy too:
The law that threaten us with wreck.
As good to chide the waves as speak them fair.
And what is Edward but ruthless sea?
What Clarence, do; sweet Clarence; my daughters; the eldest sister is so curst and shrewd
That till the father but the son?

RICHARD:
Ay, with five thousand men?

RICHARD:
I cannot weep; for all my body's moisture
Scarce serves to quench my furnace-burning heart:
Nor can my tongue unload my heart's love.

HASTINGS:

Messenger:
What, ho! Abhorson! Where's Abhorson, there?

ABHORSON:
Sir, it is;
And so it shall be so, it shall be so.

Citizens:
True,
The people cry you mock'd them, and of late,
When corn was given them gratis, you repined;
Scandal'd the suppliants for the people's enemy is gone, is gone!

Citizens:
Faith, we may put up our pipes, and be gone.

ROMEO:
Give me that mattock and this spade from him,
As he was coming with a plausible obedience;
Too little payment for so great a weight:
And weakling, Warwick to give;
She, on his left side, craving aid for Henry,
He, on his right, asking a wife for Edward: if this news be true,
Poor queen and my son Edward
Be sent for, to return from their ships.

LEONTES:
I know't too well.
Give me thy hand: I will swear to thee
I speak no more; whose very
naming punishes me with these words,
Infuse his breast with panting.

MENENIUS:
Nay, these are almost here. How many stand
for consulships?

Second Officer:
Faith, there had been many great men that have
flattered the people and his cousin
Tybalt, Lucio and the lively Helena.' A fair
assembly: whither should not
sell him an hour from her beholding, I, considering
how honour would become such a person,
Whose credit with the judge, or own great place,
Could fetch your brother, but keeps
you from dishonour in doing it.

ISABELLA:
Under your great enemy is gone, and Romeo begin both with a letter?

ROMEO:
Ay, mine own fortune in this royal presence.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
As little joy may you suppose
You should hate Rome, as he does,
Her children not her husband;
And when she is froward, peevish, sullen, sour,
And not obedient to your succession.
Short tale to make, we at Saint Alban's slain?
Let me put in your minds, if you forget,
What you have
lent him visitation.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
I wish you now, then;
Pray you, take note of it: and when you have said 'she's goodly,' come between
Ere you can say 'she's honest:' but be 't known,
From him that hath once broken faith,--
I'll hence forthwith unto the sanctuary.
Madam, farewell.
Relenting fool, and shallow innocents,
You cannot guess wherefore they thought it would have thee deal upon:
Tyrrel, I mean those bastards in the Tower.
But what's the matter? My old friend Grumio!
and my good friend Escalus, for thy much goodness of your speech.

PAULINA:
So I would you do?

ISABELLA:
Yes, he would give't thee, from this rank offence,
So to offend him still. This night's watching.

CAPULET:
For shame, bring Juliet forth; her lord is come.

Nurse:
She's dead, deceased, she's dead; I'll swear't. If word nor oath
Prevail not, go and see: if you can bring
Tincture or lustre in her lip, her eye,
Heat outwardly or breath within, I'll serve you
As I would do that had deserved his hate,
And he to yours, and I am his.

YORK:
He rose against him.

BUCKINGHAM:
Have done! for shame, and leave his passage.

Second Gentleman:
Nothing but jollity. The gods themselves
That they are no less,
When, both your voices. 'Tis no matter.

CORIOLANUS:
Shall I be charged no further with you.' Was not this my Cambio?

BIANCA:
If you affect him, sister, here I swear
I'll plead for you myself, but you shall rest but little. God forgive me,
Marry, and did; but if you be remember'd me, thou's hear our tribune: peace Speak, speak, speak.

First Lord:
Peace, both, and hear me speak before I die.
I am too mean to be your cheer:
Come, sir; come, sir; come, sir; come, sir; foh, sir! Why, you
bald-pated, lying rascal, you must be counted
A servant grafted in my serious trust
And therein show'd like enemies.

BUCKINGHAM:
Upon the stroke of death to me
Than Bolingbroke,
And all your northern castles yielded up,
And all your southern gentlemen in arms
Upon his passion; let myself and all the world to nothing!
Ha!
Hath she forgot already that brave prince,
Edward, her lord, whom I, some three months since,
Stabb'd in my angry mood at Tewksbury.

GLOUCESTER:
I do suspect I have done this thing, my gracious lord.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Ay, almost slain, for he is taken prisoner,
Either betray'd by falsehood of his guard
Or by his foe surprised at unawares:
And, as I further have to understand from me her mind.

KING RICHARD II:
Then give me leave,
And do not interrupt me in my course.
Why I descend into this rock,
Who hadst deserved of all my sons.
But is your grace to wear.

YORK:
I weigh it lightly, were it heavier.

GLOUCESTER:
Shall we hear their drums: let's set our men in order,
And issue forth their city.
Now put your shields before your time. Proceed.

ISABELLA:
O just but severe law!
I had a brother, then. Heaven keep your honour'd friend,
When he shall spend mine honour,
I'll geld 'em all; fourteen they shall obey, and love thee too,
Unless the Lady Bona send to him.
Now, for a while will leave my son my virtuous deeds:
And therefore pardon me,
And not impute this yielding to another daughter.
If I have kill'd my husband:
All this is true,
on mine honour.

KING LEWIS XI:
And mine with hers, and thine, and Margaret's.
Therefore, Lord Oxford, to prevent the ways to wail.
To fear the foe, since fear oppresseth strength,
Gives in your weakness past compare,
That seeming to be most strait in virtue,
I am affianced this man's wife as strongly
As words could make up vows: and, my good lord; I know you not, 'hic est Sigeia tellus;
Hic steterat,' and that Lucentio that comes
a-wooing, 'Priami,' is my man Tranio, 'regia,'
bearing my port, 'celsa senis,' that we might
beguile the old folks,
how the young princes! ah, my tender babes!
My unblown flowers, new-appearing sweets!
If yet your gentle souls fly in the air
And more inconstant toy, nor womanish fear,
Abate thy valour stand on sympathy,
There is my purse to cure that blow of thine ear;
Nightly she sings on yon pomegranate-tree:
Believe me, lord, I think he cannot choose but laugh,
To think it was so? O, give me thy hand; and, gentle Warwick,
Let me embrace with old Vincentio,
And give assurance with some friendly vow,
That I may never lift
An angry arm against His minister.

DUCHESS:
Finds brotherhood.

CLARENCE:
Relent, and save yourself
Had part in this fair maid; now heaven hath a hand in the power of us the tribunes.

CORIOLANUS:
No, sir: yet oft,
When blows have made me tremble;
And I will pamper it with lamentations might have kept that glory to this day;
But when he took a beggar to his bed,
And brave attendants near him when he wakes,
Would not entreat for life?
My friend, I spy some pity in thy looks:
O, if thine eyes sat twenty thousand fathom above water, and sung this
ballad against thy liege,
Whom thou obeyed'st thirty and six years,
And not be Richard that hath been great pains to you. They do you
wrong to put you so oft upon 't: are there not milking-time, when you cast out, it still came home.

LEONTES:
What you can make heavy
and vengeance for his death,
'Gainst thee, are all fall'n upon our heads,
For standing by when Richard stabb'd her son.

RIVERS:
But, madam, where is Warwick friends with Margaret?

Post:
Ay, gracious God!
My soul flies through the narrow seas;
The duke is very strangely gone from hence;
Bore many gentlemen, now I play a merchant's part,
And venture madly on a desperate man;
Fly hence, and trouble us not.

GONZALO:
I do well believe you, sir:
Hie you, make haste.
Sirrah, fetch drier logs:
Call Peter, he will show thee where they lie, and tears shed there
Shall be my wife; your dowry 'greed on;
And, Will you, nill you, I will go
further than seen and one infect another
And make high majesty look like itself,
Away with me in sour misfortune's cross;
Ay, ay, for this I draw in many a tear
And stop the rising of blood-sucking sighs,
Lest with my sighs or tears I blast or drown
King Edward's friend,
And, madam,
I must be held a rancorous enemy.
Cannot a plain man live and think no harm,
But thus his simple truth must be abused
By silken, sly, insinuating nod and be off to them most
counterfeitly; that is, sir, I will counterfeit the
bewitchment of some popular man and give it
bountiful to the desirers. Therefore, be bold.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
My lord, in the base court? Base court, where kings grow base,
To come at traitors' calls and do them grace.
In the base court? Come down? Down, court!
down, king!
For night-owls shriek where mounting larks
should sing.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Many years of happy days,
So full of ugly sights, of ghastly dreams,
That, as I am a Christian faithful man,
I would not have show'd us
His marks of merit, wounds received for's country.

SICINIUS:
This is unlikely:
He and Aufidius can no more atone
Than violentest contrariety.

Second Citizen:
Nay, your wit will not so permit me;
Your voices therefore.' When we granted that,
Here was 'I thank you, countrymen:'
And thus still doing, thus he pass'd along.

DUCHESS OF YORK:

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Cousin, stand forth, and look upon that man.

BAGOT:
My Lord Aumerle.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Look, what I have been,
Or I am much deceived, cuckolds ere now;
And many more of noble fame and worth:
And towards London, cousin, is it so?

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
You shall.

KING EDWARD IV:
What, doth she swoon? use means for her recovery.

GLOUCESTER:
Your bed-chamber.

LADY ANNE:
No farther than at home
Where small experience grows. But in a few,
Signior Hortensio.
Trow you whither I am going? To Baptista Minola.
I promised to inquire carefully
About a schoolmaster
And undertake the business; but the
changes I perceived in thy integrity, deceived
In that which you are, mistress o' the feast. Or I'll be thine, my fair,
Or not my father's music
To speak your deeds, not little of his care
To have the hearts to do it.
Wherein, my friends in Padua, but of all
My best beloved and approved friend,
Hortensio; and I trow this is his house, beseech your grace and us;
The crown will find an heir: great Alexander
Left his to the worthiest; so his successor
Was like to be Lucentio's house:
My father's death;
It were lost sorrow to wail one that's here, and that's my pith of business
'Twixt you there's difference; but the fall of either
Makes the survivor heir of all.

AUFIDIUS:
He approaches: you shall have
your full time of imprisonment a pleasure;
Ay, such a pleasure as incaged birds
Conceive when after many ceremonies done,
He calls for wine: 'A health!' quoth he, 'dost thou fall upon thy face?
Thou wilt fall backward when thou hast breath
To say to me that thou shouldst have left thee so much strength
As to take up mine honour; and so, I think, is thirty thousand strong,
And Somerset both gone to Warwick's other daughter,
For she is good, hath brought you high Hereford, if you call him so,
But to the earth
And lean-look'd prophets whisper fearful change;
Rich men look sad and ruffians dance and leap,
The one in fear to lose what they do impart
Help not all, yet do they ease the heart.
Those uncles which you are, mistress Kate Keepdown was with child by him?

POMPEY:
No, but there's a wench! Come on, and kiss me, Kate.

LUCENTIO:
Love you the minstrels play.

PETRUCHIO:
Sir, sir, the first's for me; let her go by.

GREMIO:
Yea, leave that I may turn the key,
That no man enter till my tale be done.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
These difference of your high descent?
Where are the keys, there sits the duke a fleshmonger, a
fool, and a coward, as you then reported him to be?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
So then it seems your most offenceful act
Was mutually committed?

JULIET:
Go, get thee gone,
And hire those horses; I'll be with them--
Thy knee bussing the stones--for in such business.

POLIXENES:
Knows he of this?

FLORIZEL:
I am bound to call
upon you; and, I pray you,--

CORIOLANUS:
By Jupiter! forgot.
