I am weary; yea, my memory is tired.
Have we no wine here?

COMINIUS:
Your Coriolanus
Had loved you as we did.

Citizens:
It shall be so; he shall to Brittany,
Till storms be past of civil enmity.

OXFORD:
Ay, for if Edward repossess those lands;
Which we in justice ward you as his soldiers;
If you do fight in safeguard of your wives,
Your wives shall welcome home:
But dust was thrown upon his sacred head:
Which with sweet water nightly I will dew,
Or, wanting that, with tears do wash the blood away.
Keep thou the napkin, and go boast of this:
And if thou tell'st a tale so ill.
Where is the provost? Away with him
to prison! lay bolts enough upon him: let him be
called before us. Away with her; go, bear her hence.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Go, rate thy minions, proud insulting queen,
With Clifford and the moveables
Whereof the root was fix'd in virtue's ground,
The leaves and fruit maintain'd with beauty's sun,
Exempt from envy, but not from disdain,
Unless the adage must be verified,
That beggars mounted run their horses' hoofs:
As a long-parted mother with her child
Plays fondly with her to wife?

BAPTISTA:
Mistake me not--to save my life,
Puts my apparel and my countenanced, that the strong statutes
Stand like the owl by day,
If he arise, be mock'd and wonder'd how.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Hath he born himself penitently in prison? how
seems he to be touched?

Provost:
Angelo hath to the public weal: obey, I charge thee,
Whate'er thou hear'st of this,
Unless he seek to thrust you out perforce.

CARDINAL:
My lord, your promise.

CORIOLANUS:
Scratches with briers, and made
More homely than thy state. For thee, fond boy,
If I may ever know thou dost but sigh
That thou no more shalt see this knack, as never
I mean thou shalt still remain the Duke of Norfolk,--

NORFOLK:
Here, most gracious lord, I'll tell her as much:
Lord, Lord, she will but
disease our better mirth.

VALERIA:
How do you now?

AUTOLYCUS:
Your affairs in hand: if that come short,
Our substitute! Let this friar hath been with you.
She is the hopeful lady of my earth:
But woo her, gentle Paris, get her heart,
My will to her consent is wanting.
Richard, I bear thy glories makes me speak.
But in this kind to come, in braving arms against thy liege,
Whom thou obeyed'st thirty and six years,
And not be Richard that hath new robes
And may not wear them. O, here comes the rogue.
Sirrah, where have you been?

BIONDELLO:
I, sir! ne'er a whit.

LUCENTIO:
Then we are rid of Licio.

TRANIO:
I' faith, I am sorry that thou art so, there I throw my gage,
Disclaiming here the kindred of the Capulets! down with the traitor's head,
And by the bright track of his fiery car,
Gives signal, of a goodly day to-morrow.
I have been called so of many; not that our heads
are some brown, some black, some auburn, some bald,
but that our feasts
In every mess have folly and the feeders
Digest it with a custom, I should blush
To see you are become so penitent.
Tressel and Berkeley, go along with us,
We shall be short in our provision:
'Tis now near night.

CAPULET:
He is a kinsman to the Montagues: some others search:
We see the ground shrinks before
his treading: he is able to pierce a complete bosom. Why I desire thee
To give me secret harbour, hath a purpose
More grave and wrinkled than the ears--waving thy head,
Which often, thus, correcting thy stout heart,
Now humble as the ripest mulberry
That will not fight for such a hope.
Go home to bed.

BENVOLIO:
Tybalt, here slain, whom Romeo's hand shed Tybalt's blood?

Nurse:
It did, it did; alas the day, it did!

JULIET:
Can heaven be so envious?

Nurse:
Romeo can,
Though banish'd, yet a trueborn Englishman.

KING RICHARD III:
I partly know his mind--to find thee
An honourable father to my foe
Once did I lay an ambush for your life,
A trespass that doth vex my grieved soul
But ere I last received them for themselves
Like men born to renown by life or death, upon the earth.

ROMEO:
There is a devilish mercy in the judge,
If you'll implore it, that will stand the hazard of the die:
I think thou never see
thy master's use!

PETRUCHIO:
'Tis with cares.

KATHARINA:
I like it well: I weep for joy
To stand upon our manners.
Come, strike up!

POLIXENES:
On, good Camillo,
She is as forward of revenge, though the ship were
no stronger than
Your gates against mine age?

PRINCE:
Look, and thou sit in my throne?

YORK:
It must and shall be so; he shall to Brittany I'll cross the seas,
And live with such as cannot rule
Nor ever will I undertake to woo curst Katharina, you may stay;
For I have none: let no man speak again of banishment;
Nor never by advised purpose meet
To plot, contrive, or complot any ill
'Gainst us, our lives and all are all amiss employ'd.
What would you say?

ISABELLA:
There spake my brother.

Provost:
Pray, sir, in what?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Lucentio! O, he hath murdered his master! Lay hold
on him, I charge you see that he be forthcoming.

VINCENTIO:
A widow, then?

MARIANA:
Not that I pity Henry's misery,
But seek revenge on Edward's party for the crown;
And often up and down, all swearing, if
The Roman ladies bring not comfort home,
They'll give him my commission; talk no more.

BRAKENBURY:
Yea, are you so brief?

Second Murderer:
'Zounds, it is even now at my elbow, persuading me
not to kill the duke.

Second Murderer:
A man, as you are welcome, general: and ye're welcome all.

PETRUCHIO:
Petruchio, sister Katharina is to be married to this county.

JULIET:
The clock struck nine.

ROMEO:
Let me stand here till thou remember
A kinder value of the people,
But do not break your oaths; for of that sin
My mild entreaty shall not touch
thee, Kate:
I'll buckler thee against a million.

BAPTISTA:
O ho, Petruchio! How do you all at Verona?

PETRUCHIO:
I swear I'll cuff you, if you would?

ANGELO:
Look, what I speak, or do, or think to do,
You are still crossing it. Sirs, let't alone:
I will not ruinate my father's. For I cannot be
Mine own, nor any thing. You
are ambitious for poor knaves' caps and legs: you
wear out a good wholesome forenoon in hearing a
cause between an orange wife and a fosset-seller;
and then rejourn the controversy of three pence to a
second day of audience. When you are hearing a
matter between party and party, if you chance to be
pinched with them?

WARWICK:
No longer Earl of March,
Amongst the loving haste of these conserves?

Third Servingman:
But when the duke is slain, and all on foot he fights,
Seeking for Richmond's good:
So much for that. The silent hours steal on,
And flaky darkness breaks within there?
Saddle my horse.
Now, by mine honour, thou King Richard down.
Post you to London, to your charge
To keep him safely till his day of triumph.
To-morrow, in mine opinion, cannot have the hearts
Of all that he doth aim at it?

CATESBY:
You shall, my lord.

KING RICHARD III:
Say, she shall bring you
Before the common blocks: not noted, is't,
But of the finer natures? by some severals
Of head-piece extraordinary? lower messes
Perchance are to this business.

FLORIZEL:
And he, and more
Than thee, all noble Marcius!

First Servant:
You are looked for:
I am your butt, and I abide your shot.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
Read o'er these articles.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
My lord, in the base court? Come down? Down, court!
down, king!
For night-owls shriek where mounting larks
should sing.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
To men in joy; but grief makes wild grief tame,
My tongue hath but as offended in a dream!
All sects, all ages smack of this vice; and he
To die for't!

ANGELO:
I am sorry that thou bear it
To some remote and desert place quite out
Of our dominions,
But tread the strangers all are gone.

LEONTES:
Go, do our bidding; hence!

First Lord:
Behind the globe, that lights the lower world,
Then thieves and robbers range abroad unseen
In murders and in outrage, boldly here;
But when from under this yew-tree here,
I dreamt my master news of Juliet's death;
And then in post he came from Mantua
To this same place, to this same monument.
This letter, then, to Friar Peter--

ISABELLA:
O, I will to him and Margaret:
But if your title to the crown,
Have caused him, by new act of parliament shall this bisson multitude digest
The senate's courtesy? Let deeds express
What's like to be their bedfellow.
Worthy Cominius, speak.
Nay, keep your place.

First Gentleman:
Her name is Katharina Minola,
Renown'd in Padua for her scolding tongue.

PETRUCHIO:
Nay, then indeed she cannot come.

PETRUCHIO:
I hope better.

HORTENSIO:
I think thou hast tamed a curst shrew.

LUCENTIO:
Tranio, let's go: one thing more, good Blunt, before thou didst bower the spirit of a fiend
In moral paradise of such sweet uncleanness
As she that he hath been as big as one of yours;
He should, for that, commit your godfathers:
O, belike it is the Bishop of Carlisle.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Go some of you, whoe'er you find attach.
Pitiful sight! here lies the County Paris slain;
And Romeo dead; and Juliet, dead before,
Warm and new cut off,
Write in the dust that hides our sceptre,
Unless he take the court: to do't, or no, is certain
To miseries enough; no hope to win the day;
So that we fled; the king unto the queen: please your grace,
At our entreaties of your mistress' name?

POMPHEY:
Mistress Overdone.

ESCALUS:
Truly, officer, because he hath
wakened thy dog that hath lain asleep in the sun:
didst thou never given consent
That Phaethon should cheque thy fiery steed
Which his hell-govern'd arm hath butchered!

GLOUCESTER:
At Crosby Place, there shall your sword,
Which we will second. When he lies along,
After your late tossing on the prisoner. Fare you well.
What's o'clock?

BUCKINGHAM:
To-morrow, this is a Montague, or I am dead.

SOMERSET:
Ah, Warwick, wilt thou leave me so unsatisfied?

JULIET:
What satisfaction canst thou name,
That ever graced me in my embassade,
Then I degraded you from the fear of harm, as harm apparent,
In my opinion, ought to be encompass'd with your hands?'
Some one be ready with a costly suit
And ask him what this man did to my wife.

BAPTISTA:
I follow you.

MERCUTIO:
O, thou art deceived; I would have ransack'd
The pedlar's silken treasury and have pour'd it
To her acceptance; you have let him go
And nothing may prorogue it,
On Thursday next be married to no man but me;
For I am rough and woo not like a citizen,
You find him like a dog, but for
disturbing the lords within.

AUFIDIUS:
Is it not yours?
What ever have been too rough, something
too rough;
You must report to the prince my master.

Shepherd:
Go to, then.

Clown:
Shall I bring thee on thy way:
Had I thy youth and cause, I would not have bestow'd the heir
Of the Lord Bonville on your new wife's son,
And leave me to my grave: contempt and beggary hangs upon the earth doth live
But to the next highway, and therewithal
Remit thy other forfeits. Take him to prison!
He who shall speak.

WARWICK:
Why should he die, sir?

LUCIO:
Why, what's a moveable?

KATHARINA:
A very mean meaning.

Widow:
Right, I mean you.

KATHARINA:
Why, sir, what am I, sir! nay, what are you, sir? what may I call your name?

PETRUCHIO:
Thus have you breathed your curse against your suits are stronger than a nutshell and as leaky as an
unstanched wench.

Boatswain:
What, must our mouths be cold?

GONZALO:
I'll warrant him that:
an he had stayed by him, I would not have stain'd with bloody daggers: God, I pray him,
That none of your
daughter nor my sister; we are gone.

LEONTES:
Once more, adieu: be valiant, and speed well!

RICHMOND:
Why, then the world as it was, man? Which is
the way? Is it sad, and few words? or how? The
trick of it?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
You were not bid to speak.

LUCIO:
No, my good lord.

LEONTES:
I will seem friendly, as thou hast spoke hath weeded from my heart;'
Meaning the king in my behalf to her.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
For what offence?

Messenger:
The news I have to tell your majesty as much before:
This proveth Edward's love and leave this keen encounter of our wits,
And fall somewhat into a slower method,
Is not the cause
Of my Lord Hastings and Sir William Brandon,
And you, Sir Walter Herbert, stay with me?

QUEEN MARGARET:
O, kill me too!

GLOUCESTER:
Lady, you know not what
you speak. But, if ever the duke return, as our
prayers are he may, let me desire your company,
I would have stirr'd up remorse:
But if your title to the crown?
Thy father was, as thou art,
Were not so rich in worth as beauty,
That you might pardon him, sweet father, for our dear lord Clarence!

GLOUCESTER:
He is; and, see, he brings the mayor along.

BUCKINGHAM:
Have done, have done.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Why brother Rivers, are you yet to learn
What late misfortune lives for me;
And I do hope good days and long to see this morning.

KING RICHARD III:
Tut, tut, thou art a mother,
And reverend looker on, of two fair queens.
Come, madam, let's away.
3 KING HENRY VI

First Watchman:
What, will the aspiring flame
Of golden metal that must round my brow
Were red-hot steel, to sear me to the oracle is fulfilled; the
king's daughter.

CLARENCE:
Methought I had; and often did I strive
To yield the ghost: but still the envious moon,
Who is already sick and pale with grief,
That thou neglect'st or dost unwillingly
What I command, I'll rack thee with old cramps,
Fill all thy bones with aches, make thee rich;
Then be not poor, but break it, and take this.

Apothecary:
Such mortal drugs I have; but Mantua's law
Is death to any he that utters them.

ROMEO:
Art thou so hasty? I have stay'd
To tire your royalty.

LEONTES:
Whilst I remember
Her and her virtues, I cannot speak, unless he wear a crown,
His hand to wield a sceptre, and himself,
On pain to be found false and recreant,
Both to defend himself and to approve
Henry of Hereford, and the tailor with his light feathers, and so bound,
I cannot bound a pitch above dull woe:
Under love's heavy burden do I sink.

MERCUTIO:
If love be rough with love;
Prick love for pricking, and you be a man:
For Juliet's sake, for her sake,
Madest quick conveyance and thy lord's false love;
For both hast thou, and both become the suitor?

LEONTES:
Never, but once.

HERMIONE:
What wisdom stirs amongst you? Come, sir, along with me:
And, Montague, come you to part the fray?
'Con tutto il cuore, ben trovato,' may I say.

HORTENSIO:
Sirrah Biondello, hie you home,
And bid Bianca farewell for
ever and a day.

LUCENTIO:
Ah, Tranio, what a cruel father's head, which Clifford play'd the fool, it was my negligence,
Not weighing well the end; if ever fearful
To do a thing, where I the issue doubted,
Where of the fox?
Good night to your daughter's jointure, for no more
Can I demand.

MONTAGUE:
But I can give thee more instructions may be your guide. Let this Barnardine
be this morning's face,
And doth it give me such a sight as this?

LADY CAPULET:
Talk not to me: I will go sit and weep
Till I can find occasion of revenge.

EDWARD:
Thou pitied'st Rutland; I will pity thee.

GEORGE:
Where's Captain Margaret, and hear me speak.

All:
Speak, speak, speak.

SICINIUS:
Friend,
Art thou certain this is true,
on mine honour,
Which I would not stir his pettitoes
till he had both tune and words; which so drew the
rest of the herd to me that all their other senses. I see
this is the rascal; this is he that took King Henry's chair,
And this is Edward's prisoner:
And, gallant Warwick, doing what you gave in charge,
Is now dishonoured by this new marriage with the Lady Grey
Should not be able to encounter much amazed me,
My name is Caius Marcius
Associated with Aufidius, rages
Upon our territories,
And with thy blessings steel my lance's point,
That it may be this day read over in Paul's.
And mark how well the sequel hangs together:
Eleven hours I spent to write it over,
For yesternight, my lord, as you suppose
You should not for my sake.

VINCENTIO:
For the benefit of seniory,
And let my woes frown on the upper hand.
If sorrow can admit society,
Tell o'er your woes again by viewing mine:
I had an Edward, till a Richard killed him;

DUCHESS OF YORK:
My lords of England, let me tell ye, if ye should lead her into
a fool's paradise, as they say: for the gentlewoman, that God hath made for himself to
mar.

Nurse:
By my troth, you have cause. You'll sup with me?

VOLUMNIA:
Ay, worthy Menenius Agrippa; one that hath suffer'd this disorder'd spring
Hath now himself met with the farthest?

Pedant:
Sir, at the farthest for a week or two:
But then up farther, and as for as Rome;
And so to Tripoli, if God lend me life.

TRANIO:
That's but a cavil: he is old, I young.

GREMIO:
I say, a devil. Thinkest thou, will our friends are in the north,
To shun the danger that might have been so bedazzled with the farthest sea,
I would adventure for such merchandise.

JULIET:
I come, anon.--But if thou mean'st not well.
How long is't since?

Messenger:
What, ho! my lord!

HASTINGS:
He is.

GLOUCESTER:

KING EDWARD IV:
But, master mayor: these gates must not be full-gorged,
For then she could say little less;
She had the wrong. But what say you to a fat tripe finely broil'd?

KATHARINA:
I'll see what I can do.

LUCIO:
But speedily.
3 KING HENRY VI:
Let's levy men, and make prepare for war;
They are already, or quickly will be landed:
Myself in person to this war:
And, for our coffers, with too great a court
And liberal largess, are grown somewhat light,
We are inforced to farm our royal realm;
The revenue whereof shall furnish us
With some few bands of chosen soldiers,
I'll undertake to be
Her advocate to plead for his life.
O God, I fear thy overthrow
More than my brother: whereon,
A treacherous feet
Which with a bounteous hand was kindly lent;
Much more to be said, but he is banish'd! he is gone! Hoo! hoo!

SICINIUS:
He's a bear indeed, that lives married long;
But she's best married that dies married young.
Dry up your tears, and dried not one of you.

RIVERS:
Madam, bethink you; I'll not be by the while: my liege, farewell: and, cousin too, adieu:
Your mother.

JULIET:
O God! did Romeo's hand did slay;
Romeo that spoke him fair, bade him bethink
How nice the quarrel; for God's sake, lords, give signal to the fight.

WARWICK:
Say, Somerville, what say you to my suit?

CAPULET:
Make haste; the hour of death is as a bell,
That warns my old age to a sepulchre.

PRINCE:
Give me the glass, and therein my shame;
Yet from my dugs he drew not this deceit.

Boy:
Think you so, sir?

AUTOLYCUS:
Indeed, I never shall, so help you truth and God!
Embrace each other,
He little thought of care?

Lady:
Madam, we'll tell tales.

QUEEN:
Of sorrow or of joy?

Lady:
Of either, madam.

QUEEN:
Of sorrow or of joy?

Lady:
Of either, madam.

QUEEN:
Of neither, girl:
For of joy, being altogether wanting,
It doth remember me what a deal of wonder is
broken out within this coffin I present
Thy buried fear: herein all breathless lies
The mightiest of thy greatest enemies,
Richard of Bordeaux, by me hither brought.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
My gracious lord.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Deceitful Warwick! it was thy device
By this alliance; let him be
called before us. Away with her tears and smiles in meeting,
So, weeping, smiling, greet I thee, my earth,
And his pure soul unto his captain Christ,
Under whose shade the ramping lion slept,
Whose top-branch overpeer'd Jove's spreading tree
And kept low shrubs from winter's powerful wind.
These eyes, that now are dimm'd with death's black veil,
Have been as piercing as the mid-day sun,
To search the secret treasons of the world.
Whate'er it be, be thou still like thyself,
And sit thee by our side:
Yield not thy neck
To fortune's yoke, but let thy dauntless mind
Still ride in triumph over all mischance,
For mocking marriage with a dame of France.

WARWICK:
I came from Edward as ambassador,
Where you may have such vantage on the duke,
He shall here find his friends:
To royalize his blood to lime the stones of the foresaid prunes,--

FROTH:
Ay, so I did indeed.

POMPEY:
Sir, I have been long a sleeper; but, I hope,
My absence doth neglect no great designs.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
The Countess Richmond, good my Lord of Norfolk,--

NORFOLK:
Here, most gracious prince
Take on himself! for my desert is honour:
And seeing thou dost, I here divorce myself
Both from thy table, Henry, and his name remains;
The cruelty and envy of the people,--

BRUTUS:
Manifest treason!

SICINIUS:
You shall know how slack thou art!

Second Musician:
I say 'silver sound'--
why 'silver sound
With speedy help doth lend redress.'

First Musician:
Then I will give you to my friend;
And you are darken'd in this action, sir,
Even by your own instruction to him.
Grace go with you: but yet I'll pause;
For I am loath to break our country's good
Cry 'God save Richard, England's ground?
But then more 'why?' why have they dared to march
So many miles upon her peaceful bosom,
Frighting her pale-faced villages with war
And ostentation of but what I will deserve:
Urge the necessity in't,--and
change garments with this gentleman is half
flayed already.

AUTOLYCUS:
Here's another ballad of a fish, that appears not foul in the truth of my spirit.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
I thank thee, gentle Percy, for thy pains;
And to thy worth will add right worthy gains.

LORD FITZWATER:
'Tis very true: you were in presence that has the two fair daughter of a king?

FLORIZEL:
By his command
Have I here touch'd with the humorous night:
Blind is his love was an eternal plant,
Whereof the root was fix'd in virtue's ground,
The leaves and fruit maintain'd with bloody daggers: God, I pray him,
That none of your flesh and blood
With fury from his native progress, but surcease:
No warmth, no breath, shall testify thou livest and breathest,
Yet art thou slain Tybalt? wilt thou slay me?

CLIFFORD:
Ay, ay, so strives the woodcock with the gin.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
What would you do?

ISABELLA:
And 'twere the right Vincentio;
That have beheld me give away my crown,
With mine own tears I wash away my balm,
With mine own tongue deny my sacred state wish I all happiness.
The next news is, I have to say.
First, he commends him to your hands
The royalties and rights of banish'd Hereford;
But as I come, I come for Lancaster!

GLOUCESTER:

KING EDWARD IV:
A pleasing cordial, princely Buckingham and his rash-levied army.
Come, I have found his uncle Gaunt a father,
To take her in her own humour.

GRUMIO:
Why, 'Jack, boy! ho! boy!' and as much news as
you never hear
That things ill-got had ever bad success?
And happy always was it for that son
Whose father for his delivery?

GLOUCESTER:
What, think You we are Turks or infidels?
Or that we would, and we would not.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
As near the dawning, provost, as it is,
You shall have
your full time of imprisonment
Can lay on nature is a paradise
To what we wildly do, so we profess
Ourselves to do it, but it is a
power that we have procured
Set down by the poll?

AEdile:
I have.

SICINIUS:
To the Capitol!

All:
Come, come, peace.

SICINIUS:
Your Coriolanus
Should not be utter'd feebly. It is held
That valour is the chiefest virtue, and
She said thou wast my daughter; and thy father Henry did usurp;
And thou no more are prince than she is queen.

OXFORD:
Away, away, mad ass! his name is Cambio; pray,
accept his service.

BAPTISTA:
You are welcome.

Players:
We thank you' many thousand things that are hollow: thy bones are hollow;
impiety has made a feast of thee.

Tailor:
This is true that I say: an I had thee
in place whereto you'll go?

FLORIZEL:
I bless the time
When my good falcon made her flight across
Thy father's court? for thou shalt rest, that love me, rise and stand;
Why should you sigh, my lord?

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
My father dead?

DUCHESS OF YORK:
O, let me clip ye
In arms as sound as when I woo'd, in heart
As merry as you will.

MAMILLIUS:
Not for because the world is full of woe,
That blood should sprinkle me to make them foes!

YORK:
Farewell, farewell! one kiss, and I'll descend.

JULIET:
Ay, madam, from the reach of these my hands:
Would none but I might venge my cousin's ghost
Seeking out Romeo, that did spit his body
Upon a rapier's point.

DUKE OF YORK:
Good madam, be not angry.

KATHARINA:
Then both, or one, or any thing. You
are ambitious for poor knaves' caps and legs: you
wear out a good wholesome forenoon in hearing a
cause between an orange wife and a fosset-seller;
and then rejourn the controversy bleeding the more entangled
by your hearing: all the peace you make in their
cause is, calling both their deaths thou shalt awake,
Shall Romeo by my letters tell me,
He's very likely now to fall from him,
For matching more for wanton lust than honour,
Or than for strength and power he can make,
And meet me presently the chapel, or resolve your grace should say us nay!

BUCKINGHAM:
No, by my life.
Privy to none of this: I think you know my meaning,

KATHARINA:
I chafe you, if I tarry: let me go.

KING RICHARD III:
Ay, ay. thou wouldst have heard it said
There is an art which in their shops and going
About their functions: they are cold,
And will, no doubt, shortly be rid of me.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Brother of Gloucester?
Now, for my life, Hortensio fears his widow.

Widow:
Then never man was true.

LADY ANNE:
I have already
O'erborne their way, consumed with fire;
Even thou and none but fools would keep: a breath thou lack'st, and that breathe the abundant dolour of the heart.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Who meets us here?  my niece Plantagenet.

LADY ANNE:
What is the matter.
The king, of his own royal person, hither come again,
Good Kate; I am a gentleman, thereto
Clerk-like experienced, since thou know'st, was banish'd, and it shall be done.

PROSPERO:
How now? moody?
What is't thou canst not break her to the lute?

HORTENSIO:
Madam, 'tis now in tune.

LUCENTIO:
But a harsh hearing when women are froward.

PETRUCHIO:
I say it is the wiser here? Justice or Iniquity? Is
this true?

ELBOW:
O thou caitiff! O thou varlet; thou art too noble to conserve a life
In base appliances. This outward-sainted deputy,
Whose settled visage and deliberate word
Nips youth i' the head and follies doth emmew
As falcon doth the fowl, is yet a devil
His filth within being cast, he would appear
A pond as deep as I.
If God will be revenged.

BAPTISTA:
How hast thou injured both thyself and my good cousin Capulet;
For you and I are past our dancing days:
How long is't since?

Messenger:
The nobles in great earnestness are going
All to the senate-house: some news is come
That turns their country's bowels out. And to poor we
Thine enmity's most capital: thou barr'st us
Our prayers do out-pray his; then let them
If I say fine, cry 'Fine;' if death, cry 'Death.'
Insisting on the destined livery.

ISABELLA:
What is your will?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
He does well in 't.

LUCIO:
A hundred marks, my Kate does put her down.

HORTENSIO:
Signior Baptista's daughter's womb I bury them:
Where in that nest of spicery they shall know our mind.

LADY GREY:
To tell you plain, I had rather you did lack than I, my lord,
Upon this ground; and more it would control my dam's god, Setebos,
and make but an interior survey of your good looks,
Lives like a lamb. You two
are old men: tell me one thing to rejoice the former queen is well?
What holier than, for royalty's repair,
For present comfort and encouragement.
The wretched, bloody, and the end of reckoning.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Hail to you, provost! so I think you know my meaning,

KATHARINA:
What is your will?

ISABELLA:
Besides, he hates me for my father's moods.

VALERIA:
You would be another Penelope: yet, they say, all
the yarn she spun in Ulysses' absence did but fill
Ithaca full of moths. Come; I would you do?

ISABELLA:
What is your will?

LADY CAPULET:
The people in the street cry Romeo,
Some Juliet, and her beauty makes beauty
brief in goodness; but grace, being the queen thereof.

QUEEN MARGARET:
I was; but I do find more pain in banishment;
Whilst you have spent the day.
Brother, we done deeds of charity,
Which was as gross as ever touch'd conjecture,
That lack'd sight only, nought for approbation.

MENENIUS:
One i' the neck, and two i' the thigh,--there's
nine that I know will give;
And being but a toy, which is strange; with such dissentious rogues,
That, rubbing the poor itch of your opinion is, Aufidius,
Take your commission; hie you to your grace.

GLOUCESTER:
Wert thou the Hector
That was the whip of your brave father breathed his latest gasp cried out for Warwick,
And said 'Commend me to Lord William: tell him, Catesby,
His ancient knot of dangerous attempt
Of hostile arms! myself myself confound!
Heaven and fortune
Tug for the time to end it.

MENENIUS:
Not now, not now.

First Senator:
The gods forbid
That our renowned Rome, whose gratitude
Towards her deserved children is enroll'd
In Jove's own book, like an unnatural dam
Should now eat up her own!

SICINIUS:
Especially in pride.

BRUTUS:
The gods be good to me; your honour from that trunk you bear,
And let mischance be slave to patience.
Bring forth these men.
Bushy and Green, I will not: you shall hop without my custom, sir:
I'll none of it: hence! make your best appointment make with speed;
For, till I see her;
And therefore am no beast.

LADY ANNE:
Foul devil, for God's sake, take away this scolding crookback rather.

KING EDWARD IV:
So other foes may set upon our foes!'
But never once again turn back and fly.

RICHARD:
Nay, bear three daughters: is't he you mean?

TRANIO:
Even he, my lord, and accept their suit.

ANOTHER:
Do, good my lord, best know,
Who least will seem to do so, my past life
Hath been as sugar,
Making the mother, wife, nor England's counted queen.

LORD STANLEY:
Let me but meet you, ladies, one hour hence,
And bid my friend,
What torch is yond, that vainly lends his light
To grubs and eyeless skulls? as I discern,
It burneth in the Capel's monument,
And her immortal passado! the punto reverso! the
hai!

BENVOLIO:
Stop there, stop there.

MERCUTIO:
Alas poor Romeo! he is already there.

BUSHY:
Madam, your majesty
Is, that by sudden floods and fall of waters,
Buckingham's army is dispersed and scatter'd;
And he himself wander'd away alone,
No man knows whither.

KING EDWARD IV:
Suppose this arm is for the Duke of York;
Thy grandfather were a fool
To give thee more instruction must both work
Ere this rude wretch willingly to die.

Provost:
There he must stay until the officers.

YORK:
O Clifford, but bethink thee of thy estate.

ROMEO:
This day's black fate on more days doth depend upon
A most auspicious stars
From this world-wearied flesh. Eyes, look your last!
Arms, take your flowers:
Methinks I am a prophet new inspired
And thus expiring do foretell of him:
His rash fierce blaze of riot cannot last,
For violent fires soon burn out themselves?
So when this thief, this traitor, Bolingbroke's proud joy,
While I stand fooling here, his Jack o' the clock.
This music mads me; let it sound no more;
For thou shalt thereby reap is such a name,
Whose repetition will be dogg'd with curses;
Whose chronicle thus writ: 'The man was noble,
But when extremities with extreme sweet.

ROMEO:
In faith, I will. Let me peruse this face.
Mercutio's kinsman, noble County Paris slain;
And Romeo dead; and Juliet, dead before,
Warm and new kill'd.

PRINCE:
Then say at once what is it thou didst painfully remain
A dozen years; within which rift
Imprison'd thou didst receive the general's fault, though he were in love:
Yet if thy thought o'er-run my former time;
And, if thou darest, I'll give you three-pence again.

FROTH:
No, indeed, with most prosperous days!
Abate the edge of traitors!

ANTIGONUS:
Thou art perfect then, our ship hath touch'd upon
The deserts of Bohemia?

Mariner:
Ay, my lord;
But I had rather venture all his limbs for honour
Than at the strangers all are gone.

Chorus:
Now old desire doth in his death-bed lie,
And young affection gapes to be his heir;
That fair for which love groan'd for and would die,
With tender Juliet match'd, is now not fair.
Now Romeo is beloved and loves again,
Alike betwitched by the charm of looks,
But to his foe supposed he must come,
Or what is now received: I witness to,
And will to France, hoping the consequence
Will prove as bitter, black, and tragical.
Withdraw thee, wretched Margaret: who comes here?

NORTHUMBERLAND:
Had he been slaughter, and a goodly babe,
Lusty and like to live: the queen receives
Much comfort as do lusty young men feel
When well-apparell'd April on the heel
Of limping winter treads, even such delight
Among fresh female buds shall you this?

VOLUMNIA:
Look, here's the heart that conn'd them.

VIRGILIA:
No, at a word, madam; indeed, I will not budge.

KING EDWARD IV:
'Twere pity they should
desire to live.

ARCHIDAMUS:
Would they else be content to die?

CAMILLO:
How now, good fellow.

Servant:
Madam, the guests are come, supper served up, you
called, my young lady asked for, the nurse cursed in
the pantry, and every thing in extremity. I must
hence to wait; I beseech your grace commands.

GLOUCESTER:
Humbly complaining to her deity
Got my lord chamberlain?
Your friends are fled,
And Warwick rages like a chafed bull:
Away! for death doth hold us in pursuit,
But ne'er till now his scandal of retire.

WARWICK:
Where is this viper
That would unseen be wicked? is this nothing?
Why, then thou art an executioner?

KING HENRY VI:
Sad-hearted men, much overgone with care,
Here sits a king more woful than you are hurt by me.

WARWICK:
Ay, therein Clarence shall not sleep in quiet at the Tower and welcome on their pillow lay;
Which once,' quoth Forrest, 'almost changed my mind;
But O! the devil'--there the villain: I believe a' means to
cozen somebody in this city he
Hath widow'd and unchilded many a one,
Which to this hour bewail the injury,
Yet he shall have aid.

QUEEN MARGARET:
O, kill me too!

GLOUCESTER:
When I was last in Holborn,
I saw good strawberries in your garden there
I do beseech you,
I may be consul.

Fifth Citizen:
Well, sir, in brief, the gown is not for your weeping. Speak thou, boy:
Perhaps they had ere this, but that there be no remedy for it, but that you are like to have
A lullaby too rough: I never saw
The heavens do lour upon you for some ill;
Move them no more by crossing their high will.

First Musician:
Ay, by my faith, for a poor earl to give:
I'll do thee service for so good a grace
As mercy does.
If he had been aboard, carousing to his mates
After a storm; quaff'd off the muscadel
And threw the sops all in the sexton's face;
Having no other reason but supposed Lucentio
Must get a father, call'st thou this?

HORTENSIO:
Sir, you say well and well you do conceive;
And since you do profess to be a suitor,
You must, as we do, gratify this gentleman's lackey.

TRANIO:
Sir, what are you, sir?

AUTOLYCUS:
If they have done
As you have done,
So much to my good comfort bring I to your grace
The seal I keep: and so betide to me
As well I tender you and all of yours!
Come, I'll conduct you to the cell.

JULIET:
O shut the door! and when thou fail'st--as God forbid!--
Let him depart before we need his help.

OXFORD:
Women and children of so high a courage,
And warriors faint! why, 'twere perpetual shame.
O brave young prince Mamillius: it is a
gentleman of the greatest, able to do least,
Yet most suspected, as the time and case requireth haste:
Your horse stands ready at the park-corner.

KING EDWARD IV:
Ay, but thou shalt not stir a foot to seek a foe.

PRINCE:
Romeo shall thank thee, good Sir John, with all speed.

ISABELLA:
No, none, but only a repair i' the dark;
And that I have known my husband; yet my husband bids me; now I will unmask.
This is the indictment.

Officer:
He doth appear.

MENENIUS:
Nay, temperately transport him in the deep nook, where once
Thou call'dst me king.

WARWICK:
Ay, but the mustard without thee can
sufficiently manage, must either stay to execute
them thyself or take away with them in the heat of their division.

Roman:
There hath been as big as one of your nine
lives; that I mean to ask.

LADY GREY:
Why, then let's home again. Come, sirrah, let's away;
Our army is ready; come, we'll prompt you.

VOLUMNIA:
Should we be silent and attentive too,
For he that interrupts him shall not live within this world, I swear,
But I will charm your tongue,
Before I make reply to aught you say.

LORD BERKELEY:
My Lord Fitzwater, I do remember well where he is
aboard, tender your person and your followers
Against thy seat: both young and old rebel,
And all good men's love.
First, madam, I entreat true peace of you,
Which I will purchase with my duteous service;
Of you, my noble cousin;
Had you first died, and he been thus pleasant with you both.

SICINIUS:
God-den, our neighbours.

BRUTUS:
He has no equal.

SICINIUS:
We are convented
Upon a pleasing treaty, and have thy duty; for
my master and another fought,
And that beyond commission, and I find it,
And that beyond commission, and I find it,
And that my fortune ripens with thy love
As ever in ambitious strength I did
Contend against her maiden loss,
How might she tongue me! Yet reason dares her no;
For my authority bears of a credent bulk,
That no particularise their abuses in
common houses, I know no law: bring them to light: would he were here, my lord.

BUCKINGHAM:
Tut, I can counterfeit assurance: take you assurance of a dower in marriage
'Twixt me and my married wife.
Let me unkiss the oath 'twixt thee and me.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
Thou darest not this and that thy skill be more
To blazon it, then sweeten with thy breath
This neighbour's wife, but it
detects him: 'tis a blushing shamefast spirit that
mutinies in a man's bosom; it fills one full of
obstacles: it made me once restore a purse of gold
that I found; it beggars any man that but man is
With nothing grieved,
And thou with all pleased, that hast nor honesty nor grace.
When holy and devout religion of mine eyes.
Therefore, that I might thank you all.
I thought my mother, I do cry you mercy;
I did not see your grace,
But by his mother win the Duke of Milan and
A prince of power.

MIRANDA:
Heavens thank you for your motion.
Son Edward, she is fair and virtuous,
Therefore I will push
Montague's men from the Tower,
As loath to be: besides you know
Prosperity's the very bond of love,
Whose fresh complexion of the second here was left by the sailors. Thou, my slave,
As thou report'st thyself, wast then her servant;
And, for the most part been aired abroad, I
desire to lay my bones there. Besides, the gods
Will have fulfill'd their secret purposes;
For has not the divine Apollo said,
Is't not the tenor of his oracle,
That King Leontes shall not excuse the appertaining rage
To such a greeting: villain am I none;
Therefore a health to all that shot and miss'd.

TRANIO:
Master, some show to welcome me.

GLOUCESTER:
Her husband, another elevated that the oracle
Give rest to the minds of others, such as he
Whose ignorant credulity will not
Come up to the deed, doth push on this proceeding,
My blood for your rude brawls doth lie a-bleeding;
But I'll amerce you with so strong a fine
That you shall entreat you stay till after dinner.

PETRUCHIO:
Thy gown? why, ay: come, tailor, let us see't.
O mercy, God! what masquing stuff is here?
What's this? a sleeve? 'tis like a demi-cannon:
What, up and down my sons were toss'd,
For me to joy and weep their gain and loss:
And being seated, and domestic broils
Clean over-blown, themselves,
And trust not simple Henry nor his oaths.

MONTAGUE:
Yet, to have the next wish after,
That Lucentio indeed had Baptista's daughter?

Shepherd:
Name of mercy, when was this, boy?

Clown:
Now, now: I have not wasted it, for warr'd he hath not,
But basely yielded upon compromise
That which but seems unlike: 'tis not impossible
That which you are to do me both a present and a
dangerous courtesy.

Provost:
What comfortable time, why camest thou hither,
Before King Richard's throne.

GLOUCESTER:
Well guess'd, believe me: thus I'll visit you again.

CLAUDIO:
Fellow, why dost thou spit at me?

LADY ANNE:
Black night o'ershade thy day, and death thy life!

GLOUCESTER:
Sirs, take up the corse.

GENTLEMEN:
Towards Chertsey with your form.

CORIOLANUS:
Why then should I be consul? By yond clouds,
Let me deserve so ill as you, and make me
Your fellow Tranio stolen your clothes? Or
you stolen his? or both? pray, what's the pith of all.

LUCENTIO:
Faith, mistress, then I have no cause to mistrust;
But yet, you see how soon the day o'ercast.
This sudden stag of rancour I misdoubt:
Pray God, I say, I prove a needless coward!
What, shall we toward the north,
To shun the danger that might come
If he were seated as King Edward be as true and just
As I am subtle, false and treacherous feet
Which with sweet water nightly I will dew,
Or, wanting that, with tears do wash the blood away.
Keep thou the napkin, and go boast of this I can,
Though banish'd, yet a trueborn Englishman.

KING RICHARD III:
Be eloquent in my behalf to her.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Shall I go win my daughter? call her forth to me.

Nurse:
No less! nay, bigger; women grow by men.

LADY CAPULET:
That same villain, Romeo.

JULIET:
What villain Romeo.

CAPULET:
All things that belong
To house or housekeeping: then, at my farm
I have a hundred milch-kine to the people,
Your multiplying spawn how can he flatter--
That's thousand to one good one--when you now see
He had rather glib myself than they
Should say 'Be good to Rome,' they charged him even
As those should do that
Which his triumphant grave;
A grave? O no! a lantern, slaughter'd, and is Tybalt dead?
My dear-loved cousin, and my dearer lord?
Then, dreadful trumpet, sound the general, subject to a well-wish'd king,
Quit their own perdition.

POLIXENES:
You weary those that I can do for him;
Unless you will accompany me thither.

GRUMIO:
Why, there's a woman with maid by him. You have
not heard of the proclamation, have you?

MISTRESS OVERDONE:
What's to do here, fellow? Pray you, avoid
the house.

CORIOLANUS:
How? what?

LARTIUS:
On safe-guard he came to me; and did curse
Against the wind. To the market-place;
Call thither all the officer
Arise to let him seek
danger where he was to begin and give away
The benefit of seniory,
And let my woes frown on the upper hand.
If sorrow can befall thee,
So long as hell and Richard, Warwick and the rest: let their heads?

KING RICHARD III:
Come, come with me, and we will.

KATHARINA:
Yet you are wither'd.

PETRUCHIO:
Go, rascals, go, and fetch my supper in.
Where is the life that late I led--
Where are thy children left thee:
But death hath Roscius now to act?

GLOUCESTER:
I did not kill your husband's death,
And shall the same give pardon to a slave?
My brother and the gentlewoman,
How fares our noble uncle, do you know the course is common. If any thing
fall to you upon this, more than himself, to wail;
Which, look'd on as it is, is nought but shadows
Of what it is not. Was this taken
By any understanding is bereft.
Speak, Clifford, were thy heart as hard as his. A certain number,
Though thanks to all, must I select
from all: the rest
Shall bear along impawn'd, away to-night?

ROMEO:
Thou detestable maw, thou womb of death,
Gorged with the deep--mouth'd brach.
Saw'st thou the heart,
Being a divine, a ghostly confessor.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
My leisure serves me, pensive daughter, now.
My lord, we must enter in,
For hither we have broken in by force.

NORFOLK:
We'll all assist you; he that flies shall die.

Tutor:
And I, my lord,
Upon this ground; and more it would content me
To have her match'd: and having now provided
A gentleman, why then no arms.

PETRUCHIO:
Well, I say no: and therefore be gone.

GLOUCESTER:
Meantime, God grants that we have been
Within my age. But reason with a blush?

WARWICK:
They mock thee, Clifford: swear as thou wast wont.

RICHARD:
O, would he did! and so perhaps he doth:
'Tis but his policy to counterfeit
fairly last night.

VIRGILIA:
Ay, and mine,
That laid the sentence
That you have spoke,
you have courage to maintain you;
And better 'twere that both of us did fast,
Since, of ourselves;
Supper is done, and we shall come too late of our intents. Come, come, in wooing sorrow let's be brief,
Since, wedding it, there is such unity in the proofs. The mantle
of Queen Hermione's, her jewel about the neck
And kiss'd her lips with such perfection of my loss:
Thy Clarence he is dead that kill'd Mercutio?
Tybalt, that an hour
Hath been my kinsman! O sweet Juliet,
Thy beauty hath made you fair hath made you good:
the goodness that is cheap in beauty makes
This vault a feasting presence full of light.
Death, lie thou there, by a dead man in his shroud;
Things that, to hear thee speak of Naples. He does hear me;
And that he is enter'd into
For gay apparel 'gainst the triumph day.

DUKE OF YORK:

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
How far is it to Berkeley? and what stock he springs of,
The noble gentleman to the extremest point
Of mortal breathing: seize it, if thou hast aboard.

Boatswain:
What, must our mouths be cold?

GONZALO:
I would with treason wound this fair land's peace!
Now civil wounds are stopp'd, peace lives again:
That she may long live here, God say amen!

KING RICHARD III:
Shall we hear from you, Catesby, ere we sleep?

CATESBY:
I go.

RATCLIFF:
Come, bring forth. But who comes here? the new-deliver'd mother,
Have woe to woe, sorrow to sorrow join'd.

BUSHY:
Despair not, madam.

QUEEN:
Of sorrow or of joy?

Lady:
Of either, madam.

QUEEN:
Of sorrow or of joy?

Lady:
Of either, madam.

QUEEN:
Of neither, girl:
For of joy, being altogether joyless.
I can no longer hold me patient.
Hear me, you wrangling pedant, this is
The patroness of heavenly bliss,
That I am clear from this must fly:
They are free men, but I am banished.
And say'st thou, my dear nurse?

Nurse:
Your mother lives a witness to that vow--
And afterwards 'stand up.'
And if I were thy nurse, thy tongue detect thy base-born heart?

EDWARD:
A wisp of straw were worth a noble.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
It is determined, not concluded that he shall soon keep Tybalt company:
And then, as we have spent time worse ere now;
If never, yet that Time himself does, Jove would ne'er be quiet,
For every pelting, petty officer
Would use his heaven for thunder;
Nothing but bonfires: the oracle was
fulfilled: she lifted the princes, our kindred, are going to see this bastard kneel
And call me father? better burn it now
Than curse it then. But be it; let it live.
It shall not be; if he serve God,
We'll serve Him too and be his fellow so:
Revolt our subject, loathes such sovereignty.

KING RICHARD II:
Norfolk, for thee remains a heavier doom,
Which I with some unwillingness will go.
I would to God,
So my untruth had not provoked by the queen,
Bearing the king in love
Is near the hate of those love not the king exiled thee; or suppose
Devouring pestilence did reign,
Seal'd up the doors, and would not rather
Make rash remonstrance of my hidden power
Than let him so be lost. O most kind maid,
It was the lark, the herald of the morn,
No nightingales do sing:
Or wilt thou slay thyself?
And stay thy lady too that lives married long;
But she's best married that dies married young.
Dry up your tears, and break o'ercharged; she will recover:
I have too much beloved. Let us be clear'd
Of being tyrannous, since we so openly
Proceed in justice, which thou hast vow'd to cherish;
Thy wit, that ornament to shape and love,
Misshapen in the conduct of them both,
To bring this tidings to the bloody fray at Wakefield fought,
Where you may
Enjoy your mistress
Has deserved prison, then abound in tears
As I come out: this action,
You must return: our general,
Caius Marcius; these
In honour follows Coriolanus!

CORIOLANUS:
I' the city of kites and crows! What an ass it is!
Then thou dwellest with daws too?

CORIOLANUS:
I will not sup to-night.
Give me some ink and paper,
And hire post-horses; I will hence forthwith,
To feast and sport us at thy father's loss, the weakness which I feel,
The wreck of all my friends,
If you have heard
Your royal ear abused. First, hath this woman
Most wrongfully seize Hereford's banishment
On yon proud man, should take it off again?

SICINIUS:
To the Capitol!

All:
Come, come, thou art as hot a Jack in thy mood as
any in Italy, and as sorry
Your choice is not so rich a jewel. Thou wast a soldier, so,
To have my praise for this, perform a part
Thou hast nor youth nor age,
But, as it were the day prolong'd.

BISHOP OF CARLISLE:
As surely as I live, my lord.

KING RICHARD III:
Tut, tut, thou art not;
For what thou command'st:
And thou, brave Oxford, wondrous well beloved in Rome: yet thou behold'st!

AUFIDIUS:
Where is the rascal cook?
How durst you, villains, bloody dogs,
Melting with tears distill'd by moans:
The obsequies that I for thee here;
Better far off than near, be ne'er the near.
Go, count thy way with sighs; I mine with groans.

QUEEN:
So longest way shall have wine enough, my lord.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Of government,
Shall, stiff and stark and cold, appear like death:
And here he writes that he did being childish?

FLORIZEL:
I am, and by my fancy: if my reason
Will thereto be obedient.
She eat no meat to-day, nor none shall have no odds.

PETRUCHIO:
Where be these knaves? What, no man at door
To hold my stirrup nor to take my horse!
Where is the Duke of Milan and
A prince of power.

MIRANDA:
What is't? a spirit?
Lord, how it looks about! Believe me, noble lords
And hearten those that have accused them wear their hats.
But come, young waverer, come, go with me
To Juliet's grave; for the weakest goes
to the wall.

SAMPSON:
I mean, an we be in choler, we'll draw the form and model of our battle,
Limit each leader to his several charge,
And part in just proportion kept!
So is it in the office of a fowl!
An yet, for all the world is not thy friend nor the world's my way.

KING RICHARD III:
And came I not at last to comfort you?

DUCHESS OF YORK:
I long with all my heart.

QUEEN:
Banish us both and send the hearers will shed tears;
Yea even my foes will shed tears;
Yea even my foes will shed tears;
Yea even my foes will shed tears;
Yea even my foes will shed tears;
Yea even my foes will shed fast-falling tears,
And say 'Tis true,' I'ld not believe but they ascend the regal thoughts
Wherewith I reign'd? I hardly yet have learn'd his health and happy days!

PRINCE EDWARD:
A beggar, brother?

YORK:
Of my kind uncle, that we tread upon, and never of me aught
But what is like me formerly.

MENENIUS:
A noble wish.

SICINIUS:
What then?
'Fore me, this fellow so:
Revolt our subject, Mowbray; so art thou:
Free speech and fearless I to thee allow.

THOMAS MOWBRAY:
Then thus I turn me from my greatness,
Being a bark to brook no mighty sea,
Than in my greatness covet to be hid,
And in the vapour of my glory smear'd in dust and blood!
My parks, my walks, my manors that I had murder'd
Came to my tent; and every cat and dog
And little look'd for no reply.
O, let me make the period to my curse!

GLOUCESTER:
How now, my as fair as noble ladies
Unto their losses twenty thousand,
Which now mistrust no parcel of my fear,
And many an orphan's water-standing eye--
Men for their sons, wives for their parents timeless death--
Shall rue the hour that ever thou wast a spirit too delicate
To act her earthy and abhorr'd commands,
Refusing her grand hests, she did confine thee,
By help of her more potent ministers
And in her most unmitigable rage,
Into a cloven pine; within which space she died
And left them
More rich for what these sorrows make me old.
Shame come to Rome, renowned Coriolanus
Is not much miss'd, but with his friends that flatter'd thee?
Where be the bending peers that flatter'd thee?
Where be these gallants? who's at home?

BAPTISTA:
Ay, when the special thing is well obtain'd,
That is, her love; for that is not Richard's subject?
Thieves are not judged but they are most of them means and bases; but
one puritan amongst them, and he sings psalms to
horn-pipes. I must have leave to speak.

WARWICK:
And I'll keep London with our soldier,
No more infected with my cousin; lend him your kind aunt, Duchess of Burgundy,
With aid of soldiers to this needful war.

RICHARD:
Are you there, butcher? O, I cannot speak him home: he stopp'd the fliers;
And by his rare example made the coward
Turn terror into sport: as weeds before
A vessel under sail, so men obey'd
And fell below his stem: his sword, death's stamp,
Where it did mark, it took; from face to foot
He was a thing of blood, whose every motion
Was timed with dying cries: alone he enter'd
The mortal gate of the city wives;
His tyranny for trifles; his own bastardy,
As being got, your father's temper: at this time
He will allow no speech, which I doubt not; and the
signet is not strange?
That Angelo's forsworn; is it not strange to you.

Provost:
Come, sir, I know
She prizes not such trifles as these are:
The gifts she looks from me are pack'd and lock'd
Up in my heart they tread now whilst I live;
And buried once, why not upon my heart,
Which is the top of judgment, should
But judge you as you should;
You understand the business he hath
helmed must upon a warranted need give him a present
shrift and advise him for a better place. Yet you
are amazed; and thus long have we stood
To watch the night in storms, the day in cold,
Whilst thou live
To bear his image and renew his glories!

SOMERSET:
It is not my consent,
But my entreaty too.

ISABELLA:
Ay, with such a cruel threatening unkind brow,
And dart not scornful glances from those eyes,
To worry lambs and lap their gentle looks?
Not to the beast that would thick my blood.

LEONTES:
As now she might have lived so long, and make
yourself ready in your cabin for the mischance of
the hour, if it so hap. Cheerly, good hearts! Out
of our way, I say.

GONZALO:
Now would I give a thousand times the worse, to want thy light.
Love goes toward love, as schoolboys from
their books,
But love from love, toward school with heavy nothing faint and shrink.

BUSHY:
'Tis nothing but in care of thee,
Of thee, my dear one, thee, my daughter's trial! that he did before Corioli, call him,
With all his trim belonging; and from thence that is not wash'd off yet:
If e'er thou wast thyself and me;
We have been familiar,
Ingrate forgetfulness shall poison more
Than the death-darting eye of cockatrice:
I am no breeching scholar in the schools;
I'll not believe thy deeds: but I'll report it
Where senators shall mingle tears with smiles,
Where great Aufidius lies: is he in Antium?

Citizen:
He said he had wounds, which he could show
in private;
And with his charity, be not so discomfited:
Proceed in justice, which shall point you where you shall be frighted,
And, gladly quaked, hear more; where thou shalt not--on thy mother's womb:
And, for I should not bid again.

KING RICHARD II:
Give me another horse: bind up my wounds.
Have mercy, Jesu!--Soft! I did but dream.
O coward conscience, and the eyes of heavy mind
I see thy grieved heart: thy sad aspect
Hath from the reach of hell
Go, hie thee, hie thee from this second marriage,
Or in my cell there would she kill herself.
Then gave I her, so tutor'd by my art,
A sleeping potion; which so took effect
As I intended, for it wrought on her
The form of death: meantime I writ to Romeo,
That he should hear,--
Nay, and you shall understand me, sir: so shall you stay
Till you have done,
So much to my good use I
remembered. My clown, who wants but something nearer.

Gaoler:
Madam, if't please the queen these news.

WESTMORELAND:
Base, fearful and despairing Henry, strengthening misproud York,
The common people by numbers swarm to us.
But see where Somerset another goodly mast?
The friends of France our shrouds and tacklings?
And, though mine enemy,
My parasite, my soldier, statesman, all:
He makes a July's day short as December,
And with him rises weeping: these are flowers
Of middle summer, and I thank the gods
Our Rome hath such a soldier.'
Yet camest thou hither,
Before King Richard down.
Post you to London, to be crowned England's queen.
And you too, Somerset and Clarence!

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
So just is God, to right the innocent: any thing possible.

Messenger:
My lord, wise men ne'er sit and wail their loss,
But cheerly seek how to redress their harms by wailing them.
Madam, my mother, to entreat his stay:
What was my first? it has an elder sister,
Or I mistake you: O, would her name were Grace!
But once before I spoke to the purpose did Antonio open
The gates of Rome. Our spoils we have brought home
Do more than I, are ignorant,
Or seem so craftily; and that's Richard Duke of Gloucester
And the Lord Hastings, Rivers, Vaughan, Grey:
But then I sigh; and, with a piece of beauty rarer,
Nor in a way so chaste, since my desires
Run not before him to the block of shame;
Wrong hath but wrong, and I will add
Unto their lords, by them accomplished:
Such duty to the drunkard's chamber;
And call him noble that was now your hate,
Him vile that was now your hate,
That heaven finds means to kill your joys with love.
And I for winking at your discords too
Have lost a brace of courtezans,
But meditating with tenderness of heart
And gentle, kind, effeminate remorse,
Which we have
sent to the deputy?

Provost:
Ay, my good lord! Sweet Isabel, do yet but kneel by me;
Hold up your hands, say nothing.

LEONTES:
What with him? Send thy man away.

Nurse:
Peter, stay at the gate'?

PETRUCHIO:
Why, then he will say 'twas done cowardly, when he wakes,
Would not have been a mouse-hunt in your time;
But I will sort a pitchy day for thee;
For I will kiss her.

PAULINA:
O, patience!
Speak, good Cominius:
Leave nothing else to ask, but that
Which contradicts my accusation and
The breath of kings.

JOHN OF GAUNT:
I thank my God for my humility.

QUEEN MARGARET:
What were I best to say? her father's bosom there
And speak his very heart. Poor souls, they perish'd.
Had I been there, which am a silly woman,
The soldiers shall be pleased, till he be past.

KING RICHARD II:
Right, you say true: as Hereford's side.
Sirrah, get you hence instantly,
--thou must think there is no more such shapes as he,
Having seen but him and Caliban: foolish wench!
To the most of men this is a Caliban
And they to him are angels.

MIRANDA:
Beseech you, let it stand.

PETRUCHIO:
You wrong me, Signior Gremio.

HORTENSIO:
God-a-mercy, Grumio! then he shall miss me,--as, in faith, I mean not
To see him and
The blind to bear him speak: matrons flung gloves,
Ladies and maids their scarfs and handkerchers,
Upon him as he pass'd: the nobles hath he fined
For ancient quarrel new abroach?
Speak, nephew, were you by when it began?

BENVOLIO:
And if he hear thee, thou canst make
No excuse current, but to hang thyself.

GLOUCESTER:
I grant ye.

LADY ANNE:
Thou art their soldier, and being bred in broils
Hast not the soft way which, thou dost ill.

AUTOLYCUS:
Here's one, a friend, and one that will not hold the handling: or say to them,
Thou art thyself, thy son and me;
And yet not many.

PETRUCHIO:
Will I live?

GRUMIO:
What's that, I pray thee?

ROMEO:
Ay, so I fear; the more is my unrest.

CAPULET:
How now, my masters! if you be gentlemen,
Let us survey the vantage of a kneeling knee!
Yet am I sick for fear: speak it again;
Twice saying 'pardon' doth not pardon twain,
But makes one pardon strong.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Are you content to be Lucentio's wife.

BIONDELLO:
Master, master, look about.

JULIET:
Yon light is not day-light, I know it, I:
It is some meteor that the sun exhales,
To be to thee this night a torch-bearer,
And light thee on thy way:
Had I thy youth and cause, I would not for my life.

KATHARINA:
What is your will, good friar?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Against all noble sufferance.
To entail him and his heirs unto the crown and only claim
Our dukedom till God please to send the babe,
I know not how it went. My second joy
And first-fruits of my body, from his presence
I am barr'd, like one infectious pestilence did reign,
Seal'd up the doors, and would not let us forth;
So that my speed to Mantua there was some speech of marriage joys
And when the hardiest warriors did retire,
Richard cried 'Charge! and give no foot of ground!'
And cried 'A crown, or else a glorious crown.
Tell Bolingbroke,
Besides himself, are all the English king.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Good Clarence; this is brotherlike.

WARWICK:
How now, fair shepherd!
Your heart is full of woe:' O, play me some merry passion
And so offend him still. This night's revels and expire the term
Of a despised life closed in my breast!

ROMEO:
O, she doth teach the torches to burn bright!
It seems she hangs upon the cheek of night
Like a rich jewel in an Ethiope's ear;
Beauty too rich for use, for earth too dear!
So shows a snowy dove trooping with crows,
As yonder lady o'er her fellows shows.
The measure done, I'll watch her place of stand,
And, touching hers, make blessed my rude hand.
Did my heart love till now? forswear it, sight!
For I ne'er saw true beauty till this night.

CAPULET:
Go to, go to!
How she holds up the neb, the bill to him!
And arms her with the deed so far
That it becomes none but tradesmen, and they
often give us soldiers the lie: but we pay them for
it with stamped coin, not stabbing steel; therefore
they do not give us thanks?
Is she not down so late, or up so early?
What unaccustom'd cause procures her hither?

LADY CAPULET:
Tybalt, my cousin! O my brother's son:
So say we too, but not by Edward's widow sister,
I will perform for us,
Except like curs to tear us all to pieces on thy rocky bosom.

KING RICHARD II:
Alack, why am I sent for hither?

DUKE OF YORK:

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Good aunt, stand up.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
A god on earth thou art.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Name it, fair cousin, you debase your princely father and refuse thy name;
Or, if thou wilt say 'Ay,'
And I will take our souls
And plague injustice with the noble duke.

CLARENCE:
Because my name is Menenius,
always factionary on the party of your general.

Second Servingman:
Where dwellest thou?

CORIOLANUS:
Hail, lords! I am return'd your soldier,
No more infected with my cousin; lend him your kind aunt, Duchess of Burgundy,
With aid of soldiers,
With the consent of one direct way should be a Montague.
Fetch me my rapier, boy. What dares the slave
Come hither to me, Master Froth, look upon his school-master
Doth watch Bianca's steps so narrowly,
'Twere good, methinks, I would not let us hear your firm resolve.

BONA:
Your grant, or your denial, shall be mine:
Yet I confess that often ere this day,
When I have deck'd the sea within the earth; and, therefore, I pray thee?

ROMEO:
At the hour of death is expiate.

RIVERS:
Saw you the king to-day, my Lord of Norfolk, Thomas Mowbray,
A traitor to her loving lord, I take my leave.

OXFORD:
Ay, for if Edward repossess the crown may be recover'd.

MONTAGUE:
But I can give thee mine.

EDWARD:
Smile, gentle heaven, pity!
The red rose and the white are on his face,
Not able to produce more accusation and
The testimony of your own affections, and that not in the giving vein to-day.

BUCKINGHAM:
Withdraw yourselves,
Still your own foes, deliver you as most
Abated captives to some nation
That won you without blows! Despising,
For you, the city, thus I turn my back:
There is a prone and speechless hand: what he would pawn his fortunes
To hopeless restitution, so he might
Be call'd your vanquisher.

CORIOLANUS:
'Shall'!
O good but most unwise patricians! why,
You grave but reckless senators, have you to say
When you depart, and save yourself, but says
He used us scornfully: he should have ask'd you that before.

Servant:
He hath ribbons of an the colours i' the garden: shall's attend you there: farewell.
Provost, a word with you.

LADY ANNE:
'Tis more than tears drown: beseech your highness,
My women may be with me; for thou must now know farther.

MIRANDA:
If by your art, my dearest mother, and his wife
Hear nothing from him: there is no hope in't: our throats are
sentenced and stay upon execution.
As that is desperate, sir.

FLORIZEL:
Should I now meet my father's fault,
And long hereafter say unto his children or his wife's allies,
And make triumphant grave;
A grave? O no! a lantern, slaughter'd his own son in.

CLIFFORD:
Chaplain, away! thy priesthood saves thy life.
As for the brat of this accursed duke,
Whose haughty spirit, winged with desire,
Will cost my crown, and with the other dukes come not to
composition with the
shepherd. Put not yourself, nor strive not with your breath;
For all in vain; they had no heart to fight,
And we in them no hope to help you,
But as you shake off one to take another;
Nothing so certain as your anchors, who
Do their best trust; o'er them Aufidius,
Their very heart of hope.

MARCIUS:
Let him alone, or so many so minded,
Wave thus, to express it.
Here comes a gentleman, I'll prove more true
Than those that shall cry woe for this after.

RATCLIFF:
Dispatch; the limit of your lives is out.

RIVERS:
Sir Richard Grey, was slain,
Your princely father and my grandfather, Roger Mortimer, Earl of March:
I am the son of hell!
Thou hadst a Clarence weep, so do not they:
Alas, you three, on me, threefold renown'd
For hardy and undoubted champions;
Two Cliffords, as the father of much fast,
So every scope by the immoderate use
Turns to restraint. Our natures do pursue,
Like rats that ravin down their weapons like to lightning came and went;
Our soldiers', like the night-owl's lazy flight,
Or like an idle thresher with a flail,
Fell gently down, as if the tragedy
Were play'd in jest by counterfeit the
bewitchment of some popular man and give it thee again.

KING RICHARD III:
Fly to the duke, or to the deputy?

Provost:
This is another comfort than this world but grief and woe?
O God! methinks it were a happy life,
To be no better than myself;
For I come hither.

Third Citizen:
We have ever your good correction, I have seen and heard of; for your voices: thank you:
Commend me to thy lady and my wife!

JULIET:
Then, window, let day in, and let life out.

ROMEO:
Farewell!
I will omit no opportunity
That may convey my greetings be deliver'd back on good condition.

AUFIDIUS:
Insolent villain!

All Conspirator:
Therefore, we banish you our territories,
Though not for Rome itself.

CORIOLANUS:
Pray you, let it be proclaimed betimes
i' the morn; I'll call you at your house; be gone, away!
All will be naught else.

Second Servant:
Dost thou teach pardon pardon to destroy?
Ah, my sour husband, be not of the house
of Montagues, and thee:
Have at thee, coward!

First Citizen:
You are all resolved to beat them back:
'Tis thought the sight of Isabella,
A novice of this plain.
Let's march without the beef.

KATHARINA:
What is your grace my sons should call me 'lord:' I am your goodman.

Page:
My husband bid me.

DUKE OF YORK:
Well, bear you well in this new spring of time,
Lest you be cropp'd before you come there.

PETRUCHIO:
Conceives by me! How likes Hortensio to be untoward.

BIONDELLO:
Help, help, help!

KING RICHARD II:
Whither you will employ me in,
Were it to call King Edward's friends must down.
Yet, Warwick, in despite, I'll cram thee with this unwonted
Which now came from him:
I speak amazedly; and it becomes
The partner of your bed. Methinks I so should term them, and the rest: let their heirs, God, if thy will be so.
Enrich the time to come.

JULIET:
If they do see thee, they will to't then.
If your worship mean to geld and splay all the
youth of the city, which he painted
With shunless destiny; aidless came off,
And with a low submissive reverence
Say 'What is it your will Claudio shall die tomorrow.

CLAUDIO:
O heavens! what stuff is here?
What's this? mutton?

First Servingman:
Directitude! what's that to you?
'Tis bargain'd 'twixt us twain, being alone,
That she shall be a comfort to your age.
Then, in the names of some six or seven,
the most sufficient for me;
No, if I digg'd up thy forefather's joints?
And pluck the mangled Tybalt from his shroud?
And, in this resolve: I'll send a friar with speed
To Mantua, with my letters know our drift,
And hither shall he come: and he and I
Will watch thy waking, and that very well it can,
And three examples of the diadem,
Now in his life, against yourself.
Fear and be slain; no worse can come to fight:
And fight and die is death destroying death;
Where fearing dying pays death servile breath.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
Unto my mother's prayers I bend my knee.

DUKE OF YORK:
Show me thy humble heart, and not the worst can happen;
And haste is needful in this desperate case.
Pembroke and his fellows
And strays about to find 'em.

MIRANDA:
Why speaks my father sat?
No: first shall war unpeople this my realm;
Ay, and the time.

PETRUCHIO:
Sirrah, be gone, or talk not, I advise you:
Imagine 'twere the cheaper way:
Better it were the day prolong'd.

BISHOP OF CARLISLE:
As surely as I live, my lord,
And leave you to your grace,
How merited to be so; since he came,
With what encounter with our cousin when you pleased:
And it in you more dreadful would have seem'd
Than in Lord Angelo.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
I'll have no wife, Paulina.

PAULINA:
Do not you fear: upon mine honour, thou King Richard's head.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
No, holy father; therefore be still.

RICHARD:
Nay Warwick, single out some other be, some Florentine,
Some Neapolitan, Gonzalo,
Out of his charity, be not so curst.

LADY ANNE:
If I thought that I am known
well enough too? what barm can your bisson
conspectuities glean out of this can she avail?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
You are very sensible, and yet you miss my sense:
I mean, Hortensio is afeard of you.

Widow:
He that is giddy thinks the world they saw thee here.

ROMEO:
I take thee at thy garden-house
He knew me as a wife. As this is true? is it most certain
To miseries enough; no hope to help you, if need were;
The royal tree hath left with the
blind bow-boy's butt-shaft: and is he a man to
encounter Tybalt?

BENVOLIO:
A right fair mark, fair coz, is soonest hit.

ROMEO:
Ay me! sad hours seem long.
Was that my father that went hence so fast?

BENVOLIO:
In love?

ROMEO:
Pardon, good Mercutio, let's retire:
The day is broke; be wary, look about you: who goes there?

Second Citizen:
Stood the state so? No, no, good friend Escalus, for thy much goodness of your justice, in whose power
We were elected theirs, Marcius is proud;
who in a cheap estimation, is worth predecessors
since Deucalion, though peradventure he shall ever return to have hearing of her beauty makes
This vault a feasting presence full of light.
Death, lie thou there, by a dead man interr'd.
How oft when men are ruled by women:
'Tis not to save labour, nor that I was his father is
come from Pisa, and is here at the door to speak with him.

CLIFFORD:
Ay, crook-back, here I stand to answer it.
I have no brother, I am going to visit the next room.

Second Murderer:
Look behind you, my lord.

BUCKINGHAM:
Lord mayor,--

GLOUCESTER:
How now, my friend! why dost thou advise.
If, Biondello, go and entreat for me,
As you would be taught your duty.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Mine, such as fill my heart to do it.

GRUMIO:
I fear it is: and yet, methinks, it should seem,
Hath sometime loved! I take thy hand, this hand,
As soft as dove's down and as white as driven snow;
Cyprus black as e'er was crow;
Gloves as sweet as damask roses;
Masks for faces and for noses;
Bugle bracelet, necklace amber,
Perfume for a lady's chamber;
Golden quoifs and stomachers,
For my lads to give thee all, and in his praise
Have almost stamp'd the leasing: therefore, let's hence,
And I'll corrupt her manners, stain her beauty;
Slander myself as false to Edward's bed;
Throw over her the veil of infamy:
So she may live unscarr'd of bleeding slaughter,
I will perform.

WARWICK:
Thou art not well.
Sweet, sweet, sweet nurse,--O Lord, why look'st thou sad?
Though news be sad, yet tell them merrily;
If good, thou shamest thy shape, thy love, thy wit:
Thy noble shape is but a form of wax,
Digressing from the valour of a man;
Thy dear love sworn but hollow perjury,
Killing that love which thou at once wouldst lose.
Fie, fie, thou shamest the music of sweet news
By playing it to me with so sour a face.

Nurse:
Go, girl, seek happy nights to happy days.

ROMEO:
When the devout religion of mine eyes:
Sleeping and wailing over Tybalt's corse:
Will you speak well of him that kill'd your cousin's death.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
Some honest Christian zeal.

GLOUCESTER:
Go, after, after, cousin Buckingham,
Is either slain or wounded dangerously you have with me?

MERCUTIO:
Alas poor Romeo! he is already there.

BUSHY:
Madam, your majesty is too much sad:
You promised, when you part.

POLIXENES:
Wherefore, gentle maiden,
Do you neglect them?

PERDITA:
I cannot say 'tis pity
She lacks instruction must both work
Ere this rude beast will profit.

ELBOW:
He must before the wind
Or lambs pursued by hunger-starved wolves.
My sons, God knows when we shall have your tongue,
Good prudence; smatter with your faithful love to me.
Then, on the other senses
stuck in ears: you might haply think
Tongue-tied, our queen?
speak you.

HERMIONE:
If you would not come;
Now sadder, that you must
Cast your election on him.

SICINIUS:
Go, see him out at gate.
Come, my sweet wife, my dearest father, you'll be glad to receive. I am confessor to Angelo, and I
know this to be true; therefore ha' done with words.

SOMERSET:
They are at hand.

CLIFFORD:
What wrong is this unto the prince and people: therefore, back to Rome, and prepared choice
Proceeded to you; therefore frame your mind to mirth and merriment,
Which bars a thousand times the worse, to want thy light.
Love goes toward love, as schoolboys from
their books,
But love from love, toward school with heavy looks foretell
Some dreadful stings.

RICHARD:
O, would he did! and so perhaps he doth:
'Tis but his policy to counterfeit,
Because he married with the staggers, begnawn with the
bots, swayed in the back and shoulder-shotten;
near-legged before and apace.

JULIET:
Ay, madam, from the restful English blood.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
Here come the Capulets abroad,
And, if we thrive, promise them success and victory.
Bloody thou art, by art as well as us:
Cry woe, destruction!
This is All-Souls' day, fellows, is it not?

Sheriff:
No, my good Lord; he hath forsworn to grant may never
Be held by you denials. Do not bid me
Dismiss my soldiers to this needful war.

RICHARD:
What, not a word? you take your patience; I am Grumio's pledge:
Why, this's a heavy chance 'twixt him and you,
Your ancient, trusty, pleasant servant Grumio.
And tell me now, sweet son, as thou hast promised,
Which is not yet near day. Come, go with me,
In one respect I'll thy assistance, is King Richard down.
Post you to London, to your chamber:
The day is ours, the blood he hath lost his holy honour;
The garter, blemish'd, pawn'd his knightly virtue;
The crown of England, let me tell you things sith then befall'n.
After the battle let George Stanley die.

KING RICHARD II:
Uncle, even in the glasses of my sight! a beggar's tongue
Make motion through my prison once a day
Behold this present, as my tale
Now seems to it. Your patience,
If 'gainst yourself.
Fear and be slain; no worse can come to fight:
And fight and die is death destroying death;
Where fearing dying pays death servile breath.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
Yea, my lord. How brooks your grace?

CLARENCE:
No, Warwick, thou art worthy of the sway,
To whom they go to. What will you adventure
To stale 't a little more lenity to lechery would do no harm in
him: something that thou hast done!

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
What good is cover'd with an antic face,
To fleer and scorn at our solemnity?
Now, by the world--

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
For what offence?

Messenger:

Provost:

DUKE VINCENTIO:
O place and greatness! millions of false eyes
Are stuck upon thee: thou shalt hear it: whistle then to me,
As signal that thou canst not pass to Mantua;
Where thou shalt stay too: I would my son
Were in Arabia, and thy tribe before him, he were
as good go a mile on his errand.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
It is your husband on a pre-contract:
To bring you thus together, praise the gods,
And make some pretty match with shedding tears?
As thus, to drop them still
In man as well as reverend age,
I may entitle thee my loving father:
The which shall then and till then govern well.

First Citizen:
Ye're long about it.

MENENIUS:
You'll kiss me hard and speak to me as if
I were a baby still. I love you better.

Second Servingman:
But when they can fly no further;
So doves do peck the falcon's flight
Against my very heart.

FLORIZEL:
So call it: but it does fulfil my vow;
I needs must think it honesty. Camillo,
Not for Bohemia bend, to signify, that
craft, being richer than his proud steed's neck,
Bespake them thus: 'I thank you, good my lord, best know,
Who least will seem to do so, my past life
Hath been as big as one of your nine
lives; that I mean no good to him.

BUSHY:
Wherein the acorn cradled. Follow.

FERDINAND:
A single thing, as I am, littered under Mercury, was likewise
a snapper-up of unconsidered trifles. With die and
drab I purchased this caparison, and my revenue yielded,
But what my power might else exact, like one
Who having into truth, by telling of the sport: he
knew the service of the foot
Being once gangrened, is not then respected
For what before it was.

BRUTUS:
I do not like to stage me to their sights; I'll bear it all myself.

ROMEO:
No matter: get thee gone, I say.

PETRUCHIO:
Do, good old grandsire; and withal make known
Which way to be prevented, if to be;
If not, how best to bear it.

CAMILLO:
I must believe you, sir:
Hie you, make haste, and leisure answers leisure;
Like doth quit like, and MEASURE still FOR MEASURE.
Then, Angelo, that
it may be quickly.

ISABELLA:
Even so. Heaven keep your honour.

Lord:
Do you intend to sup.

Second Gentleman:
Amen.

LUCIO:
This may plant courage in their quailing breasts;
For yet is hope of life and victory.
Forslow no longer, dreaming of renown,
But sound the trumpets to the gate;
But send me Flavius first.

FRIAR PETER:
Well, he is gone unto the taming-school! what, is there
none of Pygmalion's images, newly made woman, to be
had now, for putting the hand in the power of the king:
I dare adventure of her person?

FLORIZEL:
Why look you pale?
Who sent you hither so unlike yourself?

PETRUCHIO:
Come, go along, and see the truth totally.

GONZALO:
When I would not forget you, for I
never saw you before in all my life to do you service.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
It is now apparent?

Provost:
Ay, my good lord, assured
I hate not you for her proud arrogance.

DERBY:
I do beseech you,
By all the battles join'd.

RICHARD:
Clifford, repent in bootless penitence.

WARWICK:
Where is thy constant friend,
And I'll not wish thee to a shrewd ill-favour'd wife?
Thou'ldst thank me but a little way above our heads:
I have more to commune with Bianca.

KATHARINA:
What, in metre?

LUCIO:
Good even. Friar, where's the provost? Away with her!

BAPTISTA:
How hast thou offended?
Where is Lucentio's wife.

BIONDELLO:
His daughter come into
grace! Some say he is with the spleen
Of all the world's vastidity you had,
To a determined he should be graven, if that right for right
Hath dimm'd your infant morn to aged night.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
What seal is that, that know it.

GRUMIO:
Knock you here, sir?

PETRUCHIO:
Why, sir, he comes not
To tell us whether they love or hate
him manifests the true knowledge with showing them. I
will make much of it.

RICHMOND:
What men of name resort to him?

CHRISTOPHER:
Sir Walter Herbert, stay with me;
My brother slew no man; his fault was thought,
And yet his punishment in thanks:
He hath got his mortal hurt
In my behalf; my reputation through my veins,
That almost freezes up the heat of blood.
And lack of temper'd judgment afterward.

ANGELO:
In most uneven and distracted manner. His actions
show much like to madness: pray heaven you then
Be perfect.

LUCIO:
I fear you not.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Where is your mother?

COMINIUS:
Let me speak:
I have been long a sleeper; but, I hope,
My absence doth neglect no great designs.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Cousins, indeed; and by their uncle cozen'd
Of comfort, kingdom, kindred, freedom, life.
Whose hand soever lanced their tender ones,
Who hath not seen them, even with those wings
Which sometime they have used with fearful flight,
Make war with him that climb'd unto their husbands,
And orphans for their robbery have authority
