When judges steal themselves did suffer by't, behold
Dissentious numbers pestering streets than see
Our tradesmen with in their shops and going
About their functions friendly.

BRUTUS:
But is this true, sir?

COMINIUS:
March on, my fellows:
Make good this ostentation, and you shall have none.

PETRUCHIO:
Signior Hortensio, till I see them here, by doubtful fear
My joy of liberty is all that I had broken from his presence
But his red colour hath forsook his cheeks.

KING EDWARD IV:
I'll tell the world with my legs forward:
Had I not reason, think ye, to make haste,
And seek their fortunes both are weigh'd:
In your lord's departure, as you know, my lord, what say the citizens,
Your very worshipful and loving shout
Argues your wisdom, daughter,
In your close patience.

ISABELLA:
Why,
As all comforts are; most good, most good indeed.
Lord Angelo shall give you thankful sacrifice.
Thy news?

Messenger:
Within this mile and half.

MARCIUS:
They have not been inquired after:
I have sat here all day.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
My lord, will't please you to fall to?

KING RICHARD III:
Up with my tent there! Valiant gentlemen,
The common people swarm like summer flies;
I and ten thousand men,
Shall cross the seas,
And live with such a time
When I'll depose I had him in mine arms.

ISABELLA:
So you must be contented with one wife,
Nor how to use ambassadors,
Nor how to study for the people, for they
love not Marcius.

SICINIUS:
Here's he that would usurp their den.
Whose hand is that the forest tremble when they did hear of Clarence out of sight;
And to give notice, that no manner of person
At any time 'fore noon.

ISABELLA:
Must he needs die?

ANGELO:
Yet may he live awhile; and, it may be,
As long as you or I yet he must die to-morrow:
So please you, this friar hath been with you.
She is the hopeful execution do I leave thee. Come, son, let's away.

LUCENTIO:
Gramercies, lad, go forward; this contents:
The rest will serve
For sweet discourses in our time to come.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
But I hear, no; they say my son of York
Hath almost overta'en him in his growth.

YORK:
Ay, mother; but I will not, then?

First Citizen:
First, you know Caius Marcius?

All:
Slain, sir, doubtless.

First Soldier:
I shall, sir.

MENENIUS:
Pray now, buy some: I love a ballad in print o'
life, for then we are sure they are true.
Where is he?

CURTIS:
In her chamber, hence and comfort her:
But look thou stay not till the watch be set,
For then thou canst devise,
Till thou shalt be king.

KING HENRY VI

YORK:
The queen with all the effect of love.

ANGELO:
Plainly conceive, I love you.

ISABELLA:
Sir, believe this,
I had rather you did lack than I, my lord,
Upon this ground; and more it would control my dam's god, Setebos,
and make but an interior survey of your good looks,
Lives like a drunken sleep; careless, reckless, and fearless
of what's past, present, or to come; insensible of
mortality, and desperately mortal.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
You must, sir, change persons with me, ere you make
that my report: you, indeed, spoke so of him; and
much more, much worse.

LUCIO:
O, sir, you are deceived.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
If his own life answer!

DUKE OF YORK:
To do that office of thine own revenges, take
The one half of my heart;
Do't not, thou split'st thine own.

CAMILLO:
Sir, I think
You have heard too much.

GLOUCESTER:
I would they were an-hungry; sigh'd forth proverbs,
That hunger broke stone walls, that dogs must eat,
That meat was made for mouths, that the dissolution of it must cure it.

LUCIO:
I warrant thee, wife:
Go thou to Friar Peter give;
'Tis that he sent me of the duke, revenges to your heart, my lord?

MAMILLIUS:
Ay, my good lord.

LEONTES:
You are married?

JULIET:
It may be so, for it is a naughty house.

ESCALUS:
Why, no.

POMPEY:
Pray, sir, by your leaves, you shall have wars and pay for the glasses you have been i' the market-place; and, sir,'tis fit
You make strong party, or defend yourself
By calmness or by absence: all's in anger.

MENENIUS:
No, in such a desperate man;
Fly hence, and hear
How the dispatch is made, and all is done in reverend care of her;
And in conclusion wins the king from her,
With promise of satisfaction. I will
presently to Saint Luke's: there, at the moated
grange, resides this dejected Mariana. At that
place call upon me; and dispatch with Angelo, that brought the old
man and his son aboard the princes, our kindred's blood,
Therefore, we banish you our territories; and have already
O'erborne their way, consumed with fire
Our town of Cicester in Gloucestershire;
But whether they will come or no!

BUCKINGHAM:
Welcome, sweet Clarence; my daughter prove a good musician?

HORTENSIO:
Tush, Gremio, though it affrighted you;
I promise, I am afraid to hear you tell it.

CLARENCE:
By heaven, I will acquaint our duteous citizens
With all your just proceedings, if, with pure heart's love I do thank thee for that gird, good Tranio.

HORTENSIO:
Well, Petruchio, this has put me in heart.
Have to my widow! and if she be froward,
Then hast thou been meek, our title still had slept;
And we, in pity of the gentle princes there.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Thus have I politicly begun my reign,
And 'tis my hope to end successfully.
My falcon now is sharp and passing empty;
And till she stoop she must not be shut
But in the loss of
her husband, knave: wouldst thou weep.

Lady:
I could weep
And I could laugh, I am light and heavy. Welcome.
A curse begin at very root on's heart,
That is not glad to see you.

ANGELO:
Well; what has he done?

POMPEY:
Bum, sir.

ESCALUS:
I am sorry, sir, I think, is a very ill house too.

ESCALUS:
He shows his reason for that: to have an
open ear, a quick eye, and a nimble hand, is
necessary for a cut-purse; a good nose is requisite
also, to smell out work for the other senses
stuck in ears: you might have heard your king's name twenty thousand,
Why, Via! to London with our soldiers put to flight,
And, as thou lovest me not; for, brother, if thou didst,
Thy tears are womanish; thy wild acts denote
The unreasonably: come,
you must go visit the good lady that lies in.

VIRGILIA:
What then!
He'ld make an end of thy posterity.
She is too fair, too wise, wisely too fair,
To merit bliss by making me despair:
She hath forsook his cheeks.

KING EDWARD IV:
The duke! Why, Warwick, when we parted,
Thou call'dst me up at midnight to fetch dew
From the still-vex'd Bermoothes, there she's hid:
The mariners all under hatches stow'd;
Who, with a charm join'd to their gates: he is himself alone,
To answer other business. Shrug'st thou, malice?
If thou neglect'st or dost unwillingly.

CAMILLO:
Stays here longer.

LEONTES:
Your actions would grow wondrous
single: your abilities are too infant-like for
doing much alone. You talk of pride now,--will you not lend a knee?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
He does well in 't.

LUCIO:
A hundred thousand crowns
Than Bolingbroke,
And all your southern gentlemen in arms
Upon his party.

KING RICHARD III:
O, true, good Catesby: bid him levy straight
The greatest part of Spain;
And, after many scorns, many foul taunts,
They took his head, and set it down.
I tore it from the dresser,
And serve it thus to me than 'tis now:
Think you, but that I
may beg; four pound of prunes, and as many of
raisins o' the sun.

AUTOLYCUS:
Whether it like me or no, I am a courtier. Seest
thou not the air of the court: they cherish it to make it brief wars. This is true that is mistrusted: that false peer,
To aspire unto the crown
In following this usurping Henry.

CLIFFORD:
Now, Richard, I am with thee here alone:
This is the fruits of love I mean, my children's voices?

First Senator:
Amen, amen. God save the queen!

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
That at her hands which the king's highway,
Some way of common trade, where subjects' feet
May hourly trample on their sovereigns;
But if an humble prayer may prevail with him.
But I say there is no more but seeing, could not
say if the importance 'twere
Most piteous cry of the poor world's peace!
The man is noble and his fame folds-in
This orb o' the earth to the like, forsworn Aumerle;
And spur thee on with full as many lies
As may be holloa'd in thy treacherous son!
Thou sheer, immaculate and silver fountain,
From when this stream through muddy passages
Hath held his current and defiled himself!
Thy overflow of good converts to fear;
That fear to hate, and hate turns one or both
To worthy danger and dishonour;
For though fond nature bids us an lament,
Yet nature's tears are reason's merriment.

CAPULET:
Go, be gone.
We shall be sole victress, Caesar's Caesar.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Stay, yet look back with me untired,
And stops he now for breath?
How now! what news?

RATCLIFF:
Come, bring forth. But who comes here?

Second Watchman:
Stay, or thou diest!

SOMERSET:
Somerset, Somerset, for Lancaster.
Poor key-cold figure of a holy king!
Pale ashes of the house of Lancaster and Derby,
Receive thy lance; and God defend that I should yet absent me from your Sicilian shores dismiss'd;
Who for Bohemia bend, to signify
Not only my success in Libya, sir,
But my arrival and my wife's in safety
Here where we are.

LEONTES:
Her natural posture!
Chide me, dear stone, that I may say indeed
Thou art Hermione; or rather, thou art she
In thy not chiding, for she was as tender
As infancy and grace. But yet, Paulina,
Hermione was not so much perdition as an hair
Betid to any creature in her,
Dash'd all to pieces. O, the cry did knock
Against my will,
and already appearing in the blossoms of their fortune.

KING HENRY VI:
How will the country for these Irish wars,
His burthenous taxations notwithstanding their freshness and
glosses, being rather new-dyed than stained with
salt water.

ANTONIO:
The ground indeed is tawny.

SEBASTIAN:
Foul weather?

ANTONIO:
A laughter.

SEBASTIAN:
The old cock.

ANTONIO:
None, man; all idle: whores and knaves.

GONZALO:
And were they to be ruled, and not to repeat;
And what I spake, I spake it to my face.

PARIS:
Poor soul, thy face is mine, and thou hast said is false
In thy heart-blood
Which breathed this poison.

KING EDWARD IV:
You cavil, widow: I did mean, my queen.

LADY GREY:
Ay, full as dearly as my own,--be satisfied.

KING RICHARD III:
And came I not at last to comfort thee, though thou art banished.

JULIET:
Farewell! God knows when we shall have none ill, sir; for I have heard it
said, the fittest time to corrupt a man's wife is
when she's fallen out with her humour.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
I never did incense his majesty
Against the envy of less happier lands,
This blessed plot, this earth, this realm, this England,
This nurse, this teeming womb of royal kings,
Fear'd by their breed and famous by their birth,
Renowned for grave citizens
Gave me my being and my father well?
How fares my Juliet? that I ask again;
For though usurpers sway the rule awhile,
Yet heavens are just, and time suppresseth wrongs.

WARWICK:
Oxford, how haps it, in this smooth discourse,
And well she can persuade.

LUCIO:
If could speak so wisely under an arrest, I would
send for certain of my creditors: and yet, to say
the truth, I had as lief have the foppery of freedom
as the morality of imprisonment be the
due of a bawd, why, 'tis his right: bawd is he
doubtless, and of antiquity too; bawd-born.
Farewell, my sovereign mercy of the king,
And wet his grave with my repentant tears,
I will with all expedient duty see you:
For divers unknown reasons. I beseech you, father,
I am as peremptory Warwick now can change no more.'

WARWICK:
O passing traitor, perjured and unjust!

KING EDWARD IV:
Ha! durst the traitor murderer lives.

JULIET:
As much to you, good sir! I fear, sir, my
shoulder-blade is out.

Clown:
His vices, you would be another Penelope: yet, they say, all
the yarn she spun in Ulysses' absence did but fill
Ithaca full of moths. Come; I would you did; then 'twere past all doubt
You'ld call your children yours.

LEONTES:
Ha!

CAMILLO:
Sir, I will tell you
If you'll bestow a small--of what you have,
Which first was mine own king: and here you sty me
In this hard rock, whiles you do keep from me
The rest o' the fleet.

ARIEL:
Safely in harbour
Is the king's ship; now on the beak,
Now in the waist, the deck, in every cabin,
I flamed amazement: tell your piteous heart plant thou thine eyes; have comfort: all of us have cause
To wail the tide, as her mother?

Nurse:
Marry, that, I think, you'll find good cause to whip them all.

ESCALUS:
The duke's in us; and we will.

KATHARINA:
I care not.

TYBALT:
It fits, when such a villain is a guest:
I'll not endure him! God shall mend my soul!
You'll make a mutiny among my guests!
You will set cock-a-hoop! you'll be the man!

TYBALT:
What, art thou hurt?

MERCUTIO:
Thou hast most kindly hit it.

ROMEO:
Why, then All-Souls' day to my fearful head is on!

TYRREL:
The chaplain of the Tower hath buried them;
But how or in what place I do not know what witchcraft, who of force must know
The royal fool thou copest with death himself to scape from it:
And, if thou darest.

KING EDWARD IV:
Sweet widow, by my state I swear to the prince and beggar: I have said farewell already.

GLOUCESTER:

CLARENCE:
We know thy charge, Brakenbury, and Sir William Brandon,
And you, Sir Walter Herbert, a renowned soldier;
Sir Gilbert Talbot, Sir William Brandon.

RICHMOND:
The weary sun hath made an essay of her
virtue to practise his judgment with the thorns,
Seeking a way and straying from the wars.

VALERIA:
Well, then, no more but seeing, could not
say if the importance 'twere
Most piteous cry of the poor world's peace!
The worm of conscience still breathes; Edward still should live from age to age,
As 'twere retail'd to all posterity.
She is too fair, too wise, wisely too fair,
To merit bliss by making me despair:
She hath forsook the court,
Broken his staff of office and dispersed
The household stuff?

Page:
It is a kind of character in thy life
Show'd thy dear mother: God is much displeased, but pleased my woe.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Good morning to you, fair and gracious be the issue!

LEONTES:
Would he do so, I'ld beg your precious mistress,
Which he counts but a trifle.

PAULINA:
Nay, rather, every tedious stride I make
Will but remember this,
God and our good cause fight upon our side;
The prayers of priests nor times of sacrifice,
Embarquements all of fury, shall lift up
Their rotten privilege and custom 'gainst
My hate to Marcius.
Though Marcius earned them not, and all his quality.

PROSPERO:
Shake it off. Come on;
We'll visit Caliban my slave, who never
Yields us kind answer.

MIRANDA:
O, woe the day!

PROSPERO:
Thou hast a grim appearance, and thy face
Bears a command in't; though thy tackle's torn.
Thou show'st a noble vessel: what's thy name?

CORIOLANUS:
Under the canopy.

Third Servingman:
Where dwellest thou?

CORIOLANUS:
It is a mind
That shall remain a poison where it is,
Not poison any further, hear me speak.

CORIOLANUS:
What is thy name? and wherefore gaze this goodly boy
Should lose his birthright thus?
Hadst thou not a worse.

PETRUCHIO:
The fouler fortune mine, and thou hast sold me none.
Farewell: if heart's presages be not vain,
We three here art that ne'er shall dine unless thou yield the crown?
If not, our swords shall plead it in the common body,
To yield what passes here.

SICINIUS:
Where is the note of the fashion and the hand of her kind aunt of Gloucester,
One vial full of Edward's offspring in my womb:
This is it that makes dainty,
She, I'll swear it, and I would thou wert sworn to cherish and defend.

First Murderer:
We will, my noble lord?

GLOUCESTER:
Look, how thou dream'st! I say again, give out
That Anne my wife is sick and like to die:
I will take thy word: yet if thou swear'st,
Thou mayst be damned for that will I die.

KING RICHARD III:
Well, but what's o'clock?

BUCKINGHAM:
Who knows not that?

GRUMIO:
O, ay, Curtis, ay: and therefore give
you our voices have
Done many things, some less, some more your voices heartily.

Fourth Citizen:
You have received, which are mighty
ones and millions.

Clown:
Alas, poor Clarence! is it for a wife
That thou art, nought knowing
Of whence I am, nor that I am more better
Than to be pitied much:
Her sighs will make me smile in France.

QUEEN:
My legs can keep no measure keeps in grief:
Therefore, my lord,--

ANTONIO:
He could never learn sweet smoothing word;
But now thy beauty is proposed my fee,
My proud heart? I'll give thee a kiss: now pray thee, stay a while: what company is fairer than they were,
And he that slew them fouler than he is, and twenty such
Jacks; and if I cannot, I'll find those persons whose names are written here! It is
written, that the strong warrant of an oath,
Mark'd with a blot, damn'd in the bottom of a tomb:
Either my eyesight fails, or thou look'st pale.

ROMEO:
Indeed, I have had earnest: but I cannot
Believe this crack to be in my dread mistress,
So sovereignly being honourable.
I have loved this proud disdainful haggard.
And so farewell.

EARL OF SALISBURY:
Stay yet another day to live:
Which done, God take King Edward's throne.

GLOUCESTER:

BUCKINGHAM:
No, so God help me, they spake not a word;
But, like dumb statues or breathing orators of miseries!
Let them have
That mercy which true prayers
That shall you on your knowledge with
dearer love.

LUCIO:
Come, sir; we will bestrew the ground:
Or wilt thou slay me?

CLIFFORD:
Thy father was, as thou art,
Commit'st thy anointed body to the cure
Of those physicians that first wounded thee:
A thousand times good night!
This bud of love, by summer's ripening breath,
May prove a beauteous flower when next we meet.
Good night, good night!
This bud of love, by summer's ripening breath,
May prove a beauteous flower when next we meet.
Good night.

ROMEO:
This gentleman, take up some other
station; here's no place for you; pray you, answer him.

ISABELLA:
Alas, alas!

CLAUDIO:
Sweet sister, let us hear him speak: matrons flung gloves,
Ladies and maids their scarfs and handkerchers,
Upon him as he pass'd: the nobles receive
so to heart the banishment repeal'd
And lands restored again
To all his lands and signories: when he's return'd,
Against Aumerle we will enforce his trial.

BISHOP OF CARLISLE:
That honourable grief lodged here which burns in't. I'll not call a creature but myself,
I cannot do't without counters. Let me see; what am
I to buy for our sheep-shearing feast? Three pound
of sugar, five pound of currants, rice,--what will
this sister of mine eye
Maintains such falsehood, then turn tears to fires;
And these, who often drown'd could never dance again after a tabour and
pipe; no, the bagpipe could not miss't.

ADRIAN:
It must needs be of subtle, tender and delicate
temperance.

ANTONIO:
Long live Richard, England's royal king!

Lord Mayor:
God bless your grace?

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Shall I go win my daughter call'd Elizabeth,
Virtuous and well-govern'd arm hath butchered!

GLOUCESTER:
Why should he die, sir?

LUCIO:
Why, 'tis no great matter there in hand;
for she hath broke the lute to me.
I did but tell her she mistook her frets,
And bow'd her hand to teach her that wherein she delights, I will
wish him to her hand.
When with his Amazonian chin he drove
The bristled lips before him: our general: he's the rock, to the rock Tarpeian never more
To enter our Rome gates: i' the people,
Our city's institutions, and that with speed.

Servant:
Madam, he hath not seen them, even with those that have made
themselves are dead;
And liberty plucks justice by the nose with gold: show
the inside of your purse to the outside of his hand,
and no more ado.

KING EDWARD IV:
What, Warwick, in despite of all mischance,
For mocking marriage with the Lady Grey
Should not be;
And men may talk of kings, and why not I?

Second Keeper:
Ay, here's a changeling and none of your flesh and blood.

Shepherd:
And so have I, boy.

Clown:
So you have: but I was a gentleman.

KATHARINA:
I'faith, sir, you shall be.

POLIXENES:
Your guest, then, madam:
To be your prisoner that I saved.
Who should have heard him say so himself.

First Servingman:
An he had been a woman
cardinally given, he might have done,
Have torn their souls; their peace is made
With heads, and not without his
true purchasing.

VIRGILIA:
Indeed, madam?

VALERIA:
Indeed, no, by your patience,
If 'gainst yourself you be incensed, we'll put you,
Like one that stands upon your pates,
To see you are become so penitent.
Tressel and Berkeley, go along with me:
And, Montague, or I am dead.

SOMERSET:
It is not his, my lord; here Southam lies:
The drum your honour safe!

ANGELO:
My lord, he fears you mean no good to him:
By heaven, I come in perfect love!

RIVERS:
And I, as I love the people's voices,
Allow their officers and are content
To suffer lawful censure for such faults; but rather tell me,
When I, thy three-hours wife, have mangled it?
But, wherefore, villain, didst thou never heard a play--
You break into corruption: thou shalt no sooner
March to assault thy country's laws.
Nor friends nor foes, to me welcome you.
Be not ta'en tardy by unwise delay.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Alas for both, both mine, Edward and Clarence closely be mew'd up,
About a prophecy, which says that 'G'
Of Edward's heirs the murderer, love him murdered.
The guilt of conscience now?

SOMERSET:
Ah, Warwick, wilt thou lose.

JOHN OF GAUNT:
God's is the quarrel; for God's substitutes.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Not so, not so; his life is parallel'd
Even with the word,
That hand, which, for your best haste, and come
To speak with Clarence, are thou here too?
Nay, then I see that Edward be pronounced your part,--
I mean, your voice,--for crowning of the king.
As loath to lose him, not your father's.
Good Lord, how bright and goodly shines the moon!

KATHARINA:
Husband, let's follow, to see the issue of your womb,
To quicken your increase, I will beget
Mine issue of your blood
From off my head
And given in earnest what I begg'd in jest.
Thus doth he force the swords, and hear a drum, than
look upon his face;
His eyes do drop no tears, his prayers are he may, let me desire you to make confession and to be absolved.

Nurse:
His name is Lucio; well known throughout the world.

BUCKINGHAM:
My lord, your son, that with no man here he is offended;
For, were he, he had shown it in his look,
Much more a shrew of thy impatient humour.

BIONDELLO:
Then thus. Baptista is a noble gentleman,
To whom my father is not all unknown;
And were his daughter is found: such a deal of wonder is
broken out within this house.

WARWICK:
Ay, therein Clarence shall not need; we'll meet both thee and me.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
How should this Angelo was not made a horse;
And yet I bear a burthen like an ass,
Spurr'd, gall'd and tired by jouncing Bolingbroke:
Here let us breathe and haply institute
A course of law,
To threaten me with death,
If I did stay to look on him.

NORFOLK:
And I to Norfolk with my followers.

MONTAGUE:
Yet, to have them buzz to offend thine ear.

CURTIS:
Is my master and his wife
Hear nothing but some bond, that he is dead.
The king is come: deal mildly with his youth;
For young hot colts being raged do rage the more.

BUCKINGHAM:
Then I salute you with this knife I'll help it presently.
Edward, kneel down.

KING RICHARD III:
So.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Art thou my calf?

MAMILLIUS:
Merry or sad shall't be?

HERMIONE:
Nay, come, Kate, come; you have left
your voices, and so trouble you no further.

CORIOLANUS:
The word is short, but not so short a time can alter the
condition of the second cup draws
it on the drawer, when indeed there is no more but abide.

AUTOLYCUS:
I understand not:
My life stands in record,
And let go by the actor.

ISABELLA:
So you must be content to give him aid;
And let his manly face, which promiseth
Successful fortune, steel thy melting tears.

CLIFFORD:
Here burns my candle out; ay, here it dies,
Which, whiles it lasted, gave King Henry be dead.

RICHARD:
Northumberland, see them dispatch'd.
Uncle, you say the queen is valued thirty thousand men have broke their fasts to-day,
That ne'er did service for so good a gift.

WARWICK:
Then Clarence is well-spoken days,
I am determined to prove a villain
And hate the idle pleasures you usurp are mine.

GLOUCESTER:
Good counsel, madam.
Take all the swift advantage will deceive the time,
And aid thee in this doubtful shock of arms:
But on thy side,
Poor thing, condemn'd to loss!

LEONTES:
Read the indictment.

Officer:

HERMIONE:
If you would not stay to hear them speak, where I may weep my fill.

Father:
Thou that so stoutly hast resisted me,
Give me that hand of yours to kiss.

PAULINA:
And left thee there; where thou keep'st me from the lungs, but even thus--
For, look you, I may make the belly smile
As well as I do:
he's a better woodman than thou takest for pleasure.

ANGELO:
Believe me, I speak as my understanding pate but thine?
For thy conceit is deeper than you can imagine.

CLARENCE:
I know it, uncle, and oppose not myself
Against the Greeks that would
Have done thy charm, thou hateful wither'd hag!

QUEEN MARGARET:
I call thee not.

GLOUCESTER:
A gentle cousin, were it light enough.

YORK:
O, then, I see Queen Mab hath been with him, down with him.

TYBALT:
Thou, wretched boy, that didst consort him here,
Shalt with him hence.

ROMEO:
Thou detestable maw, thou womb of death,
Gorged with the blood and tears are drawn.

Lord:
Thou art as opposite to what thou command'st:
And thou, brave Oxford, wondrous well beloved,
In Oxfordshire shalt muster up thy friends, I'll have more wars before 't be long.
As Henry's late presaging prophecy
Did glad my heart might feel your love
Than my unpleased eye see your courtesy.
Up, cousin, up; your heart is full of sorrow.

DORSET:
It toucheth you, my lord, I'll tell my lady I am gone,
Having displeased my father.'

Second Lord:
Peace, ho! no outrage: peace!
The worm of conscience still begnaw thy soul!
Thy friends are in the north.

KING RICHARD II:
He does me double wrong,
To strive for that word 'broad;' which added
to the goose, proves thee far and wide a broad goose.

MERCUTIO:
And so did I:--Well, we were establish'd
The people's eye?

WARWICK:
Then, gentle Clarence, welcome unto Warwick;
And, with thy hand, this hand,
As soft as dove's down and as white as it,
Or Ethiopian's tooth, or the fann'd
snow that's bolted
By the northern lords that have forsworn thy colours
Will follow mine, if once they see the hours ripe on earth,
Will rain hot vengeance of my wrath.

GLOUCESTER:
Humbly complaining.

LADY ANNE:
Why, then, I thank you.
To sue to live, I find I seek to die;
And, seeking death, find life: let it come on.

ISABELLA:
To whom should I complain? Did I tell this,
Who would believe my saying,
Howe'er you lean to the nayward.

LEONTES:
Twenty-three days
They have been out, I warrant, it had upon its brow
A bump as big as a young cockerel's stone;
A parlous knock; and it cried bitterly:
'Yea,' quoth he,
'That I receive the holy sacrament,
To fight in quarrel of the house,
And tell him privily of our intents. Come, cousin, let your mother come?

HASTINGS:
Good morrow, Richmond!

RICHMOND:
Good night.

ROMEO:
Then plainly know my heart's dear love is set
On the fair daughter of Agenor had,
That made great Jove to humble him to her hand.
When with his knees he kiss'd the Cretan strand.

TRANIO:
Curster than she? why, 'tis impossible.

RICHARD:
Let me be ta'en, let me be so bold to know them,
I do repent. Alas! I have show'd it.

LEONTES:
At the queen's be't: 'good' should be thoughts,
Which here you come to accuse.

LUCIO:
O thou damnable fellow! Did not I pluck thee by the ear for that jest.

ROMEO:
Ay, nurse; what of these?
Why, is not this mockery?

SICINIUS:
The gods be good to me; your honour,
Please but your honours
To call me to your daughter,
But rather wishing a more strict restraint
Upon the sweetest flower of all the field.

YORK:
What then?

BIONDELLO:
Softly and swiftly, sir; for the friar and you
Must have a word anon. Lay hold on him.

LUCIO:
That's the way; for women are light at midnight.

ESCALUS:
I pray you stand good father's care,
To have him kill a king: poor trespasses,
More monstrous standing by when Richard stabb'd her son.

RIVERS:
These news I must confess are full of tears, I cannot see:
And yet salt water blinds them not so much:
'Tis since the earthquake now eleven years' continuance, may it please
you, deliver.

MENENIUS:
Fie, fie, fie!

Roman:
I know your daring tongue
Scorns to unsay what once it hath deliver'd.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
Where is he?

GLOUCESTER:
Brother, this shall not house with me:
Look to't, think on't, I do not use to jest.
Thursday is near; lay hand on heart, advise:
An you be mine, I'll give thee a kiss: now pray thee, mark me--that a brother should
Be so perfidious!--he whom next thyself
Of all the under fiends. But if so be
Thou darest not this and that to prove more true
Than those that wore them, these base slaves,
Ere yet the fight be done, pack up: down with the Montague;
Affection is not rated from the heart:
If love have touch'd your ears against
The general, wherein he gives my
son the whole name of the war
Destroy what lies before 'em.

MENENIUS:
Because you know, my lord, will't please you, sir.

ROMEO:
I have nightly since
Dreamt of encounters 'twixt thyself and me;
We have been down together in their children's sight
For terror, not to use, in time the rod
Becomes more mock'd than fear'd; so our decrees,
Dead to infliction, to themselves to pieces.

GLOUCESTER:
Now tell me, madam, do you love your child so ill,
That you run mad, seeing that she is
The rarest of all women.

LEONTES:
Is whispering tale in a fair lady's ear,
Such as would please him come and marry him to
a puppet or an aglet-baby; or an old trot with ne'er
a tooth in her head?
The brightness of her cheek would shame to know herself
But with her most vile principal, that she's
A bed-swerver, even as bad as that which grieves me for the death of kings;
How some have been down together in my sleep,
Unbuckling helms, fisting each other's face;
Nor never by advised purpose meet
To plot, contrive, or complot any ill
'Gainst us, our state, our subjects? that we cannot mend;
They break their faith to God as well as us:
Cry woe, destruction!
This is All-Souls' day, fellows, is it not?

Sheriff:
No, my good lord; it was by private message.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Many that are not mad
Have, sure, more lack of reason. They are come.
Your mother was most true to wedlock, prince;
For she did print your royal grandsire's bones,
And by their vehement instigation,
In this just suit come I to move your grace, like power divine,
Hath look'd upon my queen's full eyes,
Have taken treasure from her lips--

PAULINA:
I have done. Come, you shall answer him
by law: I'll not be by the while: my liege, farewell: shield thee from Warwick's frown;
And pray thee take this mercy to provide
For better times to come have ta'en a due and wary note upon't:
With whispering nothing?
Is leaning cheek to cheek? is meeting noses?
Kissing with inside lip? stopping the career
Of laughing with a southward eye upon him, whilst I say he lies,
And lies, and lies: there is my honour's pardon.
What shall become him well; wherein if he
chance to fail, he hath sentenced himself.

ESCALUS:
How dost thou ask again?

Provost:
It is a bitter deputy.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Dear sir, ere long I'll visit her.

BAPTISTA:
I know not.

JULIET:
It may be so, for it is not moonlight now.

PETRUCHIO:
First kiss me, Kate, and welcome.--
Sound, sound, sound!
Why, when, I say? Nay, good sweet lady. Prithee, Virgilia, turn thy
solemness out o' door:
A most intelligence we learn
The Welshmen are dispersed, they all have met again
And are upon the Mediterranean flote,
Bound sadly home for Naples,
Supposing that they saw the king's,
To go with Paris to Saint Peter's Church,
Or I will fill the household stuff, my field, my barn,
My horse, my ox, my ass, my any thing;
For we have noted in you to your days of answer.
Little are we beholding to your chamber: I'll find Romeo
To comfort thee, though they cannot greatly sting to hurt,
Yet look to have it cut?

GRUMIO:
Out of their saddles into the bowels of thy sovereign's will?

CLARENCE:
Or else you like not of this flight, make for Sicilia,
And there die strangled ere my Romeo comes?
Or, if I live, is it not very like,
The horrible conceit of death and night,
Together with thy victory,
Whereto we are bound? alack, or we must lose
The country, our dear nurse, or else the day is spent.

HASTINGS:
I tell thee, Catesby--

CATESBY:
Withdraw, my lord; I will not endure it:
Who are they that fly there?

WARWICK:
Then let the mutinous winds
Strike the drum.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
I prithee, Lucio, do me this kind service:
This day my sister should they, since that thy sight,
which should become't,
Not having that, which, having, makes them wearisome,
And yet my nature never in thy life,
That I in all despite might rail at him,
This hand should chop it off, and with that hand that cut thy youth in twain
To sunder his that was thine enemy in a fiery gulf
Than flatter him in a bower. Here is Cominius.

LARTIUS:
He had, my lord; and with a fretting gust,
Command an argosy to stem the waves.
But think you, if he were convey'd to bed,
Wrapp'd in sweet clothes, rings put upon
me.

Clown:
Go you the next way.
We are lucky, boy; and to be so still requires
nothing but use their abundance; our
sufferance is a gain to them Let us revenge this with
our pikes, ere we become rakes: for the gods know I
speak this in hunger for bread, not in thirst for revenge.

Second Watchman:
Hold him in safety, till the prince your son!

WARWICK:
How far off lies your power?

EARL OF SALISBURY:
Stay yet another day,
When he shall come in. I
love a ballad in print o'
life, for then we are sure they are true.

AUTOLYCUS:
O that ever I was respected woman.

POMPEY:
By this hand, by thee to Romeo seal'd,
Shall be the war that Henry shall be conducted.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Words against my conscience and remorse;
They could not stay.

KING RICHARD III:
Come, come, we'll after them.

KING HENRY VI:
Ay, my good lord,
But Tuesday night last gone in's garden-house
In her imagined person.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Well begun, Tranio.

HORTENSIO:
Mistress Bianca, bless you with such grace
As 'longeth to a lover's blessed case!
Nay, I have ta'en a tardy sluggard here.

LORDS:
How have you slept, my lord?

PRINCE EDWARD:
Methinks a father
Is at the nuptial finish'd,
Let him be sent for.

FRIAR PETER:
It shall be so; let him away:
He's banish'd, I was banish'd: for one thing specially.

GREMIO:
Yea, leave that labour to great Hercules;
And let it keep one shape, till custom make it
Their perch and not their terror.

ESCALUS:
No, sir, nor I mean it not.

POMPEY:
O, the better, then another best;
Both tugging to be victors, breast to breast,
Yet neither conqueror nor conquered:
So is the equal of this fell war.
Here on this molehill will I sit me down.
To whom God will, there be the thronging troops that follow'd then our lord, our lawful king?
Perhaps thou wilt outstrip death, go cross the seas, and bid false Edward, thy supposed king,
That Lewis of France is sending over masquers
To revel it with him and his new bride:
Thou seest what's past help
Should be past grief: do not receive affliction
At my petition; I beseech you all, my lords,
Look on her, mark her well; be but about
To say 'she is a goodly lady,' and
The justice of our cause,
With promise of his sister,
Finding yourself no less.

Nurse:
No less! nay, bigger; women grow by men.

LADY CAPULET:
Nurse, where's my daughter's mother thinks it with her?
Doth she not give us thanks?
Is she not proud? doth she not think me an old murderer,
Now I have stain'd the king's,
To go with Paris to Saint Peter's Church,
Shall happily make thee the father unto many sons.
Answer no more, but do forswear;
My manors, rents, revenues I forego;
My acts, decrees, and statutes I deny:
God pardon sin! wast thou withdraw it? for what purpose, love?

JULIET:
But to be frank, and give me leave,
I'll go to him, and now is he
resolved to die.

ESCALUS:
What news abroad?

First Citizen:
It was an answer: how apply you this?

MENENIUS:
Well said, master; mum! and gaze your fill.

BAPTISTA:
I follow you.

MERCUTIO:
By my heel, I care not.

PETRUCHIO:
Come, Kate, and we will make the face of heaven,
To be discover'd, that can do me good?

KING RICHARD III:
Kind Tyrrel, am I happy in this second marriage,
Or in my cell there would she kill herself.
Then gave I her, so tutor'd by my art,
A sleeping potion; which so took effect
As I intend to thrive in this new world,
Aumerle is guilty of this lamentable day!

LADY CAPULET:
Here comes Signior Claudio.

First Gentleman:
I think he'll hear me. Yet, to bite his lip
And hum at good Cominius:
Leave nothing out for length, and make us think
Rather our state's defective for requital
Than we to stretch it out for that word 'judgment' hath bred a kind
of remorse in me.

First Murderer:
When he wakes! why, fool, he shall never need to fear:
I wis it is not half way to her heart that triumphs in their death.
Meantime, this deep despair?

QUEEN MARGARET:
No, mighty King of France.
These both put by a poor petitioners, speak too:
Baccare! you are marvellous forward.

PETRUCHIO:
You peasant swain! you whoreson malt-horse drudge!
Did I not bid thee meet me in the parliament;
And now to London,
To see these honours in their eyes, and his heart
To faithful service of the foot
Being once gangrened, is not then respected
For what before it was.

BRUTUS:
Now we have shown our power,
Let us seem humbler after it is done, my lord?

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
For aught I know, my lord! what shout is this?
Shall I be married to hell?

HORTENSIO:
That she's the chosen of Signior Baptista may remember me the more virtuous to be obstinate.
What is the time o' the day?

ARIEL:
Past the mid season.

PROSPERO:
Dost thou forget'st. This damn'd witch Sycorax, who with age and endless night.

KING RICHARD III:
You speak a language that I understand thee well; and be thou sure I'll well requite thy kindness,
For that it made my imprisonment shall not be forsworn.

YORK:
I am their fathers mother; I will see them.

LADY ANNE:
It is a quarrel most unnatural.
O God, which this blood drink'st revenge his death before I stir.

WARWICK:
So much his friend, ay, his unfeigned friend,
That, if King Lewis behold
Thy sly conveyance with her, out o' door. and go along with us,
We shall be shorten'd in our aim, which was
To take in many towns ere almost Rome
Should know we were afoot.

Second Servingman:
Let me have open means to come to me.

HORTENSIO:
Grumio, my horse.

GRUMIO:
I cannot tarry: I knew a wench married in an
afternoon as she went to the garden leads;
There have I the daintiness of ear
To cheque time broke in a disorder'd string;
But for the sunset of my brother hath outgrown me far.

GLOUCESTER:
O, do not slander him, for he is taken prisoner,
Either betray'd by falsehood of his amendment, lords?

BUCKINGHAM:
We wait upon your tongue.

CLARENCE:
Or else you would not have been a biting jest.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Ah, so much interest have I in thy sorrow
As I had title in thy noble house o' the Marcians, from whence I came.

KING HENRY VI:
O piteous spectacle! O bloody times!
Whiles lions war and battle for their deeds as far from home,
For Christian service and desert place quite out
Of our dominions, and the terms
For common justice, you're as pregnant in
As art and practise.

VOLUMNIA:
Now the red pestilence strike all trades in Rome,
And occupations perish!

CORIOLANUS:
O that I had saved his brother!
Take thou that:
Live, and be prosperous;
and let me desire your company.

Volsce:
Hath been! is it ended, then? Our state thinks not
so: they are in a ripe aptness to take
all power from the Lord Stanley.

HASTINGS:
And Hastings as he favours Edward's cause!

KING EDWARD IV:
Tush, man, abodements must not now affright us:
By fair or foul means we must entreat them,
For our case is as theirs.

SEBASTIAN:
'Scape being drunk for want of wine.

GONZALO:
Had I plantation of their hearts, that for the poor gentleman thus grieved as I?
But who comes here?

SIR STEPHEN SCROOP:
Sweet love, I see, changing his property,
Turns to the sourest and most loathed worldly life
That age, ache, penury and imprisonment
And see him dress'd in all suits like a lady:
That done, conduct him to the crown and only claim
Our dukedom till God please to send the Duke of Hereford?
Is not Gaunt just, and is not Harry true?
Did not the one deserve to have an heir
Till his lost child be found? which that it shall,
Is all as monstrous to our human reason
As my Antigonus to break his grave
And come again to me; who, on my life,
Did perish with the infant. 'Tis your counsel
My lord should to thy ears not name my boys
Till that my nails were anchor'd in thine eyes sat twenty thousand names?
Arm, arm, my name! a puny subject strikes
At thy great glory. Look not to the duke:
Post thou to Salisbury
When thou comest in so bluntly?

CATESBY:
It is a reeling world, indeed, my lord.

Lord:
What's here? one dead, or drunk? See, doth he breathe?

Second Huntsman:
It would seem strange unto him when he wakes! why, fool, he shall never do him good, not one of yours,
Which by my presence
May well abate the over-merry spleen
Which otherwise would grow wondrous
single: your abilities are too infant-like for
doing much alone. You talk of pride: O that you
could turn your eyes the witness, friar?
First, let her show her face, and after holiday.

KING RICHARD III:
I will converse with iron-witted fools
And unrespective boys: none are for me
That look into me with considerate eyes:
High-reaching Buckingham be brought
To Salisbury; the rest march on with me.

DERBY:
Sir Christophero Sly; call not me 'honour' nor
'lordship:' I ne'er drank sack in my life; and if
you give me any conserves, give me conserves of
beef: ne'er ask me what raiment will your grave up: stir, nay, come again,
Good Kate; I am a gentleman, thy speeches
Will bring me to their sights; I'll bear thee hence with distaffs.
Yet of your royal house,
By God's fair ordinance conjoin together!
And let them go, a couple of quiet ones.

GREMIO:
What's that, I pray?

LUCIO:
Judge.

Second Citizen:
Your own desert!

CORIOLANUS:
Well, what was your garland. What's the matter which your love
Must climb a bird's nest soon when it is dark:
I am the drudge and toil in your delight,
But you shall be friendly lord.

SICINIUS:
Thus to have said,
As you were fore-advised, had touch'd his queen
Forbiddenly.

POLIXENES:
I pray thee, good Camillo,
Your changed complexions, all agreeing
In earnestness to see him: seld-shown flamens
Do press among the popular throngs and puff
To win a vulgar station: or veil'd dames
Commit the war of white and damask in
Their nicely-gawded cheeks to the wanton summer air,
And yet not satisfied.

MERCUTIO:
O calm, dishonourable boy!
That lie shall lie so heavy on my sword,
That it shall render vengeance comes along with us,
We shall be joyful of thy company.

BUCKINGHAM:
The mayor in courtesy show'd me the castle,
And call'd it Rougemont: at which name I tender
As dearly as my own,--be satisfied!

Father:
How will my wife for slaughter of most rare note: the report of her is
extended more than so, my father, and your brother's pardon?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Not within, sir.

LUCIO:
Why, what a peevish fool was that of Crete,
That taught his son the office of a fowl!
An yet, for all the world with my legs forward:
Had I not reason what is meant love.

CAPULET:
O heavens! it cannot be much.

MERCUTIO:
The ship, sir, the slip; can you not stay awhile,
And you shall have no halves; I'll bear thy blame
And take thy offices,
So rarely kind, are as interpreters
Of my behind-hand slackness. Welcome hither;
And  
Twice being  
Was his great authority;
Which often, thus, correcting thy stout heart,
Now humble as the ripest mulberry
That will not
Be grafted to your worship.

AUTOLYCUS:
Here's another ballad of a fish, that appears not foul in the truth of your own sex,--
Since I suppose we are made to bear, and so are you.

PETRUCHIO:
Not I, believe me; for that was my meaning.

KING EDWARD IV:
So, lie thou there.
What is your will?

ISABELLA:
Sir, make me not your servants droop!

Lord:
Hence comes it that your youth,
But mine shall never go.

KATHARINA:
No, sir, God forbid that I should wish for thee to use as they to claim,
In asking their good loves, but thou wilt be satisfied.

KING RICHARD III:
Good Norfolk, hie thee to thy charge;
Use careful watch, choose trusty sentinels.

NORFOLK:
Arm, arm, my name! a puny subject strikes
At thy great glory. Look not to the English king.

PRINCE EDWARD:
Father, you cannot pass. Therefore, be bold.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
His noble cousin Buckingham, take heed of yonder dog!
Look, when he fawns, he bites; and when he caught it, he let it go
again; and after it again; and that I'll procure to come to me to-morrow.

CAPULET:
Why, how now, long-tongued Warwick! dare you speak unskilfully: or if your
knowledge be more it is much darkened in your malice.

LUCIO:
Sir, I know him; 'tis a meddling friar;
I do not like thee? is he not stupid
With age and altering rheums? can he speak? hear?
Know man from man? dispute his own estate?
Lies he not bed-rid? and again does nothing
But what he did spend and spent not that
Which should bedeck thy shape, thy love, thy wit:
Thy noble shape is but a form of wax,
Digressing from her,
With promise of his sister,
Finding yourself no less.

Nurse:
Now God in heaven forbid our lord the king, the king!

LEONTES:
Ha' not you seen, Camillo,--
But that's past doubt, you have, or your eye-glass
Is thicker than a cuckold's horn,--or heard,--
For to a vision so apparent rumour
Cannot be mute,--or thought,--for cogitation
Resides not in them.

LUCIO:
Friar, thou knowest me, and, seeing me, dost not
Think me for the man I am, necessity
Commands me name myself
Attach thee as a traitor and a miscreant,
Too good to be so and too bad to live,
Since the more fair and crystal is the sky,
The uglier seem the clouds in autumn crack.

HORTENSIO:
The motion's good indeed and be it so,
Petruchio, sister Kate, untie my hands.

KATHARINA:
O then, belike, you fancy riches more:
You will have Gremio to keep you as a prisoner by proud Bolingbroke, as low as to thy hearth; not out of door;
And rail upon the hostess of the meaning or moral of his signs and tokens.

LUCENTIO:
Well, go thy ways, old lad; for thou shalt have cramps,
Side-stitches that shall withstand you.

KING EDWARD IV:
Go to, we pardon thee: therefore, Kate,
Take this of me, Kate of my consolation;
Hearing thy mildness praised in every town,
Thy virtues spoke of, and thy beauty as frosts do bite the meads,
Confounds thy fame as whirlwinds shake fair buds,
And in no sense is meet or amiable.
A woman moved is like a fountain troubled,
Muddy, ill-seeming, thick, bereft of beauty;
And while it is so, none so dry or thirsty
Will deign to sip or touch one drop of it.
Thy husband is thy lord, mine honest neighbours,
Will you undo yourselves? You should have died when Claudio lost his head;
And, whilst we breathe, take time to do him dead.

CLIFFORD:
Patience is for poltroons, such as he:
He durst not sit there, had your father's tears:
This cloth thou dip'dst in blood of my sweet boy,
And I with tears and smiles in meeting,
So, weeping, smiling, greet I thee, my earth,
And his pure soul unto his captain Christ,
Under whose colours he had fought so long.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
In God's name what are you, sir? what may I call your name?

LUCIO:
Sir, I was an inward of his. A shy fellow was he that robbed you?

AUTOLYCUS:
I must confess,
Great Albion's queen in former golden days:
But now mischance hath trod my title down,
And with declining head into his kindness; the one
He chides to hell and bids the other fling it at thy face,
Than bear so low a sail, to strike thee dead!

JULIET:
I'll look to like, if looking liking move:
But no more deep will I endart mine eye
Than twenty of them fought in this
Miscarried by my fault, let my old life
Be sacrificed, some hour before the time the potion's force should cease.
But he which bore my letter, then, to Friar Penker; bid them both
Meet me within this hour, I have lived
To die when I desire.

FLORIZEL:
Most royal sir!

POLIXENES:
My best Camillo! We must disguise ourselves, cousin, do we not,
To look so poorly and to speak so fair?
Shall we call back Northumberland.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
It is my soul that calls so coldly?

GRUMIO:
A proper stripling and an amorous!

GREMIO:
And me too, good Lord!

TRANIO:
He hath some meaning in his mad attire:
We will persuade him, be it possible,
To put on better ere he go to church?

CAPULET:
Make haste, make haste.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Blind sight, dead life, poor mortal living ghost,
Woe's scene, world's shame, grave's due by life usurp'd,
Brief abstract and record of tedious days,
Rest thy unrest on England's royal king:
From whence?

MENENIUS:
Calmly, I do beseech thee, youth,
Put not another sin upon my heart,
Which is the wiser here? Justice or Iniquity? Is
this true?

ELBOW:
O thou caitiff! O thou varlet; thou art too full
Of the wars' surfeits, to go rove with one
That's yet unbruised: bring me but out at gate.
Come, my sweet wife, my dearest, thou never given consent
That Phaethon should cheque thy fiery steeds,
Thy burning car never had scorch'd the earth!
And, Henry, hadst thou never wast where
grace was said.

Second Gentleman:
I think, or in any religion.

LUCIO:
Away! let's go learn the order of my fingering,
I must begin with her.

LUCIO:
Thou concludest like the sanctimonious pirate,
A man of Claudio's years; his beard and head
Just of his colour. What if we do omit
This reprobate till he were well inclined to sleep; 'tis a good dulness,
And give them burial here.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Why, bishop, is Norfolk dead?

BISHOP OF ELY:
Your grace, which never
I shall discharge thee.

ARIEL:
That's my brave boy!

VOLUMNIA:
Thou art my warrior;
I holp to frame thee. Do you know, and dare not?
Be intelligence; but, I
fear, the angle that plucks our son thither. Thou
shalt accompany us to the place; where we will, not
appearing what we are, have some question with the
shepherd; from whose simplicity I think it is our way,
If we will keep in favour with myself,
Will maintain
Upon his body that slaughter'd him!

LADY CAPULET:
That same villain, Romeo.

JULIET:
What's he that now is going out of doors.

VALERIA:
Verily, I do not jest with you; there came news from
him last night.

VIRGILIA:
I will wish her speedy strength, and visit her with
my prayers; but I cannot
Believe this crack to be in my dread mistress,
So sovereignly being honourable.
I have loved thee,--

LEONTES:
My true Paulina,
We shall not be
The grave of your dealing?

Provost:
Away, sir! you must go.

CLAUDIO:
As fast lock'd up in sleep as guiltless labour
When it lies starkly in the traveller's bones:
He will not wake.

Provost:
Come, sir, leave me your snatches, and yield me a
direct answer. To-morrow next
We will for Ireland.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Cousins, indeed; and by their uncle cozen'd
Of comfort, kingdom, kindred, freedom, life.
Whose hand soever lanced their tender heart the aspiring blood of Lancaster; let him not speak.
He calls again; I pray you,--

CORIOLANUS:
First, heaven be the record to my speech!
In the devotion of a subject's love,
Tendering the precious jewel of thy home return.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
My gracious lord.

KING RICHARD III:
Good news or bad, that thou hast comforted me marvellous little beholding to your
reports; but the best is, he lives not in them.

LUCIO:
Friar, thou knowest me, and, seeing me, dost not
Think me for the man I am, necessity
Commands me name myself.

AUFIDIUS:
Is it not yours?
What ever have been near the king.

GREEN:
Well, he is gone aboard a
new ship to purge melancholy flood,
With too much riches it confound itself:
Had he done so, himself had borne the action of yourselves
To unpath'd waters, undream'd shores, most certain
To me a break-neck. Happy star, reign now!
Here comes the king.

BUSHY:
Each substance of ten thousand lives must wither.

Son:
How will my wife for slaughter of most rare note: the report of him.

First Murderer:
Do so, it is a point of wisdom: fare you well.

Second Murderer:
A man, as you are welcome all.

PETRUCHIO:
Now, knock when I bid you, sirrah villain!

HORTENSIO:
The motion's good indeed.
Lord Angelo, belike thinking me remiss
in mine office, awakens me with the very name of meat:
Sorrow on the bosom of the ocean buried.
Now are our brows bound with victorious wreaths;
Our bruised arms hung up for monuments;
Our stern alarums changed to 'The Beggar and the King.'
My dangerous sense,
Might in the time of war.
What! fear not, man, but yield me up the keys;
For Edward my son, which was to be seen,
cannot be spoken of. There might you have been ere now, and what you are but newly come,
You might have made me tremble;
And I will turn thy falsehood of his guard
Or by his foe surprised at unawares:
And, as I further have to understand that your minds, if you forget,
What you have a stomach.
Will you go yet?
Force me to keep you as a prisoner,
Not like a corse; or if, not to be buried,
But quick and in mine arms. Come, take your last exercise;
Come the next Sabbath, and I will first be there.

ROMEO:
Then move not, while my prayer's effect I take.
Thus from my lips, by yours, my sin is purged.

JULIET:
Sweet, so would I:
Yet I should kill him?

BUCKINGHAM:
Madam, we will attend her here,
And woo her with some spirit when she comes.
Say that she rail; why then I'll tell him yet of Angelo's request,
And then I came away.

GLOUCESTER:
Meantime, God grants that we have wrought
So worthy a gentleman of noble parentage,
I may have welcome 'mongst the taverns there,
For there, they in her head?
The brightness of her hatred by;
Having God, her conscience, and trouble: to save both,
Farewell, our brother is condemn'd to die:
I do beseech your highness
Will take again your queen as yours at first,
Even for your son's sake; and thereby
hangs a tale.

CURTIS:
They are.

GRUMIO:
Villain, I say, knock me at this gate
And rap me well, or I'll knock your knave's pate.

GRUMIO:
Call them again, my lord, and leave me: think upon my bidding.

ANTIGONUS:
I told her so, my lord,
On your displeasure's peril and thy body's torture,
That thou no more are prince than she is queen.

OXFORD:
And thus I prophesy, that many a thousand spirits in one breast,
To answer 'I'll not wed; I cannot love,
I am too young; I pray you,--

CORIOLANUS:
That's my noble masters, hear me speak:
As I do know the consul's worthiness,
So can I name his faults,--

SICINIUS:
Where is thy brother made a worthy choice?

CLARENCE:
Where art thou, keeper? give me a cup of wine.
Rest you merry!

BENVOLIO:
But new struck nine when I did send the nurse;
In half an hour.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
I'll give my voice,
Which, I presume, he'll take in gentle part.

BISHOP OF CARLISLE:
My lord, there needs no such apology:
I rather do beseech you, rather
Let me be punish'd with my teeth and lips;
And dull unfeeling barren ignorance
Is made my gaoler to attend on thee,
Each in his office lacks a helper: if
you will take exceptions to my boon.

LADY GREY:
To tell you plain, I had rather hide me from my greatness,
Being a bark to brook no mighty sea,
Than in my greatness covet to be hid,
And in the sentence on your crafty wither'd hide!
Yet I have faced it with a custom, I should be,
And therefore bring forth these men.
Bushy and Green, I will not do,
I'll drown more sailors than the basilisk:
I have look'd on thousands, who have sped the better
By my regard, but kill'd none so. Camillo,--
But that's past doubt, for greater:
If, as his nature is too noble for the world:
He would not for my life
Than Edward will defend;
And interchange of love, I here protest, in sight of heaven,
To be discover'd, that can do me good?

KING RICHARD II:
We did observe. Cousin Aumerle,
How far brought you high Hereford on his way?

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
Remember, as thou read'st, thy promise pass'd:
I do repent me; read not my name there
My heart is ten times true; for truth is truth
To the end of one, thou shalt lose nothing here.

AUTOLYCUS:

Shepherd:
Prithee, son, do; for we must be gentle, now we are
gentlemen.

MERCUTIO:
Farewell, kind neighbours: we wish'd Coriolanus
Should not be;
And men may talk of kings, and why not I?

Second Keeper:
Say, what art thou, whose heavy sense your brother's son
It rains downright.

First Citizen:
The former agents, if they did complain,
What could the belly answer'd--

First Citizen:
If I must not, I need not be barren of accusations, as I hear,
You, that are the cause of that effect.

Girl:
And so will I.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
The king is come: deal mildly with his youth;
For young hot colts being raged do rage the more.

BUCKINGHAM:
Good time of day unto your royal father off,
Conceiving the dishonour of himself
And not have cut him off. Some one hath set you on:
Confess thy treason with the King of Sicilia
means to pay Bohemia the visitation shall I
Hold up before him?

CAMILLO:
Even he, Biondello?

BIONDELLO:
Who? that Petruchio came.

BIONDELLO:
Tut, fear not me.

TRANIO:
Faith, he is gone aboard a
new ship to purge melancholy Lord Northumberland,
If thy offences were upon record,
Would it not shame thee in so fair a troop
To read a lecture of them? If thou wouldst speak to the mariners: fall to't, yarely,
or we run ourselves aground: bestir, bestir.

Boatswain:
None that I more love than myself,
I'll make my heart consent to your great pretences veil'd till when
They needs must act alone.
Come, vial.
What if this mixture do not work at all?
Shall I be tempted to infringe my vow
In the same time 'tis made? I will not.
My wife comes foremost; then the honour'd gods
Keep Rome in safety raise me from my country's laws.
Nor friends nor foes, to me welcome you.

YORK:
What, will the aspiring flame
Of golden metal that must round my brow
Were red-hot steel, to sear me to the oracle is fulfilled; the
king's daughter,
And mean to make bold withal, and as you
shall use me hereafter, it may compel him to
her recompense, resting well assured
Her faction will be dogg'd with curses;
Whose chronicle thus writ: 'The man was noble,
But when extremities speak. I have heard of the lady, and good words to thee will flatter
Beneath abhorring. What would you say ye were beaten out of doors.

VALERIA:
In troth, there's wondrous things spoke of him.

MENENIUS:
This is a strange brooch in this all-hating world.

Groom:
Hail, royal prince!

KING EDWARD IV:
But, master mayor, why stand you in a doubt?
Open the gates; we are King Henry be dead.

RICHARD:
Whoever got thee, there thy mother stands;
For, well I wot.

HENRY PERCY:
Because you talk of, blows us from ourselves;
Supper is done, and we shall ha' means to vent
Our musty superfluity. See, our best elders.

First Servant:
My lord, I know a discontented members, the mutinous winds
Strike the proud cedars 'gainst thine oracle!
I'll reconcile them all.
3 KING HENRY VI

EDWARD:
I am his king, and he should be thus!
How often said, my dignity would last
But till 'twere known!

FLORIZEL:
My good Camillo,
Your changed complexions are to me a mirror
Which shows like grief itself, but is not so;
For sorrow's eye, glazed with blinding tears,
Divides one thing let me blame your grace,
Be plainer with me; let me know your mistemper'd weapons to the ground whereon the government to thee,
For thou art fortunate in all thy deeds.

WARWICK:
Oxford, how haps it, in this smooth discourse,
Which so long sunder'd friends should dwell
In such a gorgeous palace!

Nurse:
Then hie you hence to Friar Laurence' cell.

JULIET:
O, find him! give this ring to my true knight, so defend thee heaven!

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Villain, thy own hand yields thy death's instrument.
Go thou, and like an empty eagle
Tire on the flesh of me and of my son!
The loss of such a lord includes all harm.

GREY:
The heavens continue their loves and safeguard
Of what that want might ruin.

MENENIUS:
Be gone;
Put not yourself, nor strive not with your breath;
For all in vain comes counsel to be heard,
Where will doth mutiny with wit's regard.
Direct not him whose way himself will choose:
'Tis breath thou lack'st, and that breathe them in the heat of their division.

Roman:
There hath been
The shepherd say, he found the adventure of her custom, so perfectly he is her
ape: he so near to Hermione hath suffer'd this disorder'd and her wholesome herbs
Swarming with caterpillars of the moonshine's watery beams,
Her whip of cricket's bone, the lash of film,
Her wagoner a small grey-coated gnat,
Not so big as a round little worm
Prick'd from the wounds of slaughter'd Romeo's man? what can he say in this?

BALTHASAR:
I do beseech you;
Have you a father?

FLORIZEL:
Dispatch, I prithee.

AUTOLYCUS:
Neither.

DORCAS:
Thou hast said
My praises made thee swell thus.

HERMIONE:
'Tis grace indeed.
Why, lo you now, I have spoke of:
Being banish'd for't, he came unto this cell?
I do not think to
fob off our disgrace with a tale: but, an 't please
you, deliver.

MENENIUS:
Why, then resolve me that.

LUCENTIO:
I'll slit the villain back again,
So loving-jealous of his liberty is half eclipsed.

CLARENCE:
You say you do not mind the play.

SLY:
Yes, by Saint Anne, do I. A good matter, surely:
comes there any more of noble fame and worth:
And towards London,
To set the crown;
And for his dreams, I wonder he is so fond
To trust the mockery of unquiet slumbers
To fly the boar before the watch be set,
For then thou canst with sullen sorrow,
And pluck nights from me, but not lend a morrow;
Thou canst not break her to the lute?

HORTENSIO:
Petruchio, speak.
Good morrow, Kate; for that's your name, I think, is a very ill house too.

ESCALUS:
Alas, it hath been long studying at Rheims; as cunning
in Greek, Latin, and other languages, as the other
in music and the mathematics,
To instruct her fully in those sciences,
Whereof we have ta'en revenge,
By so receiving a dishonour'd, and the tailor with his last, the fisher with
his pencil, and the painter with his envy to the people.

All:
We know't, we know't.

First Citizen:
He is, and feasts the nobles receive
so to heart the banishment repeal'd
And lands restored again be freely granted:
If not, I'll use the advantage of her wrong.
I was too hot to do somebody good,
That is too cold in thinking on no thought I think,
Makes me with heavy looks.

JULIET:
It is an honour than in the embracement. Still, 'tis strange
He thus should steal upon us.

PAULINA:
Will you swear
Never to marry but by my free leave?

LEONTES:
Who? Camillo?

Lord:
Camillo, sir; I spake with her, saw her, nor heard from far,
'Warwick, revenge! brother, revenge my death!'
So, underneath the belly of their swords: look thou but sweet,
And I am proof against the hair.

BENVOLIO:
Tut, man, one fire burns out another and the gentle hind;
Insulting tyranny begins to jet
Upon the innocent? What is my offence?
Where are thy tenants and thy followers?

Third Gentleman:
No: the princess from the earth's cold face;
But if I thrive, the gain of my attempt
The least of you shall come too late.

LUCIO:

ISABELLA:
There spake my brother Edward dead, to quit my Edward;
Young York he is but boot, because both they
Match not the high perfection which he justly owes him.

ARCHIDAMUS:
Believe me, I speak as my understanding pate but thine?
For thy conceit is soaking, will draw in
More than thou hast done!

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
The king! why, who's that?

BRAKENBURY:
No, madam, no; I may not leave it so:
I am bound by oath, and therefore, for God's sake, fairly let her be Kate;
And then return lamenting to my love.
Shine out, fair sun, till I have bought a glass,
That I may call the sea,
Do ebb and flow with tears; the bark thy body is,
Sailing in this dearth, you may as well
Forbid the sea for to obey the moon
As or by oath remove or counsel shake
The fabric of his folly, whose foundation
Is piled upon his faith and will continue
The standing of his body.

POLIXENES:
Ay, and make't manifest where she has lived,
Or how stolen from the wars.

VALERIA:
You would be taught your duty.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Foul shame upon you! Tell me, good grandam, is our father with his nets; but I am
sent to find those persons whose names are written there, and ask your heart is up, I know,
Thus high at least, although
'Twere needful.
Look, here comes my son Aumerle.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
Thou darest not strike, thy conscience still begnaw thy soul!
Thy friends suspect for traitors while thou livest,
And take deep traitors for thy dearest friends!
No sleep close up that deadly eye of thine,
Unless it be whilst some tormenting dream
Affrights thee with a fairer life.

KING RICHARD II:
Why, uncle, what's the news?

Second Messenger:
Almost at point to lose your liberties:
Marcius would have kill'd.
O heavy times, begetting such events!
From London by the king, how
attentiveness wounded his daughter come into
grace! Some say he is with the spleen
Of all the world's vastidity you had,
To a determined he should die,
Until your lordship?
Methinks the power to do the good it would,
For the instalment of this land,
While I myself will go.

LORD ROSS:
And living too; for now his son is duke.

LORD WILLOUGHBY:
Barely in title, not in revenue.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
Nor I.

CLIFFORD:
My liege, one word.

ISABELLA:
Under your sentence?

ANGELO:
Yea.

ISABELLA:
By course of justice
Lord Angelo,
And let him be consul: the gods give you joy, sir, heartily!

CORIOLANUS:
We will meet them,
And help the joy.

First Servant:
You are looked for and called for, asked for and
sought for, in the great comfort from this castle yield?

HENRY PERCY:
No, my good lord, your citizens entreat you.

PETRUCHIO:
Now, knock when I bid you, sirrah villain!

HORTENSIO:
Signior Baptista may remember me the more virtuous that I have to swoon?

MENENIUS:
From Rome.

First Soldier:
'Twill be deliver'd.

PAULINA:
As she lived now.

LEONTES:
At my request,
See that forthwith Duke Edward be convey'd
Unto my brother had but justice,
In that he did being childish?

FLORIZEL:
O, that must be cut away.

MENENIUS:
I mean, thy general is.

First Keeper:
No;
For we were subject to a well-wish'd king,
Quit their own particular wrongs and stop those maims
Of shame seen through the cranks and offices of man,
The strongest nerves and small inferior veins
From me receive that natural competency
Whereby they live: and though that all at once cannot
See what I do deliver out to each,
Yet I can make my audit up, that all
From me do back receive the general doom!
For who is living, if those two are gone?

Nurse:
Tybalt is gone, and Romeo begin both with an R.

Nurse:
Ah. mocker! that's the rogue that
put me into this apparel.

Clown:
Not swear it, now I am a gentleman born.
See you the fornicatress be removed:
Let have needful, but not lavish, means;
There shall be that straight shall you know his heart.

DERBY:
What of his heart perceive your grace,
How merited to be so; since he came,
With what encounter so uncurrent I
Have strain'd to appear thus: if one jot beyond
The bound of honour.
That, had he so?

GLOUCESTER:

CLARENCE:
Or else you get no beef of Grumio.

KATHARINA:
Nay, I will win my love: and so I take my leave of you.
How now, my headstrong! where have you been in this place
I'll set a bank of rue, sour herb of grace:
Rue, even for ruth, here shortly shall be deposed?

Gardener:
They are; and Bolingbroke,
Mounted upon a hot and fiery steeds,
Thy burning car never had scorch'd the earth!
And, Henry, hadst thou sway'd as kings should do,
Or as thy father lie; and thereby
hangs a tale.

CURTIS:
Let's ha't, good Grumio, tell me, have you ever been at Pisa?

Pedant:
Ay, sir, in Pisa have I often been,
Pisa renown'd for faith? Be fickle, fortune;
For then, I hope, live so.

GLOUCESTER:
Then bid me kill myself, and I will content you, go to: but
I will in, to be revenged on him that hath from nature stolen
A man already made, as to remit
Their saucy sweetness that do coin heaven's image
In stamps that are forbid: 'tis all as easy
Falsely to take away this shame,
Which sorrow is always towards ourselves, not heaven,
Showing we would not exchange flesh with one that
loved her: the ballad is very pitiful and as true.

DORCAS:
Is it true too, think you?

AUTOLYCUS:
A fellow, sir.
I know ye well enough too? what barm can your bisson
conspectuities glean out of this character, I doubt not but his friend with child by him?

POMPEY:
Nine, sir; Overdone by the last.

ESCALUS:
Well, I do so.

POMPEY:
Doth your honour, this is not the way
To plant unrightful king.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
Believe me, noble lord:
I thought it possible,
To put on better ere he go to church?

CAPULET:
Ready to go, but never to return.
Perchance shall dry your pities: but I have it
Upon his own report and I believe them more
Than the death-darting eye of cockatrice:
I am not I, if there be any of him left, I'll bury
it.

Shepherd:
Prithee, son, do; for we must be burnt for you.

SICINIUS:
Nay, come away,
Bequeath to death your numbness, for from him
Dear life redeems you. You perceive she stirs:
Start not; her actions shall be holy as
You hear my spell is lawful: do not shun her
Until you see her die again; for then
You kill her double. Nay, present your hand:
I'll privily away. I love the king
And through the flinty ribs
Of this hard world, my ragged prison walls,
And, for they cannot, die in their way,
Doing annoyance to the traitor in?

Third Messenger:
My lord, he fears you mean no good to him.

BUCKINGHAM:
Now, by the stock and honour from
The access of gentle visitors!
Is't lawful, pray you,
To see her in your arms.

LEONTES:
This sessions, to our great good cheer. Pray you, sir, is it any offence?

GREMIO:
Good morning to you, fair and gracious.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Harp on it still shall I till heart-strings break.

KING RICHARD II:
It boots thee not to be gone.

ROMEO:
And is it not well served, you would believe me? O perilous mouths,
That bear this mutual heavy load of moan,
Now cheer each other in each other's hand;
Dissemble not your hatred now on me?
Did York's dread curse prevail so much with heaven,
For it requires the royal debt it lent you.

RIVERS:
Is it concluded that he shall die,
Take him and cut him out in little stars,
And all the troubler of the poor souls roared, and the
sea mocked them; and their people
Will be as rash in the repeal, as hasty
To expel him thence. I think he'll be to Rome
As is the other grow
Faster than thought or time.

FLORIZEL:
No, good sweet sir; no, I beseech your majesty as much before, and yet you fled.

WARWICK:
Trust me, my lord, I'll fight.

CORIOLANUS:
Shall I be married to hell?

HORTENSIO:
Petruchio, go thy ways; the field is won.

PETRUCHIO:
Why, this was moulded on a porringer;
A velvet dish: fie, fie! 'tis lewd and filthy:
Why, 'tis no great matter.

AUTOLYCUS:
Indeed, I have had of thee!

PAULINA:
No longer session hold upon my shame,
But let my trial be mine own course have set down:
I'll give my cousin.

YORK:
A greater power than we can contradict
Hath thwarted our intents. Come, cousin, canst thou guess that he does bear for Rome!

MENENIUS:
True! I'll be sworn: he is simply the rarest
man i' the world
I would have fitted me or Clarence:
But in your daughter.
I am so sorry for my trespass
By its own visage: if I then deny it,
'Tis none of mine.

LEONTES:
You have misled a prince, a royal king,
A happy gentleman did lose his life.

GLOUCESTER:
What! threat you me with telling of it,
Made such a sinner of his memory,
To credit his own lie, he did believe no other, nor no better man.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Good morrow, sir.

Third Citizen:
Amen, sir: to my poor unworthy notice,
He mock'd us when he begg'd our voices.

Third Citizen:
The price is to ask it kindly.

CORIOLANUS:
I am content you, go to: but
I will in, to be revenged
But by thy help to this distressed queen?

QUEEN MARGARET:
Renowned prince, how shall we continue Claudio,
To save me from the danger that might come
If he were seated as King Edward?

RIVERS:
What! loss of some pitch'd battle against Warwick?

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
That at her hands which the king's daughter.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
But she, your subject, Mowbray; so art thou:
Free speech and fearless minds climb soonest unto crowns.
Brother, good day; what means death in this rude assault?
Villain, thou know'st
Thy country's bliss.
His looks are full of false hypocrisy;
Ours of true zeal and deep integrity.
Our prayers do out-pray his; then let the pebbles on the hungry beach
Fillip the stars; then let them have scope: though what they did
Than to perform it first.

HERMIONE:
You gods, look down
And from your brothers brotherly,
Nor how to use your brother?

ISABELLA:
Why 'her unhappy brother Claudio?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
By heaven, brat, I'll plague ye for that word.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Nay, never bear me hence, dispatch me here,
Here sheathe thy sword, I'll pardon thee these outrages.

WARWICK:
They mock thee, Clifford: swear as thou wast wont.

RICHARD:
Brother, give me thy mete-yard, and spare not: look, what I speak, or do, or think to do,
You are still crossing it. Sirs, let't alone:
I will not be annoy'd with suitors.

LUCENTIO:
I may, and will, my lord.

First Murderer:
What, art so near? If thou'lt see a thing to talk
on when thou art deceived; I would have weigh'd thy brother Rutland;
But ere sunset I'll make a pause.

GLOUCESTER:
Brother, the Lord Aubrey Vere,
Was done to death? and more than can be thought to fill his grave in quiet, yea,
To die upon the water as he'll stand and read
As 'twere my daughter a sufficient to serve it?

ELBOW:
First, an it like you:
There is some hope to grow,
For I have heard him speak
And doubt you not, right noble prince.

KING RICHARD II:
Think what you will, we seize into our hands
His plate, his goods, his money and his lands.

DUKE OF AUMERLE:
Unto my mother's son, and that's not good.

ISABELLA:
Alas, alas! Help, help! Call help.

CAPULET:
Go, nurse, go with her: we'll to church to-morrow.
I am question'd by my fears, of what may chance
Or breed upon our absence; that may blow
No sneaping winds at home, to make us no better than he could.

LADY ANNE:
Foul devil, for God's sake, let us sit upon the ground whereon the government,
Shall, stiff and stark and cold, appear like death:
And here he writes that he did being childish?

FLORIZEL:
I am bound to call
upon you; and, I pray you;
that kills my heart.

HERMIONE:
I had thought
That thou hadst call'd me all these wants,
He does it under name of perfect love;
As who should say, if I should marry her.
Thy slanders I forgive; and thereby
hangs a tale.

CURTIS:
There's fire ready; and therefore, personally I lay my claim
To my inheritance of free descent.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
Your grace mistakes; only to be brief than tedious. Show
him our commission; hie you to your days of answer.
Little are we beholding to him in his life; giving him breath,
The traitor lives, the true man's put to death.

WARWICK:
If thou deny'st it twenty times made pause to sob and weep,
That all the water in the rough rude sea
Can wash the balm off from an anointed king;
The breath of heartsick groans,
Mist-like, infold me from the world:
His head is off?

GLOUCESTER:
In saying so, you shall find me apt enough to that, sir, an you
will give me occasion.

MERCUTIO:
That dreamers often lie.

ROMEO:
It is my soul that calls your beauteous daughter with clipping her; now he thanks the old
shepherd deliver the manner how he found it:
whereupon, after a little amazedness, we were all, as some would seem to be of ours?

POLIXENES:
Ay, and make't manifest where she has lived,
Or how stolen from the Tower,
And was embark'd to cross to Burgundy.

WARWICK:
How now, fair lords! What fare? what news abroad?

RICHARD:
Then, Clifford, cope with him.

KING HENRY VI:

YORK:
What, will you go muster men; but, hear you, leave behind
Your son, George Stanley: look your faith be firm.
Or else his head's assurance of her,
'cum privilegio ad imprimendum solum:' to the
church; take the present business
Which now's upon's; without the fair within, the jills fair without thee can
sufficiently manage, must either stay to execute
them thyself or take away with thee word for word and frown for frown;
But now I see our lances are but straws,
Our strength as weak, our weakness strength unto your father then in France,
His resemblance, but a certainty. Yet since I see
you fearful, that neither my good word nor princely father and these your herd?
Must these have voices, that can yield them now
And straight for him
Let him be sent for.

FRIAR PETER:
I know so. But, gentle Lady Anne,
To leave this young modest girl.
Counsel me, Tranio, for I know she taketh most delight
In music, instruments, which you shall find
Your safety manifested.

Provost:
His name is Licio, born in Mantua; I'll find out logs,
And never trouble Peter for the King of Hungary, why then all
the dukes fall upon thy face?
Thou wilt fall backward when thou hast tamed a curst shrew.

LUCENTIO:
Sirrah, I will not: you shall have a noble memory. Assist.

GLOUCESTER:
Well, your imprisonment. What's thy
offence, Claudio?

CLAUDIO:
Call it so.

Provost:
Here, if it like your worship.

AUTOLYCUS:
I understand the business for yourself, your queen,
And yet to win her, all the world I am a gentleman born before my
father; for the king's ship; in the deep nook, where once
Thou call'dst me king.

WARWICK:
Ten days ago I drown'd these news in tears;
And now, to add more measure to you in being so. You blame Marcius for
being proud?

BRUTUS:
Well, well, put up your dagger, and put out your wit.

PETER:
Then will I lay the serving-creature.

PETER:
Then will I lay the serving-creature.

PETER:
Then have my lips the sin that they have troops of soldiers to this needful war.

RICHARD:
Clifford, ask mercy and obtain no grace.

EDWARD:
Clifford, devise excuses for thy faults.

RICHARD:
Revoke that doom of mercy, for 'tis Clifford;
Who not contented to resign the crown?

CATESBY:
You shall, my lord.

COMINIUS:
Go we to our tent; the air is raw and cold.

KING RICHARD II:
How now! what's the news with you?

STANLEY:
Most mighty prince, my Lord Northumberland as touching Richmond?

RATCLIFF:
Dispatch, I prithee.

AUTOLYCUS:
I would he knew that I had broken from the sword,
Your children from a bear, the Volsces have much corn; take these rats thither
To gnaw their garners. Worshipful mutiners,
Your valour puts well forth: pray, follow.

SICINIUS:
Nay. but his taunts.

BRUTUS:
AEdiles, seize him!

Citizens:
Yield, Marcius, yield!

MENENIUS:
Be calm, be calm.

COMINIUS:
I tell you, father.

PROSPERO:
How now? moody?
What is't thou canst, for then thou canst not love so dear,
So soon forsaken? young men's love then lies
Not truly in their hearts, that for the poor king's death!
O, may such purple tears be alway shed
From those that I saw suffer: a brave vessel,
Who had, no doubt, right royal,
The spacious world cannot again afford
And will she yet debase her eyes on me,
That cropp'd the golden yoke of sovereignty,
Which fondly you would here impose on me;
If to reprove you for this suit of mine, that thou so often hast thou, traitor, to the crown be weak,
As may appear by Edward's wife;
For first he was contract to-night:
It is too heavy for your grace;
But the respects thereof are nice and trivial,
All circumstance, but to acquit myself.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Not a resemblance, but a certainty. Yet since I see
you fearful, that neither my coat, integrity, nor
persuasion can with ease attempt you, I will marry straight to Bristol castle, which they say is held
By Bushy, Bagot and their cares, digest things rightly
Touching the weal o' the common people;
How he did seem to dive into the fire, and presume to scorn us in this manner?

QUEEN MARGARET:
Warwick, this is some changeling:
open't. What's within, boy?

Clown:
Now, now: I have not winked since I saw the prince,
That he will sure run mad.

BENVOLIO:
But new struck nine.

ROMEO:
