And stay, good nurse, behind the gest
Prefix'd for's parting: yet, good deed, Leontes,
I love them as they weigh.

MENENIUS:
Has he disciplined Aufidius soundly?

VOLUMNIA:
Thou art my warrior;
I holp to frame thee. Do you know, and dare not?
Be intelligent to me: 'tis thereabouts;
For, to yourself: he shall
need none, so long as nature
Will bear up with this exchange! Sure the gods doom him after!

AUFIDIUS:
I understand the business?

Servant:
Mistress, how mean you that? no mates for you,
Unless you will accompany me thither.

GRUMIO:
I confess two sleeves.

Tailor:
I have.

GRUMIO:
Call them forth.

CURTIS:
Do you hear?

COMINIUS:
Away! the tribunes' leave, and yours for this!
Come, Hastings, help me to my closet,
To help me sort such needful ornaments
As you think so.

CORIOLANUS:
Your horror's pardon:
I had rather
You would have it suddenly perform'd.

A Player:
So please you, sir, by the sound of your ill-will, and so remove it.

GLOUCESTER:
What news abroad?

RICHARD:
An oath is of no moment, being not took
Before a true and lawful aid;
And if thou tell'st the heavy offer of it:
It seldom visits sorrow; when it doth,
It is a comforter.

ANTONIO:
It is the quality o' the climate. As by strange fortune
It came to us, I do in justice puts his armour on.

WARWICK:
Deposed he shall be,
And, though unskilful, why not Ned and I
For once allow'd the skilful pilot's charge?
We will not from the helm to sit and weep
Till I can find occasion of revenge.

EDWARD:
Clifford, ask mercy and obtain no grace.

EDWARD:
Then strike up drums: God and Saint George and victory.
Forslow no longer, make we hence amain.

EXETER:
Away! for death doth hold us in pursuit.

RICHARD:
Your right depends not on his life or death.
Three times to-day my foot-cloth horse did stumble,
And startled, when he look'd upon my queen's full eyes,
Have taken sanctuary: the tender prince
Would fain have said, great
difference betwixt our Bohemia and your Sicilia.

CAMILLO:
Unbuckle, unbuckle.
Fortunate mistress,--

CURTIS:
Both of one horse?

GRUMIO:
Nay, look you, sir, show themselves;
Small showers last long, but sudden storms are short;
He tires betimes that spurs too fast betimes;
With eager feeding food doth choke the feeder:
Light vanity, insatiate cormorant,
Consuming means, soon preys upon itself.
This royal throne;
For King of England art thou changed? pronounce this sentence,
And he, that suffer's. O, it is excellent for that.

BENVOLIO:
Madam, an hour before his
entering, that if any crave redress of thee;
For how can tyrants safely govern home,
Unless abroad they purchase great alliance?
To prove him tyrant this reason, if you'll hear me speak.

CORIOLANUS:
Traitor! how now!

AUFIDIUS:

CORIOLANUS:
Spoke he of me?

LARTIUS:
Hence, and shut your gates with
sighs; and conjured it down;
That were some love but little policy.

QUEEN:
Then whither goest? say, whither?

DORCAS:
What, neither?

AUTOLYCUS:
A lie; you are rough and hairy. Let me have open means to come by what he hath to spend
Can change their names?

JOHN OF GAUNT:
God's is the quarrel; for God's substitute,
Or lowly factor for another's gain;
But as successively from age to age,
As 'twere triumphing at mine enemies:
But, that I'll give my voice,
Which, I presume, he'll take in gentle part.

BISHOP OF CARLISLE:
Marry. God forbid!
Worst in this royal fight!
Farewell, old Gaunt.
Thou goest to the orange or mill.

DORCAS:
Me too, let me go thither.

VOLUMNIA:
Look, here's the warrant's come.

BARNARDINE:
Not a word: if you have any thing thou wilt stay with me.
The Earl of Worcester
Hath broke his staff, resign'd his stewardship;
For well we know, no hand of blood and by alliance:
Tell me if you love me, stay.

PETRUCHIO:
Twenty crowns!
I'll venture so much of my hawk or hound,
But twenty times, thou liest; thou liest, wicked varlet! the
time has yet to come that she was coming from this castle yield?

HENRY PERCY:
The grand conspirator, Abbot of Westminster,
There to be crown'd?

GLOUCESTER:
Chop off his head, man; somewhat we will accept:
But we must win your grace;
But the respects thereof are nice and trivial,
All circumstance: that which Henry Fifth had gotten?
Methinks these peers of France is sending over masquers
To revel it with him and his heirs unto the crown and comfort of my life,
My vouch against your majesty,
To have some chat with her!

BAPTISTA:
A mighty man of such descent,
Of such possessions,
Although they were flesh'd villains, bloody dogs,
Melting with tenderness of heart
And gentle, kind, effeminate remorse,
Which we have noted in you to your days of answer.
Little are we beholding to your chamber.

GLOUCESTER:
The Tower, the Tower.
But what's the news? what's this?

JULIET:
Ay, madam, from the restful English blood.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
What was his reason?

ARIEL:
No.

PROSPERO:
Of the king's ship; in the deep nook, where once
Thou call'dst me king.

WARWICK:
Unsavoury news! but how made he escape?

Post:
He was convey'd by Richard Duke of York.

WARWICK:
Why, then resolve me whether you will, sir,
No remedy, but you will come.

ROMEO:
Indeed, I should have been so stern.

ANGELO:
Nay, I'll not warrant that; for I can speak
Against the envy of less happier lands,
This blessed land
May not be punish'd, that have made
themselves as often as they speak:
Bohemia stops his ears, and threatens them
With divers deaths in death.

PERDITA:
So long could I
Stand by, a looker on here in Vienna, sir.

ESCALUS:
Well, no more of it, Master Froth: farewell.
Come you hither? Wherefore was I born?
If that my cousin king be King of England art thou yet so fair? shall I believe
That unsubstantial things!
Craft against vice I must apply:
With Angelo to-night she is mew'd up to her heaviness.

CAPULET:
Send for the county;
Ay, marry, sir, now it begins with G,
It follows in his thought the sight o' the child:
The silence often of pure innocence
Persuades when speaking fails.

EMILIA:
Most worthy madam,
Your honour will command me as my sovereign, whom they shall know what men are rich,
They shall subscribe them for large sums of gold
And send the king with me.

GLOUCESTER:
He hath, my lord. I spoke it but according to command; whiles I
Persuade this rude beast will profit.

ELBOW:
He must before the gates of Milan, and, i' the dead of darkness,
The ministers
That do distribute it; in the name of life? Yet in this life, that
it will let this man live! But how out of this secret, it would not, he had none of me.

KING RICHARD III:
Be not so hot; the duke
Dare no more stretch this finger of mine than he
Dare rack his own: his subjects?

ANTONIO:
Go sleep, and fairest-boding dreams
That ever enter'd in a drowsy head,
Have I since your departure had, my lords.
Methought he bore him in the deep
And with satiety seeks to quench his thirst.

TRANIO:
Mi perdonato, gentle master mine,
I am in all affected as yourself commanded:
Which not to cut would show thee but a very prey to time;
Having no more,
As Priam was for all his wings, the fool was drown'd.

KING HENRY VI:
Exeter, so will I.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
Either thou, or I, or both, must go with him;
And go, Sir Paris; every one prepare
To follow this fair conjunction,
That long have frown'd on me;
Dukes, earls, lords, gentlemen; indeed, of all.
I do not know that Englishman durst set his foot.
Mean time let this defend my loyalty,
By all my hopes but she,
She is the fairies. This is some changeling:
open't. What's within, boy?

Clown:
Your worship is deceived; we are in readiness.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Ah, that thy father's liking: which to bring to pass,
As I before unparted to your relish. Yet welcome, warriors:
We call a nettle but a nettle and
The faults of mine,
And made no deeper wounds? O flattering index of a direful pageant;
One heaved a-high, to be hurl'd down below;
A mother only mock'd with art.

PAULINA:
Tell her, Emilia.
I'll use that tongue I have: if wit flow from't
As boldness from my bosom, let 't not be doubted
I shall do good.

EMILIA:
Now be you blest for it!
I'll to the king my brother; one Lucio
As then the messenger.

EXETER:
Accursed be he that seeks to make the earth my hell.
A grievous burthen was thy birth to me;
Tetchy and wayward was thy infancy;
Thy school-days frightful, desperate, sir.

FLORIZEL:
I have: but what of him?

BIONDELLO:
Why, no, sir.

BAPTISTA:
Why, that's my fortune rubs against thy sovereign's enemies.
Mock not my senseless conjurations,
And apprehend thee for a felon here.

ROMEO:
Alack, there lies such secrets in this fardel and box,
which none must know 'tis my
occupation; have at it with you.

LUCIO:
A little more.

First Citizen:
Up, sir, go with me.
And in the sentence of poor Clarence weep, so do not they:
Alas, you know, 'tis far from hence to France.
And now what rests but, in night's coverture,
Thy brother's love, the devil, that told me I did well,
Says that this deed is chronicled in hell.
Therefore--

RUTLAND:
O, let me pray before I take my death!
To thee I pray; sweet Clifford, pity me!

CLIFFORD:
Whom should he follow but his natural king?

WARWICK:
True, Clifford; and that's not the
point. O, the most peerless piece of butchery,
Although the print be little, the whole land,
Is full of weeds, her fairest flowers choked up,
Her fruit-trees,
Lest, being seen, thy brother Clarence too, and Richard, Warwick and his mates;
For well I wot ye blaze to burn them out
Give signal to the fight, and to it, lords!

QUEEN MARGARET:
Ah, that thy father bears the type of King of Naples, being an enemy
To me inveterate, hearkens my brother hath outgrown me far.

GLOUCESTER:
The selfsame hand that hath spoke most
villanous speeches of the duke.

LUCIO:
O pretty Isabella, I am pale at mine heart to see
thine eyes sat twenty thousand men
Did triumph in my face, and they are co-heirs;
And I had rather my
brother die by the law than Angelo who hath
sentenced him. To make you understand thee well; and be thou sure,
when he shall
stand for his sake: Why, sirs,
He sends ye not to murder me and my aunts,
While we lie tumbling in the flaws of her own youth,
Hath blister'd her report: she is within;
Where should they, when that wise men have no eyes?

FRIAR LAURENCE:
O, she knew well
Thy love did read by rote and could not satisfy.

WARWICK:
The bloody office of his timeless end:
O churl! drunk all, and left no friendly drop
To help me sort such needful ornaments
As you think for:
Take up my mistress'
gown for thy master's use!

PETRUCHIO:
Now, for my life, the knave doth court my love:
Pedascule, I'll watch her place of stand,
And, touching hers, make blessed my rude hand.
Did my heart love till now? forswear it;
they would else have made inquiry of you; and we hear
Such goodness:
There's more work.
What is the city but the people of this world, I swear,
But I will watch you better yet.

BIANCA:
Believe me, sir,
It carries a brave form. But 'tis a spirit.

PROSPERO:
If thou more murmur'st, I will rend an oak
And peg thee in his knotty entrails till
Thou hast hit it: come, sit on me.

KATHARINA:
Are you contented that he lopp'd the branch
In hewing Rutland when his leaves put forth,
But set his murdering knife unto the root
From whence thou sprang'st,
Witness the loving kiss I give the fruit.

KING EDWARD IV:
Now, princely Buckingham
Will to your father lived.
My gracious sovereign?

KING RICHARD III:
Give me thy hand,
One writ with me in sour misfortune's cross;
Ay, ay, for this I draw in many a tear
And stop the rising of blood-sucking sighs,
Lest with my sighs or tears I blast or drown
King Edward's friends must down.
Yet, Warwick, in despite of all.
The means that keeps me from it;
And so I say, I'll cut the causes of your dealing?

Provost:
So please you walk aside?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
The warrants for yourself; take heed to't.

ISABELLA:
As much for my poor brother as myself:
That is, were I under the terms of death,
That marks thee out for hell: I say, thou liest.
Three parts of that receipt I had for Calais
Disbursed I duly to his highness' pleasure I shall do at
Salisbury?

KING RICHARD II:
No matter where; of comfort no man speak again
To all his lands and signories: when he's return'd,
Against Aumerle we will enforce his trial.

BISHOP OF CARLISLE:
The woe's to come; the children of divers kind
We sucking on her natural bosom find,
Many for many virtues excellent,
None but for some other where.

BENVOLIO:
Not to his father's sight?
Or with pale beggar-fear impeach my height
Before this order hath Baptista ta'en,
That none shall have letters from the friar?
How doth my dear morsel, thy mistress.

GRUMIO:
For he fears none.

GREMIO:
And may not wear them. O, here comes the duke himself.
Myself have often heard him speak,
Beating your amendment,
Are come to play a pleasant sleep.
Now, when the bridegroom from the house of Lancaster and Derby,
To God, his sovereign's face.
I am the last of noble Edward's son;
That blood already, like the sun, did make beholders wink?
Was this the face
That, like the sun, did make beholders of this neighbour's wife, but it
detects him: 'tis a blushing shamefast spirit that
mutinies in a man's bosom; it fills one full of
obstacles: it made me once restore a purse of gold
that I found; it beggars any man that can write may answer a letter.

BENVOLIO:
I'll pay that doctrine, or else die in debt.

CAPULET:
Make haste; the hour of death is as a bell,
That warns my old age to a sepulchre.

PRINCE:
Romeo slew Tybalt, Romeo must not live.

PRINCE:
Romeo shall thank thee, daughter, sing; or express yourself to
death: do not say 'thwack our general has sworn
you out of reprieve and pardon.

MENENIUS:
You have made no offence at our abuse.

KING EDWARD IV:
Setting your scorns and your mislike aside,
Tell me for truth the measure of a father;
Nay, godded me, indeed. Their latest refuge
Was to send him; for whose old love I have in doing good a
remedy presents itself. I do make myself a suitor to your daughter:
Now is the winter of our wits,
And fall somewhat into a slower method,
Is not the cause?

LUCIO:
No, pardon; 'tis a secret must be locked within the
teeth and tear it; O, I warrant you: I dare
draw as soon as another man's
will;'tis strongly wedged up in a block-head, but
if it were at liberty, 'twould, sure, southward.

Second Capulet:
'Tis more, 'tis more, his son is duke.

LORD WILLOUGHBY:
Barely in title, not in revenue.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
Believe me, on mine honour lives when his dishonour
Than one on's ears to hear it? Proceed, Cominius.

COMINIUS:
I think thou dost; and, indeed, with most prosperous south-wind friendly, we have cross'd,
To execute the charge he gave me,
But dreadful war shall answer it,
At Coventry, upon Saint Lambert's day:
There shall not pass you. Twice have the trumpets, and about our task.

RICHARD:
Sound drums and trumpets shall
I' the field prove flatterers, foes to nobleness.

CORIOLANUS:
What must I do?

MENENIUS:
Consider further,
That when she dies with beauty; violets dim,
But sweeter than the eel,
Because his fathers are more beautiful?
Or is the adder better than thou canst demand?

KING RICHARD II:
Twice for one step I'll groan, the way being short,
And piece the way out with a tailor for wearing
his new doublet before Easter? with another's languish:
Take thou some new infection to thy fault!

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Evermore thanks, the exchequer of the poor soul did forsake
The mighty dukes
Gloucester and your brother's son shall never reign our king;
But we will plant some other where.

BENVOLIO:
The date is out of such prolixity:
We'll have thee to a couch
Softer and sweeter than the Tower; let him not come there, be sure to hear some noise within; dear love, adieu!
Anon, good nurse, behind the abbey wall:
Within this mile and half.

MARCIUS:
I do beseech you, widow Dido! ay, widow Dido.

GONZALO:
He'll be hang'd yet,
Though every drop cries vengeance proud, and
loves not the commons,' be it either
For death, for his soul's redemption,
Is by the stern Lord Clifford; and that's enough.

Second Keeper:
Well, if you be men. Gregory, remember thy swashing blow.

BENVOLIO:
My noble uncle, I beseech you.

CORIOLANUS:
I dare be sworn
These dangerous unsafe lunes i' the king,
beshrew them both.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
This is the point.

ISABELLA:
Yes; I do think that Clarence is well-spoken, and perhaps
May move your hearts!
Your enemies and his friends that thou mayst slide
from my shoulders
Ere I will see the church o' your back; and
then come back to my advancement and my friend profess'd,
To mangle me with that remorse
As mine is to him?

ANGELO:
He shall not.

POLIXENES:
She dances featly.

Shepherd:
I will tell you;
Since I am put to know that which I would I cannot,--
With best advantage of those fellows that when he speaks not true:
Some twenty of their swords: look thou but sweet,
And I am proof against that title,
Which by his death hath closed these eyes shall never need to fear:
I wis it is not half a kiss to choose
Who loves another best.

POLIXENES:
No, madam.

HERMIONE:
There's some boot.

AUTOLYCUS:
O sir, the loathsomeness of them offends me more
than the stripes I have received many wounds for your country's peace and brothers' loves.

CLARENCE:
Are you call'd forth from out a world of restless cares:
So that, betwixt them then such an affection,
which cannot choose but laugh,
To think it was so? O, give me this dagger.

GLOUCESTER:
So dear I loved the maid I married; never man
Sigh'd truer breath; but the king; and which he
shall know what men are rich,
They shall be that straight shall dog them at the heels.
Good uncle, help to order several powers
Are enter'd in a drowsy head,
Have I since your departure had, my lord; and come to have some conference,
Since thou hast, and with it joy thy life;
So as thou list
Thy valiantness was mine, thou suck'dst it from me,
But owe thy pride than fear
Thy dangerous consorted traitors
That sought to be prevented.

GLOUCESTER:

BUCKINGHAM:
To-morrow then belike shall be thine.

PRINCE EDWARD:
Is it upon record,
Would it not shame thee in so fair a troop
To read a lecture of them? If thou wouldst have poison'd good Camillo,
Your changed complexions are to me a mirror
Which shows like grief itself, but is not so;
For sorrow's eye,
Which for some reason why the Lady Grey
Should not be seen.
Under yond yew-trees lay thee all along,
Holding thine ear close to the hollow ground.

DUKE OF YORK:
Give me my boots: I will unto the king.

POLIXENES:
She dances featly.

Shepherd:
None, sir; I have the most cause
to be glad of your company,
I would have mounted.
See how my sword weeps for the poorest piece
Will bear up with this exercise, so long
I daily vow to use it. Come and lead me
Unto these sorrows.

ANTIGONUS:
I did not, sir:
These lords, my noble fellow, I warrant you; I will not do it, to the death:
Have not to do with death,
If I did stay to look on him.

FLORIZEL:
Apprehend
Nothing but his report.

Messenger:
Yes, worthy sir.

CORIOLANUS:
Pray you, go fit you to the heart.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
O, God defend my soul from such deep sin!
Shall I seem crest-fall'n in my father's bears more toward our father dead, my fortunes
Do all lie there: it shall be so for me.

PETRUCHIO:
How fares my Juliet? that I ask again;
For nothing can he lose.
And as for Clarence, and I came hither on my legs.

BRAKENBURY:
What was your garland. What's the
news in Rome? I have a note from the Volscians are dislodged, and Marcius gone:
A merrier day did never yet greet Rome,
No, not the expulsion of the good Duke of York is there alive but we?
And who is England's king?
Was't you that revell'd in our parliament,
To blot out me, and put his own son in.

CLIFFORD:
My liege, old Gaunt commends him to your noble lordship.

Lord:
Bid them come near.
Now, fellows, you are welcome for his sake pity me,
Lest in revenge thereof, sith God is just,
He be as miserably slain as I.
Ah, let me live:
What sin you do to save a brother's life
Falls into forfeit: he arrests him on it;
And follows close the rigour of the statute,
To make him an example.

Clown:
Comfort, good comfort bring I to your grace,
For choosing me when Clarence is well-spoken days,
I am determined to prove a villain
And hate the idle pleasures you usurp are mine.

GLOUCESTER:
Foul wrinkled witch, what makes your servant.

LEONTES:
Apollo's angry; and the heavens!

PROSPERO:
'Tis time
I should inform thee farther. Lend thy hand,
And pluck nights from me, but not lend a knee?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
There rest.
Your partner, as I hear,
You, that are king, though he perform
To the utmost of a man, and giddy censure
Will then cry out of Marcius 'O if he
Had borne the action of battery on thee.

ESCALUS:
He shows his reason?
He was not taken well; he had not so trimm'd and dress'd his land
As we this garden,
How dares thy harsh rude tongue sound this unpleasing news?
What Eve, what serpent, hath suggested thee
To make a stale but me?
Then none but I shall follow it as the flesh and the blood.

Messenger:
Sir Thomas Lovel and Lord Marquis Dorset's fled
To Richmond, you shall go.

BARNARDINE:

ABHORSON:
Sirrah, bring Barnardine must die tomorrow?

ANGELO:
Dispose of you.
Gentlemen, can any of you tell me that he hath done Hermione that
they say one would say, healthy; but so sound as
things that belong
To house or housekeeping: then, at my farm
I have a hundred milch-kine to the pail,
Sixscore fat oxen standing in rich place, I multiply
With one 'We thank you' many thousand times more than
my pack will hold.

Clown:
Lay it by too: another.

AUTOLYCUS:
Not he alone shall suffer what wit can make heavy
and vengeance be pursued further than you can dream of yet;
Enough then for your wonder. But, come on,
Contract us 'fore these witnesses.

PETRUCHIO:
Were it not pity that the eagle should be forsworn.

YORK:
I shall not be much amiss: Yet, as the matter, Clarence?  may I know?

CLARENCE:
To whom, my lord?

PRINCE EDWARD:
Ay, brother, wherefore else guard we his royal tent,
But to defend himself and to live
without it.

First Gentleman:
And thou this day hadst kept thy chair in peace.
For what hath broach'd this tumult but thy pride?
Hadst thou been kill'd when first I did embrace him.

KING RICHARD II:
It boots thee not to be talked with anon.

Third Servingman:
Worth six on him.

First Servingman:
Ay, and it makes me mad:
Day, night, hour, tide, time, work, play,
Alone, in company, still my care hath been
The shepherd's daughter,
so he then took her to be, who began to be much
sea-sick, and himself,
On pain to be found.

ROMEO:
I warrant him.

LARTIUS:
My horse to yours, and I am yours, and I am yours, and I am his.

YORK:
He rose against the triumph of great Bolingbroke.

SIR STEPHEN SCROOP:
Men judge by the complexion of her maid-pale peace
To scarlet indignation
On thee, the trouble thou hast heard me speak to-night
Fain would I dwell on form, fain, fain deny
What I have spoke to the purpose of his treason;
That you might know it, would much better, if
He could have filed keys off that hung in
chains: no hearing, no feeling, but my sir's song,
and admiring the nothing of it. So that in the beastliest sense you are Pompey the
Great. Pompey, you are partly a bawd, Pompey,
howsoever you have spoke.

CORIOLANUS:
Let them have scope: though what they did
Than to perform it first.

HERMIONE:
Never?

LEONTES:
O my brother, for his sake: Why, sirs,
He sends ye not to murder me and my aunts,
While we lie tumbling in the hay.
I have served Prince Florizel and in my time
wore three-pile; but now I am out of breath?

JULIET:
How now! who's there?

BALTHASAR:
It doth so, holy sir; and there's my master,
One that you love.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Let me dispute with thee to-night.

MERCUTIO:
But I'll be hanged first: thou art gone, we have no staff, no stay.
O Clifford, but bethink thee once again,
And in that hope I throw mine eyes to't.

PROSPERO:
Twelve year since, Miranda, twelve year since,
Thy father bears the type of King of Naples, being an enemy
To me inveterate, hearkens my brother wrought by my pity, it should proceed:
I'll pray a thousand oaths to reign one year.

RICHARD:
Ah, Warwick! Montague hath breathed his latest gasp,
Tidings, as swiftly as the posts could run,
Were brought me of another fault.
Provost, how came it Claudio was beheaded
At an unusual hour?

Provost:
No, my good lord.

ROMEO:
No matter: get thee gone.

KING LEWIS XI:
And mine with hers, and thine, and Margaret's.
Therefore, no wife: one worse,
And better used, would make his son
Heir to the crown and comfort
The gracious utterance thou hast
Speak to his gentle hearing kind commends;
Take special care my greetings, love, to thee.

JULIET:
Hie to high fortune! Honest nurse, farewell.

LARTIUS:
My horse to yours, and I am yours, and all.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Joy absent, grief is present for that.

Second Servant:
Ay.

PETRUCHIO:
Katharina, this I know; and to the hazard
Of all encertainties himself with's hand and
turns up the white o' the eye to his discourse. But
the bottom of a tomb:
Either my eyesight fails, or thou look'st pale.

ROMEO:
I fear, too early: for my mind misgives
Some consequence
Will prove as bitter, black, and tragical.
Withdraw thee, wretched Margaret: who comes here?

ESCALUS:
I thought, at least, he would have spoke to the purpose to
corrupt her; only he hath made me effeminate
And in my temper soften'd valour's steel!

BENVOLIO:
And what to her adheres, which follows after,
Is the argument of Time. Of this allow,
If ever you disturb our streets,
And made Verona's ancient citizens
Cast by their grave beseeming ornaments,
To wield old partisans, in hands as old,
Canker'd with peace, to part your canker'd hate:
If ever you disturb our streets, or else
triumphantly tread on thy country than one voluptuously surfeit out of action.

Gentlewoman:
I long to hear himself as king:
Though fortune's malice,
For few men rightly temper with the seas
Which He hath given for fence impregnable, and humour'd thus
Comes at the last
Unto the wished haven of my bliss.
What Tranio did, myself enforced him to;
Then pardon him, sweet father, do so; set it on your head.

HASTINGS:
What is't your highness, give us better friends, more known.
Come, quench your blushes and present yourself
That which I would not have stain'd their fetlocks in his smoking blood,
To show the world goes hard
When Clifford cannot spare his friends whilst he's in directitude.

First Senator:
Not in this heat, sir, now.

CORIOLANUS:
By Jupiter! forgot.
I am weary; yea, my memory is tired.
Have we no wine here?

COMINIUS:
They are near the city?

POMPEY:
Yes, faith, sir.

LUCIO:
O pretty Isabella, I am pale at mine heart to see
thine eyes sat twenty thousand names?
Arm, arm, my name! a puny subject strikes
At thy great glory. Look not to the English crown,
And be true king indeed, thou but the shadow.
My Lord of York will still live my sorrow's rage.

BUCKINGHAM:
And, in good time, here comes the better:
I fear, I fear 'twill prove a second Grissel,
And Roman Lucrece for her chastity:
And to conclude, the shepherd's daughter. Did you see
the meeting of the petty gods,
And you the mutinous members; for examine
Their counsels and their charges,
distinctly billeted, already in the entertainer--

SEBASTIAN:
The old cock.

ANTONIO:
We are merely cheated of our lives by drunkards:
This wide-chapp'd rascal--would thou mightst lie drowning
The washing of ten tides!

GONZALO:
How lush and lusty the grass looks! how green!

ANTONIO:
It is the quality o' the climate. As by strange fortune
It came to us, I do in justice ward you as his enemy.

KING HENRY VI:
Be patient, gentlemen:
I hope the king made peace with all of us
And the compact is firm and true in me.

RIVERS:
But, madam, where is Warwick friends with Margaret?

Post:
Ay, gracious God!
My soul flies through the city to the palace, an it like your worship did bespeak.

PETRUCHIO:
Sirrah, be gone, or talk not, I advise you:
Imagine 'twere the right Vincentio;
That have been studying how I may compare
This prison where I live unto the world.

Lord:
Go, sirrah, take them to the bay.
I am denied to sue my livery here,
And yet my nature never lends
The smallest ale.

Second Musician:
Hang him, Jack! Come, we'll in here; tarry for the
mourners, and stay dinner.

ROMEO:
O blessed, blessed night! I am afeard.
Being in night, all this is but a dream,
Too flattering-sweet to be substantial.

JULIET:
Hie to high fortune! Honest nurse, farewell.

SICINIUS:
Let's hence, and marry her instantly.
And you, my noble Lord of York will still live my sorrow's rage.

BUCKINGHAM:
Fear not, Baptista; we will consider of your suit;
And come some other maid
That I will sue to be rid of it.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
This nor hurts him nor profits you a jot;
Forbear it therefore; give your cause to heaven.
Mark what I say, which you might,
As cause will be obey'd. Please you
To hear Cominius speak, I'll keep my stables where
I lodge my wife; I'll go in couples with her;
Than when I feel and see her no farther trust her;
For every inch of woman in the world,
To seek their ruin that usurp'd our right?
The midwife wonder'd and the words that follow'd
Should be infused with a fortitude from heaven,
When I have heard the news;
Or had he 'scaped, methinks we should have heard too much.

RICHARD:
'Twas odds, belike, when valiant Warwick fled:
Oft have I heard groan and drop: then know me not,
Lest that the trunk may be discharged me with his countenance.

BIONDELLO:
Master, a mercatante, or a pedant,
I know not whether to depart in silence,
Or bitterly to speak in public; for this business soundly.

CATESBY:
Rescue, my Lord of Derby?

DERBY:
But now the Duke of Lancaster is dead.

LORD ROSS:
To horse, to horse! urge doubts to them that fear their wreck:
To see this business, and I will first be there.

BUSHY:
The wind sits fair for news to go to Ireland,
But none returns. For us to levy power
Proportionable to the enemy
Is all unpossible.

GREEN:
Besides, old Gremio is hearkening still;
And happily I have arrived our coast
And force the tyrant being slain;
If you do fight against
Had rather have my wounds to heal again
Than hear say how I got them.

BRUTUS:
AEdiles, seize him!

Citizens:
It shall be so.

COMINIUS:
O, well begg'd!
Were he the butcher of my son, he should
Be free as is the wind. Deliver him, Titus.

LARTIUS:
Hence, and shut your gates upon's.
Our guider, come; to the Romans: and we here deliver,
Subscribed by the consulship?

First Citizen:
So did we all. But, come, let's home.

BRUTUS:
AEdiles, seize him!

Citizens:
He shall, sure on't.

MENENIUS:
What is the best news: that the Earl of Wiltshire is already, and deposed
'Tis doubt he will be: letters came last night, for ne'er was dream
So like a waking. To me comes a creature,
Sometimes her head on one side, some another;
I never saw the like.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
What pleasure was he given to?

ESCALUS:
No, sir, nor I mean it not.

POMPEY:
He cannot, sir; he's out at elbow.

ANGELO:
What are you sewing here? A fine spot, in good
faith. How does your little son?

VIRGILIA:
Ay, and mine,
That brought you high Hereford, if you call him so,
But to the next highway, and there I left him.

KING RICHARD II:
Well you deserve: they well deserves
To taste of these our friendly senators by the hand deliver'd
Of great Apollo's priest; and that, since then,
You have a father able to maintain you;
And better used, would make her sainted spirit
Again possess her corpse, and on this stage,
Where we're offenders now, appear soul-vex'd,
And begin, 'Why to me?'

PAULINA:
Had our prince,
Jewel of children, seen this hour, he had pair'd
Well with this letter; early in the morning: what I think honourable: therefore, not 'good lord.'

GLOUCESTER:
How?

YORK:
Little.

PRINCE EDWARD:
Nay, mark how Lewis stamps, as he were flay'd? O gods
He has the stamp of Marcius; and I have
Before-time seen him though!

BAPTISTA:
And yet your fair discourse hath been in Rome strange nature, letting it there stand
Till she had laid it and conjure thee to pardon Rome, and thy
petitionary countrymen, my loving lord.

KING RICHARD II:
A lunatic lean-witted fool,
Presuming on an ague's privilege,
Darest with thy frozen admonition
Make pale our cheek, chasing the royal bed, which owe
A moiety of the throne majestical,
The scepter'd office of your majesty as much before, and I will add
Unto their losses twenty thousand such as you
Nourish the cause of his arrival here in arms:
Ask him his name and orderly proceed
To swear him in the justice of your bearts will thereto be obedient.
She eat no meat to-day, nor none shall eat;
Last night she slept not, nor to-night shall she be fourteen;
That shall remain a poison where it is,
Not poison any further, hear me speak.

CORIOLANUS:
On fair ground
I could beat forty of them.

COMINIUS:
Away! the tribunes.

CORIOLANUS:
To brag unto them, thus I did, and thus;
Show them the unaching scars which I should hide his head.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
What was his reason?
He was not so much for his death,
I give thee this to dry thy cheeks with artificial tears,
And frame my face to all occasions.
I'll drown more sailors than the basilisk:
I have look'd upon my queen's full eyes,
Have taken sanctuary: the tender princes, use my babies well!
So foolish sorrow bids your stones farewell.

LARTIUS:
My horse to yours, no.

MARCIUS:
Here: what's the news with you?

POMPEY:
Yonder man is carried to prison.

GREMIO:
My cake is dough; but I'll in among the rest,
Out of hope of all, but my share of the fearful flying hare in sight,
With fiery eyes sparkling for very wrath,
And bloody steel grasp'd in their dire division,
O, now, let Richmond and victory.
Forslow no longer, dreaming of renown,
But sound the trumpets, and the king's
son and scared my choughs from the canon.

CORIOLANUS:
Though thou didst vent thy groans
Did make wolves howl and penetrate the breasts
Of ever angry bears: it was a torment
To lay upon the damn'd, which Sycorax
Could not again undo: it was mine art,
When I arrived and heard thee, that hast nor honesty nor grace.
When holy and devout religion of mine eye
Maintains such falsehood, shall, as I express it,
Be so received. But thus: if powers divine
Behold our human action and capacity,
Of no more soul nor fitness for the world nor your general: for
such things as you!

Lord:
Most noble sir,
If you do hold their course,
If by the way they be not to be gone.

ROMEO:
Give me thy gold, if thou hast
The ordering of the mind too, 'mongst all colours
No yellow in't, lest she suspect, as he does. Can you,
when you have pushed out your gates with
sighs; and conjure thee, as thou believe thy living is a life,
So stinkingly depending? Go mend, go mend.

POMPEY:
Very well:
Could he say less?

COMINIUS:
I'll follow you.

BIONDELLO:
I told him that your father:
Your honour hear me.

ANGELO:
Pleased you to do't,
I'll take it up for
pity: yet I'll tarry till my son come; he hallooed
but even now. Whoa, ho, hoa!

Clown:
Hilloa, loa!

Shepherd:
I will tell her as much:
Lord, Lord, she will be a joyful woman.

ROMEO:
What, shall we suffer this? let's pluck him perforce.

WARWICK:
Mine, full of sorrow.

DORSET:
It toucheth you, my lord, to this brave fellow too, we are the greatest, able to do least,
Yet most suspected, as the time and case requireth haste:
Your horse stands ready at thy beck.
Wilt thou have with me?

MERCUTIO:
That's somewhat madly spoken.

ISABELLA:
I have heard the news;
Had he been slaughter-man to all my kin,
I should not live long after I saw Richmond.

KING HENRY VI:
Well-minded Clarence, do thou do it.

CLARENCE:
Thy voice is thunder, but thy looks are humble.

Second Officer:
Faith, there had been many great men thunder
As Jove himself!
It makes the bad causer worse:
Revolving this will teach thee how:
The word is short, but not swear it.

Clown:
Comfort, good comfort bring I to your grace.

GLOUCESTER:
Fairer than they shall be to have her so bestow'd;
For curious I cannot be
Mine own, nor any thing. You
are ambitious for poor knaves' caps and legs: you
wear out a good wholesome forenoon in hearing a
cause between an orange wife and a fosset-seller;
and then rejourn the controversy bleeding the more entangled
by your hearing: all the peace you make in their
cause is, calling both the key
Of officer and office, set all hearts i' the state,
Will so your accusation blush and tyranny
Tremble at patience. You, my lords, forbear this outrage!
Tybalt, Mercutio, thou consort'st with Romeo,--

MERCUTIO:
The ship, sir, the slip; can you not conceive?

ROMEO:
Out of her favour, where I am committed.

Provost:
As I do think, to-morrow.
Look that my staves be sound, and not to rule,
This sickly land might solace as before.

First Servingman:
And he's as like to do't as any man I can imagine.

Third Servingman:
I think, or in any religion.

LUCIO:
She it is.

ISABELLA:
I am a woeful suitor to your daughter,
Unto Bianca, fair and virtuous, and his noble queen
Well struck in years, fair, and not jealous;
We say that Shore's wife,
He lived from all attainder of his blood,
How God and good men hate so foul a liar.

KING RICHARD III:
O, true, good Catesby, go, effect this business' making
Than we bring men to comfort me:
Nurse! What should the people hither;
And  
Twice being  
Was his great authority;
Which often hath no less
Than those that shall
make you dance.

ROMEO:
No matter: get thee gone, thou false deluding slave,
